 nārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtya naraṃ caiva narottamam
 devīṃ sarasvatīṃ caiva tato jayam udīrayet
 janamejaya uvāca
 evaṃ nirvartya codvāhaṃ saṃgataḥ saha bandhubhiḥ
 kāḥ kathāś ca cakārāsau vaiśaṃpāyana kīrtaya
 mahābhāratayaṣṭir vaḥ suparvavyāsavaṃśajā
 skhalatām avalambāya jāyatāṃ bhavavartmani
 vṛtte vivāhe hṛṣṭātmā yad uvāca yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
 tat sarvaṃ kathayasveha kṛtavanto yad uttaram
 abhraśyāmaḥ piṅgajaṭābaddhakalāpaḥ
 prāṃśur daṇḍī kṛṣṇamṛgatvakparidhānaḥ
 sākṣāl lokān pāvayamānaḥ kavimukhyaḥ
 pārāśaryaḥ parvasu rūpaṃ vivṛṇotu
 oṃ vyāsaṃ vasiṣṭhanaptāraṃ śakteḥ pautram akalmaṣam
 parāśarātmajaṃ vande śukatātaṃ taponidhim
 vyāsāya viṣṇurūpāya vyāsarūpāya viṣṇave
 namo vai brahmanidhaye vāsiṣṭhāya namo namaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a kṛtvā vivāhaṃ tu kurupravīrās
tadābhimanyor muditasvapakṣāḥ
c viśramya catvāry uṣasaḥ pratītāḥ
sabhāṃ virāṭasya tato 'bhijagmuḥ
a sabhā tu sā matsyapateḥ samṛddhā
maṇipravekottamaratnacitrā
c nyastāsanā mālyavatī sugandhā
tām abhyayus te nararājavaryāḥ
a athāsanāny āviśatāṃ purastād
ubhau virāṭadrupadau narendrau
c vṛddhaś ca mānyaḥ pṛthivīpatīnāṃ
pitāmaho rāmajanārdanābhyām
a pāñcālarājasya samīpatas tu
śinipravīraḥ saharauhiṇeyaḥ
c matsyasya rājñas tu susaṃnikṛṣṭau
janārdanaś caiva yudhiṣṭhiraś ca
a sutāś ca sarve drupadasya rājño
bhīmārjunau mādravatīsutau ca
c pradyumnasāmbau ca yudhi pravīrau
virāṭaputraś ca sahābhimanyuḥ
a sarve ca śūrāḥ pitṛbhiḥ samānā
vīryeṇa rūpeṇa balena caiva
c upāviśan draupadeyāḥ kumārāḥ
suvarṇacitreṣu varāsaneṣu
a tathopaviṣṭeṣu mahāratheṣu
vibhrājamānāmbarabhūṣaṇeṣu
c rarāja sā rājavatī samṛddhā
grahair iva dyaur vimalair upetā
a tataḥ kathās te samavāyayuktāḥ
kṛtvā vicitrāḥ puruṣapravīrāḥ
c tasthur muhūrtaṃ paricintayantaḥ
kṛṣṇaṃ nṛpās te samudīkṣamāṇāḥ
a kathāntam āsādya ca mādhavena
saṃghaṭṭitāḥ pāṇḍavakāryahetoḥ
b kṛṣṇena vṛṣṇipravareṇa tatra
c te rājasiṃhāḥ sahitā hy aśṛṇvan
vākyaṃ mahārthaṃ ca mahodayaṃ ca
 kṛṣṇa uvāca
a sarvair bhavadbhir viditaṃ yathāyaṃ
yudhiṣṭhiraḥ saubalenākṣavatyām
c jito nikṛtyāpahṛtaṃ ca rājyaṃ
punaḥ pravāse samayaḥ kṛtaś ca
a śaktair vijetuṃ tarasā mahīṃ ca
satye sthitais tac caritaṃ yathāvat
c pāṇḍoḥ sutais tad vratam ugrarūpaṃ
varṣāṇi ṣaṭ sapta ca bhāratāgryaiḥ
a trayodaśaś caiva sudustaro 'yam
ajñāyamānair bhavatāṃ samīpe
c kleśān asahyāṃś ca titikṣamāṇair
yathoṣitaṃ tad viditaṃ ca sarvam
 etaiḥ parapreṣyaniyogayuktair
 icchadbhir āptaṃ svakulena rājyam
a evaṃ gate dharmasutasya rājño
duryodhanasyāpi ca yad dhitaṃ syāt
c tac cintayadhvaṃ kurupāṇḍavānāṃ
dharmyaṃ ca yuktaṃ ca yaśaskaraṃ ca
a adharmayuktaṃ ca na kāmayeta
rājyaṃ surāṇām api dharmarājaḥ
c dharmārthayuktaṃ ca mahīpatitvaṃ
grāme 'pi kasmiṃś cid ayaṃ bubhūṣet
a pitryaṃ hi rājyaṃ viditaṃ nṛpāṇāṃ
yathāpakṛṣṭaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭraputraiḥ
c mithyopacāreṇa tathāpy anena
kṛcchraṃ mahat prāptam asahyarūpam
a na cāpi pārtho vijito raṇe taiḥ
svatejasā dhṛtarāṣṭrasya putraiḥ
c tathāpi rājā sahitaḥ suhṛdbhir
abhīpsate 'nāmayam eva teṣām
a yat tat svayaṃ pāṇḍusutair vijitya
samāhṛtaṃ bhūmipatīn nipīḍya
c tat prārthayante puruṣapravīrāḥ
kuntīsutā mādravatīsutau ca
a bālās tv ime tair vividhair upāyaiḥ
saṃprārthitā hantum amitrasāhāḥ
c rājyaṃ jihīrṣadbhir asadbhir ugraiḥ
sarvaṃ ca tad vo viditaṃ yathāvat
a teṣāṃ ca lobhaṃ prasamīkṣya vṛddhaṃ
dharmātmatāṃ cāpi yudhiṣṭhirasya
c saṃbandhitāṃ cāpi samīkṣya teṣāṃ
matiṃ kurudhvaṃ sahitāḥ pṛthak ca
a ime ca satye 'bhiratāḥ sadaiva
taṃ pārayitvā samayaṃ yathāvat
c ato 'nyathā tair upacaryamāṇā
hanyuḥ sametān dhṛtarāṣṭraputrān
a tair viprakāraṃ ca niśamya rājñaḥ
suhṛjjanās tān parivārayeyuḥ
c yuddhena bādheyur imāṃs tathaiva
tair vadhyamānā yudhi tāṃś ca hanyuḥ
d tyaktās tathā bandhujanena cāmī
d dharmeṇa vairīn nihatāś ca hanyuḥ
a tathāpi neme 'lpatayā samarthās
teṣāṃ jayāyeti bhaven mataṃ vaḥ
c sametya sarve sahitāḥ suhṛdbhis
teṣāṃ vināśāya yateyur eva
a duryodhanasyāpi mataṃ yathāvan
na jñāyate kiṃ nu kariṣyatīti
c ajñāyamāne ca mate parasya
kiṃ syāt samārabhyatamaṃ mataṃ vaḥ
a tasmād ito gacchatu dharmaśīlaḥ
śuciḥ kulīnaḥ puruṣo 'pramattaḥ
c dūtaḥ samarthaḥ praśamāya teṣāṃ
rājyārdhadānāya yudhiṣṭhirasya
a niśamya vākyaṃ tu janārdanasya
dharmārthayuktaṃ madhuraṃ samaṃ ca
c samādade vākyam athāgrajo 'sya
saṃpūjya vākyaṃ tad atīva rājan
 baladeva uvāca
a śrutaṃ bhavadbhir gadapūrvajasya
vākyaṃ yathā dharmavad arthavac ca
c ajātaśatroś ca hitaṃ hitaṃ ca
duryodhanasyāpi tathaiva rājñaḥ
a ardhaṃ hi rājyasya visṛjya vīrāḥ
kuntīsutās tasya kṛte yatante
a jitā gatāraṇyam itaḥ purā te
b mādrīsutau caiva kurupravīrau
c pradāya cārdhaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭraputraḥ
sukhī sahāsmābhir atīva modet
a labdhvā hi rājyaṃ puruṣapravīrāḥ
samyak pravṛtteṣu pareṣu caiva
c dhruvaṃ praśāntāḥ sukham āviśeyus
teṣāṃ praśāntiś ca hitaṃ prajānām
d tato vināśaḥ kurupāṇḍavānāṃ
d sabāndhavānāṃ bhavitācireṇa
d tasmād yad uktaṃ madhusūdanena
d tat sarvalokasya hitaṃ yatadhvam
a duryodhanasyāpi mataṃ ca vettuṃ
vaktuṃ ca vākyāni yudhiṣṭhirasya
b prayātu dūtaḥ puruṣaḥ pradhāno
b hitāya teṣāṃ ca tathaiva caiṣām
c priyaṃ mama syād yadi tatra kaś cid
vrajec chamārthaṃ kurupāṇḍavānām
a sa bhīṣmam āmantrya kurupravīraṃ
vaicitravīryaṃ ca mahānubhāvam
c droṇaṃ saputraṃ viduraṃ kṛpaṃ ca
gāndhārarājaṃ ca sasūtaputram
a sarve ca ye 'nye dhṛtarāṣṭraputrā
balapradhānā nigamapradhānāḥ
c sthitāś ca dharmeṣu yathā svakeṣu
lokapravīrāḥ śrutakālavṛddhāḥ
a eteṣu sarveṣu samāgateṣu
paureṣu vṛddheṣu ca saṃgateṣu
c bravītu vākyaṃ praṇipātayuktaṃ
kuntīsutasyārthakaraṃ yathā syāt
a sarvāsv avasthāsu ca te na kauṭyād
grasto hi so 'rtho balam āśritais taiḥ
c priyābhyupetasya yudhiṣṭhirasya
dyūte pramattasya hṛtaṃ ca rājyam
a nivāryamāṇaś ca kurupravīraiḥ
sarvaiḥ suhṛdbhir hy ayam apy atajjñaḥ
b sa dīvyamānaḥ pratidīvya cainaṃ
c gāndhārarājasya sutaṃ matākṣaṃ
samāhvayed devitum ājamīḍhaḥ
c hitvā hi karṇaṃ ca suyodhanaṃ ca
a durodarās tatra sahasraśo 'nye
yudhiṣṭhiro yān viṣaheta jetum
c utsṛjya tān saubalam eva cāyaṃ
samāhvayat tena jito 'kṣavatyām
a sa dīvyamānaḥ pratidevanena
akṣeṣu nityaṃ suparāṅmukheṣu
c saṃrambhamāṇo vijitaḥ prasahya
tatrāparādhaḥ śakuner na kaś cit
a tasmāt praṇamyaiva vaco bravītu
vaicitravīryaṃ bahusāmayuktam
c tathā hi śakyo dhṛtarāṣṭraputraḥ
svārthe niyoktuṃ puruṣeṇa tena
d ayuddham ākāṅkṣata kauravāṇāṃ
d sāmnaiva duryodhanam āhvayadhvam
d sāmnā jito 'rtho 'rthakaro bhaveta
d yuddhe 'nayo bhavitā neha so 'rthaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a evaṃ bruvaty eva madhupravīre
śinipravīraḥ sahasotpapāta
c tac cāpi vākyaṃ parinindya tasya
samādade vākyam idaṃ samanyuḥ
 sātyakir uvāca
a yādṛśaḥ puruṣasyātmā tādṛśaṃ saṃprabhāṣate
c yathārūpo 'ntarātmā te tathārūpaṃ prabhāṣase
a santi vai puruṣāḥ śūrāḥ santi kāpuruṣās tathā
c ubhāv etau dṛḍhau pakṣau dṛśyete puruṣān prati
a ekasminn eva jāyete kule klībamahārathau
c phalāphalavatī śākhe yathaikasmin vanaspatau
a nābhyasūyāmi te vākyaṃ bruvato lāṅgaladhvaja
c ye tu śṛṇvanti te vākyaṃ tān asūyāmi mādhava
a kathaṃ hi dharmarājasya doṣam alpam api bruvan
c labhate pariṣanmadhye vyāhartum akutobhayaḥ
a samāhūya mahātmānaṃ jitavanto 'kṣakovidāḥ
c anakṣajñaṃ yathāśraddhaṃ teṣu dharmajayaḥ kutaḥ
a yadi kuntīsutaṃ gehe krīḍantaṃ bhrātṛbhiḥ saha
c abhigamya jayeyus te tat teṣāṃ dharmato bhavet
a samāhūya tu rājānaṃ kṣatradharmarataṃ sadā
c nikṛtyā jitavantas te kiṃ nu teṣāṃ paraṃ śubham
a kathaṃ praṇipatec cāyam iha kṛtvā paṇaṃ param
c vanavāsād vimuktas tu prāptaḥ paitāmahaṃ padam
a yady ayaṃ paravittāni kāmayeta yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c evam apy ayam atyantaṃ parān nārhati yācitum
a kathaṃ ca dharmayuktās te na ca rājyaṃ jihīrṣavaḥ
c nivṛttavāsān kaunteyān ya āhur viditā iti
a anunītā hi bhīṣmeṇa droṇena ca mahātmanā
c na vyavasyanti pāṇḍūnāṃ pradātuṃ paitṛkaṃ vasu
a ahaṃ tu tāñ śitair bāṇair anunīya raṇe balāt
c pādayoḥ pātayiṣyāmi kaunteyasya mahātmanaḥ
a atha te na vyavasyanti praṇipātāya dhīmataḥ
c gamiṣyanti sahāmātyā yamasya sadanaṃ prati
d daśāśā chādayantaṃ mām ekavīraṃ madotkaṭam
d vijiṣṇuṃ manyate loko yudhyantaṃ ca mahītale
d satyaṃ mamāntevāsitvaṃ jayasya jayaśālinaḥ
d chinadmi yadi khaḍgena bhīṣmādīnāṃ śirāṃsy aham
a na hi te yuyudhānasya saṃrabdhasya yuyutsataḥ
c vegaṃ samarthāḥ saṃsoḍhuṃ vajrasyeva mahīdharāḥ
a ko hi gāṇḍīvadhanvānaṃ kaś ca cakrāyudhaṃ yudhi
c māṃ cāpi viṣahet ko nu kaś ca bhīmaṃ durāsadam
a yamau ca dṛḍhadhanvānau yamakalpau mahādyutī
b virāṭadrupadau vīrau yamakālopamadyutī
c ko jijīviṣur āsīded dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ ca pārṣatam
a pañcemān pāṇḍaveyāṃś ca draupadyāḥ kīrtivardhanān
c samapramāṇān pāṇḍūnāṃ samavīryān madotkaṭān
a saubhadraṃ ca maheṣvāsam amarair api duḥsaham
c gadapradyumnasāmbāṃś ca kālavajrānalopamān
a te vayaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrasya putraṃ śakuninā saha
c karṇena ca nihatyājāv abhiṣekṣyāma pāṇḍavam
a nādharmo vidyate kaś cic chatrūn hatvātatāyinaḥ
c adharmyam ayaśasyaṃ ca śātravāṇāṃ prayācanam
d agnido garadaś caiva śastrapāṇir dhanāpahaḥ
d kṣetradāraharaś caiva ṣaḍ ete hy ātatāyinaḥ
d ātatāyinam āyāntam api vedāntavādinam
d jighāṃsantaṃ jighāṃsīyān na tena brahmahā bhavet
a hṛdgatas tasya yaḥ kāmas taṃ kurudhvam atandritāḥ
c nisṛṣṭaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭreṇa rājyaṃ prāpnotu pāṇḍavaḥ
a adya pāṇḍusuto rājyaṃ labhatāṃ vā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c nihatā vā raṇe sarve svapsyanti vasudhātale
 drupada uvāca
a evam etan mahābāho bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ
c na hi duryodhano rājyaṃ madhureṇa pradāsyati
a anuvartsyati taṃ cāpi dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ sutapriyaḥ
c bhīṣmadroṇau ca kārpaṇyān maurkhyād rādheyasaubalau
a baladevasya vākyaṃ tu mama jñāne na yujyate
c etad dhi puruṣeṇāgre kāryaṃ sunayam icchatā
a na tu vācyo mṛdu vaco dhārtarāṣṭraḥ kathaṃ cana
c na hi mārdavasādhyo 'sau pāpabuddhir mato mama
a gardabhe mārdavaṃ kuryād goṣu tīkṣṇaṃ samācaret
c mṛdu duryodhane vākyaṃ yo brūyāt pāpacetasi
d aham eko 'pi jeṣyāmi prāk caiva prahiṇomi tam
d nāhaṃ kuryāṃ yad etad vai viśvāsād eva śāśvatam
d aham eko vijeṣyāmi prāhatān saṃvidhāya ca
d nāhaṃ karomi tadvākyaṃ praṇipātanapūrvakam
a mṛdu vai manyate pāpo bhāṣyamāṇam aśaktijam
c jitam arthaṃ vijānīyād abudho mārdave sati
a etac caiva kariṣyāmo yatnaś ca kriyatām iha
c prasthāpayāma mitrebhyo balāny udyojayantu naḥ
a śalyasya dhṛṣṭaketoś ca jayatsenasya cābhibhoḥ
c kekayānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ dūtā gacchantu śīghragāḥ
a sa tu duryodhano nūnaṃ preṣayiṣyati sarvaśaḥ
b tāvad dūtān vayaṃ tūrṇaṃ preṣayiṣyāma māciram
b sa tu duryodhano nūnaṃ preṣayiṣyati tān nṛpān
c pūrvābhipannāḥ santaś ca bhajante pūrvacodakam
a tat tvaradhvaṃ narendrāṇāṃ pūrvam eva pracodane
c mahad dhi kāryaṃ voḍhavyam iti me vartate matiḥ
a śalyasya preṣyatāṃ śīghraṃ ye ca tasyānugā nṛpāḥ
c bhagadattāya rājñe ca pūrvasāgaravāsine
a amitaujase tathogrāya hārdikyāyāhukāya ca
c dīrghaprajñāya mallāya rocamānāya cābhibho
a ānīyatāṃ bṛhantaś ca senābinduś ca pārthivaḥ
c pāpajit prativindhyaś ca citravarmā suvāstukaḥ
a bāhlīko muñjakeśaś ca caidyādhipatir eva ca
c supārśvaś ca subāhuś ca pauravaś ca mahārathaḥ
a śakānāṃ pahlavānāṃ ca daradānāṃ ca ye nṛpāḥ
c kāmbojā ṛṣikā ye ca paścimānūpakāś ca ye
a jayatsenaś ca kāśyaś ca tathā pañcanadā nṛpāḥ
c krāthaputraś ca durdharṣaḥ pārvatīyāś ca ye nṛpāḥ
a jānakiś ca suśarmā ca maṇimān pautimatsyakaḥ
c pāṃsurāṣṭrādhipaś caiva dhṛṣṭaketuś ca vīryavān
a auḍraś ca daṇḍadhāraś ca bṛhatsenaś ca vīryavān
c aparājito niṣādaś ca śreṇimān vasumān api
a bṛhadbalo mahaujāś ca bāhuḥ parapuraṃjayaḥ
c samudraseno rājā ca saha putreṇa vīryavān
a adāriś ca nadījaś ca karṇaveṣṭaś ca pārthivaḥ
c samarthaś ca suvīraś ca mārjāraḥ kanyakas tathā
c   eko vīryabalotkaṭaḥ
c vīrabāhuḥ subāhuś ca
d vīrabāhuś ca durdharṣo bhūmipo jālakīṭakaḥ
a mahāvīraś ca kadruś ca nikaras tumulaḥ krathaḥ
c nīlaś ca vīradharmā ca bhūmipālaś ca vīryavān
a durjayo dantavaktraś ca rukmī ca janamejayaḥ
c āṣāḍho vāyuvegaś ca pūrvapālī ca pārthivaḥ
d ārṣo devā budhaḥ sūtas tathā harihayopamaḥ
a bhūritejā devakaś ca ekalavyasya cātmajaḥ
c kārūṣakāś ca rājānaḥ kṣemadhūrtiś ca vīryavān
a udbhavaḥ kṣemakaś caiva vāṭadhānaś ca pārthivaḥ
c śrutāyuś ca dṛḍhāyuś ca śālvaputraś ca vīryavān
a kumāraś ca kaliṅgānām īśvaro yuddhadurmadaḥ
c eteṣāṃ preṣyatāṃ śīghram etad dhi mama rocate
a ayaṃ ca brāhmaṇaḥ śīghraṃ mama rājan purohitaḥ
c preṣyatāṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrāya vākyam asmin samarpyatām
a yathā duryodhano vācyo yathā śāṃtanavo nṛpaḥ
c dhṛtarāṣṭro yathā vācyo droṇaś ca viduṣāṃ varaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
 drupadenaivam ukte tu vākye vākyaviśāradaḥ
 vasudevasutas tatra vṛṣṇisiṃho 'bravīd idam
 vāsudeva uvāca
a upapannam idaṃ vākyaṃ somakānāṃ dhuraṃdhare
c arthasiddhikaraṃ rājñaḥ pāṇḍavasya mahaujasaḥ
a etac ca pūrvakāryaṃ naḥ sunītam abhikāṅkṣatām
c anyathā hy ācaran karma puruṣaḥ syāt subāliśaḥ
a kiṃ tu saṃbandhakaṃ tulyam asmākaṃ kurupāṇḍuṣu
c yatheṣṭaṃ vartamāneṣu pāṇḍaveṣu ca teṣu ca
a te vivāhārtham ānītā vayaṃ sarve yathā bhavān
c kṛte vivāhe muditā gamiṣyāmo gṛhān prati
a bhavān vṛddhatamo rājñāṃ vayasā ca śrutena ca
c śiṣyavat te vayaṃ sarve bhavāmeha na saṃśayaḥ
a bhavantaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭraś ca satataṃ bahu manyate
c ācāryayoḥ sakhā cāsi droṇasya ca kṛpasya ca
d tasmād yad anurūpaṃ hi sāṃprataṃ tv iha manyase
d taṃ preṣaya yathānyāyaṃ kurubhyo nṛpasattama
a sa bhavān preṣayatv adya pāṇḍavārthakaraṃ vacaḥ
c sarveṣāṃ niścitaṃ tan naḥ preṣayiṣyati yad bhavān
a yadi tāvac chamaṃ kuryān nyāyena kurupuṃgavaḥ
b kṛtam ity eva saubhrātram ācariṣyanti pāṇḍavāḥ
c na bhavet kurupāṇḍūnāṃ saubhrātreṇa mahān kṣayaḥ
a atha darpānvito mohān na kuryād dhṛtarāṣṭrajaḥ
c anyeṣāṃ preṣayitvā ca paścād asmān samāhvayeḥ
a tato duryodhano mandaḥ sahāmātyaḥ sabāndhavaḥ
c niṣṭhām āpatsyate mūḍhaḥ kruddhe gāṇḍīvadhanvani
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tataḥ satkṛtya vārṣṇeyaṃ virāṭaḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ
c gṛhān prasthāpayām āsa sagaṇaṃ sahabāndhavam
a dvārakāṃ tu gate kṛṣṇe yudhiṣṭhirapurogamāḥ
c cakruḥ sāṃgrāmikaṃ sarvaṃ virāṭaś ca mahīpatiḥ
a tataḥ saṃpreṣayām āsa virāṭaḥ saha bāndhavaiḥ
c sarveṣāṃ bhūmipālānāṃ drupadaś ca mahīpatiḥ
a vacanāt kurusiṃhānāṃ matsyapāñcālayoś ca te
c samājagmur mahīpālāḥ saṃprahṛṣṭā mahābalāḥ
a tac chrutvā pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ samāgacchan mahad balam
c dhṛtarāṣṭrasutaś cāpi samāninye mahīpatīn
a samākulā mahī rājan kurupāṇḍavakāraṇāt
c tadā samabhavat kṛtsnā saṃprayāṇe mahīkṣitām
d saṃkulā ca tadā bhūmiś caturaṅgabalānvitā
a balāni teṣāṃ vīrāṇām āgacchanti tatas tataḥ
c cālayantīva gāṃ devīṃ saparvatavanām imām
a tataḥ prajñāvayovṛddhaṃ pāñcālyaḥ svapurohitam
c kurubhyaḥ preṣayām āsa yudhiṣṭhiramate tadā
 drupada uvāca
a bhūtānāṃ prāṇinaḥ śreṣṭhāḥ prāṇināṃ buddhijīvinaḥ
c buddhimatsu narāḥ śreṣṭhā narāṇāṃ tu dvijātayaḥ
a dvijeṣu vaidyāḥ śreyāṃso vaidyeṣu kṛtabuddhayaḥ
b kṛtabuddhiṣu kartāraḥ kartṛṣu brahmavādinaḥ
c sa bhavān kṛtabuddhīnāṃ pradhāna iti me matiḥ
a kulena ca viśiṣṭo 'si vayasā ca śrutena ca
c prajñayānavamaś cāsi śukreṇāṅgirasena ca
a viditaṃ cāpi te sarvaṃ yathāvṛttaḥ sa kauravaḥ
c pāṇḍavaś ca yathāvṛttaḥ kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a dhṛtarāṣṭrasya vidite vañcitāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ paraiḥ
c vidureṇānunīto 'pi putram evānuvartate
a śakunir buddhipūrvaṃ hi kuntīputraṃ samāhvayat
c anakṣajñaṃ matākṣaḥ san kṣatravṛtte sthitaṃ śucim
a te tathā vañcayitvā tu dharmaputraṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
c na kasyāṃ cid avasthāyāṃ rājyaṃ dāsyanti vai svayam
a bhavāṃs tu dharmasaṃyuktaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ bruvan vacaḥ
c manāṃsi tasya yodhānāṃ dhruvam āvartayiṣyati
a viduraś cāpi tad vākyaṃ sādhayiṣyati tāvakam
c bhīṣmadroṇakṛpāṇāṃ ca bhedaṃ saṃjanayiṣyati
a amātyeṣu ca bhinneṣu yodheṣu vimukheṣu ca
c punar ekāgrakaraṇaṃ teṣāṃ karma bhaviṣyati
a etasminn antare pārthāḥ sukham ekāgrabuddhayaḥ
c senākarma kariṣyanti dravyāṇāṃ caiva saṃcayam
a bhidyamāneṣu ca sveṣu lambamāne ca vai tvayi
c na tathā te kariṣyanti senākarma na saṃśayaḥ
a etat prayojanaṃ cātra prādhānyenopalabhyate
c saṃgatyā dhṛtarāṣṭraś ca kuryād dharmyaṃ vacas tava
a sa bhavān dharmayuktaś ca dharmyaṃ teṣu samācaran
c kṛpāluṣu parikleśān pāṇḍavānāṃ prakīrtayan
a vṛddheṣu kuladharmaṃ ca bruvan pūrvair anuṣṭhitam
c vibhetsyati manāṃsy eṣām iti me nātra saṃśayaḥ
a na ca tebhyo bhayaṃ te 'sti brāhmaṇo hy asi vedavit
c dūtakarmaṇi yuktaś ca sthaviraś ca viśeṣataḥ
a sa bhavān puṣyayogena muhūrtena jayena ca
c kauraveyān prayātv āśu kaunteyasyārthasiddhaye
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tathānuśiṣṭaḥ prayayau drupadena mahātmanā
c purodhā vṛttasaṃpanno nagaraṃ nāgasāhvayam
d śiṣyaiḥ parivṛto vidvān nītiśāstrārthakovidaḥ
d pāṇḍavānāṃ hitārthāya kauravān prati jagmivān
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
 purohitaṃ te prasthāpya nagaraṃ nāgasāhvayam
 dūtān prasthāpayām āsuḥ pārthivebhyas tatas tataḥ
 prasthāpya dūtān anyatra dvārakāṃ puruṣarṣabhaḥ
 svayaṃ jagāma kauravyaḥ kuntīputro dhanaṃjayaḥ
a gate dvāravatīṃ kṛṣṇe baladeve ca mādhave
c saha vṛṣṇyandhakaiḥ sarvair bhojaiś ca śataśas tathā
a sarvam āgamayām āsa pāṇḍavānāṃ viceṣṭitam
c dhṛtarāṣṭrātmajo rājā dūtaiḥ praṇihitaiś caraiḥ
a sa śrutvā mādhavaṃ yātaṃ sadaśvair anilopamaiḥ
c balena nātimahatā dvārakām abhyayāt purīm
a tam eva divasaṃ cāpi kaunteyaḥ pāṇḍunandanaḥ
c ānartanagarīṃ ramyāṃ jagāmāśu dhanaṃjayaḥ
a tau yātvā puruṣavyāghrau dvārakāṃ kurunandanau
c suptaṃ dadṛśatuḥ kṛṣṇaṃ śayānaṃ copajagmatuḥ
a tataḥ śayāne govinde praviveśa suyodhanaḥ
c ucchīrṣataś ca kṛṣṇasya niṣasāda varāsane
d siṃhāsanagataṃ paścāt parivṛtya ca dṛṣṭavān
a tataḥ kirīṭī tasyānu praviveśa mahāmanāḥ
c paścārdhe ca sa kṛṣṇasya prahvo 'tiṣṭhat kṛtāñjaliḥ
a pratibuddhaḥ sa vārṣṇeyo dadarśāgre kirīṭinam
b ucchīrṣataś cāsanasthaṃ dadarśātha suyodhanam
b paścād duryodhanaṃ bhūpam ucchīrṣe saṃsthitaṃ tadā
b vaicitravīryajaṃ paścād yādavānāṃ dhuraṃdharaḥ
b paścād duryodhanaṃ śaurir apaśyad amitadyutiḥ
c sa tayoḥ svāgataṃ kṛtvā yathārhaṃ pratipūjya ca
e tadāgamanajaṃ hetuṃ papraccha madhusūdanaḥ
a tato duryodhanaḥ kṛṣṇam uvāca prahasann iva
c vigrahe 'smin bhavān sāhyaṃ mama dātum ihārhati
a samaṃ hi bhavataḥ sakhyaṃ mayi caivārjune 'pi ca
c tathā saṃbandhakaṃ tulyam asmākaṃ tvayi mādhava
a ahaṃ cābhigataḥ pūrvaṃ tvām adya madhusūdana
c pūrvaṃ cābhigataṃ santo bhajante pūrvasāriṇaḥ
a tvaṃ ca śreṣṭhatamo loke satām adya janārdana
c satataṃ saṃmataś caiva sadvṛttam anupālaya
d śrībhagavān uvāca
d svāgataṃ tava gāndhāre na mayā vidito bhavān
d duryodhanaḥ
d kiṃ cāgamanakṛtyaṃ te kasmin kāle tvam āgataḥ
d tvaddarśanārthī govinda ahaṃ pūrvam ihāgataḥ
d prītyarthī sa bhavān sāhyaṃ mama dātum ihārhati
d dhārtarāṣṭrasya tad vākyaṃ śrutvāmaravarottamaḥ
d puruṣottamas tv idaṃ vākyaṃ duryodhanam abhāṣata
 kṛṣṇa uvāca
a bhavān abhigataḥ pūrvam atra me nāsti saṃśayaḥ
c dṛṣṭas tu prathamaṃ rājan mayā pārtho dhanaṃjayaḥ
a tava pūrvābhigamanāt pūrvaṃ cāpy asya darśanāt
c sāhāyyam ubhayor eva kariṣyāmi suyodhana
a pravāraṇaṃ tu bālānāṃ pūrvaṃ kāryam iti śrutiḥ
c tasmāt pravāraṇaṃ pūrvam arhaḥ pārtho dhanaṃjayaḥ
a matsaṃhananatulyānāṃ gopānām arbudaṃ mahat
c nārāyaṇā iti khyātāḥ sarve saṃgrāmayodhinaḥ
a te vā yudhi durādharṣā bhavantv ekasya sainikāḥ
c ayudhyamānaḥ saṃgrāme nyastaśastro 'ham ekataḥ
d etad viditvā kaunteya vicārya ca punaḥ punaḥ
d tān vā varaya sāhāyye māṃ sācivyena vā punaḥ
a ābhyām anyataraṃ pārtha yat te hṛdyataraṃ matam
c tad vṛṇītāṃ bhavān agre pravāryas tvaṃ hi dharmataḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a evam uktas tu kṛṣṇena kuntīputro dhanaṃjayaḥ
c ayudhyamānaṃ saṃgrāme varayām āsa keśavam
d nārāyaṇam amitraghnaṃ kāmāj jātam ajaṃ nṛṣu
d sarvakṣatrasya purato devadānavayor api
d duryodhanas tu tat sainyaṃ sarvam āvarayat tadā
a sahasrāṇāṃ sahasraṃ tu yodhānāṃ prāpya bhārata
c kṛṣṇaṃ cāpahṛtaṃ jñātvā saṃprāpa paramāṃ mudam
a duryodhanas tu tat sainyaṃ sarvam ādāya pārthivaḥ
c tato 'bhyayād bhīmabalo rauhiṇeyaṃ mahābalam
a sarvaṃ cāgamane hetuṃ sa tasmai saṃnyavedayat
c pratyuvāca tataḥ śaurir dhārtarāṣṭram idaṃ vacaḥ
a viditaṃ te naravyāghra sarvaṃ bhavitum arhati
c yan mayoktaṃ virāṭasya purā vaivāhike tadā
a nigṛhyokto hṛṣīkeśas tvadarthaṃ kurunandana
c mayā saṃbandhakaṃ tulyam iti rājan punaḥ punaḥ
a na ca tad vākyam uktaṃ vai keśavaḥ pratyapadyata
c na cāham utsahe kṛṣṇaṃ vinā sthātum api kṣaṇam
a nāhaṃ sahāyaḥ pārthānāṃ nāpi duryodhanasya vai
c iti me niścitā buddir vāsudevam avekṣya ha
a jāto 'si bhārate vaṃśe sarvapārthivapūjite
c gaccha yudhyasva dharmeṇa kṣātreṇa bharatarṣabha
a ity evam uktaḥ sa tadā pariṣvajya halāyudham
c kṛṣṇaṃ cāpahṛtaṃ jñātvā yuddhān mene jitaṃ jayam
a so 'bhyayāt kṛtavarmāṇaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrasuto nṛpaḥ
c kṛtavarmā dadau tasya senām akṣauhiṇīṃ tadā
a sa tena sarvasainyena bhīmena kurunandanaḥ
c vṛtaḥ pratiyayau hṛṣṭaḥ suhṛdaḥ saṃpraharṣayan
d tataḥ pītāmbaradharo jagatsraṣṭā janārdanaḥ
a gate duryodhane kṛṣṇaḥ kirīṭinam athābravīt
c ayudhyamānaḥ kāṃ buddhim āsthāyāhaṃ tvayā vṛtaḥ
 arjuna uvāca
a bhavān samarthas tān sarvān nihantuṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ
c nihantum aham apy ekaḥ samarthaḥ puruṣottama
a bhavāṃs tu kīrtimāṃl loke tad yaśas tvāṃ gamiṣyati
c yaśasā cāham apy arthī tasmād asi mayā vṛtaḥ
a sārathyaṃ tu tvayā kāryam iti me mānasaṃ sadā
c cirarātrepsitaṃ kāmaṃ tad bhavān kartum arhati
 vāsudeva uvāca
a upapannam idaṃ pārtha yat spardhethā mayā saha
c sārathyaṃ te kariṣyāmi kāmaḥ saṃpadyatāṃ tava
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a evaṃ pramuditaḥ pārthaḥ kṛṣṇena sahitas tadā
c vṛto dāśārhapravaraiḥ punar āyād yudhiṣṭhiram
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a śalyaḥ śrutvā tu dūtānāṃ sainyena mahatā vṛtaḥ
c abhyayāt pāṇḍavān rājan saha putrair mahārathaiḥ
a tasya senāniveśo 'bhūd adhyardham iva yojanam
c tathā hi bahulāṃ senāṃ sa bibharti nararṣabhaḥ
d akṣauhiṇīpatī rājan mahāvīryaparākramaḥ
a vicitrakavacāḥ śūrā vicitradhvajakārmukāḥ
c vicitrābharaṇāḥ sarve vicitrarathavāhanāḥ
d vicitrasragdharāḥ sarve vicitrāmbarabhūṣaṇāḥ
a svadeśaveṣābharaṇā vīrāḥ śatasahasraśaḥ
c tasya senāpraṇetāro babhūvuḥ kṣatriyarṣabhāḥ
a vyathayann iva bhūtāni kampayann iva medinīm
c śanair viśrāmayan senāṃ sa yayau yena pāṇḍavaḥ
a tato duryodhanaḥ śrutvā mahāsenaṃ mahāratham
c upāyāntam abhidrutya svayam ānarca bhārata
d śalyasya mantribhiḥ sarvair duryodhanavaśānugaiḥ
d avijñātaṃ ca śalyasya hṛdayasya priyaṃ kṛtam
a kārayām āsa pūjārthaṃ tasya duryodhanaḥ sabhāḥ
c ramaṇīyeṣu deśeṣu ratnacitrāḥ svalaṃkṛtāḥ
d śilpibhir vividhaiś caiva krīḍās tatra prayojitāḥ
d tatra mālyāni māṃsāni bhakṣyaṃ peyaṃ ca satkṛtam
d kūpāś ca vividhākārā manoharṣavivardhanāḥ
d vāpyaś ca vividhākārā audakāni gṛhāṇi ca
a sa tāḥ sabhāḥ samāsādya pūjyamāno yathāmaraḥ
c duryodhanasya sacivair deśe deśe yathārhataḥ
e ājagāma sabhām anyāṃ devāvasathavarcasam
f tatra vāsāṃsi mālyāni bhakṣyaṃ peyaṃ ca puṣkalam
f gandhā ghrāṇasya sukhadā divyāś cittamanoharāḥ
f sarāṃsi sādaro rājā savihaṃgamṛgāni ca
a sa tatra viṣayair yuktaḥ kalyāṇair atimānuṣaiḥ
c mene 'bhyadhikam ātmānam avamene puraṃdaram
a papraccha sa tataḥ preṣyān prahṛṣṭaḥ kṣatriyarṣabhaḥ
c yudhiṣṭhirasya puruṣāḥ ke nu cakruḥ sabhā imāḥ
e ānīyantāṃ sabhākārāḥ pradeyārhā hi me matāḥ
f prasādam eṣāṃ dāsyāmi kuntīputro 'numanyatām
f duryodhanāya tat sarvaṃ kathayanti sma vismitāḥ
f saṃprahṛṣṭo yadā śalyo diditsur api jīvitam
f tataḥ prahṛṣṭaṃ rājānaṃ jñātvā te sacivās tadā
a gūḍho duryodhanas tatra darśayām āsa mātulam
c taṃ dṛṣṭvā madrarājas tu jñātvā yatnaṃ ca tasya tam
d dṛṣṭvā duryodhanaṃ rājā vismitaḥ sa narottamaḥ
d mantriṇaś cāpi śaṃsanti madrarājaṃ suvismitam
d duryodhanena te rājañ śuśrūṣitam idaṃ prabho
d priyaṃ priyārhasya sataḥ kartum arhasi bhūmipa
d tam aṅkam upaveśyāśu mūrdhni cāghrāya madrarāṭ
e pariṣvajyābravīt prīta iṣṭo 'rtho gṛhyatām iti
 duryodhana uvāca
a satyavāg bhava kalyāṇa varo vai mama dīyatām
c sarvasenāpraṇetā me bhavān bhavitum arhati
d yathaiva pāṇḍavās tubhyaṃ tathaiva bhavato hy aham
d śalyaḥ
d anumānyaṃ ca pālyaṃ ca bhaktaṃ ca bhaja māṃ vibho
d evam etan mahārāja yathā vadasi bhārata
d varaṃ dadāmi te prīta evam etad bhaviṣyati
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a kṛtam ity abravīc chalyaḥ kim anyat kriyatām iti
c kṛtam ity eva gāndhāriḥ pratyuvāca punaḥ punaḥ
d śalya uvāca
d gaccha duryodhana puraṃ svakam eva nararṣabha
d ahaṃ gamiṣye draṣṭuṃ vai yudhiṣṭhiram ariṃdamam
d dṛṣṭvā yudhiṣṭhiraṃ rājan kṣipram eṣye narādhipa
d duryodhana uvāca
d avaśyaṃ cāpi draṣṭavyaḥ pāṇḍavaḥ puruṣarṣabhaḥ
d kṣipram āgamyatāṃ rājan pāṇḍavaṃ vīkṣya pārthiva
d śalya uvāca
d tvayy adhīnāḥ sma rājendra varadānaṃ smarasva naḥ
d kṣipram eṣyāmi bhadraṃ te gacchasva svapuraṃ nṛpa
d pariṣvajya tathānyonyaṃ śalyaduryodhanāv ubhau
d dṛṣṭvā tu pāṇḍavān rājan na mithyā kartum utsahe
a sa tathā śalyam āmantrya punar āyāt svakaṃ puram
c śalyo jagāma kaunteyān ākhyātuṃ karma tasya tat
a upaplavyaṃ sa gatvā tu skandhāvāraṃ praviśya ca
c pāṇḍavān atha tān sarvāñ śalyas tatra dadarśa ha
d cirāt tu dṛṣṭvā rājānaṃ mātulaṃ samitiṃjayam
d āsanebhyaḥ samutpetuḥ sarve sahayudhiṣṭhirāḥ
a sametya tu mahābāhuḥ śalyaḥ pāṇḍusutais tadā
c pādyam arghyaṃ ca gāṃ caiva pratyagṛhṇād yathāvidhi
d kṛtāñjalir adīnātmā dharmātmā śalyam abravīt
d svāgataṃ te 'stu vai rājann etad āsanam āsyatām
d tato nyaṣīdac chalyaś ca kāñcane paramāsane
d tatra pādyam athārghyaṃ ca nyavedayata pāṇḍavaḥ
d nivedya cārghyaṃ vidhivan madrarājāya bhārata
d kuśalaṃ pāṇḍavo 'pṛcchac chalyaṃ sarvasukhāvaham
d sa taiḥ parivṛtaḥ sarvaiḥ pāṇḍavair dharmacāribhiḥ
a tataḥ kuśalapūrvaṃ sa madrarājo 'risūdanaḥ
c prītyā paramayā yuktaḥ samāśliṣya yudhiṣṭhiram
a tathā bhīmārjunau hṛṣṭau svasrīyau ca yamāv ubhau
b draupadī ca subhadrā ca abhimanyuś ca bhārata
c āsane copaviṣṭas tu śalyaḥ pārtham uvāca ha
a kuśalaṃ rājaśārdūla kaccit te kurunandana
c araṇyavāsād diṣṭyāsi vimukto jayatāṃ vara
a suduṣkaraṃ kṛtaṃ rājan nirjane vasatā vane
c bhrātṛbhiḥ saha rājendra kṛṣṇayā cānayā saha
a ajñātavāsaṃ ghoraṃ ca vasatā duṣkaraṃ kṛtam
c duḥkham eva kutaḥ saukhyaṃ rājyabhraṣṭasya bhārata
a duḥkhasyaitasya mahato dhārtarāṣṭrakṛtasya vai
c avāpsyasi sukhaṃ rājan hatvā śatrūn paraṃtapa
a viditaṃ te mahārāja lokatattvaṃ narādhipa
c tasmāl lobhakṛtaṃ kiṃ cit tava tāta na vidyate
d rājarṣīṇāṃ purāṇānāṃ mārgam anviccha bhārata
d dāne tapasi satye ca bhava tāta yudhiṣṭhira
d kṣamā damaś ca satyaṃ ca ahiṃsā ca yudhiṣṭhira
d adbhutaś ca punar lokas tvayi rājan pratiṣṭhitaḥ
d mṛdur vadānyo brahmaṇyo dātā dharmaparāyaṇaḥ
d dharmās te viditā rājan bahavo lokasākṣikāḥ
d sarvaṃ jagad idaṃ tāta viditaṃ te paraṃtapa
d diṣṭyā kṛcchram idaṃ rājan pāritaṃ bharatarṣabha
d diṣṭyā paśyāmi rājendra dharmātmānaṃ sahānugam
d nistīrṇaṃ duṣkaraṃ rājaṃs tvāṃ dharmanicayaṃ prabho
d utthānaṃ saṃyamo dākṣyam apramādo dhṛtiḥ smṛtiḥ
a tato 'syākathayad rājā duryodhanasamāgamam
c tac ca śuśrūṣitaṃ sarvaṃ varadānaṃ ca bhārata
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a sukṛtaṃ te kṛtaṃ rājan prahṛṣṭenāntarātmanā
c duryodhanasya yad vīra tvayā vācā pratiśrutam
d duryodhanasya cāsmākaṃ viśeṣo 'tra na vidyate
e ekaṃ tv icchāmi bhadraṃ te kriyamāṇaṃ mahīpate
f rājann akartavyam api kartum arhasi sattama
f mama tv avekṣayā vīra śṛṇu vijñāpayāmi te
f spardhate hi sadā karṇaḥ pārthena raṇamūrdhani
a bhavān iha mahārāja vāsudevasamo yudhi
c karṇārjunābhyāṃ saṃprāpte dvairathe rājasattama
d vāsudevena sārathyaṃ kāryaṃ pārthasya mātula
e karṇasya bhavatā kāryaṃ sārathyaṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ
a tatra pālyo 'rjuno rājan yadi matpriyam icchasi
c tejovadhaś ca te kāryaḥ sauter asmajjayāvahaḥ
e akartavyam api hy etat kartum arhasi mātula
 śalya uvāca
a śṛṇu pāṇḍava bhadraṃ te yad bravīṣi durātmanaḥ
c tejovadhanimittaṃ māṃ sūtaputrasya saṃyuge
d tejovadhanimittaṃ māṃ tat kariṣyāmi te priyam
a ahaṃ tasya bhaviṣyāmi saṃgrāme sārathir dhruvam
c vāsudevena hi samaṃ nityaṃ māṃ sa hi manyate
a tasyāhaṃ kuruśārdūla pratīpam ahitaṃ vacaḥ
c dhruvaṃ saṃkathayiṣyāmi yoddhukāmasya saṃyuge
d ahaṃ tasya bhaviṣyāmi sārathī raṇamūrdhani
a yathā sa hṛtadarpaś ca hṛtatejāś ca pāṇḍava
c bhaviṣyati sukhaṃ hantuṃ satyam etad bravīmi te
a evam etat kariṣyāmi yathā tāta tvam āttha mām
c yac cānyad api śakṣyāmi tat kariṣyāmi te priyam
a yac ca duḥkhaṃ tvayā prāptaṃ dyūte vai kṛṣṇayā saha
c paruṣāṇi ca vākyāni sūtaputrakṛtāni vai
a jaṭāsurāt parikleśaḥ kīcakāc ca mahādyute
c draupadyādhigataṃ sarvaṃ damayantyā yathāśubham
a sarvaṃ duḥkham idaṃ vīra sukhodarkaṃ bhaviṣyati
c nātra manyus tvayā kāryo vidhir hi balavattaraḥ
a duḥkhāni hi mahātmānaḥ prāpnuvanti yudhiṣṭhira
c devair api hi duḥkhāni prāptāni jagatīpate
d devadānavagandharvāḥ kiṃnaroragarākṣasāḥ
d duḥkhaṃ prāptā yathā rājaṃs tac chṛṇuṣva narādhipa
a indreṇa śrūyate rājan sabhāryeṇa mahātmanā
c anubhūtaṃ mahad duḥkhaṃ devarājena bhārata
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a katham indreṇa rājendra sabhāryeṇa mahātmanā
c duḥkhaṃ prāptaṃ paraṃ ghoram etad icchāmi veditum
 śalya uvāca
a śṛṇu rājan purā vṛttam itihāsaṃ purātanam
c sabhāryeṇa yathā prāptaṃ duḥkham indreṇa bhārata
a tvaṣṭā prajāpatir hy āsīd devaśreṣṭho mahātapāḥ
c sa putraṃ vai triśirasam indradrohāt kilāsṛjat
a aindraṃ sa prārthayat sthānaṃ viśvarūpo mahādyutiḥ
c tais tribhir vadanair ghoraiḥ sūryendujvalanopamaiḥ
a vedān ekena so 'dhīte surām ekena cāpibat
c ekena ca diśaḥ sarvāḥ pibann iva nirīkṣate
a sa tapasvī mṛdur dānto dharme tapasi codyataḥ
c tapo 'tapyan mahat tīvraṃ suduścaram ariṃdama
a tasya dṛṣṭvā tapovīryaṃ sattvaṃ cāmitatejasaḥ
c viṣādam agamac chakra indro 'yaṃ mā bhaved iti
a kathaṃ sajjeta bhogeṣu na ca tapyen mahat tapaḥ
c vivardhamānas triśirāḥ sarvaṃ tribhuvanaṃ graset
a iti saṃcintya bahudhā buddhimān bharatarṣabha
c ājñāpayat so 'psarasas tvaṣṭṛputrapralobhane
a yathā sa sajjet triśirāḥ kāmabhogeṣu vai bhṛśam
c kṣipraṃ kuruta gacchadhvaṃ pralobhayata māciram
a śṛṅgāraveṣāḥ suśroṇyo bhāvair yuktā manoharaiḥ
b hāvabhāvasamāyuktāḥ sarvāḥ saundaryaśobhitāḥ
c pralobhayata bhadraṃ vaḥ śamayadhvaṃ bhayaṃ mama
d prajāpatir bhaved eṣa candro vaiśravaṇo yamaḥ
d varuṇaḥ pāśahasto vā dharma eva bhavet svayam
a asvasthaṃ hy ātmanātmānaṃ lakṣayāmi varāṅganāḥ
c bhayam etan mahāghoraṃ kṣipraṃ nāśayatābalāḥ
 apsarasa ūcuḥ
a tathā yatnaṃ kariṣyāmaḥ śakra tasya pralobhane
c yathā nāvāpsyasi bhayaṃ tasmād balaniṣūdana
a nirdahann iva cakṣurbhyāṃ yo 'sāv āste taponidhiḥ
c taṃ pralobhayituṃ deva gacchāmaḥ sahitā vayam
e yatiṣyāmo vaśe kartuṃ vyapanetuṃ ca te bhayam
 śalya uvāca
a indreṇa tās tv anujñātā jagmus triśiraso 'ntikam
c tatra tā vividhair bhāvair lobhayantyo varāṅganāḥ
e nṛtyaṃ saṃdarśayantyaś ca tathaivāṅgeṣu sauṣṭhavam
a viceruḥ saṃpraharṣaṃ ca nābhyagacchan mahātapāḥ
c indriyāṇi vaśe kṛtvā pūrṇasāgarasaṃnibhaḥ
a tās tu yatnaṃ paraṃ kṛtvā punaḥ śakram upasthitāḥ
c kṛtāñjalipuṭāḥ sarvā devarājam athābruvan
a na sa śakyaḥ sudurdharṣo dhairyāc cālayituṃ prabho
c yat te kāryaṃ mahābhāga kriyatāṃ tadanantaram
a saṃpūjyāpsarasaḥ śakro visṛjya ca mahāmatiḥ
c cintayām āsa tasyaiva vadhopāyaṃ mahātmanaḥ
a sa tūṣṇīṃ cintayan vīro devarājaḥ pratāpavān
c viniścitamatir dhīmān vadhe triśiraso 'bhavat
a vajram asya kṣipāmy adya sa kṣipraṃ na bhaviṣyati
c śatruḥ pravṛddho nopekṣyo durbalo 'pi balīyasā
a śāstrabuddhyā viniścitya kṛtvā buddhiṃ vadhe dṛḍhām
c atha vaiśvānaranibhaṃ ghorarūpaṃ bhayāvaham
e mumoca vajraṃ saṃkruddhaḥ śakras triśirasaṃ prati
a sa papāta hatas tena vajreṇa dṛḍham āhataḥ
c parvatasyeva śikharaṃ praṇunnaṃ medinītale
a taṃ tu vajrahataṃ dṛṣṭvā śayānam acalopamam
c na śarma lebhe devendro dīpitas tasya tejasā
d ghorarūpo mahāraudras tīvras tīvraparākramaḥ
e hato 'pi dīptatejāḥ sa jīvann iva ca dṛśyate
f ghātitasya śirāṃsyājau jīvantīvādbhutāni vai
f tato 'tibhītagātras tu śakra āste vicārayan
f athājagāma paraśuṃ skandhenādāya vardhakiḥ
f tad araṇyaṃ mahārāja yatrāste 'sau nipātitaḥ
f śirāṃsi tasya jāyante trīṇy eva śakunās trayaḥ
f tittiriḥ kalaviṅkaś ca tathaiva ca kapiñjalaḥ
f viśvarūpaśirāṃsy eva jāyante tasya bhārata
a abhitas tatra takṣāṇaṃ ghaṭamānaṃ śacīpatiḥ
c apaśyad abravīc cainaṃ satvaraṃ pākaśāsanaḥ
e kṣipraṃ chindhi śirāṃsy asya kuruṣva vacanaṃ mama
 takṣovāca
a mahāskandho bhṛśaṃ hy eṣa paraśur na tariṣyati
c kartuṃ cāhaṃ na śakṣyāmi karma sadbhir vigarhitam
 indra uvāca
a mā bhais tvaṃ kṣipram etad vai kuruṣva vacanaṃ mama
c matprasādād dhi te śastraṃ vajrakalpaṃ bhaviṣyati
 takṣovāca
a kaṃ bhavantam ahaṃ vidyāṃ ghorakarmāṇam adya vai
c etad icchāmy ahaṃ śrotuṃ tattvena kathayasva me
 indra uvāca
a aham indro devarājas takṣan viditam astu te
c kuruṣvaitad yathoktaṃ me takṣan mā tvaṃ vicāraya
d mayā hi nihataḥ śete triśirās tvaṃ ca viddhi vai
d sa prahvaḥ prāñjalir bhūtvā idaṃ vacanam abravīt
 takṣovāca
a krūreṇa nāpatrapase kathaṃ śakreha karmaṇā
c ṛṣiputram imaṃ hatvā brahmahatyābhayaṃ na te
 indra uvāca
a paścād dharmaṃ cariṣyāmi pāvanārthaṃ suduścaram
c śatrur eṣa mahāvīryo vajreṇa nihato mayā
a adyāpi cāham udvignas takṣann asmād bibhemi vai
c kṣipraṃ chindhi śirāṃsi tvaṃ kariṣye 'nugrahaṃ tava
a śiraḥ paśos te dāsyanti bhāgaṃ yajñeṣu mānavāḥ
c eṣa te 'nugrahas takṣan kṣipraṃ kuru mama priyam
 śalya uvāca
a etac chrutvā tu takṣā sa mahendravacanaṃ tadā
c śirāṃsy atha triśirasaḥ kuṭhāreṇācchinat tadā
a nikṛtteṣu tatas teṣu niṣkrāmaṃs triśirās tv atha
c kapiñjalās tittirāś ca kalaviṅkāś ca sarvaśaḥ
a yena vedān adhīte sma pibate somam eva ca
c tasmād vaktrān viniṣpetuḥ kṣipraṃ tasya kapiñjalāḥ
a yena sarvā diśo rājan pibann iva nirīkṣate
c tasmād vaktrād viniṣpetus tittirās tasya pāṇḍava
a yat surāpaṃ tu tasyāsīd vaktraṃ triśirasas tadā
c kalaviṅkā viniṣpetus tenāsya bharatarṣabha
a tatas teṣu nikṛtteṣu vijvaro maghavān abhūt
b takṣṇe caiva varaṃ dattvā prahṛṣṭas tridaśeśvaraḥ
c jagāma tridivaṃ hṛṣṭas takṣāpi svagṛhān yayau
d takṣāpi svagṛhaṃ gatvā naiva śaṃsati kasya cit
d athainaṃ nābhijānanti varṣam ekaṃ tathāgatam
d atha saṃvatsare pūrṇe bhūtāḥ paśupateḥ prabho
d te cākrośanta maghavān naḥ prabhur brahmahā iti
d tata indro vrataṃ ghoram acarat pākaśāsanaḥ
d tapasā ca susaṃyuktaḥ saha devair marudgaṇaiḥ
d samudre ca pṛthivyāṃ ca vanaspatiṣu strīṣu ca
d vibhajya brahmahatyāṃ ca tāṃś ca saṃyojayad varaiḥ
d varadas tu varaṃ dattvā pṛthivyai sāgarāya ca
d vanaspatibhyaḥ strībhyaś ca brahmahatyāṃ nunoda tām
d tatas tu śuddho bhagavān devair lokaiś ca pūjitaḥ
d indrasthānam upātiṣṭhat pūjyamāno maharṣibhiḥ
d mene kṛtārtham ātmānaṃ hatvā śatruṃ surārihā
a tvaṣṭā prajāpatiḥ śrutvā śakreṇātha hataṃ sutam
c krodhasaṃraktanayana idaṃ vacanam abravīt
a tapyamānaṃ tapo nityaṃ kṣāntaṃ dāntaṃ jitendriyam
c anāparādhinaṃ yasmāt putraṃ hiṃsitavān mama
a tasmāc chakravadhārthāya vṛtram utpādayāmy aham
c lokāḥ paśyantu me vīryaṃ tapasaś ca balaṃ mahat
e sa ca paśyatu devendro durātmā pāpacetanaḥ
a upaspṛśya tataḥ kruddhas tapasvī sumahāyaśāḥ
c agniṃ hutvā samutpādya ghoraṃ vṛtram uvāca ha
e indraśatro vivardhasva prabhāvāt tapaso mama
a so 'vardhata divaṃ stabdhvā sūryavaiśvānaropamaḥ
c kiṃ karomīti covāca kālasūrya ivoditaḥ
e śakraṃ jahīti cāpy ukto jagāma tridivaṃ tataḥ
a tato yuddhaṃ samabhavad vṛtravāsavayos tadā
c saṃkruddhayor mahāghoraṃ prasaktaṃ kurusattama
d grastā lokāś ca vṛtreṇa sarve bharatasattama
d tvaṣṭṛtejovivṛddhena vṛtreṇa sumahātmanā
d sarve gandhendriyarasā hṛtā bhārata tena vai
d pṛthivī vāyur ākāśa āpo jyotiś ca pañcamaḥ
d hṛtam etan mahārāja vṛtreṇa sumahātmanā
a tato jagrāha devendraṃ vṛtro vīraḥ śatakratum
c apāvṛtya sa jagrāsa vṛtraḥ krodhasamanvitaḥ
a graste vṛtreṇa śakre tu saṃbhrāntās tridaśās tadā
c asṛjaṃs te mahāsattvā jṛmbhikāṃ vṛtranāśinīm
a vijṛmbhamāṇasya tato vṛtrasyāsyād apāvṛtāt
c svāny aṅgāny abhisaṃkṣipya niṣkrānto balasūdanaḥ
e tataḥ prabhṛti lokeṣu jṛmbhikā prāṇisaṃśritā
a jahṛṣuś ca surāḥ sarve dṛṣṭvā śakraṃ viniḥsṛtam
c tataḥ pravavṛte yuddhaṃ vṛtravāsavayoḥ punaḥ
e saṃrabdhayos tadā ghoraṃ suciraṃ bharatarṣabha
a yadā vyavardhata raṇe vṛtro balasamanvitaḥ
c tvaṣṭus tapobalād vidvāṃs tadā śakro nyavartata
a nivṛtte tu tadā devā viṣādam agaman param
c sametya śakreṇa ca te tvaṣṭus tejovimohitāḥ
e amantrayanta te sarve munibhiḥ saha bhārata
a kiṃ kāryam iti te rājan vicintya bhayamohitāḥ
c jagmuḥ sarve mahātmānaṃ manobhir viṣṇum avyayam
e upaviṣṭā mandarāgre sarve vṛtravadhepsavaḥ
 indra uvāca
 śalyaḥ
 ākhyānam uttamam idam itihāsaṃ purātanam
 śṛṇu me bhrātṛbhiḥ sārdhaṃ draupadyā ca jayāvaham
 evaṃ vicintya vibudhaiḥ śakras tribhuvaneśvaraḥ
 vṛtrasya maraṇopāyaṃ punar vacanam abravīt
 sarvaṃ vyāptaṃ jagat tena vṛtreṇetīha naḥ śrutam
 vṛtrabhūteṣu lokeṣu bhayam indram upāgamat
 athendro hi mahātejāḥ sametya saha devataiḥ
 amantrayata tejasvī vṛtrasya vadhakāraṇāt
a sarvaṃ vyāptam idaṃ devā vṛtreṇa jagad avyayam
c na hy asya sadṛśaṃ kiṃ cit pratighātāya yad bhavet
a samartho hy abhavaṃ pūrvam asamartho 'smi sāṃpratam
c kathaṃ kuryāṃ nu bhadraṃ vo duṣpradharṣaḥ sa me mataḥ
a tejasvī ca mahātmā ca yuddhe cāmitavikramaḥ
c graset tribhuvanaṃ sarvaṃ sadevāsuramānuṣam
a tasmād viniścayam imaṃ śṛṇudhvaṃ me divaukasaḥ
c viṣṇoḥ kṣayam upāgamya sametya ca mahātmanā
e tena saṃmantrya vetsyāmo vadhopāyaṃ durātmanaḥ
 śalya uvāca
a evam ukte maghavatā devāḥ sarṣigaṇās tadā
b praṇipatya mahātmānaṃ sarvabhūtanamaskṛtam
c śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ devaṃ jagmur viṣṇuṃ mahābalam
a ūcuś ca sarve deveśaṃ viṣṇuṃ vṛtrabhayārditāḥ
c tvayā lokās trayaḥ krāntās tribhir vikramaṇaiḥ prabho
a amṛtaṃ cāhṛtaṃ viṣṇo daityāś ca nihatā raṇe
c baliṃ baddhvā mahādaityaṃ śakro devādhipaḥ kṛtaḥ
a tvaṃ prabhuḥ sarvalokānāṃ tvayā sarvam idaṃ tatam
c tvaṃ hi deva mahādevaḥ sarvalokanamaskṛtaḥ
d gandharvoragarakṣāṇāṃ sarveṣām amarottama
a gatir bhava tvaṃ devānāṃ sendrāṇām amarottama
c jagad vyāptam idaṃ sarvaṃ vṛtreṇāsurasūdana
 viṣṇur uvāca
a avaśyaṃ karaṇīyaṃ me bhavatāṃ hitam uttamam
c tasmād upāyaṃ vakṣyāmi yathāsau na bhaviṣyati
a gacchadhvaṃ sarṣigandharvā yatrāsau viśvarūpadhṛk
c sāma tasya prayuñjadhvaṃ tata enaṃ vijeṣyatha
a bhaviṣyati gatir devāḥ śakrasya mama tejasā
c adṛśyaś ca pravekṣyāmi vajram asyāyudhottamam
a gacchadhvam ṛṣibhiḥ sārdhaṃ gandharvaiś ca surottamāḥ
c vṛtrasya saha śakreṇa saṃdhiṃ kuruta māciram
 śalya uvāca
a evam uktās tu devena ṛṣayas tridaśās tathā
c yayuḥ sametya sahitāḥ śakraṃ kṛtvā puraḥsaram
c   cakruś caiva vibhor vacaḥ
c tataḥ sametya vṛtreṇa
a samīpam etya ca tadā sarva eva mahaujasaḥ
c taṃ tejasā prajvalitaṃ pratapantaṃ diśo daśa
a grasantam iva lokāṃs trīn sūryācandramasau yathā
c dadṛśus tatra te vṛtraṃ śakreṇa saha devatāḥ
a ṛṣayo 'tha tato 'bhyetya vṛtram ūcuḥ priyaṃ vacaḥ
c vyāptaṃ jagad idaṃ sarvaṃ tejasā tava durjaya
a na ca śaknoṣi nirjetuṃ vāsavaṃ bhūrivikramam
c yudhyatoś cāpi vāṃ kālo vyatītaḥ sumahān iha
a pīḍyante ca prajāḥ sarvāḥ sadevāsuramānavāḥ
c sakhyaṃ bhavatu te vṛtra śakreṇa saha nityadā
e avāpsyasi sukhaṃ tvaṃ ca śakralokāṃś ca śāśvatān
a ṛṣivākyaṃ niśamyātha sa vṛtraḥ sumahābalaḥ
c uvāca tāṃs tadā sarvān praṇamya śirasāsuraḥ
a sarve yūyaṃ mahābhāgā gandharvāś caiva sarvaśaḥ
c yad brūta tac chrutaṃ sarvaṃ mamāpi śṛṇutānaghāḥ
a saṃdhiḥ kathaṃ vai bhavitā mama śakrasya cobhayoḥ
c tejasor hi dvayor devāḥ sakhyaṃ vai bhavitā katham
d etad veditum icchāmi bruvantu ṛṣisattamāḥ
 ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
a sakṛt satāṃ saṃgataṃ lipsitavyaṃ
tataḥ paraṃ bhavitā bhavyam eva
c nātikramet satpuruṣeṇa saṃgataṃ
tasmāt satāṃ saṃgataṃ lipsitavyam
a dṛḍhaṃ satāṃ saṃgataṃ cāpi nityaṃ
brūyāc cārthaṃ hy arthakṛcchreṣu dhīraḥ
c mahārthavat satpuruṣeṇa saṃgataṃ
tasmāt santaṃ na jighāṃseta dhīraḥ
a indraḥ satāṃ saṃmataś ca nivāsaś ca mahātmanām
c satyavādī hy adīnaś ca dharmavit suviniścitaḥ
a tena te saha śakreṇa saṃdhir bhavatu śāśvataḥ
c evaṃ viśvāsam āgaccha mā te bhūd buddhir anyathā
 śalya uvāca
a maharṣivacanaṃ śrutvā tān uvāca mahādyutiḥ
c avaśyaṃ bhagavanto me mānanīyās tapasvinaḥ
a bravīmi yad ahaṃ devās tat sarvaṃ kriyatām iha
c tataḥ sarvaṃ kariṣyāmi yad ūcur māṃ dvijarṣabhāḥ
a na śuṣkeṇa na cārdreṇa nāśmanā na ca dāruṇā
c na śastreṇa na vajreṇa na divā na tathā niśi
a vadhyo bhaveyaṃ viprendrāḥ śakrasya saha daivataiḥ
c evaṃ me rocate saṃdhiḥ śakreṇa saha nityadā
a bāḍham ity eva ṛṣayas tam ūcur bharatarṣabha
c evaṃ kṛte tu saṃdhāne vṛtraḥ pramudito 'bhavat
d tataḥ saṃdhiṃ mithaḥ kṛtvā ṛṣayo dīptatejasaḥ
d śakrasya saha vṛtreṇa punar jagmur yathāgatam
d atha dīrghasya kālasya śakraḥ saṃcintya bhārata
a yattaḥ sadābhavac cāpi śakro 'marṣasamanvitaḥ
c vṛtrasya vadhasaṃyuktān upāyān anucintayan
e randhrānveṣī samudvignaḥ sadābhūd balavṛtrahā
f abhisaṃdhir mahendrasya saṃdhikarmaṇi yaḥ kṛtaḥ

 śalya uvāca
a ṛṣayo 'thābruvan sarve devāś ca tridaśeśvarāḥ

a nahuṣas tāṃ tato dṛṣṭvā vismito vākyam abravīt
c svāgataṃ te varārohe kiṃ karomi śucismite
a bhaktaṃ māṃ bhaja kalyāṇi kim icchasi manasvini
c tava kalyāṇi yat kāryaṃ tat kariṣye sumadhyame
a na ca vrīḍā tvayā kāryā suśroṇi mayi viśvasa
c satyena vai śape devi kartāsmi vacanaṃ tava
 indrāṇy uvāca
a yo me tvayā kṛtaḥ kālas tam ākāṅkṣe jagatpate
c tatas tvam eva bhartā me bhaviṣyasi surādhipa
a kāryaṃ ca hṛdi me yat tad devarājāvadhāraya
c vakṣyāmi yadi me rājan priyam etat kariṣyasi
e vākyaṃ praṇayasaṃyuktaṃ tataḥ syāṃ vaśagā tava
a indrasya vājino vāhā hastino 'tha rathās tathā
c icchāmy aham ihāpūrvaṃ vāhanaṃ te surādhipa
e yan na viṣṇor na rudrasya nāsurāṇāṃ na rakṣasām
a vahantu tvāṃ mahārāja ṛṣayaḥ saṃgatā vibho
c sarve śibikayā rājann etad dhi mama rocate
a nāsureṣu na deveṣu tulyo bhavitum arhasi
c sarveṣāṃ teja ādatsva svena vīryeṇa darśanāt
e na te pramukhataḥ sthātuṃ kaś cid icchati vīryavān
 śalya uvāca
a evam uktas tu nahuṣaḥ prāhṛṣyata tadā kila
c uvāca vacanaṃ cāpi surendras tām aninditām
a apūrvaṃ vāhanam idaṃ tvayoktaṃ varavarṇini
c dṛḍhaṃ me rucitaṃ devi tvadvaśo 'smi varānane
a na hy alpavīryo bhavati yo vāhān kurute munīn
c ahaṃ tapasvī balavān bhūtabhavyabhavatprabhuḥ
a mayi kruddhe jagan na syān mayi sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam
c devadānavagandharvāḥ kiṃnaroragarākṣasāḥ
a na me kruddhasya paryāptāḥ sarve lokāḥ śucismite
c cakṣuṣā yaṃ prapaśyāmi tasya tejo harāmy aham
d aham indro 'smi devānāṃ lokānāṃ ca maheśvaraḥ
d mayi havyaṃ ca kavyaṃ ca lokāś caiva sanātanāḥ
a tasmāt te vacanaṃ devi kariṣyāmi na saṃśayaḥ
c saptarṣayo māṃ vakṣyanti sarve brahmarṣayas tathā
e paśya māhātmyam asmākam ṛddhiṃ ca varavarṇini
f hataujaso mayā sarve devagandharvadānavāḥ
f yad yasya tejaḥ paśyāmi tasya tejo harāmy aham
a evam uktvā tu tāṃ devīṃ visṛjya ca varānanām
b atha saṃcintya nahuṣo balavīryeṇa bhārata
b visṛjya supratīkaṃ ca nāgam airāvataṃ tathā
b haṃsayuktaṃ vimānaṃ ca hariyuktaṃ tathā ratham
b sa tu darpeṇa mahatā paribhūya mahāmunīn
c vimāne yojayitvā sa ṛṣīn niyamam āsthitān
a abrahmaṇyo balopeto matto varamadena ca
c kāmavṛttaḥ sa duṣṭātmā vāhayām āsa tān ṛṣīn
a nahuṣeṇa visṛṣṭā ca bṛhaspatim uvāca sā
c samayo 'lpāvaśeṣo me nahuṣeṇeha yaḥ kṛtaḥ
e śakraṃ mṛgaya śīghraṃ tvaṃ bhaktāyāḥ kuru me dayām
a bāḍham ity eva bhagavān bṛhaspatir uvāca tām
c na bhetavyaṃ tvayā devi nahuṣād duṣṭacetasaḥ
a na hy eṣa sthāsyati ciraṃ gata eṣa narādhamaḥ
c adharmajño maharṣīṇāṃ vāhanāc ca hataḥ śubhe
a iṣṭiṃ cāhaṃ kariṣyāmi vināśāyāsya durmateḥ
c śakraṃ cādhigamiṣyāmi mā bhais tvaṃ bhadram astu te
a tataḥ prajvālya vidhivaj juhāva paramaṃ haviḥ
c bṛhaspatir mahātejā devarājopalabdhaye
d hutvāgniṃ so 'bravīd rājañ chakram anviṣyatām iti
a tasmāc ca bhagavān devaḥ svayam eva hutāśanaḥ
c strīveṣam adbhutaṃ kṛtvā sahasāntaradhīyata
a sa diśaḥ pradiśaś caiva parvatāṃś ca vanāni ca
c pṛthivīṃ cāntarikṣaṃ ca vicīyātimanogatiḥ
e nimeṣāntaramātreṇa bṛhaspatim upāgamat
 agnir uvāca
a bṛhaspate na paśyāmi devarājam ahaṃ kva cit
c āpaḥ śeṣāḥ sadā cāpaḥ praveṣṭuṃ notsahāmy aham
e na me tatra gatir brahman kim anyat karavāṇi te
 śalya uvāca
a tam abravīd devagurur apo viśa mahādyute
 agnir uvāca
a nāpaḥ praveṣṭuṃ śakṣyāmi kṣayo me 'tra bhaviṣyati
c śaraṇaṃ tvāṃ prapanno 'smi svasti te 'stu mahādyute
a adbhyo 'gnir brahmataḥ kṣatram aśmano loham utthitam
c teṣāṃ sarvatragaṃ tejaḥ svāsu yoniṣu śāmyati
 bṛhaspatir uvāca
a tvam agne sarvadevānāṃ mukhaṃ tvam asi havyavāṭ
c tvam antaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ gūḍhaś carasi sākṣivat
a tvām āhur ekaṃ kavayas tvām āhus trividhaṃ punaḥ
c tvayā tyaktaṃ jagac cedaṃ sadyo naśyed dhutāśana
a kṛtvā tubhyaṃ namo viprāḥ svakarmavijitāṃ gatim
c gacchanti saha patnībhiḥ sutair api ca śāśvatīm
a tvam evāgne havyavāhas tvam eva paramaṃ haviḥ
c yajanti satrais tvām eva yajñaiś ca paramādhvare
a sṛṣṭvā lokāṃs trīn imān havyavāha
prāpte kāle pacasi punaḥ samiddhaḥ
c sarvasyāsya bhuvanasya prasūtis
tvam evāgne bhavasi punaḥ pratiṣṭhā
a tvām agne jaladān āhur vidyutaś ca tvam eva hi
c dahanti sarvabhūtāni tvatto niṣkramya hāyanāḥ
a tvayy āpo nihitāḥ sarvās tvayi sarvam idaṃ jagat
c na te 'sty aviditaṃ kiṃ cit triṣu lokeṣu pāvaka
a svayoniṃ bhajate sarvo viśasvāpo 'viśaṅkitaḥ
c ahaṃ tvāṃ vardhayiṣyāmi brāhmair mantraiḥ sanātanaiḥ
 śalya uvāca
a evaṃ stuto havyavāho bhagavān kavir uttamaḥ
c bṛhaspatim athovāca prītimān vākyam uttamam
e darśayiṣyāmi te śakraṃ satyam etad bravīmi te
a praviśyāpas tato vahniḥ sasamudrāḥ sapalvalāḥ
c ājagāma saras tac ca gūḍho yatra śatakratuḥ
a atha tatrāpi padmāni vicinvan bharatarṣabha
c anvapaśyat sa devendraṃ bisamadhyagataṃ sthitam
a āgatya ca tatas tūrṇaṃ tam ācaṣṭa bṛhaspateḥ
c aṇumātreṇa vapuṣā padmatantvāśritaṃ prabhum
a gatvā devarṣigandharvaiḥ sahito 'tha bṛhaspatiḥ
c purāṇaiḥ karmabhir devaṃ tuṣṭāva balasūdanam
a mahāsuro hataḥ śakra namucir dāruṇas tvayā
c śambaraś ca balaś caiva tathobhau ghoravikramau
a śatakrato vivardhasva sarvāñ śatrūn niṣūdaya
c uttiṣṭha vajrin saṃpaśya devarṣīṃś ca samāgatān
a mahendra dānavān hatvā lokās trātās tvayā vibho
c apāṃ phenaṃ samāsādya viṣṇutejopabṛṃhitam
e tvayā vṛtro hataḥ pūrvaṃ devarāja jagatpate
a tvaṃ sarvabhūteṣu vareṇya īḍyas
tvayā samaṃ vidyate neha bhūtam
c tvayā dhāryante sarvabhūtāni śakra
tvaṃ devānāṃ mahimānaṃ cakartha
a pāhi devān salokāṃś ca mahendra balam āpnuhi
c evaṃ saṃstūyamānaś ca so 'vardhata śanaiḥ śanaiḥ
a svaṃ caiva vapur āsthāya babhūva sa balānvitaḥ
c abravīc ca guruṃ devo bṛhaspatim upasthitam
a kiṃ kāryam avaśiṣṭaṃ vo hatas tvāṣṭro mahāsuraḥ
c vṛtraś ca sumahākāyo grastuṃ lokān iyeṣa yaḥ
 bṛhaspatir uvāca
a mānuṣo nahuṣo rājā devarṣigaṇatejasā
c devarājyam anuprāptaḥ sarvān no bādhate bhṛśam
 indra uvāca
a kathaṃ nu nahuṣo rājyaṃ devānāṃ prāpa durlabham
c tapasā kena vā yuktaḥ kiṃvīryo vā bṛhaspate
d tat sarvaṃ kathayadhvaṃ me yathendratvam upeyivān
 bṛhaspatir uvāca
 tvayi praṇaṣṭe deveśa viśvaṃ pravyathitaṃ jagat
 parasparabhayodvignaṃ babhūvārtam arājakam
 tato devaiḥ sagandharvaiḥ sarṣisaṃghaiḥ sapāvakaiḥ
 mānuṣo nahuṣo rājā devarājye 'bhiṣecitaḥ
a devā bhītāḥ śakram akāmayanta
tvayā tyaktaṃ mahad aindraṃ padaṃ tat
c tadā devāḥ pitaro 'tharṣayaś ca
gandharvasaṃghāś ca sametya sarve
a gatvābruvan nahuṣaṃ śakra tatra
tvaṃ no rājā bhava bhuvanasya goptā
c tān abravīn nahuṣo nāsmi śakta
āpyāyadhvaṃ tapasā tejasā ca
a evam uktair vardhitaś cāpi devai
rājābhavan nahuṣo ghoravīryaḥ
c trailokye ca prāpya rājyaṃ tapasvinaḥ
kṛtvā vāhān yāti lokān durātmā
a tejoharaṃ dṛṣṭiviṣaṃ sughoraṃ
mā tvaṃ paśyer nahuṣaṃ vai kadā cit
c devāś ca sarve nahuṣaṃ bhayārtā
na paśyanto gūḍharūpāś caranti
 śalya uvāca
a evaṃ vadaty aṅgirasāṃ variṣṭhe
bṛhaspatau lokapālaḥ kuberaḥ
c vaivasvataś caiva yamaḥ purāṇo
devaś ca somo varuṇaś cājagāma
a te vai samāgamya mahendram ūcur
diṣṭyā tvāṣṭro nihataś caiva vṛtraḥ
c diṣṭyā ca tvāṃ kuśalinam akṣataṃ ca
paśyāmo vai nihatāriṃ ca śakra
a sa tān yathāvat pratibhāṣya śakraḥ
saṃcodayan nahuṣasyāntareṇa
c rājā devānāṃ nahuṣo ghorarūpas
tatra sāhyaṃ dīyatāṃ me bhavadbhiḥ
d   ca hi lokapālān
d sametya vai prītamanā mahendraḥ
d uvāca cainān
a te cābruvan nahuṣo ghorarūpo
dṛṣṭīviṣas tasya bibhīma deva
c tvaṃ ced rājan nahuṣaṃ parājayes
tad vai vayaṃ bhāgam arhāma śakra
a indro 'bravīd bhavatu bhavān apāṃ patir
yamaḥ kuberaś ca mahābhiṣekam
c saṃprāpnuvantv adya sahaiva tena
ripuṃ jayāmo nahuṣaṃ ghoradṛṣṭim
a tataḥ śakraṃ jvalano 'py āha bhāgaṃ
prayaccha mahyaṃ tava sāhyaṃ kariṣye
c tam āha śakro bhavitāgne tavāpi
aindrāgno vai bhāga eko mahākratau
a evaṃ saṃcintya bhagavān mahendraḥ pākaśāsanaḥ
c kuberaṃ sarvayakṣāṇāṃ dhanānāṃ ca prabhuṃ tathā
a vaivasvataṃ pitṝṇāṃ ca varuṇaṃ cāpy apāṃ tathā
c ādhipatyaṃ dadau śakraḥ satkṛtya varadas tadā
 śalya uvāca
a atha saṃcintayānasya devarājasya dhīmataḥ
c nahuṣasya vadhopāyaṃ lokapālaiḥ sahaiva taiḥ
e tapasvī tatra bhagavān agastyaḥ pratyadṛśyata
a so 'bravīd arcya devendraṃ diṣṭyā vai vardhate bhavān
c viśvarūpavināśena vṛtrāsuravadhena ca
d diṣṭyā hatāriṃ paśyāmo devarājaṃ śatakratum
d diṣṭyā dharmaḥ sthito loke diṣṭyā lokāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ
d diṣṭyā paśyāma devendra diṣṭyā lokān punarnavān
a diṣṭyā ca nahuṣo bhraṣṭo devarājyāt puraṃdara
c diṣṭyā hatāriṃ paśyāmi bhavantaṃ balasūdana
 indra uvāca
a svāgataṃ te maharṣe 'stu prīto 'haṃ darśanāt tava
c pādyam ācamanīyaṃ ca gām arghyaṃ ca pratīccha me
 śalya uvāca
a pūjitaṃ copaviṣṭaṃ tam āsane munisattamam
c paryapṛcchata deveśaḥ prahṛṣṭo brāhmaṇarṣabham
a etad icchāmi bhagavan kathyamānaṃ dvijottama
c paribhraṣṭaḥ kathaṃ svargān nahuṣaḥ pāpaniścayaḥ
 agastya uvāca
a śṛṇu śakra priyaṃ vākyaṃ yathā rājā durātmavān
c svargād bhraṣṭo durācāro nahuṣo baladarpitaḥ
a śramārtās tu vahantas taṃ nahuṣaṃ pāpakāriṇam
c devarṣayo mahābhāgās tathā brahmarṣayo 'malāḥ
e papracchuḥ saṃśayaṃ deva nahuṣaṃ jayatāṃ vara
a ya ime brahmaṇā proktā mantrā vai prokṣaṇe gavām
c ete pramāṇaṃ bhavata utāho neti vāsava
e nahuṣo neti tān āha tamasā mūḍhacetanaḥ
 ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
a adharme saṃpravṛttas tvaṃ dharmaṃ na pratipadyase
c pramāṇam etad asmākaṃ pūrvaṃ proktaṃ maharṣibhiḥ
 agastya uvāca
a tato vivadamānaḥ sa munibhiḥ saha vāsava
c atha mām aspṛśan mūrdhni pādenādharmapīḍitaḥ
a tenābhūd dhatatejāḥ sa niḥśrīkaś ca śacīpate
c tatas tam aham āvignam avocaṃ bhayapīḍitam
a yasmāt pūrvaiḥ kṛtaṃ brahma brahmarṣibhir anuṣṭhitam
c aduṣṭaṃ dūṣayasi vai yac ca mūrdhny aspṛśaḥ padā
a yac cāpi tvam ṛṣīn mūḍha brahmakalpān durāsadān
c vāhān kṛtvā vāhayasi tena svargād dhataprabhaḥ
a dhvaṃsa pāpa paribhraṣṭaḥ kṣīṇapuṇyo mahītalam
c daśa varṣasahasrāṇi sarparūpadharo mahān
e vicariṣyasi pūrṇeṣu punaḥ svargam avāpsyasi
f dṛṣṭvā yudhiṣṭhiraṃ nāma tava vaṃśasamudbhavam
f nihato brahmaśāpena prapadyasva triviṣṭapam
a evaṃ bhraṣṭo durātmā sa devarājyād ariṃdama
b nahuṣas tu sudurbuddhir durātmā pāpacetanaḥ
c diṣṭyā vardhāmahe śakra hato brāhmaṇakaṇṭakaḥ
a triviṣṭapaṃ prapadyasva pāhi lokāñ śacīpate
c jitendriyo jitāmitraḥ stūyamāno maharṣibhiḥ
 śalya uvāca
a tato devā bhṛśaṃ tuṣṭā maharṣigaṇasaṃvṛtāḥ
c pitaraś caiva yakṣāś ca bhujagā rākṣasās tathā
a gandharvā devakanyāś ca sarve cāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ
c sarāṃsi saritaḥ śailāḥ sāgarāś ca viśāṃ pate
a upagamyābruvan sarve diṣṭyā vardhasi śatruhan
c hataś ca nahuṣaḥ pāpo diṣṭyāgastyena dhīmatā
e diṣṭyā pāpasamācāraḥ kṛtaḥ sarpo mahītale
 śalya uvāca
a tataḥ śakraḥ stūyamāno gandharvāpsarasāṃ gaṇaiḥ
c airāvataṃ samāruhya dvipendraṃ lakṣaṇair yutam
a pāvakaś ca mahātejā maharṣiś ca bṛhaspatiḥ
c yamaś ca varuṇaś caiva kuberaś ca dhaneśvaraḥ
a sarvair devaiḥ parivṛtaḥ śakro vṛtraniṣūdanaḥ
c gandharvair apsarobhiś ca yātas tribhuvanaṃ prabhuḥ
a sa sametya mahendrāṇyā devarājaḥ śatakratuḥ
c mudā paramayā yuktaḥ pālayām āsa devarāṭ
a tataḥ sa bhagavāṃs tatra aṅgirāḥ samadṛśyata
c atharvavedamantraiś ca devendraṃ samapūjayat
a tatas tu bhagavān indraḥ prahṛṣṭaḥ samapadyata
c varaṃ ca pradadau tasmai atharvāṅgirase tadā
a atharvāṅgirasaṃ nāma asmin vede bhaviṣyati
c udāharaṇam etad dhi yajñabhāgaṃ ca lapsyase
a evaṃ saṃpūjya bhagavān atharvāṅgirasaṃ tadā
c vyasarjayan mahārāja devarājaḥ śatakratuḥ
a saṃpūjya sarvāṃs tridaśān ṛṣīṃś cāpi tapodhanān
c indraḥ pramudito rājan dharmeṇāpālayat prajāḥ
a evaṃ duḥkham anuprāptam indreṇa saha bhāryayā
c ajñātavāsaś ca kṛtaḥ śatrūṇāṃ vadhakāṅkṣayā
a nātra manyus tvayā kāryo yat kliṣṭo 'si mahāvane
c draupadyā saha rājendra bhrātṛbhiś ca mahātmabhiḥ
a evaṃ tvam api rājendra rājyaṃ prāpsyasi bhārata
c vṛtraṃ hatvā yathā prāptaḥ śakraḥ kauravanandana
a durācāraś ca nahuṣo brahmadviṭ pāpacetanaḥ
c agastyaśāpābhihato vinaṣṭaḥ śāśvatīḥ samāḥ
a evaṃ tava durātmānaḥ śatravaḥ śatrusūdana
c kṣipraṃ nāśaṃ gamiṣyanti karṇaduryodhanādayaḥ
a tataḥ sāgaraparyantāṃ bhokṣyase medinīm imām
c bhrātṛbhiḥ sahito vīra draupadyā ca sahābhibho
a upākhyānam idaṃ śakravijayaṃ vedasaṃmitam
c rājñā vyūḍheṣv anīkeṣu śrotavyaṃ jayam icchatā
a tasmāt saṃśrāvayāmi tvāṃ vijayaṃ jayatāṃ vara
c saṃstūyamānā vardhante mahātmāno yudhiṣṭhira
a kṣatriyāṇām abhāvo 'yaṃ yudhiṣṭhira mahātmanām
c duryodhanāparādhena bhīmārjunabalena ca
d saṃgrāme saṃkṣayo ghoro bhaviṣyaty acirād iva
a ākhyānam indravijayaṃ ya idaṃ niyataḥ paṭhet
c dhūtapāpmā jitasvargaḥ sa pretyeha ca modate
a na cārijaṃ bhayaṃ tasya na cāputro bhaven naraḥ
c nāpadaṃ prāpnuyāt kāṃ cid dīrgham āyuś ca vindati
e sarvatra jayam āpnoti na kadā cit parājayam
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a evam āśvāsito rājā śalyena bharatarṣabha
c pūjayām āsa vidhivac chalyaṃ dharmabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
a śrutvā śalyasya vacanaṃ kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c pratyuvāca mahābāhur madrarājam idaṃ vacaḥ
a bhavān karṇasya sārathyaṃ kariṣyati na saṃśayaḥ
c tatra tejovadhaḥ kāryaḥ karṇasya mama saṃstavaiḥ
 śalya uvāca
a evam etat kariṣyāmi yathā māṃ saṃprabhāṣase
c yac cānyad api śakṣyāmi tat kariṣyāmy ahaṃ tava
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tata āmantrya kaunteyāñ śalyo madrādhipas tadā
c jagāma sabalaḥ śrīmān duryodhanam ariṃdamaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
 tataḥ śalyaḥ sahānīkaḥ kampayann iva medinīm
 jagāma dhārtarāṣṭrasya nagaraṃ nāgasāhvayam
a yuyudhānas tato vīraḥ sātvatānāṃ mahārathaḥ
c mahatā caturaṅgeṇa balenāgād yudhiṣṭhiram
a tasya yodhā mahāvīryā nānādeśasamāgatāḥ
c nānāpraharaṇā vīrāḥ śobhayāṃ cakrire balam
a paraśvadhair bhiṇḍipālaiḥ śaktitomaramudgaraiḥ
c śaktyṛṣṭiparaśuprāsaiḥ karavālaiś ca nirmalaiḥ
a khaḍgakārmukaniryūhaiḥ śaraiś ca vividhair api
c tailadhautaiḥ prakāśadbhis tad aśobhata vai balam
a tasya meghaprakāśasya śastrais taiḥ śobhitasya ca
c babhūva rūpaṃ sainyasya meghasyeva savidyutaḥ
a akṣauhiṇī hi senā sā tadā yaudhiṣṭhiraṃ balam
c praviśyāntardadhe rājan sāgaraṃ kunadī yathā
a tathaivākṣauhiṇīṃ gṛhya cedīnām ṛṣabho balī
c dhṛṣṭaketur upāgacchat pāṇḍavān amitaujasaḥ
a māgadhaś ca jayatseno jārāsaṃdhir mahābalaḥ
c akṣauhiṇyaiva sainyasya dharmarājam upāgamat
a tathaiva pāṇḍyo rājendra sāgarānūpavāsibhiḥ
c vṛto bahuvidhair yodhair yudhiṣṭhiram upāgamat
a tasya sainyam atīvāsīt tasmin balasamāgame
c prekṣaṇīyataraṃ rājan suveṣaṃ balavat tadā
a drupadasyāpy abhūt senā nānādeśasamāgataiḥ
c śobhitā puruṣaiḥ śūraiḥ putraiś cāsya mahārathaiḥ
a tathaiva rājā matsyānāṃ virāṭo vāhinīpatiḥ
c pārvatīyair mahīpālaiḥ sahitaḥ pāṇḍavān iyāt
a itaś cetaś ca pāṇḍūnāṃ samājagmur mahātmanām
c akṣauhiṇyas tu saptaiva vividhadhvajasaṃkulāḥ
e yuyutsamānāḥ kurubhiḥ pāṇḍavān samaharṣayan
a tathaiva dhārtarāṣṭrasya harṣaṃ samabhivardhayan
c bhagadatto mahīpālaḥ senām akṣauhiṇīṃ dadau
a tasya cīnaiḥ kirātaiś ca kāñcanair iva saṃvṛtam
c babhau balam anādhṛṣyaṃ karṇikāravanaṃ yathā
a tathā bhūriśravāḥ śūraḥ śalyaś ca kurunandana
c duryodhanam upāyātāv akṣauhiṇyā pṛthak pṛthak
a kṛtavarmā ca hārdikyo bhojāndhakabalaiḥ saha
c akṣauhiṇyaiva senāyā duryodhanam upāgamat
a tasya taiḥ puruṣavyāghrair vanamālādharair balam
c aśobhata yathā mattair vanaṃ prakrīḍitair gajaiḥ
a jayadrathamukhāś cānye sindhusauvīravāsinaḥ
c ājagmuḥ pṛthivīpālāḥ kampayanta ivācalān
a teṣām akṣauhiṇī senā bahulā vibabhau tadā
c vidhūyamānā vātena bahurūpā ivāmbudāḥ
a sudakṣiṇaś ca kāmbojo yavanaiś ca śakais tathā
b ājagāma mahābāhur yavaneśaś ca pārthivaḥ
c upājagāma kauravyam akṣauhiṇyā viśāṃ pate
a tasya senāsamāvāyaḥ śalabhānām ivābabhau
c sa ca saṃprāpya kauravyaṃ tatraivāntardadhe tadā
a tathā māhiṣmatīvāsī nīlo nīlāyudhaiḥ saha
c mahīpālo mahāvīryair dakṣiṇāpathavāsibhiḥ
a āvantyau ca mahīpālau mahābalasusaṃvṛtau
c pṛthag akṣauhiṇībhyāṃ tāv abhiyātau suyodhanam
a kekayāś ca naravyāghrāḥ sodaryāḥ pañca pārthivāḥ
c saṃharṣayantaḥ kauravyam akṣauhiṇyā samādravan
a itaś cetaś ca sarveṣāṃ bhūmipānāṃ mahātmanām
c tisro 'nyāḥ samavartanta vāhinyo bharatarṣabha
a evam ekādaśāvṛttāḥ senā duryodhanasya tāḥ
c yuyutsamānāḥ kaunteyān nānādhvajasamākulāḥ
a na hāstinapure rājann avakāśo 'bhavat tadā
c rājñāṃ sabalamukhyānāṃ prādhānyenāpi bhārata
a tataḥ pañcanadaṃ caiva kṛtsnaṃ ca kurujāṅgalam
c tathā rohitakāraṇyaṃ marubhūmiś ca kevalā
a ahicchatraṃ kālakūṭaṃ gaṅgākūlaṃ ca bhārata
c vāraṇā vāṭadhānaṃ ca yāmunaś caiva parvataḥ
a eṣa deśaḥ suvistīrṇaḥ prabhūtadhanadhānyavān
c babhūva kauraveyāṇāṃ balena susamākulaḥ
a tatra sainyaṃ tathāyuktaṃ dadarśa sa purohitaḥ
c yaḥ sa pāñcālarājena preṣitaḥ kauravān prati
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a sa tu kauravyam āsādya drupadasya purohitaḥ
c satkṛto dhṛtarāṣṭreṇa bhīṣmeṇa vidureṇa ca
a sarvaṃ kauśalyam uktvādau pṛṣṭvā caivam anāmayam
c sarvasenāpraṇetṝṇāṃ madhye vākyam uvāca ha
a sarvair bhavadbhir vidito rājadharmaḥ sanātanaḥ
c vākyopādānahetos tu vakṣyāmi vidite sati
a dhṛtarāṣṭraś ca pāṇḍuś ca sutāv ekasya viśrutau
c tayoḥ samānaṃ draviṇaṃ paitṛkaṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ
a dhṛtarāṣṭrasya ye putrās te prāptāḥ paitṛkaṃ vasu
c pāṇḍuputrāḥ kathaṃ nāma na prāptāḥ paitṛkaṃ vasu
a evaṃ gate pāṇḍaveyair viditaṃ vaḥ purā yathā
c na prāptaṃ paitṛkaṃ dravyaṃ dhārtarāṣṭreṇa saṃvṛtam
a prāṇāntikair apy upāyaiḥ prayatadbhir anekaśaḥ
c śeṣavanto na śakitā nayituṃ yamasādanam
a punaś ca vardhitaṃ rājyaṃ svabalena mahātmabhiḥ
c chadmanāpahṛtaṃ kṣudrair dhārtarāṣṭraiḥ sasaubalaiḥ
a tad apy anumataṃ karma tathāyuktam anena vai
c vāsitāś ca mahāraṇye varṣāṇīha trayodaśa
a sabhāyāṃ kleśitair vīraiḥ sahabhāryais tathā bhṛśam
c araṇye vividhāḥ kleśāḥ saṃprāptās taiḥ sudāruṇāḥ
a tathā virāṭanagare yonyantaragatair iva
c prāptaḥ paramasaṃkleśo yathā pāpair mahātmabhiḥ
a te sarve pṛṣṭhataḥ kṛtvā tat sarvaṃ pūrvakilbiṣam
c sāmaiva kurubhiḥ sārdham icchanti kurupuṃgavāḥ
a teṣāṃ ca vṛttam ājñāya vṛttaṃ duryodhanasya ca
c anunetum ihārhanti dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ suhṛjjanāḥ
a na hi te vigrahaṃ vīrāḥ kurvanti kurubhiḥ saha
c avināśena lokasya kāṅkṣante pāṇḍavāḥ svakam
a yaś cāpi dhārtarāṣṭrasya hetuḥ syād vigrahaṃ prati
c sa ca hetur na mantavyo balīyāṃsas tathā hi te
a akṣauhiṇyo hi saptaiva dharmaputrasya saṃgatāḥ
c yuyutsamānāḥ kurubhiḥ pratīkṣante 'sya śāsanam
a apare puruṣavyāghrāḥ sahasrākṣauhiṇīsamāḥ
c sātyakir bhīmasenaś ca yamau ca sumahābalau
a ekādaśaitāḥ pṛtanā ekataś ca samāgatāḥ
c ekataś ca mahābāhur bahurūpo dhanaṃjayaḥ
a yathā kirīṭī senābhyaḥ sarvābhyo vyatiricyate
c evam eva mahābāhur vāsudevo mahādyutiḥ
a bahulatvaṃ ca senānāṃ vikramaṃ ca kirīṭinaḥ
c buddhimattāṃ ca kṛṣṇasya buddhvā yudhyeta ko naraḥ
a te bhavanto yathādharmaṃ yathāsamayam eva ca
c prayacchantu pradātavyaṃ mā vaḥ kālo 'tyagād ayam
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā prajñāvṛddho mahādyutiḥ
c saṃpūjyainaṃ yathākālaṃ bhīṣmo vacanam abravīt
a diṣṭyā kuśalinaḥ sarve pāṇḍavāḥ saha bāndhavaiḥ
c diṣṭyā sahāyavantaś ca diṣṭyā dharme ca te ratāḥ
a diṣṭyā ca saṃdhikāmās te bhrātaraḥ kurunandanāḥ
c diṣṭyā na yuddhamanasaḥ saha dāmodareṇa te
a bhavatā satyam uktaṃ ca sarvam etan na saṃśayaḥ
c atitīkṣṇaṃ tu te vākyaṃ brāhmaṇyād iti me matiḥ
a asaṃśayaṃ kleśitās te vane ceha ca pāṇḍavāḥ
c prāptāś ca dharmataḥ sarvaṃ pitur dhanam asaṃśayam
a kirīṭī balavān pārthaḥ kṛtāstraś ca mahābalaḥ
c ko hi pāṇḍusutaṃ yuddhe viṣaheta dhanaṃjayam
a api vajradharaḥ sākṣāt kim utānye dhanurbhṛtaḥ
c trayāṇām api lokānāṃ samartha iti me matiḥ
a bhīṣme bruvati tad vākyaṃ dhṛṣṭam ākṣipya manyumān
c duryodhanaṃ samālokya karṇo vacanam abravīt
a na tan na viditaṃ brahmaṃl loke bhūtena kena cit
c punaruktena kiṃ tena bhāṣitena punaḥ punaḥ
a duryodhanārthe śakunir dyūte nirjitavān purā
c samayena gato 'raṇyaṃ pāṇḍuputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a na taṃ samayam ādṛtya rājyam icchati paitṛkam
c balam āśritya matsyānāṃ pāñcālānāṃ ca pārthivaḥ
a duryodhano bhayād vidvan na dadyāt padam antataḥ
c dharmatas tu mahīṃ kṛtsnāṃ pradadyāc chatrave 'pi ca
a yadi kāṅkṣanti te rājyaṃ pitṛpaitāmahaṃ punaḥ
c yathāpratijñaṃ kālaṃ taṃ carantu vanam āśritāḥ
a tato duryodhanasyāṅke vartantām akutobhayāḥ
c adhārmikām imāṃ buddhiṃ kuryur maurkhyād dhi kevalam
a atha te dharmam utsṛjya yuddham icchanti pāṇḍavāḥ
c āsādyemān kuruśreṣṭhān smariṣyanti vaco mama
 bhīṣma uvāca
a kiṃ nu rādheya vācā te karma tat smartum arhasi
c eka eva yadā pārthaḥ ṣaḍ rathāñ jitavān yudhi
d bahuśo jīyamānasya karma dṛṣṭaṃ tadaiva te
d virāṭanagare dhīraḥ kiṃ tvaṃ tatraiva nāgataḥ
a na ced evaṃ kariṣyāmo yad ayaṃ brāhmaṇo 'bravīt
c dhruvaṃ yudhi hatās tena bhakṣayiṣyāma pāṃsukān
d duryodhanaḥ sahāmātyo vinaṅkṣayati na saṃśayaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a dhṛtarāṣṭras tato bhīṣmam anumānya prasādya ca
c avabhartsya ca rādheyam idaṃ vacanam abravīt
a asmaddhitam idaṃ vākyaṃ bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo 'bravīt
b duryodhanasamakṣaṃ ca pārthivānāṃ ca saṃnidhau
b eṣa vakṣyati dharmātmā vākyaṃ vākyaviśāradaḥ
b asmad dhitam idaṃ vākyaṃ bhīṣmeṇoktaṃ mahātmanā
c pāṇḍavānāṃ hitaṃ caiva sarvasya jagatas tathā
a cintayitvā tu pārthebhyaḥ preṣayiṣyāmi saṃjayam
c sa bhavān pratiyātv adya pāṇḍavān eva māciram
a sa taṃ satkṛtya kauravyaḥ preṣayām āsa pāṇḍavān
c sabhāmadhye samāhūya saṃjayaṃ vākyam abravīt
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a prāptān āhuḥ saṃjaya pāṇḍuputrān
upaplavye tān vijānīhi gatvā
c ajātaśatruṃ ca sabhājayethā
diṣṭyānagha grāmam upasthitas tvam
d putro mahyaṃ mṛtyuvaśaṃ jagāma
d duryodhanaḥ saṃjaya rāgabuddhiḥ
a sarvān vadeḥ saṃjaya svastimantaḥ
kṛcchraṃ vāsam atadarhā niruṣya
c teṣāṃ śāntir vidyate 'smāsu śīghraṃ
mithyopetānām upakāriṇāṃ satām
a nāhaṃ kva cit saṃjaya pāṇḍavānāṃ
mithyāvṛttiṃ kāṃ cana jātv apaśyam
c sarvāṃ śriyaṃ hy ātmavīryeṇa labdhvā
paryākārṣuḥ pāṇḍavā mahyam eva
a doṣaṃ hy eṣāṃ nādhigacche parikṣan
nityaṃ kaṃ cid yena garheya pārthān
c dharmārthābhyāṃ karma kurvanti nityaṃ
sukhapriyā nānurudhyanti kāmān
a gharmaṃ śītaṃ kṣutpipāse tathaiva
nidrāṃ tandrīṃ krodhaharṣau pramādam
c dhṛtyā caiva prajñayā cābhibhūya
dharmārthayogān prayatanti pārthāḥ
a tyajanti mitreṣu dhanāni kāle
na saṃvāsāj jīryati maitram eṣām
c yathārhamānārthakarā hi pārthās
teṣāṃ dveṣṭā nāsty ājamīḍhasya pakṣe
a anyatra pāpād viṣamān mandabuddher
duryodhanāt kṣudratarāc ca karṇāt
c teṣāṃ hīme hīnasukhapriyāṇāṃ
mahātmanāṃ saṃjanayanti tejaḥ
d bhāgaṃ gantuṃ ghaṭate mandabuddhir
d mahātmanāṃ saṃjaya dīptatejasām
a utthānavīryaḥ sukham edhamāno
duryodhanaḥ sukṛtaṃ manyate tat
c teṣāṃ bhāgaṃ yac ca manyeta bālaḥ
śakyaṃ hartuṃ jīvatāṃ pāṇḍavānām
a yasyārjunaḥ padavīṃ keśavaś ca
vṛkodaraḥ sātyako 'jātaśatroḥ
c mādrīputrau sṛñjayāś cāpi sarve
purā yuddhāt sādhu tasya pradānam
a sa hy evaikaḥ pṛthivīṃ savyasācī
gāṇḍīvadhanvā praṇuded rathasthaḥ
c tathā viṣṇuḥ keśavo 'py apradhṛṣyo
lokatrayasyādhipatir mahātmā
a tiṣṭheta kas tasya martyaḥ purastād
yaḥ sarvadeveṣu vareṇya īḍyaḥ
c parjanyaghoṣān pravapañ śaraughān
pataṃgasaṃghān iva śīghravegān
a diśaṃ hy udīcīm api cottarān kurūn
gāṇḍīvadhanvaikaratho jigāya
c dhanaṃ caiṣām āharat savyasācī
senānugān balidāṃś caiva cakre
a yaś caiva devān khāṇḍave savyasācī
gāṇḍīvadhanvā prajigāya sendrān
c upāharat phalguno jātavedase
yaśo mānaṃ vardhayan pāṇḍavānām
a gadābhṛtāṃ nādya samo 'sti bhīmād
dhastyāroho nāsti samaś ca tasya
c rathe 'rjunād āhur ahīnam enaṃ
bāhvor bale cāyutanāgavīryam
a suśikṣitaḥ kṛtavairas tarasvī
dahet kruddhas tarasā dhārtarāṣṭrān
c sadātyamarṣī balavān na śakyo
yuddhe jetuṃ vāsavenāpi sākṣāt
a sucetasau balinau śīghrahastau
suśikṣitau bhrātarau phalgunena
c śyenau yathā pakṣipūgān rujantau
mādrīputrau neha kurūn viśetām
d etad balaṃ pūrṇam asmākam evaṃ
d yat sātvatāṃ nāsti tṛtīyam anyat
a teṣāṃ madhye vartamānas tarasvī
dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ pāṇḍavānām ihaikaḥ
c sahāmātyaḥ somakānāṃ prabarhaḥ
saṃtyaktātmā pāṇḍavānāṃ jayāya
d ajātaśatruṃ prasaheta ko 'nyo
d yeṣāṃ sa syād agraṇīr vṛṣṇisiṃhaḥ
a sahoṣitaś caritārtho vayaḥsthaḥ
śālveyānām adhipo vai virāṭaḥ
c saha putraiḥ pāṇḍavārthe ca śaśvad
yudhiṣṭhiraṃ bhakta iti śrutaṃ me
a avaruddhā balinaḥ kekayebhyo
maheṣvāsā bhrātaraḥ pañca santi
c kekayebhyo rājyam ākāṅkṣamāṇā
yuddhārthinaś cānuvasanti pārthān
a sarve ca vīrāḥ pṛthivīpatīnāṃ
samānītāḥ pāṇḍavārthe niviṣṭāḥ
c śūrān ahaṃ bhaktimataḥ śṛṇomi
prītyā yuktān saṃśritān dharmarājam
a giryāśrayā durganivāsinaś ca
yodhāḥ pṛthivyāṃ kulajā viśuddhāḥ
c mlecchāś ca nānāyudhavīryavantaḥ
samāgatāḥ pāṇḍavārthe niviṣṭāḥ
a pāṇḍyaś ca rājāmita indrakalpo
yudhi pravīrair bahubhiḥ sametaḥ
c samāgataḥ pāṇḍavārthe mahātmā
lokapravīro 'prativīryatejāḥ
a astraṃ droṇād arjunād vāsudevāt
kṛpād bhīṣmād yena kṛtaṃ śṛṇomi
c yaṃ taṃ kārṣṇipratimaṃ prāhur ekaṃ
sa sātyakiḥ pāṇḍavārthe niviṣṭaḥ
a apāśritāś cedikarūṣakāś ca
sarvotsāhair bhūmipālaiḥ sametāḥ
c teṣāṃ madhye sūryam ivātapantaṃ
śriyā vṛtaṃ cedipatiṃ jvalantam
a astambhanīyaṃ yudhi manyamānaṃ
jyākarṣatāṃ śreṣṭhatamaṃ pṛthivyām
c sarvotsāhaṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ nihatya
prasahya kṛṣṇas tarasā mamarda
a yaśomānau vardhayan yādavānāṃ
purābhinac chiśupālaṃ samīke
c yasya sarve vardhayanti sma mānaṃ
karūṣarājapramukhā narendrāḥ
a tam asahyaṃ keśavaṃ tatra matvā
sugrīvayuktena rathena kṛṣṇam
c saṃprādravaṃś cedipatiṃ vihāya
siṃhaṃ dṛṣṭvā kṣudramṛgā ivānye
a yas taṃ pratīpas tarasā pratyudīyād
āśaṃsamāno dvairathe vāsudevam
c so 'śeta kṛṣṇena hataḥ parāsur
vātenevonmathitaḥ karṇikāraḥ
a parākramaṃ me yad avedayanta
teṣām arthe saṃjaya keśavasya
c anusmaraṃs tasya karmāṇi viṣṇor
gāvalgaṇe nādhigacchāmi śāntim
a na jātu tāñ śatrur anyaḥ saheta
yeṣāṃ sa syād agraṇīr vṛṣṇisiṃhaḥ
c pravepate me hṛdayaṃ bhayena
śrutvā kṛṣṇāv ekarathe sametau
a no ced gacchet saṃgaraṃ mandabuddhis
tābhyāṃ suto me viparītacetāḥ
c no cet kurūn saṃjaya nirdahetām
indrāviṣṇū daityasenāṃ yathaiva
e mato hi me śakrasamo dhanaṃjayaḥ
sanātano vṛṣṇivīraś ca viṣṇuḥ
a dharmārāmo hrīniṣedhas tarasvī
kuntīputraḥ pāṇḍavo 'jātaśatruḥ
c duryodhanena nikṛto manasvī
no cet kruddhaḥ pradahed dhārtarāṣṭrān
a nāhaṃ tathā hy arjunād vāsudevād
bhīmād vāpi yamayor vā bibhemi
c yathā rājñaḥ krodhadīptasya sūta
manyor ahaṃ bhītataraḥ sadaiva
a alaṃ tapobrahmacaryeṇa yuktaḥ
saṃkalpo 'yaṃ mānasas tasya sidhyet
c tasya krodhaṃ saṃjayāhaṃ samīke
sthāne jānan bhṛśam asmy adya bhītaḥ
a sa gaccha śīghraṃ prahito rathena
pāñcālarājasya camūṃ paretya
c ajātaśatruṃ kuśalaṃ sma pṛccheḥ
punaḥ punaḥ prītiyuktaṃ vades tvam
a janārdanaṃ cāpi sametya tāta
mahāmātraṃ vīryavatām udāram
c anāmayaṃ madvacanena pṛccher
dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ śāntim īpsuḥ
a na tasya kiṃ cid vacanaṃ na kuryāt
kuntīputro vāsudevasya sūta
c priyaś caiṣām ātmasamaś ca kṛṣṇo
vidvāṃś caiṣāṃ karmaṇi nityayuktaḥ
a samānīya pāṇḍavān sṛñjayāṃś ca
janārdanaṃ yuyudhānaṃ virāṭam
c anāmayaṃ madvacanena pṛccheḥ
sarvāṃs tathā draupadeyāṃś ca pañca
a yad yat tatra prāptakālaṃ parebhyas
tvaṃ manyethā bhāratānāṃ hitaṃ ca
c tat tad bhāṣethāḥ saṃjaya rājamadhye
na mūrchayed yan na bhavec ca yuddham
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a rājñas tu vacanaṃ śrutvā dhṛtarāṣṭrasya saṃjayaḥ
c upaplavyaṃ yayau draṣṭuṃ pāṇḍavān amitaujasaḥ
a sa tu rājānam āsādya dharmātmānaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
c praṇipatya tataḥ pūrvaṃ sūtaputro 'bhyabhāṣata
a gāvalgaṇiḥ saṃjayaḥ sūtasūnur
ajātaśatrum avadat pratītaḥ
c diṣṭyā rājaṃs tvām arogaṃ prapaśye
sahāyavantaṃ ca mahendrakalpam
a anāmayaṃ pṛcchati tvāmbikeyo
vṛddho rājā dhṛtarāṣṭro manīṣī
c kaccid bhīmaḥ kuśalī pāṇḍavāgryo
dhanaṃjayas tau ca mādrītanūjau
a kaccit kṛṣṇā draupadī rājaputrī
satyavratā vīrapatnī saputrā
c manasvinī yatra ca vāñchasi tvam
iṣṭān kāmān bhārata svastikāmaḥ
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a gāvalgaṇe saṃjaya svāgataṃ te
prītātmāhaṃ tvābhivadāmi sūta
c anāmayaṃ pratijāne tavāhaṃ
sahānujaiḥ kuśalī cāsmi vidvan
a cirād idaṃ kuśalaṃ bhāratasya
śrutvā rājñaḥ kuruvṛddhasya sūta
c manye sākṣād dṛṣṭam ahaṃ narendraṃ
dṛṣṭvaiva tvāṃ saṃjaya prītiyogāt
a pitāmaho naḥ sthaviro manasvī
mahāprājñaḥ sarvadharmopapannaḥ
c sa kauravyaḥ kuśalī tāta bhīṣmo
yathāpūrvaṃ vṛttir apy asya kaccit
a kaccid rājā dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ saputro
vaicitravīryaḥ kuśalī mahātmā
c mahārājo bāhlikaḥ prātipeyaḥ
kaccid vidvān kuśalī sūtaputra
a sa somadattaḥ kuśalī tāta kaccid
bhūriśravāḥ satyasaṃdhaḥ śalaś ca
c droṇaḥ saputraś ca kṛpaś ca vipro
maheṣvāsāḥ kaccid ete 'py arogāḥ
c śāradvataḥ kuśalī tāta vipraḥ
a mahāprājñāḥ sarvaśāstrāvadātā
dhanurbhṛtāṃ mukhyatamāḥ pṛthivyām
c kaccin mānaṃ tāta labhanta ete
dhanurbhṛtaḥ kaccid ete 'py arogāḥ
a sarve kurubhyaḥ spṛhayanti saṃjaya
dhanurdharā ye pṛthivyāṃ yuvānaḥ
c yeṣāṃ rāṣṭre nivasati darśanīyo
maheṣvāsaḥ śīlavān droṇaputraḥ
a vaiśyāputraḥ kuśalī tāta kaccin
mahāprājño rājaputro yuyutsuḥ
c karṇo 'mātyaḥ kuśalī tāta kaccit
suyodhano yasya mando vidheyaḥ
a striyo vṛddhā bhāratānāṃ jananyo
mahānasyo dāsabhāryāś ca sūta
c vadhvaḥ putrā bhāgineyā bhaginyo
dauhitrā vā kaccid apy avyalīkāḥ
a kaccid rājā brāhmaṇānāṃ yathāvat
pravartate pūrvavat tāta vṛttim
c kaccid dāyān māmakān dhārtarāṣṭro
dvijātīnāṃ saṃjaya nopahanti
a kaccid rājā dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ saputra
upekṣate brāhmaṇātikramān vai
c kaccin na hetor iva vartmabhūta
upekṣate teṣu sa nyūnavṛttim
a etaj jyotir uttamaṃ jīvaloke
śuklaṃ prajānāṃ vihitaṃ vidhātrā
c te cel lobhaṃ na niyacchanti mandāḥ
kṛtsno nāśo bhavitā kauravāṇām
a kaccid rājā dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ saputro
bubhūṣate vṛttim amātyavarge
c kaccin na bhedena jijīviṣanti
suhṛdrūpā durhṛdaś caikamitrāḥ
a kaccin na pāpaṃ kathayanti tāta
te pāṇḍavānāṃ kuravaḥ sarva eva
b droṇaḥ saputraś ca kṛpaś ca vīro
b nāsmāsu pāpāni vadanti kaccit
b kaccid rājyaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ saputraṃ
b sametyāhuḥ kuravaḥ sarva eva
c kaccid dṛṣṭvā dasyusaṃghān sametān
smaranti pārthasya yudhāṃ praṇetuḥ
a maurvībhujāgraprahitān sma tāta
dodhūyamānena dhanurdhareṇa
c gāṇḍīvamuktān stanayitnughoṣān
ajihmagān kaccid anusmaranti
d na taṃ dṛṣṭvā kaccid atra pratīpaṃ
d gantā gṛhāñ jātu jagāma raṅgāt
a na hy apaśyaṃ kaṃ cid ahaṃ pṛthivyāṃ
śrutaṃ samaṃ vādhikam arjunena
c yasyaikaṣaṣṭir niśitās tīkṣṇadhārāḥ
suvāsasaḥ saṃmato hastavāpaḥ
a gadāpāṇir bhīmasenas tarasvī
pravepayañ śatrusaṃghān anīke
c nāgaḥ prabhinna iva naḍvalāsu
caṅkramyate kaccid enaṃ smaranti
a mādrīputraḥ sahadevaḥ kaliṅgān
samāgatān ajayad dantakūre
c vāmenāsyan dakṣiṇenaiva yo vai
mahābalaṃ kaccid enaṃ smaranti
a udyann ayaṃ nakulaḥ preṣito vai
gāvalgaṇe saṃjaya paśyatas te
c diśaṃ pratīcīṃ vaśam ānayan me
mādrīsutaṃ kaccid enaṃ smaranti
a abhyābhavo dvaitavane ya āsīd
durmantrite ghoṣayātrāgatānām
c yatra mandāñ śatruvaśaṃ prayātān
amocayad bhīmaseno jayaś ca
a ahaṃ paścād arjunam abhyarakṣaṃ
mādrīputrau bhīmasenaś ca cakre
c gāṇḍīvabhṛc chatrusaṃghān udasya
svasty āgamat kaccid enaṃ smaranti
a na karmaṇā sādhunaikena nūnaṃ
kartuṃ śakyaṃ bhavatīha saṃjaya
c sarvātmanā parijetuṃ vayaṃ cen
na śaknumo dhṛtarāṣṭrasya putram
 saṃjaya uvāca
a yathārhase pāṇḍava tat tathaiva
kurūn kuruśreṣṭha janaṃ ca pṛcchasi
c anāmayās tāta manasvinas te
kuruśreṣṭhān pṛcchasi pārtha yāṃs tvam
a santy eva vṛddhāḥ sādhavo dhārtarāṣṭre
santy eva pāpāḥ pāṇḍava tasya viddhi
c dadyād ripoś cāpi hi dhārtarāṣṭraḥ
kuto dāyāṃl lopayed brāhmaṇānām
a yad yuṣmākaṃ vartate 'sau na dharmyam
adrugdheṣu drugdhavat tan na sādhu
c mitradhruk syād dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ saputro
yuṣmān dviṣan sādhuvṛttān asādhuḥ
a na cānujānāti bhṛśaṃ ca tapyate
śocaty antaḥ sthaviro 'jātaśatro
c śṛṇoti hi brāhmaṇānāṃ sametya
mitradrohaḥ pātakebhyo garīyān
a smaranti tubhyaṃ naradeva saṃgame
yuddhe ca jiṣṇoś ca yudhāṃ praṇetuḥ
c samutkṛṣṭe dundubhiśaṅkhaśabde
gadāpāṇiṃ bhīmasenaṃ smaranti
a mādrīsutau cāpi raṇājimadhye
sarvā diśaḥ saṃpatantau smaranti
c senāṃ varṣantau śaravarṣair ajasraṃ
mahārathau samare duṣprakampyau
a na tv eva manye puruṣasya rājann
anāgataṃ jñāyate yad bhaviṣyam
c tvaṃ ced imaṃ sarvadharmopapannaḥ
prāptaḥ kleśaṃ pāṇḍava kṛcchrarūpam
a tvam evaitat sarvam ataś ca bhūyaḥ
samīkuryāḥ prajñayājātaśatro
c na kāmārthaṃ saṃtyajeyur hi dharmaṃ
pāṇḍoḥ sutāḥ sarva evendrakalpāḥ
a tvam evaitat prajñayājātaśatro
śamaṃ kuryā yena śarmāpnuyus te
c dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ sṛñjayāś ca
ye cāpy anye pārthivāḥ saṃniviṣṭāḥ
d teṣāṃ sarveṣāṃ śamam evaṃ vidadhyāḥ
a yan mābravīd dhṛtarāṣṭro niśāyām
ajātaśatro vacanaṃ pitā te
c sahāmātyaḥ sahaputraś ca rājan
sametya tāṃ vācam imāṃ nibodha
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a samāgatāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ sṛñjayāś ca
janārdano yuyudhāno virāṭaḥ
c yat te vākyaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrānuśiṣṭaṃ
gāvalgaṇe brūhi tat sūtaputra
 saṃjaya uvāca
a ajātaśatruṃ ca vṛkodaraṃ ca
dhanaṃjayaṃ mādravatīsutau ca
c āmantraye vāsudevaṃ ca śauriṃ
yuyudhānaṃ cekitānaṃ virāṭam
a pāñcālānām adhipaṃ caiva vṛddhaṃ
dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ pārṣataṃ yājñasenim
c sarve vācaṃ śṛṇutemāṃ madīyāṃ
vakṣyāmi yāṃ bhūtim icchan kurūṇām
a śamaṃ rājā dhṛtarāṣṭro 'bhinandann
ayojayat tvaramāṇo rathaṃ me
c sabhrātṛputrasvajanasya rājñas
tad rocatāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ śamo 'stu
a sarvair dharmaiḥ samupetāḥ stha pārthāḥ
prasthānena mārdavenārjavena
c jātāḥ kule anṛśaṃsā vadānyā
hrīniṣedhāḥ karmaṇāṃ niścayajñāḥ
a na yujyate karma yuṣmāsu hīnaṃ
sattvaṃ hi vas tādṛśaṃ bhīmasenāḥ
c udbhāsate hy añjanabinduvat tac
chukle vastre yad bhavet kilbiṣaṃ vaḥ
a sarvakṣayo dṛśyate yatra kṛtsnaḥ
pāpodayo nirayo 'bhāvasaṃsthaḥ
c kas tat kuryāj jātu karma prajānan
parājayo yatra samo jayaś ca
a te vai dhanyā yaiḥ kṛtaṃ jñātikāryaṃ
ye vaḥ putrāḥ suhṛdo bāndhavāś ca
c upakruṣṭaṃ jīvitaṃ saṃtyajeyus
tataḥ kurūṇāṃ niyato vai bhavaḥ syāt
a te cet kurūn anuśāsya stha pārthā
ninīya sarvān dviṣato nigṛhya
c samaṃ vas taj jīvitaṃ mṛtyunā syād
yaj jīvadhvaṃ jñātivadhe na sādhu
a ko hy eva yuṣmān saha keśavena
sacekitānān pārṣatabāhuguptān
c sasātyakīn viṣaheta prajetuṃ
labdhvāpi devān sacivān sahendrān
a ko vā kurūn droṇabhīṣmābhiguptān
aśvatthāmnā śalyakṛpādibhiś ca
c raṇe prasoḍhuṃ viṣaheta rājan
rādheyaguptān saha bhūmipālaiḥ
a mahad balaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrasya rājñaḥ
ko vai śakto hantum akṣīyamāṇaḥ
c so 'haṃ jaye caiva parājaye ca
niḥśreyasaṃ nādhigacchāmi kiṃ cit
a kathaṃ hi nīcā iva dauṣkuleyā
nirdharmārthaṃ karma kuryuś ca pārthāḥ
c so 'haṃ prasādya praṇato vāsudevaṃ
pāñcālānām adhipaṃ caiva vṛddham
a kṛtāñjaliḥ śaraṇaṃ vaḥ prapadye
kathaṃ svasti syāt kurusṛñjayānām
c na hy eva te vacanaṃ vāsudevo
dhanaṃjayo vā jātu kiṃ cin na kuryāt
a prāṇān ādau yācyamānaḥ kuto 'nyad
etad vidvan sādhanārthaṃ bravīmi
b dhanāni ratnāni bahūni rājyaṃ
b kalyāṇarūpāṇi ca vāhanāni
b na durlabhānīha narapradhānā
b vṛddhasya rājñaḥ śāsane tiṣṭhatāṃ vaḥ
c etad rājño bhīṣmapurogamasya
mataṃ yad vaḥ śāntir ihottamā syāt
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a kāṃ nu vācaṃ saṃjaya me śṛṇoṣi
yuddhaiṣiṇīṃ yena yuddhād bibheṣi
c ayuddhaṃ vai tāta yuddhād garīyaḥ
kas tal labdhvā jātu yudhyeta sūta
a akurvataś cet puruṣasya saṃjaya
sidhyet saṃkalpo manasā yaṃ yam icchet
c na karma kuryād viditaṃ mamaitad
anyatra yuddhād bahu yal laghīyaḥ
a kuto yuddhaṃ jātu naraḥ prajānan
ko daivaśapto 'bhivṛṇīta yuddham
c sukhaiṣiṇaḥ karma kurvanti pārthā
dharmād ahīnaṃ yac ca lokasya pathyam
a karmodayaṃ sukham āśaṃsamānaḥ
kṛcchropāyaṃ tattvataḥ karma duḥkham
c sukhaprepsur vijighāṃsuś ca duḥkhaṃ
ya indriyāṇāṃ prītivaśānugāmī
c kulāntakaṃ saṃjaya ko 'bhivāñchet
c karmār abhedyac ca dharmān apetam
e kāmābhidhyā svaśarīraṃ dunoti
yayā prayukto 'nukaroti duḥkham
f tṛṣṇāṃ tyajet sarvadharmād apetāṃ
a yathedhyamānasya samiddhatejaso
bhūyo balaṃ vardhate pāvakasya
c kāmārthalābhena tathaiva bhūyo
na tṛpyate sarpiṣevāgnir iddhaḥ
e saṃpaśyemaṃ bhogacayaṃ mahāntaṃ
sahāsmābhir dhṛtarāṣṭrasya rājñaḥ
f saṃmohanaṃ tasya mahat tathaitad
f yad asmābhir viprayogo nṛpasya
a nāśreyasām īśvaro vigrahāṇāṃ
nāśreyasāṃ gītaśabdaṃ śṛṇoti
c nāśreyasaḥ sevate mālyagandhān
na cāpy aśreyāṃsy anulepanāni
a nāśreyasaḥ prāvarān adhyavaste
kathaṃ tv asmān saṃpraṇudet kurubhyaḥ
c atraiva ca syād avadhūya eṣa
kāmaḥ śarīre hṛdayaṃ dunoti
a svayaṃ rājā viṣamasthaḥ pareṣu
sāmasthyam anvicchati tan na sādhu
c yathātmanaḥ paśyati vṛttam eva
tathā pareṣām api so 'bhyupaiti
a āsannam agniṃ tu nidāghakāle
gambhīrakakṣe gahane visṛjya
c yathā vṛddhaṃ vāyuvaśena śocet
kṣemaṃ mumukṣuḥ śiśiravyapāye
a prāptaiśvaryo dhṛtarāṣṭro 'dya rājā
lālapyate saṃjaya kasya hetoḥ
c pragṛhya durbuddhim anārjave rataṃ
putraṃ mandaṃ mūḍham amantriṇaṃ tu
a anāptaḥ sann āptatamasya vācaṃ
suyodhano vidurasyāvamanya
c sutasya rājā dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ priyaiṣī
saṃbudhyamāno viśate 'dharmam eva
a medhāvinaṃ hy arthakāmaṃ kurūṇāṃ
bahuśrutaṃ vāgminaṃ śīlavantam
c sūta rājā dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ kurubhyo
na so 'smarad viduraṃ putrakāmyāt
a mānaghnasya ātmakāmasya cerṣyoḥ
saṃrambhiṇaś cārthadharmātigasya
c durbhāṣiṇo manyuvaśānugasya
kāmātmano durhṛdo bhāvanasya
a aneyasyāśreyaso dīrghamanyor
mitradruhaḥ saṃjaya pāpabuddheḥ
c sutasya rājā dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ priyaiṣī
prapaśyamānaḥ prajahād dharmakāmau
a tadaiva me saṃjaya dīvyato 'bhūn
no cet kurūn āgataḥ syād abhāvaḥ
c kāvyāṃ vācaṃ viduro bhāṣamāṇo
na vindate dhṛtarāṣṭrāt praśaṃsām
a kṣattur yadā anvavartanta buddhiṃ
kṛcchraṃ kurūn na tadābhyājagāma
c yāvat prajñām anvavartanta tasya
tāvat teṣāṃ rāṣṭravṛddhir babhūva
a tadarthalubdhasya nibodha me 'dya
ye mantriṇo dhārtarāṣṭrasya sūta
c duḥśāsanaḥ śakuniḥ sūtaputro
gāvalgaṇe paśya saṃmoham asya
a so 'haṃ na paśyāmi parīkṣamāṇaḥ
kathaṃ svasti syāt kurusṛñjayānām
c āttaiśvaryo dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ parebhyaḥ
pravrājite vidure dīrghadṛṣṭau
a āśaṃsate vai dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ saputro
mahārājyam asapatnaṃ pṛthivyām
c tasmiñ śamaḥ kevalaṃ nopalabhyo
atyāsannaṃ madgataṃ manyate 'rtham
a yat tat karṇo manyate pāraṇīyaṃ
yuddhe gṛhītāyudham arjunena
c āsaṃś ca yuddhāni purā mahānti
kathaṃ karṇo nābhavad dvīpa eṣām
a karṇaś ca jānāti suyodhanaś ca
droṇaś ca jānāti pitāmahaś ca
c anye ca ye kuravas tatra santi
yathārjunān nāsty aparo dhanurdharaḥ
a jānanty ete kuravaḥ sarva eva
ye cāpy anye bhūmipālāḥ sametāḥ
c duryodhanaṃ cāparādhe carantam
ariṃdame phalgune 'vidyamāne
a tenārthabaddhaṃ manyate dhārtarāṣṭraḥ
śakyaṃ hartuṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ mamatvam
c kirīṭinā tālamātrāyudhena
tadvedinā saṃyugaṃ tatra gatvā
a gāṇḍīvavisphāritaśabdam ājāv
aśṛṇvānā dhārtarāṣṭrā dhriyante
c kruddhasya ced bhīmasenasya vegāt
suyodhano manyate siddham artham
a indro 'py etan notsahet tāta hartum
aiśvaryaṃ no jīvati bhīmasene
c dhanaṃjaye nakule caiva sūta
tathā vīre sahadeve madīye
a sa ced etāṃ pratipadyeta buddhiṃ
vṛddho rājā saha putreṇa sūta
c evaṃ raṇe pāṇḍavakopadagdhā
na naśyeyuḥ saṃjaya dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ
a jānāsi tvaṃ kleśam asmāsu vṛttaṃ
tvāṃ pūjayan saṃjayāhaṃ kṣameyam
c yac cāsmākaṃ kauravair bhūtapūrvaṃ
yā no vṛttir dhārtarāṣṭre tadāsīt
a adyāpi tat tatra tathaiva vartatāṃ
śāntiṃ gamiṣyāmi yathā tvam āttha
c indraprasthe bhavatu mamaiva rājyaṃ
suyodhano yacchatu bhāratāgryaḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a dharme nityā pāṇḍava te viceṣṭā
loke śrutā dṛśyate cāpi pārtha
c mahāsrāvaṃ jīvitaṃ cāpy anityaṃ
saṃpaśya tvaṃ pāṇḍava mā vinīnaśaḥ
a na ced bhāgaṃ kuravo 'nyatra yuddhāt
prayacchante tubhyam ajātaśatro
c bhaikṣacaryām andhakavṛṣṇirājye
śreyo manye na tu yuddhena rājyam
a alpakālaṃ jīvitaṃ yan manuṣye
mahāsrāvaṃ nityaduḥkhaṃ calaṃ ca
c bhūyaś ca tad vayaso nānurūpaṃ
tasmāt pāpaṃ pāṇḍava mā prasārṣīḥ
a kāmā manuṣyaṃ prasajanta eva
dharmasya ye vighnamūlaṃ narendra
c pūrvaṃ naras tān dhṛtimān vinighnaṃl
loke praśaṃsāṃ labhate 'navadyām
a nibandhanī hy arthatṛṣṇeha pārtha
tām eṣato bādhyate dharma eva
c dharmaṃ tu yaḥ pravṛṇīte sa buddhaḥ
kāme gṛddho hīyate 'rthānurodhāt
a dharmaṃ kṛtvā karmaṇāṃ tāta mukhyaṃ
mahāpratāpaḥ saviteva bhāti
c hānena dharmasya mahīm apīmāṃ
labdhvā naraḥ sīdati pāpabuddhiḥ
a vedo 'dhītaś caritaṃ brahmacaryaṃ
yajñair iṣṭaṃ brāhmaṇebhyaś ca dattam
c paraṃ sthānaṃ manyamānena bhūya
ātmā datto varṣapūgaṃ sukhebhyaḥ
a sukhapriye sevamāno 'tivelaṃ
yogābhyāse yo na karoti karma
c vittakṣaye hīnasukho 'tivelaṃ
duḥkhaṃ śete kāmavegapraṇunnaḥ
a evaṃ punar arthacaryāprasakto
hitvā dharmaṃ yaḥ prakaroty adharmam
c aśraddadhat paralokāya mūḍho
hitvā dehaṃ tapyate pretya mandaḥ
a na karmaṇāṃ vipraṇāśo 'sty amutra
puṇyānāṃ vāpy atha vā pāpakānām
c pūrvaṃ kartur gacchati puṇyapāpaṃ
paścāt tv etad anuyāty eva kartā
a nyāyopetaṃ brāhmaṇebhyo yadannaṃ
śraddhāpūtaṃ gandharasopapannam
c anvāhāryeṣūttamadakṣiṇeṣu
tathārūpaṃ karma vikhyāyate te
a iha kṣetre kriyate pārtha kāryaṃ
na vai kiṃ cid vidyate pretya kāryam
c kṛtaṃ tvayā pāralokyaṃ ca kāryaṃ
puṇyaṃ mahat sadbhir anupraśastam
a jahāti mṛtyuṃ ca jarāṃ bhayaṃ ca
na kṣutpipāse manasaś cāpriyāṇi
c na kartavyaṃ vidyate tatra kiṃ cid
anyatra vai indriyaprīṇanārthāt
a evaṃrūpaṃ karmaphalaṃ narendra
mātrāvatā hṛdayasya priyeṇa
c sa krodhajaṃ pāṇḍava harṣajaṃ ca
lokāv ubhau mā prahāsīś cirāya
a antaṃ gatvā karmaṇāṃ yā praśaṃsā
satyaṃ damaś cārjavam ānṛśaṃsyam
c aśvamedho rājasūyas tatheṣṭaḥ
pāpasyāntaṃ karmaṇo mā punar gāḥ
a tac ced evaṃ deśarūpeṇa pārthāḥ
kariṣyadhvaṃ karma pāpaṃ cirāya
c nivasadhvaṃ varṣapūgān vaneṣu
duḥkhaṃ vāsaṃ pāṇḍavā dharmahetoḥ
a apravrajye yojayitvā purastād
ātmādhīnaṃ yad balaṃ te tadāsīt
c nityaṃ pāñcālāḥ sacivās taveme
janārdano yuyudhānaś ca vīraḥ
a matsyo rājā rukmarathaḥ saputraḥ
prahāribhiḥ saha putrair virāṭaḥ
c rājānaś ca ye vijitāḥ purastāt
tvām eva te saṃśrayeyuḥ samastāḥ
a mahāsahāyaḥ pratapan balasthaḥ
puraskṛto vāsudevārjunābhyām
c varān haniṣyan dviṣato raṅgamadhye
vyaneṣyathā dhārtarāṣṭrasya darpam
a balaṃ kasmād vardhayitvā parasya
nijān kasmāt karśayitvā sahāyān
c niruṣya kasmād varṣapūgān vaneṣu
yuyutsase pāṇḍava hīnakālam
a aprajño vā pāṇḍava yudhyamāno
adharmajño vā bhūtipathād vyapaiti
c prajñāvān vā budhyamāno 'pi dharmaṃ
saṃrambhād vā so 'pi bhūter apaiti
a nādharme te dhīyate pārtha buddhir
na saṃrambhāt karma cakartha pāpam
c addhā kiṃ tat kāraṇaṃ yasya hetoḥ
prajñāviruddhaṃ karma cikīrṣasīdam
a avyādhijaṃ kaṭukaṃ śīrṣarogaṃ
yaśomuṣaṃ pāpaphalodayaṃ ca
c satāṃ peyaṃ yan na pibanty asanto
manyuṃ mahārāja piba praśāmya
a pāpānubandhaṃ ko nu taṃ kāmayeta
kṣamaiva te jyāyasī nota bhogāḥ
c yatra bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo hataḥ syād
yatra droṇaḥ sahaputro hataḥ syāt
a kṛpaḥ śalyaḥ saumadattir vikarṇo
viviṃśatiḥ karṇaduryodhanau ca
c etān hatvā kīdṛśaṃ tat sukhaṃ syād
yad vindethās tad anubrūhi pārtha
a labdhvāpīmāṃ pṛthivīṃ sāgarāntāṃ
jarāmṛtyū naiva hi tvaṃ prajahyāḥ
c priyāpriye sukhaduḥkhe ca rājann
evaṃ vidvān naiva yuddhaṃ kuruṣva
a amātyānāṃ yadi kāmasya hetor
evaṃyuktaṃ karma cikīrṣasi tvam
c apākrameḥ saṃpradāya svam ebhyo
