mā gās tvaṃ vai devayānāt patho 'dya
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a asaṃśayaṃ saṃjaya satyam etad
dharmo varaḥ karmaṇāṃ yat tvam āttha
c jñātvā tu māṃ saṃjaya garhayes tvaṃ
yadi dharmaṃ yady adharmaṃ carāmi
a yatrādharmo dharmarūpāṇi bibhrad
dharmaḥ kṛtsno dṛśyate 'dharmarūpaḥ
c tathā dharmo dhārayan dharmarūpaṃ
vidvāṃsas taṃ saṃprapaśyanti buddhyā
a evam etāv āpadi liṅgam etad
dharmādharmau vṛttinityau bhajetām
c ādyaṃ liṅgaṃ yasya tasya pramāṇam
āpaddharmaṃ saṃjaya taṃ nibodha
a luptāyāṃ tu prakṛtau yena karma
niṣpādayet tat parīpsed vihīnaḥ
c prakṛtisthaś cāpadi vartamāna
ubhau garhyau bhavataḥ saṃjayaitau
a avilopam icchatāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ
prāyaścittaṃ vihitaṃ yad vidhātrā
c āpady athākarmasu vartamānān
vikarmasthān saṃjaya garhayeta
a manīṣiṇāṃ tattvavicchedanāya
vidhīyate satsu vṛttiḥ sadaiva
c abrāhmaṇāḥ santi tu ye na vaidyāḥ
sarvocchedaṃ sādhu manyeta tebhyaḥ
a tadarthā naḥ pitaro ye ca pūrve
pitāmahā ye ca tebhyaḥ pare 'nye
c prajñaiṣiṇo ye ca hi karma cakrur
nāsty antato nāsti nāstīti manye
a yat kiṃ cid etad vittam asyāṃ pṛthivyāṃ
yad devānāṃ tridaśānāṃ paratra
c prājāpatyaṃ tridivaṃ brahmalokaṃ
nādharmataḥ saṃjaya kāmaye tat
a dharmeśvaraḥ kuśalo nītimāṃś cāpy
upāsitā brāhmaṇānāṃ manīṣī
c nānāvidhāṃś caiva mahābalāṃś ca
rājanyabhojān anuśāsti kṛṣṇaḥ
a yadi hy ahaṃ visṛjan syām agarhyo
yudhyamāno yadi jahyāṃ svadharmam
c mahāyaśāḥ keśavas tad bravītu
vāsudevas tūbhayor arthakāmaḥ
a śaineyā hi caitrakāś cāndhakāś ca
vārṣṇeyabhojāḥ kaukurāḥ sṛñjayāś ca
c upāsīnā vāsudevasya buddhiṃ
nigṛhya śatrūn suhṛdo nandayanti
a vṛṣṇyandhakā hy ugrasenādayo vai
kṛṣṇapraṇītāḥ sarva evendrakalpāḥ
c manasvinaḥ satyaparākramāś ca
mahābalā yādavā bhogavantaḥ
a kāśyo babhruḥ śriyam uttamāṃ gato
labdhvā kṛṣṇaṃ bhrātaram īśitāram
c yasmai kāmān varṣati vāsudevo
grīṣmātyaye megha iva prajābhyaḥ
a īdṛśo 'yaṃ keśavas tāta bhūyo
vidmo hy enaṃ karmaṇāṃ niścayajñam
c priyaś ca naḥ sādhutamaś ca kṛṣṇo
nātikrame vacanaṃ keśavasya
 vāsudeva uvāca
a avināśaṃ saṃjaya pāṇḍavānām
icchāmy ahaṃ bhūtim eṣāṃ priyaṃ ca
c tathā rājño dhṛtarāṣṭrasya sūta
sadāśaṃse bahuputrasya vṛddhim
a kāmo hi me saṃjaya nityam eva
nānyad brūyāṃ tān prati śāmyateti
c rājñaś ca hi priyam etac chṛṇomi
manye caitat pāṇḍavānāṃ samartham
a suduṣkaraś cātra śamo hi nūnaṃ
pradarśitaḥ saṃjaya pāṇḍavena
c yasmin gṛddho dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ saputraḥ
kasmād eṣāṃ kalaho nātra mūrcchet
a tattvaṃ dharmaṃ vicaran saṃjayeha
mattaś ca jānāsi yudhiṣṭhirāc ca
c atho kasmāt saṃjaya pāṇḍavasya
utsāhinaḥ pūrayataḥ svakarma
e yathākhyātam āvasataḥ kuṭumbaṃ
purākalpāt sādhu vilopam āttha
a asmin vidhau vartamāne yathāvad
uccāvacā matayo brāhmaṇānām
c karmaṇāhuḥ siddhim eke paratra
hitvā karma vidyayā siddhim eke
d no vindanti kṣatriyāḥ saṃjayāpi
e nābhuñjāno bhakṣyabhojyasya tṛpyed
vidvān apīha viditaṃ brāhmaṇānām
a yā vai vidyāḥ sādhayantīha karma
tāsāṃ phalaṃ vidyate netarāsām
c tatreha vai dṛṣṭaphalaṃ tu karma
pītvodakaṃ śāmyati tṛṣṇayārtaḥ
a so 'yaṃ vidhir vihitaḥ karmaṇaiva
tad vartate saṃjaya tatra karma
c tatra yo 'nyat karmaṇaḥ sādhu manyen
moghaṃ tasya lapitaṃ durbalasya
a karmaṇāmī bhānti devāḥ paratra
karmaṇaiveha plavate mātariśvā
c ahorātre vidadhat karmaṇaiva
atandrito nityam udeti sūryaḥ
a māsārdhamāsān atha nakṣatrayogān
atandritaś candramā abhyupaiti
c atandrito dahate jātavedāḥ
samidhyamānaḥ karma kurvan prajābhyaḥ
a atandritā bhāram imaṃ mahāntaṃ
bibharti devī pṛthivī balena
c atandritāḥ śīghram apo vahanti
saṃtarpayantyaḥ sarvabhūtāni nadyaḥ
a atandrito varṣati bhūritejāḥ
saṃnādayann antarikṣaṃ divaṃ ca
c atandrito brahmacaryaṃ cacāra
śreṣṭhatvam icchan balabhid devatānām
a hitvā sukhaṃ manasaś ca priyāṇi
tena śakraḥ karmaṇā śraiṣṭhyam āpa
c satyaṃ dharmaṃ pālayann apramatto
damaṃ titikṣāṃ samatāṃ priyaṃ ca
e etāni sarvāṇy upasevamāno
devarājyaṃ maghavān prāpa mukhyam
a bṛhaspatir brahmacaryaṃ cacāra
samāhitaḥ saṃśitātmā yathāvat
c hitvā sukhaṃ pratirudhyendriyāṇi
tena devānām agamad gauravaṃ saḥ
a nakṣatrāṇi karmaṇāmutra bhānti
rudrādityā vasavo 'thāpi viśve
c yamo rājā vaiśravaṇaḥ kubero
gandharvayakṣāpsarasaś ca śubhrāḥ
e brahmacaryaṃ vedavidyāḥ kriyāś ca
niṣevamāṇā munayo 'mutra bhānti
a jānann imaṃ sarvalokasya dharmaṃ
brāhmaṇānāṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ viśāṃ ca
c sa kasmāt tvaṃ jānatāṃ jñānavān san
vyāyacchase saṃjaya kauravārthe
a āmnāyeṣu nityasaṃyogam asya
tathāśvamedhe rājasūye ca viddhi
c saṃyujyate dhanuṣā varmaṇā ca
hastatrāṇai rathaśastraiś ca bhūyaḥ
a te ced ime kauravāṇām upāyam
adhigaccheyur avadhenaiva pārthāḥ
c dharmatrāṇaṃ puṇyam eṣāṃ kṛtaṃ syād
ārye vṛtte bhīmasenaṃ nigṛhya
a te cet pitrye karmaṇi vartamānā
āpadyeran diṣṭavaśena mṛtyum
c yathāśaktyā pūrayantaḥ svakarma
tad apy eṣāṃ nidhanaṃ syāt praśastam
a utāho tvaṃ manyase sarvam eva
rājñāṃ yuddhe vartate dharmatantram
c ayuddhe vā vartate dharmatantraṃ
tathaiva te vācam imāṃ śṛṇomi
a cāturvarṇyasya prathamaṃ vibhāgam
avekṣya tvaṃ saṃjaya svaṃ ca karma
c niśamyātho pāṇḍavānāṃ svakarma
praśaṃsa vā ninda vā yā matis te
a adhīyīta brāhmaṇo 'tho yajeta
dadyād iyāt tīrthamukhyāni caiva
c adhyāpayed yājayec cāpi yājyān
pratigrahān vā viditān pratīcchet
d adhīyīta kṣatriyo 'tho yajeta
d dadyād dhanaṃ na tu yāceta kiṃ cit
d na yājayen na tu cādhyāpayīta
d evaṃ smṛtaḥ kṣatradharmaḥ purāṇaḥ
a tathā rājanyo rakṣaṇaṃ vai prajānāṃ
kṛtvā dharmeṇāpramatto 'tha dattvā
c yajñair iṣṭvā sarvavedān adhītya
dārān kṛtvā puṇyakṛd āvased gṛhān
d sa dharmātmā dharmam adhītya puṇyaṃ
d yad icchayā vrajati brahmalokam
a vaiśyo 'dhītya kṛṣigorakṣapaṇyair
vittaṃ cinvan pālayann apramattaḥ
c priyaṃ kurvan brāhmaṇakṣatriyāṇāṃ
dharmaśīlaḥ puṇyakṛd āvased gṛhān
a paricaryā vandanaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ
nādhīyīta pratiṣiddho 'sya yajñaḥ
c nityotthito bhūtaye 'tandritaḥ syād
eṣa smṛtaḥ śūdradharmaḥ purāṇaḥ
a etān rājā pālayann apramatto
niyojayan sarvavarṇān svadharme
c akāmātmā samavṛttiḥ prajāsu
nādhārmikān anurudhyeta kāmān
a śreyāṃs tasmād yadi vidyeta kaś cid
abhijñātaḥ sarvadharmopapannaḥ
b yatrāpramatto rakṣati bhūmipālo
b niyojayan sveṣu dharmeṣu varṇān
c sa taṃ duṣṭam anuśiṣyāt prajānan
na ced gṛdhyed iti tasmin na sādhu
a yadā gṛdhyet parabhūmiṃ nṛśaṃso
vidhiprakopād balam ādadānaḥ
c tato rājñāṃ bhavitā yuddham etat
tatra jātaṃ varma śastraṃ dhanuś ca
e indreṇedaṃ dasyuvadhāya karma
utpāditaṃ varma śastraṃ dhanuś ca
f tatra puṇyaṃ dasyuvadhena labhyate
f so 'yaṃ doṣaḥ kurubhis tīvrarūpaḥ
f adharmajñair dharmam abudhyamānaiḥ
f prādurbhūtaḥ saṃjaya tan na sādhu
f tatra rājā dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ saputro
f dhanaṃ haret pāṇḍavānām akasmāt
f nāvekṣante rājadharmaṃ purāṇaṃ
f tadanvayāḥ kuravaḥ sarva eva
a steno hared yatra dhanaṃ hy adṛṣṭaḥ
prasahya vā yatra hareta dṛṣṭaḥ
c ubhau garhyau bhavataḥ saṃjayaitau
kiṃ vai pṛthak tvaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrasya putre
e yo 'yaṃ lobhān manyate dharmam etaṃ
yam icchate manyuvaśānugāmī
e svadharmaṃ vai paravittāpahārān
e nāsau dharmaḥ steyam āhur vidhijñāḥ
a bhāgaḥ punaḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ niviṣṭas
taṃ no 'kasmād ādadīran pare vai
c asmin pade yudhyatāṃ no vadho 'pi
ślāghyaḥ pitryaḥ pararājyād viśiṣṭaḥ
e etān dharmān kauravāṇāṃ purāṇān
ācakṣīthāḥ saṃjaya rājyamadhye
a ye te mandā mṛtyuvaśābhipannāḥ
samānītā dhārtarāṣṭreṇa mūḍhāḥ
c idaṃ punaḥ karma pāpīya eva
sabhāmadhye paśya vṛttaṃ kurūṇām
a priyāṃ bhāryāṃ draupadīṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ
yaśasvinīṃ śīlavṛttopapannām
c yad upekṣanta kuravo bhīṣmamukhyāḥ
kāmānugenoparuddhāṃ rudantīm
d kāmātmāno mandabuddher viceṣṭāṃ
a taṃ cet tadā te sakumāravṛddhā
avārayiṣyan kuravaḥ sametāḥ
c mama priyaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭro 'kariṣyat
putrāṇāṃ ca kṛtam asyābhaviṣyat
a duḥśāsanaḥ prātilomyān nināya
sabhāmadhye śvaśurāṇāṃ ca kṛṣṇām
c sā tatra nītā karuṇāny avocan
nānyaṃ kṣattur nātham adṛṣṭa kaṃ cit
a kārpaṇyād eva sahitās tatra rājño
nāśaknuvan prativaktuṃ sabhāyām
c ekaḥ kṣattā dharmyam arthaṃ bruvāṇo
dharmaṃ buddhvā pratyuvācālpabuddhim
a anuktvā tvaṃ dharmam evaṃ sabhāyām
athecchase pāṇḍavasyopadeṣṭum
c kṛṣṇā tv etat karma cakāra śuddhaṃ
suduṣkaraṃ tad dhi sabhāṃ sametya
e yena kṛcchrāt pāṇḍavān ujjahāra
tathātmānaṃ naur iva sāgaraughāt
a yatrābravīt sūtaputraḥ sabhāyāṃ
kṛṣṇāṃ sthitāṃ śvaśurāṇāṃ samīpe
c na te gatir vidyate yājñaseni
prapadyedānīṃ dhārtarāṣṭrasya veśma
e parājitās te patayo na santi
patiṃ cānyaṃ bhāmini tvaṃ vṛṇīṣva
a yo bībhatsor hṛdaye prauḍha āsīd
asthipracchinmarmaghātī sughoraḥ
c karṇāc charo vāṅmayas tigmatejāḥ
pratiṣṭhito hṛdaye phalgunasya
a kṛṣṇājināni paridhit samānān
duḥśāsanaḥ kaṭukāny abhyabhāṣat
c ete sarve ṣaṇḍhatilā vinaṣṭāḥ
kṣayaṃ gatā narakaṃ dīrghakālam
a gāndhārarājaḥ śakunir nikṛtyā
yad abravīd dyūtakāle sa pārthān
c parājito nakulaḥ kiṃ tavāsti
kṛṣṇayā tvaṃ dīvya vai yājñasenyā
a jānāsi tvaṃ saṃjaya sarvam etad
dyūte 'vācyaṃ vākyam evaṃ yathoktam
c svayaṃ tv ahaṃ prārthaye tatra gantuṃ
samādhātuṃ kāryam etad vipannam
d jānāsi tvaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrasya mohaṃ
d durātmanaḥ pāpavaśānugasya
a ahāpayitvā yadi pāṇḍavārthaṃ
śamaṃ kurūṇām atha cec careyam
c puṇyaṃ ca me syāc caritaṃ mahodayaṃ
mucyeraṃś ca kuravo mṛtyupāśāt
a api vācaṃ bhāṣamāṇasya kāvyāṃ
dharmārāmām arthavatīm ahiṃsrām
c avekṣeran dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ samakṣaṃ
māṃ ca prāptaṃ kuravaḥ pūjayeyuḥ
a ato 'nyathā rathinā phalgunena
bhīmena caivāhavadaṃśitena
c parāsiktān dhārtarāṣṭrāṃs tu viddhi
pradahyamānān karmaṇā svena mandān
a parājitān pāṇḍaveyāṃs tu vāco
raudrarūpā bhāṣate dhārtarāṣṭraḥ
c gadāhasto bhīmaseno 'pramatto
duryodhanaṃ smārayitvā hi kāle
a suyodhano manyumayo mahādrumaḥ
skandhaḥ karṇaḥ śakunis tasya śākhāḥ
c duḥśāsanaḥ puṣpaphale samṛddhe
mūlaṃ rājā dhṛtarāṣṭro 'manīṣī
a yudhiṣṭhiro dharmamayo mahādrumaḥ
skandho 'rjuno bhīmaseno 'sya śākhāḥ
c mādrīputrau puṣpaphale samṛddhe
mūlaṃ tv ahaṃ brahma ca brāhmaṇāś ca
a vanaṃ rājā dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ saputro
vyāghrā vane saṃjaya pāṇḍaveyāḥ
b dhārtarāṣṭro vanaṃ rājā vyāghrāḥ pāṇḍusutā matāḥ
b latādharmā dhṛtarāṣṭrasya putrā
b naravyāghrāḥ saṃjaya pāṇḍaveyāḥ
b siṃhābhiguptaṃ na vanaṃ vinaśyet
b siṃho na naśyeta vanābhiguptaḥ
b vanaṃ rājā dhṛtarāṣṭro vane vyāghrāś ca pāṇḍavāḥ
c mā vanaṃ chindhi savyāghraṃ mā vyāghrān nīnaśo vanāt
a nirvano vadhyate vyāghro nirvyāghraṃ chidyate vanam
c tasmād vyāghro vanaṃ rakṣed vanaṃ vyāghraṃ ca pālayet
a latādharmā dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ śālāḥ saṃjaya pāṇḍavāḥ
c na latā vardhate jātu anāśritya mahādrumam
a sthitāḥ śuśrūṣituṃ pārthāḥ sthitā yoddhum ariṃdamāḥ
c yatkṛtyaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrasya tat karotu narādhipaḥ
a sthitāḥ śame mahātmānaḥ pāṇḍavā dharmacāriṇaḥ
c yodhāḥ samṛddhās tad vidvan nācakṣīthā yathātatham
 saṃjaya uvāca
a āmantraye tvā naradevadeva
gacchāmy ahaṃ pāṇḍava svasti te 'stu
c kaccin na vācā vṛjinaṃ hi kiṃ cid
uccāritaṃ me manaso 'bhiṣaṅgāt
a janārdanaṃ bhīmasenārjunau ca
mādrīsutau sātyakiṃ cekitānam
c āmantrya gacchāmi śivaṃ sukhaṃ vaḥ
saumyena māṃ paśyata cakṣuṣā nṛpāḥ
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a anujñātaḥ saṃjaya svasti gaccha
na no 'kārṣīr apriyaṃ jātu kiṃ cit
c vidmaś ca tvā te ca vayaṃ ca sarve
śuddhātmānaṃ madhyagataṃ sabhāstham
a āpto dūtaḥ saṃjaya supriyo 'si
kalyāṇavāk śīlavān dṛṣṭimāṃś ca
c na muhyes tvaṃ saṃjaya jātu matyā
na ca krudhyer ucyamāno 'pi tathyam
a na marmagāṃ jātu vaktāsi rūkṣāṃ
nopastutiṃ kaṭukāṃ nota śuktām
c dharmārāmām arthavatīm ahiṃsrām
etāṃ vācaṃ tava jānāmi sūta
a tvam eva naḥ priyatamo 'si dūta
ihāgacched viduro vā dvitīyaḥ
c abhīkṣṇadṛṣṭo 'si purā hi nas tvaṃ
dhanaṃjayasyātmasamaḥ sakhāsi
a ito gatvā saṃjaya kṣipram eva
upātiṣṭhethā brāhmaṇān ye tadarhāḥ
c viśuddhavīryāṃś caraṇopapannān
kule jātān sarvadharmopapannān
a svādhyāyino brāhmaṇā bhikṣavaś ca
tapasvino ye ca nityā vaneṣu
c abhivādyā vai madvacanena vṛddhās
tathetareṣāṃ kuśalaṃ vadethāḥ
a purohitaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrasya rājña
ācāryāś ca ṛtvijo ye ca tasya
c taiś ca tvaṃ tāta sahitair yathārhaṃ
saṃgacchethāḥ kuśalenaiva sūta
d aśrotriyā ye ca vasanti vṛddhā
d manasvinaḥ śīlabalopapannāḥ
d āśaṃsanto 'smākam anusmaranto
d yathāśakti dharmamātrāṃ carantaḥ
d ślāghasva māṃ kuśalinaṃ sma tebhyo
d hy anāmayaṃ tāta pṛccher jaghanyam
d tato 'vyagras tanmanāḥ prāñjaliś ca
d kuryā namo madvacanena tebhyaḥ
d ye jīvanti vyavahāreṇa rāṣṭre
d ye pālayanto nivasanti rāṣṭre
d kṛṣīvalā bibhrati ye ca lokaṃ
d teṣāṃ sarveṣāṃ kuśalaṃ sma pṛccheḥ
a ācārya iṣṭo 'napago vidheyo
vedān īpsan brahmacaryaṃ cacāra
c yo 'straṃ catuṣpāt punar eva cakre
droṇaḥ prasanno 'bhivādyo yathārham
a adhītavidyaś caraṇopapanno
yo 'straṃ catuṣpāt punar eva cakre
c gandharvaputrapratimaṃ tarasvinaṃ
tam aśvatthāmānaṃ kuśalaṃ sma pṛccheḥ
a śāradvatasyāvasathaṃ sma gatvā
mahārathasyāstravidāṃ varasya
c tvaṃ mām abhīkṣṇaṃ parikīrtayan vai
kṛpasya pādau saṃjaya pāṇinā spṛśeḥ
a yasmiñ śauryam ānṛśaṃsyaṃ tapaś ca
prajñā śīlaṃ śrutisattve dhṛtiś ca
b nivedayāsmāsu yathānuvṛttam
c pādau gṛhītvā kurusattamasya
bhīṣmasya māṃ tatra nivedayethāḥ
a prajñācakṣur yaḥ praṇetā kurūṇāṃ
bahuśruto vṛddhasevī manīṣī
c tasmai rājñe sthavirāyābhivādya
ācakṣīthāḥ saṃjaya mām arogam
a jyeṣṭhaḥ putro dhṛtarāṣṭrasya mando
mūrkhaḥ śaṭhaḥ saṃjaya pāpaśīlaḥ
c praśāstā vai pṛthivī yena sarvā
suyodhanaṃ kuśalaṃ tāta pṛccheḥ
a bhrātā kanīyān api tasya mandas
tathāśīlaḥ saṃjaya so 'pi śaśvat
c maheṣvāsaḥ śūratamaḥ kurūṇāṃ
duḥśāsanaṃ kuśalaṃ tāta pṛccheḥ
d tathaiva ye tasya vaśānugāś ca
d ye cāpy anye pārthivāś ca pradhānāḥ
d tebhyo yathārhaṃ kuśalaṃ sma sarvaṃ
d tathā vācyaṃ madvacanād dhi sūta
a vṛndārakaṃ kavim artheṣv amūḍhaṃ
mahāprajñaṃ sarvadharmopapannam
c na tasya yuddhaṃ rocate vai kadā cid
vaiśyāputraṃ kuśalaṃ tāta pṛccheḥ
a nikartane devane yo 'dvitīyaś
channopadhaḥ sādhudevī matākṣaḥ
c yo durjayo devitavyena saṃkhye
sa citrasenaḥ kuśalaṃ tāta vācyaḥ
a yasya kāmo vartate nityam eva
nānyaḥ śamād bhāratānām iti sma
c sa bāhlikānām ṛṣabho manasvī
purā yathā mābhivadet prasannaḥ
a guṇair anekaiḥ pravaraiś ca yukto
vijñānavān naiva ca niṣṭhuro yaḥ
c snehād amarṣaṃ sahate sadaiva
sa somadattaḥ pūjanīyo mato me
a arhattamaḥ kuruṣu saumadattiḥ
sa no bhrātā saṃjaya matsakhā ca
c maheṣvāso rathinām uttamo yaḥ
sahāmātyaḥ kuśalaṃ tasya pṛccheḥ
d bhūriśravās tāta nipātayodhī
d maheṣvāso rathinām uttamo 'gryaḥ
d gatvā sma taṃ madvacanena brūyāḥ
d śalyaṃ tathā madvacanāt pratītaḥ
d maheṣvāso rathinām uttamo 'gryaḥ
d samaḥ śalo rakṣitā pṛṣṭham asya
d hrīniṣedho devitā vai matākṣaḥ
d satyavrataḥ purumitro jayaś ca
d ye prasthānaṃ tatra me nābhyanandaṃs
d teṣāṃ sarveṣāṃ kuśalaṃ tāta pṛccheḥ
a ye caivānye kurumukhyā yuvānaḥ
putrāḥ pautrā bhrātaraś caiva ye naḥ
c yaṃ yam eṣāṃ yena yenābhigaccher
anāmayaṃ madvacanena vācyaḥ
a ye rājānaḥ pāṇḍavāyodhanāya
samānītā dhārtarāṣṭreṇa ke cit
c vasātayaḥ śālvakāḥ kekayāś ca
tathāmbaṣṭhā ye trigartāś ca mukhyāḥ
a prācyodīcyā dākṣiṇātyāś ca śūrās
tathā pratīcyāḥ pārvatīyāś ca sarve
c anṛśaṃsāḥ śīlavṛttopapannās
teṣāṃ sarveṣāṃ kuśalaṃ tāta pṛccheḥ
a hastyārohā rathinaḥ sādinaś ca
padātayaś cāryasaṃghā mahāntaḥ
c ākhyāya māṃ kuśalinaṃ sma teṣām
anāmayaṃ paripṛccheḥ samagrān
a tathā rājño hy arthayuktān amātyān
dauvārikān ye ca senāṃ nayanti
c āyavyayaṃ ye gaṇayanti yuktā
arthāṃś ca ye mahataś cintayanti
a gāndhārarājaḥ śakuniḥ pārvatīyo
nikartane yo 'dvitīyo 'kṣadevī
c mānaṃ kurvan dhārtarāṣṭrasya sūta
mithyābuddheḥ kuśalaṃ tāta pṛccheḥ
a yaḥ pāṇḍavān ekarathena vīraḥ
samutsahaty apradhṛṣyān vijetum
c yo muhyatāṃ mohayitādvitīyo
vaikartanaṃ kuśalaṃ tāta pṛccheḥ
a sa eva bhaktaḥ sa guruḥ sa bhṛtyaḥ
sa vai pitā sa ca mātā suhṛc ca
c agādhabuddhir viduro dīrghadarśī
sa no mantrī kuśalaṃ tāta pṛccheḥ
d vṛddhāṃ gāndhārīṃ samupetya saṃjaya
d kuntyā dvitīyām abhivādya pṛccheḥ
a vṛddhāḥ striyo yāś ca guṇopapannā
yā jñāyante saṃjaya mātaras tāḥ
c tābhiḥ sarvābhiḥ sahitābhiḥ sametya
strībhir vṛddhābhir abhivādaṃ vadethāḥ
a kaccit putrā jīvaputrāḥ susamyag
vartante vo vṛttim anṛśaṃsarūpām
c iti smoktvā saṃjaya brūhi paścād
ajātaśatruḥ kuśalī saputraḥ
a yā no bhāryāḥ saṃjaya vettha tatra
tāsāṃ sarvāsāṃ kuśalaṃ tāta pṛccheḥ
c susaṃguptāḥ surabhayo 'navadyāḥ
kaccid gṛhān āvasathāpramattāḥ
d ākhyāya māṃ kuśalinaṃ sma tebhyo
d hy anāmayaṃ saṃjaya tāta pṛccheḥ
a kaccid vṛttiṃ śvaśureṣu bhadrāḥ
kalyāṇīṃ vartadhvam anṛśaṃsarūpām
c yathā ca vaḥ syuḥ patayo 'nukūlās
tathā vṛttim ātmanaḥ sthāpayadhvam
a yā naḥ snuṣāḥ saṃjaya vettha tatra
prāptāḥ kulebhyaś ca guṇopapannāḥ
c prajāvatyo brūhi sametya tāś ca
yudhiṣṭhiro vo 'bhyavadat prasannaḥ
a kanyāḥ svajethāḥ sadaneṣu saṃjaya
anāmayaṃ madvacanena pṛṣṭvā
c kalyāṇā vaḥ santu patayo 'nukūlā
yūyaṃ patīnāṃ bhavatānukūlāḥ
a alaṃkṛtā vastravatyaḥ sugandhā
abībhatsāḥ sukhitā bhogavatyaḥ
c laghu yāsāṃ darśanaṃ vāk ca laghvī
veśastriyaḥ kuśalaṃ tāta pṛccheḥ
a dāsīputrā ye ca dāsāḥ kurūṇāṃ
tadāśrayā bahavaḥ kubjakhañjāḥ
c ākhyāya māṃ kuśalinaṃ sma tebhyo
anāmayaṃ paripṛccher jaghanyam
a kaccid vṛttir vartate vai purāṇī
kaccid bhogān dhārtarāṣṭro dadāti
c aṅgahīnān kṛpaṇān vāmanāṃś ca
ānṛśaṃsyād dhṛtarāṣṭro bibharti
a andhāś ca sarve sthavirās tathaiva
hastājīvā bahavo ye 'tra santi
c ākhyāya māṃ kuśalinaṃ sma teṣām
anāmayaṃ paripṛccher jaghanyam
a mā bhaiṣṭa duḥkhena kujīvitena
nūnaṃ kṛtaṃ paralokeṣu pāpam
c nigṛhya śatrūn suhṛdo 'nugṛhya
vāsobhir annena ca vo bhariṣye
d na cāpy etac chakyam ekena vaktuṃ
d nānādeśyā bahavo jātisaṃghāḥ
d viproṣito bālavad draṣṭum icchan
d namasye 'haṃ saṃjaya bhaimasenān
d te me yathā vācam imāṃ yathoktāṃ
d tvayocyamānāṃ śṛṇuyus tathā kuru
a santy eva me brāhmaṇebhyaḥ kṛtāni
bhāvīny atho no bata vartayanti
c paśyāmy ahaṃ yuktarūpāṃs tathaiva
tām eva siddhiṃ śrāvayethā nṛpaṃ tam
a ye cānāthā durbalāḥ sarvakālam
ātmany eva prayatante 'tha mūḍhāḥ
c tāṃś cāpi tvaṃ kṛpaṇān sarvathaiva
asmadvākyāt kuśalaṃ tāta pṛccheḥ
a ye cāpy anye saṃśritā dhārtarāṣṭrān
nānādigbhyo 'bhyāgatāḥ sūtaputra
c dṛṣṭvā tāṃś caivārhataś cāpi sarvān
saṃpṛcchethāḥ kuśalaṃ cāvyayaṃ ca
a evaṃ sarvānāgatābhyāgatāṃś ca
rājño dūtān sarvadigbhyo 'bhyupetān
c pṛṣṭvā sarvān kuśalaṃ tāṃś ca sūta
paścād ahaṃ kuśalī teṣu vācyaḥ
a na hīdṛśāḥ santy apare pṛthivyāṃ
ye yodhakā dhārtarāṣṭreṇa labdhāḥ
c dharmas tu nityo mama dharma eva
mahābalaḥ śatrunibarhaṇāya
a idaṃ punar vacanaṃ dhārtarāṣṭraṃ
suyodhanaṃ saṃjaya śrāvayethāḥ
c yas te śarīre hṛdayaṃ dunoti
kāmaḥ kurūn asapatno 'nuśiṣyām
a na vidyate yuktir etasya kā cin
naivaṃvidhāḥ syāma yathā priyaṃ te
c dadasva vā śakrapuraṃ mamaiva
yudhyasva vā bhāratamukhya vīra
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a uta santam asantaṃ ca bālaṃ vṛddhaṃ ca saṃjaya
c utābalaṃ balīyāṃsaṃ dhātā prakurute vaśe
a uta bālāya pāṇḍityaṃ paṇḍitāyota bālatām
c dadāti sarvam īśānaḥ purastāc chukram uccaran
a alaṃ vijñāpanāya syād ācakṣīthā yathātatham
c atho mantraṃ mantrayitvā anyonyenātihṛṣṭavat
a gāvalgaṇe kurūn gatvā dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ mahābalam
c abhivādyopasaṃgṛhya tataḥ pṛccher anāmayam
a brūyāś cainaṃ tvam āsīnaṃ kurubhiḥ parivāritam
c tavaiva rājan vīryeṇa sukhaṃ jīvanti pāṇḍavāḥ
a tava prasādād bālās te prāptā rājyam ariṃdama
c rājye tān sthāpayitvāgre nopekṣīr vinaśiṣyataḥ
a sarvam apy etad ekasya nālaṃ saṃjaya kasya cit
c tāta saṃhatya jīvāmo mā dviṣadbhyo vaśaṃ gamaḥ
a tathā bhīṣmaṃ śāṃtanavaṃ bhāratānāṃ pitāmaham
c śirasābhivadethās tvaṃ mama nāma prakīrtayan
a abhivādya ca vaktavyas tato 'smākaṃ pitāmahaḥ
c bhavatā śaṃtanor vaṃśo nimagnaḥ punar uddhṛtaḥ
a sa tvaṃ kuru tathā tāta svamatena pitāmaha
c yathā jīvanti te pautrāḥ prītimantaḥ parasparam
a tathaiva viduraṃ brūyāḥ kurūṇāṃ mantradhāriṇam
c ayuddhaṃ saumya bhāṣasva hitakāmo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a atho suyodhanaṃ brūyā rājaputram amarṣaṇam
c madhye kurūṇām āsīnam anunīya punaḥ punaḥ
a apaśyan mām upekṣantaṃ kṛṣṇām ekāṃ sabhāgatām
c tadduḥkham atitikṣāma mā vadhīṣma kurūn iti
a evaṃ pūrvāparān kleśān atitikṣanta pāṇḍavāḥ
c yathā balīyasaḥ santas tat sarvaṃ kuravo viduḥ
a yan naḥ prāvrājayaḥ saumya ajinaiḥ prativāsitān
c tadduḥkham atitikṣāma mā vadhīṣma kurūn iti
a yat tat sabhāyām ākramya kṛṣṇāṃ keśeṣv adharṣayat
c duḥśāsanas te 'numate tac cāsmābhir upekṣitam
a yathocitaṃ svakaṃ bhāgaṃ labhemahi paraṃtapa
c nivartaya paradravye buddhiṃ gṛddhāṃ nararṣabha
a śāntir evaṃ bhaved rājan prītiś caiva parasparam
c rājyaikadeśam api naḥ prayaccha śamam icchatām
a kuśasthalaṃ vṛkasthalam āsandī vāraṇāvatam
c avasānaṃ bhaved atra kiṃ cid eva tu pañcamam
a bhrātṝṇāṃ dehi pañcānāṃ grāmān pañca suyodhana
c śāntir no 'stu mahāprājña jñātibhiḥ saha saṃjaya
a bhrātā bhrātaram anvetu pitā putreṇa yujyatām
c smayamānāḥ samāyāntu pāñcālāḥ kurubhiḥ saha
a akṣatān kurupāñcālān paśyema iti kāmaye
c sarve sumanasas tāta śāmyāma bharatarṣabha
a alam eva śamāyāsmi tathā yuddhāya saṃjaya
c dharmārthayor alaṃ cāhaṃ mṛdave dāruṇāya ca
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a anujñātaḥ pāṇḍavena prayayau saṃjayas tadā
c śāsanaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrasya sarvaṃ kṛtvā mahātmanaḥ
d tatas tu saṃjayaḥ kṣipram ekāhnaiva paraṃtapa
d yāti sma hāstinapuraṃ niśākāle samāviśat
a saṃprāpya hāstinapuraṃ śīghraṃ ca praviveśa ha
c antaḥpuram upasthāya dvāḥsthaṃ vacanam abravīt
a ācakṣva māṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrāya dvāḥstha
upāgataṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ sakāśāt
b ācakṣva dhṛtarāṣṭrāya dvāḥstha māṃ samupāgatam
b sakāśāt pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ saṃjayaṃ mā ciraṃ kṛthāḥ
c jāgarti ced abhivades tvaṃ hi kṣattaḥ
praviśeyaṃ vidito bhūmipasya
d nivedyam atrātyayikaṃ hi me 'sti
d dvāḥstho 'tha śrutvā nṛpatiṃ jagāda
d jāgarti ced abhivādyasya pādau
d nivedyāhaṃ pāṇḍavoktiṃ sayuktim
 dvāḥstha uvāca
a saṃjayo 'yaṃ bhūmipate namas te
didṛkṣayā dvāram upāgatas te
c prāpto dūtaḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ sakāśāt
praśādhi rājan kim ayaṃ karotu
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a ācakṣva māṃ sukhinaṃ kālyam asmai
praveśyatāṃ svāgataṃ saṃjayāya
c na cāham etasya bhavāmy akālyaḥ
sa me kasmād dvāri tiṣṭheta kṣattaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tataḥ praviśyānumate nṛpasya
mahad veśma prājñaśūrāryaguptam
c siṃhāsanasthaṃ pārthivam āsasāda
vaicitravīryaṃ prāñjaliḥ sūtaputraḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a saṃjayo 'haṃ bhūmipate namas te
prāpto 'smi gatvā naradeva pāṇḍavān
c abhivādya tvāṃ pāṇḍuputro manasvī
yudhiṣṭhiraḥ kuśalaṃ cānvapṛcchat
a sa te putrān pṛcchati prīyamāṇaḥ
kaccit putraiḥ prīyase naptṛbhiś ca
c tathā suhṛdbhiḥ sacivaiś ca rājan
ye cāpi tvām upajīvanti taiś ca
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a abhyetya tvāṃ tāta vadāmi saṃjaya
ajātaśatruṃ ca sukhena pārtham
c kaccit sa rājā kuśalī saputraḥ
sahāmātyaḥ sānujaḥ kauravāṇām
 saṃjaya uvāca
a sahāmātyaḥ kuśalī pāṇḍuputro
bhūyaś cāto yac ca te 'gre mano 'bhūt
c nirṇiktadharmārthakaro manasvī
bahuśruto dṛṣṭimāñ śīlavāṃś ca
a paraṃ dharmāt pāṇḍavasyānṛśaṃsyaṃ
dharmaḥ paro vittacayān mato 'sya
c sukhapriye dharmahīne na pārtho
'nurudhyate bhārata tasya viddhi
d akurvataḥ sidhyati cāpi sarvaṃ
d tasmād āhuḥ puruṣaṃ karmaṇo 'nyat
a paraprayuktaḥ puruṣo viceṣṭate
sūtraprotā dārumayīva yoṣā
c imaṃ dṛṣṭvā niyamaṃ pāṇḍavasya
manye paraṃ karma daivaṃ manuṣyāt
a imaṃ ca dṛṣṭvā tava karmadoṣaṃ
pādodarkaṃ ghoram avarṇarūpam
c yāvan naraḥ kāmayate 'tikālyaṃ
tāvan naro 'yaṃ labhate praśaṃsām
a ajātaśatrus tu vihāya pāpaṃ
jīrṇāṃ tvacaṃ sarpa ivāsamarthām
c virocate 'hāryavṛttena dhīro
yudhiṣṭhiras tvayi pāpaṃ visṛjya
a aṅgātmanaḥ karma nibodha rājan
dharmārthayuktād āryavṛttād apetam
c upakrośaṃ ceha gato 'si rājan
noheś ca pāpaṃ prasajed amutra
a sa tvam arthaṃ saṃśayitaṃ vinā tair
āśaṃsase putravaśānugo 'dya
c adharmaśabdaś ca mahān pṛthivyāṃ
nedaṃ karma tvatsamaṃ bhāratāgrya
a hīnaprajño dauṣkuleyo nṛśaṃso
dīrghavairī kṣatravidyāsv adhīraḥ
c evaṃdharmā nāpadaḥ saṃtitīrṣed
dhīnavīryo yaś ca bhaved aśiṣṭaḥ
a kule jāto dharmavān yo yaśasvī
bahuśrutaḥ sukhajīvī yatātmā
c dharmārthayor grathitayor bibharti
nānyatra diṣṭasya vaśād upaiti
a kathaṃ hi mantrāgryadharo manīṣī
dharmārthayor āpadi saṃpraṇetā
c evaṃyuktaḥ sarvamantrair ahīno
anānṛśaṃsyaṃ karma kuryād amūḍhaḥ
a tavāpīme mantravidaḥ sametya
samāsate karmasu nityayuktāḥ
c teṣām ayaṃ balavān niścayaś ca
kurukṣayārthe nirayo vyapādi
a akālikaṃ kuravo nābhaviṣyan
pāpena cet pāpam ajātaśatruḥ
c icchej jātu tvayi pāpaṃ visṛjya
nindā ceyaṃ tava loke 'bhaviṣyat
a kim anyatra viṣayād īśvarāṇāṃ
yatra pārthaḥ paralokaṃ dadarśa
c atyakrāmat sa tathā saṃmataḥ syān
na saṃśayo nāsti manuṣyakāraḥ
a etān guṇān karmakṛtān avekṣya
bhāvābhāvau vartamānāv anityau
c balir hi rājā pāram avindamāno
nānyat kālāt kāraṇaṃ tatra mene
a cakṣuḥ śrotre nāsikā tvak ca jihvā
jñānasyaitāny āyatanāni jantoḥ
c tāni prītāny eva tṛṣṇākṣayānte
tāny avyatho duḥkhahīnaḥ praṇudyāt
a na tv eva manye puruṣasya karma
saṃvartate suprayuktaṃ yathāvat
c mātuḥ pituḥ karmaṇābhiprasūtaḥ
saṃvardhate vidhivad bhojanena
a priyāpriye sukhaduḥkhe ca rājan
nindāpraśaṃse ca bhajeta enam
c paras tv enaṃ garhayate 'parādhe
praśaṃsate sādhuvṛttaṃ tam eva
a sa tvā garhe bhāratānāṃ virodhād
anto nūnaṃ bhavitāyaṃ prajānām
c no ced idaṃ tava karmāparādhāt
kurūn dahet kṛṣṇavartmeva kakṣam
a tvam evaiko jātaputreṣu rājan
vaśaṃ gantā sarvaloke narendra
c kāmātmanāṃ ślāghase dyūtakāle
nānyac chamāt paśya vipākam asya
a anāptānāṃ pragrahāt tvaṃ narendra
tathāptānāṃ nigrahāc caiva rājan
c bhūmiṃ sphītāṃ durbalatvād anantāṃ
na śaktas tvaṃ rakṣituṃ kauraveya
a anujñāto rathavegāvadhūtaḥ
śrānto nipadye śayanaṃ nṛsiṃha
c prātaḥ śrotāraḥ kuravaḥ sabhāyām
ajātaśatror vacanaṃ sametāḥ
d dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
d anujñāto 'syāvasathaṃ paraihi
d prapadyasva śayanaṃ sūtaputra
d prātaḥ śrotāraḥ kuravaḥ sabhāyām
d ajātaśatror vacanaṃ tvayoktam
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a dvāḥsthaṃ prāha mahāprājño dhṛtarāṣṭro mahīpatiḥ
c viduraṃ draṣṭum icchāmi tam ihānaya māciram
a prahito dhṛtarāṣṭreṇa dūtaḥ kṣattāram abravīt
c īśvaras tvāṃ mahārājo mahāprājña didṛkṣati
a evam uktas tu viduraḥ prāpya rājaniveśanam
c abravīd dhṛtarāṣṭrāya dvāḥstha māṃ prativedaya
 dvāḥstha uvāca
a viduro 'yam anuprāpto rājendra tava śāsanāt
c draṣṭum icchati te pādau kiṃ karotu praśādhi mām
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a praveśaya mahāprājñaṃ viduraṃ dīrghadarśinam
c ahaṃ hi vidurasyāsya nākālyo jātu darśane
 dvāḥstha uvāca
a praviśāntaḥpuraṃ kṣattar mahārājasya dhīmataḥ
c na hi te darśane 'kālyo jātu rājā bravīti mām
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tataḥ praviśya viduro dhṛtarāṣṭraniveśanam
c abravīt prāñjalir vākyaṃ cintayānaṃ narādhipam
d evam uktaḥ praviśyātha kṣattā rājānam abravīt
a viduro 'haṃ mahāprājña saṃprāptas tava śāsanāt
c yadi kiṃ cana kartavyam ayam asmi praśādhi mām
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a saṃjayo vidura prāpto garhayitvā ca māṃ gataḥ
c ajātaśatroḥ śvo vākyaṃ sabhāmadhye sa vakṣyati
a tasyādya kuruvīrasya na vijñātaṃ vaco mayā
c tan me dahati gātrāṇi tad akārṣīt prajāgaram
a jāgrato dahyamānasya śreyo yad iha paśyasi
c tad brūhi tvaṃ hi nas tāta dharmārthakuśalo hy asi
a yataḥ prāptaḥ saṃjayaḥ pāṇḍavebhyo
na me yathāvan manasaḥ praśāntiḥ
c sarvendriyāṇy aprakṛtiṃ gatāni
kiṃ vakṣyatīty eva hi me 'dya cintā
d tan me brūhi vidura sarvaṃ yathāvat
d sāntvaṃ tasmai sarvam ajātaśatroḥ
d yathā ca nas tāta hitaṃ bhaveta
d prājñāś ca sarve sukhino bhaveyuḥ
 vidura uvāca
a abhiyuktaṃ balavatā durbalaṃ hīnasādhanam
c hṛtasvaṃ kāminaṃ coram āviśanti prajāgarāḥ
a kaccid etair mahādoṣair na spṛṣṭo 'si narādhipa
c kaccin na paravitteṣu gṛdhyan viparitapyase
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a śrotum icchāmi te dharmyaṃ paraṃ naiḥśreyasaṃ vacaḥ
c asmin rājarṣivaṃśe hi tvam ekaḥ prājñasaṃmataḥ
 vidura uvāca
 rājā lakṣaṇasaṃpannas trailokyasyāpi yo bhavet
 preṣyas te preṣitaś caiva dhṛtarāṣṭra yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
 viparītataraś ca tvaṃ bhāgadheyena saṃmataḥ
 arciṣā prajñayā caiva dharmātmā dharmakovidaḥ
 ānṛśaṃsyād anukrośād dharmāt satyaparākramāt
 gurutvaṃ tvayi saṃprekṣya bahūn kleśāṃs titikṣate
 duryodhane saubaleye karṇe duḥśāsane tathā
 eteṣv aiśvaryam ādhāya kathaṃ tvaṃ bhūtim icchasi
 ātmajñānaṃ samārambhas titikṣā dharmanityatā
 vāksaṃyamaś ca dānaṃ ca naiteṣv etāni kṛtsnaśaḥ
 ekasmād vṛkṣād yajñapātrāṇi rājan
 sruk ca droṇī voḍhanī pīḍanī ca
 etad rājan bruvato me nibodha
 ekasmāt puruṣāj jāyate 'sac ca sac ca
a niṣevate praśastāni ninditāni na sevate
c anāstikaḥ śraddadhāna etat paṇḍitalakṣaṇam
a krodho harṣaś ca darpaś ca hrīstambho mānyamānitā
c yam arthān nāpakarṣanti sa vai paṇḍita ucyate
d yo 'nyathā santam ātmānam anyathā pratipadyate
d kitavena kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ caureṇātmāpahāriṇā
a yasya kṛtyaṃ na jānanti mantraṃ vā mantritaṃ pare
c kṛtam evāsya jānanti sa vai paṇḍita ucyate
a yasya kṛtyaṃ na vighnanti śītam uṣṇaṃ bhayaṃ ratiḥ
c samṛddhir asamṛddhir vā sa vai paṇḍita ucyate
a yasya saṃsāriṇī prajñā dharmārthāv anuvartate
c kāmād arthaṃ vṛṇīte yaḥ sa vai paṇḍita ucyate
d kāmād arthaṃ vṛṇīte yo mokṣād arthaṃ sa vindati
d rājanītiṃ samīkṣyātha sa vai paṇḍita ucyate
a yathāśakti cikīrṣanti yathāśakti ca kurvate
c na kiṃ cid avamanyante paṇḍitā bharatarṣabha
a kṣipraṃ vijānāti ciraṃ śṛṇoti
vijñāya cārthaṃ bhajate na kāmāt
c nāsaṃpṛṣṭo vyupayuṅkte parārthe
tat prajñānaṃ prathamaṃ paṇḍitasya
a nāprāpyam abhivāñchanti naṣṭaṃ necchanti śocitum
c āpatsu ca na muhyanti narāḥ paṇḍitabuddhayaḥ
a niścitya yaḥ prakramate nāntar vasati karmaṇaḥ
c avandhyakālo vaśyātmā sa vai paṇḍita ucyate
a āryakarmaṇi rajyante bhūtikarmāṇi kurvate
c hitaṃ ca nābhyasūyanti paṇḍitā bharatarṣabha
a na hṛṣyaty ātmasaṃmāne nāvamānena tapyate
c gāṅgo hrada ivākṣobhyo yaḥ sa paṇḍita ucyate
a tattvajñaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ yogajñaḥ sarvakarmaṇām
c upāyajño manuṣyāṇāṃ naraḥ paṇḍita ucyate
a pravṛttavāk citrakatha ūhavān pratibhānavān
c āśu granthasya vaktā ca sa vai paṇḍita ucyate
a śrutaṃ prajñānugaṃ yasya prajñā caiva śrutānugā
c asaṃbhinnāryamaryādaḥ paṇḍitākhyāṃ labheta saḥ
a aśrutaś ca samunnaddho daridraś ca mahāmanāḥ
c arthāṃś cākarmaṇā prepsur mūḍha ity ucyate budhaiḥ
a svam arthaṃ yaḥ parityajya parārtham anutiṣṭhati
c mithyā carati mitrārthe yaś ca mūḍhaḥ sa ucyate
d yaḥ prāpya mānuṣaṃ janma mokṣadvāram apāvṛtam
d gṛheṣu sajjate mūḍhas tam ārūḍhacyutaṃ viduḥ
a akāmān kāmayati yaḥ kāmayānān paridviṣan
c balavantaṃ ca yo dveṣṭi tam āhur mūḍhacetasam
a amitraṃ kurute mitraṃ mitraṃ dveṣṭi hinasti ca
c karma cārabhate duṣṭaṃ tam āhur mūḍhacetasam
a saṃsārayati kṛtyāni sarvatra vicikitsate
c ciraṃ karoti kṣiprārthe sa mūḍho bharatarṣabha
d śrāddhaṃ pitṛbhyo na dadāti daivatāni na cārcati
d suhṛn mitraṃ na labhate tam āhur mūḍhalakṣaṇam
a anāhūtaḥ praviśati apṛṣṭo bahu bhāṣate
c viśvasaty apramatteṣu mūḍhacetā narādhamaḥ
a paraṃ kṣipati doṣeṇa vartamānaḥ svayaṃ tathā
c yaś ca krudhyaty anīśaḥ san sa ca mūḍhatamo naraḥ
a ātmano balam ajñāya dharmārthaparivarjitam
c alabhyam icchan naiṣkarmyān mūḍhabuddhir ihocyate
a aśiṣyaṃ śāsti yo rājan yaś ca śūnyam upāsate
c kadaryaṃ bhajate yaś ca tam āhur mūḍhacetasam
a arthaṃ mahāntam āsādya vidyām aiśvaryam eva vā
c vicaraty asamunnaddho yaḥ sa paṇḍita ucyate
a ekaḥ saṃpannam aśnāti vas te vāsaś ca śobhanam
c yo 'saṃvibhajya bhṛtyebhyaḥ ko nṛśaṃsataras tataḥ
a ekaḥ pāpāni kurute phalaṃ bhuṅkte mahājanaḥ
c bhoktāro vipramucyante kartā doṣeṇa lipyate
a ekaṃ hanyān na vā hanyād iṣur mukto dhanuṣmatā
c buddhir buddhimatotsṛṣṭā hanyād rāṣṭraṃ sarājakam
a ekayā dve viniścitya trīṃś caturbhir vaśe kuru
c pañca jitvā viditvā ṣaṭ sapta hitvā sukhī bhava
a ekaṃ viṣaraso hanti śastreṇaikaś ca vadhyate
c sarāṣṭraṃ saprajaṃ hanti rājānaṃ mantravisravaḥ
a ekaḥ svādu na bhuñjīta ekaś cārthān na cintayet
c eko na gacched adhvānaṃ naikaḥ supteṣu jāgṛyāt
a ekam evādvitīyaṃ tad yad rājan nāvabudhyase
c satyaṃ svargasya sopānaṃ pārāvārasya naur iva
a ekaḥ kṣamāvatāṃ doṣo dvitīyo nopalabhyate
c yad enaṃ kṣamayā yuktam aśaktaṃ manyate janaḥ
d so 'sya doṣo na mantavyaḥ kṣamā hi paramaṃ balam
d kṣamā guṇo hy aśaktānāṃ śaktānāṃ bhūṣaṇaṃ kṣamā
d kṣamā vaśīkṛtir loke kṣamayā kiṃ na sādhyate
d śāntikhaḍgaḥ kare yasya kiṃ kariṣyati durjanaḥ
d atṛṇe patito vahniḥ svayam evopaśāmyati
d akṣamāvān paraṃ doṣair ātmānaṃ caiva yojayet
a eko dharmaḥ paraṃ śreyaḥ kṣamaikā śāntir uttamā
c vidyaikā paramā dṛṣṭir ahiṃsaikā sukhāvahā
a dvāv imau grasate bhūmiḥ sarpo bilaśayān iva
c rājānaṃ cāviroddhāraṃ brāhmaṇaṃ cāpravāsinam
d pṛthivyāṃ sāgarāntāyāṃ dvāv imau puruṣādhamau
a dve karmaṇī naraḥ kurvann asmiṃl loke virocate
c abruvan paruṣaṃ kiṃ cid asato nārthayaṃs tathā
a dvāv imau puruṣavyāghra parapratyayakāriṇau
c striyaḥ kāmitakāminyo lokaḥ pūjitapūjakaḥ
a dvāv imau kaṇṭakau tīkṣṇau śarīrapariśoṣaṇau
c yaś cādhanaḥ kāmayate yaś ca kupyaty anīśvaraḥ
d dvāv imau puruṣau loke sūryamaṇḍalabhedinau
d parivrāḍyogayuktaś ca raṇe cābhimukho hataḥ
d dvāv imau na virājete viparītena karmaṇā
d gṛhasthaś ca nirārambhaḥ kāryavāṃś caiva bhikṣukaḥ
a dvāv imau puruṣau rājan svargasyopari tiṣṭhataḥ
c prabhuś ca kṣamayā yukto daridraś ca pradānavān
a nyāyāgatasya dravyasya boddhavyau dvāv atikramau
c apātre pratipattiś ca pātre cāpratipādanam
d dvāv ambhasi niveṣṭavyau gale baddhvā dṛḍhāṃ śilām
d dhanavantam adātāraṃ daridraṃ cātapasvinam
a trayo nyāyā manuṣyāṇāṃ śrūyante bharatarṣabha
c kanīyān madhyamaḥ śreṣṭha iti vedavido viduḥ
a trividhāḥ puruṣā rājann uttamādhamamadhyamāḥ
c niyojayed yathāvat tāṃs trividheṣv eva karmasu
a traya evādhanā rājan bhāryā dāsas tathā sutaḥ
c yat te samadhigacchanti yasya te tasya tad dhanam
d haraṇaṃ ca parasvānāṃ paradārābhimarśanam
d suhṛdaś ca parityāgas trayo doṣāḥ kṣayāvahāḥ
d trividhaṃ narakasyedaṃ dvāraṃ nāśanam ātmanaḥ
d kāmaḥ krodhas tathā lobhas tasmād etat trayaṃ tyajet
d bhaktaṃ ca bhajamānaṃ ca tavāsmīti ca vādinam
d trīn etāñ śaraṇaṃ prāptān viṣame 'pi na saṃtyajet
d varapradānaṃ rājyaṃ ca putrajanma ca bhārata
d śatroś ca mokṣaṇaṃ kṛcchrāt trīṇi caikaṃ ca tatsamam
a catvāri rājñā tu mahābalena
varjyāny āhuḥ paṇḍitas tāni vidyāt
c alpaprajñaiḥ saha mantraṃ na kuryān
na dīrghasūtrair alasaiś cāraṇaiś ca
a catvāri te tāta gṛhe vasantu
śriyābhijuṣṭasya gṛhasthadharme
c vṛddho jñātir avasannaḥ kulīnaḥ
sakhā daridro bhaginī cānapatyā
a catvāry āha mahārāja sadyaskāni bṛhaspatiḥ
c pṛcchate tridaśendrāya tānīmāni nibodha me
a devatānāṃ ca saṃkalpam anubhāvaṃ ca dhīmatām
c vinayaṃ kṛtavidyānāṃ vināśaṃ pāpakarmaṇām
d catvāri karmāṇy abhayaṃkarāṇi
d bhayaṃ prayacchanty ayathākṛtāni
d mānāgnihotram uta mānamaunaṃ
d mānenādhītam uta mānayajñaḥ
a pañcāgnayo manuṣyeṇa paricaryāḥ prayatnataḥ
c pitā mātāgnir ātmā ca guruś ca bharatarṣabha
a pañcaiva pūjayaṃl loke yaśaḥ prāpnoti kevalam
c devān pitṝn manuṣyāṃś ca bhikṣūn atithipañcamān
a pañca tvānugamiṣyanti yatra yatra gamiṣyasi
c mitrāṇy amitrā madhyasthā upajīvyopajīvinaḥ
a pañcendriyasya martyasya chidraṃ ced ekam indriyam
c tato 'sya sravati prajñā dṛteḥ pādād ivodakam
a ṣaḍ doṣāḥ puruṣeṇeha hātavyā bhūtim icchatā
c nidrā tandrī bhayaṃ krodha ālasyaṃ dīrghasūtratā
a ṣaḍ imān puruṣo jahyād bhinnāṃ nāvam ivārṇave
c apravaktāram ācāryam anadhīyānam ṛtvijam
a arakṣitāraṃ rājānaṃ bhāryāṃ cāpriyavādinīm
c grāmakāmaṃ ca gopālaṃ vanakāmaṃ ca nāpitam
a ṣaḍ eva tu guṇāḥ puṃsā na hātavyāḥ kadā cana
c satyaṃ dānam anālasyam anasūyā kṣamā dhṛtiḥ
d ṣaḍ imāni vinaśyanti muhūrtam anavekṣaṇāt
d gāvaḥ sevā kṛṣir bhāryā vidyā vṛṣalasaṃgatiḥ
d ṣaḍ ete hy avamanyante nityaṃ pūrvopakāriṇam
d ācāryaṃ śikṣitāḥ śiṣyāḥ kṛtadārāś ca mātaram
d nārīṃ vigatakāmās tu kṛtārthāś ca prayojanam
d nāvaṃ nistīrṇakāntārā āturāś ca cikitsakam
d ārogyam ānṛṇyam avipravāsaḥ
d sadbhir manuṣyaiḥ saha saṃprayogaḥ
d svapratyayā vṛttir abhītavāsaḥ
d ṣaḍ jīvalokasya sukhāni rājan
d īrṣur ghṛṇī na saṃtuṣṭaḥ krodhano nityaśaṅkitaḥ
d parabhāgyopajīvī ca ṣaḍ ete nityaduḥkhitāḥ
d arthāgamo nityam arogitā ca
d priyā ca bhāryā priyavādinī ca
d vaśyaś ca putro 'rthakarī ca vidyā
d ṣaḍ jīvalokasya sukhāni rājan
a ṣaṇṇām ātmani nityānām aiśvaryaṃ yo 'dhigacchati
c na sa pāpaiḥ kuto 'narthair yujyate vijitendriyaḥ
a ṣaḍ ime ṣaṭsu jīvanti saptamo nopalabhyate
c corāḥ pramatte jīvanti vyādhiteṣu cikitsakāḥ
a pramadāḥ kāmayāneṣu yajamāneṣu yājakāḥ
c rājā vivadamāneṣu nityaṃ mūrkheṣu paṇḍitāḥ
a sapta doṣāḥ sadā rājñā hātavyā vyasanodayāḥ
c prāyaśo yair vinaśyanti kṛtamūlāś ca pārthivāḥ
a striyo 'kṣā mṛgayā pānaṃ vākpāruṣyaṃ ca pañcamam
c mahac ca daṇḍapāruṣyam arthadūṣaṇam eva ca
a aṣṭau pūrvanimittāni narasya vinaśiṣyataḥ
c brāhmaṇān prathamaṃ dveṣṭi brāhmaṇaiś ca virudhyate
a brāhmaṇasvāni cādatte brāhmaṇāṃś ca jighāṃsati
c ramate nindayā caiṣāṃ praśaṃsāṃ nābhinandati
a naitān smarati kṛtyeṣu yācitaś cābhyasūyati
b yasyaitāni nimittāni tasyāsan naḥ parābhavaḥ
c etān doṣān naraḥ prājño buddhyā buddhvā vivarjayet
a aṣṭāv imāni harṣasya navanītāni bhārata
c vartamānāni dṛśyante tāny eva susukhāny api
a samāgamaś ca sakhibhir mahāṃś caiva dhanāgamaḥ
c putreṇa ca pariṣvaṅgaḥ saṃnipātaś ca maithune
a samaye ca priyālāpaḥ svayūtheṣu ca saṃnatiḥ
c abhipretasya lābhaś ca pūjā ca janasaṃsadi
a navadvāram idaṃ veśma tristhūṇaṃ pañcasākṣikam
c kṣetrajñādhiṣṭhitaṃ vidvān yo veda sa paraḥ kaviḥ
a daśa dharmaṃ na jānanti dhṛtarāṣṭra nibodha tān
c mattaḥ pramatta unmattaḥ śrāntaḥ kruddho bubhukṣitaḥ
a tvaramāṇaś ca bhīruś ca lubdhaḥ kāmī ca te daśa
c tasmād eteṣu bhāveṣu na prasajjeta paṇḍitaḥ
a atraivodāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanam
c putrārtham asurendreṇa gītaṃ caiva sudhanvanā
a yaḥ kāmamanyū prajahāti rājā
pātre pratiṣṭhāpayate dhanaṃ ca
c viśeṣavic chrutavān kṣiprakārī
taṃ sarvalokaḥ kurute pramāṇam
a jānāti viśvāsayituṃ manuṣyān
vijñātadoṣeṣu dadhāti daṇḍam
c jānāti mātrāṃ ca tathā kṣamāṃ ca
taṃ tādṛśaṃ śrīr juṣate samagrā
a sudurbalaṃ nāvajānāti kaṃ cid
yukto ripuṃ sevate buddhipūrvam
c na vigrahaṃ rocayate balasthaiḥ
kāle ca yo vikramate sa dhīraḥ
a prāpyāpadaṃ na vyathate kadā cid
udyogam anvicchati cāpramattaḥ
c duḥkhaṃ ca kāle sahate jitātmā
dhuraṃdharas tasya jitāḥ sapatnāḥ
a anarthakaṃ vipravāsaṃ gṛhebhyaḥ
pāpaiḥ saṃdhiṃ paradārābhimarśam
c dambhaṃ stainyaṃ paiśunaṃ madyapānaṃ
na sevate yaḥ sa sukhī sadaiva
a na saṃrambheṇārabhate 'rthavargam
ākāritaḥ śaṃsati tathyam eva
c na mātrārthe rocayate vivādaṃ
nāpūjitaḥ kupyati cāpy amūḍhaḥ
a na yo 'bhyasūyaty anukampate ca
na durbalaḥ prātibhāvyaṃ karoti
c nātyāha kiṃ cit kṣamate vivādaṃ
sarvatra tādṛg labhate praśaṃsām
a yo noddhataṃ kurute jātu veṣaṃ
na pauruṣeṇāpi vikatthate 'nyān
c na mūrcchitaḥ kaṭukāny āha kiṃ cit
priyaṃ sadā taṃ kurute jano 'pi
a na vairam uddīpayati praśāntaṃ
na darpam ārohati nāstam eti
c na durgato 'smīti karoti manyuṃ
tam āryaśīlaṃ param āhur agryam
a na sve sukhe vai kurute praharṣaṃ
nānyasya duḥkhe bhavati pratītaḥ
c dattvā na paścāt kurute 'nutāpaṃ
na katthate satpuruṣāryaśīlaḥ
a deśācārān samayāñ jātidharmān
bubhūṣate yas tu parāvarajñaḥ
c sa tatra tatrādhigataḥ sadaiva
mahājanasyādhipatyaṃ karoti
a dambhaṃ mohaṃ matsaraṃ pāpakṛtyaṃ
rājadviṣṭaṃ paiśunaṃ pūgavairam
c mattonmattair durjanaiś cāpi vādaṃ
yaḥ prajñāvān varjayet sa pradhānaḥ
a damaṃ śaucaṃ daivataṃ maṅgalāni
prāyaścittaṃ vividhāṃl lokavādān
c etāni yaḥ kurute naityakāni
tasyotthānaṃ devatā rādhayanti
a samair vivāhaṃ kurute na hīnaiḥ
samaiḥ sakhyaṃ vyavahāraṃ kathāś ca
c guṇair viśiṣṭāṃś ca purodadhāti
vipaścitas tasya nayāḥ sunītāḥ
a mitaṃ bhuṅkte saṃvibhajyāśritebhyo
mitaṃ svapity amitaṃ karma kṛtvā
c dadāty amitreṣv api yācitaḥ saṃs
tam ātmavantaṃ prajahaty anarthāḥ
a cikīrṣitaṃ viprakṛtaṃ ca yasya
nānye janāḥ karma jānanti kiṃ cit
c mantre gupte samyag anuṣṭhite ca
svalpo nāsya vyathate kaś cid arthaḥ
a yaḥ sarvabhūtapraśame niviṣṭaḥ
satyo mṛdur dānakṛc chuddhabhāvaḥ
c atīva saṃjñāyate jñātimadhye
mahāmaṇir jātya iva prasannaḥ
a ya ātmanāpatrapate bhṛśaṃ naraḥ
sa sarvalokasya gurur bhavaty uta
c anantatejāḥ sumanāḥ samāhitaḥ
svatejasā sūrya ivāvabhāsate
a vane jātāḥ śāpadagdhasya rājñaḥ
pāṇḍoḥ putrāḥ pañca pañcendrakalpāḥ
c tvayaiva bālā vardhitāḥ śikṣitāś ca
tavādeśaṃ pālayanty āmbikeya
a pradāyaiṣām ucitaṃ tāta rājyaṃ
sukhī putraiḥ sahito modamānaḥ
c na devānāṃ nāpi ca mānuṣāṇāṃ
bhaviṣyasi tvaṃ tarkaṇīyo narendra
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a jāgrato dahyamānasya yat kāryam anupaśyasi
c tad brūhi tvaṃ hi nas tāta dharmārthakuśalaḥ śuciḥ
a tvaṃ māṃ yathāvad vidura praśādhi
prajñāpūrvaṃ sarvam ajātaśatroḥ
c yan manyase pathyam adīnasattva
śreyaskaraṃ brūhi tad vai kurūṇām
a pāpāśaṅkī pāpam evānupaśyan
pṛcchāmi tvāṃ vyākulenātmanāham
c kave tan me brūhi sarvaṃ yathāvan
manīṣitaṃ sarvam ajātaśatroḥ
 vidura uvāca
 sulabhāḥ puruṣā rājan satataṃ priyavādinaḥ
 apriyasya ca pathyasya vaktā śrotā ca durlabhaḥ
a śubhaṃ vā yadi vā pāpaṃ dveṣyaṃ vā yadi vā priyam
c apṛṣṭas tasya tad brūyād yasya necchet parābhavam
a tasmād vakṣyāmi te rājan bhavam icchan kurūn prati
c vacaḥ śreyaskaraṃ dharmyaṃ bruvatas tan nibodha me
a mithyopetāni karmāṇi sidhyeyur yāni bhārata
c anupāyaprayuktāni mā sma teṣu manaḥ kṛthāḥ
a tathaiva yogavihitaṃ na sidhyet karma yan nṛpa
c upāyayuktaṃ medhāvī na tatra glapayen manaḥ
a anubandhān avekṣeta sānubandheṣu karmasu
c saṃpradhārya ca kurvīta na vegena samācaret
a anubandhaṃ ca saṃprekṣya vipākāṃś caiva karmaṇām
c utthānam ātmanaś caiva dhīraḥ kurvīta vā na vā
a yaḥ pramāṇaṃ na jānāti sthāne vṛddhau tathā kṣaye
c kośe janapade daṇḍe na sa rājye 'vatiṣṭhate
a yas tv etāni pramāṇāni yathoktāny anupaśyati
c yukto dharmārthayor jñāne sa rājyam adhigacchati
a na rājyaṃ prāptam ity eva vartitavyam asāṃpratam
c śriyaṃ hy avinayo hanti jarā rūpam ivottamam
a bhakṣyottamapraticchannaṃ matsyo baḍiśam āyasam
c rūpābhipātī grasate nānubandham avekṣate
a yac chakyaṃ grasituṃ grasyaṃ grastaṃ pariṇamec ca yat
c hitaṃ ca pariṇāme yat tad adyaṃ bhūtim icchatā
a vanaspater apakvāni phalāni pracinoti yaḥ
c sa nāpnoti rasaṃ tebhyo bījaṃ cāsya vinaśyati
a yas tu pakvam upādatte kāle pariṇataṃ phalam
c phalād rasaṃ sa labhate bījāc caiva phalaṃ punaḥ
a yathā madhu samādatte rakṣan puṣpāṇi ṣaṭpadaḥ
c tadvad arthān manuṣyebhya ādadyād avihiṃsayā
a puṣpaṃ puṣpaṃ vicinvīta mūlacchedaṃ na kārayet
c mālākāra ivārāme na yathāṅgārakārakaḥ
a kiṃ nu me syād idaṃ kṛtvā kiṃ nu me syād akurvataḥ
c iti karmāṇi saṃcintya kuryād vā puruṣo na vā
a anārabhyā bhavanty arthāḥ ke cin nityaṃ tathāgatāḥ
c kṛtaḥ puruṣakāro 'pi bhaved yeṣu nirarthakaḥ
d anarthe caiva niratam arthe caiva parāṅmukham
a kāṃś cid arthān naraḥ prājño laghumūlān mahāphalān
c kṣipram ārabhate kartuṃ na vighnayati tādṛśān
a ṛju paśyati yaḥ sarvaṃ cakṣuṣānupibann iva
c āsīnam api tūṣṇīkam anurajyanti taṃ prajāḥ
d supuṣpitaḥ syād aphalaḥ phalitaḥ syād durāruhaḥ
d apakvaḥ pakvasaṃkāśo na tu śīryeta karhi cit
a cakṣuṣā manasā vācā karmaṇā ca caturvidham
c prasādayati lokaṃ yaḥ taṃ loko 'nuprasīdati
a yasmāt trasyanti bhūtāni mṛgavyādhān mṛgā iva
c sāgarāntām api mahīṃ labdhvā sa parihīyate
a pitṛpaitāmahaṃ rājyaṃ prāptavān svena tejasā
c vāyur abhram ivāsādya bhraṃśayaty anaye sthitaḥ
a dharmam ācarato rājñaḥ sadbhiś caritam āditaḥ
c vasudhā vasusaṃpūrṇā vardhate bhūtivardhanī
a atha saṃtyajato dharmam adharmaṃ cānutiṣṭhataḥ
c pratisaṃveṣṭate bhūmir agnau carmāhitaṃ yathā
a ya eva yatnaḥ kriyate pararāṣṭrāvamardane
c sa eva yatnaḥ kartavyaḥ svarāṣṭraparipālane
a dharmeṇa rājyaṃ vindeta dharmeṇa paripālayet
c dharmamūlāṃ śriyaṃ prāpya na jahāti na hīyate
a apy unmattāt pralapato bālāc ca parisarpataḥ
c sarvataḥ sāram ādadyād aśmabhya iva kāñcanam
a suvyāhṛtāni sudhiyāṃ sukṛtāni tatas tataḥ
c saṃcinvan dhīra āsīta śilāhārī śilaṃ yathā
a gandhena gāvaḥ paśyanti vedaiḥ paśyanti brāhmaṇāḥ
c cāraiḥ paśyanti rājānaś cakṣurbhyām itare janāḥ
a bhūyāṃsaṃ labhate kleśaṃ yā gaur bhavati durduhā
c atha yā suduhā rājan naiva tāṃ vinayanty api
a yad ataptaṃ praṇamati na tat saṃtāpayanty api
c yac ca svayaṃ nataṃ dāru na tat saṃnāmayanty api
a etayopamayā dhīraḥ saṃnameta balīyase
c indrāya sa praṇamate namate yo balīyase
a parjanyanāthāḥ paśavo rājāno mitrabāndhavāḥ
c patayo bāndhavāḥ strīṇāṃ brāhmaṇā vedabāndhavāḥ
a satyena rakṣyate dharmo vidyā yogena rakṣyate
c mṛjayā rakṣyate rūpaṃ kulaṃ vṛttena rakṣyate
a mānena rakṣyate dhānyam aśvān rakṣaty anukramaḥ
c abhīkṣṇadarśanād gāvaḥ striyo rakṣyāḥ kucelataḥ
a na kulaṃ vṛttahīnasya pramāṇam iti me matiḥ
c antyeṣv api hi jātānāṃ vṛttam eva viśiṣyate
a ya īrṣyuḥ paravitteṣu rūpe vīrye kulānvaye
c sukhe saubhāgyasatkāre tasya vyādhir anantakaḥ
a akāryakaraṇād bhītaḥ kāryāṇāṃ ca vivarjanāt
c akāle mantrabhedāc ca yena mādyen na tat pibet
a vidyāmado dhanamadas tṛtīyo 'bhijano madaḥ
c ete madāvaliptānām eta eva satāṃ damāḥ
a asanto 'bhyarthitāḥ sadbhiḥ kiṃ cit kāryaṃ kadā cana
b tāvan na tasya sukṛtaṃ kiṃ cit kāryaṃ kadā cana
c manyante santam ātmānam asantam api viśrutam
a gatir ātmavatāṃ santaḥ santa eva satāṃ gatiḥ
c asatāṃ ca gatiḥ santo na tv asantaḥ satāṃ gatiḥ
a jitā sabhā vastravatā samāśā gomatā jitā
c adhvā jito yānavatā sarvaṃ śīlavatā jitam
a śīlaṃ pradhānaṃ puruṣe tad yasyeha praṇaśyati
c na tasya jīvitenārtho na dhanena na bandhubhiḥ
a āḍhyānāṃ māṃsaparamaṃ madhyānāṃ gorasottaram
c lavaṇottaraṃ daridrāṇāṃ bhojanaṃ bharatarṣabha
a saṃpannataram evānnaṃ daridrā bhuñjate sadā
c kṣut svādutāṃ janayati sā cāḍhyeṣu sudurlabhā
a prāyeṇa śrīmatāṃ loke bhoktuṃ śaktir na vidyate
c daridrāṇāṃ tu rājendra api kāṣṭhaṃ hi jīryate
d yathā yathā mahat tantraṃ vistaraś ca yathā yathā
d tathā tathā mahad duḥkhaṃ sukhaṃ tu na tathā tathā
a avṛttir bhayam antyānāṃ madhyānāṃ maraṇād bhayam
c uttamānāṃ tu martyānām avamānāt paraṃ bhayam
a aiśvaryamadapāpiṣṭhā madāḥ pānamadādayaḥ
c aiśvaryamadamatto hi nāpatitvā vibudhyate
a indriyair indriyārtheṣu vartamānair anigrahaiḥ
c tair ayaṃ tāpyate loko nakṣatrāṇi grahair iva
a yo jitaḥ pañcavargeṇa sahajenātmakarśinā
c āpadas tasya vardhante śuklapakṣa ivoḍurāṭ
a avijitya ya ātmānam amātyān vijigīṣate
c amitrān vājitāmātyaḥ so 'vaśaḥ parihīyate
a ātmānam eva prathamaṃ deśarūpeṇa yo jayet
c tato 'mātyān amitrāṃś ca na moghaṃ vijigīṣate
a vaśyendriyaṃ jitāmātyaṃ dhṛtadaṇḍaṃ vikāriṣu
c parīkṣyakāriṇaṃ dhīram atyantaṃ śrīr niṣevate
a rathaḥ śarīraṃ puruṣasya rājan
nātmā niyantendriyāṇy asya cāśvāḥ
c tair apramattaḥ kuśalaḥ sadaśvair
dāntaiḥ sukhaṃ yāti rathīva dhīraḥ
a etāny anigṛhītāni vyāpādayitum apy alam
c avidheyā ivādāntā hayāḥ pathi kusārathim
a anartham arthataḥ paśyann arthaṃ caivāpy anarthataḥ
c indriyaiḥ prasṛto bālaḥ suduḥkhaṃ manyate sukham
a dharmārthau yaḥ parityajya syād indriyavaśānugaḥ
c śrīprāṇadhanadārebhya kṣipraṃ sa parihīyate
a arthānām īśvaro yaḥ syād indriyāṇām anīśvaraḥ
c indriyāṇām anaiśvaryād aiśvaryād bhraśyate hi saḥ
a ātmanātmānam anvicchen manobuddhīndriyair yataiḥ
c ātmaiva hy ātmano bandhur ātmaiva ripur ātmanaḥ
d bandhur ātmātmanas tasya yenaivātmātmanā jitaḥ
d sa eva niyato bandhuḥ sa eva niyato ripuḥ
a kṣudrākṣeṇeva jālena jhaṣāv apihitāv ubhau
c kāmaś ca rājan krodhaś ca tau prajñānaṃ vilumpataḥ
a samavekṣyeha dharmārthau saṃbhārān yo 'dhigacchati
c sa vai saṃbhṛtasaṃbhāraḥ satataṃ sukham edhate
a yaḥ pañcābhyantarāñ śatrūn avijitya matikṣayān
c jigīṣati ripūn anyān ripavo 'bhibhavanti tam
a dṛśyante hi durātmāno vadhyamānāḥ svakarmabhiḥ
c indriyāṇām anīśatvād rājāno rājyavibhramaiḥ
a asaṃtyāgāt pāpakṛtām apāpāṃs
tulyo daṇḍaḥ spṛśate miśrabhāvāt
c śuṣkeṇārdraṃ dahyate miśrabhāvāt
tasmāt pāpaiḥ saha saṃdhiṃ na kuryāt
a nijān utpatataḥ śatrūn pañca pañcaprayojanān
c yo mohān na nigṛhṇāti tam āpad grasate naram
a anasūyārjavaṃ śaucaṃ saṃtoṣaḥ priyavāditā
c damaḥ satyam anāyāso na bhavanti durātmanām
a ātmajñānam anāyāsas titikṣā dharmanityatā
c vāk caiva guptā dānaṃ ca naitāny antyeṣu bhārata
a ākrośaparivādābhyāṃ vihiṃsanty abudhā budhān
c vaktā pāpam upādatte kṣamamāṇo vimucyate
a hiṃsā balam asādhūnāṃ rājñāṃ daṇḍavidhir balam
c śuśrūṣā tu balaṃ strīṇāṃ kṣamā guṇavatāṃ balam
a vāksaṃyamo hi nṛpate suduṣkaratamo mataḥ
c arthavac ca vicitraṃ ca na śakyaṃ bahu bhāṣitum
a abhyāvahati kalyāṇaṃ vividhā vāk subhāṣitā
c saiva durbhāṣitā rājann anarthāyopapadyate
a saṃrohati śarair viddhaṃ vanaṃ paraśunā hatam
c vācā duruktaṃ bībhatsaṃ na saṃrohati vākkṣatam
a karṇinālīkanārācā nirharanti śarīrataḥ
c vākśalyas tu na nirhartuṃ śakyo hṛdiśayo hi saḥ
a vāksāyakā vadanān niṣpatanti
yair āhataḥ śocati rātryahāni
c parasya nāmarmasu te patanti
tān paṇḍito nāvasṛjet pareṣu
a yasmai devāḥ prayacchanti puruṣāya parābhavam
c buddhiṃ tasyāpakarṣanti so 'pācīnāni paśyati
a buddhau kaluṣabhūtāyāṃ vināśe pratyupasthite
c anayo nayasaṃkāśo hṛdayān nāpasarpati
d na devā yaṣṭim ādāya rakṣanti paśupālavat
d yaṃ hi rakṣitum icchanti buddhyā saṃyojayanti tam
a seyaṃ buddhiḥ parītā te putrāṇāṃ tava bhārata
c pāṇḍavānāṃ virodhena na cainām avabudhyase
a rājā lakṣaṇasaṃpannas trailokyasyāpi yo bhavet
c śiṣyas te śāsitā so 'stu dhṛtarāṣṭra yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a atīva sarvān putrāṃs te bhāgadheyapuraskṛtaḥ
c tejasā prajñayā caiva yukto dharmārthatattvavit
a ānṛśaṃsyād anukrośād yo 'sau dharmabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
c gauravāt tava rājendra bahūn kleśāṃs titikṣati
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a brūhi bhūyo mahābuddhe dharmārthasahitaṃ vacaḥ
c śṛṇvato nāsti me tṛptir vicitrāṇīha bhāṣase
 vidura uvāca
a sarvatīrtheṣu vā snānaṃ sarvabhūteṣu cārjavam
c ubhe ete same syātām ārjavaṃ vā viśiṣyate
a ārjavaṃ pratipadyasva putreṣu satataṃ vibho
c iha kīrtiṃ parāṃ prāpya pretya svargam avāpsyasi
a yāvat kīrtir manuṣyasya puṇyā lokeṣu gīyate
c tāvat sa puruṣavyāghra svargaloke mahīyate
a atrāpy udāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanam
c virocanasya saṃvādaṃ keśinyarthe sudhanvanā
d svayaṃvare sthitā kanyā keśinī nāma nāmataḥ
d rūpeṇāpratimā rājan viśiṣṭapatikāmyayā
d virocano 'tha daiteyas tadā tatrājagāma ha
d prāptum icchaṃs tatas tatra daityendraṃ prāha keśinī
 keśiny uvāca
a kiṃ brāhmaṇāḥ svic chreyāṃso ditijāḥ svid virocana
c atha kena sma paryaṅkaṃ sudhanvā nādhirohati
 virocana uvāca
a prājāpatyā hi vai śreṣṭhā vayaṃ keśini sattamāḥ
c asmākaṃ khalv ime lokāḥ ke devāḥ ke dvijātayaḥ
 keśiny uvāca
a ihaivāssva pratīkṣāva upasthāne virocana
c sudhanvā prātar āgantā paśyeyaṃ vāṃ samāgatau
 virocana uvāca
a tathā bhadre kariṣyāmi yathā tvaṃ bhīru bhāṣase
c sudhanvānaṃ ca māṃ caiva prātar draṣṭāsi saṃgatau
d atītāyāṃ ca śarvaryām udite sūryamaṇḍale
d athājagāma taṃ deśaṃ sudhanvā rājasattama
d virocano yatra vibho keśinyā sahitaḥ sthitaḥ
d sudhanvā ca samāgacchat prāhlādiṃ keśinīṃ tathā
d samāgataṃ dvijaṃ dṛṣṭvā keśinī bharatarṣabha
d pratyutthāyāsanaṃ tasmai pādyam arghyaṃ dadau punaḥ
d etasminn antare tatra sudhanvā pratyadṛśyata
d iti hovāca vacanaṃ virocanam anuttamam
 sudhanvovāca
a anvālabhe hiraṇmayaṃ prāhrāde 'haṃ tavāsanam
c ekatvam upasaṃpanno na tv āseyaṃ tvayā saha
 virocana uvāca
a anvāharantu phalakaṃ kūrcaṃ vāpy atha vā bṛsīm
b na matto hy adhiko 'si tvaṃ guṇato janmato 'pi vā
c sudhanvan na tvam arho 'si mayā saha samāsanam
 sudhanvovāca
 pitāputrau sahāsītāṃ dvau viprau dvau ca pārthivau
 dvau caiva vaiśyau śūdrau ca na tv anyāv itaretaraṃ
a pitāpi te samāsīnam upāsītaiva mām adhaḥ
c bālaḥ sukhaidhito gehe na tvaṃ kiṃ cana budhyase
 virocana uvāca
a hiraṇyaṃ ca gavāśvaṃ ca yad vittam asureṣu naḥ
c sudhanvan vipaṇe tena praśnaṃ pṛcchāva ye viduḥ
 sudhanvovāca
a hiraṇyaṃ ca gavāśvaṃ ca tavaivāstu virocana
c prāṇayos tu paṇaṃ kṛtvā praśnaṃ pṛcchāva ye viduḥ
 virocana uvāca
a āvāṃ kutra gamiṣyāvaḥ prāṇayor vipaṇe kṛte
c na hi deveṣv ahaṃ sthātā na manuṣyeṣu karhi cit
 sudhanvovāca
a pitaraṃ te gamiṣyāvaḥ prāṇayor vipaṇe kṛte
c putrasyāpi sa hetor hi prahrādo nānṛtaṃ vadet
d vidura uvāca
d evaṃ kṛtapaṇau kruddhau tatrābhijagmatus tadā
d virocanasudhanvānau prahrādo yatra tiṣṭhati
d ity uktvā jagmatus tau tu prahrādasya gṛhaṃ prati
d gatvā taṃ dadṛśus tatra daityānām īśvaraṃ tadā
d tāv āgatāv abhiprekṣya prahrādo vismitas tadā
d papracchāgamane hetuṃ ubhayor ditijas tataḥ
 prahrāda uvāca
a imau tau saṃpradṛśyete yābhyāṃ na caritaṃ saha
c āśīviṣāv iva kruddhāv ekamārgam ihāgatau
a kiṃ vai sahaiva carato na purā carataḥ saha
b tat tvāṃ sudhanvan pṛcchāmi mā pṛṣṭam anṛtaṃ vadīḥ
c virocanaitat pṛcchāmi kiṃ te sakhyaṃ sudhanvanā
 virocana uvāca
a na me sudhanvanā sakhyaṃ prāṇayor vipaṇāvahe
c prahrāda tat tvāṃ pṛcchāmi mā praśnam anṛtaṃ vadīḥ
d prahlādaḥ
d na kalmāṣo na kapilo na kṛṣṇo na ca lohitaḥ
d sudhanvā
d aṇīyān kṣuradhārāyāḥ ko dharmaṃ vaktum arhati
d yad yat tattvaṃ vakṣyasi tvaṃ yadi vā nāpi vakṣyasi
d prahlāda praśnam anaghaṃ mūrdhnā te viphaliṣyati
 prahrāda uvāca
a udakaṃ madhuparkaṃ cāpy ānayantu sudhanvane
c brahmann abhyarcanīyo 'si śvetā gauḥ pīvarīkṛtā
 sudhanvovāca
a udakaṃ madhuparkaṃ ca patha evārpitaṃ mama
c prahrāda tvaṃ tu nau praśnaṃ tathyaṃ prabrūhi pṛcchatoḥ
d kiṃ brāhmaṇāḥ svic chreyāṃsa utāho svid virocanaḥ
d satyaṃ prabrūhi daityendra satyaṃ hi paramaṃ tapaḥ
 prahrāda uvāca
a putro vānyo bhavān brahman sākṣye caiva bhavet sthitaḥ
c tayor vivadatoḥ praśnaṃ katham asmadvidho vadet
d viduraḥ
d ādityena sahāyāntaṃ prahlādo haṃsam abravīt
d prahlādaḥ
d dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ mahāprājñaṃ sarvajñaṃ priyadarśanam
d putravān yo bhaved brahman sākṣye cāpi bhavet sthitaḥ
d tayor vivadator haṃsa kathaṃ dharmaḥ pravartate
d sudhanvovāca
d gāṃ pradadyās tv aurasāya yad vānyat syāt priyaṃ dhanam
d dvayor vivadatos tathyaṃ vācyaṃ ca matimaṃs tvayā
a atha yo naiva prabrūyāt satyaṃ vā yadi vānṛtam
c etat sudhanvan pṛcchāmi durvivaktā sma kiṃ vaset
d haṃsaḥ
d pṛṣṭo dharmaṃ na vibrūyād gokarṇaśithilaṃ caran
d dharmād bhraśyati rājaṃs tu nāsya loko 'sti na prajāḥ
d dharma etān saṃrujati yathā nady anukūlajān
d ye dharmam anupaśyantas tūṣṇīṃ dhyāyanta āsate
d śreṣṭho 'rdhaṃ tu haret tatra bhavet pādaś ca kartari
d pādas teṣu sabhāsatsu yatra nindyo na nindyate
d anenā bhavati śreṣṭho mucyante ca sabhāsadaḥ
d kartāram eno gacchec ca nindyo yatra hi nindyate
d prahlādaḥ
d mohād vā caiva kāmād vā mithyāvādaṃ yadi bruvan
d dhṛtarāṣṭra tvāṃ pṛcchāmi durvivaktā tu kāṃ vaset
 sudhanvovāca
a yāṃ rātrim adhivinnā strī yāṃ caivākṣaparājitaḥ
c yāṃ ca bhārābhitaptāṅgo durvivaktā sma tāṃ vaset
a nagare pratiruddhaḥ san bahirdvāre bubhukṣitaḥ
c amitrān bhūyasaḥ paśyan durvivaktā sma tāṃ vaset
d yāṃ ca rātrim abhidrugdho yāṃ ca mitre priye mṛte
d sarvasvena ca yo hīno durvivaktā tu tāṃ vaset
a pañca paśvanṛte hanti daśa hanti gavānṛte
c śatam aśvānṛte hanti sahasraṃ puruṣānṛte
a hanti jātān ajātāṃś ca hiraṇyārthe 'nṛtaṃ vadan
c sarvaṃ bhūmyanṛte hanti mā sma bhūmyanṛtaṃ vadīḥ
 prahrāda uvāca
a mattaḥ śreyān aṅgirā vai sudhanvā tvad virocana
c mātāsya śreyasī mātus tasmāt tvaṃ tena vai jitaḥ
a virocana sudhanvāyaṃ prāṇānām īśvaras tava
c sudhanvan punar icchāmi tvayā dattaṃ virocanam
 sudhanvovāca
a yad dharmam avṛṇīthās tvaṃ na kāmād anṛtaṃ vadīḥ
c punar dadāmi te tasmāt putraṃ prahrāda durlabham
a eṣa prahrāda putras te mayā datto virocanaḥ
c pādaprakṣālanaṃ kuryāt kumāryāḥ saṃnidhau mama
 vidura uvāca
a tasmād rājendra bhūmyarthe nānṛtaṃ vaktum arhasi
c mā gamaḥ sasutāmātyo 'tyayaṃ putrān anubhraman
a na devā yaṣṭim ādāya rakṣanti paśupālavat
c yaṃ tu rakṣitum icchanti buddhyā saṃvibhajanti tam
a yathā yathā hi puruṣaḥ kalyāṇe kurute manaḥ
c tathā tathāsya sarvārthāḥ sidhyante nātra saṃśayaḥ
a na chandāṃsi vṛjināt tārayanti
māyāvinaṃ māyayā vartamānam
c nīḍaṃ śakuntā iva jātapakṣāś
chandāṃsy enaṃ prajahaty antakāle
a mattāpānaṃ kalahaṃ pūgavairaṃ
bhāryāpatyor antaraṃ jñātibhedam
c rājadviṣṭaṃ strīpumāṃsor vivādaṃ
varjyāny āhur yaś ca panthāḥ praduṣṭaḥ
a sāmudrikaṃ vaṇijaṃ corapūrvaṃ
śalākadhūrtaṃ ca cikitsakaṃ ca
c ariṃ ca mitraṃ ca kuśīlavaṃ ca
naitān sākṣyeṣv adhikurvīta sapta
a mānāgnihotram uta mānamaunaṃ
mānenādhītam uta mānayajñaḥ
c etāni catvāry abhayaṃkarāṇi
bhayaṃ prayacchanty ayathākṛtāni
a agāradāhī garadaḥ kuṇḍāśī somavikrayī
c parvakāraś ca sūcī ca mitradhruk pāradārikaḥ
a bhrūṇahā gurutalpī ca yaś ca syāt pānapo dvijaḥ
c atitīkṣṇaś ca kākaś ca nāstiko vedanindakaḥ
a sruvapragrahaṇo vrātyaḥ kīnāśaś cārthavān api
c rakṣety uktaś ca yo hiṃsyāt sarve brahmahaṇaiḥ samāḥ
a tṛṇolkayā jñāyate jātarūpaṃ
yuge bhadro vyavahāreṇa sādhuḥ
c śūro bhayeṣv arthakṛcchreṣu dhīraḥ
kṛcchrāsv āpatsu suhṛdaś cārayaś ca
a jarā rūpaṃ harati hi dhairyam āśā
mṛtyuḥ prāṇān dharmacaryām asūyā
c krodhaḥ śriyaṃ śīlam anāryasevā
hriyaṃ kāmaḥ sarvam evābhimānaḥ
d na krodhino 'rtho na nṛśaṃsasya mitraṃ
d krūrasya na strī sukhino na vidyā
d na kāmino hrīr alasasya kośaḥ
d sarvaṃ tu na syād anavasthitasya
a śrīr maṅgalāt prabhavati prāgalbhyāt saṃpravardhate
c dākṣyāt tu kurute mūlaṃ saṃyamāt pratitiṣṭhati
a aṣṭau guṇāḥ puruṣaṃ dīpayanti
prajñā ca kaulyaṃ ca damaḥ śrutaṃ ca
c parākramaś cābahubhāṣitā ca
dānaṃ yathāśakti kṛtajñatā ca
a etān guṇāṃs tāta mahānubhāvān
eko guṇaḥ saṃśrayate prasahya
c rājā yadā satkurute manuṣyaṃ
sarvān guṇān eṣa guṇo 'tibhāti
a aṣṭau nṛpemāni manuṣyaloke
svargasya lokasya nidarśanāni
c catvāry eṣām anvavetāni sadbhiś
catvāry eṣām anvavayanti santaḥ
a yajño dānam adhyayanaṃ tapaś ca
catvāry etāny anvavetāni sadbhiḥ
c damaḥ satyam ārjavam ānṛśaṃsyaṃ
catvāry etāny anvavayanti santaḥ
d ijyādhyayanadānāni tapaḥ satyaṃ kṣamā ghṛṇā
d alobha iti mārgo 'yaṃ dharmasyāṣṭavidhaḥ smṛtaḥ
d tatra pūrvacaturvargo dambhārtham api sevyate
d uttaras tu caturvargo nāmahātmasu tiṣṭhati
a na sā sabhā yatra na santi vṛddhā
na te vṛddhā ye na vadanti dharmam
c nāsau dharmo yatra na satyam asti
na tat satyaṃ yac chalenānuviddham
a satyaṃ rūpaṃ śrutaṃ vidyā kaulyaṃ śīlaṃ balaṃ dhanam
c śauryaṃ ca citrabhāṣyaṃ ca daśa saṃsargayonayaḥ
d atha yo naiva vibrūyān na satyaṃ nānṛtaṃ vadet
d ye dharmam abhyasūyantas tūṣṇīṃ dhyāyanta āsate
d śreṣṭhaḥ pādaṃ haret tatra bhavet pādaś ca kartari
d pādas teṣu sabhāsatsu yatra nindyo na nindyate
d anenāḥ śreṣṭho bhavati pramucyante sabhāsadaḥ
d eno gacchati kartāraṃ nindārho yatra nindyate
a pāpaṃ kurvan pāpakīrtiḥ pāpam evāśnute phalam
c puṇyaṃ kurvan puṇyakīrtiḥ puṇyam evāśnute phalam
d tasmāt pāpaṃ na kurvīta puruṣaḥ śaṃsitavrataḥ
a pāpaṃ prajñāṃ nāśayati kriyamāṇaṃ punaḥ punaḥ
c naṣṭaprajñaḥ pāpam eva nityam ārabhate naraḥ
a puṇyaṃ prajñāṃ vardhayati kriyamāṇaṃ punaḥ punaḥ
c vṛddhaprajñaḥ puṇyam eva nityam ārabhate naraḥ
d puṇyaṃ kurvan puṇyakīrtiḥ puṇyaṃ sthānaṃ sma gacchati
d tasmāt puṇyaṃ niṣeveta puruṣaḥ susamāhitaḥ
a asūyako dandaśūko niṣṭhuro vairakṛn naraḥ
c sa kṛcchraṃ mahad āpnoti nacirāt pāpam ācaran
a anasūyaḥ kṛtaprajñaḥ śobhanāny ācaran sadā
b pūjāṃ ca mahatīṃ prāpya sa sarvatra virocate
c akṛcchrāt sukham āpnoti sarvatra ca virājate
a prajñām evāgamayati yaḥ prājñebhyaḥ sa paṇḍitaḥ
c prājño hy avāpya dharmārthau śaknoti sukham edhitum
a divasenaiva tat kuryād yena rātrau sukhaṃ vaset
c aṣṭamāsena tat kuryād yena varṣāḥ sukhaṃ vaset
a pūrve vayasi tat kuryād yena vṛddhaḥ sukhaṃ vaset
c yāvajjīvena tat kuryād yena pretya sukhaṃ vaset
a jīrṇam annaṃ praśaṃsanti bhāryāṃ ca gatayauvanām
c śūraṃ vigatasaṃgrāmaṃ gatapāraṃ tapasvinam
a dhanenādharmalabdhena yac chidram apidhīyate
c asaṃvṛtaṃ tad bhavati tato 'nyad avadīryate
a gurur ātmavatāṃ śāstā śāstā rājā durātmanām
c atha pracchannapāpānāṃ śāstā vaivasvato yamaḥ
a ṛṣīṇāṃ ca nadīnāṃ ca kulānāṃ ca mahātmanām
c prabhavo nādhigantavyaḥ strīṇāṃ duścaritasya ca
a dvijātipūjābhirato dātā jñātiṣu cārjavī
c kṣatriyaḥ svargabhāg rājaṃś ciraṃ pālayate mahīm
a suvarṇapuṣpāṃ pṛthivīṃ cinvanti puruṣās trayaḥ
c śūraś ca kṛtavidyaś ca yaś ca jānāti sevitum
a buddhiśreṣṭhāni karmāṇi bāhumadhyāni bhārata
c tāni jaṅghājaghanyāni bhārapratyavarāṇi ca
a duryodhane ca śakunau mūḍhe duḥśāsane tathā
c karṇe caiśvaryam ādhāya kathaṃ tvaṃ bhūtim icchasi
a sarvair guṇair upetāś ca pāṇḍavā bharatarṣabha
c pitṛvat tvayi vartante teṣu vartasva putravat
 vidura uvāca
a atraivodāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanam
c ātreyasya ca saṃvādaṃ sādhyānāṃ ceti naḥ śrutam
a carantaṃ haṃsarūpeṇa maharṣiṃ saṃśitavratam
c sādhyā devā mahāprājñaṃ paryapṛcchanta vai purā
a sādhyā devā vayam asmo maharṣe
dṛṣṭvā bhavantaṃ na śaknumo 'numātum
c śrutena dhīro buddhimāṃs tvaṃ mato naḥ
kāvyāṃ vācaṃ vaktum arhasy udārām
 haṃsa uvāca
a etat kāryam amarāḥ saṃśrutaṃ me
dhṛtiḥ śamaḥ satyadharmānuvṛttiḥ
c granthiṃ vinīya hṛdayasya sarvaṃ
priyāpriye cātmavaśaṃ nayīta
a ākruśyamāno nākrośen manyur eva titikṣitaḥ
b punāti hy ātmanātmānaṃ sukṛtaṃ cāsya vindati
c ākroṣṭāraṃ nirdahati sukṛtaṃ cāsya vindati
a nākrośī syān nāvamānī parasya
mitradrohī nota nīcopasevī
c na cātimānī na ca hīnavṛtto
rūkṣāṃ vācaṃ ruśatīṃ varjayīta
a marmāṇy asthīni hṛdayaṃ tathāsūn
ghorā vāco nirdahantīha puṃsām
c tasmād vācaṃ ruśatīṃ rūkṣarūpāṃ
dharmārāmo nityaśo varjayīta
a aruṃtudaṃ paruṣaṃ rūkṣavācaṃ
vākkaṇṭakair vitudantaṃ manuṣyān
c vidyād alakṣmīkatamaṃ janānāṃ
mukhe nibaddhāṃ nirṛtiṃ vahantam
a paraś ced enam adhividhyeta bāṇair
bhṛśaṃ sutīkṣṇair analārkadīptaiḥ
c viricyamāno 'py atiricyamāno
vidyāt kaviḥ sukṛtaṃ me dadhāti
a yadi santaṃ sevate yady asantaṃ
tapasvinaṃ yadi vā stenam eva
c vāso yathā raṅgavaśaṃ prayāti
tathā sa teṣāṃ vaśam abhyupaiti
a vādaṃ tu yo na pravaden na vādayed
yo nāhataḥ pratihanyān na ghātayet
c yo hantukāmasya na pāpam icchet
tasmai devāḥ spṛhayanty āgatāya
a avyāhṛtaṃ vyāhṛtāc chreya āhuḥ
satyaṃ vaded vyāhṛtaṃ tad dvitīyam
c priyaṃ vaded vyāhṛtaṃ tat tṛtīyaṃ
dharmyaṃ vaded vyāhṛtaṃ tac caturtham
a yādṛśaiḥ saṃvivadate yādṛśāṃś copasevate
c yādṛg icchec ca bhavituṃ tādṛg bhavati pūruṣaḥ
a yato yato nivartate tatas tato vimucyate
c nivartanād dhi sarvato na vetti duḥkham aṇv api
a na jīyate nota jigīṣate 'nyān
na vairakṛc cāpratighātakaś ca
c nindāpraśaṃsāsu samasvabhāvo
na śocate hṛṣyati naiva cāyam
a bhāvam icchati sarvasya nābhāve kurute matim
c satyavādī mṛdur dānto yaḥ sa uttamapūruṣaḥ
a nānarthakaṃ sāntvayati pratijñāya dadāti ca
c rāddhāparāddhe jānāti yaḥ sa madhyamapūruṣaḥ
a duḥśāsanas tūpahantā na śāstā
nāvartate manyuvaśāt kṛtaghnaḥ
c na kasya cin mitram atho durātmā
kalāś caitā adhamasyeha puṃsaḥ
a na śraddadhāti kalyāṇaṃ parebhyo 'py ātmaśaṅkitaḥ
c nirākaroti mitrāṇi yo vai so 'dhamapūruṣaḥ
a uttamān eva seveta prāpte kāle tu madhyamān
c adhamāṃs tu na seveta ya icchec chreya ātmanaḥ
a prāpnoti vai vittam asadbalena
nityotthānāt prajñayā pauruṣeṇa
c na tv eva samyag labhate praśaṃsāṃ
na vṛttam āpnoti mahākulānām
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a mahākulānāṃ spṛhayanti devā
dharmārthavṛddhāś ca bahuśrutāś ca
c pṛcchāmi tvāṃ vidura praśnam etaṃ
bhavanti vai kāni mahākulāni
 vidura uvāca
a tapo damo brahmavit tvaṃ vitānāḥ
puṇyā vivāhāḥ satatānnadānam
c yeṣv evaite sapta guṇā bhavanti
samyag vṛttās tāni mahākulāni
a yeṣāṃ na vṛttaṃ vyathate na yonir
vṛttaprasādena caranti dharmam
c ye kīrtim icchanti kule viśiṣṭāṃ
tyaktānṛtās tāni mahākulāni
a anijyayāvivāhaiś ca vedasyotsādanena ca
c kulāny akulatāṃ yānti dharmasyātikrameṇa ca
a devadravyavināśena brahmasvaharaṇena ca
c kulāny akulatāṃ yānti brāhmaṇātikrameṇa ca
a brāhmaṇānāṃ paribhavāt parivādāc ca bhārata
c kulāny akulatāṃ yānti nyāsāpaharaṇena ca
a kulāni samupetāni gobhiḥ puruṣato 'śvataḥ
c kulasaṃkhyāṃ na gacchanti yāni hīnāni vṛttataḥ
a vṛttatas tv avihīnāni kulāny alpadhanāny api
c kulasaṃkhyāṃ tu gacchanti karṣanti ca mahad yaśaḥ
d vṛttaṃ yatnena saṃrakṣed vittam eti ca yāti ca
d akṣīṇo vittataḥ kṣīṇo vṛttatas tu hato hataḥ
d gobhiḥ paśubhir aśvaiś ca kṛṣyā ca susamṛddhayā
d kulāni na prarohanti yāni hīnāni vṛttataḥ
a mā naḥ kule vairakṛt kaś cid astu
rājāmātyo mā parasvāpahārī
c mitradrohī naikṛtiko 'nṛtī vā
pūrvāśī vā pitṛdevātithibhyaḥ
a yaś ca no brāhmaṇaṃ hanyād yaś ca no brāhmaṇān dviṣet
c na naḥ sa samitiṃ gacched yaś ca no nirvapet kṛṣim
a tṛṇāni bhūmir udakaṃ vāk caturthī ca sūnṛtā
c satām etāni geheṣu nocchidyante kadā cana
a śraddhayā parayā rājann upanītāni satkṛtim
c pravṛttāni mahāprājña dharmiṇāṃ puṇyakarmaṇām
a sūkṣmo 'pi bhāraṃ nṛpate syandano vai
śakto voḍhuṃ na tathānye mahījāḥ
c evaṃ yuktā bhārasahā bhavanti
mahākulīnā na tathānye manuṣyāḥ
a na tan mitraṃ yasya kopād bibheti
yad vā mitraṃ śaṅkitenopacaryam
c yasmin mitre pitarīvāśvasīta
tad vai mitraṃ saṃgatānītarāṇi
a yadi ced apy asaṃbandho mitrabhāvena vartate
c sa eva bandhus tan mitraṃ sā gatis tatparāyaṇam
a calacittasya vai puṃso vṛddhān anupasevataḥ
c pāriplavamater nityam adhruvo mitrasaṃgrahaḥ
a calacittam anātmānam indriyāṇāṃ vaśānugam
c arthāḥ samativartante haṃsāḥ śuṣkaṃ saro yathā
a akasmād eva kupyanti prasīdanty animittataḥ
c śīlam etad asādhūnām abhraṃ pāriplavaṃ yathā
a satkṛtāś ca kṛtārthāś ca mitrāṇāṃ na bhavanti ye
c tān mṛtān api kravyādāḥ kṛtaghnān nopabhuñjate
a arthayed eva mitrāṇi sati vāsati vā dhane
c nānarthayan vijānāti mitrāṇāṃ sāraphalgutām
a saṃtāpād bhraśyate rūpaṃ saṃtāpād bhraśyate balam
c saṃtāpād bhraśyate jñānaṃ saṃtāpād vyādhim ṛcchati
a anavāpyaṃ ca śokena śarīraṃ copatapyate
c amitrāś ca prahṛṣyanti mā sma śoke manaḥ kṛthāḥ
a punar naro mriyate jāyate ca
punar naro hīyate vardhate punaḥ
c punar naro yācati yācyate ca
punar naraḥ śocati śocyate punaḥ
a sukhaṃ ca duḥkhaṃ ca bhavābhavau ca
lābhālābhau maraṇaṃ jīvitaṃ ca
c paryāyaśaḥ sarvam iha spṛśanti
tasmād dhīro naiva hṛṣyen na śocet
a calāni hīmāni ṣaḍindriyāṇi
teṣāṃ yad yad vartate yatra yatra
c tatas tataḥ sravate buddhir asya
chidrodakumbhād iva nityam ambhaḥ
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a tanur ucchaḥ śikhī rājā mithyopacarito mayā
c mandānāṃ mama putrāṇāṃ yuddhenāntaṃ kariṣyati
a nityodvignam idaṃ sarvaṃ nityodvignam idaṃ manaḥ
c yat tat padam anudvignaṃ tan me vada mahāmate
 vidura uvāca
a nānyatra vidyātapasor nānyatrendriyanigrahāt
c nānyatra lobhasaṃtyāgāc chāntiṃ paśyāmi te 'nagha
a buddhyā bhayaṃ praṇudati tapasā vindate mahat
c guruśuśrūṣayā jñānaṃ śāntiṃ tyāgena vindati
a anāśritā dānapuṇyaṃ vedapuṇyam anāśritāḥ
c rāgadveṣavinirmuktā vicarantīha mokṣiṇaḥ
a svadhītasya suyuddhasya sukṛtasya ca karmaṇaḥ
c tapasaś ca sutaptasya tasyānte sukham edhate
a svāstīrṇāni śayanāni prapannā
na vai bhinnā jātu nidrāṃ labhante
c na strīṣu rājan ratim āpnuvanti
na māgadhaiḥ stūyamānā na sūtaiḥ
a na vai bhinnā jātu caranti dharmaṃ
na vai sukhaṃ prāpnuvantīha bhinnāḥ
c na vai bhinnā gauravaṃ mānayanti
na vai bhinnāḥ praśamaṃ rocayanti
a na vai teṣāṃ svadate pathyam uktaṃ
yogakṣemaṃ kalpate nota teṣām
c bhinnānāṃ vai manujendra parāyaṇaṃ
na vidyate kiṃ cid anyad vināśāt
a saṃbhāvyaṃ goṣu saṃpannaṃ saṃbhāvyaṃ brāhmaṇe tapaḥ
c saṃbhāvyaṃ strīṣu cāpalyaṃ saṃbhāvyaṃ jñātito bhayam
a tantavo 'py āyatā nityaṃ tantavo bahulāḥ samāḥ
c bahūn bahutvād āyāsān sahantīty upamā satām
a dhūmāyante vyapetāni jvalanti sahitāni ca
c dhṛtarāṣṭrolmukānīva jñātayo bharatarṣabha
a brāhmaṇeṣu ca ye śūrāḥ strīṣu jñātiṣu goṣu ca
c vṛntād iva phalaṃ pakvaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭra patanti te
a mahān apy ekajo vṛkṣo balavān supratiṣṭhitaḥ
c prasahya eva vātena śākhāskandhaṃ vimarditum
a atha ye sahitā vṛkṣāḥ saṃghaśaḥ supratiṣṭhitāḥ
c te hi śīghratamān vātān sahante 'nyonyasaṃśrayāt
a evaṃ manuṣyam apy ekaṃ guṇair api samanvitam
c śakyaṃ dviṣanto manyante vāyur drumam ivaikajam
a anyonyasamupaṣṭambhād anyonyāpāśrayeṇa ca
c jñātayaḥ saṃpravardhante sarasīvotpalāny uta
a avadhyā brāhmaṇā gāvaḥ striyo bālāś ca jñātayaḥ
c yeṣāṃ cānnāni bhuñjīta ye ca syuḥ śaraṇāgatāḥ
d mahaty apy aparādhe 'pi teṣāṃ daṇḍo visarjanam
a na manuṣye guṇaḥ kaś cid anyo dhanavatām api
c anāturatvād bhadraṃ te mṛtakalpā hi rogiṇaḥ
a avyādhijaṃ kaṭukaṃ śīrṣarogaṃ
pāpānubandhaṃ paruṣaṃ tīkṣṇam ugram
c satāṃ peyaṃ yan na pibanty asanto
manyuṃ mahārāja piba praśāmya
a rogārditā na phalāny ādriyante
na vai labhante viṣayeṣu tattvam
c duḥkhopetā rogiṇo nityam eva
na budhyante dhanabhogān na saukhyam
a purā hy ukto nākaros tvaṃ vaco me
dyūte jitāṃ draupadīṃ prekṣya rājan
c duryodhanaṃ vārayety akṣavatyāṃ
kitavatvaṃ paṇḍitā varjayanti
a na tad balaṃ yan mṛdunā virudhyate
miśro dharmas tarasā sevitavyaḥ
c pradhvaṃsinī krūrasamāhitā śrīr
mṛduprauḍhā gacchati putrapautrān
a dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ pāṇḍavān pālayantu
pāṇḍoḥ sutās tava putrāṃś ca pāntu
c ekārimitrāḥ kuravo hy ekamantrā
jīvantu rājan sukhinaḥ samṛddhāḥ
a meḍhībhūtaḥ kauravāṇāṃ tvam adya
tvayy ādhīnaṃ kurukulam ājamīḍha
c pārthān bālān vanavāsaprataptān
gopāyasva svaṃ yaśas tāta rakṣan
a saṃdhatsva tvaṃ kauravān pāṇḍuputrair
mā te 'ntaraṃ ripavaḥ prārthayantu
c satye sthitās te naradeva sarve
duryodhanaṃ sthāpaya tvaṃ narendra
 vidura uvāca
a saptadaśemān rājendra manuḥ svāyaṃbhuvo 'bravīt
c vaicitravīrya puruṣān ākāśaṃ muṣṭibhir ghnataḥ
a tān evendrasya hi dhanur anāmyaṃ namato 'bravīt
c atho marīcinaḥ pādān anāmyān namatas tathā
a yaś cāśiṣyaṃ śāsati yaś ca kupyate
yaś cātivelaṃ bhajate dviṣantam
c striyaś ca yo 'rakṣati bhadram astu te
yaś cāyācyaṃ yācati yaś ca katthate
a yaś cābhijātaḥ prakaroty akāryaṃ
yaś cābalo balinā nityavairī
c aśraddadhānāya ca yo bravīti
yaś cākāmyaṃ kāmayate narendra
a vadhvā hāsaṃ śvaśuro yaś ca manyate
vadhvā vasann uta yo mānakāmaḥ
c parakṣetre nirvapati yaś ca bījaṃ
striyaṃ ca yaḥ parivadate 'tivelam
a yaś caiva labdhvā na smarāmīty uvāca
dattvā ca yaḥ katthati yācyamānaḥ
c yaś cāsataḥ sāntvam upāsatīha
ete 'nuyānty anilaṃ pāśahastāḥ
a yasmin yathā vartate yo manuṣyas
tasmiṃs tathā vartitavyaṃ sa dharmaḥ
c māyācāro māyayā vartitavyaḥ
sādhv ācāraḥ sādhunā pratyudeyaḥ
d jarā rūpaṃ harati hi dhairyam āśā
d mṛtyuḥ prāṇān dharmacaryām asūyā
d kāmo hriyaṃ vṛttam anāryasevā
d krodhaḥ śriyaṃ sarvam evābhimānaḥ
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a śatāyur uktaḥ puruṣaḥ sarvavedeṣu vai yadā
c nāpnoty atha ca tat sarvam āyuḥ keneha hetunā
 vidura uvāca
a ativādo 'timānaś ca tathātyāgo narādhipa
c krodhaś cātivivitsā ca mitradrohaś ca tāni ṣaṭ
a eta evāsayas tīkṣṇāḥ kṛntanty āyūṃṣi dehinām
c etāni mānavān ghnanti na mṛtyur bhadram astu te
a viśvastasyaiti yo dārān yaś cāpi gurutalpagaḥ
c vṛṣalīpatir dvijo yaś ca pānapaś caiva bhārata
d ādeśakṛd vṛttihantā dvijānāṃ preṣakaś ca yaḥ
a śaraṇāgatahā caiva sarve brahmahaṇaiḥ samāḥ
c etaiḥ sametya kartavyaṃ prāyaścittam iti śrutiḥ
a gṛhī vadānyo 'napaviddhavākyaḥ
śeṣānnabhoktāpy avihiṃsakaś ca
c nānarthakṛt tyaktakaliḥ kṛtajñaḥ
satyo mṛduḥ svargam upaiti vidvān
a sulabhāḥ puruṣā rājan satataṃ priyavādinaḥ
c apriyasya tu pathyasya vaktā śrotā ca durlabhaḥ
a yo hi dharmaṃ vyapāśritya hitvā bhartuḥ priyāpriye
c apriyāṇy āha pathyāni tena rājā sahāyavān
a tyajet kulārthe puruṣaṃ grāmasyārthe kulaṃ tyajet
c grāmaṃ janapadasyārthe ātmārthe pṛthivīṃ tyajet
a āpadarthaṃ dhanaṃ rakṣed dārān rakṣed dhanair api
c ātmānaṃ satataṃ rakṣed dārair api dhanair api
d dyūtam etat purākalpe dṛṣṭaṃ vairakaraṃ nṛṇām
d tasmād dyūtaṃ na seveta hāsyārtham api buddhimān
a uktaṃ mayā dyūtakāle 'pi rājan
naivaṃ yuktaṃ vacanaṃ prātipīya
c tadauṣadhaṃ pathyam ivāturasya
na rocate tava vaicitravīrya
a kākair imāṃś citrabarhān mayūrān
parājaiṣṭhāḥ pāṇḍavān dhārtarāṣṭraiḥ
c hitvā siṃhān kroṣṭukān gūhamānaḥ
prāpte kāle śocitā tvaṃ narendra
a yas tāta na krudhyati sarvakālaṃ
bhṛtyasya bhaktasya hite ratasya
c tasmin bhṛtyā bhartari viśvasanti
na cainam āpatsu parityajanti
a na bhṛtyānāṃ vṛttisaṃrodhanena
bāhyaṃ janaṃ saṃjighṛkṣed apūrvam
c tyajanti hy enam ucitāvaruddhāḥ
snigdhā hy amātyāḥ parihīnabhogāḥ
a kṛtyāni pūrvaṃ parisaṃkhyāya sarvāṇy
āyavyayāv anurūpāṃ ca vṛttim
c saṃgṛhṇīyād anurūpān sahāyān
sahāyasādhyāni hi duṣkarāṇi
a abhiprāyaṃ yo viditvā tu bhartuḥ
sarvāṇi kāryāṇi karoty atandrīḥ
c vaktā hitānām anurakta āryaḥ
śaktijña ātmeva hi so 'nukampyaḥ
d bāṇaḥ śākuniko mantrī ekākī stambhasevakaḥ
d sadyorogī vivādī ca saptaitān sevakāṃs tyajet
a vākyaṃ tu yo nādriyate 'nuśiṣṭaḥ
pratyāha yaś cāpi niyujyamānaḥ
c prajñābhimānī pratikūlavādī
tyājyaḥ sa tādṛk tvarayaiva bhṛtyaḥ
a astabdham aklībam adīrghasūtraṃ
sānukrośaṃ ślakṣṇam ahāryam anyaiḥ
c arogajātīyam udāravākyaṃ
dūtaṃ vadanty aṣṭaguṇopapannam
a na viśvāsāj jātu parasya gehaṃ
gacchen naraś cetayāno vikāle
c na catvare niśi tiṣṭhen nigūḍho
na rājanyāṃ yoṣitaṃ prārthayīta
a na nihnavaṃ satragatasya gacchet
saṃsṛṣṭamantrasya kusaṃgatasya
c na ca brūyān nāśvasāmi tvayīti
sakāraṇaṃ vyapadeśaṃ tu kuryāt
a ghṛṇī rājā puṃścalī rājabhṛtyaḥ
putro bhrātā vidhavā bālaputrā
c senājīvī coddhṛtabhakta eva
vyavahāre vai varjanīyāḥ syur ete
a guṇā daśa snānaśīlaṃ bhajante
balaṃ rūpaṃ svaravarṇapraśuddhiḥ
c sparśaś ca gandhaś ca viśuddhatā ca
śrīḥ saukumāryaṃ pravarāś ca nāryaḥ
a guṇāś ca ṣaṇmitabhuktaṃ bhajante
ārogyam āyuś ca sukhaṃ balaṃ ca
c anāvilaṃ cāsya bhaved apatyaṃ
na cainam ādyūna iti kṣipanti
a akarmaśīlaṃ ca mahāśanaṃ ca
lokadviṣṭaṃ bahumāyaṃ nṛśaṃsam
c adeśakālajñam aniṣṭaveṣam
etān gṛhe na prativāsayīta
a kadaryam ākrośakam aśrutaṃ ca
varākasaṃbhūtam amānyamāninam
c niṣṭhūriṇaṃ kṛtavairaṃ kṛtaghnam
etān bhṛśārto 'pi na jātu yācet
a saṃkliṣṭakarmāṇam atipravādaṃ
nityānṛtaṃ cādṛḍhabhaktikaṃ ca
c vikṛṣṭarāgaṃ bahumāninaṃ cāpy
etān na seveta narādhamān ṣaṭ
a sahāyabandhanā hy arthāḥ sahāyāś cārthabandhanāḥ
c anyonyabandhanāv etau vinānyonyaṃ na sidhyataḥ
a utpādya putrān anṛṇāṃś ca kṛtvā
vṛttiṃ ca tebhyo 'nuvidhāya kāṃ cit
c sthāne kumārīḥ pratipādya sarvā
araṇyasaṃstho munivad bubhūṣet
a hitaṃ yat sarvabhūtānām ātmanaś ca sukhāvaham
c tat kuryād īśvaro hy etan mūlaṃ dharmārthasiddhaye
a buddhiḥ prabhāvas tejaś ca sattvam utthānam eva ca
c vyavasāyaś ca yasya syāt tasyāvṛttibhayaṃ kutaḥ
a paśya doṣān pāṇḍavair vigrahe tvaṃ
yatra vyatherann api devāḥ saśakrāḥ
c putrair vairaṃ nityam udvignavāso
yaśaḥpraṇāśo dviṣatāṃ ca harṣaḥ
a bhīṣmasya kopas tava cendrakalpa
droṇasya rājñaś ca yudhiṣṭhirasya
c utsādayel lokam imaṃ pravṛddhaḥ
śveto grahas tiryag ivāpatan khe
a tava putraśataṃ caiva karṇaḥ pañca ca pāṇḍavāḥ
c pṛthivīm anuśāseyur akhilāṃ sāgarāmbarām
a dhārtarāṣṭrā vanaṃ rājan vyāghrāḥ pāṇḍusutā matāḥ
c mā vanaṃ chindhi savyāghraṃ mā vyāghrān nīnaśo vanāt
a na syād vanam ṛte vyāghrān vyāghrā na syur ṛte vanam
c vanaṃ hi rakṣyate vyāghrair vyāghrān rakṣati kānanam
a na tathecchanty akalyāṇāḥ pareṣāṃ vedituṃ guṇān
c yathaiṣāṃ jñātum icchanti nairguṇyaṃ pāpacetasaḥ
a arthasiddhiṃ parām icchan dharmam evāditaś caret
c na hi dharmād apaity arthaḥ svargalokād ivāmṛtam
a yasyātmā virataḥ pāpāt kalyāṇe ca niveśitaḥ
c tena sarvam idaṃ buddhaṃ prakṛtir vikṛtiś ca yā
a yo dharmam arthaṃ kāmaṃ ca yathākālaṃ niṣevate
c dharmārthakāmasaṃyogaṃ so 'mutreha ca vindati
a saṃniyacchati yo vegam utthitaṃ krodhaharṣayoḥ
c sa śriyo bhājanaṃ rājan yaś cāpatsu na muhyati
a balaṃ pañcavidhaṃ nityaṃ puruṣāṇāṃ nibodha me
c yat tu bāhubalaṃ nāma kaniṣṭhaṃ balam ucyate
a amātyalābho bhadraṃ te dvitīyaṃ balam ucyate
c dhanalābhas tṛtīyaṃ tu balam āhur jigīṣavaḥ
a yat tv asya sahajaṃ rājan pitṛpaitāmahaṃ balam
c abhijātabalaṃ nāma tac caturthaṃ balaṃ smṛtam
a yena tv etāni sarvāṇi saṃgṛhītāni bhārata
c yad balānāṃ balaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ tat prajñābalam ucyate
a mahate yo 'pakārāya narasya prabhaven naraḥ
c tena vairaṃ samāsajya dūrastho 'smīti nāśvaset
a strīṣu rājasu sarpeṣu svādhyāye śatruseviṣu
c bhoge cāyuṣi viśvāsaṃ kaḥ prājñaḥ kartum arhati
a prajñāśareṇābhihatasya jantoś
cikitsakāḥ santi na cauṣadhāni
c na homamantrā na ca maṅgalāni
nātharvaṇā nāpy agadāḥ susiddhāḥ
a sarpaś cāgniś ca siṃhaś ca kulaputraś ca bhārata
c nāvajñeyā manuṣyeṇa sarve te hy atitejasaḥ
a agnis tejo mahal loke gūḍhas tiṣṭhati dāruṣu
c na copayuṅkte tad dāru yāvan no dīpyate paraiḥ
a sa eva khalu dārubhyo yadā nirmathya dīpyate
c tadā tac ca vanaṃ cānyan nirdahaty āśu tejasā
a evam eva kule jātāḥ pāvakopamatejasaḥ
c kṣamāvanto nirākārāḥ kāṣṭhe 'gnir iva śerate
a latādharmā tvaṃ saputraḥ śālāḥ pāṇḍusutā matāḥ
c na latā vardhate jātu mahādrumam anāśritā
a vanaṃ rājaṃs tvaṃ saputro 'mbikeya
siṃhān vane pāṇḍavāṃs tāta viddhi
c siṃhair vihīnaṃ hi vanaṃ vinaśyet
siṃhā vinaśyeyur ṛte vanena
 vidura uvāca
a ūrdhvaṃ prāṇā hy utkrāmanti yūnaḥ sthavira āyati
c pratyutthānābhivādābhyāṃ punas tān pratipadyate
a pīṭhaṃ dattvā sādhave 'bhyāgatāya
ānīyāpaḥ parinirṇijya pādau
c sukhaṃ pṛṣṭvā prativedyātmasaṃsthaṃ
tato dadyād annam avekṣya dhīraḥ
a yasyodakaṃ madhuparkaṃ ca gāṃ ca
namantravit pratigṛhṇāti gehe
c lobhād bhayād arthakārpaṇyato vā
tasyānarthaṃ jīvitam āhur āryāḥ
a cikitsakaḥ śalyakartāvakīrṇī
stenaḥ krūro madyapo bhrūṇahā ca
c senājīvī śrutivikrāyakaś ca
bhṛśaṃ priyo 'py atithir nodakārhaḥ
a avikreyaṃ lavaṇaṃ pakvam annaṃ
dadhi kṣīraṃ madhu tailaṃ ghṛtaṃ ca
c tilā māṃsaṃ mūlaphalāni śākaṃ
raktaṃ vāsaḥ sarvagandhā guḍaś ca
a aroṣaṇo yaḥ samaloṣṭakāñcanaḥ
prahīṇaśoko gatasaṃdhivigrahaḥ
c nindāpraśaṃsoparataḥ priyāpriye
carann udāsīnavad eṣa bhikṣukaḥ
a nīvāramūleṅgudaśākavṛttiḥ
susaṃyatātmāgnikāryeṣv acodyaḥ
c vane vasann atithiṣv apramatto
dhuraṃdharaḥ puṇyakṛd eṣa tāpasaḥ
a apakṛtvā buddhimato dūrastho 'smīti nāśvaset
c dīrghau buddhimato bāhū yābhyāṃ hiṃsati hiṃsitaḥ
a na viśvased aviśvaste viśvaste nātiviśvaset
c viśvāsād bhayam utpannaṃ mūlāny api nikṛntati
a anīrṣyur guptadāraḥ syāt saṃvibhāgī priyaṃvadaḥ
c ślakṣṇo madhuravāk strīṇāṃ na cāsāṃ vaśago bhavet
a pūjanīyā mahābhāgāḥ puṇyāś ca gṛhadīptayaḥ
c striyaḥ śriyo gṛhasyoktās tasmād rakṣyā viśeṣataḥ
a pitur antaḥpuraṃ dadyān mātur dadyān mahānasam
c goṣu cātmasamaṃ dadyāt svayam eva kṛṣiṃ vrajet
e bhṛtyair vaṇijyācāraṃ ca putraiḥ seveta brāhmaṇān
a adbhyo 'gnir brahmataḥ kṣatram aśmano loham utthitam
c teṣāṃ sarvatragaṃ tejaḥ svāsu yoniṣu śāmyati
a nityaṃ santaḥ kule jātāḥ pāvakopamatejasaḥ
c kṣamāvanto nirākārāḥ kāṣṭhe 'gnir iva śerate
a yasya mantraṃ na jānanti bāhyāś cābhyantarāś ca ye
c sa rājā sarvataścakṣuś ciram aiśvaryam aśnute
a kariṣyan na prabhāṣeta kṛtāny eva ca darśayet
c dharmakāmārthakāryāṇi tathā mantro na bhidyate
a giripṛṣṭham upāruhya prāsādaṃ vā rahogataḥ
c araṇye niḥśalāke vā tatra mantro vidhīyate
a nāsuhṛt paramaṃ mantraṃ bhāratārhati veditum
c apaṇḍito vāpi suhṛt paṇḍito vāpy anātmavān
d nāparīkṣya mahīpālaḥ kuryāt sacivam ātmanaḥ
e amātye hy arthalipsā ca mantrarakṣaṇam eva ca
a kṛtāni sarvakāryāṇi yasya vā pārṣadā viduḥ
b dharme cārthe ca kāme ca sa rājā rājasattamaḥ
c gūḍhamantrasya nṛpates tasya siddhir asaṃśayam
a apraśastāni karmāṇi yo mohād anutiṣṭhati
c sa teṣāṃ viparibhraṃśe bhraśyate jīvitād api
a karmaṇāṃ tu praśastānām anuṣṭhānaṃ sukhāvaham
c teṣām evānanuṣṭhānaṃ paścāttāpakaraṃ mahat
d anadhītya yathā vedān na vipraḥ śrāddham arhati
d evam aśrutaṣāḍguṇyo na mantraṃ śrotum arhati
a sthānavṛddhikṣayajñasya ṣāḍguṇyaviditātmanaḥ
c anavajñātaśīlasya svādhīnā pṛthivī nṛpa
a amoghakrodhaharṣasya svayaṃ kṛtyānvavekṣiṇaḥ
c ātmapratyayakośasya vasudheyaṃ vasuṃdharā
a nāmamātreṇa tuṣyeta chatreṇa ca mahīpatiḥ
c bhṛtyebhyo visṛjed arthān naikaḥ sarvaharo bhavet
a brāhmaṇo brāhmaṇaṃ veda bhartā veda striyaṃ tathā
c amātyaṃ nṛpatir veda rājā rājānam eva ca
a na śatrur aṅkam āpanno moktavyo vadhyatāṃ gataḥ
b nyag bhūtvā paryupāsīta vadhyaṃ hanyād bale sati
b ahanyamāno bhayakṛn na hatāj jāyate bhayam
c ahatād dhi bhayaṃ tasmāj jāyate nacirād iva
a daivateṣu ca yatnena rājasu brāhmaṇeṣu ca
c niyantavyaḥ sadā krodho vṛddhabālātureṣu ca
a nirarthaṃ kalahaṃ prājño varjayen mūḍhasevitam
c kīrtiṃ ca labhate loke na cānarthena yujyate
a prasādo niṣphalo yasya krodhaś cāpi nirarthakaḥ
c na taṃ bhartāram icchanti ṣaṇḍhaṃ patim iva striyaḥ
a na buddhir dhanalābhāya na jāḍyam asamṛddhaye
c lokaparyāyavṛttāntaṃ prājño jānāti netaraḥ
a vidyāśīlavayovṛddhān buddhivṛddhāṃś ca bhārata
c dhanābhijanavṛddhāṃś ca nityaṃ mūḍho 'vamanyate
a anāryavṛttam aprājñam asūyakam adhārmikam
c anarthāḥ kṣipram āyānti vāgduṣṭaṃ krodhanaṃ tathā
a avisaṃvādanaṃ dānaṃ samayasyāvyatikramaḥ
c āvartayanti bhūtāni samyak praṇihitā ca vāk
a avisaṃvādako dakṣaḥ kṛtajño matimān ṛjuḥ
c api saṃkṣīṇakośo 'pi labhate parivāraṇam
a dhṛtiḥ śamo damaḥ śaucaṃ kāruṇyaṃ vāg aniṣṭhurā
c mitrāṇāṃ cānabhidrohaḥ saptaitāḥ samidhaḥ śriyaḥ
a asaṃvibhāgī duṣṭātmā kṛtaghno nirapatrapaḥ
c tādṛṅ narādhamo loke varjanīyo narādhipa
a na sa rātrau sukhaṃ śete sasarpa iva veśmani
c yaḥ kopayati nirdoṣaṃ sadoṣo 'bhyantaraṃ janam
a yeṣu duṣṭeṣu doṣaḥ syād yogakṣemasya bhārata
c sadā prasādanaṃ teṣāṃ devatānām ivācaret
a ye 'rthāḥ strīṣu samāsaktāḥ prathamotpatiteṣu ca
c ye cānāryasamāsaktāḥ sarve te saṃśayaṃ gatāḥ
a yatra strī yatra kitavo yatra bālo 'nuśāsti ca
c majjanti te 'vaśā deśā nadyām aśmaplavā iva
a prayojaneṣu ye saktā na viśeṣeṣu bhārata
c tān ahaṃ paṇḍitān manye viśeṣā hi prasaṅginaḥ
a yaṃ praśaṃsanti kitavā yaṃ praśaṃsanti cāraṇāḥ
c yaṃ praśaṃsanti bandhakyo na sa jīvati mānavaḥ
a hitvā tān parameṣvāsān pāṇḍavān amitaujasaḥ
c āhitaṃ bhārataiśvaryaṃ tvayā duryodhane mahat
a taṃ drakṣyasi paribhraṣṭaṃ tasmāt tvaṃ nacirād iva
c aiśvaryamadasaṃmūḍhaṃ baliṃ lokatrayād iva
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a anīśvaro 'yaṃ puruṣo bhavābhave
sūtraprotā dārumayīva yoṣā
c dhātrā tu diṣṭasya vaśe kilāyaṃ
tasmād vada tvaṃ śravaṇe dhṛto 'ham
 vidura uvāca
a aprāptakālaṃ vacanaṃ bṛhaspatir api bruvan
c labhate buddhyavajñānam avamānaṃ ca bhārata
a priyo bhavati dānena priyavādena cāparaḥ
c mantraṃ mūlabalenānyo yaḥ priyaḥ priya eva saḥ
a dveṣyo na sādhur bhavati na medhāvī na paṇḍitaḥ
c priye śubhāni karmāṇi dveṣye pāpāni bhārata
d uktaṃ mayā jātamātre 'pi rājan
d duryodhanaṃ tyaja putraṃ tvam ekam
d tasya tyāgāt putraśatasya vṛddhir
d asyātyāgāt putraśatasya nāśaḥ
d na vṛddhir bahumantavyā yā vṛddhiḥ kṣayam āvahet
d kṣayo 'pi bahumantavyo yaḥ kṣayo vṛddhim āvahet
a na sa kṣayo mahārāja yaḥ kṣayo vṛddhim āvahet
c kṣayaḥ sa tv iha mantavyo yaṃ labdhvā bahu nāśayet
a samṛddhā guṇataḥ ke cid bhavanti dhanato 'pare
c dhanavṛddhān guṇair hīnān dhṛtarāṣṭra vivarjayet
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a sarvaṃ tvam āyatīyuktaṃ bhāṣase prājñasaṃmatam
c na cotsahe sutaṃ tyaktuṃ yato dharmas tato jayaḥ
 vidura uvāca
a svabhāvaguṇasaṃpanno na jātu vinayānvitaḥ
c susūkṣmam api bhūtānām upamardaṃ prayokṣyate
a parāpavādaniratāḥ paraduḥkhodayeṣu ca
c parasparavirodhe ca yatante satatotthitāḥ
a sadoṣaṃ darśanaṃ yeṣāṃ saṃvāse sumahad bhayam
c arthādāne mahān doṣaḥ pradāne ca mahad bhayam
d ye vai bhedanaśīlās tu sakāmā nistrapāḥ śaṭhāḥ
a ye pāpā iti vikhyātāḥ saṃvāse parigarhitāḥ
c yuktāś cānyair mahādoṣair ye narās tān vivarjayet
a nivartamāne sauhārde prītir nīce praṇaśyati
c yā caiva phalanirvṛttiḥ sauhṛde caiva yat sukham
a yatate cāpavādāya yatnam ārabhate kṣaye
c alpe 'py apakṛte mohān na śāntim upagacchati
a tādṛśaiḥ saṃgataṃ nīcair nṛśaṃsair akṛtātmabhiḥ
c niśāmya nipuṇaṃ buddhyā vidvān dūrād vivarjayet
a yo jñātim anugṛhṇāti daridraṃ dīnam āturam
c sa putrapaśubhir vṛddhiṃ yaśaś cāvyayam aśnute
a jñātayo vardhanīyās tair ya icchanty ātmanaḥ śubham
c kulavṛddhiṃ ca rājendra tasmāt sādhu samācara
