a śreyasā yokṣyase rājan kurvāṇo jñātisatkriyām
c viguṇā hy api saṃrakṣyā jñātayo bharatarṣabha
a kiṃ punar guṇavantas te tvatprasādābhikāṅkṣiṇaḥ
c prasādaṃ kuru dīnānāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ viśāṃ pate
a dīyantāṃ grāmakāḥ ke cit teṣāṃ vṛttyartham īśvara
c evaṃ loke yaśaḥprāpto bhaviṣyasi narādhipa
a vṛddhena hi tvayā kāryaṃ putrāṇāṃ tāta rakṣaṇam
c mayā cāpi hitaṃ vācyaṃ viddhi māṃ tvaddhitaiṣiṇam
a jñātibhir vigrahas tāta na kartavyo bhavārthinā
c sukhāni saha bhojyāni jñātibhir bharatarṣabha
a saṃbhojanaṃ saṃkathanaṃ saṃprītiś ca parasparam
c jñātibhiḥ saha kāryāṇi na virodhaḥ kathaṃ cana
a jñātayas tārayantīha jñātayo majjayanti ca
c suvṛttās tārayantīha durvṛttā majjayanti ca
a suvṛtto bhava rājendra pāṇḍavān prati mānada
c adharṣaṇīyaḥ śatrūṇāṃ tair vṛtas tvaṃ bhaviṣyasi
a śrīmantaṃ jñātim āsādya yo jñātir avasīdati
b sīdatā yat kṛtaṃ tena tat pāpaṃ samam aśnute
c digdhahastaṃ mṛga iva sa enas tasya vindati
a paścād api naraśreṣṭha tava tāpo bhaviṣyati
c tān vā hatān sutān vāpi śrutvā tad anucintaya
a yena khaṭvāṃ samārūḍhaḥ paritapyeta karmaṇā
c ādāv eva na tat kuryād adhruve jīvite sati
a na kaś cin nāpanayate pumān anyatra bhārgavāt
c śeṣasaṃpratipattis tu buddhimatsv eva tiṣṭhati
a duryodhanena yady etat pāpaṃ teṣu purā kṛtam
c tvayā tat kulavṛddhena pratyāneyaṃ nareśvara
a tāṃs tvaṃ pade pratiṣṭhāpya loke vigatakalmaṣaḥ
c bhaviṣyasi naraśreṣṭha pūjanīyo manīṣiṇām
a suvyāhṛtāni dhīrāṇāṃ phalataḥ pravicintya yaḥ
c adhyavasyati kāryeṣu ciraṃ yaśasi tiṣṭhati
d asamyag upayuktaṃ hi jñānaṃ sukuśalair api
d upalabhyāpy aviditaṃ viditaṃ cāpy anuṣṭhitam
d pāpodayaphalaṃ vidvān yo nārabhati vardhate
d yas tu pūrvakṛtaṃ pāpam avimṛśyānuvartate
d so 'nyāparādhe durmedhā viṣame vinipātyate
d mantrabhedasya ṣaṭ prājño dvārāṇīmāni lakṣayet
d arthasaṃtatikāmaś ca rakṣed etāni nityaśaḥ
d madaṃ svapnam avijñānam ākāraṃ cātmasaṃbhavam
d duṣṭāmātyeṣu viśrambhaṃ dūtāc cākuśalād api
d dvārāṇy etāni yo jñātvā saṃvṛṇoti sadā nṛpaḥ
d trivargacaraṇe yuktaḥ sa śatrūn adhitiṣṭhati
d na vai śrutam avijñāya vṛddhān anupasevya ca
d dharmārthau vedituṃ śakyau bṛhaspatisamair api
d naṣṭaṃ samudre patitaṃ naṣṭaṃ vākyam aśṛṇvati
d anātmani śrutaṃ naṣṭaṃ naṣṭaṃ śrutam anagnikam
d matyā parīkṣya medhāvī buddhyā saṃpādya cāsakṛt
d śrutvā dṛṣṭvātha vijñāya prājño mantraṃ samācaret
a avṛttiṃ vinayo hanti hanty anarthaṃ parākramaḥ
c hanti nityaṃ kṣamā krodham ācāro hanty alakṣaṇam
a paricchadena kṣetreṇa veśmanā paricaryayā
c parīkṣeta kulaṃ rājan bhojanācchādanena ca
d upasthitasya kāmasya prativādo na vidyate
d api nirmuktadehasya kāmaraktasya kiṃ punaḥ
d prājñopasevinaṃ vaidyaṃ dhārmikaṃ priyadarśanam
d mitravantaṃ suvākyaṃ ca suhṛdaṃ paripālayet
d duṣkulīnaḥ kulīno vā maryādāṃ yo na laṅghayet
d dharmāpekṣī mṛdur hrīmān sa kulīnaśatād varaḥ
d arthasaṃtatikāmaś ca rakṣed etāni nityaśaḥ
a yayoś cittena vā cittaṃ naibhṛtaṃ naibhṛtena vā
c sameti prajñayā prajñā tayor maitrī na jīryate
a durbuddhim akṛtaprajñaṃ channaṃ kūpaṃ tṛṇair iva
c vivarjayīta medhāvī tasmin maitrī praṇaśyati
a avalipteṣu mūrkheṣu raudrasāhasikeṣu ca
c tathaivāpetadharmeṣu na maitrīm ācared budhaḥ
a kṛtajñaṃ dhārmikaṃ satyam akṣudraṃ dṛḍhabhaktikam
c jitendriyaṃ sthitaṃ sthityāṃ mitram atyāgi ceṣyate
a indriyāṇām anutsargo mṛtyunā na viśiṣyate
c atyarthaṃ punar utsargaḥ sādayed daivatāny api
a mārdavaṃ sarvabhūtānām anasūyā kṣamā dhṛtiḥ
c āyuṣyāṇi budhāḥ prāhur mitrāṇāṃ cāvimānanā
a apanītaṃ sunītena yo 'rthaṃ pratyāninīṣate
c matim āsthāya sudṛḍhāṃ tad akāpuruṣavratam
a āyatyāṃ pratikārajñas tadātve dṛḍhaniścayaḥ
c atīte kāryaśeṣajño naro 'rthair na prahīyate
a karmaṇā manasā vācā yad abhīkṣṇaṃ niṣevate
c tad evāpaharaty enaṃ tasmāt kalyāṇam ācaret
a maṅgalālambhanaṃ yogaḥ śrutam utthānam ārjavam
c bhūtim etāni kurvanti satāṃ cābhīkṣṇadarśanam
a anirvedaḥ śriyo mūlaṃ duḥkhanāśe sukhasya ca
c mahān bhavaty anirviṇṇaḥ sukhaṃ cātyantam aśnute
a nātaḥ śrīmattaraṃ kiṃ cid anyat pathyatamaṃ tathā
c prabhaviṣṇor yathā tāta kṣamā sarvatra sarvadā
a kṣamed aśaktaḥ sarvasya śaktimān dharmakāraṇāt
c arthānarthau samau yasya tasya nityaṃ kṣamā hitā
a yat sukhaṃ sevamāno 'pi dharmārthābhyāṃ na hīyate
c kāmaṃ tad upaseveta na mūḍhavratam ācaret
a duḥkhārteṣu pramatteṣu nāstikeṣv alaseṣu ca
c na śrīr vasaty adānteṣu ye cotsāhavivarjitāḥ
a ārjavena naraṃ yuktam ārjavāt savyapatrapam
c aśaktimantaṃ manyanto dharṣayanti kubuddhayaḥ
a atyāryam atidātāram atiśūram ativratam
c prajñābhimāninaṃ caiva śrīr bhayān nopasarpati
d na cātiguṇavatsv eṣā nātyantaṃ nirguṇeṣu ca
d naiṣā guṇān kāmayate nairguṇyān nānurajyate
d unmattā gaur ivāndhā śrīḥ kva cid evāvatiṣṭhate
a agnihotraphalā vedāḥ śīlavṛttaphalaṃ śrutam
c ratiputraphalā dārā dattabhuktaphalaṃ dhanam
a adharmopārjitair arthair yaḥ karoty aurdhvadehikam
c na sa tasya phalaṃ pretya bhuṅkte 'rthasya durāgamāt
a kāntāravanadurgeṣu kṛcchrāsv āpatsu saṃbhrame
c udyateṣu ca śastreṣu nāsti śeṣavatāṃ bhayam
a utthānaṃ saṃyamo dākṣyam apramādo dhṛtiḥ smṛtiḥ
c samīkṣya ca samārambho viddhi mūlaṃ bhavasya tat
a tapo balaṃ tāpasānāṃ brahma brahmavidāṃ balam
c hiṃsā balam asādhūnāṃ kṣamā guṇavatāṃ balam
a aṣṭau tāny avrataghnāni āpo mūlaṃ phalaṃ payaḥ
c havir brāhmaṇakāmyā ca guror vacanam auṣadham
a na tatparasya saṃdadhyāt pratikūlaṃ yadātmanaḥ
b ātmanaḥ pratikūlāni vijānan na samācaret
c saṃgraheṇaiṣa dharmaḥ syāt kāmād anyaḥ pravartate
a akrodhena jayet krodham asādhuṃ sādhunā jayet
c jayet kadaryaṃ dānena jayet satyena cānṛtam
a strīdhūrtake 'lase bhīrau caṇḍe puruṣamānini
c caure kṛtaghne viśvāso na kāryo na ca nāstike
a abhivādanaśīlasya nityaṃ vṛddhopasevinaḥ
c catvāri saṃpravardhante kīrtir āyur yaśobalam
a atikleśena ye 'rthāḥ syur dharmasyātikrameṇa ca
c arer vā praṇipātena mā sma teṣu manaḥ kṛthāḥ
a avidyaḥ puruṣaḥ śocyaḥ śocyaṃ mithunam aprajam
c nirāhārāḥ prajāḥ śocyāḥ śocyaṃ rāṣṭram arājakam
a adhvā jarā dehavatāṃ parvatānāṃ jalaṃ jarā
c asaṃbhogo jarā strīṇāṃ vākśalyaṃ manaso jarā
a anāmnāyamalā vedā brāhmaṇasyāvrataṃ malam
b malaṃ pṛthivyā vāhīkāḥ puruṣasyānṛtaṃ malam
c kautūhalamalā sādhvī vipravāsamalāḥ striyaḥ
a suvarṇasya malaṃ rūpyaṃ rūpyasyāpi malaṃ trapu
c jñeyaṃ trapumalaṃ sīsaṃ sīsasyāpi malaṃ malam
a na svapnena jayen nidrāṃ na kāmena striyaṃ jayet
c nendhanena jayed agniṃ na pānena surāṃ jayet
a yasya dānajitaṃ mitram amitrā yudhi nirjitāḥ
c annapānajitā dārāḥ saphalaṃ tasya jīvitam
a sahasriṇo 'pi jīvanti jīvanti śatinas tathā
c dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ vimuñcecchāṃ na kathaṃ cin na jīvyate
a yat pṛthivyāṃ vrīhiyavaṃ hiraṇyaṃ paśavaḥ striyaḥ
c nālam ekasya tat sarvam iti paśyan na muhyati
a rājan bhūyo bravīmi tvāṃ putreṣu samam ācara
c samatā yadi te rājan sveṣu pāṇḍusuteṣu ca
 vidura uvāca
a yo 'bhyarthitaḥ sadbhir asajjamānaḥ
karoty arthaṃ śaktim ahāpayitvā
c kṣipraṃ yaśas taṃ samupaiti santam alaṃ
prasannā hi sukhāya santaḥ
a mahāntam apy artham adharmayuktaṃ
yaḥ saṃtyajaty anupākruṣṭa eva
c sukhaṃ sa duḥkhāny avamucya śete
jīrṇāṃ tvacaṃ sarpa ivāvamucya
a anṛtaṃ ca samutkarṣe rājagāmi ca paiśunam
c guroś cālīkanirbandhaḥ samāni brahmahatyayā
a asūyaikapadaṃ mṛtyur ativādaḥ śriyo vadhaḥ
c aśuśrūṣā tvarā ślāghā vidyāyāḥ śatravas trayaḥ
d ālasyaṃ madamohau ca cāpalaṃ goṣṭhir eva ca
d stabdhatā cābhimānitvaṃ tathātyāgitvam eva ca
d ete vai sapta doṣās tu sadā vidyārthināṃ matāḥ
a sukhārthinaḥ kuto vidyā nāsti vidyārthinaḥ sukham
c sukhārthī vā tyajed vidyāṃ vidyārthī vā sukhaṃ tyajet
a nāgnis tṛpyati kāṣṭhānāṃ nāpagānāṃ mahodadhiḥ
c nāntakaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ na puṃsāṃ vāmalocanā
a āśā dhṛtiṃ hanti samṛddhim antakaḥ
krodhaḥ śriyaṃ hanti yaśaḥ kadaryatā
c apālanaṃ hanti paśūṃś ca rājann
ekaḥ kruddho brāhmaṇo hanti rāṣṭram
a ajaś ca kāṃsyaṃ ca rathaś ca nityaṃ
madhv ākarṣaḥ śakuniḥ śrotriyaś ca
c vṛddho jñātir avasanno vayasya
etāni te santu gṛhe sadaiva
a ajokṣā candanaṃ vīṇā ādarśo madhusarpiṣī
c viṣam audumbaraṃ śaṅkhaḥ svarṇaṃ nābhiś ca rocanā
a gṛhe sthāpayitavyāni dhanyāni manur abravīt
c devabrāhmaṇapūjārtham atithīnāṃ ca bhārata
a idaṃ ca tvāṃ sarvaparaṃ bravīmi
puṇyaṃ padaṃ tāta mahāviśiṣṭam
c na jātu kāmān na bhayān na lobhād
dharmaṃ tyajej jīvitasyāpi hetoḥ
a nityo dharmaḥ sukhaduḥkhe tv anitye
nityo jīvo dhātur asya tv anityaḥ
c tyaktvānityaṃ pratitiṣṭhasva nitye
saṃtuṣya tvaṃ toṣaparo hi lābhaḥ
a mahābalān paśya mahānubhāvān
praśāsya bhūmiṃ dhanadhānyapūrṇām
c rājyāni hitvā vipulāṃś ca bhogān
gatān narendrān vaśam antakasya
a mṛtaṃ putraṃ duḥkhapuṣṭaṃ manuṣyā
utkṣipya rājan svagṛhān nirharanti
c taṃ muktakeśāḥ karuṇaṃ rudantaś
citāmadhye kāṣṭham iva kṣipanti
a anyo dhanaṃ pretagatasya bhuṅkte
vayāṃsi cāgniś ca śarīradhātūn
c dvābhyām ayaṃ saha gacchaty amutra
puṇyena pāpena ca veṣṭyamānaḥ
a utsṛjya vinivartante jñātayaḥ suhṛdaḥ sutāḥ
b apuṣpān aphalān vṛkṣān yathā tāta patatriṇaḥ
c agnau prāstaṃ tu puruṣaṃ karmānveti svayaṃkṛtam
d tasmāt tu puruṣo yatnād dharmaṃ saṃcinuyāc chanaiḥ
a asmāl lokād ūrdhvam amuṣya cādho
mahat tamas tiṣṭhati hy andhakāram
c tad vai mahāmohanam indriyāṇāṃ
budhyasva mā tvāṃ pralabheta rājan
a idaṃ vacaḥ śakṣyasi ced yathāvan
niśamya sarvaṃ pratipattum evam
c yaśaḥ paraṃ prāpsyasi jīvaloke
bhayaṃ na cāmutra na ceha te 'sti
a ātmā nadī bhārata puṇyatīrthā
satyodakā dhṛtikūlā damormiḥ
c tasyāṃ snātaḥ pūyate puṇyakarmā
puṇyo hy ātmā nityam ambho 'mbha eva
a kāmakrodhagrāhavatīṃ pañcendriyajalāṃ nadīm
c kṛtvā dhṛtimayīṃ nāvaṃ janmadurgāṇi saṃtara
a prajñāvṛddhaṃ dharmavṛddhaṃ svabandhuṃ
vidyāvṛddhaṃ vayasā cāpi vṛddham
c kāryākārye pūjayitvā prasādya
yaḥ saṃpṛcchen na sa muhyet kadā cit
a dhṛtyā śiśnodaraṃ rakṣet pāṇipādaṃ ca cakṣuṣā
c cakṣuḥśrotre ca manasā mano vācaṃ ca karmaṇā
a nityodakī nityayajñopavītī
nityasvādhyāyī patitānnavarjī
c ṛtaṃ bruvan gurave karma kurvan
na brāhmaṇaś cyavate brahmalokāt
a adhītya vedān parisaṃstīrya cāgnīn
iṣṭvā yajñaiḥ pālayitvā prajāś ca
c gobrāhmaṇārthe śastrapūtāntarātmā
hataḥ saṃgrāme kṣatriyaḥ svargam eti
a vaiśyo 'dhītya brāhmaṇān kṣatriyāṃś ca
dhanaiḥ kāle saṃvibhajyāśritāṃś ca
c tretāpūtaṃ dhūmam āghrāya puṇyaṃ
pretya svarge devasukhāni bhuṅkte
a brahmakṣatraṃ vaiśyavarṇaṃ ca śūdraḥ
krameṇaitān nyāyataḥ pūjayānaḥ
c tuṣṭeṣv eteṣv avyatho dagdhapāpas
tyaktvā dehaṃ svargasukhāni bhuṅkte
a cāturvarṇyasyaiṣa dharmas tavokto
hetuṃ cātra bruvato me nibodha
c kṣātrād dharmād dhīyate pāṇḍuputras
taṃ tvaṃ rājan rājadharme niyuṅkṣva
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a evam etad yathā māṃ tvam anuśāsasi nityadā
c mamāpi ca matiḥ saumya bhavaty evaṃ yathāttha mām
a sā tu buddhiḥ kṛtāpy evaṃ pāṇḍavān prati me sadā
c duryodhanaṃ samāsādya punar viparivartate
a na diṣṭam abhyatikrāntuṃ śakyaṃ martyena kena cit
c diṣṭam eva kṛtaṃ manye pauruṣaṃ tu nirarthakam
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a anuktaṃ yadi te kiṃ cid vācā vidura vidyate
c tan me śuśrūṣave brūhi vicitrāṇi hi bhāṣase
 vidura uvāca
a dhṛtarāṣṭra kumāro vai yaḥ purāṇaḥ sanātanaḥ
c sanatsujātaḥ provāca mṛtyur nāstīti bhārata
a sa te guhyān prakāśāṃś ca sarvān hṛdayasaṃśrayān
c pravakṣyati mahārāja sarvabuddhimatāṃ varaḥ
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a kiṃ tvaṃ na veda tad bhūyo yan me brūyāt sanātanaḥ
c tvam eva vidura brūhi prajñāśeṣo 'sti cet tava
 vidura uvāca
a śūdrayonāv ahaṃ jāto nāto 'nyad vaktum utsahe
c kumārasya tu yā buddhir veda tāṃ śāśvatīm aham
a brāhmīṃ hi yonim āpannaḥ suguhyam api yo vadet
c na tena garhyo devānāṃ tasmād etad bravīmi te
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a bravīhi vidura tvaṃ me purāṇaṃ taṃ sanātanam
c katham etena dehena syād ihaiva samāgamaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a cintayām āsa viduras tam ṛṣiṃ saṃśitavratam
c sa ca tac cintitaṃ jñātvā darśayām āsa bhārata
a sa cainaṃ pratijagrāha vidhidṛṣṭena karmaṇā
c sukhopaviṣṭaṃ viśrāntam athainaṃ viduro 'bravīt
a bhagavan saṃśayaḥ kaś cid dhṛtarāṣṭrasya mānase
c yo na śakyo mayā vaktuṃ tam asmai vaktum arhasi
e yaṃ śrutvāyaṃ manuṣyendraḥ sukhaduḥkhātigo bhavet
a lābhālābhau priyadveṣyau yathainaṃ na jarāntakau
c viṣaheran bhayāmarṣau kṣutpipāse madodbhavau
e aratiś caiva tandrī ca kāmakrodhau kṣayodayau
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tato rājā dhṛtarāṣṭro manīṣī
saṃpūjya vākyaṃ vidureritaṃ tat
c sanatsujātaṃ rahite mahātmā
papraccha buddhiṃ paramāṃ bubhūṣan
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a sanatsujāta yadīdaṃ śṛṇomi
mṛtyur hi nāstīti tavopadeśam
c devāsurā hy ācaran brahmacaryam
amṛtyave tat kataran nu satyam
 sanatsujāta uvāca
a amṛtyuḥ karmaṇā ke cin mṛtyur nāstīti cāpare
c śṛṇu me bruvato rājan yathaitan mā viśaṅkithāḥ
a ubhe satye kṣatriyādyapravṛtte
moho mṛtyuḥ saṃmato yaḥ kavīnām
c pramādaṃ vai mṛtyum ahaṃ bravīmi
sadāpramādam amṛtatvaṃ bravīmi
a pramādād vai asurāḥ parābhavann
apramādād brahmabhūtā bhavanti
c na vai mṛtyur vyāghra ivātti jantūn
na hy asya rūpam upalabhyate ha
a yamaṃ tv eke mṛtyum ato 'nyam āhur
ātmāvasannam amṛtaṃ brahmacaryam
c pitṛloke rājyam anuśāsti devaḥ
śivaḥ śivānām aśivo 'śivānām
a āsyād eṣa niḥsarate narāṇāṃ
krodhaḥ pramādo moharūpaś ca mṛtyuḥ
b ahaṃgatenaiva caran vimārgān
b na cātmano yogam upaiti kaś cit
c te mohitās tadvaśe vartamānā
itaḥ pretās tatra punaḥ patanti
a tatas taṃ devā anu viplavante
ato mṛtyur maraṇākhyām upaiti
c karmodaye karmaphalānurāgās
tatrānu yānti na taranti mṛtyum
d sadarthayogān avagamāt samantāt
d pravartate bhogayogena dehī
d tad vai mahāmohanam indriyāṇāṃ
d mithyārthayogasya gatir hi nityā
d mithyārthayogābhihatāntarātmā
d smarann upāste viṣayān samantāt
a yo 'bhidhyāyann utpatiṣṇūn nihanyād
anādareṇāpratibudhyamānaḥ
c sa vai mṛtyur mṛtyur ivātti bhūtvā
evaṃ vidvān yo vinihanti kāmān
a kāmānusārī puruṣaḥ kāmān anu vinaśyati
c kāmān vyudasya dhunute yat kiṃ cit puruṣo rajaḥ
a tamo 'prakāśo bhūtānāṃ narako 'yaṃ pradṛśyate
c gṛhyanta iva dhāvanti gacchantaḥ śvabhram unmukhāḥ
a abhidhyā vai prathamaṃ hanti cainaṃ
kāmakrodhau gṛhya cainaṃ tu paścāt
c ete bālān mṛtyave prāpayanti
dhīrās tu dhairyeṇa taranti mṛtyum
d amūḍhavṛtteḥ puruṣasyeha kuryāt
d kiṃ vai mṛtyus tārṇa ivāsya vyāghraḥ
a amanyamānaḥ kṣatriya kiṃ cid anyan
nādhīyate tārṇa ivāsya vyāghraḥ
c krodhāl lobhān mohamayāntarātmā
sa vai mṛtyus tvac charīre ya eṣaḥ
a evaṃ mṛtyuṃ jāyamānaṃ viditvā
jñāne tiṣṭhan na bibhetīha mṛtyoḥ
c vinaśyate viṣaye tasya mṛtyur
mṛtyor yathā viṣayaṃ prāpya martyaḥ
d dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
d yān evāhur ijyayā sādhulokān
d dvijātīnāṃ puṇyatamān sanātanān
d teṣāṃ parārthaṃ kathayantīha vedā
d sanatsujāta uvāca
d etad vidvān naiti kathaṃ nu karma
d evaṃ hy avidvān upayāti tatra
d tathārthajātaṃ ca vadanti vedāḥ
d sa neha āyāti paraṃ parātmā
d dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
d prayāti mārgeṇa nihatya mārgān
d ko 'sau niyuṅkte tam ajaṃ purāṇaṃ
d sa ced idaṃ sarvam anukrameṇa
d kiṃ vāsya kāryam atha vā sukhaṃ ca
d sanatsujāta uvāca
d tan me vidvan brūhi sarvaṃ yathāvat
d doṣo mahān atra vibhedayoge
d hy anādiyogena bhavanti nityāḥ
d tathāsya nādhikyam apaiti kiṃ cid
d anādiyogena bhavanti puṃsaḥ
d ya etad vā bhagavān sa nityo
d vikārayogena karoti viśvam
d tathā ca tacchaktir iti sma manyate
d tathārthayoge ca bhavanti vedāḥ
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a ye 'smin dharmān nācarantīha ke cit
tathā dharmān ke cid ihācaranti
c dharmaḥ pāpena pratihanyate sma
utāho dharmaḥ pratihanti pāpam
 sanatsujāta uvāca
a ubhayam eva tatropabhujyate phalaṃ
dharmasyaivetarasya ca
b tasmin sthito vāpy ubhayaṃ hi nityaṃ
b jñānena vidvān pratihanti siddham
b tathānyathā puṇyam upaiti dehī
b tathāgataṃ pāpam upaiti siddham
b gatvobhayaṃ karmaṇā bhujyate 'sthiraṃ
b śubhasya pāpasya sa cāpi karmaṇā
c dharmeṇādharmaṃ praṇudatīha vidvān
dharmo balīyān iti tasya viddhi
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a yān imān āhuḥ svasya dharmasya lokān
dvijātīnāṃ puṇyakṛtāṃ sanātanān
c teṣāṃ parikramān kathayantas tato 'nyān
naitad vidvan naiva kṛtaṃ ca karma
 sanatsujāta uvāca
a yeṣāṃ bale na vispardhā bale balavatām iva
c te brāhmaṇā itaḥ pretya svargaloke prakāśate
d yeṣāṃ dharme na ca spardhā teṣāṃ tajjñānasādhanam
d te brāhmaṇā ito muktāḥ svargaṃ yānti triviṣṭapam
d tasya samyak samācāram āhur vedavido janāḥ
d nainaṃ manyeta bhūyiṣṭhaṃ bāhyam ābhyantaraṃ janam
a yatra manyeta bhūyiṣṭhaṃ prāvṛṣīva tṛṇolapam
c annaṃ pānaṃ ca brāhmaṇas taj jīvan nānusaṃjvaret
a yatrākathayamānasya prayacchaty aśivaṃ bhayam
c atiriktam ivākurvan sa śreyān netaro janaḥ
a yo vākathayamānasya ātmānaṃ nānusaṃjvaret
b eko vai hy antarātmānaṃ brāhmaṇo hantum arhati
c brahmasvaṃ nopabhuñjed vā tadannaṃ saṃmataṃ satām
d kuśavalkalacelādyaṃ brahmasvaṃ yogino viduḥ
a yathā svaṃ vāntam aśnāti śvā vai nityam abhūtaye
c evaṃ te vāntam aśnanti svavīryasyopajīvanāt
a nityam ajñātacaryā me iti manyeta brāhmaṇaḥ
c jñātīnāṃ tu vasan madhye naiva vidyeta kiṃ cana
a ko hy evam antarātmānaṃ brāhmaṇo hantum arhati
b nirliṅgam acalaṃ śuddhaṃ sarvadvandvavivarjitam
c tasmād dhi kiṃ cit kṣatriya brahmāvasati paśyati
d yo 'nyathā santam ātmānam anyathā pratipadyate
d kiṃ tena na kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ coreṇātmāpahāriṇā
a aśrāntaḥ syād anādānāt saṃmato nirupadravaḥ
c śiṣṭo na śiṣṭavat sa syād brāhmaṇo brahmavit kaviḥ
a anāḍhyā mānuṣe vitte āḍhyā vedeṣu ye dvijāḥ
c te durdharṣā duṣprakampyā vidyāt tān brahmaṇas tanum
a sarvān sviṣṭakṛto devān vidyād ya iha kaś cana
c na samāno brāhmaṇasya yasmin prayatate svayam
a yam aprayatamānaṃ tu mānayanti sa mānitaḥ
c na mānyamāno manyeta nāmānād abhisaṃjvaret
d lokaḥ svabhāvavṛttir hi nimeṣonmeṣavat sadā
a vidvāṃso mānayantīha iti manyeta mānitaḥ
c adharmaviduṣo mūḍhā lokaśāstraviśāradāḥ
e na mānyaṃ mānayiṣyanti iti manyed amānitaḥ
a na vai mānaṃ ca maunaṃ ca sahitau carataḥ sadā
c ayaṃ hi loko mānasya asau mānasya tad viduḥ
a śrīḥ sukhasyeha saṃvāsaḥ sā cāpi paripanthinī
c brāhmī sudurlabhā śrīr hi prajñāhīnena kṣatriya
a dvārāṇi tasyā hi vadanti santo
bahuprakārāṇi durāvarāṇi
c satyārjave hrīr damaśaucavidyāḥ
ṣaṇmānamohapratibādhanāni
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
 kasyaiṣa maunaḥ kataran nu maunaṃ
 prabrūhi vidvann iha maunabhāvam
 maunena vidvān uta yāti maunaṃ
 sanatsujāta uvāca
 kathaṃ mune maunam ihācaranti
 yato na vedā manasā sahainam
 anupraviśanti tato 'tha maunam
 yatrotthito vedaśabdas tathāyaṃ
 sa tanmayatvena vibhāti rājan
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a ṛco yajūṃṣy adhīte yaḥ sāmavedaṃ ca yo dvijaḥ
c pāpāni kurvan pāpena lipyate na sa lipyate
 sanatsujāta uvāca
a nainaṃ sāmāny ṛco vāpi na yajūṃṣi vicakṣaṇa
c trāyante karmaṇaḥ pāpān na te mithyā bravīmy aham
a na chandāṃsi vṛjināt tārayanti
māyāvinaṃ māyayā vartamānam
c nīḍaṃ śakuntā iva jātapakṣāś
chandāṃsy enaṃ prajahaty antakāle
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a na ced vedā vedavidaṃ śaktās trātuṃ vicakṣaṇa
c atha kasmāt pralāpo 'yaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ sanātanaḥ
 sanatsujāta uvāca
 tasyaiva nāmādiviśeṣarūpair
 idaṃ jagad bhāti mahānubhāva
 nirdiśya samyak pravadanti vedās
 tad viśvavairūpyam udāharanti
 tadartham uktaṃ tapa etad ijyā
 tābhyām asau puṇyam upaiti vidvān
 puṇyena pāpaṃ vinihatya paścāt
 saṃjāyate jñānavidīpitātmā
 jñānena cātmānam upaiti vidvān
 athānyathā vargaphalānukāṅkṣī
 asmin kṛtaṃ tat parigṛhya sarvam
 amutra bhuṅkte punar eti mārgam
 tapas tapyati yo 'raṇye munir mūlaphalāśanaḥ
 brāhmaṇānāṃ tapaḥ svṛddham anyeṣāṃ tāvad eva tat
 etat samṛddham atyṛddhaṃ tapo bhavati kevalam
a asmiṃl loke tapas taptaṃ phalam anyatra dṛśyate
c brāhmaṇānām ime lokā ṛddhe tapasi saṃyatāḥ
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a kathaṃ samṛddham apy ṛddhaṃ tapo bhavati kevalam
c sanatsujāta tad brūhi yathā vidyāma tad vayam
d sanatsujāta uvāca
d niṣkalmaṣaṃ tapas tv etat kevalaṃ paricakṣate
d etat samṛddham apy ṛddhaṃ tapo bhavati nānyathā
d tapomūlam idaṃ sarvaṃ yan māṃ pṛcchasi kṣatriya
d dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
d tapasā vedavidvāṃsaḥ paraṃ tv amṛtam āpnuyuḥ
d kalmaṣaṃ tapaso brūhi śrutaṃ niṣkalmaṣaṃ tapaḥ
d sanatsujāta yenedaṃ vidyāṃ guhyaṃ sanātanam
d śrīr evam ekā yo 'dhīte tac ca tāvac ca tatsamam
 sanatsujāta uvāca
a krodhādayo dvādaśa yasya doṣās
tathā nṛśaṃsādi ṣaḍ atra rājan
c dharmādayo dvādaśa cātatānāḥ
śāstre guṇā ye viditā dvijānām
a krodhaḥ kāmo lobhamohau vivitsā
kṛpāsūyā mānaśokau spṛhā ca
c īrṣyā jugupsā ca manuṣyadoṣā
varjyāḥ sadā dvādaśaite nareṇa
a ekaikam ete rājendra manuṣyān paryupāsate
c lipsamāno 'ntaraṃ teṣāṃ mṛgāṇām iva lubdhakaḥ
a vikatthanaḥ spṛhayālur manasvī
bibhrat kopaṃ capalo 'rakṣaṇaś ca
c ete prāptāḥ ṣaṇ narān pāpadharmān
prakurvate nota santaḥ sudurge
a saṃbhogasaṃvid dviṣam edhamāno
dattānutāpī kṛpaṇo 'balīyān
c vargapraśaṃsī vanitāsu dveṣṭā
ete 'pare sapta nṛśaṃsadharmāḥ
a dharmaś ca satyaṃ ca damas tapaś ca
amātsaryaṃ hrīs titikṣānasūyā
c yajñaś ca dānaṃ ca dhṛtiḥ śrutaṃ ca
mahāvratā dvādaśa brāhmaṇasya
a yas tv etebhyaḥ pravased dvādaśebhyaḥ
sarvām apīmāṃ pṛthivīṃ praśiṣyāt
c tribhir dvābhyām ekato vā viśiṣṭo
nāsya svam astīti sa veditavyaḥ
a damas tyāgo 'pramādaś ca eteṣv amṛtam āhitam
c tāni satyamukhāny āhur brāhmaṇā ye manīṣiṇaḥ
d doṣatyāgo 'pramādaḥ syāt sa cāpy aṣṭaguṇo mataḥ
a damo 'ṣṭādaśadoṣaḥ syāt pratikūlaṃ kṛtākṛte
c anṛtaṃ cābhyasūyā ca kāmārthau ca tathā spṛhā
a krodhaḥ śokas tathā tṛṣṇā lobhaḥ paiśunyam eva ca
c matsaraś ca vivitsā ca paritāpas tathā ratiḥ
a apasmāraḥ sātivādas tathā saṃbhāvanātmani
b lokadveṣo 'bhimānaś ca vivādaḥ prāṇipīḍanam
b parivādo 'tivādaś ca paritāpo 'kṣamā dhṛtiḥ
b asiddhiḥ pāpakṛtyaṃ ca hiṃsā ceti prakīrtitāḥ
c etair vimukto doṣair yaḥ sa damaḥ sadbhir ucyate
d mado 'ṣṭādaśadoṣaḥ syāt tyāgo bhavati ṣaḍguṇaḥ
d viparyayāḥ smṛtā ete madadoṣā udāhṛtāḥ
d śreyāṃs tu ṣaḍvidhas tyāgas tṛtīyas tatra duṣkaraḥ
d tena duḥkhaṃ taranty eva tasmiṃs tyakte jitaṃ bhavet
d doṣā damasya ye proktās tān doṣān parivarjayet
a śreyāṃs tu ṣaḍvidhas tyāgaḥ priyaṃ prāpya na hṛṣyati
c apriye tu samutpanne vyathāṃ jātu na cārcchati
a iṣṭān dārāṃś ca putrāṃś ca na cānyaṃ yad vaco bhavet
c arhate yācamānāya pradeyaṃ tad vaco bhavet
d iṣṭāpūrtaṃ dvitīyaṃ syān nityaṃ vairāgyayogataḥ
d kāmatyāgaś ca rājendra sa tṛtīya iti smṛtaḥ
d apramādī bhaved etaiḥ sa cāpy aṣṭaguṇo mahān
d satyaṃ dhyānaṃ samādhānaṃ codyaṃ vairāgyam eva ca
d asteyo brahmacaryaṃ ca tathāsaṃgraha eva ca
d evaṃ doṣā madasyoktās tān doṣān parivarjayet
d doṣatyāgo 'pramādaḥ syāt sa cāpy aṣṭaguṇo mataḥ
d tāṃs tu satyamukhān āhuḥ satye hy amṛtam āhitam
d satyātmā bhava rājendra satye lokāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ
d nivṛttenaiva doṣeṇa tapovratam ihācaret
d etad dhātṛkṛtaṃ vṛttaṃ satyam eva satāṃ vratam
e apy avācyaṃ vadaty eva sa tṛtīyo guṇaḥ smṛtaḥ
a tyaktair dravyair yo bhavati nopayuṅkte ca kāmataḥ
b na ca dravyais tad bhavati nopayuktaiś ca kāmataḥ
c na ca karmasu tad dhīnaḥ śiṣyabuddhir naro yathā
e sarvair eva guṇair yukto dravyavān api yo bhavet
f ṣaṭprakāram imaṃ tyāgaṃ buddhvānyan nāvaśiṣyate
a apramādo 'ṣṭadoṣaḥ syāt tān doṣān parivarjayet
c indriyebhyaś ca pañcabhyo manasaś caiva bhārata
e atītānāgatebhyaś ca mukto hy etaiḥ sukhī bhavet
a doṣair etair vimuktaṃ tu guṇair etaiḥ samanvitam
c etat samṛddham apy ṛddhaṃ tapo bhavati kevalam
e yan māṃ pṛcchasi rājendra kiṃ bhūyaḥ śrotum icchasi
f etat pāpaharaṃ śuddhaṃ janmamṛtyujarāpaham
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a ākhyānapañcamair vedair bhūyiṣṭhaṃ kathyate janaḥ
c tathaivānye caturvedās trivedāś ca tathāpare
a dvivedāś caikavedāś ca anṛcaś ca tathāpare
c teṣāṃ tu katamaḥ sa syād yam ahaṃ veda brāhmaṇam
 sanatsujāta uvāca
a ekasya vedasyājñānād vedās te bahavo 'bhavan
c satyasyaikasya rājendra satye kaś cid avasthitaḥ
e evaṃ vedam anutsādya prajñāṃ mahati kurvate
a dānam adhyayanaṃ yajño lobhād etat pravartate
c satyāt pracyavamānānāṃ saṃkalpo vitatho bhavet
a tato yajñaḥ pratāyeta satyasyaivāvadhāraṇāt
c manasānyasya bhavati vācānyasyota karmaṇā
e saṃkalpasiddhaḥ puruṣaḥ saṃkalpān adhitiṣṭhati
a anaibhṛtyena vai tasya dīkṣitavratam ācaret
c nāmaitad dhātunirvṛttaṃ satyam eva satāṃ param
e jñānaṃ vai nāma pratyakṣaṃ parokṣaṃ jāyate tapaḥ
a vidyād bahu paṭhantaṃ tu bahupāṭhīti brāhmaṇam
c tasmāt kṣatriya mā maṃsthā jalpitenaiva brāhmaṇam
e ya eva satyān nāpaiti sa jñeyo brāhmaṇas tvayā
f chandāṃsi nāma dvipadāṃ variṣṭha
f svacchandayogena bhavanti tatra
f chandovidas tena ca tān adhītya
f gatā hi vedasya na vedyam āryāḥ
f na vedānāṃ veditā kaś cid asti
f vedyena vedaṃ na vidur na vedyam
f yo veda vedaṃ sa ca veda vedyaṃ
f yo veda vedyaṃ na sa veda satyam
f yo veda vedān sa ca veda vedyaṃ
f na taṃ vidur vedavido na vedāḥ
f tathāpi vedena vidanti vedaṃ
f ye brāhmaṇā vedavido bhavanti
f dhāmāṃśabhāgasya tathā hi vedā
f yathā hi śākhā ca mahīruhasya
f saṃvedane caiva yathāmananti
f tasmin hi satye paramātmano 'rthe
a chandāṃsi nāma kṣatriya tāny atharvā
jagau purastād ṛṣisarga eṣaḥ
c chandovidas te ya u tān adhītya
na vedyavedasya vidur na vedyam
a na vedānāṃ veditā kaś cid asti
kaś cid vedān budhyate vāpi rājan
c yo veda vedān na sa veda vedyaṃ
satye sthito yas tu sa veda vedyam
a abhijānāmi brāhmaṇam ākhyātāraṃ vicakṣaṇam
b evaṃ yo hi vijānāti sa jānāti paraṃ hi tat
b paraṃ hi tat paraṃ brahma jānāty eva ca brāhmaṇaḥ
b yo vai vijānāti paraṃ mayoktaṃ
b sa vai vijānāti paraṃ krameṇa
b nāsya paryeṣaṇaṃ gacchet pratyarthiṣu kathaṃ cana
b avicinvann imaṃ vede tataḥ paśyati taṃ prabhum
c yaś chinnavicikitsaḥ sann ācaṣṭe sarvasaṃśayān
a tasya paryeṣaṇaṃ gacchet prācīnaṃ nota dakṣiṇam
c nārvācīnaṃ kutas tiryaṅ nādiśaṃ tu kathaṃ cana
a tūṣṇīṃbhūta upāsīta na ceṣṭen manasā api
c abhyāvarteta brahmāsya antarātmani vai śritam
a maunād dhi sa munir bhavati nāraṇyavasanān muniḥ
c akṣaraṃ tat tu yo veda sa muniḥ śreṣṭha ucyate
a sarvārthānāṃ vyākaraṇād vaiyākaraṇa ucyate
b tan mūlato vyākaraṇaṃ vyākarotīti tat tathā
c pratyakṣadarśī lokānāṃ sarvadarśī bhaven naraḥ
a satye vai brāhmaṇas tiṣṭhan brahma paśyati kṣatriya
b jñānādiṣu sthito 'py evaṃ kṣatriya brahma paśyati
c vedānāṃ cānupūrvyeṇa etad vidvan bravīmi te
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a sanatsujāta yad imāṃ parārthāṃ
brāhmīṃ vācaṃ pravadasi viśvarūpām
c parāṃ hi kāmeṣu sudurlabhāṃ kathāṃ
tad brūhi me vākyam etat kumāra
 sanatsujāta uvāca
a naitad brahma tvaramāṇena labhyaṃ
yan māṃ pṛcchasy abhihṛṣyasy atīva
b buddhau pralīne manasi pracintyā
b vidyā hi sā brahmacaryeṇa labhyā
c avyaktavidyām abhidhāsye purāṇīṃ
buddhyā ca teṣāṃ brahmacaryeṇa siddhām
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a avyaktavidyām iti yat sanātanīṃ
bravīṣi tvaṃ brahmacaryeṇa siddhām
b ādyāṃ vidyāṃ vadasi hi satyarūpāṃ
b yā prāpyate brahmacaryeṇa sadbhiḥ
b yāṃ prāpyaitāṃ martyalokaṃ tyajanti
b yā vai vidyā guruvṛddheṣu nityā
b dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
b brahmacaryeṇa yā vidyā śakyā veditum añjasā
b tat kathaṃ brahmacaryaṃ syād etad vidvan bravīhi me
c anārabhyā vasatīhārya kāle
kathaṃ brāhmaṇyam amṛtatvaṃ labheta
 sanatsujāta uvāca
a ye 'smiṃl loke vijayantīha kāmān
brāhmīṃ sthitim anutitikṣamāṇāḥ
c ta ātmānaṃ nirharantīha dehān
muñjād iṣīkām iva sattvasaṃsthāḥ
d yadi sarve pramucyante kāmā ye hṛdi saṃsthitāḥ
d atha mṛtyor mṛta iti tatra brahma samaśnute
a śarīram etau kurutaḥ pitā mātā ca bhārata
c ācāryaśāstā yā jātiḥ sā satyā sājarāmarā
d ācāryatas tu yaj janma tat satyaṃ vai tathāmṛtam
d tasmāt tām eva yatnena buddhimān pratipadyate
a ācāryayonim iha ye praviśya
bhūtvā garbhaṃ brahmacaryaṃ caranti
c ihaiva te śāstrakārā bhavanti
prahāya dehaṃ paramaṃ yānti yogam
a ya āvṛṇoty avitathena karṇā
vṛtaṃ kurvann amṛtaṃ saṃprayacchan
c taṃ manyeta pitaraṃ mātaraṃ ca
tasmai na druhyet kṛtam asya jānan
a guruṃ śiṣyo nityam abhimanyamānaḥ
svādhyāyam icchec chucir apramattaḥ
c mānaṃ na kuryān na dadhīta roṣam
eṣa prathamo brahmacaryasya pādaḥ
d śiṣyavṛttikrameṇaiva vidyām āpnoti yaḥ śuciḥ
d brahmacaryavratasyāsya prathamaḥ pāda ucyate
a ācāryasya priyaṃ kuryāt prāṇair api dhanair api
c karmaṇā manasā vācā dvitīyaḥ pāda ucyate
a samā gurau yathā vṛttir gurupatnyāṃ tathā bhavet
c yathoktakārī priyakṛt tṛtīyaḥ pāda ucyate
d ācāryeṇa kṛtaṃ jñātvā bhāvito 'smīti manyate
d taṃ guruṃ prati hṛṣṭaḥ saṃstṛtīyaḥ pāda ucyate
d ācāryeṇātmakṛtaṃ vijānañ
d jñātvā cārthaṃ bhāvito 'smīty anena
d yan manyate taṃ prati hṛṣṭabuddhiḥ
d sa vai tṛtīyo brahmacaryasya pādaḥ
a nācāryāyehopakṛtvā pravādaṃ
prājñaḥ kurvīta naitad ahaṃ karomi
c itīva manyeta na bhāṣayeta
sa vai caturtho brahmacaryasya pādaḥ
d evaṃ vasantaṃ yad upaplaved dhi
d nācāryāya kṛtam iti cābhimānāt
d prājño manye naitad ahaṃ karomi
d sa vai caturtho brahmacaryasya pādaḥ
d kālena pādaṃ labhate tathārthaṃ
d tataś ca pādaṃ guruyogataś ca
d utsāhayogena ca pādam ṛcchec
d chāstreṇa pādaṃ ca tato 'bhiyāti
d jñānādayo dvādaśa yasya rūpam
d anyāni cāṅgāni tathā balaṃ ca
d ācāryayoge phalatīti cāhur
d brahmārthayogena ca brahmacaryam
a evaṃ vasantaṃ yad upaplaved dhanam
ācāryāya tad anuprayacchet
c satāṃ vṛttiṃ bahuguṇām evam eti
guroḥ putre bhavati ca vṛttir eṣā
a evaṃ vasan sarvato vardhatīha
bahūn putrāṃl labhate ca pratiṣṭhām
c varṣanti cāsmai pradiśo diśaś ca
vasanty asmin brahmacarye janāś ca
a etena brahmacaryeṇa devā devatvam āpnuvan
c ṛṣayaś ca mahābhāgā brahmalokaṃ manīṣiṇaḥ
a gandharvāṇām anenaiva rūpam apsarasām abhūt
c etena brahmacaryeṇa sūryo ahnāya jāyate
d ākāṅkṣārthasya saṃyogād rasabhedārthinām iva
d evaṃ hy etat samājñāya tādṛg bhāvaṃ gatā ime
a ya āśayet pāṭayec cāpi rājan
sarvaṃ śarīraṃ tapasā tapyamānaḥ
c etenāsau bālyam atyeti vidvān
mṛtyuṃ tathā rodhayaty antakāle
a antavantaḥ kṣatriya te jayanti
lokāñ janāḥ karmaṇā nirmitena
c brahmaiva vidvāṃs tena abhyeti sarvaṃ
nānyaḥ panthā ayanāya vidyate
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a ābhāti śuklam iva lohitam iva
atho kṛṣṇam athāñjanaṃ kādravaṃ vā
c tad brāhmaṇaḥ paśyati yo 'tra vidvān
kathaṃrūpaṃ tad amṛtam akṣaraṃ padam
 sanatsujāta uvāca
a nābhāti śuklam iva lohitam iva
atho kṛṣṇam āyasam arkavarṇam
c na pṛthivyāṃ tiṣṭhati nāntarikṣe
naitat samudre salilaṃ bibharti
a na tārakāsu na ca vidyud āśritaṃ
na cābhreṣu dṛśyate rūpam asya
c na cāpi vāyau na ca devatāsu
na tac candre dṛśyate nota sūrye
a naivarkṣu tan na yajuḥṣu nāpy atharvasu
na caiva dṛśyaty amaleṣu sāmasu
c rathaṃtare bārhate cāpi rājan
mahāvrate naiva dṛśyed dhruvaṃ tat
a apāraṇīyaṃ tamasaḥ parastāt
tad antako 'py eti vināśakāle
c aṇīyarūpaṃ kṣuradhārayā tan
mahac ca rūpaṃ tv api parvatebhyaḥ
a sā pratiṣṭhā tad amṛtaṃ lokās tad brahma tad yaśaḥ
c bhūtāni jajñire tasmāt pralayaṃ yānti tatra ca
a anāmayaṃ tan mahad udyataṃ yaśo
vāco vikārān kavayo vadanti
c tasmiñ jagat sarvam idaṃ pratiṣṭhitaṃ
ye tad vidur amṛtās te bhavanti
d sanatsujāta uvāca
d śokaḥ krodhaś ca lobhaś ca kāmo mānaḥ parāsutā
d īrṣyā moho vivitsā ca kṛpāsūyā jugupsutā
d dvādaśaite mahādoṣā manuṣyaprāṇanāśanāḥ
d ekaikam ete rājendra manuṣyān paryupāsate
d yair āviṣṭo naraḥ pāpaṃ mūḍhasaṃjño vyavasyati
d spṛhayālur ugraḥ paruṣo vāvadānyaḥ
d krodhaṃ bibhran manasā vai vikatthī
d nṛśaṃsadharmāḥ ṣaḍ ime janā vai
d prāpyāpy arthaṃ nota sabhājayante
d saṃbhogasaṃvid viṣamo 'timānī
d dattvā vikatthī kṛpaṇo durbalaś ca
d bahupraśaṃsī vanitādviṭ sadaiva
d saptaivoktāḥ pāpaśīlā nṛśaṃsāḥ
d dharmaś ca satyaṃ ca tapo damaś ca
d amātsaryaṃ hrīs titikṣānasūyā
d dānaṃ śrutaṃ caiva dhṛtiḥ kṣamā ca
d mahāvratā dvādaśa brāhmaṇasya
d yo naitebhyaḥ pracyaved dvādaśabhyaḥ
d sarvām apīmāṃ pṛthivīṃ sa śiṣyāt
d tribhir dvābhyām ekato vārthito yo
d nāsya svam astīti ca veditavyam
d damas tyāgo 'thāpramāda ity eteṣv amṛtaṃ sthitam
d etāni brahmamukhyānāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ manīṣiṇām
d sad vāsad vā parīvādo brāhmaṇasya na śasyate
d narakapratiṣṭhās te vai syur ya evaṃ kurvate narāḥ
d mado 'ṣṭādaśadoṣaḥ sa syāt purā yo 'prakīrtitaḥ
d lokadveṣyaṃ prātikūlyam abhyasūyā mṛṣāvacaḥ
d kāmakrodhau pāratantryaṃ parivādo 'tha paiśunam
d arthahānir vivitsā ca mātsaryaṃ prāṇipīḍanam
d īrṣyā moho 'tivādaś ca saṃjñānāśo 'bhyasūyitā
d tasmāt prājño na mādyeta sadā hy etad vigarhitam
d sauhṛde vai ṣaḍ guṇā veditavyāḥ
d priye hṛṣyanty apriye ca vyathante
d syād ātmanaḥ suciraṃ yācate yo
d dadāty ayācyam api deyaṃ khalu syāt
d iṣṭān putrān vibhavān svāṃś ca dārān
d abhyarthitaś cārhati śuddhabhāvaḥ
d tyaktadravyaḥ saṃvasen neha kāmād
d bhuṅkte karma svāśiṣaṃ bādhate ca
d dravyavān guṇavān evaṃ tyāgī bhavati sāttvikaḥ
d pañca bhūtāni pañcabhyo nivartayati tādṛśaḥ
d etat samṛddham apy ūrdhvaṃ tapo bhavati kevalam
d sattvāt pracyavamānānāṃ saṃkalpena samāhitam
d yato yajñāḥ pravardhante satyasyaivāvarodhanāt
d manasānyasya bhavati vācānyasyātha karmaṇā
d saṃkalpasiddhaṃ puruṣam asaṃkalpo 'dhitiṣṭhati
d brāhmaṇasya viśeṣeṇa kiṃ cānyad api me śruṇu
d adhyāpayen mahad etad yaśasyaṃ
d vāco vikāraṃ kavayo vadanti
d asmin yoge sarvam idaṃ pratiṣṭhitaṃ
d ye tad vidur amṛtās te bhavanti
d na karmaṇā sukṛtenaiva rājan
d satyaṃ vadej juhuyād vā yajed vā
d naitena bālo 'mṛtyum abhyeti rājan
d ratiṃ cāsau na labhaty antakāle
d tūṣṇīm eka upāsīta ceṣṭeta manasāpi na
d tathā saṃstutinindābhyāṃ prītiroṣau vivarjayet
d atraiva tiṣṭhan kṣatriya brahmāviśati paśyati
d vedeṣu cānupūrvyeṇa etad vidvan bravīmi te
d tad etad ahnā saṃsthitaṃ bhāti sarvaṃ
d tad ātmavit paśyati jñānayogāt
d tasmiñ jagat sarvam idaṃ pratiṣṭhitaṃ
d ya etad vidur amṛtās te bhavanti
 sanatsujāta uvāca
a yat tac chukraṃ mahaj jyotir dīpyamānaṃ mahad yaśaḥ
c tad vai devā upāsante yasmād arko virājate
e yoginas taṃ prapaśyanti bhagavantaṃ sanātanam
a śukrād brahma prabhavati brahma śukreṇa vardhate
c tac chukraṃ jyotiṣāṃ madhye 'taptaṃ tapati tāpanam
e yoginas taṃ prapaśyanti bhagavantaṃ sanātanam
a āpo 'tha adbhyaḥ salilasya madhye
ubhau devau śiśriyāte 'ntarikṣe
c sa sadhrīcīḥ sa viṣūcīr vasānā
ubhe bibharti pṛthivīṃ divaṃ ca
e yoginas taṃ prapaśyanti bhagavantaṃ sanātanam
f apa eva sasarjādau tāsu vīryam athāsṛjat
f tad aṇḍam abhavad dhaimaṃ sahasrāṃśusamaprabham
f tasmiñ jajñe svayaṃ brahmā sarvalokapitāmahaḥ
f yoginas taṃ prapaśyanti bhagavantaṃ sanātanam
a ubhau ca devau pṛthivīṃ divaṃ ca
diśaś ca śukraṃ bhuvanaṃ bibharti
c tasmād diśaḥ saritaś ca sravanti
tasmāt samudrā vihitā mahāntaḥ
e yoginas taṃ prapaśyanti bhagavantaṃ sanātanam
a cakre rathasya tiṣṭhantaṃ dhruvasyāvyayakarmaṇaḥ
c ketumantaṃ vahanty aśvās taṃ divyam ajaraṃ divi
e yoginas taṃ prapaśyanti bhagavantaṃ sanātanam
a na sādṛśye tiṣṭhati rūpam asya
na cakṣuṣā paśyati kaś cid enam
c manīṣayātho manasā hṛdā ca
ya evaṃ vidur amṛtās te bhavanti
d yasya deve parā bhaktir yathā deve tathā gurau
d tasya te kathitā hy arthāḥ prakāśante mahātmanaḥ
e yoginas taṃ prapaśyanti bhagavantaṃ sanātanam
a dvādaśapūgāṃ saritaṃ devarakṣitam
c madhu īśantas tadā saṃcaranti ghoram
e yoginas taṃ prapaśyanti bhagavantaṃ sanātanam
a tad ardhamāsaṃ pibati saṃcitya bhramaro madhu
c īśānaḥ sarvabhūteṣu havirbhūtam akalpayat
e yoginas taṃ prapaśyanti bhagavantaṃ sanātanam
a hiraṇyaparṇam aśvattham abhipatya apakṣakāḥ
c te tatra pakṣiṇo bhūtvā prapatanti yathādiśam
e yoginas taṃ prapaśyanti bhagavantaṃ sanātanam
a pūrṇāt pūrṇāny uddharanti pūrṇāt pūrṇāni cakrire
c haranti pūrṇāt pūrṇāni pūrṇam evāvaśiṣyate
e yoginas taṃ prapaśyanti bhagavantaṃ sanātanam
a tasmād vai vāyur āyātas tasmiṃś ca prayataḥ sadā
c tasmād agniś ca somaś ca tasmiṃś ca prāṇa ātataḥ
c   yasmiṃś ca pralayaṃ gatau
c tasmād vai vāyur ātataḥ
d yoginas taṃ prapaśyanti bhagavantaṃ sanātanam
d yasmād vai vāyur āyāto yasmāc ca prāṇa āgataḥ
d tat pratiṣṭhās tad amṛtaṃ lokās tad brahma tad yaśaḥ
d bhūtāni jajñire tasmāt pralayaṃ yānti tatra ca
d yoginas taṃ prapaśyanti bhagavantaṃ sanātanam
a sarvam eva tato vidyāt tat tad vaktuṃ na śaknumaḥ
c yoginas taṃ prapaśyanti bhagavantaṃ sanātanam
a apānaṃ girati prāṇaḥ prāṇaṃ girati candramāḥ
c ādityo girate candram ādityaṃ girate paraḥ
e yoginas taṃ prapaśyanti bhagavantaṃ sanātanam
a ekaṃ pādaṃ notkṣipati salilād dhaṃsa uccaran
c taṃ cet satatam ṛtvijaṃ na mṛtyur nāmṛtaṃ bhavet
e yoginas taṃ prapaśyanti bhagavantaṃ sanātanam
f aṅguṣṭhamātraḥ puruṣo 'ntarātmā
f liṅgasya yogena sa yāti nityam
f tam īśam īḍyam anukalpam ādyaṃ
f paśyanti mūḍhā na virājamānam
f yoginas taṃ prapaśyanti bhagavantaṃ sanātanam
f nātmānam ātmastham avaiti mūḍhaḥ
f saṃsārakūpe parivartate yaḥ
f tyaktvātmarūpaṃ viṣayāṃś ca bhuṅkte
f sa vai jano gardabha eva sākṣāt
f yoginas taṃ prapaśyanti bhagavantaṃ sanātanam
a evaṃ devo mahātmā sa pāvakaṃ puruṣo giran
c yo vai taṃ puruṣaṃ veda tasyehātmā na riṣyate
e yoginas taṃ prapaśyanti bhagavantaṃ sanātanam
a yaḥ sahasraṃ sahasrāṇāṃ pakṣān saṃtatya saṃpatet
c madhyame madhya āgacched api cet syān manojavaḥ
e yoginas taṃ prapaśyanti bhagavantaṃ sanātanam
a na darśane tiṣṭhati rūpam asya
paśyanti cainaṃ suviśuddhasattvāḥ
c hito manīṣī manasābhipaśyed
ye taṃ śrayeyur amṛtās te bhavanti
e yoginas taṃ prapaśyanti bhagavantaṃ sanātanam
a gūhanti sarpā iva gahvarāṇi
svaśikṣayā svena vṛttena martyāḥ
c teṣu pramuhyanti janā vimūḍhā
yathādhvānaṃ mohayante bhayāya
e yoginas taṃ prapaśyanti bhagavantaṃ sanātanam
a sadā sadāsatkṛtaḥ syān na mṛtyur amṛtaṃ kutaḥ
c satyānṛte satyasamānabandhane
sataś ca yonir asataś caika eva
e yoginas taṃ prapaśyanti bhagavantaṃ sanātanam
a na sādhunā nota asādhunā vā
samānam etad dṛśyate mānuṣeṣu
c samānam etad amṛtasya vidyād
evaṃyukto madhu tad vai parīpset
e yoginas taṃ prapaśyanti bhagavantaṃ sanātanam
a nāsyātivādā hṛdayaṃ tāpayanti
nānadhītaṃ nāhutam agnihotram
c mano brāhmīṃ laghutām ādadhīta
prajñānam asya nāma dhīrā labhante
e yoginas taṃ prapaśyanti bhagavantaṃ sanātanam
a evaṃ yaḥ sarvabhūteṣu ātmānam anupaśyati
c anyatrānyatra yukteṣu kiṃ sa śocet tataḥ param
a yathodapāne mahati sarvataḥ saṃplutodake
c evaṃ sarveṣu vedeṣu brāhmaṇasya vijānataḥ
a aṅguṣṭhamātraḥ puruṣo mahātmā
na dṛśyate 'sau hṛdaye niviṣṭaḥ
c ajaś caro divārātram atandritaś ca
sa taṃ matvā kavir āste prasannaḥ
a aham evāsmi vo mātā pitā putro 'smy ahaṃ punaḥ
c ātmāham api sarvasya yac ca nāsti yad asti ca
a pitāmaho 'smi sthaviraḥ pitā putraś ca bhārata
c mamaiva yūyam ātmasthā na me yūyaṃ na vo 'py aham
a ātmaiva sthānaṃ mama janma cātmā
vedaprokto 'ham ajarapratiṣṭhaḥ
a aṇor aṇīyān sumanāḥ sarvabhūteṣu jāgṛmi
c pitaraṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ puṣkare nihitaṃ viduḥ
d viṣaṃ bhuṅkṣva sahāmātyair vināśaṃ prāpnuhi dhruvam
d rājan kena vinā nābhyāṃ sphītaṃ kṛṣṇājinaṃ varam
 namaḥ puṃse purāṇāya pūrṇānandāya viṣṇave
 nirastanikhiladhvāntatejase viśvahetave
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a evaṃ sanatsujātena vidureṇa ca dhīmatā

a tasyāṃ rajanyāṃ vyuṣṭāyāṃ rājānaḥ sarva eva te

a śuśrūṣamāṇāḥ pārthānāṃ vaco dharmārthasaṃhitam

a sudhāvadātāṃ vistīrṇāṃ kanakājirabhūṣitām

c aśvatthāmā vikarṇaś ca somadattaś ca bāhlikaḥ
a viduraś ca mahāprājño yuyutsuś ca mahārathaḥ
c sarve ca sahitāḥ śūrāḥ pārthivā bharatarṣabha

c durmukho duḥsahaḥ karṇa ulūko 'tha viviṃśatiḥ
d duḥśāsanaḥ saubalaś ca śakuniḥ śalatośalau
d ete cānye ca bahavaḥ pārthivā bharatarṣabha
a kururājaṃ puraskṛtya duryodhanam amarṣaṇam

a āsanastheṣu sarveṣu teṣu rājasu bhārata

c dūto nas tūrṇam āyātaḥ saindhavaiḥ sādhuvāhibhiḥ
a upayāya tu sa kṣipraṃ rathāt praskandya kuṇḍalī
c praviveśa sabhāṃ pūrṇāṃ mahīpālair mahātmabhiḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a prāpto 'smi pāṇḍavān gatvā tad vijānīta kauravāḥ
c yathāvayaḥ kurūn sarvān pratinandanti pāṇḍavāḥ
a abhivādayanti vṛddhāṃś ca vayasyāṃś ca vayasyavat
c yūnaś cābhyavadan pārthāḥ pratipūjya yathāvayaḥ
a yathāhaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭreṇa śiṣṭaḥ pūrvam ito gataḥ
c abruvaṃ pāṇḍavān gatvā tan nibodhata pārthivāḥ
d abrūtāṃ tāta dharmeṇa vāsudevadhanaṃjayau
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a pṛcchāmi tvāṃ saṃjaya rājamadhye
kim abravīd vākyam adīnasattvaḥ
c dhanaṃjayas tāta yudhāṃ praṇetā
durātmanāṃ jīvitacchin mahātmā
 saṃjaya uvāca
a duryodhano vācam imāṃ śṛṇotu
yad abravīd arjuno yotsyamānaḥ
c yudhiṣṭhirasyānumate mahātmā

a anvatrasto bāhuvīryaṃ vidāna

c avocan māṃ yotsyamānaḥ kirīṭī

d saṃśṛṇvatas tasya durbhāṣiṇo vai
d durātmanaḥ sūtaputrasya sūta
d yo yoddhum āśaṃsati māṃ sadaiva
d mandaprajñaḥ kālapakvo 'timūḍhaḥ
a ye vai rājānaḥ pāṇḍavāyodhanāya

a yeṣāṃ yuddhaṃ bhīmasenārjunābhyāṃ
tathāśvibhyāṃ vāsudevena caiva
b tathā pāñcālaiḥ sṛñjayaiś cāpi rājan
c śaineyena dhruvam āttāyudhena
dhṛṣṭadyumnenātha śikhaṇḍinā ca

yo 'padhyānān nirdahed gāṃ divaṃ ca
a taiś ced yuddhaṃ manyate dhārtarāṣṭro
nirvṛtto 'rthaḥ sakalaḥ pāṇḍavānām
b nūnaṃ hy etān nirdahed gāṇḍivaṃ ca
c mā tat kārṣīḥ pāṇḍavārthāya hetor

a yāṃ tāṃ vane duḥkhaśayyām uvāsa
pravrājitaḥ pāṇḍavo dharmacārī
b tapodamābhyāṃ dharmaguptyā dhanena
c āśiṣyate duḥkhatarām anarthām

a hriyā jñānena tapasā damena

a ārtasvaraṃ hanyamānaṃ hataṃ ca
vikīrṇakeśāsthikapālasaṃgham
c prajāpateḥ karma yathārdhaniṣṭhitaṃ
tadā dṛṣṭvā tapsyate mandabuddhiḥ
a yadā rathe gāṇḍivaṃ vāsudevaṃ
divyaṃ śaṅkhaṃ pāñcajanyaṃ hayāṃś ca
b yadā mūrvyāṃ mūlaniḥśeṣam ugraṃ
b mahāśabdaṃ vajraniṣpeṣatulyam
b dodhūyamānasya mahāraṇe mayā
b gāñjīvanādaṃ śroṣyate mandabuddhiḥ
c tūṇāv akṣayyau devadattaṃ ca māṃ ca
draṣṭā yuddhe dhārtarāṣṭraḥ sametān
a udvartayan dasyusaṃghān sametān
pravartayan yugam anyad yugānte
c yadā dhakṣyāmy agnivat kauraveyāṃs
tadā taptā dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ saputraḥ
a sahabhrātā sahaputraḥ sasainyo
bhraṣṭaiśvaryaḥ krodhavaśo 'lpacetāḥ
c darpasyānte vihite vepamānaḥ
paścān mandas tapsyati dhārtarāṣṭraḥ
a pūrvāhṇe māṃ kṛtajapyaṃ kadā cid
vipraḥ provācodakānte manojñam
c kartavyaṃ te duṣkaraṃ karma pārtha
yoddhavyaṃ te śatrubhiḥ savyasācin
a indro vā te harivān vajrahastaḥ
purastād yātu samare 'rīn vinighnan
c sugrīvayuktena rathena vā te
paścāt kṛṣṇo rakṣatu vāsudevaḥ
a vavre cāhaṃ vajrahastān mahendrād
asmin yuddhe vāsudevaṃ sahāyam
c sa me labdho dasyuvadhāya kṛṣṇo
manye caitad vihitaṃ daivatair me
a ayudhyamāno manasāpi yasya
jayaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ puruṣasyābhinandet
c dhruvaṃ sarvān so 'bhyatīyād amitrān
sendrān devān mānuṣe nāsti cintā
a sa bāhubhyāṃ sāgaram uttitīrṣen
mahodadhiṃ salilasyāprameyam
c tejasvinaṃ kṛṣṇam atyantaśūraṃ
yuddhena yo vāsudevaṃ jigīṣet
a giriṃ ya iccheta talena bhettuṃ
śiloccayaṃ śvetam atipramāṇam
c tasyaiva pāṇiḥ sanakho viśīryen
na cāpi kiṃ cit sa gires tu kuryāt
a agniṃ samiddhaṃ śamayed bhujābhyāṃ
candraṃ ca sūryaṃ ca nivārayeta
c hared devānām amṛtaṃ prasahya
yuddhena yo vāsudevaṃ jigīṣet
a yo rukmiṇīm ekarathena bhojyām
utsādya rājñāṃ viṣayaṃ prasahya
c uvāha bhāryāṃ yaśasā jvalantīṃ
yasyāṃ jajñe raukmiṇeyo mahātmā
a ayaṃ gāndhārāṃs tarasā saṃpramathya
jitvā putrān nagnajitaḥ samagrān
c baddhaṃ mumoca vinadantaṃ prasahya
sudarśanīyaṃ devatānāṃ lalāmam
a ayaṃ kavāṭe nijaghāna pāṇḍyaṃ
tathā kaliṅgān dantakūre mamarda
c anena dagdhā varṣapūgān vināthā
vārāṇasī nagarī saṃbabhūva
a yaṃ sma yuddhe manyate 'nyair ajeyam
ekalavyaṃ nāma niṣādarājam
c vegeneva śailam abhihatya jambhaḥ
śete sa kṛṣṇena hataḥ parāsuḥ
a tathograsenasya sutaṃ praduṣṭaṃ
vṛṣṇyandhakānāṃ madhyagāṃ tapantam
c apātayad baladevadvitīyo
hatvā dadau cograsenāya rājyam
a ayaṃ saubhaṃ yodhayām āsa khasthaṃ
vibhīṣaṇaṃ māyayā śālvarājam
c saubhadvāri pratyagṛhṇāc chataghnīṃ
dorbhyāṃ ka enaṃ viṣaheta martyaḥ
a prāgjyotiṣaṃ nāma babhūva durgaṃ
puraṃ ghoram asurāṇām asahyam
c mahābalo narakas tatra bhaumo
jahārādityā maṇikuṇḍale śubhe
a na taṃ devāḥ saha śakreṇa sehire
samāgatā āharaṇāya bhītāḥ
c dṛṣṭvā ca te vikramaṃ keśavasya
balaṃ tathaivāstram avāraṇīyam
a jānanto 'sya prakṛtiṃ keśavasya
nyayojayan dasyuvadhāya kṛṣṇam
c sa tat karma pratiśuśrāva duṣkaram
aiśvaryavān siddhiṣu vāsudevaḥ
a nirmocane ṣaṭ sahasrāṇi hatvā
saṃchidya pāśān sahasā kṣurāntān
c muraṃ hatvā vinihatyaugharākṣasaṃ
nirmocanaṃ cāpi jagāma vīraḥ
a tatraiva tenāsya babhūva yuddhaṃ
mahābalenātibalasya viṣṇoḥ
c śete sa kṛṣṇena hataḥ parāsur
vāteneva mathitaḥ karṇikāraḥ
a āhṛtya kṛṣṇo maṇikuṇḍale te
hatvā ca bhaumaṃ narakaṃ muraṃ ca
c śriyā vṛto yaśasā caiva dhīmān
pratyājagāmāpratimaprabhāvaḥ
a tasmai varān adadaṃs tatra devā
dṛṣṭvā bhīmaṃ karma raṇe kṛtaṃ tat
c śramaś ca te yudhyamānasya na syād
ākāśe vā apsu caiva kramaḥ syāt
a śastrāṇi gātre ca na te kramerann
ity eva kṛṣṇaś ca tataḥ kṛtārthaḥ
c evaṃrūpe vāsudeve 'prameye
mahābale guṇasaṃpat sadaiva
a tam asahyaṃ viṣṇum anantavīryam
āśaṃsate dhārtarāṣṭro balena
c yadā hy enaṃ tarkayate durātmā
tac cāpy ayaṃ sahate 'smān samīkṣya
a paryāgataṃ mama kṛṣṇasya caiva
yo manyate kalahaṃ saṃprayujya
c śakyaṃ hartuṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ mamatvaṃ
tad veditā saṃyugaṃ tatra gatvā
a namaskṛtvā śāṃtanavāya rājñe
droṇāyātho sahaputrāya caiva
c śāradvatāyāpratidvandvine ca
yotsyāmy ahaṃ rājyam abhīpsamānaḥ
a dharmeṇāstraṃ niyataṃ tasya manye
yo yotsyate pāṇḍavair dharmacārī
c mithyāglahe nirjitā vai nṛśaṃsaiḥ
saṃvatsarān dvādaśa pāṇḍuputrāḥ
a avāpya kṛcchraṃ vihitaṃ hy araṇye
dīrghaṃ kālaṃ caikam ajñātacaryām
c te hy akasmāj jīvitaṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ
na mṛṣyante dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ padasthāḥ
a te ced asmān yudhyamānāñ jayeyur
devair apīndrapramukhaiḥ sahāyaiḥ
c dharmād adharmaś carito garīyān
iti dhruvaṃ nāsti kṛtaṃ na sādhu
a na ced imaṃ puruṣaṃ karmabaddhaṃ
na ced asmān manyate 'sau viśiṣṭān
c āśaṃse 'haṃ vāsudevadvitīyo
duryodhanaṃ sānubandhaṃ nihantum
a na ced idaṃ karma nareṣu baddhaṃ
na vidyate puruṣasya svakarma
c idaṃ ca tac cāpi samīkṣya nūnaṃ
parājayo dhārtarāṣṭrasya sādhuḥ
a pratyakṣaṃ vaḥ kuravo yad bravīmi
yudhyamānā dhārtarāṣṭrā na santi
c anyatra yuddhāt kuravaḥ parīpsan
na yudhyatāṃ śeṣa ihāsti kaś cit
a hatvā tv ahaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrān sakarṇān
rājyaṃ kurūṇām avajetā samagram
c yad vaḥ kāryaṃ tat kurudhvaṃ yathāsvam
iṣṭān dārān ātmajāṃś copabhuṅkta
a apy evaṃ no brāhmaṇāḥ santi vṛddhā
bahuśrutāḥ śīlavantaḥ kulīnāḥ
c sāṃvatsarā jyotiṣi cāpi yuktā
nakṣatrayogeṣu ca niścayajñāḥ
a uccāvacaṃ daivayuktaṃ rahasyaṃ
divyāḥ praśnā mṛgacakrā muhūrtāḥ
c kṣayaṃ mahāntaṃ kurusṛñjayānāṃ
nivedayante pāṇḍavānāṃ jayaṃ ca
a tathā hi no manyate 'jātaśatruḥ
saṃsiddhārtho dviṣatāṃ nigrahāya
c janārdanaś cāpy aparokṣavidyo
na saṃśayaṃ paśyati vṛṣṇisiṃhaḥ
a ahaṃ ca jānāmi bhaviṣyarūpaṃ
paśyāmi buddhyā svayam apramattaḥ
c dṛṣṭiś ca me na vyathate purāṇī
yudhyamānā dhārtarāṣṭrā na santi
a anālabdhaṃ jṛmbhati gāṇḍivaṃ dhanur
anālabdhā kampati me dhanurjyā
c bāṇāś ca me tūṇamukhād visṛjya
muhur muhur gantum uśanti caiva
a saikyaḥ kośān niḥsarati prasanno
hitveva jīrṇām uragas tvacaṃ svām
c dhvaje vāco raudrarūpā vadanti
kadā ratho yokṣyate te kirīṭin
a gomāyusaṃghāś ca vadanti rātrau
rakṣāṃsy atho niṣpatanty antarikṣāt
c mṛgāḥ śṛgālāḥ śitikaṇṭhāś ca kākā
gṛdhrā baḍāś caiva tarakṣavaś ca
a suparṇapātāś ca patanti paścād
dṛṣṭvā rathaṃ śvetahayaprayuktam
c ahaṃ hy ekaḥ pārthivān sarvayodhāñ
śarān varṣan mṛtyulokaṃ nayeyam
a samādadānaḥ pṛthag astramārgān
yathāgnir iddho gahanaṃ nidāghe
c sthūṇākarṇaṃ pāśupataṃ ca ghoraṃ
tathā brahmāstraṃ yac ca śakro viveda
a vadhe dhṛto vegavataḥ pramuñcan
nāhaṃ prajāḥ kiṃ cid ivāvaśiṣye
c śāntiṃ lapsye paramo hy eṣa bhāvaḥ
sthiro mama brūhi gāvalgaṇe tān
a nityaṃ punaḥ sacivair yair avocad
devān apīndrapramukhān sahāyān
c tair manyate kalahaṃ saṃprayujya
sa dhārtarāṣṭraḥ paśyata moham asya
a vṛddho bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ kṛpaś ca
droṇaḥ saputro viduraś ca dhīmān
c ete sarve yad vadante tad astu
āyuṣmantaḥ kuravaḥ santu sarve
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a samaveteṣu sarveṣu teṣu rājasu bhārata
c duryodhanam idaṃ vākyaṃ bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo 'bravīt
a bṛhaspatiś cośanā ca brahmāṇaṃ paryupasthitau
c marutaś ca sahendreṇa vasavaś ca sahāśvinau
a ādityāś caiva sādhyāś ca ye ca saptarṣayo divi
c viśvāvasuś ca gandharvaḥ śubhāś cāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ
a namaskṛtvopajagmus te lokavṛddhaṃ pitāmaham
c parivārya ca viśveśaṃ paryāsata divaukasaḥ
a teṣāṃ manaś ca tejaś cāpy ādadānau divaukasām
c pūrvadevau vyatikrāntau naranārāyaṇāv ṛṣī
a bṛhaspatiś ca papraccha brāhmaṇaṃ kāv imāv iti
c bhavantaṃ nopatiṣṭhete tau naḥ śaṃsa pitāmaha
 brahmovāca
a yāv etau pṛthivīṃ dyāṃ ca bhāsayantau tapasvinau
c jvalantau rocamānau ca vyāpyātītau mahābalau
a naranārāyaṇāv etau lokāl lokaṃ samāsthitau
c ūrjitau svena tapasā mahāsattvaparākramau
a etau hi karmaṇā lokān nandayām āsatur dhruvau
b dvidhābhūtau mahāprājñau viddhi brahman paraṃtapau
c asurāṇām abhāvāya devagandharvapūjitau
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a jagāma śakras tac chrutvā yatra tau tepatus tapaḥ
c sārdhaṃ devagaṇaiḥ sarvair bṛhaspatipurogamaiḥ
a tadā devāsure ghore bhaye jāte divaukasām
c ayācata mahātmānau naranārāyaṇau varam
a tāv abrūtāṃ vṛṇīṣveti tadā bharatasattama
c athaitāv abravīc chakraḥ sāhyaṃ naḥ kriyatām iti
a tatas tau śakram abrūtāṃ kariṣyāvo yad icchasi
c tābhyāṃ ca sahitaḥ śakro vijigye daityadānavān
a nara indrasya saṃgrāme hatvā śatrūn paraṃtapaḥ
c paulomān kālakhañjāṃś ca sahasrāṇi śatāni ca
a eṣa bhrānte rathe tiṣṭhan bhallenāpaharac chiraḥ
c jambhasya grasamānasya yajñam arjuna āhave
a eṣa pāre samudrasya hiraṇyapuram ārujat
c hatvā ṣaṣṭisahasrāṇi nivātakavacān raṇe
a eṣa devān sahendreṇa jitvā parapuraṃjayaḥ
c atarpayan mahābāhur arjuno jātavedasam
e nārāyaṇas tathaivātra bhūyaso 'nyāñ jaghāna ha
a evam etau mahāvīryau tau paśyata samāgatau
c vāsudevārjunau vīrau samavetau mahārathau
a naranārāyaṇau devau pūrvadevāv iti śrutiḥ
c ajeyau mānuṣe loke sendrair api surāsuraiḥ
a eṣa nārāyaṇaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ phalgunas tu naraḥ smṛtaḥ
c nārāyaṇo naraś caiva sattvam ekaṃ dvidhākṛtam
a etau hi karmaṇā lokān aśnuvāte 'kṣayān dhruvān
c tatra tatraiva jāyete yuddhakāle punaḥ punaḥ
d tasmād etau mahābhāgau prapadya śaraṇaṃ vibho
d śriyaṃ bhuṅkṣva mahābāho saputrajñātibāndhavaḥ
a tasmāt karmaiva kartavyam iti hovāca nāradaḥ
c etad dhi sarvam ācaṣṭa vṛṣṇicakrasya vedavit
a śaṅkhacakragadāhastaṃ yadā drakṣyasi keśavam
c paryādadānaṃ cāstrāṇi bhīmadhanvānam arjunam
a sanātanau mahātmānau kṛṣṇāv ekarathe sthitau
c duryodhana tadā tāta smartāsi vacanaṃ mama
a no ced ayam abhāvaḥ syāt kurūṇāṃ pratyupasthitaḥ
c arthāc ca tāta dharmāc ca tava buddhir upaplutā
a na ced grahīṣyase vākyaṃ śrotāsi subahūn hatān
c tavaiva hi mataṃ sarve kuravaḥ paryupāsate
a trayāṇām eva ca mataṃ tattvam eko 'numanyase
c rāmeṇa caiva śaptasya karṇasya bharatarṣabha
a durjāteḥ sūtaputrasya śakuneḥ saubalasya ca
c tathā kṣudrasya pāpasya bhrātur duḥśāsanasya ca
 karṇa uvāca
a naivam āyuṣmatā vācyaṃ yan mām āttha pitāmaha
c kṣatradharme sthito hy asmi svadharmād anapeyivān
a kiṃ cānyan mayi durvṛttaṃ yena māṃ parigarhase
c na hi me vṛjinaṃ kiṃ cid dhārtarāṣṭrā viduḥ kva cit
d kāmāl lobhāc ca kāruṇyāt snehāc ca bharatarṣabha
d nācaraṃ vṛjinaṃ kiṃ cid dhārtarāṣṭrasya nityaśaḥ
d ahaṃ hi pāṇḍavān sarvān haniṣyāmi raṇe sthitān
d prāg viruddhaiḥ śamaṃ sadbhiḥ kathaṃ vā kriyate punaḥ
a rājño hi dhṛtarāṣṭrasya sarvaṃ kāryaṃ priyaṃ mayā
c tathā duryodhanasyāpi sa hi rājye samāhitaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a karṇasya tu vacaḥ śrutvā bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavaḥ punaḥ
c dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ mahārājam ābhāṣyedaṃ vaco 'bravīt
a yad ayaṃ katthate nityaṃ hantāhaṃ pāṇḍavān iti
c nāyaṃ kalāpi saṃpūrṇā pāṇḍavānāṃ mahātmanām
d teṣām ekakalāṃ pūrṇāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ na cārhati
a anayo yo 'yam āgantā putrāṇāṃ te durātmanām
c tad asya karma jānīhi sūtaputrasya durmateḥ
a enam āśritya putras te mandabuddhiḥ suyodhanaḥ
c avamanyata tān vīrān devaputrān ariṃdamān
a kiṃ cāpy anena tat karma kṛtaṃ pūrvaṃ suduṣkaram
c tair yathā pāṇḍavaiḥ sarvair ekaikena kṛtaṃ purā
a dṛṣṭvā virāṭanagare bhrātaraṃ nihataṃ priyam
c dhanaṃjayena vikramya kim anena tadā kṛtam
d sarve hy astravidaḥ śūrāḥ sarve prāptā mahad yaśaḥ
d api sarvāmaraiśvaryaṃ tyajeyur na punar jayam
a sahitān hi kurūn sarvān abhiyāto dhanaṃjayaḥ
c pramathya cācchinad gāvaḥ kim ayaṃ proṣitas tadā
a gandharvair ghoṣayātrāyāṃ hriyate yat sutas tava
c kva tadā sūtaputro 'bhūd ya idānīṃ vṛṣāyate
a nanu tatrāpi pārthena bhīmena ca mahātmanā
c yamābhyām eva cāgamya gandharvās te parājitāḥ
a etāny asya mṛṣoktāni bahūni bharatarṣabha
c vikatthanasya bhadraṃ te sadā dharmārthalopinaḥ
a bhīṣmasya tu vacaḥ śrutvā bhāradvājo mahāmanāḥ
c dhṛtarāṣṭram uvācedaṃ rājamadhye 'bhipūjayan
a yad āha bharataśreṣṭho bhīṣmas tat kriyatāṃ nṛpa
c na kāmam arthalipsūnāṃ vacanaṃ kartum arhasi
a purā yuddhāt sādhu manye pāṇḍavaiḥ saha saṃgamam
b ajeyāḥ pāṇḍavā rājan sendrair api surāsuraiḥ
c yad vākyam arjunenoktaṃ saṃjayena niveditam
a sarvaṃ tad abhijānāmi kariṣyati ca pāṇḍavaḥ
c na hy asya triṣu lokeṣu sadṛśo 'sti dhanurdharaḥ
a anādṛtya tu tad vākyam arthavad droṇabhīṣmayoḥ
c tataḥ sa saṃjayaṃ rājā paryapṛcchata pāṇḍavam
a tadaiva kuravaḥ sarve nirāśā jīvite 'bhavan
c bhīṣmadroṇau yadā rājā na samyag anubhāṣate
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a kim asau pāṇḍavo rājā dharmaputro 'bhyabhāṣata
c śrutvemā bahulāḥ senāḥ pratyarthena samāgatāḥ
a kim icchaty abhisaṃrambhād yotsyamāno yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c kasya svid bhrātṛputrāṇāṃ cintāsu mukham īkṣate
a ke svid enaṃ vārayanti śāmya yudhyeti vā punaḥ
c nikṛtyā kopitaṃ mandair dharmajñaṃ dharmacāriṇam
 saṃjaya uvāca
a rājño mukham udīkṣante pāñcālāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha
c yudhiṣṭhirasya bhadraṃ te sa sarvān anuśāsti ca
a pṛthagbhūtāḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ pāñcālānāṃ rathavrajāḥ
c āyāntam abhinandanti kuntīputraṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
a tamaḥ sūryam ivodyantaṃ kaunteyaṃ dīptatejasam
c pāñcālāḥ pratinandanti tejorāśim ivodyatam
a ā gopālāvipālebhyo nandamānaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
c pāñcālāḥ kekayā matsyāḥ pratinandanti pāṇḍavam
a brāhmaṇyo rājaputryaś ca viśāṃ duhitaraś ca yāḥ
c krīḍantyo 'bhisamāyānti pārthaṃ saṃnaddham īkṣitum
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a saṃjayācakṣva kenāsmān pāṇḍavā abhyayuñjata
c dhṛṣṭadyumnena senānyā somakāḥ kiṃbalā iva
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a gāvalgaṇis tu tat pṛṣṭaḥ sabhāyāṃ kurusaṃsadi
c niḥśvasya subhṛśaṃ dīrghaṃ muhuḥ saṃcintayann iva

c tair asya puruṣavyāghrair bhṛśam udvejitaṃ manaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a saṃjayaś cetanāṃ labdhvā pratyāśvasyedam abravīt
c dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ mahārāja sabhāyāṃ kurusaṃsadi
a dṛṣṭavān asmi rājendra kuntīputrān mahārathān
c matsyarājagṛhāvāsād avarodhena karśitān
e śṛṇu yair hi mahārāja pāṇḍavā abhyayuñjata
f dhṛṣṭadyumnena vīreṇa yuddhe vaste 'bhyayuñjata
a yo naiva roṣān na bhayān na kāmān nārthakāraṇāt
c na hetuvādād dharmātmā satyaṃ jahyāt kathaṃ cana
a yaḥ pramāṇaṃ mahārāja dharme dharmabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
c ajātaśatruṇā tena pāṇḍavā abhyayuñjata
a yasya bāhubale tulyaḥ pṛthivyāṃ nāsti kaś cana
c yo vai sarvān mahīpālān vaśe cakre dhanurdharaḥ
e tena vo bhīmasenena pāṇḍavā abhyayuñjata
a niḥsṛtānāṃ jatugṛhād dhiḍimbāt puruṣādakāt
c ya eṣām abhavad dvīpaḥ kuntīputro vṛkodaraḥ
a yājñasenīm atho yatra sindhurājo 'pakṛṣṭavān
c tatraiṣām abhavad dvīpaḥ kuntīputro vṛkodaraḥ
a yaś ca tān saṃgatān sarvān pāṇḍavān vāraṇāvate
c dahyato mocayām āsa tena vas te 'bhyayuñjata
a kṛṣṇāyāś caratā prītiṃ yena krodhavaśā hatāḥ
c praviśya viṣamaṃ ghoraṃ parvataṃ gandhamādanam
a yasya nāgāyutaṃ vīryaṃ bhujayoḥ sāram arpitam
c tena vo bhīmasenena pāṇḍavā abhyayuñjata
a kṛṣṇadvitīyo vikramya tuṣṭyarthaṃ jātavedasaḥ
c ajayad yaḥ purā vīro yudhyamānaṃ puraṃdaram
a yaḥ sa sākṣān mahādevaṃ giriśaṃ śūlapāṇinam
c toṣayām āsa yuddhena devadevam umāpatim
a yaś ca sarvān vaśe cakre lokapālān dhanurdharaḥ
c tena vo vijayenājau pāṇḍavā abhyayuñjata
a yaḥ pratīcīṃ diśaṃ cakre vaśe mlecchagaṇāyutām
c sa tatra nakulo yoddhā citrayodhī vyavasthitaḥ
a tena vo darśanīyena vīreṇātidhanurbhṛtā
c mādrīputreṇa kauravya pāṇḍavā abhyayuñjata
a yaḥ kāśīn aṅgamagadhān kaliṅgāṃś ca yudhājayat
c tena vaḥ sahadevena pāṇḍavā abhyayuñjata
a yasya vīryeṇa sadṛśāś catvāro bhuvi mānavāḥ
c aśvatthāmā dhṛṣṭaketuḥ pradyumno rukmir eva ca
a tena vaḥ sahadevena pāṇḍavā abhyayuñjata
c yavīyasā nṛvīreṇa mādrīnandikareṇa ca
a tapaś cacāra yā ghoraṃ kāśikanyā purā satī
c bhīṣmasya vadham icchantī pretyāpi bharatarṣabha
a pāñcālasya sutā jajñe daivāc ca sa punaḥ pumān
c strīpuṃsoḥ puruṣavyāghra yaḥ sa veda guṇāguṇān
a yaḥ kaliṅgān samāpede pāñcālo yuddhadurmadaḥ
c śikhaṇḍinā vaḥ kuravaḥ kṛtāstreṇābhyayuñjata
a yāṃ yakṣaḥ puruṣaṃ cakre bhīṣmasya nidhane kila
c maheṣvāsena raudreṇa pāṇḍavā abhyayuñjata
a maheṣvāsā rājaputrā bhrātaraḥ pañca kekayāḥ
c sumṛṣṭakavacāḥ śūrās taiś ca vas te 'bhyayuñjata
a yo dīrghabāhuḥ kṣiprāstro dhṛtimān satyavikramaḥ
c tena vo vṛṣṇivīreṇa yuyudhānena saṃgaraḥ
a ya āsīc charaṇaṃ kāle pāṇḍavānāṃ mahātmanām
c raṇe tena virāṭena pāṇḍavā abhyayuñjata
d yaś ca droṇavināśāya samutpanno mahāmanāḥ
d dhṛṣṭadyumnena senānyā pāṇḍavā abhyayuñjata
a yaḥ sa kāśipatī rājā vārāṇasyāṃ mahārathaḥ
c sa teṣām abhavad yoddhā tena vas te 'bhyayuñjata
a śiśubhir durjayaiḥ saṃkhye draupadeyair mahātmabhiḥ
c āśīviṣasamasparśaiḥ pāṇḍavā abhyayuñjata
a yaḥ kṛṣṇasadṛśo vīrye yudhiṣṭhirasamo dame
c tenābhimanyunā saṃkhye pāṇḍavā abhyayuñjata
a yaś caivāpratimo vīrye dhṛṣṭaketur mahāyaśāḥ
c duḥsahaḥ samare kruddhaḥ śaiśupālir mahārathaḥ
e tena vaś cedirājena pāṇḍavā abhyayuñjata
f akṣauhiṇyā parivṛtaḥ pāṇḍavān yo 'bhisaṃśritaḥ
f pāṇḍavān yo 'bhisaṃsṛtya āste yadukulodbhavaḥ
a yaḥ saṃśrayaḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ devānām iva vāsavaḥ
c tena vo vāsudevena pāṇḍavā abhyayuñjata
a tathā cedipater bhrātā śarabho bharatarṣabha
c karakarṣeṇa sahitas tābhyāṃ vas te 'bhyayuñjata
a jārāsaṃdhiḥ sahadevo jayatsenaś ca tāv ubhau
b yuddhe 'pratirathau vīrau pāṇḍavārthe vyavasthitau
c drupadaś ca mahātejā balena mahatā vṛtaḥ
e tyaktātmā pāṇḍavārthāya yotsyamāno vyavasthitaḥ
a ete cānye ca bahavaḥ prācyodīcyā mahīkṣitaḥ
c śataśo yān apāśritya dharmarājo vyavasthitaḥ
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a sarva ete mahotsāhā ye tvayā parikīrtitāḥ
c ekatas tv eva te sarve sametā bhīma ekataḥ
a bhīmasenād dhi me bhūyo bhayaṃ saṃjāyate mahat
c kruddhād amarṣaṇāt tāta vyāghrād iva mahāruroḥ
a jāgarmi rātrayaḥ sarvā dīrgham uṣṇaṃ ca niḥśvasan
c bhīto vṛkodarāt tāta siṃhāt paśur ivābalaḥ
a na hi tasya mahābāhoḥ śakrapratimatejasaḥ
c sainye 'smin pratipaśyāmi ya enaṃ viṣahed yudhi
a amarṣaṇaś ca kaunteyo dṛḍhavairaś ca pāṇḍavaḥ
c anarmahāsī sonmādas tiryakprekṣī mahāsvanaḥ
a mahāvego mahotsāho mahābāhur mahābalaḥ
c mandānāṃ mama putrāṇāṃ yuddhenāntaṃ kariṣyati
a ūrugrāhagṛhītānāṃ gadāṃ bibhrad vṛkodaraḥ
c kurūṇām ṛṣabho yuddhe daṇḍapāṇir ivāntakaḥ
a śaikyāyasamayīṃ ghorāṃ gadāṃ kāñcanabhūṣitām

a yathā rurūṇāṃ yūtheṣu siṃho jātabalaś caret
c māmakeṣu tathā bhīmo baleṣu vicariṣyati
a sarveṣāṃ mama putrāṇāṃ sa ekaḥ krūravikramaḥ
c bahvāśī vipratīpaś ca bālye 'pi rabhasaḥ sadā
a udvepate me hṛdayaṃ yadā duryodhanādayaḥ
c bālye 'pi tena yudhyanto vāraṇeneva marditāḥ
a tasya vīryeṇa saṃkliṣṭā nityam eva sutā mama
b sa vai bhīmo mahāvīryaḥ kruddhaḥ parapuraṃjayaḥ
c sa eva hetur bhedasya bhīmo bhīmaparākramaḥ
a grasamānam anīkāni naravāraṇavājinām
c paśyāmīvāgrato bhīmaṃ krodhamūrchitam āhave
a astre droṇārjunasamaṃ vāyuvegasamaṃ jave
b maheśvarasamaṃ krodhe ko hanyād bhīmam āhave
c saṃjayācakṣva me śūraṃ bhīmasenam amarṣaṇam
a atilābhaṃ tu manye 'haṃ yat tena ripughātinā
c tadaiva na hatāḥ sarve mama putrā manasvinā
a yena bhīmabalā yakṣā rākṣasāś ca samāhatāḥ
b hiḍimbabakakirmīrapramukhāś ca mahābalāḥ
c kathaṃ tasya raṇe vegaṃ mānuṣaḥ prasahiṣyati
a na sa jātu vaśe tasthau mama bālo 'pi saṃjaya
c kiṃ punar mama duṣputraiḥ kliṣṭaḥ saṃprati pāṇḍavaḥ
a niṣṭhuraḥ sa ca naiṣṭhuryād bhajyed api na saṃnamet
c tiryakprekṣī saṃhatabhrūḥ kathaṃ śāmyed vṛkodaraḥ
a bṛhadaṃso 'pratibalo gauras tāla ivodgataḥ
c pramāṇato bhīmasenaḥ prādeśenādhiko 'rjunāt
a javena vājino 'tyeti balenātyeti kuñjarān
c avyaktajalpī madhvakṣo madhyamaḥ pāṇḍavo balī
a iti bālye śrutaḥ pūrvaṃ mayā vyāsamukhāt purā
c rūpato vīryataś caiva yāthātathyena pāṇḍavaḥ
a āyasena sa daṇḍena rathān nāgān hayān narān
c haniṣyati raṇe kruddho bhīmaḥ praharatāṃ varaḥ
a amarṣī nityasaṃrabdho raudraḥ krūraparākramaḥ
c mama tāta pratīpāni kurvan pūrvaṃ vimānitaḥ
a niṣkīrṇām āyasīṃ sthūlāṃ suparvāṃ kāñcanīṃ gadām
c śataghnīṃ śatanirhrādāṃ kathaṃ śakṣyanti me sutāḥ
a apāram aplavāgādhaṃ samudraṃ śaraveginam
c bhīmasenamayaṃ durgaṃ tāta mandās titīrṣavaḥ
a krośato me na śṛṇvanti bālāḥ paṇḍitamāninaḥ
c viṣamaṃ nāvabudhyante prapātaṃ madhudarśinaḥ
a saṃyugaṃ ye kariṣyanti nararūpeṇa vāyunā
c niyataṃ coditā dhātrā siṃheneva mahāmṛgāḥ
a śaikyāṃ tāta catuṣkiṣkuṃ ṣaḍasrim amitaujasam
c prahitāṃ duḥkhasaṃsparśāṃ kathaṃ śakṣyanti me sutāḥ
a gadāṃ bhrāmayatas tasya bhindato hastimastakān
c sṛkkiṇī lelihānasya bāṣpam utsṛjato muhuḥ
a uddiśya pātān patataḥ kurvato bhairavān ravān
c pratīpān patato mattān kuñjarān pratigarjataḥ
a vigāhya rathamārgeṣu varān uddiśya nighnataḥ
c agneḥ prajvalitasyeva api mucyeta me prajā
a vīthīṃ kurvan mahābāhur drāvayan mama vāhinīm
c nṛtyann iva gadāpāṇir yugāntaṃ darśayiṣyati
a prabhinna iva mātaṅgaḥ prabhañjan puṣpitān drumān
c pravekṣyati raṇe senāṃ putrāṇāṃ me vṛkodaraḥ
a kurvan rathān vipuruṣān vidhvajān bhagnapuṣkarān
c ārujan puruṣavyāghro rathinaḥ sādinas tathā
a gaṅgāvega ivānūpāṃs tīrajān vividhān drumān
c pravekṣyati mahāsenāṃ putrāṇāṃ mama saṃjaya
a vaśaṃ nūnaṃ gamiṣyanti bhīmasenabalārditāḥ
c mama putrāś ca bhṛtyāś ca rājānaś caiva saṃjaya
a yena rājā mahāvīryaḥ praviśyāntaḥpuraṃ purā
c vāsudevasahāyena jarāsaṃdho nipātitaḥ
a kṛtsneyaṃ pṛthivī devī jarāsaṃdhena dhīmatā
c māgadhendreṇa balinā vaśe kṛtvā pratāpitā
a bhīṣmapratāpāt kuravo nayenāndhakavṛṣṇayaḥ
c te na tasya vaśaṃ jagmuḥ kevalaṃ daivam eva vā
a sa gatvā pāṇḍuputreṇa tarasā bāhuśālinā
c anāyudhena vīreṇa nihataḥ kiṃ tato 'dhikam
a dīrghakālena saṃsiktaṃ viṣam āśīviṣo yathā
c sa mokṣyati raṇe tejaḥ putreṣu mama saṃjaya
a mahendra iva vajreṇa dānavān devasattamaḥ
c bhīmaseno gadāpāṇiḥ sūdayiṣyati me sutān
a aviṣahyam anāvāryaṃ tīvravegaparākramam
c paśyāmīvātitāmrākṣam āpatantaṃ vṛkodaram
a agadasyāpy adhanuṣo virathasya vivarmaṇaḥ
c bāhubhyāṃ yudhyamānasya kas tiṣṭhed agrataḥ pumān
a bhīṣmo droṇaś ca vipro 'yaṃ kṛpaḥ śāradvatas tathā
c jānanty ete yathaivāhaṃ vīryajñas tasya dhīmataḥ
a āryavrataṃ tu jānantaḥ saṃgarān na bibhitsavaḥ
c senāmukheṣu sthāsyanti māmakānāṃ nararṣabhāḥ
a balīyaḥ sarvato diṣṭaṃ puruṣasya viśeṣataḥ
c paśyann api jayaṃ teṣāṃ na niyacchāmi yat sutān
a te purāṇaṃ maheṣvāsā mārgam aindraṃ samāsthitāḥ
c tyakṣyanti tumule prāṇān rakṣantaḥ pārthivaṃ yaśaḥ
a yathaiṣāṃ māmakās tāta tathaiṣāṃ pāṇḍavā api
c pautrā bhīṣmasya śiṣyāś ca droṇasya ca kṛpasya ca
a yat tv asmad āśrayaṃ kiṃ cid dattam iṣṭaṃ ca saṃjaya
c tasyāpacitim āryatvāt kartāraḥ sthavirās trayaḥ
a ādadānasya śastraṃ hi kṣatradharmaṃ parīpsataḥ
c nidhanaṃ brāhmaṇasyājau varam evāhur uttamam
a sa vai śocāmi sarvān vai ye yuyutsanti pāṇḍavān
c vikruṣṭaṃ vidureṇādau tad etad bhayam āgatam
a na tu manye vighātāya jñānaṃ duḥkhasya saṃjaya
c bhavaty atibale hy etaj jñānam apy upaghātakam
a ṛṣayo hy api nirmuktāḥ paśyanto lokasaṃgrahān
c sukhe bhavanti sukhinas tathā duḥkhena duḥkhitāḥ
a kiṃ punar yo 'ham āsaktas tatra tatra sahasradhā
c putreṣu rājyadāreṣu pautreṣv api ca bandhuṣu
a saṃśaye tu mahaty asmin kiṃ nu me kṣamam uttamam
c vināśaṃ hy eva paśyāmi kurūṇām anucintayan
a dyūtapramukham ābhāti kurūṇāṃ vyasanaṃ mahat
c mandenaiśvaryakāmena lobhāt pāpam idaṃ kṛtam
a manye paryāyadharmo 'yaṃ kālasyātyantagāminaḥ
c cakre pradhir ivāsakto nāsya śakyaṃ palāyitum
a kiṃ nu kāryaṃ kathaṃ kuryāṃ kva nu gacchāmi saṃjaya
c ete naśyanti kuravo mandāḥ kālavaśaṃ gatāḥ
a avaśo 'haṃ purā tāta putrāṇāṃ nihate śate
c śroṣyāmi ninadaṃ strīṇāṃ kathaṃ māṃ maraṇaṃ spṛśet
a yathā nidāghe jvalanaḥ samiddho
dahet kakṣaṃ vāyunā codyamānaḥ
c gadāhastaḥ pāṇḍavas tadvad eva
hantā madīyān sahito 'rjunena
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a yasya vai nānṛtā vācaḥ pravṛttā anuśuśrumaḥ
c trailokyam api tasya syād yoddhā yasya dhanaṃjayaḥ
a tasyaiva ca na paśyāmi yudhi gāṇḍīvadhanvanaḥ
c aniśaṃ cintayāno 'pi yaḥ pratīyād rathena tam
a asyataḥ karṇinālīkān mārgaṇān hṛdayacchidaḥ
c pratyetā na samaḥ kaś cid yudhi gāṇḍīvadhanvanaḥ
a droṇakarṇau pratīyātāṃ yadi vīrau nararṣabhau
b kṛtāstrau balināṃ śreṣṭhau samareṣv aparājitau
c māhātmyāt saṃśayo loke na tv asti vijayo mama
a ghṛṇī karṇaḥ pramādī ca ācāryaḥ sthaviro guruḥ
c samartho balavān pārtho dṛḍhadhanvā jitaklamaḥ

a yasya yantā hṛṣīkeśaḥ śīlavṛttasamo yudhi
c dhruvas tasya jayas tāta yathendrasya jayas tathā
a kṛṣṇāv ekarathe yattāv adhijyaṃ gāṇḍivaṃ dhanuḥ
c yugapat trīṇi tejāṃsi sametāny anuśuśrumaḥ
a naiva no 'sti dhanus tādṛṅ na yoddhā na ca sārathiḥ
c tac ca mandā na jānanti duryodhanavaśānugāḥ
a śeṣayed aśanir dīpto nipatan mūrdhni saṃjaya
c na tu śeṣaṃ śarāḥ kuryur astās tāta kirīṭinā
a api cāsyann ivābhāti nighnann iva ca phalgunaḥ
c uddharann iva kāyebhyaḥ śirāṃsi śaravṛṣṭibhiḥ
a api bāṇamayaṃ tejaḥ pradīptam iva sarvataḥ
c gāṇḍīveddhaṃ dahetājau putrāṇāṃ mama vāhinīm
a api sā rathaghoṣeṇa bhayārtā savyasācinaḥ
c vitrastā bahulā senā bhāratī pratibhāti me
a yathā kakṣaṃ dahaty agniḥ pravṛddhaḥ sarvataś caran
c mahārcir aniloddhūtas tadvad dhakṣyati māmakān
a yadodvaman niśitān bāṇasaṃghān
sthātātatāyī samare kirīṭī
c sṛṣṭo 'ntakaḥ sarvaharo vidhātrā
yathā bhavet tadvad avāraṇīyaḥ
a yadā hy abhīkṣṇaṃ subahūn prakārāñ
śrotāsmi tān āvasathe kurūṇām
c teṣāṃ samantāc ca tathā raṇāgre
kṣayaḥ kilāyaṃ bharatān upaiti
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a yathaiva pāṇḍavāḥ sarve parākrāntā jigīṣavaḥ
c tathaivābhisarās teṣāṃ tyaktātmāno jaye dhṛtāḥ
a tvam eva hi parākrāntān ācakṣīthāḥ parān mama
c pāñcālān kekayān matsyān māgadhān vatsabhūmipān
a yaś ca sendrān imāṃl lokān icchan kuryād vaśe balī
c sa śreṣṭho jagataḥ kṛṣṇaḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ jaye dhṛtaḥ
a samastām arjunād vidyāṃ sātyakiḥ kṣipram āptavān
c śaineyaḥ samare sthātā bījavat pravapañ śarān
a dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pāñcālyaḥ krūrakarmā mahārathaḥ
c māmakeṣu raṇaṃ kartā baleṣu paramāstravit
a yudhiṣṭhirasya ca krodhād arjunasya ca vikramāt
c yamābhyāṃ bhīmasenāc ca bhayaṃ me tāta jāyate
a amānuṣaṃ manuṣyendrair jālaṃ vitatam antarā
c mama senāṃ haniṣyanti tataḥ krośāmi saṃjaya
a darśanīyo manasvī ca lakṣmīvān brahmavarcasī
c medhāvī sukṛtaprajño dharmātmā pāṇḍunandanaḥ
a mitrāmātyaiḥ susaṃpannaḥ saṃpanno yojyayojakaiḥ
c bhrātṛbhiḥ śvaśuraiḥ putrair upapanno mahārathaiḥ
a dhṛtyā ca puruṣavyāghro naibhṛtyena ca pāṇḍavaḥ
c anṛśaṃso vadānyaś ca hrīmān satyaparākramaḥ
a bahuśrutaḥ kṛtātmā ca vṛddhasevī jitendriyaḥ
c taṃ sarvaguṇasaṃpannaṃ samiddham iva pāvakam
a tapantam iva ko mandaḥ patiṣyati pataṃgavat
c pāṇḍavāgnim anāvāryaṃ mumūrṣur mūḍhacetanaḥ
a tanur uccaḥ śikhī rājā śuddhajāmbūnadaprabhaḥ
c mandānāṃ mama putrāṇāṃ yuddhenāntaṃ kariṣyati
a tair ayuddhaṃ sādhu manye kuravas tan nibodhata
c yuddhe vināśaḥ kṛtsnasya kulasya bhavitā dhruvam
a eṣā me paramā śāntir yayā śāmyati me manaḥ
c yadi tv ayuddham iṣṭaṃ vo vayaṃ śāntyai yatāmahe
a na tu naḥ śikṣamāṇānām upekṣeta yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c jugupsati hy adharmeṇa mām evoddiśya kāraṇam
 saṃjaya uvāca
a evam etan mahārāja yathā vadasi bhārata
c yuddhe vināśaḥ kṣatrasya gāṇḍīvena pradṛśyate
a idaṃ tu nābhijānāmi tava dhīrasya nityaśaḥ
c yat putravaśam āgaccheḥ sattvajñaḥ savyasācinaḥ
a naiṣa kālo mahārāja tava śaśvat kṛtāgasaḥ
c tvayā hy evāditaḥ pārthā nikṛtā bharatarṣabha
d svīkṛtās tair janapadāḥ kuravas te sajāṅgalāḥ
d kathaṃ vīraur jitāṃ bhūmim akhilāṃ pratipadyathāḥ
a pitā śreṣṭhaḥ suhṛd yaś ca samyak praṇihitātmavān
c āstheyaṃ hi hitaṃ tena na drogdhā gurur ucyate
a idaṃ jitam idaṃ labdham iti śrutvā parājitān
c dyūtakāle mahārāja smayase sma kumāravat
a paruṣāṇy ucyamānān sma purā pārthān upekṣase
c kṛtsnaṃ rājyaṃ jayantīti prapātaṃ nānupaśyasi
a pitryaṃ rājyaṃ mahārāja kuravas te sajāṅgalāḥ
b prārthayanti mahāyuddhe nānubandham avekṣase
c atha vīrair jitāṃ bhūmim akhilāṃ pratyapadyathāḥ
a bāhuvīryārjitā bhūmis tava pārthair niveditā
c mayedaṃ kṛtam ity eva manyase rājasattama
a grastān gandharvarājena majjato hy aplave 'mbhasi
c ānināya punaḥ pārthaḥ putrāṃs te rājasattama
a kumāravac ca smayase dyūte vinikṛteṣu yat
c pāṇḍaveṣu vanaṃ rājan pravrajatsu punaḥ punaḥ
a pravarṣataḥ śaravrātān arjunasya śitān bahūn
c apy arṇavā viśuṣyeyuḥ kiṃ punar māṃsayonayaḥ
a asyatāṃ phalgunaḥ śreṣṭho gāṇḍīvaṃ dhanuṣāṃ varam
c keśavaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ cakrāṇāṃ ca sudarśanam
a vānaro rocamānaś ca ketuḥ ketumatāṃ varaḥ
c evam etāni saratho vahañ śvetahayo raṇe
e kṣapayiṣyati no rājan kālacakram ivodyatam
a tasyādya vasudhā rājan nikhilā bharatarṣabha
c yasya bhīmārjunau yodhau sa rājā rājasattama
a tathā bhīmahataprāyāṃ majjantīṃ tava vāhinīm
c duryodhanamukhā dṛṣṭvā kṣayaṃ yāsyanti kauravāḥ
a na hi bhīmabhayād bhītā lapsyante vijayaṃ vibho
c tava putrā mahārāja rājānaś cānusāriṇaḥ
a matsyās tvām adya nārcanti pāñcālāś ca sakekayāḥ
c śālveyāḥ śūrasenāś ca sarve tvām avajānate
e pārthaṃ hy ete gatāḥ sarve vīryajñās tasya dhīmataḥ
f bhaktyā hy asya virudhyante tava putraiḥ sadaiva te
a anarhān eva tu vadhe dharmayuktān vikarmaṇā
b yo 'kleśayat pāṇḍuputrān yo vidveṣṭy adhunāpi vai
c sarvopāyair niyantavyaḥ sānugaḥ pāpapūruṣaḥ
d aparokṣaṃ mahārāja sākṣāc cainaṃ bravīmy aham
e tava putro mahārāja nātra śocitum arhasi
a dyūtakāle mayā coktaṃ vidureṇa ca dhīmatā
c yad idaṃ te vilapitaṃ pāṇḍavān prati bhārata
e anīśeneva rājendra sarvam etan nirarthakam
 duryodhana uvāca
a na bhetavyaṃ mahārāja na śocyā bhavatā vayam
c samarthāḥ sma parān rājan vijetuṃ samare vibho
a vanaṃ pravrājitān pārthān yad āyān madhusūdanaḥ
c mahatā balacakreṇa pararāṣṭrāvamardinā
a kekayā dhṛṣṭaketuś ca dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥ
c rājānaś cānvayuḥ pārthān bahavo 'nye 'nuyāyinaḥ
a indraprasthasya cādūrāt samājagmur mahārathāḥ
c vyagarhayaṃś ca saṃgamya bhavantaṃ kurubhiḥ saha
a te yudhiṣṭhiram āsīnam ajinaiḥ prativāsitam
c kṛṣṇapradhānāḥ saṃhatya paryupāsanta bhārata
a pratyādānaṃ ca rājyasya kāryam ūcur narādhipāḥ
c bhavataḥ sānubandhasya samucchedaṃ cikīrṣavaḥ
a śrutvā caitan mayoktās tu bhīṣmadroṇakṛpās tadā
c jñātikṣayabhayād rājan bhītena bharatarṣabha
a na te sthāsyanti samaye pāṇḍavā iti me matiḥ
c samucchedaṃ hi naḥ kṛtsnaṃ vāsudevaś cikīrṣati
a ṛte ca viduraṃ sarve yūyaṃ vadhyā mahātmanaḥ
c dhṛtarāṣṭraś ca dharmajño na vadhyaḥ kurusattamaḥ
a samucchedaṃ ca kṛtsnaṃ naḥ kṛtvā tāta janārdanaḥ
c ekarājyaṃ kurūṇāṃ sma cikīrṣati yudhiṣṭhire
a tatra kiṃ prāptakālaṃ naḥ praṇipātaḥ palāyanam
c prāṇān vā saṃparityajya pratiyudhyāmahe parān
a pratiyuddhe tu niyataḥ syād asmākaṃ parājayaḥ
c yudhiṣṭhirasya sarve hi pārthivā vaśavartinaḥ
a viraktarāṣṭrāś ca vayaṃ mitrāṇi kupitāni naḥ
c dhikkṛtāḥ pārthivaiḥ sarvaiḥ svajanena ca sarvaśaḥ
a praṇipāte tu doṣo 'sti bandhūnāṃ śāśvatīḥ samāḥ
c pitaraṃ tv eva śocāmi prajñānetraṃ janeśvaram
e matkṛte duḥkham āpannaṃ kleśaṃ prāptam anantakam
a kṛtaṃ hi tava putraiś ca pareṣām avarodhanam
c matpriyārthaṃ puraivaitad viditaṃ te narottama
a te rājño dhṛtarāṣṭrasya sāmātyasya mahārathāḥ
c vairaṃ pratikariṣyanti kulocchedena pāṇḍavāḥ
a tato droṇo 'bravīd bhīṣmaḥ kṛpo drauṇiś ca bhārata
c matvā māṃ mahatīṃ cintām āsthitaṃ vyathitendriyam
a abhidrugdhāḥ pare cen no na bhetavyaṃ paraṃtapa
c asamarthāḥ pare jetum asmān yudhi janeśvara
a ekaikaśaḥ samarthāḥ smo vijetuṃ sarvapārthivān
c āgacchantu vineṣyāmo darpam eṣāṃ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a puraikena hi bhīṣmeṇa vijitāḥ sarvapārthivāḥ
c mṛte pitary abhikruddho rathenaikena bhārata
a jaghāna subahūṃs teṣāṃ saṃrabdhaḥ kurusattamaḥ
c tatas te śaraṇaṃ jagmur devavratam imaṃ bhayāt
a sa bhīṣmaḥ susamartho 'yam asmābhiḥ sahito raṇe
c parān vijetuṃ tasmāt te vyetu bhīr bharatarṣabha
e ity eṣāṃ niścayo hy āsīt tatkālam amitaujasām
a purā pareṣāṃ pṛthivī kṛtsnāsīd vaśavartinī
c asmān punar amī nādya samarthā jetum āhave
e chinnapakṣāḥ pare hy adya vīryahīnāś ca pāṇḍavāḥ
a asmatsaṃsthā ca pṛthivī vartate bharatarṣabha
c ekārthāḥ sukhaduḥkheṣu mayānītāś ca pārthivāḥ
a apy agniṃ praviśeyus te samudraṃ vā paraṃtapa
c madarthe pārthivāḥ sarve tad viddhi kurusattama
a unmattam iva cāpi tvāṃ prahasantīha duḥkhitam
c vilapantaṃ bahuvidhaṃ bhītaṃ paravikatthane
a eṣāṃ hy ekaikaśo rājñāṃ samarthaḥ pāṇḍavān prati
c ātmānaṃ manyate sarvo vyetu te bhayam āgatam
a sarvāṃ samagrāṃ senāṃ me vāsavo 'pi na śaknuyāt
c hantum akṣayyarūpeyaṃ brahmaṇāpi svayambhuvā
a yudhiṣṭhiraḥ puraṃ hitvā pañca grāmān sa yācati
c bhīto hi māmakāt sainyāt prabhāvāc caiva me prabho
a samarthaṃ manyase yac ca kuntīputraṃ vṛkodaram
c tan mithyā na hi me kṛtsnaṃ prabhāvaṃ vettha bhārata
a matsamo hi gadāyuddhe pṛthivyāṃ nāsti kaś cana
c nāsīt kaś cid atikrānto bhavitā na ca kaś cana
a yukto duḥkhocitaś cāhaṃ vidyāpāragatas tathā
c tasmān na bhīmān nānyebhyo bhayaṃ me vidyate kva cit
a duryodhanasamo nāsti gadāyām iti niścayaḥ
c saṃkarṣaṇasya bhadraṃ te yat tadainam upāvasam
a yuddhe saṃkarṣaṇasamo balenābhyadhiko bhuvi
c gadāprahāraṃ bhīmo me na jātu viṣahed yudhi
a ekaṃ prahāraṃ yaṃ dadyāṃ bhīmāya ruṣito nṛpa
c sa evainaṃ nayed ghoraṃ kṣipraṃ vaivasvatakṣayam
a iccheyaṃ ca gadāhastaṃ rājan draṣṭuṃ vṛkodaram
c suciraṃ prārthito hy eṣa mama nityaṃ manorathaḥ
a gadayā nihato hy ājau mama pārtho vṛkodaraḥ
c viśīrṇagātraḥ pṛthivīṃ parāsuḥ prapatiṣyati
a gadāprahārābhihato himavān api parvataḥ
c sakṛn mayā viśīryeta giriḥ śatasahasradhā
a sa cāpy etad vijānāti vāsudevārjunau tathā
c duryodhanasamo nāsti gadāyām iti niścayaḥ
a tat te vṛkodaramayaṃ bhayaṃ vyetu mahāhave
c vyapaneṣyāmy ahaṃ hy enaṃ mā rājan vimanā bhava
a tasmin mayā hate kṣipram arjunaṃ bahavo rathāḥ
c tulyarūpā viśiṣṭāś ca kṣepsyanti bharatarṣabha
a bhīṣmo droṇaḥ kṛpo drauṇiḥ karṇo bhūriśravās tathā
c prāgjyotiṣādhipaḥ śalyaḥ sindhurājo jayadrathaḥ
a ekaika eṣāṃ śaktas tu hantuṃ bhārata pāṇḍavān
c samastās tu kṣaṇenaitān neṣyanti yamasādanam
a samagrā pārthivī senā pārtham ekaṃ dhanaṃjayam
c kasmād aśaktā nirjetum iti hetur na vidyate
a śaravrātais tu bhīṣmeṇa śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
c droṇadrauṇikṛpaiś caiva gantā pārtho yamakṣayam
a pitāmaho hi gāṅgeyaḥ śaṃtanor adhi bhārata
c brahmarṣisadṛśo jajñe devair api durutsahaḥ
d na hantā vidyate cāpi rājan bhīṣmasya kaś cana
e pitrā hy uktaḥ prasannena nākāmas tvaṃ mariṣyasi
a brahmarṣeś ca bharadvājād droṇyāṃ droṇo vyajāyata
c droṇāj jajñe mahārāja drauṇiś ca paramāstravit
a kṛpaś cācāryamukhyo 'yaṃ maharṣer gautamād api
c śarastambodbhavaḥ śrīmān avadhya iti me matiḥ
a ayonijaṃ trayaṃ hy etat pitā mātā ca mātulaḥ
c aśvatthāmno mahārāja sa ca śūraḥ sthito mama
a sarva ete mahārāja devakalpā mahārathāḥ
c śakrasyāpi vyathāṃ kuryuḥ saṃyuge bharatarṣabha
d naiteṣām arjunaḥ śakta ekaikaṃ prati vīkṣitum
d sahitās tu naravyāghrā haniṣyanti dhanaṃjayam
a bhīṣmadroṇakṛpāṇāṃ ca tulyaḥ karṇo mato mama
c anujñātaś ca rāmeṇa matsamo 'sīti bhārata
a kuṇḍale rucire cāstāṃ karṇasya sahaje śubhe
c te śacyarthe mahendreṇa yācitaḥ sa paraṃtapaḥ
e amoghayā mahārāja śaktyā paramabhīmayā
a tasya śaktyopagūḍhasya kasmāj jīved dhanaṃjayaḥ
c vijayo me dhruvaṃ rājan phalaṃ pāṇāv ivāhitam
e abhivyaktaḥ pareṣāṃ ca kṛtsno bhuvi parājayaḥ
a ahnā hy ekena bhīṣmo 'yam ayutaṃ hanti bhārata
c tat samāś ca maheṣvāsā droṇadrauṇikṛpā api
a saṃśaptāni ca vṛndāni kṣatriyāṇāṃ paraṃtapa
c arjunaṃ vayam asmān vā dhanaṃjaya iti sma ha
a tāṃś cālam iti manyante savyasācivadhe vibho
c pārthivāḥ sa bhavān rājann akasmād vyathate katham
a bhīmasene ca nihate ko 'nyo yudhyeta bhārata
c pareṣāṃ tan mamācakṣva yadi vettha paraṃtapa
d pāñcāleṣu ca bhagneṣu ko 'nyaḥ sthātum ihārhati
a pañca te bhrātaraḥ sarve dhṛṣṭadyumno 'tha sātyakiḥ
c pareṣāṃ sapta ye rājan yodhāḥ paramakaṃ balam
a asmākaṃ tu viśiṣṭā ye bhīṣmadroṇakṛpādayaḥ
c drauṇir vaikartanaḥ karṇaḥ somadatto 'tha bāhlikaḥ
a prāgjyotiṣādhipaḥ śalya āvantyo 'tha jayadrathaḥ
c duḥśāsano durmukhaś ca duḥsahaś ca viśāṃ pate
a śrutāyuś citrasenaś ca purumitro viviṃśatiḥ
c śalo bhūriśravāś cobhau vikarṇaś ca tavātmajaḥ
a akṣauhiṇyo hi me rājan daśaikā ca samāhṛtāḥ
c nyūnāḥ pareṣāṃ saptaiva kasmān me syāt parājayaḥ
a balaṃ triguṇato hīnaṃ yodhyaṃ prāha bṛhaspatiḥ
c parebhyas triguṇā ceyaṃ mama rājann anīkinī
a guṇahīnaṃ pareṣāṃ ca bahu paśyāmi bhārata
c guṇodayaṃ bahuguṇam ātmanaś ca viśāṃ pate
a etat sarvaṃ samājñāya balāgryaṃ mama bhārata
c nyūnatāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ ca na mohaṃ gantum arhasi
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a ity uktvā saṃjayaṃ bhūyaḥ paryapṛcchata bhārata
c vidhitsuḥ prāptakālāni jñātvā parapuraṃjayaḥ
 duryodhana uvāca
a akṣauhiṇīḥ sapta labdhvā rājabhiḥ saha saṃjaya
c kiṃ svid icchati kaunteyo yuddhaprepsur yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a atīva mudito rājan yuddhaprepsur yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c bhīmasenārjunau cobhau yamāv api na bibhyataḥ
a rathaṃ tu divyaṃ kaunteyaḥ sarvā vibhrājayan diśaḥ
c mantraṃ jijñāsamānaḥ san bībhatsuḥ samayojayat
a tam apaśyāma saṃnaddhaṃ meghaṃ vidyutprabhaṃ yathā
c sa mantrān samabhidhyāya hṛṣyamāṇo 'bhyabhāṣata
a pūrvarūpam idaṃ paśya vayaṃ jeṣyāma saṃjaya
c bībhatsur māṃ yathovāca tathāvaimy aham apy uta
 duryodhana uvāca
a praśaṃsasy abhinandaṃs tān pārthān akṣaparājitān
c arjunasya rathe brūhi katham aśvāḥ kathaṃ dhvajaḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a bhauvanaḥ saha śakreṇa bahucitraṃ viśāṃ pate
c rūpāṇi kalpayām āsa tvaṣṭā dhātrā sahābhibho
a dhvaje hi tasmin rūpāṇi cakrus te devamāyayā
c mahādhanāni divyāni mahānti ca laghūni ca
d bhīmasenānurodhāya hanūmān mārutātmajaḥ
d ātmapratikṛtiṃ tasmin dhvaja āropayiṣyati
a sarvā diśo yojanamātram antaraṃ
sa tiryag ūrdhvaṃ ca rurodha vai dhvajaḥ
c na saṃsajjet tarubhiḥ saṃvṛto 'pi
tathā hi māyā vihitā bhauvanena
a yathākāśe śakradhanuḥ prakāśate
na caikavarṇaṃ na ca vidma kiṃ nu tat
c tathā dhvajo vihito bhauvanena
bahvākāraṃ dṛśyate rūpam asya
a yathāgnidhūmo divam eti ruddhvā
varṇān bibhrat taijasaṃ tac charīram
c tathā dhvajo vihito bhauvanena
na ced bhāro bhavitā nota rodhaḥ
a śvetās tasmin vātavegāḥ sadaśvā
divyā yuktāś citrarathena dattāḥ
b bhuvy antarikṣe divi vā narendra
b eṣāṃ gatir hīyate nātra sarvā
c śataṃ yat tat pūryate nityakālaṃ
hataṃ hataṃ dattavaraṃ purastāt
a tathā rājño dantavarṇā bṛhanto
rathe yuktā bhānti tadvīryatulyāḥ
c ṛśyaprakhyā bhīmasenasya vāhā
raṇe vāyos tulyavegā babhūvuḥ
a kalmāṣāṅgās tittiricitrapṛṣṭhā
bhrātrā dattāḥ prīyatā phalgunena
c bhrātur vīrasya svais turaṃgair viśiṣṭā
mudā yuktāḥ sahadevaṃ vahanti
a mādrīputraṃ nakulaṃ tv ājamīḍhaṃ
mahendradattā harayo vājimukhyāḥ
c samā vāyor balavantas tarasvino
vahanti vīraṃ vṛtraśatruṃ yathendram
a tulyāś caibhir vayasā vikrameṇa
javena caivāpratirūpāḥ sadaśvāḥ
c saubhadrādīn draupadeyān kumārān
vahanty aśvā devadattā bṛhantaḥ
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a kāṃs tatra saṃjayāpaśyaḥ pratyarthena samāgatān
c ye yotsyante pāṇḍavārthe putrasya mama vāhinīm
 saṃjaya uvāca
a mukhyam andhakavṛṣṇīnām apaśyaṃ kṛṣṇam āgatam
c cekitānaṃ ca tatraiva yuyudhānaṃ ca sātyakim
a pṛthag akṣauhiṇībhyāṃ tau pāṇḍavān abhisaṃśritau
c mahārathau samākhyātāv ubhau puruṣamāninau
a akṣauhiṇyātha pāñcālyo daśabhis tanayair vṛtaḥ
c satyajitpramukhair vīrair dhṛṣṭadyumnapurogamaiḥ
a drupado vardhayan mānaṃ śikhaṇḍiparipālitaḥ
c upāyāt sarvasainyānāṃ praticchādya tadā vapuḥ
a virāṭaḥ saha putrābhyāṃ śaṅkhenaivottareṇa ca
c sūryadattādibhir vīrair madirāśvapurogamaiḥ
a sahitaḥ pṛthivīpālo bhrātṛbhis tanayais tathā
c akṣauhiṇyaiva sainyasya vṛtaḥ pārthaṃ samāśritaḥ
a jārāsaṃdhir māgadhaś ca dhṛṣṭaketuś ca cedirāṭ
c pṛthak pṛthag anuprāptau pṛthag akṣauhiṇīvṛtau
a kekayā bhrātaraḥ pañca sarve lohitakadhvajāḥ
c akṣauhiṇīparivṛtāḥ pāṇḍavān abhisaṃśritāḥ
a etān etāvatas tatra yān apaśyaṃ samāgatān
c ye pāṇḍavārthe yotsyanti dhārtarāṣṭrasya vāhinīm
a yo veda mānuṣaṃ vyūhaṃ daivaṃ gāndharvam āsuram
c sa tasya senāpramukhe dhṛṣṭadyumno mahāmanāḥ
a bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo rājan bhāgaḥ kḷptaḥ śikhaṇḍinaḥ
c taṃ virāṭo 'nu saṃyātā saha matsyaiḥ prahāribhiḥ
a jyeṣṭhasya pāṇḍuputrasya bhāgo madrādhipo balī
c tau tu tatrābruvan ke cid viṣamau no matāv iti
a duryodhanaḥ sahasutaḥ sārdhaṃ bhrātṛśatena ca
c prācyāś ca dākṣiṇātyāś ca bhīmasenasya bhāgataḥ
a arjunasya tu bhāgena karṇo vaikartano mataḥ
c aśvatthāmā vikarṇaś ca saindhavaś ca jayadrathaḥ
a aśakyāś caiva ye ke cit pṛthivyāṃ śūramāninaḥ
c sarvāṃs tān arjunaḥ pārthaḥ kalpayām āsa bhāgataḥ
a maheṣvāsā rājaputrā bhrātaraḥ pañca kekayāḥ
c kekayān eva bhāgena kṛtvā yotsyanti saṃyuge
a teṣām eva kṛto bhāgo mālavāḥ śālvakekayāḥ
c trigartānāṃ ca dvau mukhyau yau tau saṃśaptakāv iti
a duryodhanasutāḥ sarve tathā duḥśāsanasya ca
c saubhadreṇa kṛto bhāgo rājā caiva bṛhadbalaḥ
a draupadeyā maheṣvāsāḥ suvarṇavikṛtadhvajāḥ
c dhṛṣṭadyumnamukhā droṇam abhiyāsyanti bhārata
a cekitānaḥ somadattaṃ dvairathe yoddhum icchati
c bhojaṃ tu kṛtavarmāṇaṃ yuyudhāno yuyutsati
a sahadevas tu mādreyaḥ śūraḥ saṃkrandano yudhi
c svam aṃśaṃ kalpayām āsa śyālaṃ te subalātmajam
a ulūkaṃ cāpi kaitavyaṃ ye ca sārasvatā gaṇāḥ
c nakulaḥ kalpayām āsa bhāgaṃ mādravatīsutaḥ
a ye cānye pārthivā rājan pratyudyāsyanti saṃyuge
c samāhvānena tāṃś cāpi pāṇḍuputrā akalpayan
a evam eṣām anīkāni pravibhaktāni bhāgaśaḥ
c yat te kāryaṃ saputrasya kriyatāṃ tad akālikam
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a na santi sarve putrā me mūḍhā durdyūtadevinaḥ
c yeṣāṃ yuddhaṃ balavatā bhīmena raṇamūrdhani
a rājānaḥ pārthivāḥ sarve prokṣitāḥ kāladharmaṇā
c gāṇḍīvāgniṃ pravekṣyanti pataṅgā iva pāvakam
a vidrutāṃ vāhinīṃ manye kṛtavairair mahātmabhiḥ
c tāṃ raṇe ke 'nuyāsyanti prabhagnāṃ pāṇḍavair yudhi
a sarve hy atirathāḥ śūrāḥ kīrtimantaḥ pratāpinaḥ
c sūryapāvakayos tulyās tejasā samitiṃjayāḥ
a yeṣāṃ yudhiṣṭhiro netā goptā ca madhusūdanaḥ
c yodhau ca pāṇḍavau vīrau savyasācivṛkodarau
a nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥ
c sātyakir drupadaś caiva dhṛṣṭadyumnasya cātmajaḥ
a uttamaujāś ca pāñcālyo yudhāmanyuś ca durjayaḥ
c śikhaṇḍī kṣatradevaś ca tathā vairāṭir uttaraḥ
d tataḥ śvetas tu vairāṭiḥ ketumān vāhinīpatiḥ
a kāśayaś cedayaś caiva matsyāḥ sarve ca sṛñjayāḥ
c virāṭaputro babhrūś ca pāñcālāś ca prabhadrakāḥ
a yeṣām indro 'py akāmānāṃ na haret pṛthivīm imām
c vīrāṇāṃ raṇadhīrāṇāṃ ye bhindyuḥ parvatān api
a tān sarvān guṇasaṃpannān amanuṣyapratāpinaḥ
c krośato mama duṣputro yoddhum icchati saṃjaya
 duryodhana uvāca
a ubhau sva ekajātīyau tathobhau bhūmigocarau
c atha kasmāt pāṇḍavānām ekato manyase jayam
a pitāmahaṃ ca droṇaṃ ca kṛpaṃ karṇaṃ ca durjayam
c jayadrathaṃ somadattam aśvatthāmānam eva ca
a sucetaso maheṣvāsān indro 'pi sahito 'maraiḥ
c aśaktaḥ samare jetuṃ kiṃ punas tāta pāṇḍavāḥ
a sarvā ca pṛthivī sṛṣṭā madarthe tāta pāṇḍavān
c āryān dhṛtimataḥ śūrān agnikalpān prabādhitum
a na māmakān pāṇḍavās te samarthāḥ prativīkṣitum
c parākrānto hy ahaṃ pāṇḍūn saputrān yoddhum āhave
a matpriyaṃ pārthivāḥ sarve ye cikīrṣanti bhārata
c te tān āvārayiṣyanti aiṇeyān iva tantunā
a mahatā rathavaṃśena śarajālaiś ca māmakaiḥ
c abhidrutā bhaviṣyanti pāñcālāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a unmatta iva me putro vilapaty eṣa saṃjaya
c na hi śakto yudhā jetuṃ dharmarājaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
a jānāti hi sadā bhīṣmaḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ yaśasvinām
c balavattāṃ saputrāṇāṃ dharmajñānāṃ mahātmanām
a yato nārocayam ahaṃ vigrahaṃ tair mahātmabhiḥ
