c kiṃ tu saṃjaya me brūhi punas teṣāṃ viceṣṭitam
a kas tāṃs tarasvino bhūyaḥ saṃdīpayati pāṇḍavān
c arciṣmato maheṣvāsān haviṣā pāvakān iva
 saṃjaya uvāca
a dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ sadaivaitān saṃdīpayati bhārata
c yudhyadhvam iti mā bhaiṣṭa yuddhād bharatasattamāḥ
a ye ke cit pārthivās tatra dhārtarāṣṭreṇa saṃvṛtāḥ
c yuddhe samāgamiṣyanti tumule kavacahrade
a tān sarvān āhave kruddhān sānubandhān samāgatān
c aham ekaḥ samādāsye timir matsyān ivaudakān
a bhīṣmaṃ droṇaṃ kṛpaṃ karṇaṃ drauṇiṃ śalyaṃ suyodhanam
c etāṃś cāpi nirotsyāmi veleva makarālayam
a tathā bruvāṇaṃ dharmātmā prāha rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c tava dhairyaṃ ca vīryaṃ ca pāñcālāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha
e sarve samadhirūḍhāḥ sma saṃgrāmān naḥ samuddhara
a jānāmi tvāṃ mahābāho kṣatradharme vyavasthitam
c samartham ekaṃ paryāptaṃ kauravāṇāṃ yuyutsatām
e bhavatā yad vidhātavyaṃ tan naḥ śreyaḥ paraṃtapa
e   kauravāṇāṃ vinigrahe
e purastād upayātānāṃ
a saṃgrāmād apayātānāṃ bhagnānāṃ śaraṇaiṣiṇām
c pauruṣaṃ darśayañ śūro yas tiṣṭhed agrataḥ pumān
e krīṇīyāt taṃ sahasreṇa nītiman nāma tat padam
a sa tvaṃ śūraś ca vīraś ca vikrāntaś ca nararṣabha
c bhayārtānāṃ paritrātā saṃyugeṣu na saṃśayaḥ
a evaṃ bruvati kaunteye dharmātmani yudhiṣṭhire
c dhṛṣṭadyumna uvācedaṃ māṃ vaco gatasādhvasaḥ
a sarvāñ janapadān sūta yodhā duryodhanasya ye
c sabāhlīkān kurūn brūyāḥ prātipeyāñ śaradvataḥ
a sūtaputraṃ tathā droṇaṃ sahaputraṃ jayadratham
c duḥśāsanaṃ vikarṇaṃ ca tathā duryodhanaṃ nṛpam
a bhīṣmaṃ caiva brūhi gatvā tvam āśu
yudhiṣṭhiraṃ sādhunaivābhyupeta
c mā vo vadhīd arjuno devaguptaḥ
kṣipraṃ yācadhvaṃ pāṇḍavaṃ lokavīram
c rājyaṃ daddhvaṃ dharmarājasya tūrṇaṃ
a naitādṛśo hi yodho 'sti pṛthivyām iha kaś cana
c yathāvidhaḥ savyasācī pāṇḍavaḥ śastravittamaḥ
a devair hi saṃbhṛto divyo ratho gāṇḍīvadhanvanaḥ
c na sa jeyo manuṣyeṇa mā sma kṛdhvaṃ mano yudhi
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a kṣatratejā brahmacārī kaumārād api pāṇḍavaḥ
c tena saṃyugam eṣyanti mandā vilapato mama
a duryodhana nivartasva yuddhād bharatasattama
c na hi yuddhaṃ praśaṃsanti sarvāvastham ariṃdama
a alam ardhaṃ pṛthivyās te sahāmātyasya jīvitum
c prayaccha pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ yathocitam ariṃdama
a etad dhi kuravaḥ sarve manyante dharmasaṃhitam
c yat tvaṃ praśāntim icchethāḥ pāṇḍuputrair mahātmabhiḥ
a aṅgemāṃ samavekṣasva putra svām eva vāhinīm
c jāta eva tava srāvas tvaṃ tu mohān na budhyase
a na hy ahaṃ yuddham icchāmi naitad icchati bāhlikaḥ
c na ca bhīṣmo na ca droṇo nāśvatthāmā na saṃjayaḥ
a na somadatto na śalyo na kṛpo yuddham icchati
c satyavrataḥ purumitro jayo bhūriśravās tathā
a yeṣu saṃpratitiṣṭheyuḥ kuravaḥ pīḍitāḥ paraiḥ
c te yuddhaṃ nābhinandanti tat tubhyaṃ tāta rocatām
a na tvaṃ karoṣi kāmena karṇaḥ kārayitā tava
c duḥśāsanaś ca pāpātmā śakuniś cāpi saubalaḥ
 duryodhana uvāca
a nāhaṃ bhavati na droṇe nāśvatthāmni na saṃjaye
c na vikarṇe na kāmboje na kṛpe na ca bāhlike
a satyavrate purumitre bhūriśravasi vā punaḥ
c anyeṣu vā tāvakeṣu bhāraṃ kṛtvā samāhvaye
a ahaṃ ca tāta karṇaś ca raṇayajñaṃ vitatya vai
c yudhiṣṭhiraṃ paśuṃ kṛtvā dīkṣitau bharatarṣabha
a ratho vedī sruvaḥ khaḍgo gadā sruk kavacaṃ sadaḥ
c cāturhotraṃ ca dhuryā me śarā darbhā havir yaśaḥ
a ātmayajñena nṛpate iṣṭvā vaivasvataṃ raṇe
c vijitya svayam eṣyāvo hatāmitrau śriyā vṛtau
a ahaṃ ca tāta karṇaś ca bhrātā duḥśāsanaś ca me
c ete vayaṃ haniṣyāmaḥ pāṇḍavān samare trayaḥ
a ahaṃ hi pāṇḍavān hatvā praśāstā pṛthivīm imām
c māṃ vā hatvā pāṇḍuputrā bhoktāraḥ pṛthivīm imām
a tyaktaṃ me jīvitaṃ rājan dhanaṃ rājyaṃ ca pārthiva
c na jātu pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdhaṃ vaseyam aham acyuta
a yāvad dhi sūcyās tīkṣṇāyā vidhyed agreṇa māriṣa
c tāvad apy aparityājyaṃ bhūmer naḥ pāṇḍavān prati
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a sarvān vas tāta śocāmi tyakto duryodhano mayā
c ye mandam anuyāsyadhvaṃ yāntaṃ vaivasvatakṣayam
a rurūṇām iva yūtheṣu vyāghrāḥ praharatāṃ varāḥ
c varān varān haniṣyanti sametā yudhi pāṇḍavāḥ
a pratīpam iva me bhāti yuyudhānena bhāratī
c vyastā sīmantinī trastā pramṛṣṭā dīrghabāhunā
a saṃpūrṇaṃ pūrayan bhūyo balaṃ pārthasya mādhavaḥ
c śaineyaḥ samare sthātā bījavat pravapañ śarān
a senāmukhe prayuddhānāṃ bhīmaseno bhaviṣyati
c taṃ sarve saṃśrayiṣyanti prākāram akutobhayam
a yadā drakṣyasi bhīmena kuñjarān vinipātitān
c viśīrṇadantān giryābhān bhinnakumbhān saśoṇitān
a tān abhiprekṣya saṃgrāme viśīrṇān iva parvatān
c bhīto bhīmasya saṃsparśāt smartāsi vacanasya me
a nirdagdhaṃ bhīmasenena sainyaṃ hatarathadvipam
c gatim agner iva prekṣya smartāsi vacanasya me
a mahad vo bhayam āgāmi na cec chāmyatha pāṇḍavaiḥ
c gadayā bhīmasenena hatāḥ śamam upaiṣyatha
a mahāvanam iva chinnaṃ yadā drakṣyasi pātitam
c balaṃ kurūṇāṃ saṃgrāme tadā smartāsi me vacaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a etāvad uktvā rājā tu sa sarvān pṛthivīpatīn
c anubhāṣya mahārāja punaḥ papraccha saṃjayam
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a yad abrūtāṃ mahātmānau vāsudevadhanaṃjayau
c tan me brūhi mahāprājña śuśrūṣe vacanaṃ tava
 saṃjaya uvāca
a śṛṇu rājan yathā dṛṣṭau mayā kṛṣṇadhanaṃjayau
c ūcatuś cāpi yad vīrau tat te vakṣyāmi bhārata
a pādāṅgulīr abhiprekṣan prayato 'haṃ kṛtāñjaliḥ
c śuddhāntaṃ prāviśaṃ rājann ākhyātuṃ naradevayoḥ
a naivābhimanyur na yamau taṃ deśam abhiyānti vai
c yatra kṛṣṇau ca kṛṣṇā ca satyabhāmā ca bhāminī
a ubhau madhvāsavakṣībāv ubhau candanarūṣitau
b ekaparyaṅkaśayanau dṛṣṭau me keśavārjunau
c sragviṇau varavastrau tau divyābharaṇabhūṣitau
a naikaratnavicitraṃ tu kāñcanaṃ mahad āsanam
c vividhāstaraṇāstīrṇaṃ yatrāsātām ariṃdamau
d satyāṅkam upadhānaṃ tu kṛtvā śete janārdanaḥ
a arjunotsaṅgagau pādau keśavasyopalakṣaye
c arjunasya ca kṛṣṇāyāṃ satyāyāṃ ca mahātmanaḥ
a kāñcanaṃ pādapīṭhaṃ tu pārtho me prādiśat tadā
c tad ahaṃ pāṇinā spṛṣṭvā tato bhūmāv upāviśam
a ūrdhvarekhatalau pādau pārthasya śubhalakṣaṇau
c pādapīṭhād apahṛtau tatrāpaśyam ahaṃ śubhau
d na nūnaṃ kalmaṣaṃ kiṃ cin mama karmasu vidyate
d strīratnābhyāṃ sametau yan mitho mām abhyabhāṣatām
d vismayo me mahān āsīd āstraṃ me bahu saṃgatam
d hṛṣṭāni caiva romāṇi dṛṣṭvā tau sahitāv ubhau
a śyāmau bṛhantau taruṇau śālaskandhāv ivodgatau
c ekāsanagatau dṛṣṭvā bhayaṃ māṃ mahad āviśat
d tato 'bhyacintayaṃ tatra dṛṣṭvā tau puruṣarṣabhau
a indraviṣṇusamāv etau mandātmā nāvabudhyate
c saṃśrayād droṇabhīṣmābhyāṃ karṇasya ca vikatthanāt
a nideśasthāv imau yasya mānasas tasya setsyate
c saṃkalpo dharmarājasya niścayo me tadābhavat
a satkṛtaś cānnapānābhyām ācchanno labdhasatkriyaḥ
c añjaliṃ mūrdhni saṃdhāya tau saṃdeśam acodayam
a dhanurbāṇocitenaikapāṇinā śubhalakṣaṇam
c pādam ānamayan pārthaḥ keśavaṃ samacodayat
a indraketur ivotthāya sarvābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ
c indravīryopamaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ saṃviṣṭo mābhyabhāṣata
a vācaṃ sa vadatāṃ śreṣṭho hlādinīṃ vacanakṣamām
c trāsanīṃ dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ mṛdupūrvāṃ sudāruṇām
d bahiścarasya prāṇasya priyasya priyakāriṇaḥ
d matimān matim āsthāya keśavaḥ saṃdadhe vacaḥ
a vācaṃ tāṃ vacanārhasya śikṣākṣarasamanvitām
c aśrauṣam aham iṣṭārthāṃ paścād dhṛdayaśoṣiṇīm
 vāsudeva uvāca
a saṃjayedaṃ vaco brūyā dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ manīṣiṇam
c śṛṇvataḥ kurumukhyasya droṇasyāpi ca śṛṇvataḥ
d āvayor vacanāt sūta jyeṣṭhān apy abhivādayan
d yavīyasaś ca kuśalaṃ paścāt pṛṣṭvaivam uttaram
a yajadhvaṃ vipulair yajñair viprebhyo datta dakṣiṇāḥ
c putrair dāraiś ca modadhvaṃ mahad vo bhayam āgatam
a arthāṃs tyajata pātrebhyaḥ sutān prāpnuta kāmajān
c priyaṃ priyebhyaś carata rājā hi tvarate jaye
a ṛṇam etat pravṛddhaṃ me hṛdayān nāpasarpati
c yad govindeti cukrośa kṛṣṇā māṃ dūravāsinam
a tejomayaṃ durādharṣaṃ gāṇḍīvaṃ yasya kārmukam
c maddvitīyena teneha vairaṃ vaḥ savyasācinā
d kṛṣṇasya tad vacaḥ śrutvā bhayaṃ māṃ mahad āviśat
d tava putrasya lobhaṃ tu vartamānaṃ pramṛśyataḥ
a maddvitīyaṃ punaḥ pārthaṃ kaḥ prārthayitum icchati
c yo na kālaparīto vāpy api sākṣāt puraṃdaraḥ
a bāhubhyām udvahed bhūmiṃ dahet kruddha imāḥ prajāḥ
c pātayet tridivād devān yo 'rjunaṃ samare jayet
a devāsuramanuṣyeṣu yakṣagandharvabhogiṣu
c na taṃ paśyāmy ahaṃ yuddhe pāṇḍavaṃ yo 'bhyayād raṇe
a yat tad virāṭanagare śrūyate mahad adbhutam
c ekasya ca bahūnāṃ ca paryāptaṃ tan nidarśanam
a ekena pāṇḍuputreṇa virāṭanagare yadā
c bhagnāḥ palāyanta diśaḥ paryāptaṃ tan nidarśanam
a balaṃ vīryaṃ ca tejaś ca śīghratā laghuhastatā
c aviṣādaś ca dhairyaṃ ca pārthān nānyatra vidyate
 saṃjaya uvāca
a ity abravīd dhṛṣīkeśaḥ pārtham uddharṣayan girā
c garjan samayavarṣīva gagane pākaśāsanaḥ
a keśavasya vacaḥ śrutvā kirīṭī śvetavāhanaḥ
c arjunas tan mahad vākyam abravīl lomaharṣaṇam
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a saṃjayasya vacaḥ śrutvā prajñācakṣur nareśvaraḥ
c tataḥ saṃkhyātum ārebhe tad vaco guṇadoṣataḥ
a prasaṃkhyāya ca saukṣmyeṇa guṇadoṣān vicakṣaṇaḥ
c yathāvan matitattvena jayakāmaḥ sutān prati
a balābale viniścitya yāthātathyena buddhimān
b yadā tu mene bhūyiṣṭhaṃ tad vaco guṇadoṣataḥ
b punar eva kurūṇāṃ ca pāṇḍavānāṃ ca buddhimān
c śaktiṃ saṃkhyātum ārebhe tadā vai manujādhipaḥ
a devamānuṣayoḥ śaktyā tejasā caiva pāṇḍavān
c kurūñ śaktyālpatarayā duryodhanam athābravīt
a duryodhaneyaṃ cintā me śaśvan nāpy upaśāmyati
b īdṛśe 'bhiniviṣṭasya pṛthivīkṣayakārake
b adharme cāyaśasye ca kārye mahati dāruṇe
b pāṇḍavair vigrahas tāta sarvathā taṃ na rocaye
c satyaṃ hy etad ahaṃ manye pratyakṣaṃ nānumānataḥ
a ātmajeṣu paraṃ snehaṃ sarvabhūtāni kurvate
c priyāṇi caiṣāṃ kurvanti yathāśakti hitāni ca
a evam evopakartṝṇāṃ prāyaśo lakṣayāmahe
c icchanti bahulaṃ santaḥ pratikartuṃ mahat priyam
a agniḥ sācivyakartā syāt khāṇḍave tat kṛtaṃ smaran
c arjunasyātibhīme 'smin kurupāṇḍusamāgame
a jātagṛdhyābhipannāś ca pāṇḍavānām anekaśaḥ
c dharmādayo bhaviṣyanti samāhūtā divaukasaḥ
a bhīṣmadroṇakṛpādīnāṃ bhayād aśanisaṃmitam
c rirakṣiṣantaḥ saṃrambhaṃ gamiṣyantīti me matiḥ
a te devasahitāḥ pārthā na śakyāḥ prativīkṣitum
c mānuṣeṇa naravyāghrā vīryavanto 'strapāragāḥ
a durāsadaṃ yasya divyaṃ gāṇḍīvaṃ dhanur uttamam
c vāruṇau cākṣayau divyau śarapūrṇau maheṣudhī
a vānaraś ca dhvajo divyo niḥsaṅgo dhūmavad gatiḥ
c rathaś ca caturantāyāṃ yasya nāsti samas tviṣā
a mahāmeghanibhaś cāpi nirghoṣaḥ śrūyate janaiḥ
c mahāśanisamaḥ śabdaḥ śātravāṇāṃ bhayaṃkaraḥ
a yaṃ cātimānuṣaṃ vīrye kṛtsno loko vyavasyati
c devānām api jetāraṃ yaṃ viduḥ pārthivā raṇe
a śatāni pañca caiveṣūn udvapann iva dṛśyate
c nimeṣāntaramātreṇa muñcan dūraṃ ca pātayan
a yam āha bhīṣmo droṇaś ca kṛpo drauṇis tathaiva ca
c madrarājas tathā śalyo madhyasthā ye ca mānavāḥ
a yuddhāyāvasthitaṃ pārthaṃ pārthivair atimānuṣaiḥ
c aśakyaṃ rathaśārdūlaṃ parājetum ariṃdamam
a kṣipaty ekena vegena pañca bāṇaśatāni yaḥ
c sadṛśaṃ bāhuvīryeṇa kārtavīryasya pāṇḍavam
a tam arjunaṃ maheṣvāsaṃ mahendropendrarakṣitam
c nighnantam iva paśyāmi vimarde 'smin mahāmṛdhe
a ity evaṃ cintayan kṛtsnam ahorātrāṇi bhārata
c anidro niḥsukhaś cāsmi kurūṇāṃ śamacintayā
a kṣayodayo 'yaṃ sumahān kurūṇāṃ pratyupasthitaḥ
c asya cet kalahasyāntaḥ śamād anyo na vidyate
a śamo me rocate nityaṃ pārthais tāta na vigrahaḥ
c kurubhyo hi sadā manye pāṇḍavāñ śaktimattarān
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a pitur etad vacaḥ śrutvā dhārtarāṣṭro 'tyamarṣaṇaḥ
c ādhāya vipulaṃ krodhaṃ punar evedam abravīt
a aśakyā devasacivāḥ pārthāḥ syur iti yad bhavān
c manyate tadbhayaṃ vyetu bhavato rājasattama
a akāmadveṣasaṃyogād drohāl lobhāc ca bhārata
c upekṣayā ca bhāvānāṃ devā devatvam āpnuvan
a iti dvaipāyano vyāso nāradaś ca mahātapāḥ
c jāmadagnyaś ca rāmo naḥ kathām akathayat purā
a naiva mānuṣavad devāḥ pravartante kadā cana
c kāmāl lobhād anukrośād dveṣāc ca bharatarṣabha
a yadi hy agniś ca vāyuś ca dharma indro 'śvināv api
c kāmayogāt pravarteran na pārthā duḥkham āpnuyuḥ
a tasmān na bhavatā cintā kāryaiṣā syāt kadā cana
c daiveṣv apekṣakā hy ete śaśvad bhāveṣu bhārata
a atha cet kāmasaṃyogād dveṣāl lobhāc ca lakṣyate
c deveṣu devaprāmāṇyaṃ naiva tad vikramiṣyati
a mayābhimantritaḥ śaśvaj jātavedāḥ praśaṃsati
c didhakṣuḥ sakalāṃl lokān parikṣipya samantataḥ
a yad vā paramakaṃ tejo yena yuktā divaukasaḥ
c mamāpy anupamaṃ bhūyo devebhyo viddhi bhārata
a pradīryamāṇāṃ vasudhāṃ girīṇāṃ śikharāṇi ca
c lokasya paśyato rājan sthāpayāmy abhimantraṇāt
a cetanācetanasyāsya jaṅgamasthāvarasya ca
c vināśāya samutpannaṃ mahāghoraṃ mahāsvanam
a aśmavarṣaṃ ca vāyuṃ ca śamayāmīha nityaśaḥ
c jagataḥ paśyato 'bhīkṣṇaṃ bhūtānām anukampayā
a stambhitāsv apsu gacchanti mayā rathapadātayaḥ
c devāsurāṇāṃ bhāvānām aham ekaḥ pravartitā
a akṣauhiṇībhir yān deśān yāmi kāryeṇa kena cit
c tatrāpo me pravartante yatra yatrābhikāmaye
a bhayāni viṣaye rājan vyālādīni na santi me
c mattaḥ suptāni bhūtāni na hiṃsanti bhayaṃkarāḥ
a nikāmavarṣī parjanyo rājan viṣayavāsinām
c dharmiṣṭhāś ca prajāḥ sarvā ītayaś ca na santi me
a aśvināv atha vāyvagnī marudbhiḥ saha vṛtrahā
c dharmaś caiva mayā dviṣṭān notsahante 'bhirakṣitum
a yadi hy ete samarthāḥ syur maddviṣas trātum ojasā
c na sma trayodaśa samāḥ pārthā duḥkham avāpnuyuḥ
a naiva devā na gandharvā nāsurā na ca rākṣasāḥ
c śaktās trātuṃ mayā dviṣṭaṃ satyam etad bravīmi te
a yad abhidhyāmy ahaṃ śaśvac chubhaṃ vā yadi vāśubham
c naitad vipannapūrvaṃ me mitreṣv ariṣu cobhayoḥ
a bhaviṣyatīdam iti vā yad bravīmi paraṃtapa
c nānyathā bhūtapūrvaṃ tat satyavāg iti māṃ viduḥ
a lokasākṣikam etan me māhātmyaṃ dikṣu viśrutam
c āśvāsanārthaṃ bhavataḥ proktaṃ na ślāghayā nṛpa
a na hy ahaṃ ślāghano rājan bhūtapūrvaḥ kadā cana
c asad ācaritaṃ hy etad yad ātmānaṃ praśaṃsati
a pāṇḍavāṃś caiva matsyāṃś ca pāñcālān kekayaiḥ saha
c sātyakiṃ vāsudevaṃ ca śrotāsi vijitān mayā
a saritaḥ sāgaraṃ prāpya yathā naśyanti sarvaśaḥ
c tathaiva te vinaṅkṣyanti mām āsādya sahānvayāḥ
a parā buddhiḥ paraṃ tejo vīryaṃ ca paramaṃ mayi
c parā vidyā paro yogo mama tebhyo viśiṣyate
a pitāmahaś ca droṇaś ca kṛpaḥ śalyaḥ śalas tathā
c astreṣu yat prajānanti sarvaṃ tan mayi vidyate
a ity uktvā saṃjayaṃ bhūyaḥ paryapṛcchata bhārata
c jñātvā yuyutsuḥ kāryāṇi prāptakālam ariṃdama
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tathā tu pṛcchantam atīva pārthān
vaicitravīryaṃ tam acintayitvā
c uvāca karṇo dhṛtarāṣṭraputraṃ
praharṣayan saṃsadi kauravāṇām
a mithyā pratijñāya mayā yad astraṃ
rāmād dhṛtaṃ brahmapuraṃ purastāt
c vijñāya tenāsmi tadaivam uktas
tavāntakāle 'pratibhāsyatīti
a mahāparādhe hy api saṃnatena
maharṣiṇāhaṃ guruṇā ca śaptaḥ
c śaktaḥ pradagdhuṃ hy api tigmatejāḥ
sasāgarām apy avaniṃ maharṣiḥ
a prasāditaṃ hy asya mayā mano 'bhūc
chuśrūṣayā svena ca pauruṣeṇa
c tatas tad astraṃ mama sāvaśeṣaṃ
tasmāt samartho 'smi mamaiṣa bhāraḥ
a nimeṣamātraṃ tam ṛṣiprasādam
avāpya pāñcālakarūṣamatsyān
c nihatya pārthāṃś ca saputrapautrāṃl
lokān ahaṃ śastrajitān prapatsye
a pitāmahas tiṣṭhatu te samīpe
droṇaś ca sarve ca narendramukhyāḥ
c yathāpradhānena balena yātvā
pārthān haniṣyāmi mamaiṣa bhāraḥ
a evaṃ bruvāṇaṃ tam uvāca bhīṣmaḥ
kiṃ katthase kālaparītabuddhe
c na karṇa jānāsi yathā pradhāne
hate hatāḥ syur dhṛtarāṣṭraputrāḥ
a yat khāṇḍavaṃ dāhayatā kṛtaṃ hi
kṛṣṇadvitīyena dhanaṃjayena
c śrutvaiva tat karma niyantum ātmā
śakyas tvayā vai saha bāndhavena
a yāṃ cāpi śaktiṃ tridaśādhipas te
dadau mahātmā bhagavān mahendraḥ
c bhasmīkṛtāṃ tāṃ patitāṃ viśīrṇāṃ
cakrāhatāṃ drakṣyasi keśavena
a yas te śaraḥ sarpamukho vibhāti
sadāgryamālyair mahitaḥ prayatnāt
c sa pāṇḍuputrābhihataḥ śaraughaiḥ
saha tvayā yāsyati karṇa nāśam
a bāṇasya bhaumasya ca karṇa hantā
kirīṭinaṃ rakṣati vāsudevaḥ
c yas tvādṛśānāṃ ca garīyasāṃ ca
hantā ripūṇāṃ tumule pragāḍhe
 karṇa uvāca
a asaṃśayaṃ vṛṣṇipatir yathoktas
tathā ca bhūyaś ca tato mahātmā
c ahaṃ yad uktaḥ paruṣaṃ tu kiṃ cit
pitāmahas tasya phalaṃ śṛṇotu
a nyasyāmi śastrāṇi na jātu saṃkhye
pitāmaho drakṣyati māṃ sabhāyām
c tvayi praśānte tu mama prabhāvaṃ
drakṣyanti sarve bhuvi bhūmipālāḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a ity evam uktvā sa mahādhanuṣmān
hitvā sabhāṃ svaṃ bhavanaṃ jagāma
c bhīṣmas tu duryodhanam eva rājan
madhye kurūṇāṃ prahasann uvāca
a satyapratijñaḥ kila sūtaputras
tathā sa bhāraṃ viṣaheta kasmāt
c vyūhaṃ prativyūhya śirāṃsi bhittvā
lokakṣayaṃ paśyata bhīmasenāt
a āvantyakāliṅgajayadratheṣu
vedidhvaje tiṣṭhati bāhlike ca
c ahaṃ haniṣyāmi sadā pareṣāṃ
sahasraśaś cāyutaśaś ca yodhān
a yadaiva rāme bhagavaty anindye
brahma bruvāṇaḥ kṛtavāṃs tad astram
c tadaiva dharmaś ca tapaś ca naṣṭaṃ
vaikartanasyādhamapūruṣasya
a athoktavākye nṛpatau tu bhīṣme
nikṣipya śastrāṇi gate ca karṇe
c vaicitravīryasya suto 'lpabuddhir
duryodhanaḥ śāṃtanavaṃ babhāṣe
 duryodhana uvāca
a sadṛśānāṃ manuṣyeṣu sarveṣāṃ tulyajanmanām
c katham ekāntatas teṣāṃ pārthānāṃ manyase jayam
d vayaṃ ca te 'pi tulyā vai vīryeṇa ca parākramaiḥ
d samena vayasā caiva prātibhena śrutena ca
d astreṇa yodhayugyāsu śīghratve kauśale tathā
a sarve sma samajātīyāḥ sarve mānuṣayonayaḥ
c pitāmaha vijānīṣe pārtheṣu vijayaṃ katham
a nāhaṃ bhavati na droṇe na kṛpe na ca bāhlike
c anyeṣu ca narendreṣu parākramya samārabhe
a ahaṃ vaikartanaḥ karṇo bhrātā duḥśāsanaś ca me
c pāṇḍavān samare pañca haniṣyāmaḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a tato rājan mahāyajñair vividhair bhūridakṣiṇaiḥ
c brāhmaṇāṃs tarpayiṣyāmi gobhir aśvair dhanena ca
d sukhāny avāpya sahitāḥ kṛtvā karma suduṣkaram
d visrabdhāḥ svargam eṣyāmaḥ kāle prāpte gatajvarāḥ
d athābravīn mahārājo dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ sudurmanāḥ
d viduraṃ viduṣāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ sarvapārthivasaṃnidhau
d mohito mṛtyupāśena kālasya vaśam āgataḥ
d tāta karṇena sahitaḥ putro duryodhano mama
d yadā parikariṣyanti aiṇeyān iva tantunā
d ataritrān iva jale bāhubhir māmakā raṇe
d paśyantas te parāṃs tatra rathanāgasamākulān
d vidura uvāca
d tadā darpaṃ vimokṣyanti pāṇḍavāḥ sa ca keśavaḥ
d iha niḥśreyasaṃ prāhur vṛddhā niścitadarśinaḥ
d brāhmaṇasya viśeṣeṇa damo dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ
d tasya dānaṃ kṣamā siddhir yathāvad upapadyate
d damo dānaṃ tapo jñānam adhītaṃ cānuvartate
d damas tejo vardhayati pavitraṃ dama uttamam
d vipāpmā vṛddhatejās tu puruṣo vindate mahat
d kravyādbhya iva bhūtānām adāntebhyaḥ sadā bhayam
d teṣāṃ ca pratiṣedhārthaṃ kṣatraṃ sṛṣṭaṃ svayaṃbhuvā
d āśrameṣu caturṣv āhur damam evottamaṃ vratam
d tasya liṅgaṃ pravakṣyāmi yeṣāṃ samudayo damaḥ
d kṣamā dhṛtir ahiṃsā ca samatā satyam ārjavam
d indriyābhijayo dhairyaṃ mārdavaṃ hrīr acāpalam
d akārpaṇyam asaṃrambhaḥ saṃtoṣaḥ śraddadhānatā
d etāni yasya rājendra sa dāntaḥ puruṣaḥ smṛtaḥ
d kāmo lobhaś ca darpaś ca manyur nidrā vikatthanam
d māna īrṣyā ca śokaś ca naitad dānto niṣevate
d ajihmam aśaṭhaṃ śuddham etad dāntasya lakṣaṇam
d alolupas tathālpepsuḥ kāmānām avicintitā
d samudrakalpaḥ puruṣaḥ sa dāntaḥ parikīrtitaḥ
d suvṛttaḥ śīlasaṃpannaḥ prasannātmātmavid budhaḥ
d prāpyeha loke saṃmānaṃ sugatiṃ pretya gacchati
d abhayaṃ yasya bhūtebhyaḥ sarveṣām abhayaṃ yataḥ
d sa vai pariṇataprajñaḥ prakhyāto manujottamaḥ
d sarvabhūtahito maitras tasmān nodvijate janaḥ
d samudra iva gambhīraḥ prajñātṛptaḥ praśāmyati
d karmaṇācaritaṃ pūrvaṃ sadbhir ācaritaṃ ca yat
d tad evāsthāya modante dāntāḥ śamaparāyaṇāḥ
d naiṣkarmyaṃ vā samāsthāya jñānatṛpto jitendriyaḥ
d kālākāṅkṣī caraṃl loke brahmabhūyāya kalpate
d śakunīnām ivākāśe padaṃ naivopalabhyate
d evaṃ prajñānatṛptasya muner vartma na dṛśyate
d utsṛjya vā gṛhān yas tu mokṣam evābhimanyate
d lokās tejomayās tasya kalpante śāśvatā divi
 vidura uvāca
a śakunīnām ihārthāya pāśaṃ bhūmāv ayojayat
c kaś cic chākunikas tāta pūrveṣām iti śuśruma
a tasmin dvau śakunau baddhau yugapat samapauruṣau
c tāv upādāya taṃ pāśaṃ jagmatuḥ khacarāv ubhau
a tau vihāyasam ākrāntau dṛṣṭvā śākunikas tadā
c anvadhāvad anirviṇṇo yena yena sma gacchataḥ
a tathā tam anudhāvantaṃ mṛgayuṃ śakunārthinam
c āśramastho muniḥ kaś cid dadarśātha kṛtāhnikaḥ
a tāv antarikṣagau śīghram anuyāntaṃ mahīcaram
c ślokenānena kauravya papraccha sa munis tadā
a vicitram idam āścaryaṃ mṛgahan pratibhāti me
c plavamānau hi khacarau padātir anudhāvasi
 śākunika uvāca
a pāśam ekam ubhāv etau sahitau harato mama
c yatra vai vivadiṣyete tatra me vaśam eṣyataḥ
 vidura uvāca
a tau vivādam anuprāptau śakunau mṛtyusaṃdhitau
c vigṛhya ca sudurbuddhī pṛthivyāṃ saṃnipetatuḥ
a tau yudhyamānau saṃrabdhau mṛtyupāśavaśānugau
c upasṛtyāparijñāto jagrāha mṛgayus tadā
a evaṃ ye jñātayo 'rtheṣu mitho gacchanti vigraham
c te 'mitravaśam āyānti śakunāv iva vigrahāt
a saṃbhojanaṃ saṃkathanaṃ saṃpraśno 'tha samāgamaḥ
c etāni jñātikāryāṇi na virodhaḥ kadā cana
a yasmin kāle sumanasaḥ sarve vṛddhān upāsate
c siṃhaguptam ivāraṇyam apradhṛṣyā bhavanti te
a ye 'rthaṃ saṃtatam āsādya dīnā iva samāsate
c śriyaṃ te saṃprayacchanti dviṣadbhyo bharatarṣabha
a dhūmāyante vyapetāni jvalanti sahitāni ca
c dhṛtarāṣṭrolmukānīva jñātayo bharatarṣabha
a idam anyat pravakṣyāmi yathā dṛṣṭaṃ girau mayā
c śrutvā tad api kauravya yathā śreyas tathā kuru
a vayaṃ kirātaiḥ sahitā gacchāmo girim uttaram
c brāhmaṇair devakalpaiś ca vidyājambhakavātikaiḥ
a kuñjabhūtaṃ giriṃ sarvam abhito gandhamādanam
c dīpyamānauṣadhigaṇaṃ siddhagandharvasevitam
a tatra paśyāmahe sarve madhu pītam amākṣikam
c maruprapāte viṣame niviṣṭaṃ kumbhasaṃmitam
a āśīviṣai rakṣyamāṇaṃ kuberadayitaṃ bhṛśam
c yat prāśya puruṣo martyo amaratvaṃ nigacchati
a acakṣur labhate cakṣur vṛddho bhavati vai yuvā
c iti te kathayanti sma brāhmaṇā jambhasādhakāḥ
a tataḥ kirātās tad dṛṣṭvā prārthayanto mahīpate
c vineśur viṣame tasmin sasarpe girigahvare
d āśābaddhāḥ patanti sma sarva eva gatāsavaḥ
a tathaiva tava putro 'yaṃ pṛthivīm eka icchati
c madhu paśyati saṃmohāt prapātaṃ nānupaśyati
a duryodhano yoddhumanāḥ samare savyasācinā
c na ca paśyāmi tejo 'sya vikramaṃ vā tathāvidham
a ekena ratham āsthāya pṛthivī yena nirjitā
b bhīṣmadroṇaprabhṛtayaḥ saṃtrastāḥ sādhuyāyinaḥ
b virāṭanagare bhagnāḥ kiṃ tatra tava dṛśyatām
c pratīkṣamāṇo yo vīraḥ kṣamate vīkṣitaṃ tava
a drupado matsyarājaś ca saṃkruddhaś ca dhanaṃjayaḥ
c na śeṣayeyuḥ samare vāyuyuktā ivāgnayaḥ
a aṅke kuruṣva rājānaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭra yudhiṣṭhiram
c yudhyator hi dvayor yuddhe naikāntena bhavej jayaḥ
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a duryodhana vijānīhi yat tvāṃ vakṣyāmi putraka
c utpathaṃ manyase mārgam anabhijña ivādhvagaḥ
a pañcānāṃ pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ yat tejaḥ pramimīṣasi
c pañcānām iva bhūtānāṃ mahatāṃ sumahātmanām
a yudhiṣṭhiraṃ hi kaunteyaṃ paraṃ dharmam ihāsthitam
c parāṃ gatim asaṃprekṣya na tvaṃ vettum ihārhasi
a bhīmasenaṃ ca kaunteyaṃ yasya nāsti samo bale
c raṇāntakaṃ tarkayase mahāvātam iva drumaḥ
a sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ meruṃ śikhariṇām iva
c yudhi gāṇḍīvadhanvānaṃ ko nu yudhyeta buddhimān
a dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pāñcālyaḥ kam ivādya na śātayet
c śatrumadhye śarān muñcan devarāḍ aśanīm iva
a sātyakiś cāpi durdharṣaḥ saṃmato 'ndhakavṛṣṇiṣu
c dhvaṃsayiṣyati te senāṃ pāṇḍaveyahite rataḥ
a yaḥ punaḥ pratimānena trīṃl lokān atiricyate
c taṃ kṛṣṇaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ ko nu yudhyeta buddhimān
a ekato hy asya dārāś ca jñātayaś ca sabāndhavāḥ
c ātmā ca pṛthivī ceyam ekataś ca dhanaṃjayaḥ
a vāsudevo 'pi durdharṣo yatātmā yatra pāṇḍavaḥ
c aviṣahyaṃ pṛthivyāpi tad balaṃ yatra keśavaḥ
a tiṣṭha tāta satāṃ vākye suhṛdām arthavādinām
c vṛddhaṃ śāṃtanavaṃ bhīṣmaṃ titikṣasva pitāmaham
a māṃ ca bruvāṇaṃ śuśrūṣa kurūṇām arthavādinam
c droṇaṃ kṛpaṃ vikarṇaṃ ca mahārājaṃ ca bāhlikam
a ete hy api yathaivāhaṃ mantum arhasi tāṃs tathā
c sarve dharmavido hy ete tulyasnehāś ca bhārata
a yat tad virāṭanagare saha bhrātṛbhir agrataḥ
c utsṛjya gāḥ susaṃtrastaṃ balaṃ te samaśīryata
a yac caiva tasmin nagare śrūyate mahad adbhutam
c ekasya ca bahūnāṃ ca paryāptaṃ tan nidarśanam
a arjunas tat tathākārṣīt kiṃ punaḥ sarva eva te
c sabhrātṝn abhijānīhi vṛttyā ca pratipādaya
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a evam uktvā mahāprājño dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ suyodhanam
c punar eva mahābhāgaḥ saṃjayaṃ paryapṛcchata
a brūhi saṃjaya yac cheṣaṃ vāsudevād anantaram
c yad arjuna uvāca tvāṃ paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi me
 saṃjaya uvāca
a vāsudevavacaḥ śrutvā kuntīputro dhanaṃjayaḥ
c uvāca kāle durdharṣo vāsudevasya śṛṇvataḥ
a pitāmahaṃ śāṃtanavaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ ca saṃjaya
c droṇaṃ kṛpaṃ ca karṇaṃ ca mahārājaṃ ca bāhlikam
a drauṇiṃ ca somadattaṃ ca śakuniṃ cāpi saubalam
c duḥśāsanaṃ śalaṃ caiva purumitraṃ viviṃśatim
a vikarṇaṃ citrasenaṃ ca jayatsenaṃ ca pārthivam
c vindānuvindāv āvantyau durmukhaṃ cāpi kauravam
a saindhavaṃ duḥsahaṃ caiva bhūriśravasam eva ca
c bhagadattaṃ ca rājānaṃ jalasaṃdhaṃ ca pārthivam
a ye cāpy anye pārthivās tatra yoddhuṃ
samāgatāḥ kauravāṇāṃ priyārtham
c mumūrṣavaḥ pāṇḍavāgnau pradīpte
samānītā dhārtarāṣṭreṇa sūta
a yathānyāyaṃ kauśalaṃ vandanaṃ ca
samāgatā madvacanena vācyāḥ
c idaṃ brūyāḥ saṃjaya rājamadhye
suyodhanaṃ pāpakṛtāṃ pradhānam
a amarṣaṇaṃ durmatiṃ rājaputraṃ
pāpātmānaṃ dhārtarāṣṭraṃ sulubdham
c sarvaṃ mamaitad vacanaṃ samagraṃ
sahāmātyaṃ saṃjaya śrāvayethāḥ
a evaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya dhanaṃjayo māṃ
tato 'rthavad dharmavac cāpi vākyam
c provācedaṃ vāsudevaṃ samīkṣya
pārtho dhīmāṃl lohitāntāyatākṣaḥ
a yathā śrutaṃ te vadato mahātmano
madhupravīrasya vacaḥ samāhitam
c tathaiva vācyaṃ bhavatā hi madvacaḥ
samāgateṣu kṣitipeṣu sarvaśaḥ
a śarāgnidhūme rathaneminādite
dhanuḥsruveṇāstrabalāpahāriṇā
c yathā na homaḥ kriyate mahāmṛdhe
tathā sametya prayatadhvam ādṛtāḥ
a na cet prayacchadhvam amitraghātino
yudhiṣṭhirasyāṃśam abhīpsitaṃ svakam
c nayāmi vaḥ svāśvapadātikuñjarān
diśaṃ pitṝṇām aśivāṃ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ
a tato 'ham āmantrya caturbhujaṃ hariṃ
dhanaṃjayaṃ caiva namasya satvaraḥ
c javena saṃprāpta ihāmaradyute
tavāntikaṃ prāpayituṃ vaco mahat
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a duryodhane dhārtarāṣṭre tad vaco 'pratinandati
c tūṣṇīṃbhūteṣu sarveṣu samuttasthur nareśvarāḥ
a utthiteṣu mahārāja pṛthivyāṃ sarvarājasu
c rahite saṃjayaṃ rājā paripraṣṭuṃ pracakrame
a āśaṃsamāno vijayaṃ teṣāṃ putravaśānugaḥ
c ātmanaś ca pareṣāṃ ca pāṇḍavānāṃ ca niścayam
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a gāvalgaṇe brūhi naḥ sāraphalgu
svasenāyāṃ yāvad ihāsti kiṃ cit
c tvaṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ nipuṇaṃ vettha sarvaṃ
kim eṣāṃ jyāyaḥ kim u teṣāṃ kanīyaḥ
a tvam etayoḥ sāravit sarvadarśī
dharmārthayor nipuṇo niścayajñaḥ
c sa me pṛṣṭaḥ saṃjaya brūhi sarvaṃ
yudhyamānāḥ katare 'smin na santi
 saṃjaya uvāca
a na tvāṃ brūyāṃ rahite jātu kiṃ cid
asūyā hi tvāṃ prasaheta rājan
c ānayasva pitaraṃ saṃśitavrataṃ
gāṃdhārīṃ ca mahiṣīm ājamīḍha
a tau te 'sūyāṃ vinayetāṃ narendra
dharmajñau tau nipuṇau niścayajñau
c tayos tu tvāṃ saṃnidhau tad vadeyaṃ
kṛtsnaṃ mataṃ vāsudevārjunābhyām
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
 ity uktena ca gāndhārī vyāsaś cātrājagāma ha
 ānītau vidureṇeha sabhāṃ śīghraṃ praveśitau
a tatas tan matam ājñāya saṃjayasyātmajasya ca
b trikāladarśī bhagavān dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ mahāmuniḥ
c abhyupetya mahāprājñaḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyano 'bravīt
a saṃpṛcchate dhṛtarāṣṭrāya saṃjaya
ācakṣva sarvaṃ yāvad eṣo 'nuyuṅkte
c sarvaṃ yāvad vettha tasmin yathāvad
yāthātathyaṃ vāsudeve 'rjune ca
 saṃjaya uvāca
a arjuno vāsudevaś ca dhanvinau paramārcitau
c kāmād anyatra saṃbhūtau sarvābhāvāya saṃmitau
a dyām antaraṃ samāsthāya yathāyuktaṃ manasvinaḥ
c cakraṃ tad vāsudevasya māyayā vartate vibho
a sāpahnavaṃ pāṇḍaveṣu pāṇḍavānāṃ susaṃmatam
c sārāsārabalaṃ jñātvā tat samāsena me śṛṇu
a narakaṃ śambaraṃ caiva kaṃsaṃ caidyaṃ ca mādhavaḥ
c jitavān ghorasaṃkāśān krīḍann iva janārdanaḥ
a pṛthivīṃ cāntarikṣaṃ ca dyāṃ caiva puruṣottamaḥ
c manasaiva viśiṣṭātmā nayaty ātmavaśaṃ vaśī
a bhūyo bhūyo hi yad rājan pṛcchase pāṇḍavān prati
c sārāsārabalaṃ jñātuṃ tan me nigadataḥ śṛṇu
a ekato vā jagat kṛtsnam ekato vā janārdanaḥ
c sārato jagataḥ kṛtsnād atirikto janārdanaḥ
a bhasma kuryāj jagad idaṃ manasaiva janārdanaḥ
c na tu kṛtsnaṃ jagac chaktaṃ bhasma kartuṃ janārdanam
a yataḥ satyaṃ yato dharmo yato hrīr ārjavaṃ yataḥ
c tato bhavati govindo yataḥ kṛṣṇas tato jayaḥ
a pṛthivīṃ cāntarikṣaṃ ca divaṃ ca puruṣottamaḥ
c viceṣṭayati bhūtātmā krīḍann iva janārdanaḥ
d bhasmīkuryāj jagat sarvaṃ nimeṣeṇeti me matiḥ
d yatra bhāve 'pi yad rājan pṛcchase pāṇḍavān prati
a sa kṛtvā pāṇḍavān satraṃ lokaṃ saṃmohayann iva
c adharmaniratān mūḍhān dagdhum icchati te sutān
a kālacakraṃ jagaccakraṃ yugacakraṃ ca keśavaḥ
c ātmayogena bhagavān parivartayate 'niśam
a kālasya ca hi mṛtyoś ca jaṅgamasthāvarasya ca
c īśate bhagavān ekaḥ satyam etad bravīmi te
a īśann api mahāyogī sarvasya jagato hariḥ
c karmāṇy ārabhate kartuṃ kīnāśa iva durbalaḥ
a tena vañcayate lokān māyāyogena keśavaḥ
c ye tam eva prapadyante na te muhyanti mānavāḥ
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a kathaṃ tvaṃ mādhavaṃ vettha sarvalokamaheśvaram
c katham enaṃ na vedāhaṃ tan mamācakṣva saṃjaya
 saṃjaya uvāca
a vidyā rājan na te vidyā mama vidyā na hīyate
c vidyāhīnas tamodhvasto nābhijānāti keśavam
a vidyayā tāta jānāmi triyugaṃ madhusūdanam
c kartāram akṛtaṃ devaṃ bhūtānāṃ prabhavāpyayam
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a gāvalgaṇe 'tra kā bhaktir yā te nityā janārdane
c yayā tvam abhijānāsi triyugaṃ madhusūdanam
 saṃjaya uvāca
a māyāṃ na seve bhadraṃ te na vṛthādharmam ācare
c śuddhabhāvaṃ gato bhaktyā śāstrād vedmi janārdanam
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a duryodhana hṛṣīkeśaṃ prapadyasva janārdanam
c āpto naḥ saṃjayas tāta śaraṇaṃ gaccha keśavam
 duryodhana uvāca
a bhagavān devakīputro lokaṃ cen nihaniṣyati
c pravadann arjune sakhyaṃ nāhaṃ gacche 'dya keśavam
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a avāg gāndhāri putrās te gacchaty eṣa sudurmatiḥ
c īrṣyur durātmā mānī ca śreyasāṃ vacanātigaḥ
 gāndhāry uvāca
a aiśvaryakāma duṣṭātman vṛddhānāṃ śāsanātiga
c aiśvaryajīvite hitvā pitaraṃ māṃ ca bāliśa
a vardhayan durhṛdāṃ prītiṃ māṃ ca śokena vardhayan
c nihato bhīmasenena smartāsi vacanaṃ pituḥ
 vyāsa uvāca
a dayito 'si rājan kṛṣṇasya dhṛtarāṣṭra nibodha me
c yasya te saṃjayo dūto yas tvāṃ śreyasi yokṣyate
a jānāty eṣa hṛṣīkeśaṃ purāṇaṃ yac ca vai navam
c śuśrūṣamāṇam ekāgraṃ mokṣyate mahato bhayāt
a vaicitravīrya puruṣāḥ krodhaharṣatamovṛtāḥ
c sitā bahuvidhaiḥ pāśair ye na tuṣṭāḥ svakair dhanaiḥ
a yamasya vaśam āyānti kāmamūḍhāḥ punaḥ punaḥ
c andhanetrā yathaivāndhā nīyamānāḥ svakarmabhiḥ
a eṣa ekāyanaḥ panthā yena yānti manīṣiṇaḥ
c taṃ dṛṣṭvā mṛtyum atyeti mahāṃs tatra na sajjate
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a aṅga saṃjaya me śaṃsa panthānam akutobhayam
c yena gatvā hṛṣīkeśaṃ prāpnuyāṃ śāntim uttamām
 saṃjaya uvāca
a nākṛtātmā kṛtātmānaṃ jātu vidyāj janārdanam
c ātmanas tu kriyopāyo nānyatrendriyanigrahāt
a indriyāṇām udīrṇānāṃ kāmatyāgo 'pramādataḥ
c apramādo 'vihiṃsā ca jñānayonir asaṃśayam
a indriyāṇāṃ yame yatto bhava rājann atandritaḥ
c buddhiś ca mā te cyavatu niyacchaitāṃ yatas tataḥ
a etaj jñānaṃ vidur viprā dhruvam indriyadhāraṇam
c etaj jñānaṃ ca panthāś ca yena yānti manīṣiṇaḥ
a aprāpyaḥ keśavo rājann indriyair ajitair nṛbhiḥ
c āgamādhigato yogād vaśī tattve prasīdati
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a bhūyo me puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ saṃjayācakṣva pṛcchate
c nāmakarmārthavit tāta prāpnuyāṃ puruṣottamam
 saṃjaya uvāca
a śrutaṃ me tasya devasya nāmanirvacanaṃ śubham
c yāvat tatrābhijāne 'ham aprameyo hi keśavaḥ
a vasanāt sarvabhūtānāṃ vasutvād devayonitaḥ
c vāsudevas tato vedyo vṛṣatvād vṛṣṇir ucyate
a maunād dhyānāc ca yogāc ca viddhi bhārata mādhavam
c sarvatattvalayāc caiva madhuhā madhusūdanaḥ
a kṛṣir bhūvācakaḥ śabdo ṇaś ca nirvṛtivācakaḥ
c kṛṣṇas tadbhāvayogāc ca kṛṣṇo bhavati śāśvataḥ
a puṇḍarīkaṃ paraṃ dhāma nityam akṣayam akṣaram
c tadbhāvāt puṇḍarīkākṣo dasyutrāsāj janārdanaḥ
a yataḥ sattvaṃ na cyavate yac ca sattvān na hīyate
c sattvataḥ sātvatas tasmād ārṣabhād vṛṣabhekṣaṇaḥ
a na jāyate janitryāṃ yad ajas tasmād anīkajit
c devānāṃ svaprakāśatvād damād dāmodaraṃ viduḥ
a harṣāt saukhyāt sukhaiśvaryād dhṛṣīkeśatvam aśnute
c bāhubhyāṃ rodasī bibhran mahābāhur iti smṛtaḥ
a adho na kṣīyate jātu yasmāt tasmād adhokṣajaḥ
c narāṇām ayanāc cāpi tena nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ
d purāṇasadanāc caiva purātana iti smṛtaḥ
e pūraṇāt sadanāc caiva tato 'sau puruṣottamaḥ
a asataś ca sataś caiva sarvasya prabhavāpyayāt
b uddhoṣayed dharer nāma kākavat tattvacintane
b caraṇāyudhavad dhyāne bakavat sarvataḥ sthitiḥ
c sarvasya ca sadā jñānāt sarvam enaṃ pracakṣate
a satye pratiṣṭhitaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ satyam atra pratiṣṭhitam
c satyāt satyaṃ ca govindas tasmāt satyo 'pi nāmataḥ
a viṣṇur vikramaṇād eva jayanāj jiṣṇur ucyate
c śāśvatatvād anantaś ca govindo vedanād gavām
a atattvaṃ kurute tattvaṃ tena mohayate prajāḥ
c evaṃvidho dharmanityo bhagavān munibhiḥ saha
e āgantā hi mahābāhur ānṛśaṃsyārtham acyutaḥ
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a cakṣuṣmatāṃ vai spṛhayāmi saṃjaya
drakṣyanti ye vāsudevaṃ samīpe
c vibhrājamānaṃ vapuṣā pareṇa
prakāśayantaṃ pradiśo diśaś ca
d saṃjayaḥ
d vaktā vācaṃ rājamadhye sabhāyāṃ
d vṛṣṇiśreṣṭho munibhir bhrājamānaḥ
a īrayantaṃ bhāratīṃ bhāratānām
abhyarcanīyāṃ śaṃkarīṃ sṛñjayānām
c bubhūṣadbhir grahaṇīyām anindyāṃ
parāsūnām agrahaṇīyarūpām
a samudyantaṃ sātvatam ekavīraṃ
praṇetāram ṛṣabhaṃ yādavānām
c nihantāraṃ kṣobhaṇaṃ śātravāṇāṃ
muṣṇantaṃ ca dviṣatāṃ vai yaśāṃsi
a draṣṭāro hi kuravas taṃ sametā
mahātmānaṃ śatruhaṇaṃ vareṇyam
c bruvantaṃ vācam anṛśaṃsarūpāṃ
vṛṣṇiśreṣṭhaṃ mohayantaṃ madīyān
a ṛṣiṃ sanātanatamaṃ vipaścitaṃ
vācaḥ samudraṃ kalaśaṃ yatīnām
c ariṣṭanemiṃ garuḍaṃ suparṇaṃ
patiṃ prajānāṃ bhuvanasya dhāma
a sahasraśīrṣaṃ puruṣaṃ purāṇam
anādimadhyāntam anantakīrtim
c śukrasya dhātāram ajaṃ janitraṃ
paraṃ parebhyaḥ śaraṇaṃ prapadye
a trailokyanirmāṇakaraṃ janitraṃ
devāsurāṇām atha nāgarakṣasām
c narādhipānāṃ viduṣāṃ pradhānam
indrānujaṃ taṃ śaraṇaṃ prapadye
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
 janamejaya uvāca
 prayāte saṃjaye sādhau pāṇḍavān prati vai tadā
 kiṃ cakruḥ pāṇḍavās tatra mama pūrvapitāmahāḥ
 etat sarvaṃ dvijaśreṣṭha śrotum icchāmi śaṃsa me
a saṃjaye pratiyāte tu dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
b arjunaṃ bhīmasenaṃ ca mādrīputrau ca bhrātarau
b virāṭadrupadau caiva kekayānāṃ mahāratham
b abravīd upasaṃgamya śaṅkhacakragadādharam
b abhiyācāmahe gatvā prayātuṃ kurusaṃsadam
b yathā bhīṣmeṇa droṇena bāhlīkena ca dhīmatā
b anyaiś ca kurubhiḥ sārdhaṃ na yudhyemahi saṃyuge
b eṣa naḥ prathamaḥ kalpa etan naḥ śreya uttamam
b evam uktvā sumanasas te 'bhijagmur janārdanam
b pāṇḍavaiḥ saha rājāno marutvantam ivāmarāḥ
b tathā ca duḥsahāḥ sarve sadasyaiś ca nararṣabhāḥ
b janārdanaṃ samāsādya kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
b tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājann upagamya nararṣabham
c abhyabhāṣata dāśārham ṛṣabhaṃ sarvasātvatām
a ayaṃ sa kālaḥ saṃprāpto mitrāṇāṃ me janārdana
c na ca tvad anyaṃ paśyāmi yo na āpatsu tārayet
a tvāṃ hi mādhava saṃśritya nirbhayā mohadarpitam
c dhārtarāṣṭraṃ sahāmātyaṃ svam aṃśam anuyuñjmahe
a yathā hi sarvāsv āpatsu pāsi vṛṣṇīn ariṃdama
c tathā te pāṇḍavā rakṣyāḥ pāhy asmān mahato bhayāt
 bhagavān uvāca
a ayam asmi mahābāho brūhi yat te vivakṣitam
c kariṣyāmi hi tat sarvaṃ yat tvaṃ vakṣyasi bhārata
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
 mṛdupūrvaṃ sāmamiśraṃ sāntvam ugraṃ ca mādhava
 na tu tan nyāyam āsthāya garhitāś ca tato vayam
a śrutaṃ te dhṛtarāṣṭrasya saputrasya cikīrṣitam
c etad dhi sakalaṃ kṛṣṇa saṃjayo māṃ yad abravīt
a tan mataṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrasya so 'syātmā vivṛtāntaraḥ
c yathoktaṃ dūta ācaṣṭe vadhyaḥ syād anyathā bruvan
a apradānena rājyasya śāntim asmāsu mārgati
c lubdhaḥ pāpena manasā carann asamam ātmanaḥ
a yat tad dvādaśa varṣāṇi vane nirvyuṣitā vayam
c chadmanā śaradaṃ caikāṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrasya śāsanāt
a sthātā naḥ samaye tasmin dhṛtarāṣṭra iti prabho
c nāhāsma samayaṃ kṛṣṇa tad dhi no brāhmaṇā viduḥ
a vṛddho rājā dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ svadharmaṃ nānupaśyati
c paśyan vā putragṛddhitvān mandasyānveti śāsanam
a suyodhanamate tiṣṭhan rājāsmāsu janārdana
c mithyā carati lubdhaḥ saṃś caran priyam ivātmanaḥ
a ito duḥkhataraṃ kiṃ nu yatrāhaṃ mātaraṃ tataḥ
c saṃvidhātuṃ na śaknomi mitrāṇāṃ vā janārdana
a kāśibhiś cedipāñcālair matsyaiś ca madhusūdana
c bhavatā caiva nāthena pañca grāmā vṛtā mayā
a kuśasthalaṃ vṛkasthalam āsandī vāraṇāvatam
c avasānaṃ ca govinda kiṃ cid evātra pañcamam
a pañca nas tāta dīyantāṃ grāmā vā nagarāṇi vā
c vasema sahitā yeṣu mā ca no bharatā naśan
a na ca tān api duṣṭātmā dhārtarāṣṭro 'numanyate
c svāmyam ātmani matvāsāv ato duḥkhataraṃ nu kim
a kule jātasya vṛddhasya paravitteṣu gṛdhyataḥ
c lobhaḥ prajñānam āhanti prajñā hanti hatā hriyam
a hrīr hatā bādhate dharmaṃ dharmo hanti hataḥ śriyam
c śrīr hatā puruṣaṃ hanti puruṣasyāsvatā vadhaḥ
a asvato hi nivartante jñātayaḥ suhṛdartvijaḥ
c apuṣpād aphalād vṛkṣād yathā tāta patatriṇaḥ
a etac ca maraṇaṃ tāta yad asmāt patitād iva
c jñātayo vinivartante pretasattvād ivāsavaḥ
a nātaḥ pāpīyasīṃ kāṃ cid avasthāṃ śambaro 'bravīt
c yatra naivādya na prātar bhojanaṃ pratidṛśyate
a dhanam āhuḥ paraṃ dharmaṃ dhane sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam
c jīvanti dhanino loke mṛtā ye tv adhanā narāḥ
a ye dhanād apakarṣanti naraṃ svabalam āśritāḥ
c te dharmam arthaṃ kāmaṃ ca pramathnanti naraṃ ca tam
a etām avasthāṃ prāpyaike maraṇaṃ vavrire janāḥ
c grāmāyaike vanāyaike nāśāyaike pravavrajuḥ
a unmādam eke puṣyanti yānty anye dviṣatāṃ vaśam
c dāsyam eke nigacchanti pareṣām arthahetunā
a āpad evāsya maraṇāt puruṣasya garīyasī
c śriyo vināśas tad dhy asya nimittaṃ dharmakāmayoḥ
a yad asya dharmyaṃ maraṇaṃ śāśvataṃ lokavartma tat
c samantāt sarvabhūtānāṃ na tad atyeti kaś cana
a na tathā bādhyate kṛṣṇa prakṛtyā nirdhano janaḥ
c yathā bhadrāṃ śriyaṃ prāpya tayā hīnaḥ sukhaidhitaḥ
a sa tadātmāparādhena saṃprāpto vyasanaṃ mahat
c sendrān garhayate devān nātmānaṃ ca kathaṃ cana
a na cāsmin sarvaśāstrāṇi prataranti nigarhaṇām
c so 'bhikrudhyati bhṛtyānāṃ suhṛdaś cābhyasūyati
a taṃ tadā manyur evaiti sa bhūyaḥ saṃpramuhyati
c sa mohavaśam āpannaḥ krūraṃ karma niṣevate
a pāpakarmātyayāyaiva saṃkaraṃ tena puṣyati
c saṃkaro narakāyaiva sā kāṣṭhā pāpakarmaṇām
a na cet prabudhyate kṛṣṇa narakāyaiva gacchati
c tasya prabodhaḥ prajñaiva prajñācakṣur na riṣyati
a prajñālābhe hi puruṣaḥ śāstrāṇy evānvavekṣate
c śāstranityaḥ punar dharmaṃ tasya hrīr aṅgam uttamam
a hrīmān hi pāpaṃ pradveṣṭi tasya śrīr abhivardhate
c śrīmān sa yāvad bhavati tāvad bhavati pūruṣaḥ
a dharmanityaḥ praśāntātmā kāryayogavahaḥ sadā
c nādharme kurute buddhiṃ na ca pāpeṣu vartate
a ahrīko vā vimūḍho vā naiva strī na punaḥ pumān
c nāsyādhikāro dharme 'sti yathā śūdras tathaiva saḥ
a hrīmān avati devāṃś ca pitṝn ātmānam eva ca
c tenāmṛtatvaṃ vrajati sā kāṣṭhā puṇyakarmaṇām
a tad idaṃ mayi te dṛṣṭaṃ pratyakṣaṃ madhusūdana
c yathā rājyāt paribhraṣṭo vasāmi vasatīr imāḥ
a te vayaṃ na śriyaṃ hātum alaṃ nyāyena kena cit
c atra no yatamānānāṃ vadhaś ced api sādhu tat
a tatra naḥ prathamaḥ kalpo yad vayaṃ te ca mādhava
c praśāntāḥ samabhūtāś ca śriyaṃ tān aśnuvīmahi
a tatraiṣā paramā kāṣṭhā raudrakarmakṣayodayā
c yad vayaṃ kauravān hatvā tāni rāṣṭrāṇy aśīmahi
a ye punaḥ syur asaṃbaddhā anāryāḥ kṛṣṇa śatravaḥ
c teṣām apy avadhaḥ kāryaḥ kiṃ punar ye syur īdṛśāḥ
a jñātayaś ca hi bhūyiṣṭhāḥ sahāyā guravaś ca naḥ
c teṣāṃ vadho 'tipāpīyān kiṃ nu yuddhe 'sti śobhanam
a pāpaḥ kṣatriyadharmo 'yaṃ vayaṃ ca kṣatrabāndhavāḥ
c sa naḥ svadharmo 'dharmo vā vṛttir anyā vigarhitā
a śūdraḥ karoti śuśrūṣāṃ vaiśyā vipaṇijīvinaḥ
c vayaṃ vadhena jīvāmaḥ kapālaṃ brāhmaṇair vṛtam
a kṣatriyaḥ kṣatriyaṃ hanti matsyo matsyena jīvati
c śvā śvānaṃ hanti dāśārha paśya dharmo yathāgataḥ
a yuddhe kṛṣṇa kalir nityaṃ prāṇāḥ sīdanti saṃyuge
c balaṃ tu nītimātrāya haṭhe jayaparājayau
a nātmacchandena bhūtānāṃ jīvitaṃ maraṇaṃ tathā
c nāpy akāle sukhaṃ prāpyaṃ duḥkhaṃ vāpi yadūttama
a eko hy api bahūn hanti ghnanty ekaṃ bahavo 'py uta
c śūraṃ kāpuruṣo hanti ayaśasvī yaśasvinam
a jayaś caivobhayor dṛṣṭa ubhayoś ca parājayaḥ
c tathaivāpacayo dṛṣṭo vyapayāne kṣayavyayau
a sarvathā vṛjinaṃ yuddhaṃ ko ghnan na pratihanyate
c hatasya ca hṛṣīkeśa samau jayaparājayau
a parājayaś ca maraṇān manye naiva viśiṣyate
c yasya syād vijayaḥ kṛṣṇa tasyāpy apacayo dhruvam
a antato dayitaṃ ghnanti ke cid apy apare janāḥ
c tasyāṅga balahīnasya putrān bhrātṝn apaśyataḥ
e nirvedo jīvite kṛṣṇa sarvataś copajāyate
a ye hy eva vīrā hrīmanta āryāḥ karuṇavedinaḥ
c ta eva yuddhe hanyante yavīyān mucyate janaḥ
a hatvāpy anuśayo nityaṃ parān api janārdana
c anubandhaś ca pāpo 'tra śeṣaś cāpy avaśiṣyate
a śeṣo hi balam āsādya na śeṣam avaśeṣayet
c sarvocchede ca yatate vairasyāntavidhitsayā
a jayo vairaṃ prasṛjati duḥkham āste parājitaḥ
c sukhaṃ praśāntaḥ svapiti hitvā jayaparājayau
a jātavairaś ca puruṣo duḥkhaṃ svapiti nityadā
c anirvṛtena manasā sasarpa iva veśmani
a utsādayati yaḥ sarvaṃ yaśasā sa viyujyate
c akīrtiṃ sarvabhūteṣu śāśvatīṃ sa niyacchati
a na hi vairāṇi śāmyanti dīrghakālakṛtāny api
c ākhyātāraś ca vidyante pumāṃś cotpadyate kule
a na cāpi vairaṃ vaireṇa keśava vyupaśāmyati
c haviṣāgnir yathā kṛṣṇa bhūya evābhivardhate
a ato 'nyathā nāsti śāntir nityam antaram antataḥ
c antaraṃ lipsamānānām ayaṃ doṣo nirantaraḥ
a pauruṣeyo hi balavān ādhir hṛdayabādhanaḥ
c tasya tyāgena vā śāntir nivṛttyā manaso 'pi vā
a atha vā mūlaghātena dviṣatāṃ madhusūdana
c phalanirvṛttir iddhā syāt tan nṛśaṃsataraṃ bhavet
a yā tu tyāgena śāntiḥ syāt tad ṛte vadha eva saḥ
c saṃśayāc ca samucchedād dviṣatām ātmanas tathā
a na ca tyaktuṃ tad icchāmo na cecchāmaḥ kulakṣayam
c atra yā praṇipātena śāntiḥ saiva garīyasī
a sarvathā yatamānānām ayuddham abhikāṅkṣatām
c sāntve pratihate yuddhaṃ prasiddham aparākramam
a pratighātena sāntvasya dāruṇaṃ saṃpravartate
c tac chunām iva gopāde paṇḍitair upalakṣitam
a lāṅgūlacālanaṃ kṣveḍaḥ pratirāvo vivartanam
c dantadarśanam ārāvas tato yuddhaṃ pravartate
a tatra yo balavān kṛṣṇa jitvā so 'tti tad āmiṣam
c evam eva manuṣyeṣu viśeṣo nāsti kaś cana
a sarvathā tv etad ucitaṃ durbaleṣu balīyasām
c anādaro virodhaś ca praṇipātī hi durbalaḥ
a pitā rājā ca vṛddhaś ca sarvathā mānam arhati
c tasmān mānyaś ca pūjyaś ca dhṛtarāṣṭro janārdana
a putrasnehas tu balavān dhṛtarāṣṭrasya mādhava
c sa putravaśam āpannaḥ praṇipātaṃ prahāsyati
a tatra kiṃ manyase kṛṣṇa prāptakālam anantaram
c katham arthāc ca dharmāc ca na hīyemahi mādhava
a īdṛśe hy arthakṛcchre 'smin kam anyaṃ madhusūdana
c upasaṃpraṣṭum arhāmi tvām ṛte puruṣottama
a priyaś ca priyakāmaś ca gatijñaḥ sarvakarmaṇām
c ko hi kṛṣṇāsti nas tvādṛk sarvaniścayavit suhṛt
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a evam uktaḥ pratyuvāca dharmarājaṃ janārdanaḥ
c ubhayor eva vām arthe yāsyāmi kurusaṃsadam
a śamaṃ tatra labheyaṃ ced yuṣmadartham ahāpayan
c puṇyaṃ me sumahad rājaṃś caritaṃ syān mahāphalam
a mocayeyaṃ mṛtyupāśāt saṃrabdhān kurusṛñjayān
c pāṇḍavān dhārtarāṣṭrāṃś ca sarvāṃ ca pṛthivīm imām
d evam uktaḥ pratyuvāca dharmarājo janārdanam
d bhrātṝṇāṃ samavetānāṃ sa kāle puruṣottamam
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a na mamaitan mataṃ kṛṣṇa yat tvaṃ yāyāḥ kurūn prati
c suyodhanaḥ sūktam api na kariṣyati te vacaḥ
d suyodhanaś ca duṣṭātmā karṇaś ca sahasaubalaḥ
a sametaṃ pārthivaṃ kṣatraṃ suyodhanavaśānugam
c teṣāṃ madhyāvataraṇaṃ tava kṛṣṇa na rocaye
a na hi naḥ prīṇayed dravyaṃ na devatvaṃ kutaḥ sukham
c na ca sarvāmaraiśvaryaṃ tava rodhena mādhava
 bhagavān uvāca
a jānāmy etāṃ mahārāja dhārtarāṣṭrasya pāpatām
c avācyās tu bhaviṣyāmaḥ sarvaloke mahīkṣitām
a na cāpi mama paryāptāḥ sahitāḥ sarvapārthivāḥ
c kruddhasya pramukhe sthātuṃ siṃhasyevetare mṛgāḥ
a atha cet te pravarteran mayi kiṃ cid asāṃpratam
c nirdaheyaṃ kurūn sarvān iti me dhīyate matiḥ
a na jātu gamanaṃ tatra bhavet pārtha nirarthakam
c arthaprāptiḥ kadā cit syād antato vāpy avācyatā
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a yat tubhyaṃ rocate kṛṣṇa svasti prāpnuhi kauravān
c kṛtārthaṃ svastimantaṃ tvāṃ drakṣyāmi punarāgatam
a viṣvaksena kurūn gatvā bhāratāñ śamayeḥ prabho
c yathā sarve sumanasaḥ saha syāmaḥ sucetasaḥ
a bhrātā cāsi sakhā cāsi bībhatsor mama ca priyaḥ
c sauhṛdenāviśaṅkyo 'si svasti prāpnuhi bhūtaye
a asmān vettha parān vettha vetthārthaṃ vettha bhāṣitam
c yad yad asmaddhitaṃ kṛṣṇa tat tad vācyaḥ suyodhanaḥ
a yad yad dharmeṇa saṃyuktam upapadyed dhitaṃ vacaḥ
c tat tat keśava bhāṣethāḥ sāntvaṃ vā yadi vetarat
 bhagavān uvāca
a saṃjayasya śrutaṃ vākyaṃ bhavataś ca śrutaṃ mayā
c sarvaṃ jānāmy abhiprāyaṃ teṣāṃ ca bhavataś ca yaḥ
a tava dharmāśritā buddhis teṣāṃ vairāśritā matiḥ
c yad ayuddhena labhyeta tat te bahumataṃ bhavet
a na ca tan naiṣṭhikaṃ karma kṣatriyasya viśāṃ pate
c āhur āśramiṇaḥ sarve yad bhaikṣaṃ kṣatriyaś caret
a jayo vadho vā saṃgrāme dhātrā diṣṭaḥ sanātanaḥ
c svadharmaḥ kṣatriyasyaiṣa kārpaṇyaṃ na praśasyate
a na hi kārpaṇyam āsthāya śakyā vṛttir yudhiṣṭhira
c vikramasva mahābāho jahi śatrūn ariṃdama
a atigṛddhāḥ kṛtasnehā dīrghakālaṃ sahoṣitāḥ
c kṛtamitrāḥ kṛtabalā dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ paraṃtapa
a na paryāyo 'sti yat sāmyaṃ tvayi kuryur viśāṃ pate
c balavattāṃ hi manyante bhīṣmadroṇakṛpādibhiḥ
a yāvac ca mārdavenaitān rājann upacariṣyasi
c tāvad ete hariṣyanti tava rājyam ariṃdama
a nānukrośān na kārpaṇyān na ca dharmārthakāraṇāt
c alaṃ kartuṃ dhārtarāṣṭrās tava kāmam ariṃdama
a etad eva nimittaṃ te pāṇḍavās tu yathā tvayi
c nānvatapyanta kaupīnaṃ tāvat kṛtvāpi duṣkaram
a pitāmahasya droṇasya vidurasya ca dhīmataḥ
b brāhmaṇānāṃ ca sādhūnāṃ rājñaś ca nagarasya ca
c paśyatāṃ kurumukhyānāṃ sarveṣām eva tattvataḥ
a dānaśīlaṃ mṛduṃ dāntaṃ dharmakāmam anuvratam
c yat tvām upadhinā rājan dyūtenāvañcayat tadā
e na cāpatrapate pāpo nṛśaṃsas tena karmaṇā
a tathāśīlasamācāre rājan mā praṇayaṃ kṛthāḥ
c vadhyās te sarvalokasya kiṃ punas tava bhārata
a vāgbhis tv apratirūpābhir atudat sakanīyasam
c ślāghamānaḥ prahṛṣṭaḥ san bhāṣate bhrātṛbhiḥ saha
a etāvat pāṇḍavānāṃ hi nāsti kiṃ cid iha svakam
c nāmadheyaṃ ca gotraṃ ca tad apy eṣāṃ na śiṣyate
a kālena mahatā caiṣāṃ bhaviṣyati parābhavaḥ
c prakṛtiṃ te bhajiṣyanti naṣṭaprakṛtayo janāḥ
d duḥśāsanena pāpena tadā dyūte pravartite
d anāthavat tadā devī draupadī sudurātmanā
d ākṛṣya keśe rudatī sabhāyāṃ rājasaṃsadi
d bhīṣmadroṇapramukhato gaur iti vyāhṛtā muhuḥ
d bhavatā vāritāḥ sarve bhrātaro bhīmavikramāḥ
d dharmapāśanibaddhāś ca na kiṃ cit pratipedire
a etāś cānyāś ca paruṣā vācaḥ sa samudīrayan
c ślāghate jñātimadhye sma tvayi pravrajite vanam
a ye tatrāsan samānītās te dṛṣṭvā tvām anāgasam
c aśrukaṇṭhā rudantaś ca sabhāyām āsate tadā
a na cainam abhyanandaṃs te rājāno brāhmaṇaiḥ saha
c sarve duryodhanaṃ tatra nindanti sma sabhāsadaḥ
a kulīnasya ca yā nindā vadhaś cāmitrakarśana
c mahāguṇo vadho rājan na tu nindā kujīvikā
a tadaiva nihato rājan yadaiva nirapatrapaḥ
c ninditaś ca mahārāja pṛthivyāṃ sarvarājasu
a īṣatkāryo vadhas tasya yasya cāritram īdṛśam
c praskambhanapratistabdhaś chinnamūla iva drumaḥ
a vadhyaḥ sarpa ivānāryaḥ sarvalokasya durmatiḥ
c jahy enaṃ tvam amitraghna mā rājan vicikitsithāḥ
a sarvathā tvatkṣamaṃ caitad rocate ca mamānagha
c yat tvaṃ pitari bhīṣme ca praṇipātaṃ samācareḥ
a ahaṃ tu sarvalokasya gatvā chetsyāmi saṃśayam
c yeṣām asti dvidhābhāvo rājan duryodhanaṃ prati
a madhye rājñām ahaṃ tatra prātipauruṣikān guṇān
c tava saṃkīrtayiṣyāmi ye ca tasya vyatikramāḥ
a bruvatas tatra me vākyaṃ dharmārthasahitaṃ hitam
c niśamya pārthivāḥ sarve nānājanapadeśvarāḥ
a tvayi saṃpratipatsyante dharmātmā satyavāg iti
c tasmiṃś cādhigamiṣyanti yathā lobhād avartata
a garhayiṣyāmi caivainaṃ paurajānapadeṣv api
c vṛddhabālān upādāya cāturvarṇyasamāgame
a śamaṃ ced yācamānas tvaṃ na dharmaṃ tatra lapsyase
c kurūn vigarhayiṣyanti dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ ca pārthivāḥ
a tasmiṃl lokaparityakte kiṃ kāryam avaśiṣyate
c hate duryodhane rājan yad anyat kriyatām iti
a yātvā cāhaṃ kurūn sarvān yuṣmadartham ahāpayan
c yatiṣye praśamaṃ kartuṃ lakṣayiṣye ca ceṣṭitam
a kauravāṇāṃ pravṛttiṃ ca gatvā yuddhādhikārikām
c niśāmya vinivartiṣye jayāya tava bhārata
a sarvathā yuddham evāham āśaṃsāmi paraiḥ saha
c nimittāni hi sarvāṇi tathā prādurbhavanti me
a mṛgāḥ śakuntāś ca vadanti ghoraṃ
hastyaśvamukhyeṣu niśāmukheṣu
c ghorāṇi rūpāṇi tathaiva cāgnir
varṇān bahūn puṣyati ghorarūpān
e manuṣyalokakṣapaṇo 'tha ghoro
no ced anuprāpta ihāntakaḥ syāt
a śastrāṇi patraṃ kavacān rathāṃś ca
nāgān dhvajāṃś ca pratipādayitvā
c yodhāś ca sarve kṛtaniśramās te
bhavantu hastyaśvaratheṣu yattāḥ
e sāṃgrāmikaṃ te yad upārjanīyaṃ
sarvaṃ samagraṃ kuru tan narendra
a duryodhano na hy alam adya dātuṃ
jīvaṃs tavaitan nṛpate kathaṃ cit
c yat te purastād abhavat samṛddhaṃ
dyūte hṛtaṃ pāṇḍavamukhya rājyam
 bhīmasena uvāca
a yathā yathaiva śāntiḥ syāt kurūṇāṃ madhusūdana
c tathā tathaiva bhāṣethā mā sma yuddhena bhīṣayeḥ
a amarṣī nityasaṃrabdhaḥ śreyodveṣī mahāmanāḥ
c nograṃ duryodhano vācyaḥ sāmnaivainaṃ samācareḥ
a prakṛtyā pāpasattvaś ca tulyacetāś ca dasyubhiḥ
c aiśvaryamadamattaś ca kṛtavairaś ca pāṇḍavaiḥ
a adīrghadarśī niṣṭhūrī kṣeptā krūraparākramaḥ
c dīrghamanyur aneyaś ca pāpātmā nikṛtipriyaḥ
a mriyetāpi na bhajyeta naiva jahyāt svakaṃ matam
c tādṛśena śamaṃ kṛṣṇa manye paramaduṣkaram
a suhṛdām apy avācīnas tyaktadharmaḥ priyānṛtaḥ
c pratihanty eva suhṛdāṃ vācaś caiva manāṃsi ca
a sa manyuvaśam āpannaḥ svabhāvaṃ duṣṭam āsthitaḥ
c svabhāvāt pāpam anveti tṛṇais tunna ivoragaḥ
a duryodhano hi yat senaḥ sarvathā viditas tava
c yacchīlo yatsvabhāvaś ca yadbalo yatparākramaḥ
a purā prasannāḥ kuravaḥ sahaputrās tathā vayam
c indrajyeṣṭhā ivābhūma modamānāḥ sabāndhavāḥ
a duryodhanasya krodhena bhāratā madhusūdana
c dhakṣyante śiśirāpāye vanānīva hutāśanaiḥ
a aṣṭādaśeme rājānaḥ prakhyātā madhusūdana
c ye samuccicchidur jñātīn suhṛdaś ca sabāndhavān
a asurāṇāṃ samṛddhānāṃ jvalatām iva tejasā
c paryāyakāle dharmasya prāpte balir ajāyata
a haihayānām udāvarto nīpānāṃ janamejayaḥ
c bahulas tālajaṅghānāṃ kṛmīṇām uddhato vasuḥ
a ajabinduḥ suvīrāṇāṃ surāṣṭrāṇāṃ kuśarddhikaḥ
c arkajaś ca balīhānāṃ cīnānāṃ dhautamūlakaḥ
a hayagrīvo videhānāṃ varapraś ca mahaujasām
c bāhuḥ sundaravegānāṃ dīptākṣāṇāṃ purūravāḥ
a sahajaś cedimatsyānāṃ pracetānāṃ bṛhadbalaḥ
c dhāraṇaś cendravatsānāṃ mukuṭānāṃ vigāhanaḥ
a śamaś ca nandivegānām ity ete kulapāṃsanāḥ
c yugānte kṛṣṇa saṃbhūtāḥ kuleṣu puruṣādhamāḥ
a apy ayaṃ naḥ kurūṇāṃ syād yugānte kālasaṃbhṛtaḥ
c duryodhanaḥ kulāṅgāro jaghanyaḥ pāpapūruṣaḥ
a tasmān mṛdu śanair enaṃ brūyā dharmārthasaṃhitam
c kāmānubandhabahulaṃ nogram ugraparākramam
a api duryodhanaṃ kṛṣṇa sarve vayam adhaścarāḥ
c nīcair bhūtvānuyāsyāmo mā sma no bharatā naśan
a apy udāsīnavṛttiḥ syād yathā naḥ kurubhiḥ saha
c vāsudeva tathā kāryaṃ na kurūn anayaḥ spṛśet
a vācyaḥ pitāmaho vṛddho ye ca kṛṣṇa sabhāsadaḥ
c bhrātṝṇām astu saubhrātraṃ dhārtarāṣṭraḥ praśāmyatām
a aham etad bravīmy evaṃ rājā caiva praśaṃsati
c arjuno naiva yuddhārthī bhūyasī hi dayārjune
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a etac chrutvā mahābāhuḥ keśavaḥ prahasann iva
c abhūtapūrvaṃ bhīmasya mārdavopagataṃ vacaḥ
a girer iva laghutvaṃ tac chītatvam iva pāvake
c matvā rāmānujaḥ śauriḥ śārṅgadhanvā vṛkodaram
a saṃtejayaṃs tadā vāgbhir mātariśveva pāvakam
c uvāca bhīmam āsīnaṃ kṛpayābhipariplutam
a tvam anyadā bhīmasena yuddham eva praśaṃsasi
c vadhābhinandinaḥ krūrān dhārtarāṣṭrān mimardiṣuḥ
a na ca svapiṣi jāgarṣi nyubjaḥ śeṣe paraṃtapa
c ghorām aśāntāṃ ruśatīṃ sadā vācaṃ prabhāṣase
a niḥśvasann agnivarṇena saṃtaptaḥ svena manyunā
c apraśāntamanā bhīma sadhūma iva pāvakaḥ
a ekānte niṣṭanañ śeṣe bhārārta iva durbalaḥ
c api tvāṃ ke cid unmattaṃ manyante 'tadvido janāḥ
a ārujya vṛkṣān nirmūlān gajaḥ paribhujann iva
c nighnan padbhiḥ kṣitiṃ bhīma niṣṭanan paridhāvasi
a nāsmiñ jane 'bhiramase rahaḥ kṣiyasi pāṇḍava
c nānyaṃ niśi divā vāpi kadā cid abhinandasi
a akasmāt smayamānaś ca rahasy āsse rudann iva
c jānvor mūrdhānam ādhāya ciram āsse pramīlitaḥ
a bhrukuṭiṃ ca punaḥ kurvann oṣṭhau ca vilihann iva
c abhīkṣṇaṃ dṛśyase bhīma sarvaṃ tan manyukāritam
a yathā purastāt savitā dṛśyate śukram uccaran
c yathā ca paścān nirmukto dhruvaṃ paryeti raśmivān
a tathā satyaṃ bravīmy etan nāsti tasya vyatikramaḥ
c hantāhaṃ gadayābhyetya duryodhanam amarṣaṇam
a iti sma madhye bhrātṝṇāṃ satyenālabhase gadām
c tasya te praśame buddhir dhīyate 'dya paraṃtapa
a aho yuddhapratīpāni yuddhakāla upasthite
c paśyasīvāpratīpāni kiṃ tvāṃ bhīr bhīma vindati
a aho pārtha nimittāni viparītāni paśyasi
c svapnānte jāgarānte ca tasmāt praśamam icchasi
a aho nāśaṃsase kiṃ cit puṃstvaṃ klība ivātmani
c kaśmalenābhipanno 'si tena te vikṛtaṃ manaḥ
a udvepate te hṛdayaṃ manas te praviṣīdati
c ūrustambhagṛhīto 'si tasmāt praśamam icchasi
a anityaṃ kila martyasya cittaṃ pārtha calācalam
c vātavegapracalitā aṣṭhīlā śālmaler iva
a tavaiṣā vikṛtā buddhir gavāṃ vāg iva mānuṣī
c manāṃsi pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ majjayaty aplavān iva
a idaṃ me mahad āścaryaṃ parvatasyeva sarpaṇam
c yadīdṛśaṃ prabhāṣethā bhīmasenāsamaṃ vacaḥ
a sa dṛṣṭvā svāni karmāṇi kule janma ca bhārata
c uttiṣṭhasva viṣādaṃ mā kṛthā vīra sthiro bhava
a na caitad anurūpaṃ te yat te glānir ariṃdama
c yad ojasā na labhate kṣatriyo na tad aśnute
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tathokto vāsudevena nityamanyur amarṣaṇaḥ
c sadaśvavat samādhāvad babhāṣe tadanantaram
a anyathā māṃ cikīrṣantam anyathā manyase 'cyuta
c praṇītabhāvam atyantaṃ yudhi satyaparākramam
a vettha dāśārha sattvaṃ me dīrghakālaṃ sahoṣitaḥ
c uta vā māṃ na jānāsi plavan hrada ivālpavaḥ
e tasmād apratirūpābhir vāgbhir māṃ tvaṃ samarchasi
a kathaṃ hi bhīmasenaṃ māṃ jānan kaś cana mādhava
c brūyād apratirūpāṇi yathā māṃ vaktum arhasi
a tasmād idaṃ pravakṣyāmi vacanaṃ vṛṣṇinandana
c ātmanaḥ pauruṣaṃ caiva balaṃ ca na samaṃ paraiḥ
a sarvathā nāryakarmaitat praśaṃsā svayam ātmanaḥ
c ativādāpaviddhas tu vakṣyāmi balam ātmanaḥ
a paśyeme rodasī kṛṣṇa yayor āsann imāḥ prajāḥ
c acale cāpy anante ca pratiṣṭhe sarvamātarau
a yadīme sahasā kruddhe sameyātāṃ śile iva
c aham ete nigṛhṇīyāṃ bāhubhyāṃ sacarācare
a paśyaitad antaraṃ bāhvor mahāparighayor iva
c ya etat prāpya mucyeta na taṃ paśyāmi pūruṣam
a himavāṃś ca samudraś ca vajrī ca balabhit svayam
c mayābhipannaṃ trāyeran balam āsthāya na trayaḥ
a yudhyeyaṃ kṣatriyān sarvān pāṇḍaveṣv ātatāyinaḥ
c adhaḥ pādatalenaitān adhiṣṭhāsyāmi bhūtale
a na hi tvaṃ nābhijānāsi mama vikramam acyuta
c yathā mayā vinirjitya rājāno vaśagāḥ kṛtāḥ
a atha cen māṃ na jānāsi sūryasyevodyataḥ prabhām
c vigāḍhe yudhi saṃbādhe vetsyase māṃ janārdana
a kiṃ mātyavākṣīḥ paruṣair vraṇaṃ sūcyā ivānagha
c yathāmati bravīmy etad viddhi mām adhikaṃ tataḥ
a draṣṭāsi yudhi saṃbādhe pravṛtte vaiśase 'hani
c mayā praṇunnān mātaṅgān rathinaḥ sādinas tathā
a tathā narān abhikruddhaṃ nighnantaṃ kṣatriyarṣabhān
c draṣṭā māṃ tvaṃ ca lokaś ca vikarṣantaṃ varān varān
a na me sīdanti majjāno na mamodvepate manaḥ
c sarvalokād abhikruddhān na bhayaṃ vidyate mama
a kiṃ tu sauhṛdam evaitat kṛpayā madhusūdana
c sarvāṃs titikṣe saṃkleśān mā sma no bharatā naśan
 bhagavān uvāca
a bhāvaṃ jijñāsamāno 'haṃ praṇayād idam abruvam
c na cākṣepān na pāṇḍityān na krodhān na vivakṣayā
a vedāhaṃ tava māhātmyam uta te veda yad balam
c uta te veda karmāṇi na tvāṃ paribhavāmy aham
a yathā cātmani kalyāṇaṃ saṃbhāvayasi pāṇḍava
c sahasraguṇam apy etat tvayi saṃbhāvayāmy aham
a yādṛśe ca kule janma sarvarājābhipūjite
c bandhubhiś ca suhṛdbhiś ca bhīma tvam asi tādṛśaḥ
a jijñāsanto hi dharmasya saṃdigdhasya vṛkodara
c paryāyaṃ na vyavasyanti daivamānuṣayor janāḥ
a sa eva hetur bhūtvā hi puruṣasyārthasiddhiṣu
c vināśe 'pi sa evāsya saṃdigdhaṃ karma pauruṣam
a anyathā paridṛṣṭāni kavibhir doṣadarśibhiḥ
c anyathā parivartante vegā iva nabhasvataḥ
a sumantritaṃ sunītaṃ ca nyāyataś copapāditam
c kṛtaṃ mānuṣyakaṃ karma daivenāpi virudhyate
a daivam apy akṛtaṃ karma pauruṣeṇa vihanyate
c śītam uṣṇaṃ tathā varṣaṃ kṣutpipāse ca bhārata
a yad anyad diṣṭabhāvasya puruṣasya svayaṃkṛtam
c tasmād anavarodhaś ca vidyate tatra lakṣaṇam
a lokasya nānyato vṛttiḥ pāṇḍavānyatra karmaṇaḥ
b bāhuśālin mahāvīrya bhīmasena vicakṣaṇa
b   mātrā syād avadhāraṇe
c evaṃbuddhiḥ pravarteta phalaṃ syād ubhayānvayāt
a ya evaṃ kṛtabuddhiḥ san karmasv eva pravartate
c nāsiddhau vyathate tasya na siddhau harṣam aśnute
a tatreyam arthamātrā me bhīmasena vivakṣitā
c naikāntasiddhir mantavyā kurubhiḥ saha saṃyuge
a nātipraṇītaraśmiḥ syāt tathā bhavati paryaye
c viṣādam arched glāniṃ vā etadarthaṃ bravīmi te
a śvobhūte dhṛtarāṣṭrasya samīpaṃ prāpya pāṇḍava
c yatiṣye praśamaṃ kartuṃ yuṣmadartham ahāpayan
a śamaṃ cet te kariṣyanti tato 'nantaṃ yaśo mama
c bhavatāṃ ca kṛtaḥ kāmas teṣāṃ ca śreya uttamam
a te ced abhinivekṣyanti nābhyupaiṣyanti me vacaḥ
c kuravo yuddham evātra raudraṃ karma bhaviṣyati
a asmin yuddhe bhīmasena tvayi bhāraḥ samāhitaḥ
c dhūr arjunena dhāryā syād voḍhavya itaro janaḥ
a ahaṃ hi yantā bībhatsor bhavitā saṃyuge sati
c dhanaṃjayasyaiṣa kāmo na hi yuddhaṃ na kāmaye
a tasmād āśaṅkamāno 'haṃ vṛkodara matiṃ tava
c tudann aklībayā vācā tejas te samadīpayam
 arjuna uvāca
a uktaṃ yudhiṣṭhireṇaiva yāvad vācyaṃ janārdana
c tava vākyaṃ tu me śrutvā pratibhāti paraṃtapa
a naiva praśamam atra tvaṃ manyase sukaraṃ prabho
c lobhād vā dhṛtarāṣṭrasya dainyād vā samupasthitāt
a aphalaṃ manyase cāpi puruṣasya parākramam
c na cāntareṇa karmāṇi pauruṣeṇa phalodayaḥ
a tad idaṃ bhāṣitaṃ vākyaṃ tathā ca na tathaiva ca
c na caitad evaṃ draṣṭavyam asādhyam iti kiṃ cana
a kiṃ caitan manyase kṛcchram asmākaṃ pāpam āditaḥ
c kurvanti teṣāṃ karmāṇi yeṣāṃ nāsti phalodayaḥ
a saṃpādyamānaṃ samyak ca syāt karma saphalaṃ prabho
c sa tathā kṛṣṇa vartasva yathā śarma bhavet paraiḥ
a pāṇḍavānāṃ kurūṇāṃ ca bhavān paramakaḥ suhṛt
c surāṇām asurāṇāṃ ca yathā vīra prajāpatiḥ
a kurūṇāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ ca pratipatsva nirāmayam
c asmaddhitam anuṣṭhātuṃ na manye tava duṣkaram
a evaṃ cet kāryatām eti kāryaṃ tava janārdana
c gamanād evam eva tvaṃ kariṣyasi na saṃśayaḥ
a cikīrṣitam athānyat te tasmin vīra durātmani
c bhaviṣyati tathā sarvaṃ yathā tava cikīrṣitam
a śarma taiḥ saha vā no 'stu tava vā yac cikīrṣitam
c vicāryamāṇo yaḥ kāmas tava kṛṣṇa sa no guruḥ
a na sa nārhati duṣṭātmā vadhaṃ sasutabāndhavaḥ
c yena dharmasute dṛṣṭvā na sā śrīr upamarṣitā
a yac cāpy apaśyatopāyaṃ dharmiṣṭhaṃ madhusūdana
c upāyena nṛśaṃsena hṛtā durdyūtadevinā
a kathaṃ hi puruṣo jātaḥ kṣatriyeṣu dhanurdharaḥ
c samāhūto nivarteta prāṇatyāge 'py upasthite
a adharmeṇa jitān dṛṣṭvā vane pravrajitāṃs tathā
c vadhyatāṃ mama vārṣṇeya nirgato 'sau suyodhanaḥ
a na caitad adbhutaṃ kṛṣṇa mitrārthe yac cikīrṣasi
c kriyā kathaṃ nu mukhyā syān mṛdunā vetareṇa vā
a atha vā manyase jyāyān vadhas teṣām anantaram
c tad eva kriyatām āśu na vicāryam atas tvayā
a jānāsi hi yathā tena draupadī pāpabuddhinā
c parikliṣṭā sabhāmadhye tac ca tasyāpi marṣitam
a sa nāma samyag varteta pāṇḍaveṣv iti mādhava
c na me saṃjāyate buddhir bījam uptam ivoṣare
a tasmād yan manyase yuktaṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ ca yad dhitam
c tad āśu kuru vārṣṇeya yan naḥ kāryam anantaram
 bhagavān uvāca
a evam etan mahābāho yathā vadasi pāṇḍava
b pāṇḍavānāṃ kurūṇāṃ ca pratipatsye nirāmayam
c sarvaṃ tv idaṃ samāyattaṃ bībhatso karmaṇor dvayoḥ
a kṣetraṃ hi rasavac chuddhaṃ karṣakeṇopapāditam
c ṛte varṣaṃ na kaunteya jātu nirvartayet phalam
a tatra vai pauruṣaṃ brūyur āsekaṃ yatnakāritam
c tatra cāpi dhruvaṃ paśyec choṣaṇaṃ daivakāritam
a tad idaṃ niścitaṃ buddhyā pūrvair api mahātmabhiḥ
c daive ca mānuṣe caiva saṃyuktaṃ lokakāraṇam
a ahaṃ hi tat kariṣyāmi paraṃ puruṣakārataḥ
c daivaṃ tu na mayā śakyaṃ karma kartuṃ kathaṃ cana
a sa hi dharmaṃ ca satyaṃ ca tyaktvā carati durmatiḥ
c na hi saṃtapyate tena tathārūpeṇa karmaṇā
a tāṃ cāpi buddhiṃ pāpiṣṭhāṃ vardhayanty asya mantriṇaḥ
c śakuniḥ sūtaputraś ca bhrātā duḥśāsanas tathā
a sa hi tyāgena rājyasya na śamaṃ samupeṣyati
c antareṇa vadhāt pārtha sānubandhaḥ suyodhanaḥ
a na cāpi praṇipātena tyaktum icchati dharmarāṭ
c yācyamānas tu rājyaṃ sa na pradāsyati durmatiḥ
a na tu manye sa tad vācyo yad yudhiṣṭhiraśāsanam
c uktaṃ prayojanaṃ tatra dharmarājena bhārata
a tathā pāpas tu tat sarvaṃ na kariṣyati kauravaḥ
c tasmiṃś cākriyamāṇe 'sau lokavadhyo bhaviṣyati
a mama cāpi sa vadhyo vai jagataś cāpi bhārata
c yena kaumārake yūyaṃ sarve viprakṛtās tathā
a vipraluptaṃ ca vo rājyaṃ nṛśaṃsena durātmanā
c na copaśāmyate pāpaḥ śriyaṃ dṛṣṭvā yudhiṣṭhire
a asakṛc cāpy ahaṃ tena tvatkṛte pārtha bheditaḥ
c na mayā tad gṛhītaṃ ca pāpaṃ tasya cikīrṣitam
a jānāsi hi mahābāho tvam apy asya paraṃ matam
c priyaṃ cikīrṣamāṇaṃ ca dharmarājasya mām api
a sa jānaṃs tasya cātmānaṃ mama caiva paraṃ matam
c ajānann iva cākasmād arjunādyābhiśaṅkase
a yac cāpi paramaṃ divyaṃ tac cāpy avagataṃ tvayā
c vidhānavihitaṃ pārtha kathaṃ śarma bhavet paraiḥ
a yat tu vācā mayā śakyaṃ karmaṇā cāpi pāṇḍava
c kariṣye tad ahaṃ pārtha na tv āśaṃse śamaṃ paraiḥ
a kathaṃ goharaṇe brūyād icchañ śarma tathāvidham
c yācyamāno 'pi bhīṣmeṇa saṃvatsaragate 'dhvani
a tadaiva te parābhūtā yadā saṃkalpitās tvayā
c lavaśaḥ kṣaṇaśaś cāpi na ca tuṣṭaḥ suyodhanaḥ
a sarvathā tu mayā kāryaṃ dharmarājasya śāsanam
c vibhāvyaṃ tasya bhūyaś ca karma pāpaṃ durātmanaḥ
 nakula uvāca
a uktaṃ bahuvidhaṃ vākyaṃ dharmarājena mādhava
c dharmajñena vadānyena dharmayuktaṃ ca tattvataḥ
a matam ājñāya rājñaś ca bhīmasenena mādhava
c saṃśamo bāhuvīryaṃ ca khyāpitaṃ mādhavātmanaḥ
a tathaiva phalgunenāpi yad uktaṃ tat tvayā śrutam
c ātmanaś ca mataṃ vīra kathitaṃ bhavatāsakṛt
a sarvam etad atikramya śrutvā paramataṃ bhavān
c yat prāptakālaṃ manyethās tat kuryāḥ puruṣottama
a tasmiṃs tasmin nimitte hi mataṃ bhavati keśava
c prāptakālaṃ manuṣyeṇa svayaṃ kāryam ariṃdama
a anyathā cintito hy arthaḥ punar bhavati so 'nyathā
c anityamatayo loke narāḥ puruṣasattama
a anyathā buddhayo hy āsann asmāsu vanavāsiṣu
c adṛśyeṣv anyathā kṛṣṇa dṛśyeṣu punar anyathā
a asmākam api vārṣṇeya vane vicaratāṃ tadā
c na tathā praṇayo rājye yathā saṃprati vartate
a nivṛttavanavāsān naḥ śrutvā vīra samāgatāḥ
c akṣauhiṇyo hi saptemās tvatprasādāj janārdana
a imān hi puruṣavyāghrān acintyabalapauruṣān
c āttaśastrān raṇe dṛṣṭvā na vyathed iha kaḥ pumān
a sa bhavān kurumadhye taṃ sāntvapūrvaṃ bhayānvitam
c brūyād vākyaṃ yathā mando na vyatheta suyodhanaḥ
a yudhiṣṭhiraṃ bhīmasenaṃ bībhatsuṃ cāparājitam
c sahadevaṃ ca māṃ caiva tvāṃ ca rāmaṃ ca keśava
a sātyakiṃ ca mahāvīryaṃ virāṭaṃ ca sahātmajam
c drupadaṃ ca sahāmātyaṃ dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ ca pārṣatam
a kāśirājaṃ ca vikrāntaṃ dhṛṣṭaketuṃ ca cedipam
c māṃsaśoṇitabhṛn martyaḥ pratiyudhyeta ko yudhi
a sa bhavān gamanād eva sādhayiṣyaty asaṃśayam
c iṣṭam arthaṃ mahābāho dharmarājasya kevalam
a viduraś caiva bhīṣmaś ca droṇaś ca sahabāhlikaḥ
c śreyaḥ samarthā vijñātum ucyamānaṃ tvayānagha
a te cainam anuneṣyanti dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ janādhipam
c taṃ ca pāpasamācāraṃ sahāmātyaṃ suyodhanam
a śrotā cārthasya viduras tvaṃ ca vaktā janārdana
c kam ivārthaṃ vivartantaṃ sthāpayetāṃ na vartmani
 sahadeva uvāca
a yad etat kathitaṃ rājñā dharma eṣa sanātanaḥ
c yathā tu yuddham eva syāt tathā kāryam ariṃdama
a yadi praśamam iccheyuḥ kuravaḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha
c tathāpi yuddhaṃ dāśārha yojayethāḥ sahaiva taiḥ
a kathaṃ nu dṛṣṭvā pāñcālīṃ tathā kliṣṭāṃ sabhāgatām
c avadhena praśāmyeta mama manyuḥ suyodhane
a yadi bhīmārjunau kṛṣṇa dharmarājaś ca dhārmikaḥ
c dharmam utsṛjya tenāhaṃ yoddhum icchāmi saṃyuge
d brūhi madvacanaṃ kṛṣṇa suyodhanam apaṇḍitam
d kṛcchre vane vā vastavyaṃ pure vā nāgasāhvaye
 sātyakir uvāca
a satyam āha mahābāho sahadevo mahāmatiḥ
c duryodhanavadhe śāntis tasya kopasya me bhavet
a jānāsi hi yathā dṛṣṭvā cīrājinadharān vane
c tavāpi manyur udbhūto duḥkhitān prekṣya pāṇḍavān
a tasmān mādrīsutaḥ śūro yad āha puruṣarṣabhaḥ
c vacanaṃ sarvayodhānāṃ tan mataṃ puruṣottama
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a evaṃ vadati vākyaṃ tu yuyudhāne mahāmatau
c subhīmaḥ siṃhanādo 'bhūd yodhānāṃ tatra sarvaśaḥ
a sarve hi sarvato vīrās tad vacaḥ pratyapūjayan
c sādhu sādhv iti śaineyaṃ harṣayanto yuyutsavaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a rājñas tu vacanaṃ śrutvā dharmārthasahitaṃ hitam
c kṛṣṇā dāśārham āsīnam abravīc chokakarṣitā
a sutā drupadarājasya svasitāyatamūrdhajā
c saṃpūjya sahadevaṃ ca sātyakiṃ ca mahāratham
a bhīmasenaṃ ca saṃśāntaṃ dṛṣṭvā paramadurmanāḥ
c aśrupūrṇekṣaṇā vākyam uvācedaṃ manasvinī
a viditaṃ te mahābāho dharmajña madhusūdana
c yathā nikṛtim āsthāya bhraṃśitāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ sukhāt
a dhṛtarāṣṭrasya putreṇa sāmātyena janārdana
c yathā ca saṃjayo rājñā mantraṃ rahasi śrāvitaḥ
a yudhiṣṭhireṇa dāśārha tac cāpi viditaṃ tava
c yathoktaḥ saṃjayaś caiva tac ca sarvaṃ śrutaṃ tvayā
a pañca nas tāta dīyantāṃ grāmā iti mahādyute
c kuśasthalaṃ vṛkasthalam āsandī vāraṇāvatam
a avasānaṃ mahābāho kiṃ cid eva tu pañcamam
c iti duryodhano vācyaḥ suhṛdaś cāsya keśava
a tac cāpi nākarod vākyaṃ śrutvā kṛṣṇa suyodhanaḥ
c yudhiṣṭhirasya dāśārha hrīmataḥ saṃdhim icchataḥ
a apradānena rājyasya yadi kṛṣṇa suyodhanaḥ
c saṃdhim icchen na kartavyas tatra gatvā kathaṃ cana
a śakṣyanti hi mahābāho pāṇḍavāḥ sṛñjayaiḥ saha
c dhārtarāṣṭrabalaṃ ghoraṃ kruddhaṃ pratisamāsitum
a na hi sāmnā na dānena śakyo 'rthas teṣu kaś cana
c tasmāt teṣu na kartavyā kṛpā te madhusūdana
a sāmnā dānena vā kṛṣṇa ye na śāmyanti śatravaḥ
c moktavyas teṣu daṇḍaḥ syāj jīvitaṃ parirakṣatā
a tasmāt teṣu mahādaṇḍaḥ kṣeptavyaḥ kṣipram acyuta
c tvayā caiva mahābāho pāṇḍavaiḥ saha sṛñjayaiḥ
a etat samarthaṃ pārthānāṃ tava caiva yaśaskaram
c kriyamāṇaṃ bhavet kṛṣṇa kṣatrasya ca sukhāvaham
a kṣatriyeṇa hi hantavyaḥ kṣatriyo lobham āsthitaḥ
c akṣatriyo vā dāśārha svadharmam anutiṣṭhatā
a anyatra brāhmaṇāt tāta sarvapāpeṣv avasthitāt
c gurur hi sarvavarṇānāṃ brāhmaṇaḥ prasṛtāgrabhuk
a yathāvadhye bhaved doṣo vadhyamāne janārdana
c sa vadhyasyāvadhe dṛṣṭa iti dharmavido viduḥ
a yathā tvāṃ na spṛśed eṣa doṣaḥ kṛṣṇa tathā kuru
c pāṇḍavaiḥ saha dāśārha sṛñjayaiś ca sasainikaiḥ
a punar uktaṃ ca vakṣyāmi viśrambheṇa janārdana
c kā nu sīmantinī mādṛk pṛthivyām asti keśava
a sutā drupadarājasya vedimadhyāt samutthitā
c dhṛṣṭadyumnasya bhaginī tava kṛṣṇa priyā sakhī
a ājamīḍhakulaṃ prāptā snuṣā pāṇḍor mahātmanaḥ
c mahiṣī pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ pañcendrasamavarcasām
a sutā me pañcabhir vīraiḥ pañca jātā mahārathāḥ
c abhimanyur yathā kṛṣṇa tathā te tava dharmataḥ
a sāhaṃ keśagrahaṃ prāptā parikliṣṭā sabhāṃ gatā
c paśyatāṃ pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ tvayi jīvati keśava
a jīvatsu kauraveyeṣu pāñcāleṣv atha vṛṣṇiṣu
c dāsībhūtāsmi pāpānāṃ sabhāmadhye vyavasthitā
a nirāmarṣeṣv aceṣṭeṣu prekṣamāṇeṣu pāṇḍuṣu
c trāhi mām iti govinda manasā kāṅkṣito 'si me
a yatra māṃ bhagavān rājā śvaśuro vākyam abravīt
c varaṃ vṛṇīṣva pāñcāli varārhāsi matāsi me
a adāsāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ santu sarathāḥ sāyudhā iti
c mayokte yatra nirmuktā vanavāsāya keśava
a evaṃvidhānāṃ duḥkhānām abhijño 'si janārdana
c trāhi māṃ puṇḍarīkākṣa sabhartṛjñātibāndhavām
a nanv ahaṃ kṛṣṇa bhīṣmasya dhṛtarāṣṭrasya cobhayoḥ
c snuṣā bhavāmi dharmeṇa sāhaṃ dāsīkṛtābhavam
a dhig balaṃ bhīmasenasya dhik pārthasya dhanuṣmatām
c yatra duryodhanaḥ kṛṣṇa muhūrtam api jīvati
a yadi te 'ham anugrāhyā yadi te 'sti kṛpā mayi
c dhārtarāṣṭreṣu vai kopaḥ sarvaḥ kṛṣṇa vidhīyatām
a ity uktvā mṛdusaṃhāraṃ vṛjināgraṃ sudarśanam
c sunīlam asitāpāṅgī puṇyagandhādhivāsitam
a sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpannaṃ mahābhujagavarcasam
c keśapakṣaṃ varārohā gṛhya savyena pāṇinā
a padmākṣī puṇḍarīkākṣam upetya gajagāminī
c aśrupūrṇekṣaṇā kṛṣṇā kṛṣṇaṃ vacanam abravīt
a ayaṃ te puṇḍarīkākṣa duḥśāsanakaroddhṛtaḥ
c smartavyaḥ sarvakāleṣu pareṣāṃ saṃdhim icchatā
a yadi bhīmārjunau kṛṣṇa kṛpaṇau saṃdhikāmukau
c pitā me yotsyate vṛddhaḥ saha putrair mahārathaiḥ
a pañca caiva mahāvīryāḥ putrā me madhusūdana
c abhimanyuṃ puraskṛtya yotsyanti kurubhiḥ saha
a duḥśāsanabhujaṃ śyāmaṃ saṃchinnaṃ pāṃsuguṇṭhitam
c yady ahaṃ taṃ na paśyāmi kā śāntir hṛdayasya me
a trayodaśa hi varṣāṇi pratīkṣantyā gatāni me
c nidhāya hṛdaye manyuṃ pradīptam iva pāvakam
a vidīryate me hṛdayaṃ bhīmavākśalyapīḍitam
c yo 'yam adya mahābāhur dharmaṃ samanupaśyati
a ity uktvā bāṣpasannena kaṇṭhenāyatalocanā
c ruroda kṛṣṇā sotkampaṃ sasvaraṃ bāṣpagadgadam
a stanau pīnāyataśroṇī sahitāv abhivarṣatī
c dravībhūtam ivātyuṣṇam utsṛjad vāri netrajam
a tām uvāca mahābāhuḥ keśavaḥ parisāntvayan
c acirād drakṣyase kṛṣṇe rudatīr bharatastriyaḥ
a evaṃ tā bhīru rotsyanti nihatajñātibāndhavāḥ
c hatamitrā hatabalā yeṣāṃ kruddhāsi bhāmini
a ahaṃ ca tat kariṣyāmi bhīmārjunayamaiḥ saha
c yudhiṣṭhiraniyogena daivāc ca vidhinirmitāt
a dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ kālapakvā na cec chṛṇvanti me vacaḥ
c śeṣyante nihatā bhūmau śvaśṛgālādanīkṛtāḥ
a caled dhi himavāñ śailo medinī śatadhā bhavet
c dyauḥ patec ca sanakṣatrā na me moghaṃ vaco bhavet
d dyauḥ patet pṛthivī śīryed dhimavāñ chithilībhavet
d śuṣyet toyanidhiḥ kṛṣṇe na me moghaṃ vaco bhavet
a satyaṃ te pratijānāmi kṛṣṇe bāṣpo nigṛhyatām
c hatāmitrāñ śriyā yuktān acirād drakṣyase patīn
 arjuna uvāca
a kurūṇām adya sarveṣāṃ bhavān suhṛd anuttamaḥ
c saṃbandhī dayito nityam ubhayoḥ pakṣayor api
a pāṇḍavair dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ pratipādyam anāmayam
c samarthaḥ praśamaṃ caiṣāṃ kartuṃ tvam asi keśava
a tvam itaḥ puṇḍarīkākṣa suyodhanam amarṣaṇam
c śāntyarthaṃ bhārataṃ brūyā yat tad vācyam amitrahan
a tvayā dharmārthayuktaṃ ced uktaṃ śivam anāmayam
c hitaṃ nādāsyate bālo diṣṭasya vaśam eṣyati
 bhagavān uvāca
a dharmyam asmaddhitaṃ caiva kurūṇāṃ yad anāmayam
c eṣa yāsyāmi rājānaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭram abhīpsayā
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tato vyapete tamasi sūrye vimala udgate
c maitre muhūrte saṃprāpte mṛdvarciṣi divākare
a kaumude māsi revatyāṃ śaradante himāgame
c sphītasasyasukhe kāle kalyaḥ sattvavatāṃ varaḥ
a maṅgalyāḥ puṇyanirghoṣā vācaḥ śṛṇvaṃś ca sūnṛtāḥ
c brāhmaṇānāṃ pratītānām ṛṣīṇām iva vāsavaḥ
a kṛtvā paurvāhṇikaṃ kṛtyaṃ snātaḥ śucir alaṃkṛtaḥ
c upatasthe vivasvantaṃ pāvakaṃ ca janārdanaḥ
a ṛṣabhaṃ pṛṣṭha ālabhya brāhmaṇān abhivādya ca
c agniṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā paśyan kalyāṇam agrataḥ
a tat pratijñāya vacanaṃ pāṇḍavasya janārdanaḥ
c śiner naptāram āsīnam abhyabhāṣata sātyakim
a ratha āropyatāṃ śaṅkhaś cakraṃ ca gadayā saha
c upāsaṅgāś ca śaktyaś ca sarvapraharaṇāni ca
a duryodhano hi duṣṭātmā karṇaś ca sahasaubalaḥ
c na ca śatrur avajñeyaḥ prākṛto 'pi balīyasā
a tatas tan matam ājñāya keśavasya puraḥsarāḥ
c prasasrur yojayiṣyanto rathaṃ cakragadābhṛtaḥ
a taṃ dīptam iva kālāgnim ākāśagam ivādhvagam
c candrasūryaprakāśābhyāṃ cakrābhyāṃ samalaṃkṛtam
a ardhacandraiś ca candraiś ca matsyaiḥ samṛgapakṣibhiḥ
c puṣpaiś ca vividhaiś citraṃ maṇiratnaiś ca sarvaśaḥ
c   bhūṣaṇair vividhair api
c vipraiś ca vividhaiś citrair
a taruṇādityasaṃkāśaṃ bṛhantaṃ cārudarśanam
c maṇihemavicitrāṅgaṃ sudhvajaṃ supatākinam
a sūpaskaram anādhṛṣyaṃ vaiyāghraparivāraṇam
c yaśoghnaṃ pratyamitrāṇāṃ yadūnāṃ nandivardhanam
a vājibhiḥ sainyasugrīvameghapuṣpabalāhakaiḥ
c snātaiḥ saṃpādayāṃ cakruḥ saṃpannaiḥ sarvasaṃpadā
a mahimānaṃ tu kṛṣṇasya bhūya evābhivardhayan
c sughoṣaḥ patagendreṇa dhvajena yuyuje rathaḥ
a taṃ meruśikharaprakhyaṃ meghadundubhinisvanam
b sārathyakarmadakṣeṇa rakṣitaṃ dārukeṇa ca
b kṛtvā pradakṣiṇaṃ śauriḥ prasthānocitabhūṣaṇaḥ
c āruroha rathaṃ śaurir vimānam iva puṇyakṛt
a tataḥ sātyakim āropya prayayau puruṣottamaḥ
c pṛthivīṃ cāntarikṣaṃ ca rathaghoṣeṇa nādayan
a vyapoḍhābhraghanaḥ kālaḥ kṣaṇena samapadyata
c śivaś cānuvavau vāyuḥ praśāntam abhavad rajaḥ
a pradakṣiṇānulomāś ca maṅgalyā mṛgapakṣiṇaḥ
c prayāṇe vāsudevasya babhūvur anuyāyinaḥ
a maṅgalyārthapadaiḥ śabdair anvavartanta sarvaśaḥ
c sārasāḥ śatapatrāś ca haṃsāś ca madhusūdanam
a mantrāhutimahāhomair hūyamānaś ca pāvakaḥ
c pradakṣiṇaśikho bhūtvā vidhūmaḥ samapadyata
a vasiṣṭho vāmadevaś ca bhūridyumno gayaḥ krathaḥ
c śukranāradavālmīkā marutaḥ kuśiko bhṛguḥ
a brahmadevarṣayaś caiva kṛṣṇaṃ yadusukhāvaham
c pradakṣiṇam avartanta sahitā vāsavānujam
a evam etair mahābhāgair maharṣigaṇasādhubhiḥ
c pūjitaḥ prayayau kṛṣṇaḥ kurūṇāṃ sadanaṃ prati
d devatābhyo namaskṛtya brāhmaṇān svasti vācya ca
d prayayau puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ sātyakena sahācyutaḥ
a taṃ prayāntam anuprāyāt kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c bhīmasenārjunau cobhau mādrīputrau ca pāṇḍavau
a cekitānaś ca vikrānto dhṛṣṭaketuś ca cedipaḥ
c drupadaḥ kāśirājaś ca śikhaṇḍī ca mahārathaḥ
a dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ saputraś ca virāṭaḥ kekayaiḥ saha
c saṃsādhanārthaṃ prayayuḥ kṣatriyāḥ kṣatriyarṣabham
a tato 'nuvrajya govindaṃ dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c rājñāṃ sakāśe dyutimān uvācedaṃ vacas tadā
a yo naiva kāmān na bhayān na lobhān nārthakāraṇāt
c anyāyam anuvarteta sthirabuddhir alolupaḥ
a dharmajño dhṛtimān prājñaḥ sarvabhūteṣu keśavaḥ
c īśvaraḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ devadevaḥ pratāpavān
a taṃ sarvaguṇasaṃpannaṃ śrīvatsakṛtalakṣaṇam
c saṃpariṣvajya kaunteyaḥ saṃdeṣṭum upacakrame
a yā sā bālyāt prabhṛty asmān paryavardhayatābalā
c upavāsatapaḥśīlā sadā svastyayane ratā
a devatātithipūjāsu guruśuśrūṣaṇe ratā
c vatsalā priyaputrā ca priyāsmākaṃ janārdana
a suyodhanabhayād yā no 'trāyatāmitrakarśana
c mahato mṛtyusaṃbādhād uttaran naur ivārṇavāt
a asmatkṛte ca satataṃ yayā duḥkhāni mādhava
c anubhūtāny aduḥkhārhā tāṃ sma pṛccher anāmayam
a bhṛśam āśvāsayeś caināṃ putraśokapariplutām
c abhivādya svajethāś ca pāṇḍavān parikīrtayan
a ūḍhāt prabhṛti duḥkhāni śvaśurāṇām ariṃdama
c nikārān atadarhā ca paśyantī duḥkham aśnute
a api jātu sa kālaḥ syāt kṛṣṇa duḥkhaviparyayaḥ
c yad ahaṃ mātaraṃ kliṣṭāṃ sukhe dadhyām ariṃdama
a pravrajanto 'nvadhāvat sā kṛpaṇā putragṛddhinī
c rudatīm apahāyainām upagacchāma yad vanam
a na nūnaṃ mriyate duḥkhaiḥ sā cej jīvati keśava
c tathā putrādhibhir gāḍham ārtā hy ānartasatkṛtā
a abhivādyā tu sā kṛṣṇa tvayā madvacanād vibho
b saṃkṣāmyātha namaskāryā sarveṣāṃ vacanād api
c dhṛtarāṣṭraś ca kauravyo rājānaś ca vayo 'dhikāḥ
a bhīṣmaṃ droṇaṃ kṛpaṃ caiva mahārājaṃ ca bāhlikam
c drauṇiṃ ca somadattaṃ ca sarvāṃś ca bharatān pṛthak
d yathāvayo yathāsthānaṃ pūjayasva janārdana
a viduraṃ ca mahāprājñaṃ kurūṇāṃ mantradhāriṇam
c agādhabuddhiṃ dharmajñaṃ svajethā madhusūdana
a ity uktvā keśavaṃ tatra rājamadhye yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c anujñāto nivavṛte kṛṣṇaṃ kṛtvā pradakṣiṇam
a vrajann eva tu bībhatsuḥ sakhāyaṃ puruṣarṣabham
c abravīt paravīraghnaṃ dāśārham aparājitam
a yad asmākaṃ vibho vṛttaṃ purā vai mantraniścaye
c ardharājyasya govinda viditaṃ sarvarājasu
a tac ced dadyād asaṅgena satkṛtyānavamanya ca
b dadāti govinda paraṃ dharmarājñe suyodhanaḥ
c priyaṃ me syān mahābāho mucyeran mahato bhayāt
a ataś ced anyathā kartā dhārtarāṣṭro 'nupāyavit
c antaṃ nūnaṃ kariṣyāmi kṣatriyāṇāṃ janārdana
a evam ukte pāṇḍavena paryahṛṣyad vṛkodaraḥ
c muhur muhuḥ krodhavaśāt prāvepata ca pāṇḍavaḥ
a vepamānaś ca kaunteyaḥ prākrośan mahato ravān
c dhanaṃjayavacaḥ śrutvā harṣotsiktamanā bhṛśam
a tasya taṃ ninadaṃ śrutvā saṃprāvepanta dhanvinaḥ
c vāhanāni ca sarvāṇi śakṛnmūtraṃ prasusruvuḥ
a ity uktvā keśavaṃ tatra tathā coktvā viniścayam
c anujñāto nivavṛte pariṣvajya janārdanam
a teṣu rājasu sarveṣu nivṛtteṣu janārdanaḥ
c tūrṇam abhyapatad dhṛṣṭaḥ sainyasugrīvavāhanaḥ
a te hayā vāsudevasya dārukeṇa pracoditāḥ
c panthānam ācemur iva grasamānā ivāmbaram
a athāpaśyan mahābāhur ṛṣīn adhvani keśavaḥ
c brāhmyā śriyā dīpyamānān sthitān ubhayataḥ pathi
a so 'vatīrya rathāt tūrṇam abhivādya janārdanaḥ
c yathāvat tān ṛṣīn sarvān abhyabhāṣata pūjayan
a kaccil lokeṣu kuśalaṃ kaccid dharmaḥ svanuṣṭhitaḥ
c brāhmaṇānāṃ trayo varṇāḥ kaccit tiṣṭhanti śāsane
d pitṛdevātithibhyaś ca kaccit pūjā svanuṣṭhitā
a tebhyaḥ prayujya tāṃ pūjāṃ provāca madhusūdanaḥ
c bhagavantaḥ kva saṃsiddhāḥ kā vīthī bhavatām iha
a kiṃ vā bhagavatāṃ kāryam ahaṃ kiṃ karavāṇi vaḥ
c kenārthenopasaṃprāptā bhagavanto mahītalam
d evam uktāḥ keśavena munayaḥ saṃśitavratāḥ
d nāradapramukhāḥ sarve pratyanandanta keśavam
d adhaḥśirāḥ sarpamālī maharṣiḥ satyadevalaḥ
d arvāvasuś ca jānuś ca maitreyaḥ śunako balī
d bako dālbhyaḥ sthūlaśirāḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanas tathā
d āyodadhaumyo dhaumyaś ca āṇimāṇḍavyakauśikau
d dāmoṣṇīṣas triṣavaṇaḥ parṇādo ghaṭajānukaḥ
d mauñjāyano vāyubhakṣaḥ pārāśaryo 'tha śārikaḥ
d śīlavān aśanirdhātā śūnyapālo 'kṛtaśramaḥ
d śvetaketuś ca katthāmā vaidaś cāpi hiraṇyadaḥ
a tam abravīj jāmadagnya upetya madhusūdanam
c pariṣvajya ca govindaṃ purā sucarite sakhā
a devarṣayaḥ puṇyakṛto brāhmaṇāś ca bahuśrutāḥ
c rājarṣayaś ca dāśārha mānayantas tapasvinaḥ
a devāsurasya draṣṭāraḥ purāṇasya mahādyute
c sametaṃ pārthivaṃ kṣatraṃ didṛkṣantaś ca sarvataḥ
a sabhāsadaś ca rājānas tvāṃ ca satyaṃ janārdana
c etan mahat prekṣaṇīyaṃ draṣṭuṃ gacchāma keśava
a dharmārthasahitā vācaḥ śrotum icchāma mādhava
c tvayocyamānāḥ kuruṣu rājamadhye paraṃtapa
d sabhāyāṃ madhurā vācaḥ śuśrūṣantas tvayeritāḥ
d kurūṇāṃ pratipattiṃ ca śrotum icchāma keśava
a bhīṣmadroṇādayaś caiva viduraś ca mahāmatiḥ
c tvaṃ ca yādavaśārdūla sabhāyāṃ vai sameṣyatha
a tava vākyāni divyāni tatra teṣāṃ ca mādhava
c śrotum icchāma govinda satyāni ca śubhāni ca
d tvatpādasparśasaṃśuddhā bhūmir duṣṭavivarjitā
d dharmavṛddhyā śobhamānā prītiṃ cādhāsyatīha naḥ
a āpṛṣṭo 'si mahābāho punar drakṣyāmahe vayam
c yāhy avighnena vai vīra drakṣyāmas tvāṃ sabhāgatam
d āsīnam āsane divye balatejaḥsamāhitam
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a prayāntaṃ devakīputraṃ paravīrarujo daśa
c mahārathā mahābāhum anvayuḥ śastrapāṇayaḥ
a padātīnāṃ sahasraṃ ca sādināṃ ca paraṃtapa
c bhojyaṃ ca vipulaṃ rājan preṣyāś ca śataśo 'pare
 janamejaya uvāca
a kathaṃ prayāto dāśārho mahātmā madhusūdanaḥ
c kāni vā vrajatas tasya nimittāni mahaujasaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tasya prayāṇe yāny āsann adbhutāni mahātmanaḥ
c tāni me śṛṇu divyāni daivāny autpātikāni ca
a anabhre 'śaninirghoṣaḥ savidyutsamajāyata
c anvag eva ca parjanyaḥ prāvarṣad vighane bhṛśam
a pratyag ūhur mahānadyaḥ prāṅmukhāḥ sindhusattamāḥ
c viparītā diśaḥ sarvā na prājñāyata kiṃ cana
a prājvalann agnayo rājan pṛthivī samakampata
c udapānāś ca kumbhāś ca prāsiñcañ śataśo jalam
a tamaḥsaṃvṛtam apy āsīt sarvaṃ jagad idaṃ tadā
c na diśo nādiśo rājan prajñāyante sma reṇunā
a prādurāsīn mahāñ śabdaḥ khe śarīraṃ na dṛśyate
c sarveṣu rājan deśeṣu tad adbhutam ivābhavat
a prāmathnād dhāstinapuraṃ vāto dakṣiṇapaścimaḥ
c ārujan gaṇaśo vṛkṣān paruṣo bhīmanisvanaḥ
a yatra yatra tu vārṣṇeyo vartate pathi bhārata
c tatra tatra sukho vāyuḥ sarvaṃ cāsīt pradakṣiṇam
a vavarṣa puṣpavarṣaṃ ca kamalāni ca bhūriśaḥ
c samaś ca panthā nirduḥkho vyapetakuśakaṇṭakaḥ
a sa gacchan brāhmaṇai rājaṃs tatra tatra mahābhujaḥ
c arcyate madhuparkaiś ca sumanobhir vasupradaḥ
a taṃ kiranti mahātmānaṃ vanyaiḥ puṣpaiḥ sugandhibhiḥ
c striyaḥ pathi samāgamya sarvabhūtahite ratam
a sa śālibhavanaṃ ramyaṃ sarvasasyasamācitam
c sukhaṃ paramadharmiṣṭham atyagād bharatarṣabha
a paśyan bahupaśūn grāmān ramyān hṛdayatoṣaṇān
c purāṇi ca vyatikrāman rāṣṭrāṇi vividhāni ca
a nityahṛṣṭāḥ sumanaso bhāratair abhirakṣitāḥ
c nodvignāḥ paracakrāṇām anayānām akovidāḥ
a upaplavyād athāyāntaṃ janāḥ puranivāsinaḥ
c pathy atiṣṭhanta sahitā viṣvaksenadidṛkṣayā
a te tu sarve sunāmānam agnim iddham iva prabhum
c arcayām āsur arcyaṃ taṃ deśātithim upasthitam
a vṛkasthalaṃ samāsādya keśavaḥ paravīrahā
c prakīrṇaraśmāv āditye vimale lohitāyati
a avatīrya rathāt tūrṇaṃ kṛtvā śaucaṃ yathāvidhi
c rathamocanam ādiśya saṃdhyām upaviveśa ha
a dāruko 'pi hayān muktvā paricarya ca śāstrataḥ
c mumoca sarvaṃ varmāṇi muktvā cainān avāsṛjat
a abhyatītya tu tat sarvam uvāca madhusūdanaḥ
c yudhiṣṭhirasya kāryārtham iha vatsyāmahe kṣapām
a tasya tan matam ājñāya cakrur āvasathaṃ narāḥ
c kṣaṇena cānnapānāni guṇavanti samārjayan
a tasmin grāme pradhānās tu ya āsan brāhmaṇā nṛpa
c āryāḥ kulīnā hrīmanto brāhmīṃ vṛttim anuṣṭhitāḥ
a te 'bhigamya mahātmānaṃ hṛṣīkeśam ariṃdamam
c pūjāṃ cakrur yathānyāyam āśīrmaṅgalasaṃyutām
a te pūjayitvā dāśārhaṃ sarvalokeṣu pūjitam
c nyavedayanta veśmāni ratnavanti mahātmane
a tān prabhuḥ kṛtam ity uktvā satkṛtya ca yathārhataḥ
c abhyetya teṣāṃ veśmāni punar āyāt sahaiva taiḥ
a sumṛṣṭaṃ bhojayitvā ca brāhmaṇāṃs tatra keśavaḥ
c bhuktvā ca saha taiḥ sarvair avasat tāṃ kṣapāṃ sukham
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tathā dūtaiḥ samājñāya āyāntaṃ madhusūdanam
c dhṛtarāṣṭro 'bravīd bhīṣmam arcayitvā mahābhujam
a droṇaṃ ca saṃjayaṃ caiva viduraṃ ca mahāmatim
c duryodhanaṃ ca sāmātyaṃ hṛṣṭaromābravīd idam
a adbhutaṃ mahad āścaryaṃ śrūyate kurunandana
c striyo bālāś ca vṛddhāś ca kathayanti gṛhe gṛhe
a satkṛtyācakṣate cānye tathaivānye samāgatāḥ
c pṛthagvādāś ca vartante catvareṣu sabhāsu ca
a upayāsyati dāśārhaḥ pāṇḍavārthe parākramī
c sa no mānyaś ca pūjyaś ca sarvathā madhusūdanaḥ
a tasmin hi yātrā lokasya bhūtānām īśvaro hi saḥ
c tasmin dhṛtiś ca vīryaṃ ca prajñā caujaś ca mādhave
a sa mānyatāṃ naraśreṣṭhaḥ sa hi dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ
c pūjito hi sukhāya syād asukhaḥ syād apūjitaḥ
a sa cet tuṣyati dāśārha upacārair ariṃdamaḥ
c kṛtsnān sarvān abhiprāyān prāpsyāmaḥ sarvarājasu
a tasya pūjārtham adyaiva saṃvidhatsva paraṃtapa
c sabhāḥ pathi vidhīyantāṃ sarvakāmasamāhitāḥ
a yathā prītir mahābāho tvayi jāyeta tasya vai
c tathā kuruṣva gāndhāre kathaṃ vā bhīṣma manyase
a tato bhīṣmādayaḥ sarve dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ janādhipam
c ūcuḥ paramam ity evaṃ pūjayanto 'sya tad vacaḥ
a teṣām anumataṃ jñātvā rājā duryodhanas tadā
c sabhāvāstūni ramyāṇi pradeṣṭum upacakrame
a tato deśeṣu deśeṣu ramaṇīyeṣu bhāgaśaḥ
c sarvaratnasamākīrṇāḥ sabhāś cakrur anekaśaḥ
a āsanāni vicitrāṇi yuktāni vividhair guṇaiḥ
c striyo gandhān alaṃkārān sūkṣmāṇi vasanāni ca
a guṇavanty annapānāni bhojyāni vividhāni ca
c mālyāni ca sugandhīni tāni rājā dadau tataḥ
a viśeṣataś ca vāsārthaṃ sabhāṃ grāme vṛkasthale
c vidadhe kauravo rājā bahuratnāṃ manoramām
a etad vidhāya vai sarvaṃ devārham atimānuṣam
c ācakhyau dhṛtarāṣṭrāya rājā duryodhanas tadā
a tāḥ sabhāḥ keśavaḥ sarvā ratnāni vividhāni ca
c asamīkṣyaiva dāśārha upāyāt kurusadma tat
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a upaplavyād iha kṣattar upayāto janārdanaḥ
c vṛkasthale nivasati sa ca prātar iheṣyati
a āhukānām adhipatiḥ purogaḥ sarvasātvatām
c mahāmanā mahāvīryo mahāmātro janārdanaḥ
a sphītasya vṛṣṇivaṃśasya bhartā goptā ca mādhavaḥ
c trayāṇām api lokānāṃ bhagavān prapitāmahaḥ
a vṛṣṇyandhakāḥ sumanaso yasya prajñām upāsate
c ādityā vasavo rudrā yathā buddhiṃ bṛhaspateḥ
a tasmai pūjāṃ prayokṣyāmi dāśārhāya mahātmane
c pratyakṣaṃ tava dharmajña tan me kathayataḥ śṛṇu
a ekavarṇaiḥ sukṛṣṇāṅgair bāhlijātair hayottamaiḥ
c caturyuktān rathāṃs tasmai raukmān dāsyāmi ṣoḍaśa
a nityaprabhinnān mātaṅgān īṣādantān prahāriṇaḥ
c aṣṭānucaram ekaikam aṣṭau dāsyāmi keśave
a dāsīnām aprajātānāṃ śubhānāṃ rukmavarcasām
c śatam asmai pradāsyāmi dāsānām api tāvataḥ
a āvikaṃ bahu susparśaṃ pārvatīyair upāhṛtam
c tad apy asmai pradāsyāmi sahasrāṇi daśāṣṭa ca
a ajinānāṃ sahasrāṇi cīnadeśodbhavāni ca
c tāny apy asmai pradāsyāmi yāvad arhati keśavaḥ
a divā rātrau ca bhāty eṣa sutejā vimalo maṇiḥ
c tam apy asmai pradāsyāmi tam apy arhati keśavaḥ
a ekenāpi pataty ahnā yojanāni caturdaśa
c yānam aśvatarīyuktaṃ dāsye tasmai tad apy aham
a yāvanti vāhanāny asya yāvantaḥ puruṣāś ca te
c tato 'ṣṭaguṇam apy asmai bhojyaṃ dāsyāmy ahaṃ sadā
a mama putrāś ca pautrāś ca sarve duryodhanād ṛte
