c pratyudyāsyanti dāśārhaṃ rathair mṛṣṭair alaṃkṛtāḥ
a svalaṃkṛtāś ca kalyāṇyaḥ pādair eva sahasraśaḥ
c vāramukhyā mahābhāgaṃ pratyudyāsyanti keśavam
a nagarād api yāḥ kāś cid gamiṣyanti janārdanam
c draṣṭuṃ kanyāś ca kalyāṇyas tāś ca yāsyanty anāvṛtāḥ
a sastrīpuruṣabālaṃ hi nagaraṃ madhusūdanam
c udīkṣate mahātmānaṃ bhānumantam iva prajāḥ
a mahādhvajapatākāś ca kriyantāṃ sarvatodiśam
c jalāvasikto virajāḥ panthās tasyeti cānvaśāt
a duḥśāsanasya ca gṛhaṃ duryodhanagṛhād varam
c tad asya kriyatāṃ kṣipraṃ susaṃmṛṣṭam alaṃkṛtam
a etad dhi rucirākāraiḥ prāsādair upaśobhitam
c śivaṃ ca ramaṇīyaṃ ca sarvartu sumahādhanam
a sarvam asmin gṛhe ratnaṃ mama duryodhanasya ca
c yad yad arhet sa vārṣṇeyas tat tad deyam asaṃśayam
 vidura uvāca
a rājan bahumataś cāsi trailokyasyāpi sattamaḥ
c saṃbhāvitaś ca lokasya saṃmataś cāsi bhārata
a yat tvam evaṃgate brūyāḥ paścime vayasi sthitaḥ
c śāstrād vā supratarkād vā susthiraḥ sthaviro hy asi
a lekhāśmanīva bhāḥ sūrye mahormir iva sāgare
c dharmas tvayi mahān rājann iti vyavasitāḥ prajāḥ
a sadaiva bhāvito loko guṇaughais tava pārthiva
c guṇānāṃ rakṣaṇe nityaṃ prayatasva sabāndhavaḥ
a ārjavaṃ pratipadyasva mā bālyād bahudhā naśīḥ
c rājyaṃ putrāṃś ca pautrāṃś ca suhṛdaś cāpi supriyān
a yat tvaṃ ditsasi kṛṣṇāya rājann atithaye bahu
c etad anyac ca dāśārhaḥ pṛthivīm api cārhati
a na tu tvaṃ dharmam uddiśya tasya vā priyakāraṇāt
c etad icchasi kṛṣṇāya satyenātmānam ālabhe
a māyaiṣātattvam evaitac chadmaitad bhūridakṣiṇa
c jānāmi te mataṃ rājan gūḍhaṃ bāhyena karmaṇā
a pañca pañcaiva lipsanti grāmakān pāṇḍavā nṛpa
c na ca ditsasi tebhyas tāṃs tac chamaṃ kaḥ kariṣyati
a arthena tu mahābāhuṃ vārṣṇeyaṃ tvaṃ jihīrṣasi
c anenaivābhyupāyena pāṇḍavebhyo bibhitsasi
a na ca vittena śakyo 'sau nodyamena na garhayā
c anyo dhanaṃjayāt kartum etat tattvaṃ bravīmi te
a veda kṛṣṇasya māhātmyaṃ vedāsya dṛḍhabhaktitām
c atyājyam asya jānāmi prāṇais tulyaṃ dhanaṃjayam
a anyat kumbhād apāṃ pūrṇād anyat pādāvasecanāt
c anyat kuśalasaṃpraśnān naiṣiṣyati janārdanaḥ
a yat tv asya priyam ātithyaṃ mānārhasya mahātmanaḥ
c tad asmai kriyatāṃ rājan mānārho hi janārdanaḥ
a āśaṃsamānaḥ kalyāṇaṃ kurūn abhyeti keśavaḥ
c yenaiva rājann arthena tad evāsmā upākuru
a śamam icchati dāśārhas tava duryodhanasya ca
c pāṇḍavānāṃ ca rājendra tad asya vacanaṃ kuru
a pitāsi rājan putrās te vṛddhas tvaṃ śiśavaḥ pare
c vartasva pitṛvat teṣu vartante te hi putravat
d nirvairān matsyapāñcālān pāṇḍavān kurubhiḥ saha
d kṛtvā sukhaṃ yathādharmaṃ kīrtiṃ ca samavāpnuhi
 duryodhana uvāca
a yad āha viduraḥ kṛṣṇe sarvaṃ tat satyam ucyate
c anurakto hy asaṃhāryaḥ pārthān prati janārdanaḥ
a yat tu satkārasaṃyuktaṃ deyaṃ vasu janārdane
c anekarūpaṃ rājendra na tad deyaṃ kadā cana
a deśaḥ kālas tathāyukto na hi nārhati keśavaḥ
c maṃsyaty adhokṣajo rājan bhayād arcati mām iti
a avamānaś ca yatra syāt kṣatriyasya viśāṃ pate
c na tat kuryād budhaḥ kāryam iti me niścitā matiḥ
a sa hi pūjyatamo devaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ kamalalocanaḥ
c trayāṇām api lokānāṃ viditaṃ mama sarvathā
a na tu tasmin pradeyaṃ syāt tathā kāryagatiḥ prabho
c vigrahaḥ samupārabdho na hi śāmyaty avigrahāt
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā bhīṣmaḥ kurupitāmahaḥ
c vaicitravīryaṃ rājānam idaṃ vacanam abravīt
a satkṛto 'satkṛto vāpi na krudhyeta janārdanaḥ
c nālam anyam avajñātum avajñāto 'pi keśavaḥ
a yat tu kāryaṃ mahābāho manasā kāryatāṃ gatam
c sarvopāyair na tac chakyaṃ kena cit kartum anyathā
a sa yad brūyān mahābāhus tat kāryam aviśaṅkayā
c vāsudevena tīrthena kṣipraṃ saṃśāmya pāṇḍavaiḥ
a dharmyam arthyaṃ sa dharmātmā dhruvaṃ vaktā janārdanaḥ
c tasmin vācyāḥ priyā vāco bhavatā bāndhavaiḥ saha
 duryodhana uvāca
a na paryāyo 'sti yad rājañ śriyaṃ niṣkevalām aham
c taiḥ sahemām upāśnīyāṃ jīvañ jīvaiḥ pitāmaha
a idaṃ tu sumahat kāryaṃ śṛṇu me yat samarthitam
b na bhedasyāntaraṃ dātuṃ prayāṇāyāsya vā punaḥ
c parāyaṇaṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ niyaṃsyāmi janārdanam
a tasmin baddhe bhaviṣyanti vṛṣṇayaḥ pṛthivī tathā
c pāṇḍavāś ca vidheyā me sa ca prātar iheṣyati
a atropāyaṃ yathā samyaṅ na budhyeta janārdanaḥ
c na cāpāyo bhavet kaś cit tad bhavān prabravītu me
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā ghoraṃ kṛṣṇābhisaṃhitam
c dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ sahāmātyo vyathito vimanābhavat
a tato duryodhanam idaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭro 'bravīd vacaḥ
c maivaṃ vocaḥ prajāpāla naiṣa dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ
a dūtaś ca hi hṛṣīkeśaḥ saṃbandhī ca priyaś ca naḥ
c apāpaḥ kauraveyeṣu kathaṃ bandhanam arhati
 bhīṣma uvāca
a parīto dhṛtarāṣṭrāyaṃ tava putraḥ sumandadhīḥ
c vṛṇoty anarthaṃ na tv arthaṃ yācyamānaḥ suhṛdgaṇaiḥ
a imam utpathi vartantaṃ pāpaṃ pāpānubandhinam
c vākyāni suhṛdāṃ hitvā tvam apy asyānuvartase
a kṛṣṇam akliṣṭakarmāṇam āsādyāyaṃ sudurmatiḥ
c tava putraḥ sahāmātyaḥ kṣaṇena na bhaviṣyati
a pāpasyāsya nṛśaṃsasya tyaktadharmasya durmateḥ
c notsahe 'narthasaṃyuktāṃ vācaṃ śrotuṃ kathaṃ cana
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a ity uktvā bharataśreṣṭho vṛddhaḥ paramamanyumān
c utthāya tasmāt prātiṣṭhad bhīṣmaḥ satyaparākramaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a prātar utthāya kṛṣṇas tu kṛtavān sarvam āhnikam
c brāhmaṇair abhyanujñātaḥ prayayau nagaraṃ prati
a taṃ prayāntaṃ mahābāhum anujñāpya tato nṛpa
c paryavartanta te sarve vṛkasthalanivāsinaḥ
d prayayau puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ kurūṇāṃ sadanaṃ prati
d ācakramuś ca panthānaṃ grasamānā ivāmbaram
d dārukeṇa pracoditā hayās tasya mahātmanaḥ
d annāni śayyā vāsāṃsi tathā ratnāni sarvaśaḥ
d duryodhanena kṛṣṇārthaṃ pathi saṃvihitaṃ bahu
d tāḥ sabhāḥ puṇḍarīkākṣo ratnāni ca mahāyaśāḥ
d nābhyanandan mahābāhur upāyāt kurusaṃsadam
a dhārtarāṣṭrās tam āyāntaṃ pratyujjagmuḥ svalaṃkṛtāḥ
c duryodhanam ṛte sarve bhīṣmadroṇakṛpādayaḥ
a paurāś ca bahulā rājan hṛṣīkeśaṃ didṛkṣavaḥ
c yānair bahuvidhair anye padbhir eva tathāpare
a sa vai pathi samāgamya bhīṣmeṇākliṣṭakarmaṇā
c droṇena dhārtarāṣṭraiś ca tair vṛto nagaraṃ yayau
a kṛṣṇasaṃmānanārthaṃ ca nagaraṃ samalaṃkṛtam
c babhūvū rājamārgāś ca bahuratnasamācitāḥ
a na sma kaś cid gṛhe rājaṃs tad āsīd bharatarṣabha
c na strī na vṛddho na śiśur vāsudevadidṛkṣayā
a rājamārge narā na sma saṃbhavanty avaniṃ gatāḥ
c tathā hi sumahad rājan hṛṣīkeśapraveśane
a āvṛtāni varastrībhir gṛhāṇi sumahānty api
c pracalantīva bhāreṇa dṛśyante sma mahītale
a tathā ca gatimantas te vāsudevasya vājinaḥ
c pranaṣṭagatayo 'bhūvan rājamārge narair vṛte
a sa gṛhaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrasya prāviśac chatrukarśanaḥ
c pāṇḍuraṃ puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ prāsādair upaśobhitam
a tisraḥ kakṣyā vyatikramya keśavo rājaveśmanaḥ
c vaicitravīryaṃ rājānam abhyagacchad ariṃdamaḥ
a abhyāgacchati dāśārhe prajñācakṣur nareśvaraḥ
c sahaiva droṇabhīṣmābhyām udatiṣṭhan mahāyaśāḥ
a kṛpaś ca somadattaś ca mahārājaś ca bāhlikaḥ
c āsanebhyo 'calan sarve pūjayanto janārdanam
a tato rājānam āsādya dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ yaśasvinam
c sa bhīṣmaṃ pūjayām āsa vārṣṇeyo vāgbhir añjasā
d te svadharmān akurvanta saṃpūjya madhusūdanam
a teṣu dharmānupūrvīṃ tāṃ prayujya madhusūdanaḥ
c yathāvayaḥ samīyāya rājabhis tatra mādhavaḥ
a atha droṇaṃ saputraṃ sa bāhlīkaṃ ca yaśasvinam
c kṛpaṃ ca somadattaṃ ca samīyāya janārdanaḥ
a tatrāsīd ūrjitaṃ mṛṣṭaṃ kāñcanaṃ mahad āsanam
c śāsanād dhṛtarāṣṭrasya tatropāviśad acyutaḥ
a atha gāṃ madhuparkaṃ cāpy udakaṃ ca janārdane
c upajahrur yathānyāyaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrapurohitāḥ
a kṛtātithyas tu govindaḥ sarvān parihasan kurūn
c āste saṃbandhakaṃ kurvan kurubhiḥ parivāritaḥ
a so 'rcito dhṛtarāṣṭreṇa pūjitaś ca mahāyaśāḥ
c rājānaṃ samanujñāpya nirākrāmad ariṃdamaḥ
a taiḥ sametya yathānyāyaṃ kurubhiḥ kurusaṃsadi
c vidurāvasathaṃ ramyam upātiṣṭhata mādhavaḥ
a viduraḥ sarvakalyāṇair abhigamya janārdanam
c arcayām āsa dāśārhaṃ sarvakāmair upasthitam
d yā prītiḥ puṇḍarīkākṣa tavāgamanakāraṇāt
a kṛtātithyaṃ tu govindaṃ viduraḥ sarvadharmavit
c kuśalaṃ pāṇḍuputrāṇām apṛcchan madhusūdanam
a prīyamāṇasya suhṛdo viduṣo buddhisattamaḥ
c dharmanityasya ca tadā gatadoṣasya dhīmataḥ
a tasya sarvaṃ savistāraṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ viceṣṭitam
c kṣattur ācaṣṭa dāśārhaḥ sarvapratyakṣadarśivān
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a athopagamya viduram aparāhṇe janārdanaḥ
c pitṛṣvasāraṃ govindaḥ so 'bhyagacchad ariṃdamaḥ
a sā dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇam āyāntaṃ prasannādityavarcasam
c kaṇṭhe gṛhītvā prākrośat pṛthā pārthān anusmaran
a teṣāṃ sattvavatāṃ madhye govindaṃ sahacāriṇam
c cirasya dṛṣṭvā vārṣṇeyaṃ bāṣpam āhārayat pṛthā
a sābravīt kṛṣṇam āsīnaṃ kṛtātithyaṃ yudhāṃ patim
c bāṣpagadgadapūrṇena mukhena pariśuṣyatā
a ye te bālyāt prabhṛtyeva guruśuśrūṣaṇe ratāḥ
c parasparasya suhṛdaḥ saṃmatāḥ samacetasaḥ
a nikṛtyā bhraṃśitā rājyāj janārhā nirjanaṃ gatāḥ
c vinītakrodhaharṣāś ca brahmaṇyāḥ satyavādinaḥ
a tyaktvā priyasukhe pārthā rudantīm apahāya mām
c ahārṣuś ca vanaṃ yāntaḥ samūlaṃ hṛdayaṃ mama
a atadarhā mahātmānaḥ kathaṃ keśava pāṇḍavāḥ
c ūṣur mahāvane tāta siṃhavyāghragajākule
a bālā vihīnāḥ pitrā te mayā satatalālitāḥ
c apaśyantaḥ svapitarau katham ūṣur mahāvane
a śaṅkhadundubhinirghoṣair mṛdaṅgair vaiṇavair api
c pāṇḍavāḥ samabodhyanta bālyāt prabhṛti keśava
a ye sma vāraṇaśabdena hayānāṃ heṣitena ca
c rathanemininādaiś ca vyabodhyanta sadā gṛhe
a śaṅkhabherīninādena veṇuvīṇānunādinā
c puṇyāhaghoṣamiśreṇa pūjyamānā dvijātibhiḥ
a vastrai ratnair alaṃkāraiḥ pūjayanto dvijanmanaḥ
c gīrbhir maṅgalayuktābhir brāhmaṇānāṃ mahātmanām
a arcitair arcanārhaiś ca stuvadbhir abhinanditāḥ
c prāsādāgreṣv abodhyanta rāṅkavājinaśāyinaḥ
a te nūnaṃ ninadaṃ śrutvā śvāpadānāṃ mahāvane
c na smopayānti nidrāṃ vai atadarhā janārdana
a bherīmṛdaṅganinadaiḥ śaṅkhavaiṇavanisvanaiḥ
c strīṇāṃ gītaninādaiś ca madhurair madhusūdana
a bandimāgadhasūtaiś ca stuvadbhir bodhitāḥ katham
c mahāvane vyabodhyanta śvāpadānāṃ rutena te
a hrīmān satyadhṛtir dānto bhūtānām anukampitā
c kāmadveṣau vaśe kṛtvā satāṃ vartmānuvartate
a ambarīṣasya māndhātur yayāter nahuṣasya ca
c bharatasya dilīpasya śiber auśīnarasya ca
a rājarṣīṇāṃ purāṇānāṃ dhuraṃ dhatte durudvahām
c śīlavṛttopasaṃpanno dharmajñaḥ satyasaṃgaraḥ
a rājā sarvaguṇopetas trailokyasyāpi yo bhavet
c ajātaśatrur dharmātmā śuddhajāmbūnadaprabhaḥ
a śreṣṭhaḥ kuruṣu sarveṣu dharmataḥ śrutavṛttataḥ
c priyadarśano dīrghabhujaḥ kathaṃ kṛṣṇa yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a yaḥ sa nāgāyutaprāṇo vātaraṃhā vṛkodaraḥ
c amarṣī pāṇḍavo nityaṃ priyo bhrātuḥ priyaṃkaraḥ
a kīcakasya ca sajñāter yo hantā madhusūdana
c śūraḥ krodhavaśānāṃ ca hiḍimbasya bakasya ca
a parākrame śakrasamo vāyuvegasamo jave
c maheśvarasamaḥ krodhe bhīmaḥ praharatāṃ varaḥ
a krodhaṃ balam amarṣaṃ ca yo nidhāya paraṃtapaḥ
c jitātmā pāṇḍavo 'marṣī bhrātus tiṣṭhati śāsane
a tejorāśiṃ mahātmānaṃ balaugham amitaujasam
c bhīmaṃ pradarśanenāpi bhīmasenaṃ janārdana
e taṃ mamācakṣva vārṣṇeya katham adya vṛkodaraḥ
a āste parighabāhuḥ sa madhyamaḥ pāṇḍavo 'cyuta
c arjunenārjuno yaḥ sa kṛṣṇa bāhusahasriṇā
e dvibāhuḥ spardhate nityam atītenāpi keśava
a kṣipaty ekena vegena pañca bāṇaśatāni yaḥ
c iṣvastre sadṛśo rājñaḥ kārtavīryasya pāṇḍavaḥ
a tejasādityasadṛśo maharṣipratimo dame
c kṣamayā pṛthivītulyo mahendrasamavikramaḥ
a ādhirājyaṃ mahad dīptaṃ prathitaṃ madhusūdana
c āhṛtaṃ yena vīryeṇa kurūṇāṃ sarvarājasu
a yasya bāhubalaṃ ghoraṃ kauravāḥ paryupāsate
c sa sarvarathināṃ śreṣṭhaḥ pāṇḍavaḥ satyavikramaḥ
d yaṃ gatvābhimukhaḥ saṃkhye na jīvan kaś cid āvrajet
d yo jetā sarvabhūtānām ajeyo jiṣṇur acyuta
a yo 'pāśrayaḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ devānām iva vāsavaḥ
c sa te bhrātā sakhā caiva katham adya dhanaṃjayaḥ
a dayāvān sarvabhūteṣu hrīniṣedho mahāstravit
c mṛduś ca sukumāraś ca dhārmikaś ca priyaś ca me
a sahadevo maheṣvāsaḥ śūraḥ samitiśobhanaḥ
c bhrātṝṇāṃ kṛṣṇa śuśrūṣur dharmārthakuśalo yuvā
a sadaiva sahadevasya bhrātaro madhusūdana
c vṛttaṃ kalyāṇavṛttasya pūjayanti mahātmanaḥ
a jyeṣṭhāpacāyinaṃ vīraṃ sahadevaṃ yudhāṃ patim
c śuśrūṣuṃ mama vārṣṇeya mādrīputraṃ pracakṣva me
a sukumāro yuvā śūro darśanīyaś ca pāṇḍavaḥ
c bhrātṝṇāṃ kṛṣṇa sarveṣāṃ priyaḥ prāṇo bahiścaraḥ
a citrayodhī ca nakulo maheṣvāso mahābalaḥ
c kaccit sa kuśalī kṛṣṇa vatso mama sukhaidhitaḥ
a sukhocitam aduḥkhārhaṃ sukumāraṃ mahāratham
c api jātu mahābāho paśyeyaṃ nakulaṃ punaḥ
a pakṣmasaṃpātaje kāle nakulena vinākṛtā
c na labhāmi sukhaṃ vīra sādya jīvāmi paśya mām
a sarvaiḥ putraiḥ priyatamā draupadī me janārdana
c kulīnā śīlasaṃpannā sarvaiḥ samuditā guṇaiḥ
d putrī drupadarājasya vikhyātā satyavādinī
a putralokāt patilokān vṛṇvānā satyavādinī
c priyān putrān parityajya pāṇḍavān anvapadyata
a mahābhijanasaṃpannā sarvakāmaiḥ supūjitā
c īśvarī sarvakalyāṇī draupadī katham acyuta
a patibhiḥ pañcabhiḥ śūrair agnikalpaiḥ prahāribhiḥ
c upapannā maheṣvāsair draupadī duḥkhabhāginī
a caturdaśam imaṃ varṣaṃ yan nāpaśyam ariṃdama
c putrādhibhiḥ paridyūnāṃ draupadīṃ satyavādinīm
a na nūnaṃ karmabhiḥ puṇyair aśnute puruṣaḥ sukham
c draupadī cet tathāvṛttā nāśnute sukham avyayam
a na priyo mama kṛṣṇāya bībhatsur na yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c bhīmaseno yamau vāpi yad apaśyaṃ sabhāgatām
a na me duḥkhataraṃ kiṃ cid bhūtapūrvaṃ tato 'dhikam
c yad draupadīṃ nivātasthāṃ śvaśurāṇāṃ samīpagām
a ānāyitām anāryeṇa krodhalobhānuvartinā
c sarve praikṣanta kurava ekavastrāṃ sabhāgatām
a tatraiva dhṛtarāṣṭraś ca mahārājaś ca bāhlikaḥ
c kṛpaś ca somadattaś ca nirviṇṇāḥ kuravas tathā
a tasyāṃ saṃsadi sarvasyāṃ kṣattāraṃ pūjayāmy aham
c vṛttena hi bhavaty āryo na dhanena na vidyayā
a tasya kṛṣṇa mahābuddher gambhīrasya mahātmanaḥ
c kṣattuḥ śīlam alaṃkāro lokān viṣṭabhya tiṣṭhati
a sā śokārtā ca hṛṣṭā ca dṛṣṭvā govindam āgatam
c nānāvidhāni duḥkhāni sarvāṇy evānvakīrtayat
d janmaprabhṛti saṃprāptaṃ duḥkhaṃ nānāvidhaṃ bahu
d aśrupūrṇamukhī khinnā sarvaṃ caivānvacintayat
a pūrvair ācaritaṃ yat tat kurājabhir ariṃdama
c akṣadyūtaṃ mṛgavadhaḥ kaccid eṣāṃ sukhāvaham
d tan naḥ kleśatamaṃ me syāt putraiḥ saha paraṃtapa
a tan māṃ dahati yat kṛṣṇā sabhāyāṃ kurusaṃnidhau
c dhārtarāṣṭraiḥ parikliṣṭā yathā nakuśalaṃ tathā
a nirvāsanaṃ ca nagarāt pravrajyā ca paraṃtapa
c nānāvidhānāṃ duḥkhānām āvāso 'smi janārdana
e ajñātacaryā bālānām avarodhaś ca keśava
a na sma kleśatamaṃ me syāt putraiḥ saha paraṃtapa
c duryodhanena nikṛtā varṣam adya caturdaśam
a duḥkhād api sukhaṃ na syād yadi puṇyaphalakṣayaḥ
c na me viśeṣo jātv āsīd dhārtarāṣṭreṣu pāṇḍavaiḥ
a tena satyena kṛṣṇa tvāṃ hatāmitraṃ śriyā vṛtam
c asmād vimuktaṃ saṃgrāmāt paśyeyaṃ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha
e naiva śakyāḥ parājetuṃ sattvaṃ hy eṣāṃ tathāgatam
a pitaraṃ tv eva garheyaṃ nātmānaṃ na suyodhanam
c yenāhaṃ kuntibhojāya dhanaṃ dhūrtair ivārpitā
a bālāṃ mām āryakas tubhyaṃ krīḍantīṃ kanduhastakām
c adadāt kuntibhojāya sakhā sakhye mahātmane
a sāhaṃ pitrā ca nikṛtā śvaśuraiś ca paraṃtapa
c atyantaduḥkhitā kṛṣṇa kiṃ jīvitaphalaṃ mama
a yan mā vāg abravīn naktaṃ sūtake savyasācinaḥ
c putras te pṛthivīṃ jetā yaśaś cāsya divaṃ spṛśet
a hatvā kurūn grāmajanye rājyaṃ prāpya dhanaṃjayaḥ
c bhrātṛbhiḥ saha kaunteyas trīn medhān āhariṣyati
a nāhaṃ tām abhyasūyāmi namo dharmāya vedhase
c kṛṣṇāya mahate nityaṃ dharmo dhārayati prajāḥ
a dharmaś ced asti vārṣṇeya tathā satyaṃ bhaviṣyati
c tvaṃ cāpi tat tathā kṛṣṇa sarvaṃ saṃpādayiṣyasi
a na māṃ mādhava vaidhavyaṃ nārthanāśo na vairitā
c tathā śokāya bhavati yathā putrair vinābhavaḥ
a yāhaṃ gāṇḍīvadhanvānaṃ sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varam
c dhanaṃjayaṃ na paśyāmi kā śāntir hṛdayasya me
a idaṃ caturdaśaṃ varṣaṃ yan nāpaśyaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
c dhanaṃjayaṃ ca govinda yamau taṃ ca vṛkodaram
a jīvanāśaṃ pranaṣṭānāṃ śrāddhaṃ kurvanti mānavāḥ
c arthatas te mama mṛtās teṣāṃ cāhaṃ janārdana
a brūyā mādhava rājānaṃ dharmātmānaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
c bhūyāṃs te hīyate dharmo mā putraka vṛthā kṛthāḥ
a parāśrayā vāsudeva yā jīvāmi dhig astu mām
c vṛtteḥ kṛpaṇalabdhāyā apratiṣṭhaiva jyāyasī
a atho dhanaṃjayaṃ brūyā nityodyuktaṃ vṛkodaram
c yadarthaṃ kṣatriyā sūte tasya kālo 'yam āgataḥ
a asmiṃś ced āgate kāle kālo vo 'tikramiṣyati
c lokasaṃbhāvitāḥ santaḥ sunṛśaṃsaṃ kariṣyatha
a nṛśaṃsena ca vo yuktāṃs tyajeyaṃ śāśvatīḥ samāḥ
c kāle hi samanuprāpte tyaktavyam api jīvitam
a mādrīputrau ca vaktavyau kṣatradharmaratau sadā
c vikrameṇārjitān bhogān vṛṇītaṃ jīvitād api
a vikramādhigatā hy arthāḥ kṣatradharmeṇa jīvataḥ
c mano manuṣyasya sadā prīṇanti puruṣottama
a gatvā brūhi mahābāho sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varam
c arjunaṃ pāṇḍavaṃ vīraṃ draupadyāḥ padavīṃ cara
a viditau hi tavātyantaṃ kruddhāv iva yathāntakau
c bhīmārjunau nayetāṃ hi devān api parāṃ gatim
a tayoś caitad avajñānaṃ yat sā kṛṣṇā sabhāṃ gatā
c duḥśāsanaś ca karṇaś ca paruṣāṇy abhyabhāṣatām
a duryodhano bhīmasenam abhyagacchan manasvinam
c paśyatāṃ kurumukhyānāṃ tasya drakṣyati yat phalam
a na hi vairaṃ samāsādya praśāmyati vṛkodaraḥ
c sucirād api bhīmasya na hi vairaṃ praśāmyati
e yāvadantaṃ na nayati śātravāñ śatrukarśanaḥ
f tāvad eva mahābāhur niśāsu na sukhaṃ labhet
a na duḥkhaṃ rājyaharaṇaṃ na ca dyūte parājayaḥ
c pravrājanaṃ ca putrāṇāṃ na me tad duḥkhakāraṇam
d paśyatāṃ kuruputrāṇāṃ na me tad duḥkhakāraṇam
a yat tu sā bṛhatī śyāmā ekavastrā sabhāṃ gatā
c aśṛṇot paruṣā vācas tato duḥkhataraṃ nu kim
a strīdharmiṇī varārohā kṣatradharmaratā sadā
c nādhyagacchat tathā nāthaṃ kṛṣṇā nāthavatī satī
d sa tv asyā devaputrāyās tvaṃ nātho madhusūdana
a yasyā mama saputrāyās tvaṃ nātho madhusūdana
c rāmaś ca balināṃ śreṣṭhaḥ pradyumnaś ca mahārathaḥ
a sāham evaṃvidhaṃ duḥkhaṃ sahe 'dya puruṣottama
c bhīme jīvati durdharṣe vijaye cāpalāyini
a tata āśvāsayām āsa putrādhibhir abhiplutām
c pitṛṣvasāraṃ śocantīṃ śauriḥ pārthasakhaḥ pṛthām
a kā nu sīmantinī tvādṛg lokeṣv asti pitṛṣvasaḥ
c śūrasya rājño duhitā ājamīḍhakulaṃ gatā
a mahākulīnā bhavatī hradād dhradam ivāgatā
c īśvarī sarvakalyāṇī bhartrā paramapūjitā
a vīrasūr vīrapatnī ca sarvaiḥ samuditā guṇaiḥ
c sukhaduḥkhe mahāprājñe tvādṛśī soḍhum arhati
a nidrātandrī krodhaharṣau kṣutpipāse himātapau
c etāni pārthā nirjitya nityaṃ vīrāḥ sukhe ratāḥ
a tyaktagrāmyasukhāḥ pārthā nityaṃ vīrasukhapriyāḥ
c na te svalpena tuṣyeyur mahotsāhā mahābalāḥ
a antaṃ dhīrā niṣevante madhyaṃ grāmyasukhapriyāḥ
c uttamāṃś ca parikleśān bhogāṃś cātīva mānuṣān
a anteṣu remire dhīrā na te madhyeṣu remire
c antaprāptiṃ sukhām āhur duḥkham antaram antayoḥ
a abhivādayanti bhavatīṃ pāṇḍavāḥ saha kṛṣṇayā
c ātmānaṃ ca kuśalinaṃ nivedyāhur anāmayam
a arogān sarvasiddhārthān kṣipraṃ drakṣyasi pāṇḍavān
c īśvarān sarvalokasya hatāmitrāñ śriyā vṛtān
a evam āśvāsitā kuntī pratyuvāca janārdanam
c putrādhibhir abhidhvastā nigṛhyābuddhijaṃ tamaḥ
a yad yat teṣāṃ mahābāho pathyaṃ syān madhusūdana
c yathā yathā tvaṃ manyethāḥ kuryāḥ kṛṣṇa tathā tathā
a avilopena dharmasya anikṛtyā paraṃtapa
c prabhāvajñāsmi te kṛṣṇa satyasyābhijanasya ca
a vyavasthāyāṃ ca mitreṣu buddhivikramayos tathā
c tvam eva naḥ kule dharmas tvaṃ satyaṃ tvaṃ tapo mahat
a tvaṃ trātā tvaṃ mahad brahma tvayi sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam
c yathaivāttha tathaivaitat tvayi satyaṃ bhaviṣyati
d kurūṇāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ ca lokānāṃ cāparājita
d sarvasyaitasya vārṣṇeya gatis tvam asi mādhava
d prabhāvaṃ buddhivīryaṃ ca tādṛśaṃ tava keśava
a tām āmantrya ca govindaḥ kṛtvā cābhipradakṣiṇam
c prātiṣṭhata mahābāhur duryodhanagṛhān prati
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a pṛthām āmantrya govindaḥ kṛtvā cāpi pradakṣiṇam
c duryodhanagṛhaṃ śaurir abhyagacchad ariṃdamaḥ
a lakṣmyā paramayā yuktaṃ puraṃdaragṛhopamam
b vicitrair āsanair yuktaṃ praviveśa janārdanaḥ
c tasya kakṣyā vyatikramya tisro dvāḥsthair avāritaḥ
a tato 'bhraghanasaṃkāśaṃ girikūṭam ivocchritam
c śriyā jvalantaṃ prāsādam āruroha mahāyaśāḥ
a tatra rājasahasraiś ca kurubhiś cābhisaṃvṛtam
c dhārtarāṣṭraṃ mahābāhuṃ dadarśāsīnam āsane
a duḥśāsanaṃ ca karṇaṃ ca śakuniṃ cāpi saubalam
c duryodhanasamīpe tān āsanasthān dadarśa saḥ
a abhyāgacchati dāśārhe dhārtarāṣṭro mahāyaśāḥ
c udatiṣṭhat sahāmātyaḥ pūjayan madhusūdanam
a sametya dhārtarāṣṭreṇa sahāmātyena keśavaḥ
c rājabhis tatra vārṣṇeyaḥ samāgacchad yathāvayaḥ
a tatra jāmbūnadamayaṃ paryaṅkaṃ supariṣkṛtam
c vividhāstaraṇāstīrṇam abhyupāviśad acyutaḥ
a tasmin gāṃ madhuparkaṃ ca upahṛtya janārdane
c nivedayām āsa tadā gṛhān rājyaṃ ca kauravaḥ
d āsanaṃ sarvatobhadraṃ sarvaratnavibhūṣitam
d kṛṣṇārtham eva saṃsiddhaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrasya śāsanāt
a tatra govindam āsīnaṃ prasannādityavarcasam
c upāsāṃ cakrire sarve kuravo rājabhiḥ saha
a tato duryodhano rājā vārṣṇeyaṃ jayatāṃ varam
c nyamantrayad bhojanena nābhyanandac ca keśavaḥ
c   nābhyanandaj janārdanaḥ
c punaḥ punaḥ kauraveyo bhojanena nyamantrayat
c asakṛt prārthyamāno 'pi
a tato duryodhanaḥ kṛṣṇam abravīd rājasaṃsadi
c mṛdupūrvaṃ śaṭhodarkaṃ karṇam ābhāṣya kauravaḥ
a kasmād annāni pānāni vāsāṃsi śayanāni ca
c tvadartham upanītāni nāgrahīs tvaṃ janārdana
a ubhayoś cādadaḥ sāhyam ubhayoś ca hite rataḥ
c saṃbandhī dayitaś cāsi dhṛtarāṣṭrasya mādhava
a tvaṃ hi govinda dharmārthau vettha tattvena sarvaśaḥ
c tatra kāraṇam icchāmi śrotuṃ cakragadādhara
a sa evam ukto govindaḥ pratyuvāca mahāmanāḥ
c oghameghasvanaḥ kāle pragṛhya vipulaṃ bhujam
a anambūkṛtam agrastam anirastam asaṃkulam
c rājīvanetro rājānaṃ hetumadvākyam uttamam
a kṛtārthā bhuñjate dūtāḥ pūjāṃ gṛhṇanti caiva hi
c kṛtārthaṃ māṃ sahāmātyas tvam arciṣyasi bhārata
a evam uktaḥ pratyuvāca dhārtarāṣṭro janārdanam
c na yuktaṃ bhavatāsmāsu pratipattum asāṃpratam
a kṛtārthaṃ cākṛtārthaṃ ca tvāṃ vayaṃ madhusūdana
c yatāmahe pūjayituṃ govinda na ca śaknumaḥ
a na ca tat kāraṇaṃ vidmo yasmin no madhusūdana
c pūjāṃ kṛtāṃ prīyamāṇair nāmaṃsthāḥ puruṣottama
a vairaṃ no nāsti bhavatā govinda na ca vigrahaḥ
c sa bhavān prasamīkṣyaitan nedṛśaṃ vaktum arhati
a evam uktaḥ pratyuvāca dhārtarāṣṭraṃ janārdanaḥ
c abhivīkṣya sahāmātyaṃ dāśārhaḥ prahasann iva
a nāhaṃ kāmān na saṃrambhān na dveṣān nārthakāraṇāt
c na hetuvādāl lobhād vā dharmaṃ jahyāṃ kathaṃ cana
d pūjāṃ kṛtāṃ prīyamāṇo ko vidvāṃs tyaktum arhati
a saṃprītibhojyāny annāni āpadbhojyāni vā punaḥ
c na ca saṃprīyase rājan na cāpy āpadgatā vayam
a akasmād dviṣase rājañ janmaprabhṛti pāṇḍavān
c priyānuvartino bhrātṝn sarvaiḥ samuditān guṇaiḥ
a akasmāc caiva pārthānāṃ dveṣaṇaṃ nopapadyate
c dharme sthitāḥ pāṇḍaveyāḥ kas tān kiṃ vaktum arhati
a yas tān dveṣṭi sa māṃ dveṣṭi yas tān anu sa mām anu
c aikātmyaṃ māṃ gataṃ viddhi pāṇḍavair dharmacāribhiḥ
a kāmakrodhānuvartī hi yo mohād virurutsate
c guṇavantaṃ ca yo dveṣṭi tam āhuḥ puruṣādhamam
a yaḥ kalyāṇaguṇāñ jñātīn mohāl lobhād didṛkṣate
c so 'jitātmājitakrodho na ciraṃ tiṣṭhati śriyam
a atha yo guṇasaṃpannān hṛdayasyāpriyān api
c priyeṇa kurute vaśyāṃś ciraṃ yaśasi tiṣṭhati
d dviṣadannaṃ na bhoktavyaṃ dviṣantaṃ naiva bhojayet
d pāṇḍavān dviṣase rājan mama prāṇā hi pāṇḍavāḥ
a sarvam etad abhoktavyam annaṃ duṣṭābhisaṃhitam
c kṣattur ekasya bhoktavyam iti me dhīyate matiḥ
a evam uktvā mahābāhur duryodhanam amarṣaṇam
c niścakrāma tataḥ śubhrād dhārtarāṣṭraniveśanāt
a niryāya ca mahābāhur vāsudevo mahāmanāḥ
c niveśāya yayau veśma vidurasya mahātmanaḥ
a tam abhyagacchad droṇaś ca kṛpo bhīṣmo 'tha bāhlikaḥ
c kuravaś ca mahābāhuṃ vidurasya gṛhe sthitam
a te 'bhigamyābruvaṃs tatra kuravo madhusūdanam
c nivedayāmo vārṣṇeya saratnāṃs te gṛhānvayam
a tān uvāca mahātejāḥ kauravān madhusūdanaḥ
c sarve bhavanto gacchantu sarvā me 'pacitiḥ kṛtā
d na nītir asmat pūjā vo bhavatāṃ kurusattamāḥ
d duryodhanaś ca yuṣmāsu na ca prītiṃ kariṣyati
d ta evam uktāḥ kṛṣṇena evam astv iti niryayuḥ
a yāteṣu kuruṣu kṣattā dāśārham aparājitam
c abhyarcayām āsa tadā sarvakāmaiḥ prayatnavān
a tataḥ kṣattānnapānāni śucīni guṇavanti ca
c upāharad anekāni keśavāya mahātmane
a tair tarpayitvā prathamaṃ brāhmaṇān madhusūdanaḥ
c vedavidbhyo dadau kṛṣṇaḥ paramadraviṇāny api
d bhuktavatsu dvijendreṣu niṣaṇṇasya varāsane
d śuciḥ suprayato bhūtvā viduro 'nnam upāharat
d śraddhayā parayā yukta idaṃ vacanam abravīt
d saṃbhramais tuṣya govinda etan naḥ paramaṃ dhanam
d anyathā vā viśeṣeṇa kas tvām arcitum arhati
d udārasya tṛṇaṃ vittaṃ śūrasya maraṇaṃ tṛṇam
d viraktasya tṛṇaṃ nārī niḥspṛhasya tṛṇaṃ jagat
d taṃ bhuktavantaṃ vividhāḥ suśabdāḥ sūtamāgadhāḥ
d abhituṣṭuvur āsīnaṃ dāśārham aparājitam
a tato 'nuyāyibhiḥ sārdhaṃ marudbhir iva vāsavaḥ
c vidurānnāni bubhuje śucīni guṇavanti ca
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a taṃ bhuktavantam āśvastaṃ niśāyāṃ viduro 'bravīt
b mahātmāno yam icchanti tapaḥ kṛtvā tv anekadhā
b sa devo 'sya samāyāto mama locanagocare
b tavātithyaṃ jagannātha kiṃ karomy adya keśava
b kṛṣṇa uvāca
b aham asmi mahīpīṭhe nirdhanānāṃ śiromaṇiḥ
b sādhu sādhu mahāprājña sarvaśāstraviśārada
b yas tvaṃ vinayasaṃpanno vayas tvayy eva dṛśyate
b tavādya vacasā tuṣye dadāmi kurunandana
b vidura uvāca
b varaṃ vṛṇīṣva dāsye 'haṃ yat te manasi rocate
b acalā keśave bhaktir mānasaṃ tvadgataṃ sadā
b dharme cintā kule janma dehi me madhusūdana
b mā matiḥ paradravyeṣu paradāreṣu mā matiḥ
b parāpavādinī jihvā mā bhūd deva kadā cana
b āsanaṃ sutasaṃkīrṇaṃ viprasaṃkīrṇamandiram
b hṛdayaṃ śāstrasaṃkīrṇaṃ dehi me madhusūdana
b durbhikṣe cānnadātāhaṃ subhikṣe ca hiraṇyadaḥ
b āture 'haṃ bhayatrātā trīṇi kṛṣṇa bhavantu me
b satyaṃ śaucaṃ dayā dānaṃ bhaktiś caiva janārdane
b etān varān ahaṃ yāce yadi tuṣṭo 'si mādhava
c nedaṃ samyag vyavasitaṃ keśavāgamanaṃ tava
a arthadharmātigo mūḍhaḥ saṃrambhī ca janārdana
c mānaghno mānakāmaś ca vṛddhānāṃ śāsanātigaḥ
a dharmaśāstrātigo mando durātmā pragrahaṃ gataḥ
c aneyaḥ śreyasāṃ pāpo dhārtarāṣṭro janārdana
a kāmātmā prājñamānī ca mitradhruk sarvaśaṅkitaḥ
c akartā cākṛtajñaś ca tyaktadharmaḥ priyānṛtaḥ
d mūḍhaś cākṛtabuddhiś ca indriyāṇām anīśvaraḥ
d kāmānusārī kṛtyeṣu sarveṣv akṛtaniścayaḥ
a etaiś cānyaiś ca bahubhir doṣair eṣa samanvitaḥ
c tvayocyamānaḥ śreyo 'pi saṃrambhān na grahīṣyati
a senāsamudayaṃ dṛṣṭvā pārthivaṃ madhusūdana
c kṛtārthaṃ manyate bāla ātmānam avicakṣaṇaḥ
a ekaḥ karṇaḥ parāñ jetuṃ samartha iti niścitam
c dhārtarāṣṭrasya durbuddheḥ sa śamaṃ nopayāsyati
a bhīṣme droṇe kṛpe karṇe droṇaputre jayadrathe
c bhūyasīṃ vartate vṛttiṃ na śame kurute manaḥ
a niścitaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ sakarṇānāṃ janārdana
c bhīṣmadroṇakṛpān pārthā na śaktāḥ prativīkṣitum
a saṃvic ca dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ sarveṣām eva keśava
c śame prayatamānasya tava saubhrātrakāṅkṣiṇaḥ
a na pāṇḍavānām asmābhiḥ pratideyaṃ yathocitam
c iti vyavasitās teṣu vacanaṃ syān nirarthakam
a yatra sūktaṃ duruktaṃ ca samaṃ syān madhusūdana
c na tatra pralapet prājño badhireṣv iva gāyanaḥ
a avijānatsu mūḍheṣu nirmaryādeṣu mādhava
c na tvaṃ vākyaṃ bruvan yuktaś cāṇḍāleṣu dvijo yathā
a so 'yaṃ balastho mūḍhaś ca na kariṣyati te vacaḥ
c tasmin nirarthakaṃ vākyam uktaṃ saṃpatsyate tava
a teṣāṃ samupaviṣṭānāṃ sarveṣāṃ pāpacetasām
c tava madhyāvataraṇaṃ mama kṛṣṇa na rocate
a durbuddhīnām aśiṣṭānāṃ bahūnāṃ pāpacetasām
c pratīpaṃ vacanaṃ madhye tava kṛṣṇa na rocate
a anupāsitavṛddhatvāc chriyā mohāc ca darpitaḥ
c vayodarpād amarṣāc ca na te śreyo grahīṣyati
a balaṃ balavad apy asya yadi vakṣyasi mādhava
c tvayy asya mahatī śaṅkā na kariṣyati te vacaḥ
d mānī maurkhyeṇa pārthānāṃ na paśyaty adhikaṃ balam
a nedam adya yudhā śakyam indreṇāpi sahāmaraiḥ
c iti vyavasitāḥ sarve dhārtarāṣṭrā janārdana
a teṣv evam upapanneṣu kāmakrodhānuvartiṣu
c samartham api te vākyam asamarthaṃ bhaviṣyati
a madhye tiṣṭhan hastyanīkasya mando
rathāśvayuktasya balasya mūḍhaḥ
c duryodhano manyate vītamanyuḥ
kṛtsnā mayeyaṃ pṛthivī jiteti
a āśaṃsate dhṛtarāṣṭrasya putro
mahārājyam asapatnaṃ pṛthivyām
c tasmiñ śamaḥ kevalo nopalabhyo
baddhaṃ santam āgataṃ manyate 'rtham
a paryasteyaṃ pṛthivī kālapakvā
duryodhanārthe pāṇḍavān yoddhukāmāḥ
c samāgatāḥ sarvayodhāḥ pṛthivyāṃ
rājānaś ca kṣitipālaiḥ sametāḥ
a sarve caite kṛtavairāḥ purastāt
tvayā rājāno hṛtasārāś ca kṛṣṇa
c tavodvegāt saṃśritā dhārtarāṣṭrān
susaṃhatāḥ saha karṇena vīrāḥ
a tyaktātmānaḥ saha duryodhanena
sṛṣṭā yoddhuṃ pāṇḍavān sarvayodhāḥ
b mṛtyur jayo veti kṛtaikabhāvāḥ
b kāmātmāno manyuvaśāvinītāḥ
c teṣāṃ madhye praviśethā yadi tvaṃ
na tan mataṃ mama dāśārha vīra
a teṣāṃ samupaviṣṭānāṃ bahūnāṃ duṣṭacetasām
c kathaṃ madhyaṃ prapadyethāḥ śatrūṇāṃ śatrukarśana
a sarvathā tvaṃ mahābāho devair api durutsahaḥ
c prabhāvaṃ pauruṣaṃ buddhiṃ jānāmi tava śatruhan
a yā me prītiḥ pāṇḍaveṣu bhūyaḥ sā tvayi mādhava
c premṇā ca bahumānāc ca sauhṛdāc ca bravīmy aham
d yā me prītiḥ puṣkarākṣa tvaddarśanasamudbhavā
d sā kim ākhyāyate tubhyam antarātmāsi dehinām
 vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
 vidurasya vacaḥ śrutvā praśritaṃ puruṣottamaḥ
 idaṃ hovāca vacanaṃ bhagavān madhusūdanaḥ
 bhagavān uvāca
a yathā brūyān mahāprājño yathā brūyād vicakṣaṇaḥ
c yathā vācyas tvadvidhena suhṛdā madvidhaḥ suhṛt
a dharmārthayuktaṃ tathyaṃ ca yathā tvayy upapadyate
c tathā vacanam ukto 'smi tvayaitat pitṛmātṛvat
a satyaṃ prāptaṃ ca yuktaṃ cāpy evam eva yathāttha mām
c śṛṇuṣvāgamane hetuṃ vidurāvahito bhava
a daurātmyaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrasya kṣatriyāṇāṃ ca vairitām
c sarvam etad ahaṃ jānan kṣattaḥ prāpto 'dya kauravān
a paryastāṃ pṛthivīṃ sarvāṃ sāśvāṃ sarathakuñjarām
c yo mocayen mṛtyupāśāt prāpnuyād dharmam uttamam
a dharmakāryaṃ yatañ śaktyā na cec chaknoti mānavaḥ
c prāpto bhavati tat puṇyam atra me nāsti saṃśayaḥ
a manasā cintayan pāpaṃ karmaṇā nābhirocayan
c na prāpnoti phalaṃ tasya evaṃ dharmavido viduḥ
a so 'haṃ yatiṣye praśamaṃ kṣattaḥ kartum amāyayā
c kurūṇāṃ sṛñjayānāṃ ca saṃgrāme vinaśiṣyatām
a seyam āpan mahāghorā kuruṣv eva samutthitā
c karṇaduryodhanakṛtā sarve hy ete tadanvayāḥ
a vyasanaiḥ kliśyamānaṃ hi yo mitraṃ nābhipadyate
c anunīya yathāśakti taṃ nṛśaṃsaṃ vidur budhāḥ
a ā keśagrahaṇān mitram akāryāt saṃnivartayan
c avācyaḥ kasya cid bhavati kṛtayatno yathābalam
a tat samarthaṃ śubhaṃ vākyaṃ dharmārthasahitaṃ hitam
c dhārtarāṣṭraḥ sahāmātyo grahītuṃ vidurārhati
a hitaṃ hi dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ tathaiva ca
c pṛthivyāṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ ca yatiṣye 'ham amāyayā
a hite prayatamānaṃ māṃ śaṅked duryodhano yadi
c hṛdayasya ca me prītir ānṛṇyaṃ ca bhaviṣyati
a jñātīnāṃ hi mitho bhede yan mitraṃ nābhipadyate
c sarvayatnena madhyasthaṃ na tan mitraṃ vidur budhāḥ
a na māṃ brūyur adharmajñā mūḍhā asuhṛdas tathā
c śakto nāvārayat kṛṣṇaḥ saṃrabdhān kurupāṇḍavān
a ubhayoḥ sādhayann artham aham āgata ity uta
c tatra yatnam ahaṃ kṛtvā gaccheyaṃ nṛṣv avācyatām
a mama dharmārthayuktaṃ hi śrutvā vākyam anāmayam
c na ced ādāsyate bālo diṣṭasya vaśam eṣyati
a ahāpayan pāṇḍavārthaṃ yathāvac
chamaṃ kurūṇāṃ yadi cācareyam
c puṇyaṃ ca me syāc caritaṃ mahārthaṃ
mucyeraṃś ca kuravo mṛtyupāśāt
a api vācaṃ bhāṣamāṇasya kāvyāṃ
dharmārāmām arthavatīm ahiṃsrām
c avekṣeran dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ samarthāṃ
māṃ ca prāptaṃ kuravaḥ pūjayeyuḥ
a na cāpi mama paryāptāḥ sahitāḥ sarvapārthivāḥ
c kruddhasya pramukhe sthātuṃ siṃhasyevetare mṛgāḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a ity evam uktvā vacanaṃ vṛṣṇīnām ṛṣabhas tadā
c śayane sukhasaṃsparśe śiśye yadusukhāvahaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tathā kathayator eva tayor buddhimatos tadā
c śivā nakṣatrasaṃpannā sā vyatīyāya śarvarī
a dharmārthakāmayuktāś ca vicitrārthapadākṣarāḥ
c śṛṇvato vividhā vāco vidurasya mahātmanaḥ
a kathābhir anurūpābhiḥ kṛṣṇasyāmitatejasaḥ
c akāmasyeva kṛṣṇasya sā vyatīyāya śarvarī
a tatas tu svarasaṃpannā bahavaḥ sūtamāgadhāḥ
c śaṅkhadundubhinirghoṣaiḥ keśavaṃ pratyabodhayan
d brahmādivasudevāntaṃ vaṃśaṃ samanukīrtayan
d tuṣṭuvuḥ keśavaṃ tatra bahavaḥ sūtamāgadhāḥ
a tata utthāya dāśārha ṛṣabhaḥ sarvasātvatām
c sarvam āvaśyakaṃ cakre prātaḥkāryaṃ janārdanaḥ
a kṛtodakāryajapyaḥ sa hutāgniḥ samalaṃkṛtaḥ
c tata ādityam udyantam upātiṣṭhata mādhavaḥ
a atha duryodhanaḥ kṛṣṇaṃ śakuniś cāpi saubalaḥ
c saṃdhyāṃ tiṣṭhantam abhyetya dāśārham aparājitam
a ācakṣetāṃ tu kṛṣṇasya dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ sabhāgatam
c kurūṃś ca bhīṣmapramukhān rājñaḥ sarvāṃś ca pārthivān
a tvām arthayante govinda divi śakram ivāmarāḥ
c tāv abhyanandad govindaḥ sāmnā paramavalgunā
d tān abhyanandad govindaḥ sāmnā paramavalgunā
d te 'bhyarcya devakīputraṃ divi śakram ivāmarāḥ
a tato vimala āditye brāhmaṇebhyo janārdanaḥ
c dadau hiraṇyaṃ vāsāṃsi gāś cāśvāṃś ca paraṃtapaḥ
a visṛṣṭavantaṃ ratnāni dāśārham aparājitam
c tiṣṭhantam upasaṃgamya vavande sārathis tadā
d tato rathena śubhreṇa mahatā kiṅkiṇīkinā
d hayottamayujā śīghram upātiṣṭhata dārukaḥ
d tasmai rathavaro yuktaḥ śuśubhe lokaviśrutaḥ
d vājibhiḥ sainyasugrīvameghapuṣpabalāhakaiḥ
d sainyas tu śukapatrābhaḥ sugrīvaḥ kiṃśukaprabhaḥ
d meghapuṣpo meghavarṇaḥ pāṇḍaras tu balāhakaḥ
d dakṣiṇaṃ cāvahat sainyaḥ sugrīvaḥ savyato 'vahat
d pṛṣṭhavāhau tayor āstāṃ meghapuṣpabalāhakau
d viśvakarmakṛtāpīḍā ratnajālavibhūṣitā
d āśritā vai rathe tasmin dhvajayaṣṭir aśobhata
d vainateyaḥ sthitas tasyāṃ prabhākaram iva spṛśan
d tasya sattvavataḥ ketau bhujagārir aśobhata
d tasya kīrtimatas tena bhāsvareṇa virājatā
d śuśubhe syandanaśreṣṭhaḥ patagendreṇa ketunā
d rukmajālaiḥ patākābhiḥ sauvarṇena ca ketunā
d babhūva sa rathaśreṣṭhaḥ kālasūrya ivoditaḥ
d pakṣidhvajavitānaiś ca rukmajālakṛtāntaraiḥ
d daṇḍamārgavibhāgaiś ca sukṛtair viśvakarmaṇā
d pravālamaṇihemaiś ca muktāvaiḍūryabhūṣaṇaiḥ
d kiṅkiṇīśatasaṃghaiś ca vālajālakṛtāntaraiḥ
d kārtasvaramayībhiś ca padminībhir alaṃkṛtaḥ
d śuśubhe syandanaśreṣṭhas tāpanīyaiś ca pādapaiḥ
d vyāghrasiṃhavarāhaiś ca govṛṣair mṛgapakṣibhiḥ
d tārābhir bhāskaraiś cāpi vāraṇaiś ca hiraṇmayaiḥ
d vajrāṅkuśavimānaiś ca kūbarāvartasaṃdhiṣu
d samucchritamahānābhiḥ stanayitnumahāsvanaḥ
a tam upasthitam ājñāya rathaṃ divyaṃ mahāmanāḥ
c mahābhraghananirghoṣaṃ sarvaratnavibhūṣitam
a agniṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā brāhmaṇāṃś ca janārdanaḥ
c kaustubhaṃ maṇim āmucya śriyā paramayā jvalan
a kurubhiḥ saṃvṛtaḥ kṛṣṇo vṛṣṇibhiś cābhirakṣitaḥ
c ātiṣṭhata rathaṃ śauriḥ sarvayādavanandanaḥ
a anvāruroha dāśārhaṃ viduraḥ sarvadharmavit
c sarvaprāṇabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ sarvadharmabhṛtāṃ varam
a tato duryodhanaḥ kṛṣṇaṃ śakuniś cāpi saubalaḥ
c dvitīyena rathenainam anvayātāṃ paraṃtapam
a sātyakiḥ kṛtavarmā ca vṛṣṇīnāṃ ca mahārathāḥ
c pṛṣṭhato 'nuyayuḥ kṛṣṇaṃ rathair aśvair gajair api
a teṣāṃ hemapariṣkārā yuktāḥ paramavājibhiḥ
c gacchatāṃ ghoṣiṇaś citrāś cāru babhrājire rathāḥ
a saṃmṛṣṭasaṃsiktarajaḥ pratipede mahāpatham
c rājarṣicaritaṃ kāle kṛṣṇo dhīmāñ śriyā jvalan
a tataḥ prayāte dāśārhe prāvādyantaikapuṣkarāḥ
c śaṅkhāś ca dadhmire tatra vādyāny anyāni yāni ca
a pravīrāḥ sarvalokasya yuvānaḥ siṃhavikramāḥ
c parivārya rathaṃ śaurer agacchanta paraṃtapāḥ
a tato 'nye bahusāhasrā vicitrādbhutavāsasaḥ
c asiprāsāyudhadharāḥ kṛṣṇasyāsan puraḥsarāḥ
d yodhāḥ paraśuhastāś ca śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
a gajāḥ paraḥśatās tatra varāś cāśvāḥ sahasraśaḥ
c prayāntam anvayur vīraṃ dāśārham aparājitam
a puraṃ kurūṇāṃ saṃvṛttaṃ draṣṭukāmaṃ janārdanam
c savṛddhabālaṃ sastrīkaṃ rathyāgatam ariṃdamam
a vedikāpāśritābhiś ca samākrāntāny anekaśaḥ
c pracalantīva bhāreṇa yoṣidbhir bhavanāny uta
a saṃpūjyamānaḥ kurubhiḥ saṃśṛṇvan vividhāḥ kathāḥ
c yathārhaṃ pratisatkurvan prekṣamāṇaḥ śanair yayau
a tataḥ sabhāṃ samāsādya keśavasyānuyāyinaḥ
c saśaṅkhair veṇunirghoṣair diśaḥ sarvā vyanādayan
a tataḥ sā samitiḥ sarvā rājñām amitatejasām
c saṃprākampata harṣeṇa kṛṣṇāgamanakāṅkṣayā
a tato 'bhyāśagate kṛṣṇe samahṛṣyan narādhipāḥ
c śrutvā taṃ rathanirghoṣaṃ parjanyaninadopamam
a āsādya tu sabhādvāram ṛṣabhaḥ sarvasātvatām
c avatīrya rathāc chauriḥ kailāsaśikharopamāt
a nagameghapratīkāśāṃ jvalantīm iva tejasā
c mahendrasadanaprakhyāṃ praviveśa sabhāṃ tataḥ
a pāṇau gṛhītvā viduraṃ sātyakiṃ ca mahāyaśāḥ
c jyotīṃṣy ādityavad rājan kurūn pracchādayañ śriyā
a agrato vāsudevasya karṇaduryodhanāv ubhau
c vṛṣṇayaḥ kṛtavarmā ca āsan kṛṣṇasya pṛṣṭhataḥ
a dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ puraskṛtya bhīṣmadroṇādayas tataḥ
c āsanebhyo 'calan sarve pūjayanto janārdanam
a abhyāgacchati dāśārhe prajñācakṣur mahāmanāḥ
c sahaiva bhīṣmadroṇābhyām udatiṣṭhan mahāyaśāḥ
a uttiṣṭhati mahārāje dhṛtarāṣṭre janeśvare
c tāni rājasahasrāṇi samuttasthuḥ samantataḥ
a āsanaṃ sarvatobhadraṃ jāmbūnadapariṣkṛtam
c kṛṣṇārthe kalpitaṃ tatra dhṛtarāṣṭrasya śāsanāt
d duryodhana uvāca
d bhīṣmadroṇau parityajya tvayā māṃ madhusūdana
d bhagavān uvāca
d kimarthaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣa kṛtaṃ vṛṣalabhojanam
d bhaktaṃ pṛcchasi rājendra ādaraṃ kiṃ na pṛcchasi
d bhojanaṃ gatajīrṇaṃ tu ādaram ajarāmaram
d ādareṇopanītāni śākāny api phalāni ca
d prīṇanti mama gātrāṇi nāmṛtaṃ mānavarjitam
d varaṃ hālāhalaṃ prītaṃ sadyaḥ prāṇaharaṃ ca yat
d na tu bhuktaṃ dhanāḍhyasya bhruvā kuṭiliteyuṣe sic
d na jātiḥ kāraṇaṃ tāta guṇāḥ kalyāṇakāraṇam
d cāṇḍālam api sadvṛttaṃ taṃ devā brāhmaṇaṃ viduḥ
d kaivartīgarbhasaṃbhūto vyāso nāma mahāmuniḥ
d tapasā brāhmaṇo jātas tasmāj jātir na kāraṇam
a smayamānas tu rājānaṃ bhīṣmadroṇau ca mādhavaḥ
c abhyabhāṣata dharmātmā rājñaś cānyān yathāvayaḥ
a tatra keśavam ānarcuḥ samyag abhyāgataṃ sabhām
c rājānaḥ pārthivāḥ sarve kuravaś ca janārdanam
a tatra tiṣṭhan sa dāśārho rājamadhye paraṃtapaḥ
c apaśyad antarikṣasthān ṛṣīn parapuraṃjayaḥ
a tatas tān abhisaṃprekṣya nāradapramukhān ṛṣīn
c abhyabhāṣata dāśārho bhīṣmaṃ śāṃtanavaṃ śanaiḥ
a pārthivīṃ samitiṃ draṣṭum ṛṣayo 'bhyāgatā nṛpa
c nimantryantām āsanaiś ca satkāreṇa ca bhūyasā
a naiteṣv anupaviṣṭeṣu śakyaṃ kena cid āsitum
c pūjā prayujyatām āśu munīnāṃ bhāvitātmanām
a ṛṣīñ śāṃtanavo dṛṣṭvā sabhādvāram upasthitān
c tvaramāṇas tato bhṛtyān āsanānīty acodayat
a āsanāny atha mṛṣṭāni mahānti vipulāni ca
c maṇikāñcanacitrāṇi samājahrus tatas tataḥ
a teṣu tatropaviṣṭeṣu gṛhītārgheṣu bhārata
c niṣasādāsane kṛṣṇo rājānaś ca yathāsanam
a duḥśāsanaḥ sātyakaye dadāv āsanam uttamam
c viviṃśatir dadau pīṭhaṃ kāñcanaṃ kṛtavarmaṇe
a avidūre 'tha kṛṣṇasya karṇaduryodhanāv ubhau
c ekāsane mahātmānau niṣīdatur amarṣaṇau
a gāndhārarājaḥ śakunir gāndhārair abhirakṣitaḥ
c niṣasādāsane rājā sahaputro viśāṃ pate
a viduro maṇipīṭhe tu śuklaspardhyājinottare
c saṃspṛśann āsanaṃ śaurer mahāmatir upāviśat
a cirasya dṛṣṭvā dāśārhaṃ rājānaḥ sarvapārthivāḥ
c amṛtasyeva nātṛpyan prekṣamāṇā janārdanam
a atasīpuṣpasaṃkāśaḥ pītavāsā janārdanaḥ
c vyabhrājata sabhāmadhye hemnīvopahito maṇiḥ
a tatas tūṣṇīṃ sarvam āsīd govindagatamānasam
c na tatra kaś cit kiṃ cid dhi vyājahāra pumān kva cit
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a teṣv āsīneṣu sarveṣu tūṣṇīṃbhūteṣu rājasu
c vākyam abhyādade kṛṣṇaḥ sudaṃṣṭro dundubhisvanaḥ
a jīmūta iva gharmānte sarvāṃ saṃśrāvayan sabhām
c dhṛtarāṣṭram abhiprekṣya samabhāṣata mādhavaḥ
a kurūṇāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ ca śamaḥ syād iti bhārata
c aprayatnena vīrāṇām etad yatitum āgataḥ
a rājan nānyat pravaktavyaṃ tava niḥśreyasaṃ vacaḥ
c viditaṃ hy eva te sarvaṃ veditavyam ariṃdama
a idam adya kulaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ sarvarājasu pārthiva
b tvan nimittaṃ viśeṣeṇa neha yuktaṃ viśiṣyate
c śrutavṛttopasaṃpannaṃ sarvaiḥ samuditaṃ guṇaiḥ
a kṛpānukampā kāruṇyam ānṛśaṃsyaṃ ca bhārata
c tathārjavaṃ kṣamā satyaṃ kuruṣv etad viśiṣyate
a tasminn evaṃvidhe rājan kule mahati tiṣṭhati
c tvannimittaṃ viśeṣeṇa neha yuktam asāṃpratam
a tvaṃ hi vārayitā śreṣṭhaḥ kurūṇāṃ kurusattama
c mithyā pracaratāṃ tāta bāhyeṣv ābhyantareṣu ca
a te putrās tava kauravya duryodhanapurogamāḥ
c dharmārthau pṛṣṭhataḥ kṛtvā pracaranti nṛśaṃsavat
a aśiṣṭā gatamaryādā lobhena hṛtacetasaḥ
c sveṣu bandhuṣu mukhyeṣu tad vettha bharatarṣabha
a seyam āpan mahāghorā kuruṣv eva samutthitā
c upekṣyamāṇā kauravya pṛthivīṃ ghātayiṣyati
a śakyā ceyaṃ śamayituṃ tvaṃ ced icchasi bhārata
c na duṣkaro hy atra śamo mato me bharatarṣabha
a tvayy adhīnaḥ śamo rājan mayi caiva viśāṃ pate
b sahabhūtās tathaivaite sarvanāśāya bhārata
c putrān sthāpaya kauravya sthāpayiṣyāmy ahaṃ parān
d hitaṃ hi dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ tathā hitam
d śame prayatamānānāṃ tava śāsanakāṅkṣiṇām
a ājñā tava hi rājendra kāryā putraiḥ sahānvayaiḥ
c hitaṃ balavad apy eṣāṃ tiṣṭhatāṃ tava śāsane
a tava caiva hitaṃ rājan pāṇḍavānām atho hitam
c śame prayatamānasya mama śāsanakāṅkṣiṇām
a svayaṃ niṣkalam ālakṣya saṃvidhatsva viśāṃ pate
c sahabhūtās tu bharatās tavaiva syur janeśvara
a dharmārthayos tiṣṭha rājan pāṇḍavair abhirakṣitaḥ
c na hi śakyās tathābhūtā yatnād api narādhipa
a na hi tvāṃ pāṇḍavair jetuṃ rakṣyamāṇaṃ mahātmabhiḥ
c indro 'pi devaiḥ sahitaḥ prasaheta kuto nṛpāḥ
a yatra bhīṣmaś ca droṇaś ca kṛpaḥ karṇo viviṃśatiḥ
c aśvatthāmā vikarṇaś ca somadatto 'tha bāhlikaḥ
a saindhavaś ca kaliṅgaś ca kāmbojaś ca sudakṣiṇaḥ
c yudhiṣṭhiro bhīmasenaḥ savyasācī yamau tathā
a sātyakiś ca mahātejā yuyutsuś ca mahārathaḥ
b ko nu tān yudhi śatrughna sahitān kurupāṇḍavaiḥ
c ko nu tān viparītātmā yudhyeta bharatarṣabha
a lokasyeśvaratāṃ bhūyaḥ śatrubhiś cāpradhṛṣyatām
c prāpsyasi tvam amitraghna sahitaḥ kurupāṇḍavaiḥ
a tasya te pṛthivīpālās tvatsamāḥ pṛthivīpate
c śreyāṃsaś caiva rājānaḥ saṃdhāsyante paraṃtapa
a sa tvaṃ putraiś ca pautraiś ca bhrātṛbhiḥ pitṛbhis tathā
c suhṛdbhiḥ sarvato guptaḥ sukhaṃ śakṣyasi jīvitum
a etān eva purodhāya satkṛtya ca yathā purā
c akhilāṃ bhokṣyase sarvāṃ pṛthivīṃ pṛthivīpate
a etair hi sahitaḥ sarvaiḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ svaiś ca bhārata
c anyān vijeṣyase śatrūn eṣa svārthas tavākhilaḥ
a tair evopārjitāṃ bhūmiṃ bhokṣyase ca paraṃtapa
c yadi saṃpatsyase putraiḥ sahāmātyair narādhipa
a saṃyuge vai mahārāja dṛśyate sumahān kṣayaḥ
c kṣaye cobhayato rājan kaṃ dharmam anupaśyasi
a pāṇḍavair nihataiḥ saṃkhye putrair vāpi mahābalaiḥ
c yad vindethāḥ sukhaṃ rājaṃs tad brūhi bharatarṣabha
a śūrāś ca hi kṛtāstrāś ca sarve yuddhābhikāṅkṣiṇaḥ
c pāṇḍavās tāvakāś caiva tān rakṣa mahato bhayāt
a na paśyema kurūn sarvān pāṇḍavāṃś caiva saṃyuge
c kṣīṇān ubhayataḥ śūrān rathebhyo rathibhir hatān
a samavetāḥ pṛthivyāṃ hi rājāno rājasattama
c amarṣavaśam āpannā nāśayeyur imāḥ prajāḥ
a trāhi rājann imaṃ lokaṃ na naśyeyur imāḥ prajāḥ
c tvayi prakṛtim āpanne śeṣaṃ syāt kurunandana
a śuklā vadānyā hrīmanta āryāḥ puṇyābhijātayaḥ
c anyonyasacivā rājaṃs tān pāhi mahato bhayāt
a śiveneme bhūmipālāḥ samāgamya parasparam
c saha bhuktvā ca pītvā ca pratiyāntu yathāgṛham
a suvāsasaḥ sragviṇaś ca satkṛtya bharatarṣabha
c amarṣāṃś ca nirākṛtya vairāṇi ca paraṃtapa
a hārdaṃ yat pāṇḍaveṣv āsīt prāpte 'sminn āyuṣaḥ kṣaye
c tad eva te bhavatv adya śaśvac ca bharatarṣabha
a bālā vihīnāḥ pitrā te tvayaiva parivardhitāḥ
c tān pālaya yathānyāyaṃ putrāṃś ca bharatarṣabha
a bhavataiva hi rakṣyās te vyasaneṣu viśeṣataḥ
c mā te dharmas tathaivārtho naśyeta bharatarṣabha
a āhus tvāṃ pāṇḍavā rājann abhivādya prasādya ca
c bhavataḥ śāsanād duḥkham anubhūtaṃ sahānugaiḥ
a dvādaśemāni varṣāṇi vane nirvyuṣitāni naḥ
c trayodaśaṃ tathājñātaiḥ sajane parivatsaram
a sthātā naḥ samaye tasmin piteti kṛtaniścayāḥ
c nāhāsma samayaṃ tāta tac ca no brāhmaṇā viduḥ
a tasmin naḥ samaye tiṣṭha sthitānāṃ bharatarṣabha
c nityaṃ saṃkleśitā rājan svarājyāṃśaṃ labhemahi
a tvaṃ dharmam arthaṃ yuñjānaḥ samyaṅ nas trātum arhasi
c gurutvaṃ bhavati prekṣya bahūn kleśāṃs titikṣmahe
a sa bhavān mātṛpitṛvad asmāsu pratipadyatām
c guror garīyasī vṛttir yā ca śiṣyasya bhārata
d vartāmahe tvayi ca tāṃ tvaṃ ca vartasva nas tathā
a pitrā sthāpayitavyā hi vayam utpatham āsthitāḥ
c saṃsthāpaya pathiṣv asmāṃs tiṣṭha rājan svavartmani
a āhuś cemāṃ pariṣadaṃ putrās te bharatarṣabha
c dharmajñeṣu sabhāsatsu neha yuktam asāṃpratam
a yatra dharmo hy adharmeṇa satyaṃ yatrānṛtena ca
c hanyate prekṣamāṇānāṃ hatās tatra sabhāsadaḥ
a viddho dharmo hy adharmeṇa sabhāṃ yatra prapadyate
c na cāsya śalyaṃ kṛntanti viddhās tatra sabhāsadaḥ
e dharma etān ārujati yathā nady anukūlajān
a ye dharmam anupaśyantas tūṣṇīṃ dhyāyanta āsate
c te satyam āhur dharmaṃ ca nyāyyaṃ ca bharatarṣabha
a śakyaṃ kim anyad vaktuṃ te dānād anyaj janeśvara
c bruvantu vā mahīpālāḥ sabhāyāṃ ye samāsate
e dharmārthau saṃpradhāryaiva yadi satyaṃ bravīmy aham
a pramuñcemān mṛtyupāśāt kṣatriyān kṣatriyarṣabha
c praśāmya bharataśreṣṭha mā manyuvaśam anvagāḥ
a pitryaṃ tebhyaḥ pradāyāṃśaṃ pāṇḍavebhyo yathocitam
c tataḥ saputraḥ siddhārtho bhuṅkṣva bhogān paraṃtapa
a ajātaśatruṃ jānīṣe sthitaṃ dharme satāṃ sadā
c saputre tvayi vṛttiṃ ca vartate yāṃ narādhipa
a dāhitaś ca nirastaś ca tvām evopāśritaḥ punaḥ
c indraprasthaṃ tvayaivāsau saputreṇa vivāsitaḥ
a sa tatra nivasan sarvān vaśam ānīya pārthivān
c tvanmukhān akarod rājan na ca tvām atyavartata
a tasyaivaṃ vartamānasya saubalena jihīrṣatā
c rāṣṭrāṇi dhanadhānyaṃ ca prayuktaḥ paramopadhiḥ
a sa tām avasthāṃ saṃprāpya kṛṣṇāṃ prekṣya sabhāgatām
c kṣatradharmād ameyātmā nākampata yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a ahaṃ tu tava teṣāṃ ca śreya icchāmi bhārata
c dharmād arthāt sukhāc caiva mā rājan nīnaśaḥ prajāḥ
a anartham arthaṃ manvānā arthaṃ vānartham ātmanaḥ
c lobhe 'tiprasṛtān putrān nigṛhṇīṣva viśāṃ pate
a sthitāḥ śuśrūṣituṃ pārthāḥ sthitā yoddhum ariṃdamāḥ
c yat te pathyatamaṃ rājaṃs tasmiṃs tiṣṭha paraṃtapa
a tad vākyaṃ pārthivāḥ sarve hṛdayaiḥ samapūjayan
c na tatra kaś cid vaktuṃ hi vācaṃ prākrāmad agrataḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tasminn abhihite vākye keśavena mahātmanā
c stimitā hṛṣṭaromāṇa āsan sarve sabhāsadaḥ
a kaḥ svid uttaram etasmād vaktum utsahate pumān
c iti sarve manobhis te cintayanti sma pārthivāḥ
a tathā teṣu ca sarveṣu tūṣṇīṃbhūteṣu rājasu
c jāmadagnya idaṃ vākyam abravīt kurusaṃsadi
a imām ekopamāṃ rājañ śṛṇu satyām aśaṅkitaḥ
c tāṃ śrutvā śreya ādatsva yadi sādhv iti manyase
a rājā dambhodbhavo nāma sārvabhaumaḥ purābhavat
c akhilāṃ bubhuje sarvāṃ pṛthivīm iti naḥ śrutam
a sa sma nityaṃ niśāpāye prātar utthāya vīryavān
c brāhmaṇān kṣatriyāṃś caiva pṛcchann āste mahārathaḥ
a asti kaś cid viśiṣṭo vā madvidho vā bhaved yudhi
c śūdro vaiśyaḥ kṣatriyo vā brāhmaṇo vāpi śastrabhṛt
a iti bruvann anvacarat sa rājā pṛthivīm imām
c darpeṇa mahatā mattaḥ kaṃ cid anyam acintayan
a taṃ sma vaidyā akṛpaṇā brāhmaṇāḥ sarvato 'bhayāḥ
c pratyaṣedhanta rājānaṃ ślāghamānaṃ punaḥ punaḥ
a pratiṣidhyamāno 'py asakṛt pṛcchaty eva sa vai dvijān
c abhimānī śriyā mattas tam ūcur brāhmaṇās tadā
a tapasvino mahātmāno vedavratasamanvitāḥ
c udīryamāṇaṃ rājānaṃ krodhadīptā dvijātayaḥ
d tapasvinau mahātmānau vedapratyayadarśakau
a anekajananaṃ sakhyaṃ yayoḥ puruṣasiṃhayoḥ
c tayos tvaṃ na samo rājan bhavitāsi kadā cana
a evam uktaḥ sa rājā tu punaḥ papraccha tān dvijān
c kva tau vīrau kvajanmānau kiṃkarmāṇau ca kau ca tau
 brāhmaṇā ūcuḥ
a naro nārāyaṇaś caiva tāpasāv iti naḥ śrutam
c āyātau mānuṣe loke tābhyāṃ yudhyasva pārthiva
a śrūyate tau mahātmānau naranārāyaṇāv ubhau
c tapo ghoram anirdeśyaṃ tapyete gandhamādane
 rāma uvāca
a sa rājā mahatīṃ senāṃ yojayitvā ṣaḍaṅginīm
c amṛṣyamāṇaḥ saṃprāyād yatra tāv aparājitau
a sa gatvā viṣamaṃ ghoraṃ parvataṃ gandhamādanam
c mṛgayāṇo 'nvagacchat tau tāpasāv aparājitau
a tau dṛṣṭvā kṣutpipāsābhyāṃ kṛśau dhamanisaṃtatau
c śītavātātapaiś caiva karśitau puruṣottamau
e abhigamyopasaṃgṛhya paryapṛcchad anāmayam
a tam arcitvā mūlaphalair āsanenodakena ca
c nyamantrayetāṃ rājānaṃ kiṃ kāryaṃ kriyatām iti
d tatas tām ānupūrvīṃ sa punar evānvakīrtayat
 dambhodbhava uvāca
a bāhubhyāṃ me jitā bhūmir nihatāḥ sarvaśatravaḥ
c bhavadbhyāṃ yuddham ākāṅkṣann upayāto 'smi parvatam
e ātithyaṃ dīyatām etat kāṅkṣitaṃ me ciraṃ prati
 naranārāyaṇāv ūcatuḥ
a apetakrodhalobho 'yam āśramo rājasattama
c na hy asminn āśrame yuddhaṃ kutaḥ śastraṃ kuto 'nṛjuḥ
e anyatra yuddham ākāṅkṣva bahavaḥ kṣatriyāḥ kṣitau
 rāma uvāca
a ucyamānas tathāpi sma bhūya evābhyabhāṣata
c punaḥ punaḥ kṣamyamāṇaḥ sāntvyamānaś ca bhārata
e dambhodbhavo yuddham icchann āhvayaty eva tāpasau
a tato naras tv iṣīkāṇāṃ muṣṭim ādāya kaurava
c abravīd ehi yudhyasva yuddhakāmuka kṣatriya
a sarvaśastrāṇi cādatsva yojayasva ca vāhinīm
c ahaṃ hi te vineṣyāmi yuddhaśraddhām itaḥ param
d saṃnahyasva ca varmāṇi yāni cānyāni santi te
d yad āhvayasi darpeṇa brāhmaṇapramukhāñ janān
 dambhodbhava uvāca
a yady etad astram asmāsu yuktaṃ tāpasa manyase
c etenāpi tvayā yotsye yuddhārthī hy aham āgataḥ
 rāma uvāca
a ity uktvā śaravarṣeṇa sarvataḥ samavākirat
c dambhodbhavas tāpasaṃ taṃ jighāṃsuḥ sahasainikaḥ
a tasya tān asyato ghorān iṣūn paratanucchidaḥ
c kadarthīkṛtya sa munir iṣīkābhir apānudat
a tato 'smai prāsṛjad ghoram aiṣīkam aparājitaḥ
c astram apratisaṃdheyaṃ tad adbhutam ivābhavat
a teṣām akṣīṇi karṇāṃś ca nastakāṃś caiva māyayā
c nimittavedhī sa munir iṣīkābhiḥ samarpayat
a sa dṛṣṭvā śvetam ākāśam iṣīkābhiḥ samācitam
c pādayor nyapatad rājā svasti me 'stv iti cābravīt
a tam abravīn naro rājañ śaraṇyaḥ śaraṇaiṣiṇām
c brahmaṇyo bhava dharmātmā mā ca smaivaṃ punaḥ kṛthāḥ
d naitādṛk puruṣo rājan kṣatradharmam anusmaran
d manasā nṛpaśārdūla bhavet purapuraṃjayaḥ
a mā ca darpasamāviṣṭaḥ kṣepsīḥ kāṃś cit kadā cana
c alpīyāṃsaṃ viśiṣṭaṃ vā tat te rājan paraṃ hitam
a kṛtaprajño vītalobho nirahaṃkāra ātmavān
c dāntaḥ kṣānto mṛduḥ kṣemaḥ prajāḥ pālaya pārthiva
d mā sma bhūyaḥ kṣipeḥ kaṃ cid aviditvā balābalam
a anujñātaḥ svasti gaccha maivaṃ bhūyaḥ samācareḥ
c kuśalaṃ brāhmaṇān pṛccher āvayor vacanād bhṛśam
a tato rājā tayoḥ pādāv abhivādya mahātmanoḥ
c pratyājagāma svapuraṃ dharmaṃ caivācinod bhṛśam
a sumahac cāpi tat karma yan nareṇa kṛtaṃ purā
c tato guṇaiḥ subahubhiḥ śreṣṭho nārāyaṇo 'bhavat
a tasmād yāvad dhanuḥśreṣṭhe gāṇḍīve 'straṃ na yujyate
c tāvat tvaṃ mānam utsṛjya gaccha rājan dhanaṃjayam
a kākudīkaṃ śukaṃ nākam akṣisaṃtarjanaṃ tathā
c saṃtānaṃ nartanaṃ ghoram āsyamodakam aṣṭamam
a etair viddhāḥ sarva eva maraṇaṃ yānti mānavāḥ
b kāmakrodhau lobhamohau madamānau tathaiva ca
b mātsaryāhaṃkṛtī caiva kramād eta udāhṛtāḥ
c unmattāś ca viceṣṭante naṣṭasaṃjñā vicetasaḥ
a svapante ca plavante ca chardayanti ca mānavāḥ
c mūtrayante ca satataṃ rudanti ca hasanti ca
a asaṃkhyeyā guṇāḥ pārthe tadviśiṣṭo janārdanaḥ
c tvam eva bhūyo jānāsi kuntīputraṃ dhanaṃjayam
a naranārāyaṇau yau tau tāv evārjunakeśavau
c vijānīhi mahārāja pravīrau puruṣarṣabhau
d nirmātā sarvalokānām īśvaraḥ sarvakarmakṛt
d yasya nārāyaṇo bandhur arjuno duḥsaho yudhi
d kas tam utsahate jetuṃ triṣu lokeṣu bhārata
d vīraṃ kapidhvajaṃ jiṣṇuṃ yasya nāsti samo yudhi
a yady etad evaṃ jānāsi na ca mām atiśaṅkase
c āryāṃ matiṃ samāsthāya śāmya bhārata pāṇḍavaiḥ
a atha cen manyase śreyo na me bhedo bhaved iti
c praśāmya bharataśreṣṭha mā ca yuddhe manaḥ kṛthāḥ
a bhavatāṃ ca kuruśreṣṭha kulaṃ bahumataṃ bhuvi
c tat tathaivāstu bhadraṃ te svārtham evānucintaya
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a jāmadagnyavacaḥ śrutvā kaṇvo 'pi bhagavān ṛṣiḥ
c duryodhanam idaṃ vākyam abravīt kurusaṃsadi
a akṣayaś cāvyayaś caiva brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ
c tathaiva bhagavantau tau naranārāyaṇāv ṛṣī
a ādityānāṃ hi sarveṣāṃ viṣṇur ekaḥ sanātanaḥ
c ajayyaś cāvyayaś caiva śāśvataḥ prabhur īśvaraḥ
a nimittamaraṇās tv anye candrasūryau mahī jalam
c vāyur agnis tathākāśaṃ grahās tārāgaṇās tathā
a te ca kṣayānte jagato hitvā lokatrayaṃ sadā
c kṣayaṃ gacchanti vai sarve sṛjyante ca punaḥ punaḥ
a muhūrtamaraṇās tv anye mānuṣā mṛgapakṣiṇaḥ
c tiryagyonyaś ca ye cānye jīvalokacarāḥ smṛtāḥ
a bhūyiṣṭhena tu rājānaḥ śriyaṃ bhuktvāyuṣaḥ kṣaye
c maraṇaṃ pratigacchanti bhoktuṃ sukṛtaduṣkṛtam
a sa bhavān dharmaputreṇa śamaṃ kartum ihārhati
c pāṇḍavāḥ kuravaś caiva pālayantu vasuṃdharām
a balavān aham ity eva na mantavyaṃ suyodhana
c balavanto hi balibhir dṛśyante puruṣarṣabha
a na balaṃ balināṃ madhye balaṃ bhavati kaurava
c balavanto hi te sarve pāṇḍavā devavikramāḥ
a atrāpy udāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanam
c mātaler dātukāmasya kanyāṃ mṛgayato varam
a matas trailokyarājasya mātalir nāma sārathiḥ
c tasyaikaiva kule kanyā rūpato lokaviśrutā
a guṇakeśīti vikhyātā nāmnā sā devarūpiṇī
c śriyā ca vapuṣā caiva striyo 'nyāḥ sātiricyate
a tasyāḥ pradānasamayaṃ mātaliḥ saha bhāryayā
c jñātvā vimamṛśe rājaṃs tatparaḥ paricintayan
a dhik khalv alaghuśīlānām ucchritānāṃ yaśasvinām
c narāṇām ṛddhasattvānāṃ kule kanyāprarohaṇam
a mātuḥ kulaṃ pitṛkulaṃ yatra caiva pradīyate
c kulatrayaṃ saṃśayitaṃ kurute kanyakā satām
a devamānuṣalokau dvau mānasenaiva cakṣuṣā
c avagāhyaiva vicitau na ca me rocate varaḥ
a na devān naiva ditijān na gandharvān na mānuṣān
c arocayaṃ varakṛte tathaiva bahulān ṛṣīn
a bhāryayā tu sa saṃmantrya saha rātrau sudharmayā
c mātalir nāgalokāya cakāra gamane matim
a na me devamanuṣyeṣu guṇakeśyāḥ samo varaḥ
c rūpato dṛśyate kaś cin nāgeṣu bhavitā dhruvam
a ity āmantrya sudharmāṃ sa kṛtvā cābhipradakṣiṇam
c kanyāṃ śirasy upāghrāya praviveśa mahītalam
 kaṇva uvāca
a mātalis tu vrajan mārge nāradena maharṣiṇā
c varuṇaṃ gacchatā draṣṭuṃ samāgacchad yadṛcchayā
a nārado 'thābravīd enaṃ kva bhavān gantum udyataḥ
c svena vā sūta kāryeṇa śāsanād vā śatakratoḥ
a mātalir nāradenaivaṃ saṃpṛṣṭaḥ pathi gacchatā
c yathāvat sarvam ācaṣṭa svakāryaṃ varuṇaṃ prati
a tam uvācātha sa munir gacchāvaḥ sahitāv iti
c salileśadidṛkṣārtham aham apy udyato divaḥ
a ahaṃ te sarvam ākhyāsye darśayan vasudhātalam
c dṛṣṭvā tatra varaṃ kaṃ cid rocayiṣyāva mātale
a avagāhya tato bhūmim ubhau mātalināradau
c dadṛśāte mahātmānau lokapālam apāṃ patim
a tatra devarṣisadṛśīṃ pūjāṃ prāpa sa nāradaḥ
c mahendrasadṛśīṃ caiva mātaliḥ pratyapadyata
a tāv ubhau prītamanasau kāryavattāṃ nivedya ha
c varuṇenābhyanujñātau nāgalokaṃ viceratuḥ
a nāradaḥ sarvabhūtānām antarbhūminivāsinām
c jānaṃś cakāra vyākhyānaṃ yantuḥ sarvam aśeṣataḥ
 nārada uvāca
a dṛṣṭas te varuṇas tāta putrapautrasamāvṛtaḥ
c paśyodakapateḥ sthānaṃ sarvatobhadram ṛddhimat
a eṣa putro mahāprājño varuṇasyeha gopateḥ
c eṣa taṃ śīlavṛttena śaucena ca viśiṣyate
a eṣo 'sya putro 'bhimataḥ puṣkaraḥ puṣkarekṣaṇaḥ
c rūpavān darśanīyaś ca somaputryā vṛtaḥ patiḥ
a jyotsnākālīti yām āhur dvitīyāṃ rūpataḥ śriyam
c ādityasyaiva goḥ putro jyeṣṭhaḥ putraḥ kṛtaḥ smṛtaḥ
a bhavanaṃ paśya vāruṇyā yad etat sarvakāñcanam
b eṣā vai vāruṇī kanyā surā lokeṣu viśrutā
c yāṃ prāpya suratāṃ prāptāḥ surāḥ surapateḥ sakhe
a etāni hṛtarājyānāṃ daiteyānāṃ sma mātale
c dīpyamānāni dṛśyante sarvapraharaṇāny uta
a akṣayāṇi kilaitāni vivartante sma mātale
c anubhāvaprayuktāni surair avajitāni ha
a atra rākṣasajātyaś ca bhūtajātyaś ca mātale
c divyapraharaṇāś cāsan pūrvadaivatanirmitāḥ
a agnir eṣa mahārciṣmāñ jāgarti varuṇahrade
c vaiṣṇavaṃ cakram āviddhaṃ vidhūmena haviṣmatā
a eṣa gāṇḍīmayaś cāpo lokasaṃhārasaṃbhṛtaḥ
c rakṣyate daivatair nityaṃ yatas tad gāṇḍivaṃ dhanuḥ
a eṣa kṛtye samutpanne tat tad dhārayate balam
c sahasraśatasaṃkhyena prāṇena satataṃ dhruvam
a aśāsyān api śāsty eṣa rakṣobandhuṣu rājasu
c sṛṣṭaḥ prathamajo daṇḍo brahmaṇā brahmavādinā
a etac chatraṃ narendrāṇāṃ mahac chakreṇa bhāṣitam
c putrāḥ salilarājasya dhārayanti mahodayam
a etat salilarājasya chatraṃ chatragṛhe sthitam
c sarvataḥ salilaṃ śītaṃ jīmūta iva varṣati
a etac chatrāt paribhraṣṭaṃ salilaṃ somanirmalam
c tamasā mūrchitaṃ yāti yena nārchati darśanam
a bahūny adbhutarūpāṇi draṣṭavyānīha mātale
c tava kāryoparodhas tu tasmād gacchāva māciram
 nārada uvāca
a etat tu nāgalokasya nābhisthāne sthitaṃ puram
c pātālam iti vikhyātaṃ daityadānavasevitam
a idam adbhiḥ samaṃ prāptā ye ke cid dhruvajaṅgamāḥ
c praviśanto mahānādaṃ nadanti bhayapīḍitāḥ
a atrāsuro 'gniḥ satataṃ dīpyate vāribhojanaḥ
c vyāpāreṇa dhṛtātmānaṃ nibaddhaṃ samabudhyata
a atrāmṛtaṃ suraiḥ pītvā nihitaṃ nihatāribhiḥ
c ataḥ somasya hāniś ca vṛddhiś caiva pradṛśyate
a atra divyaṃ hayaśiraḥ kāle parvaṇi parvaṇi
c uttiṣṭhati suvarṇābhaṃ vārbhir āpūrayañ jagat
a yasmād atra samagrās tāḥ patanti jalamūrtayaḥ
c tasmāt pātālam ity etat khyāyate puram uttamam
a airāvato 'smāt salilaṃ gṛhītvā jagato hitaḥ
c megheṣv āmuñcate śītaṃ yan mahendraḥ pravarṣati
a atra nānāvidhākārās timayo naikarūpiṇaḥ
c apsu somaprabhāṃ pītvā vasanti jalacāriṇaḥ
a atra sūryāṃśubhir bhinnāḥ pātālatalam āśritāḥ
c mṛtā divasataḥ sūta punar jīvanti te niśi
a udaye nityaśaś cātra candramā raśmibhir vṛtaḥ
c amṛtaṃ spṛśya saṃsparśāt saṃjīvayati dehinaḥ
a atra te 'dharmaniratā baddhāḥ kālena pīḍitāḥ
c daiteyā nivasanti sma vāsavena hṛtaśriyaḥ
a atra bhūtapatir nāma sarvabhūtamaheśvaraḥ
c bhūtaye sarvabhūtānām acarat tapa uttamam
a atra govratino viprāḥ svādhyāyāmnāyakarśitāḥ
c tyaktaprāṇā jitasvargā nivasanti maharṣayaḥ
a yatratatraśayo nityaṃ yenakenacidāśitaḥ
c yenakenacidācchannaḥ sa govrata ihocyate
a airāvato nāgarājo vāmanaḥ kumudo 'ñjanaḥ
c prasūtāḥ supratīkasya vaṃśe vāraṇasattamāḥ
a paśya yady atra te kaś cid rocate guṇato varaḥ
c varayiṣyāva taṃ gatvā yatnam āsthāya mātale
a aṇḍam etaj jale nyastaṃ dīpyamānam iva śriyā
c ā prajānāṃ nisargād vai nodbhidyati na sarpati
a nāsya jātiṃ nisargaṃ vā kathyamānaṃ śṛṇomi vai
c pitaraṃ mātaraṃ vāpi nāsya jānāti kaś cana
a ataḥ kila mahān agnir antakāle samutthitaḥ
c dhakṣyate mātale sarvaṃ trailokyaṃ sacarācaram
 kaṇva uvāca
a mātalis tv abravīc chrutvā nāradasyātha bhāṣitam
c na me 'tra rocate kaś cid anyato vraja māciram
 nārada uvāca
a hiraṇyapuram ity etat khyātaṃ puravaraṃ mahat
c daityānāṃ dānavānāṃ ca māyāśatavicāriṇām
a analpena prayatnena nirmitaṃ viśvakarmaṇā
c mayena manasā sṛṣṭaṃ pātālatalam āśritam
a atra māyāsahasrāṇi vikurvāṇā mahaujasaḥ
c dānavā nivasanti sma śūrā dattavarāḥ purā
a naite śakreṇa nānyena varuṇena yamena vā
c śakyante vaśam ānetuṃ tathaiva dhanadena ca
a asurāḥ kālakhañjāś ca tathā viṣṇupadodbhavāḥ
c nairṛtā yātudhānāś ca brahmavedodbhavāś ca ye
a daṃṣṭriṇo bhīmarūpāś ca nivasanty ātmarakṣiṇaḥ
c māyāvīryopasaṃpannā nivasanty ātmarakṣiṇaḥ
a nivātakavacā nāma dānavā yuddhadurmadāḥ
c jānāsi ca yathā śakro naitāñ śaknoti bādhitum
a bahuśo mātale tvaṃ ca tava putraś ca gomukhaḥ
c nirbhagno devarājaś ca sahaputraḥ śacīpatiḥ
a paśya veśmāni raukmāṇi mātale rājatāni ca
c karmaṇā vidhiyuktena yuktāny upagatāni ca
a vaiḍūryaharitānīva pravālarucirāṇi ca
c arkasphaṭikaśubhrāṇi vajrasārojjvalāni ca
a pārthivānīva cābhānti punar nagamayāni ca
c śailānīva ca dṛśyante tārakāṇīva cāpy uta
a sūryarūpāṇi cābhānti dīptāgnisadṛśāni ca
c maṇijālavicitrāṇi prāṃśūni nibiḍāni ca
a naitāni śakyaṃ nirdeṣṭuṃ rūpato dravyatas tathā
c guṇataś caiva siddhāni pramāṇaguṇavanti ca
a ākrīḍān paśya daityānāṃ tathaiva śayanāny uta
c ratnavanti mahārhāṇi bhājanāny āsanāni ca
a jaladābhāṃs tathā śailāṃs toyaprasravaṇānvitān
c kāmapuṣpaphalāṃś caiva pādapān kāmacāriṇaḥ
a mātale kaś cid atrāpi rucitas te varo bhavet
c atha vānyāṃ diśaṃ bhūmer gacchāva yadi manyase
 kaṇva uvāca
a mātalis tv abravīd enaṃ bhāṣamāṇaṃ tathāvidham
c devarṣe naiva me kāryaṃ vipriyaṃ tridivaukasām
a nityānuṣaktavairā hi bhrātaro devadānavāḥ
c aripakṣeṇa saṃbandhaṃ rocayiṣyāmy ahaṃ katham
a anyatra sādhu gacchāvo draṣṭuṃ nārhāmi dānavān
c jānāmi tu tathātmānaṃ ditsātmakamalaṃ yathā
 nārada uvāca
a ayaṃ lokaḥ suparṇānāṃ pakṣiṇāṃ pannagāśinām
c vikrame gamane bhāre naiṣām asti pariśramaḥ
a vainateyasutaiḥ sūta ṣaḍbhis tatam idaṃ kulam
c sumukhena sunāmnā ca sunetreṇa suvarcasā
a surūpapakṣirājena subalena ca mātale
c vardhitāni prasūtyā vai vinatākulakartṛbhiḥ
a pakṣirājābhijātyānāṃ sahasrāṇi śatāni ca
c kaśyapasya tato vaṃśe jātair bhūtivivardhanaiḥ
a sarve hy ete śriyā yuktāḥ sarve śrīvatsalakṣaṇāḥ
c sarve śriyam abhīpsanto dhārayanti balāny uta
a karmaṇā kṣatriyāś caite nirghṛṇā bhogibhojinaḥ
c jñātisaṃkṣayakartṛtvād brāhmaṇyaṃ na labhanti vai
a nāmāni caiṣāṃ vakṣyāmi yathā prādhānyataḥ śṛṇu
c mātale ślāghyam etad dhi kulaṃ viṣṇuparigraham
a daivataṃ viṣṇur eteṣāṃ viṣṇur eva parāyaṇam
c hṛdi caiṣāṃ sadā viṣṇur viṣṇur eva gatiḥ sadā
a suvarṇacūḍo nāgāśī dāruṇaś caṇḍatuṇḍakaḥ
c analaś cānilaś caiva viśālākṣo 'tha kuṇḍalī
a kāśyapir dhvajaviṣkambho vainateyo 'tha vāmanaḥ
c vātavego diśācakṣur nimeṣo nimiṣas tathā
a trivāraḥ saptavāraś ca vālmīkir dvīpakas tathā
c daityadvīpaḥ sariddvīpaḥ sārasaḥ padmakesaraḥ
a sumukhaḥ sukhaketuś ca citrabarhas tathānaghaḥ
c meghakṛt kumudo dakṣaḥ sarpāntaḥ somabhojanaḥ
a gurubhāraḥ kapotaś ca sūryanetraś cirāntakaḥ
c viṣṇudhanvā kumāraś ca paribarho haris tathā
a susvaro madhuparkaś ca hemavarṇas tathaiva ca
c malayo mātariśvā ca niśākaradivākarau
a ete pradeśamātreṇa mayoktā garuḍātmajāḥ
c prādhānyato 'tha yaśasā kīrtitāḥ prāṇataś ca te
a yady atra na ruciḥ kā cid ehi gacchāva mātale
c taṃ nayiṣyāmi deśaṃ tvāṃ ruciṃ yatropalapsyase
 nārada uvāca
a idaṃ rasātalaṃ nāma saptamaṃ pṛthivītalam
c yatrāste surabhir mātā gavām amṛtasaṃbhavā
a kṣarantī satataṃ kṣīraṃ pṛthivīsārasaṃbhavam
c ṣaṇṇāṃ rasānāṃ sāreṇa rasam ekam anuttamam
a amṛtenābhitṛptasya sāram udgirataḥ purā
c pitāmahasya vadanād udatiṣṭhad aninditā
a yasyāḥ kṣīrasya dhārāyā nipatantyā mahītale
c hradaḥ kṛtaḥ kṣīranidhiḥ pavitraṃ param uttamam
a puṣpitasyeva phenasya paryantam anuveṣṭitam
c pibanto nivasanty atra phenapā munisattamāḥ
a phenapā nāma nāmnā te phenāhārāś ca mātale
c ugre tapasi vartante yeṣāṃ bibhyati devatāḥ
a asyāś catasro dhenvo 'nyā dikṣu sarvāsu mātale
c nivasanti diśāpālyo dhārayantyo diśaḥ smṛtāḥ
a pūrvāṃ diśaṃ dhārayate surūpā nāma saurabhī
c dakṣiṇāṃ haṃsakā nāma dhārayaty aparāṃ diśam
a paścimā vāruṇī dik ca dhāryate vai subhadrayā
c mahānubhāvayā nityaṃ mātale viśvarūpayā
a sarvakāmadughā nāma dhenur dhārayate diśam
c uttarāṃ mātale dharmyāṃ tathailavilasaṃjñitām
a āsāṃ tu payasā miśraṃ payo nirmathya sāgare
c manthānaṃ mandaraṃ kṛtvā devair asurasaṃhitaiḥ
a uddhṛtā vāruṇī lakṣmīr amṛtaṃ cāpi mātale
c uccaiḥśravāś cāśvarājo maṇiratnaṃ ca kaustubham
a sudhāhāreṣu ca sudhāṃ svadhābhojiṣu ca svadhām
c amṛtaṃ cāmṛtāśeṣu surabhiḥ kṣarate payaḥ
a atra gāthā purā gītā rasātalanivāsibhiḥ
c paurāṇī śrūyate loke gīyate yā manīṣibhiḥ
a na nāgaloke na svarge na vimāne triviṣṭape
c parivāsaḥ sukhas tādṛg rasātalatale yathā
 nārada uvāca
a iyaṃ bhogavatī nāma purī vāsukipālitā
c yādṛśī devarājasya purīvaryāmarāvatī
a eṣa śeṣaḥ sthito nāgo yeneyaṃ dhāryate sadā
c tapasā lokamukhyena prabhāvamahatā mahī
a śvetoccayanibhākāro nānāvidhavibhūṣaṇaḥ
c sahasraṃ dhārayan mūrdhnāṃ jvālājihvo mahābalaḥ
a iha nānāvidhākārā nānāvidhavibhūṣaṇāḥ
c surasāyāḥ sutā nāgā nivasanti gatavyathāḥ
a maṇisvastikacakrāṅkāḥ kamaṇḍalukalakṣaṇāḥ
c sahasrasaṃkhyā balinaḥ sarve raudrāḥ svabhāvataḥ
a sahasraśirasaḥ ke cit ke cit pañcaśatānanāḥ
c śataśīrṣās tathā ke cit ke cit triśiraso 'pi ca
a dvipañcaśirasaḥ ke cit ke cit saptamukhās tathā
c mahābhogā mahākāyāḥ parvatābhogabhoginaḥ
a bahūnīha sahasrāṇi prayutāny arbudāni ca
c nāgānām ekavaṃśānāṃ yathāśreṣṭhāṃs tu me śṛṇu
a vāsukis takṣakaś caiva karkoṭakadhanaṃjayau
c kālīyo nahuṣaś caiva kambalāśvatarāv ubhau
a bāhyakuṇḍo maṇir nāgas tathaivāpūraṇaḥ khagaḥ
c vāmanaś cailapatraś ca kukuraḥ kukuṇas tathā
a āryako nandakaś caiva tathā kalaśapotakau
c kailāsakaḥ piñjarako nāgaś cairāvatas tathā
a sumanomukho dadhimukhaḥ śaṅkho nandopanandakau
c āptaḥ koṭanakaś caiva śikhī niṣṭhūrikas tathā
a tittirir hastibhadraś ca kumudo mālyapiṇḍakaḥ
c dvau padmau puṇḍarīkaś ca puṣpo mudgaraparṇakaḥ
a karavīraḥ pīṭharakaḥ saṃvṛtto vṛtta eva ca
c piṇḍāro bilvapatraś ca mūṣikādaḥ śirīṣakaḥ
a dilīpaḥ śaṅkhaśīrṣaś ca jyotiṣko 'thāparājitaḥ
c kauravyo dhṛtarāṣṭraś ca kumāraḥ kuśakas tathā
a virajā dhāraṇaś caiva subāhur mukharo jayaḥ
c badhirāndhau vikuṇḍaś ca virasaḥ surasas tathā
a ete cānye ca bahavaḥ kaśyapasyātmajāḥ smṛtāḥ
c mātale paśya yady atra kaś cit te rocate varaḥ
 kaṇva uvāca
a mātalis tv ekam avyagraḥ satataṃ saṃnirīkṣya vai
c papraccha nāradaṃ tatra prītimān iva cābhavat
d maharṣe śaṃsa me sarvaṃ pṛcchato jñātum icchataḥ
d karāmalakavat sarvaṃ tava jñānaṃ mahāmune
a sthito ya eṣa purataḥ kauravyasyāryakasya ca
c dyutimān darśanīyaś ca kasyaiṣa kulanandanaḥ
a kaḥ pitā jananī cāsya katamasyaiṣa bhoginaḥ
c vaṃśasya kasyaiṣa mahān ketubhūta iva sthitaḥ
a praṇidhānena dhairyeṇa rūpeṇa vayasā ca me
c manaḥ praviṣṭo devarṣe guṇakeśyāḥ patir varaḥ
a mātaliṃ prītimanasaṃ dṛṣṭvā sumukhadarśanāt
c nivedayām āsa tadā māhātmyaṃ janma karma ca
a airāvatakule jātaḥ sumukho nāma nāgarāṭ
c āryakasya mataḥ pautro dauhitro vāmanasya ca
a etasya hi pitā nāgaś cikuro nāma mātale
c nacirād vainateyena pañcatvam upapāditaḥ
a tato 'bravīt prītamanā mātalir nāradaṃ vacaḥ
c eṣa me rucitas tāta jāmātā bhujagottamaḥ
a kriyatām atra yatno hi prītimān asmy anena vai
c asya nāgapater dātuṃ priyāṃ duhitaraṃ mune
 kaṇvaḥ
 mātaler vacanaṃ śrutvā nārado munisattamaḥ
 abravīn nāgarājānam āryakaṃ kurunandana
 nārada uvāca
a sūto 'yaṃ mātalir nāma śakrasya dayitaḥ suhṛt
c śuciḥ śīlaguṇopetas tejasvī vīryavān balī
a śakrasyāyaṃ sakhā caiva mantrī sārathir eva ca
c alpāntaraprabhāvaś ca vāsavena raṇe raṇe
a ayaṃ harisahasreṇa yuktaṃ jaitraṃ rathottamam
c devāsureṣu yuddheṣu manasaiva niyacchati
a anena vijitān aśvair dorbhyāṃ jayati vāsavaḥ
c anena prahṛte pūrvaṃ balabhit praharaty uta
a asya kanyā varārohā rūpeṇāsadṛśī bhuvi
c sattvaśīlaguṇopetā guṇakeśīti viśrutā
a tasyāsya yatnāc caratas trailokyam amaradyute
c sumukho bhavataḥ pautro rocate duhituḥ patiḥ
a yadi te rocate saumya bhujagottama māciram
c kriyatām āryaka kṣipraṃ buddhiḥ kanyāpratigrahe
a yathā viṣṇukule lakṣmīr yathā svāhā vibhāvasoḥ
c kule tava tathaivāstu guṇakeśī sumadhyamā
a pautrasyārthe bhavāṃs tasmād guṇakeśīṃ pratīcchatu
c sadṛśīṃ pratirūpasya vāsavasya śacīm iva
a pitṛhīnam api hy enaṃ guṇato varayāmahe
c bahumānāc ca bhavatas tathaivairāvatasya ca
e sumukhasya guṇaiś caiva śīlaśaucadamādibhiḥ
a abhigamya svayaṃ kanyām ayaṃ dātuṃ samudyataḥ
c mātales tasya saṃmānaṃ kartum arho bhavān api
 kaṇva uvāca
a sa tu dīnaḥ prahṛṣṭaś ca prāha nāradam āryakaḥ
c vriyamāṇe tathā pautre putre ca nidhanaṃ gate
d katham icchāmi devarṣe guṇakeśīṃ snuṣāṃ prati
a na me naitad bahumataṃ devarṣe vacanaṃ tava
c sakhā śakrasya saṃyuktaḥ kasyāyaṃ nepsito bhavet
a kāraṇasya tu daurbalyāc cintayāmi mahāmune
c asya dehakaras tāta mama putro mahādyute
e bhakṣito vainateyena duḥkhārtās tena vai vayam
a punar eva ca tenoktaṃ vainateyena gacchatā
c māsenānyena sumukhaṃ bhakṣayiṣya iti prabho
a dhruvaṃ tathā tad bhavitā jānīmas tasya niścayam
c tena harṣaḥ pranaṣṭo me suparṇavacanena vai
d kaṇvaḥ
d āryakasya vacaḥ śrutvā garuḍaṃ prati bhāṣitam
a mātalis tv abravīd enaṃ buddhir atra kṛtā mayā
c jāmātṛbhāvena vṛtaḥ sumukhas tava putrajaḥ
a so 'yaṃ mayā ca sahito nāradena ca pannagaḥ
c trilokeśaṃ surapatiṃ gatvā paśyatu vāsavam
a śeṣeṇaivāsya kāryeṇa prajñāsyāmy aham āyuṣaḥ
c suparṇasya vighāte ca prayatiṣyāmi sattama
a sumukhaś ca mayā sārdhaṃ deveśam abhigacchatu
c kāryasaṃsādhanārthāya svasti te 'stu bhujaṃgama
d āryakeṇābhyanujñāto gamyatām iti bhārata
a tatas te sumukhaṃ gṛhya sarva eva mahaujasaḥ
c dadṛśuḥ śakram āsīnaṃ devarājaṃ mahādyutim
a saṃgatyā tatra bhagavān viṣṇur āsīc caturbhujaḥ
c tatas tat sarvam ācakhyau nārado mātaliṃ prati
a tataḥ puraṃdaraṃ viṣṇur uvāca bhuvaneśvaram
c amṛtaṃ dīyatām asmai kriyatām amaraiḥ samaḥ
a mātalir nāradaś caiva sumukhaś caiva vāsava
c labhantāṃ bhavataḥ kāmāt kāmam etaṃ yathepsitam
a puraṃdaro 'tha saṃcintya vainateyaparākramam
c viṣṇum evābravīd enaṃ bhavān eva dadātv iti
 viṣṇur uvāca
a īśas tvam asi lokānāṃ carāṇām acarāś ca ye
c tvayā dattam adattaṃ kaḥ kartum utsahate vibho
 kaṇva uvāca
a prādāc chakras tatas tasmai pannagāyāyur uttamam
c na tv enam amṛtaprāśaṃ cakāra balavṛtrahā
a labdhvā varaṃ tu sumukhaḥ sumukhaḥ saṃbabhūva ha
c kṛtadāro yathākāmaṃ jagāma ca gṛhān prati
a nāradas tv āryakaś caiva kṛtakāryau mudā yutau
c pratijagmatur abhyarcya devarājaṃ mahādyutim
 kaṇva uvāca
a garuḍas tat tu śuśrāva yathāvṛttaṃ mahābalaḥ
c āyuḥpradānaṃ śakreṇa kṛtaṃ nāgasya bhārata
a pakṣavātena mahatā ruddhvā tribhuvanaṃ khagaḥ
c suparṇaḥ paramakruddho vāsavaṃ samupādravat
 garuḍa uvāca
a bhagavan kim avajñānāt kṣudhāṃ prati bhaye mama
c kāmakāravaraṃ dattvā punaś calitavān asi
a nisargāt sarvabhūtānāṃ sarvabhūteśvareṇa me
c āhāro vihito dhātrā kimarthaṃ vāryate tvayā
a vṛtaś caiṣa mahānāgaḥ sthāpitaḥ samayaś ca me
c anena ca mayā deva bhartavyaḥ prasavo mahān
a etasmiṃs tv anyathābhūte nānyaṃ hiṃsitum utsahe
c krīḍase kāmakāreṇa devarāja yathecchakam
a so 'haṃ prāṇān vimokṣyāmi tathā parijano mama
c ye ca bhṛtyā mama gṛhe prītimān bhava vāsava
d kaṇva uvāca
d śrutvā suparṇavacanaṃ sumukho durmukhas tadā
d tyaktvā rūpaṃ vivarṇas tu sarparūpadharo 'bhavat
d indra uvāca
d gatvā viṣṇusamīpaṃ tu pādapīṭhaṃ samāśliṣat
d na mayā kṛtaṃ vainateya na māṃ kroddhuṃ tvam arhasi
d dattābhayaḥ sa sumukho viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā
d śrutvā puraṃdareṇoktam uvāca vinatāsutaḥ
d tataḥ puraṃdaro vākyam uvāca garuḍaṃ prati
a etac caivāham arhāmi bhūyaś ca balavṛtrahan
c trailokyasyeśvaro yo 'haṃ parabhṛtyatvam āgataḥ
a tvayi tiṣṭhati deveśa na viṣṇuḥ kāraṇaṃ mama
c trailokyarāja rājyaṃ hi tvayi vāsava śāśvatam
a mamāpi dakṣasya sutā jananī kaśyapaḥ pitā
c aham apy utsahe lokān samastān voḍhum añjasā
a asahyaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ mamāpi vipulaṃ balam
c mayāpi sumahat karma kṛtaṃ daiteyavigrahe
a śrutaśrīḥ śrutasenaś ca vivasvān rocanāmukhaḥ
c prasabhaḥ kālakākṣaś ca mayāpi ditijā hatāḥ
a yat tu dhvajasthānagato yatnāt paricarāmy aham
c vahāmi caivānujaṃ te tena mām avamanyase
a ko 'nyo bhārasaho hy asti ko 'nyo 'sti balavattaraḥ
b so 'haṃ pakṣaikadeśena kṣobhaye sāgarān api
c mayā yo 'haṃ viśiṣṭaḥ san vahāmīmaṃ sabāndhavam
a avajñāya tu yat te 'haṃ bhojanād vyaparopitaḥ
c tena me gauravaṃ naṣṭaṃ tvattaś cāsmāc ca vāsava
a adityāṃ ya ime jātā balavikramaśālinaḥ
c tvam eṣāṃ kila sarveṣāṃ viśeṣād balavattaraḥ
a so 'haṃ pakṣaikadeśena vahāmi tvāṃ gataklamaḥ
c vimṛśa tvaṃ śanais tāta ko nv atra balavān iti
 kaṇva uvāca
a tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā khagasyodarkadāruṇam
c akṣobhyaṃ kṣobhayaṃs tārkṣyam uvāca rathacakrabhṛt
a garutman manyase ''tmānaṃ balavantaṃ sudurbalam
c alam asmatsamakṣaṃ te stotum ātmānam aṇḍaja
a trailokyam api me kṛtsnam aśaktaṃ dehadhāraṇe
c aham evātmanātmānaṃ vahāmi tvāṃ ca dhāraye
d na tvaṃ vahasi māṃ dorbhyāṃ moghaṃ tava vikatthanam
a imaṃ tāvan mamaikaṃ tvaṃ bāhuṃ savyetaraṃ vaha
c yady enaṃ dhārayasy ekaṃ saphalaṃ te vikatthitam
a tataḥ sa bhagavāṃs tasya skandhe bāhuṃ samāsajat
b spṛṣṭamātro nakhāgreṇa garutmān kaśyapātmajaḥ
b svahastanyastabhāro 'bhūd dvayasya snehakāraṇāt
b āropitaṃ samudvoḍhuṃ bhāraṃ taṃ nāśakad balāt
c nipapāta sa bhārārto vihvalo naṣṭacetanaḥ
a yāvān hi bhāraḥ kṛtsnāyāḥ pṛthivyāḥ parvataiḥ saha
c ekasyā dehaśākhāyās tāvad bhāram amanyata
a na tv enaṃ pīḍayām āsa balena balavattaraḥ
c tato hi jīvitaṃ tasya na vyanīnaśad acyutaḥ
a vipakṣaḥ srastakāyaś ca vicetā vihvalaḥ khagaḥ
c mumoca patrāṇi tadā gurubhāraprapīḍitaḥ
a sa viṣṇuṃ śirasā pakṣī praṇamya vinatāsutaḥ
c vicetā vihvalo dīnaḥ kiṃ cid vacanam abravīt
a bhagavaṃl lokasārasya sadṛśena vapuṣmatā
c bhujena svairamuktena niṣpiṣṭo 'smi mahītale
a kṣantum arhasi me deva vihvalasyālpacetasaḥ
c baladāhavidagdhasya pakṣiṇo dhvajavāsinaḥ
a na vijñātaṃ balaṃ deva mayā te paramaṃ vibho
c tena manyāmy ahaṃ vīryam ātmano 'sadṛśaṃ paraiḥ
a tataś cakre sa bhagavān prasādaṃ vai garutmataḥ
c maivaṃ bhūya iti snehāt tadā cainam uvāca ha
d pādāṅguṣṭhena cikṣepa sumukhaṃ garuḍorasi
d tataḥ prabhṛti rājendra saha sarpeṇa vartate
d evaṃ viṣṇubalākrānto garvanāśam upāgamat
d garuḍo balavān rājan vainateyo mahāyaśāḥ
a tathā tvam api gāndhāre yāvat pāṇḍusutān raṇe
c nāsādayasi tān vīrāṃs tāvaj jīvasi putraka
a bhīmaḥ praharatāṃ śreṣṭho vāyuputro mahābalaḥ
c dhanaṃjayaś cendrasuto na hanyātāṃ tu kaṃ raṇe
a viṣṇur vāyuś ca śakraś ca dharmas tau cāśvināv ubhau
c ete devās tvayā kena hetunā śakyam īkṣitum
a tad alaṃ te virodhena śamaṃ gaccha nṛpātmaja
c vāsudevena tīrthena kulaṃ rakṣitum arhasi
a pratyakṣo hy asya sarvasya nārado 'yaṃ mahātapāḥ
c māhātmyaṃ yat tadā viṣṇor yo 'yaṃ cakragadādharaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a duryodhanas tu tac chrutvā niḥśvasan bhṛkuṭīmukhaḥ
c rādheyam abhisaṃprekṣya jahāsa svanavat tadā
a kadarthīkṛtya tad vākyam ṛṣeḥ kaṇvasya durmatiḥ
c ūruṃ gajakarākāraṃ tāḍayann idam abravīt
a yathaiveśvarasṛṣṭo 'smi yad bhāvi yā ca me gatiḥ
c tathā maharṣe vartāmi kiṃ pralāpaḥ kariṣyati
 janamejaya uvāca
a anarthe jātanirbandhaṃ parārthe lobhamohitam
c anāryakeṣv abhirataṃ maraṇe kṛtaniścayam
a jñātīnāṃ duḥkhakartāraṃ bandhūnāṃ śokavardhanam
c suhṛdāṃ kleśadātāraṃ dviṣatāṃ harṣavardhanam
a kathaṃ nainaṃ vimārgasthaṃ vārayantīha bāndhavāḥ
c sauhṛdād vā suhṛtsnigdho bhagavān vā pitāmahaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a uktaṃ bhagavatā vākyam uktaṃ bhīṣmeṇa yat kṣamam
c uktaṃ bahuvidhaṃ caiva nāradenāpi tac chṛṇu
 nārada uvāca
a durlabho vai suhṛc chrotā durlabhaś ca hitaḥ suhṛt
c tiṣṭhate hi suhṛd yatra na bandhus tatra tiṣṭhati
a śrotavyam api paśyāmi suhṛdāṃ kurunandana
c na kartavyaś ca nirbandho nirbandho hi sudāruṇaḥ
a atrāpy udāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanam
c yathā nirbandhataḥ prāpto gālavena parājayaḥ
a viśvāmitraṃ tapasyantaṃ dharmo jijñāsayā purā
c abhyagacchat svayaṃ bhūtvā vasiṣṭho bhagavān ṛṣiḥ
a saptarṣīṇām anyatamaṃ veṣam āsthāya bhārata
c bubhukṣuḥ kṣudhito rājann āśramaṃ kauśikasya ha
a viśvāmitro 'tha saṃbhrāntaḥ śrapayām āsa vai carum
c paramānnasya yatnena na ca sa pratyapālayat
a annaṃ tena yadā bhuktam anyair dattaṃ tapasvibhiḥ
c atha gṛhyānnam atyuṣṇaṃ viśvāmitro 'bhyupāgamat
a bhuktaṃ me tiṣṭha tāvat tvam ity uktvā bhagavān yayau
c viśvāmitras tato rājan sthita eva mahādyutiḥ
a bhaktaṃ pragṛhya mūrdhnā tad bāhubhyāṃ pārśvato 'gamat
c sthitaḥ sthāṇur ivābhyāśe niśceṣṭo mārutāśanaḥ
a tasya śuśrūṣaṇe yatnam akarod gālavo muniḥ
c gauravād bahumānāc ca hārdena priyakāmyayā
a atha varṣaśate pūrṇe dharmaḥ punar upāgamat
c vāsiṣṭhaṃ veṣam āsthāya kauśikaṃ bhojanepsayā
a sa dṛṣṭvā śirasā bhaktaṃ dhriyamāṇaṃ maharṣiṇā
c tiṣṭhatā vāyubhakṣeṇa viśvāmitreṇa dhīmatā
a pratigṛhya tato dharmas tathaivoṣṇaṃ tathā navam
c bhuktvā prīto 'smi viprarṣe tam uktvā sa munir gataḥ
a kṣatrabhāvād apagato brāhmaṇatvam upāgataḥ
c dharmasya vacanāt prīto viśvāmitras tadābhavat
a viśvāmitras tu śiṣyasya gālavasya tapasvinaḥ
c śuśrūṣayā ca bhaktyā ca prītimān ity uvāca tam
e anujñāto mayā vatsa yatheṣṭaṃ gaccha gālava
a ity uktaḥ pratyuvācedaṃ gālavo munisattamam
c prīto madhurayā vācā viśvāmitraṃ mahādyutim
a dakṣiṇāṃ kāṃ prayacchāmi bhavate gurukarmaṇi
c dakṣiṇābhir upetaṃ hi karma sidhyati mānavam
a dakṣiṇānāṃ hi sṛṣṭānām apavargeṇa bhujyate
c svarge kratuphalaṃ sadbhir dakṣiṇā śāntir ucyate
e kim āharāmi gurvarthaṃ bravītu bhagavān iti
a jānamānas tu bhagavāñ jitaḥ śuśrūṣaṇena ca
c viśvāmitras tam asakṛd gaccha gacchety acodayat
a asakṛd gaccha gaccheti viśvāmitreṇa bhāṣitaḥ
c kiṃ dadānīti bahuśo gālavaḥ pratyabhāṣata
a nirbandhatas tu bahuśo gālavasya tapasvinaḥ
c kiṃ cid āgatasaṃrambho viśvāmitro 'bravīd idam
a ekataḥśyāmakarṇānāṃ śatāny aṣṭau dadasva me
c hayānāṃ candraśubhrāṇāṃ gaccha gālava māciram
 nārada uvāca
a evam uktas tadā tena viśvāmitreṇa dhīmatā
c nāste na śete nāhāraṃ kurute gālavas tadā
a tvagasthibhūto hariṇaś cintāśokaparāyaṇaḥ
c śocamāno 'timātraṃ sa dahyamānaś ca manyunā
d gālavo duḥkhito duḥkhād vilalāpa suyodhana
a kutaḥ puṣṭāni mitrāṇi kuto 'rthāḥ saṃcayaḥ kutaḥ
c hayānāṃ candraśubhrāṇāṃ śatāny aṣṭau kuto mama
a kuto me bhojanaśraddhā sukhaśraddhā kutaś ca me
c śraddhā me jīvitasyāpi chinnā kiṃ jīvitena me
a ahaṃ pāraṃ samudrasya pṛthivyā vā paraṃ parāt
c gatvātmānaṃ vimuñcāmi kiṃ phalaṃ jīvitena me
a adhanasyākṛtārthasya tyaktasya vividhaiḥ phalaiḥ
c ṛṇaṃ dhārayamāṇasya kutaḥ sukham anīhayā
a suhṛdāṃ hi dhanaṃ bhuktvā kṛtvā praṇayam īpsitam
c pratikartum aśaktasya jīvitān maraṇaṃ varam
a pratiśrutya kariṣyeti kartavyaṃ tad akurvataḥ
c mithyāvacanadagdhasya iṣṭāpūrtaṃ praṇaśyati
a na rūpam anṛtasyāsti nānṛtasyāsti saṃtatiḥ
c nānṛtasyādhipatyaṃ ca kuta eva gatiḥ śubhā
a kutaḥ kṛtaghnasya yaśaḥ kutaḥ sthānaṃ kutaḥ sukham
c aśraddheyaḥ kṛtaghno hi kṛtaghne nāsti niṣkṛtiḥ
a na jīvaty adhanaḥ pāpaḥ kutaḥ pāpasya tantraṇam
c pāpo dhruvam avāpnoti vināśaṃ nāśayan kṛtam
a so 'haṃ pāpaḥ kṛtaghnaś ca kṛpaṇaś cānṛto 'pi ca
c guror yaḥ kṛtakāryaḥ saṃs tat karomi na bhāṣitam
e so 'haṃ prāṇān vimokṣyāmi kṛtvā yatnam anuttamam
a arthanā na mayā kā cit kṛtapūrvā divaukasām
c mānayanti ca māṃ sarve tridaśā yajñasaṃstare
a ahaṃ tu vibudhaśreṣṭhaṃ devaṃ tribhuvaneśvaram
c viṣṇuṃ gacchāmy ahaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ gatiṃ gatimatāṃ varam
a bhogā yasmāt pratiṣṭhante vyāpya sarvān surāsurān
c prayato draṣṭum icchāmi mahāyoginam avyayam
a evam ukte sakhā tasya garuḍo vinatātmajaḥ
c darśayām āsa taṃ prāha saṃhṛṣṭaḥ priyakāmyayā
a suhṛd bhavān mama mataḥ suhṛdāṃ ca mataḥ suhṛt
c īpsitenābhilāṣeṇa yoktavyo vibhave sati
a vibhavaś cāsti me vipra vāsavāvarajo dvija
c pūrvam uktas tvadarthaṃ ca kṛtaḥ kāmaś ca tena me
a sa bhavān etu gacchāva nayiṣye tvāṃ yathāsukham
c deśaṃ pāraṃ pṛthivyā vā gaccha gālava māciram
 suparṇa uvāca
a anuśiṣṭo 'smi devena gālavājñātayoninā
c brūhi kām anusaṃyāmi draṣṭuṃ prathamato diśam
a pūrvāṃ vā dakṣiṇāṃ vāham atha vā paścimāṃ diśam
c uttarāṃ vā dvijaśreṣṭha kuto gacchāmi gālava
a yasyām udayate pūrvaṃ sarvalokaprabhāvanaḥ
c savitā yatra saṃdhyāyāṃ sādhyānāṃ vartate tapaḥ
a yasyāṃ pūrvaṃ matir jātā yayā vyāptam idaṃ jagat
c cakṣuṣī yatra dharmasya yatra caiṣa pratiṣṭhitaḥ
a hutaṃ yatomukhair havyaṃ sarpate sarvatodiśam
c etad dvāraṃ dvijaśreṣṭha divasasya tathādhvanaḥ
a yatra pūrvaṃ prasūtā vai dākṣāyaṇyaḥ prajāḥ striyaḥ
c yasyāṃ diśi pravṛddhāś ca kaśyapasyātmasaṃbhavāḥ
a yatomūlā surāṇāṃ śrīr yatra śakro 'bhyaṣicyata

a ata eva ca pūrveṣāṃ pūrvām āśām avekṣatām
c pūrvakāryāṇi kāryāṇi daivāni sukham īpsatā

c atraivoktā savitrāsīt sāvitrī brahmavādiṣu

c atra labdhavaraiḥ somaḥ suraiḥ kratuṣu pīyate

c atra pātālam āśritya varuṇaḥ śriyam āpa ca
a atra pūrvaṃ vasiṣṭhasya paurāṇasya dvijarṣabha
c sūtiś caiva pratiṣṭhā ca nidhanaṃ ca prakāśate

a prokṣitā yatra bahavo varāhādyā mṛgā vane
c śakreṇa yatra bhāgārthe daivateṣu prakalpitāḥ
a atrāhitāḥ kṛtaghnāś ca mānuṣāś cāsurāś ca ye
c udayaṃs tān hi sarvān vai krodhād dhanti vibhāvasuḥ
a etad dvāraṃ trilokasya svargasya ca sukhasya ca
c eṣa pūrvo diśābhāgo viśāvainaṃ yadīcchasi
a priyaṃ kāryaṃ hi me tasya yasyāsmi vacane sthitaḥ
c brūhi gālava yāsyāmi śṛṇu cāpy aparāṃ diśam
 suparṇa uvāca
a iyaṃ vivasvatā pūrvaṃ śrautena vidhinā kila
c gurave dakṣiṇā dattā dakṣiṇety ucyate 'tha dik

c gatadāro gatāmātyo gatarājyo vanaṃ gataḥ
a atra sāvarṇinā caiva yavakrītātmajena ca
c maryādā sthāpitā brahman yāṃ sūryo nātivartate

c atra sarvāsavaḥ prāptāḥ punar gacchanti pañcadhā

c atra vaitaraṇī nāma nadī vitaraṇair vṛtā
e atra gatvā sukhasyāntaṃ duḥkhasyāntaṃ prapadyate
a atrāvṛtto dinakaraḥ kṣarate surasaṃ payaḥ
c kāṣṭhāṃ cāsādya dhāniṣṭhāṃ himam utsṛjate punaḥ
a atrāhaṃ gālava purā kṣudhārtaḥ paricintayan
c labdhavān yudhyamānau dvau bṛhantau gajakacchapau
a atra śakradhanur nāma sūryāj jāto mahān ṛṣiḥ
c vidur yaṃ kapilaṃ devaṃ yenāttāḥ sagarātmajāḥ
a atra siddhāḥ śivā nāma brāhmaṇā vedapāragāḥ
c adhītya sakhilān vedān ālabhante yamakṣayam
a atra bhogavatī nāma purī vāsukipālitā
c takṣakeṇa ca nāgena tathaivairāvatena ca
a atra niryāṇakāleṣu tamaḥ saṃprāpyate mahat
c abhedyaṃ bhāskareṇāpi svayaṃ vā kṛṣṇavartmanā
a eṣa tasyāpi te mārgaḥ paritāpasya gālava
c brūhi me yadi gantavyaṃ pratīcīṃ śṛṇu vā mama
 suparṇa uvāca
a iyaṃ dig dayitā rājño varuṇasya tu gopateḥ
c sadā salilarājasya pratiṣṭhā cādir eva ca
a atra paścād ahaḥ sūryo visarjayati bhāḥ svayam
c paścimety abhivikhyātā dig iyaṃ dvijasattama
a yādasām atra rājyena salilasya ca guptaye
c kaśyapo bhagavān devo varuṇaṃ smābhyaṣecayat

c jāyate taruṇaḥ somaḥ śuklasyādau tamisrahā

c asto nāma yataḥ saṃdhyā paścimā pratisarpati
a ato rātriś ca nidrā ca nirgatā divasakṣaye

c api varṣasahasreṇa na cāsyānto 'dhigamyate
a atra kāñcanaśailasya kāñcanāmbuvahasya ca
c udadhes tīram āsādya surabhiḥ kṣarate payaḥ
a atra madhye samudrasya kabandhaḥ pratidṛśyate
c svarbhānoḥ sūryakalpasya somasūryau jighāṃsataḥ

c adṛśyasyāprameyasya śrūyate vipulo dhvaniḥ

c ākāśe tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti tasthau sūryasya śāsanāt

c āhnikaṃ caiva naiśaṃ ca duḥkhasparśaṃ vimuñcati
e ataḥ prabhṛti sūryasya tiryag āvartate gatiḥ
a atra jyotīṃṣi sarvāṇi viśanty ādityamaṇḍalam
c aṣṭāviṃśatirātraṃ ca caṅkramya saha bhānunā
e niṣpatanti punaḥ sūryāt somasaṃyogayogataḥ
a atra nityaṃ sravantīnāṃ prabhavaḥ sāgarodayaḥ
c atra lokatrayasyāpas tiṣṭhanti varuṇāśrayāḥ
a atra pannagarājasyāpy anantasya niveśanam
c anādinidhanasyātra viṣṇoḥ sthānam anuttamam
a atrānalasakhasyāpi pavanasya niveśanam
c maharṣeḥ kaśyapasyātra mārīcasya niveśanam
a eṣa te paścimo mārgo digdvāreṇa prakīrtitaḥ
c brūhi gālava gacchāvo buddhiḥ kā dvijasattama
d diktrayaṃ te śrutaṃ brahmañ śṛṇu cāpy uttarāṃ diśam
 suparṇa uvāca
a yasmād uttāryate pāpād yasmān niḥśreyaso 'śnute
c tasmād uttāraṇaphalād uttarety ucyate budhaiḥ
a uttarasya hiraṇyasya parivāpasya gālava
c mārgaḥ paścimapūrvābhyāṃ digbhyāṃ vai madhyamaḥ smṛtaḥ
a asyāṃ diśi variṣṭhāyām uttarāyāṃ dvijarṣabha
c nāsaumyo nāvidheyātmā nādharmyo vasate janaḥ
a atra nārāyaṇaḥ kṛṣṇo jiṣṇuś caiva narottamaḥ
c badaryām āśramapade tathā brahmā ca śāśvataḥ
a atra vai himavatpṛṣṭhe nityam āste maheśvaraḥ
b prakṛtyā puruṣaḥ sārdhaṃ yugāntāgnisamaprabhaḥ
b na sa dṛśyo munigaṇais tathā devaiḥ savāsavaiḥ
b gandharvayakṣasiddhair vā naranārāyaṇād ṛte
b atra viṣṇuḥ sahasrākṣaḥ sahasracaraṇo 'vyayaḥ
b sahasraśirasaḥ śrīmān ekaḥ paśyati māyayā

c pratigṛhya dadau loke mānuṣe brahmavittama

c atra kāmaś ca roṣaś ca śailaś comā ca saṃbabhuḥ

c ādhipatyena kailāse dhanado 'py abhiṣecitaḥ
a atra caitrarathaṃ ramyam atra vaikhānasāśramaḥ
c atra mandākinī caiva mandaraś ca dvijarṣabha

a atra saṃyamanityānāṃ siddhānāṃ svairacāriṇām

c atra tiṣṭhati vai svātir atrāsyā udayaḥ smṛtaḥ
a atra yajñaṃ samāruhya dhruvaṃ sthātā pitāmahaḥ
c jyotīṃṣi candrasūryau ca parivartanti nityaśaḥ
a atra gāyantikādvāraṃ rakṣanti dvijasattamāḥ
c dhāmā nāma mahātmāno munayaḥ satyavādinaḥ
a na teṣāṃ jñāyate sūtir nākṛtir na tapaś citam
c parivartasahasrāṇi kāmabhogyāni gālava
a yathā yathā praviśati tasmāt parataraṃ naraḥ
c tathā tathā dvijaśreṣṭha pravilīyati gālava

c ṛte nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ naraṃ vā jiṣṇum avyayam
a atra kailāsam ity uktaṃ sthānam ailavilasya tat
c atra vidyutprabhā nāma jajñire 'psaraso daśa

c trilokavikrame brahmann uttarāṃ diśam āśritam

c sākṣād dhaimavataḥ puṇyo vimalaḥ kamalākaraḥ
a brāhmaṇeṣu ca yat kṛtsnaṃ svantaṃ kṛtvā dhanaṃ mahat
c vavre vanaṃ maharṣiḥ sa jaimūtaṃ tad vanaṃ tataḥ

 gālava uvāca

c nāgāṃś ca naravaktrāṃś ca paśyāmy unmathitān iva

c na dṛśyate ravis tāta na diśo na ca khaṃ khaga

a śarīre tu na paśyāmi tava caivātmanaś ca ha
c pade pade tu paśyāmi salilād agnim utthitam

a na me prayojanaṃ kiṃ cid gamane pannagāśana

 nārada uvāca
a evaṃ bahu ca dīnaṃ ca bruvāṇaṃ gālavaṃ tadā

 nārada uvāca
