b grahītuṃ hi manaś cakre rūpāt sākṣād iva śriyam

a suparṇo 'thābravīd vipraṃ pradhyātaṃ vai mayā dvija

c yatra dharmaś ca yajñaś ca tatreyaṃ nivased iti

c sukṛtaṃ duṣkṛtaṃ vā tvaṃ māhātmyāt kṣantum arhasi
a sā tau tadābravīt tuṣṭā patagendradvijarṣabhau
c na bhetavyaṃ suparṇo 'si suparṇa tyaja saṃbhramam
a ninditāsmi tvayā vatsa na ca nindāṃ kṣamāmy aham
c lokebhyaḥ sa paribhraśyed yo māṃ nindeta pāpakṛt
a hīnayālakṣaṇaiḥ sarvais tathāninditayā mayā
c ācāraṃ pratigṛhṇantyā siddhiḥ prāpteyam uttamā
a ācārāl labhate dharmam ācārāl labhate dhanam
c ācārāc chriyam āpnoti ācāro hanty alakṣaṇam
a tadāyuṣman khagapate yatheṣṭaṃ gamyatām itaḥ
c na ca te garhaṇīyāpi garhitavyāḥ striyaḥ kva cit
d yadi tvam ātmano hy arthair māṃ caivādātum icchasi
d tadaiva naṣṭadehas tu yad vai tvaṃ pannagāśana
d tasyaiva hi prasādena devadevasya cintanāt
d tvaṃ tu sāṅgas tu saṃjātaḥ punar eva bhaviṣyasi
a bhavitāsi yathāpūrvaṃ balavīryasamanvitaḥ
c babhūvatus tatas tasya pakṣau draviṇavattarau
a anujñātaś ca śāṇḍilyā yathāgatam upāgamat
c naiva cāsādayām āsa tathārūpāṃs turaṃgamān
a viśvāmitro 'tha taṃ dṛṣṭvā gālavaṃ cādhvani sthitam
c uvāca vadatāṃ śreṣṭho vainateyasya saṃnidhau
a yas tvayā svayam evārthaḥ pratijñāto mama dvija
c tasya kālo 'pavargasya yathā vā manyate bhavān
a pratīkṣiṣyāmy ahaṃ kālam etāvantaṃ tathā param
c yathā saṃsidhyate vipra sa mārgas tu niśamyatām
a suparṇo 'thābravīd dīnaṃ gālavaṃ bhṛśaduḥkhitam
c pratyakṣaṃ khalv idānīṃ me viśvāmitro yad uktavān
a tad āgaccha dvijaśreṣṭha mantrayiṣyāva gālava
c nādattvā gurave śakyaṃ kṛtsnam arthaṃ tvayāsitum
 nārada uvāca
a athāha gālavaṃ dīnaṃ suparṇaḥ patatāṃ varaḥ
c nirmitaṃ vahninā bhūmau vāyunā vaidhitaṃ tathā
e yasmād dhiraṇmayaṃ sarvaṃ hiraṇyaṃ tena cocyate
a dhatte dhārayate cedam etasmāt kāraṇād dhanam
c tad etat triṣu lokeṣu dhanaṃ tiṣṭhati śāśvatam
a nityaṃ proṣṭhapadābhyāṃ ca śukre dhanapatau tathā
c manuṣyebhyaḥ samādatte śukraś cittārjitaṃ dhanam
a ajaikapādahirbudhnyai rakṣyate dhanadena ca
c evaṃ na śakyate labdhum alabdhavyaṃ dvijarṣabha
a ṛte ca dhanam aśvānāṃ nāvāptir vidyate tava
c arthaṃ yācātra rājānaṃ kaṃ cid rājarṣivaṃśajam
e apīḍya rājā paurān hi yo nau kuryāt kṛtārthinau
a asti somānvavāye me jātaḥ kaś cin nṛpaḥ sakhā
c abhigacchāvahe taṃ vai tasyāsti vibhavo bhuvi
a yayātir nāma rājarṣir nāhuṣaḥ satyavikramaḥ
c sa dāsyati mayā cokto bhavatā cārthitaḥ svayam
a vibhavaś cāsya sumahān āsīd dhanapater iva
c evaṃ sa tu dhanaṃ vidvān dānenaiva vyaśodhayat
a tathā tau kathayantau ca cintayantau ca yat kṣamam
c pratiṣṭhāne narapatiṃ yayātiṃ pratyupasthitau
a pratigṛhya ca satkāram arghādiṃ bhojanaṃ varam
c pṛṣṭaś cāgamane hetum uvāca vinatāsutaḥ
a ayaṃ me nāhuṣa sakhā gālavas tapaso nidhiḥ
c viśvāmitrasya śiṣyo 'bhūd varṣāṇy ayutaśo nṛpa
a so 'yaṃ tenābhyanujñāta upakārepsayā dvijaḥ
c tam āha bhagavān kāṃ te dadāni gurudakṣiṇām
a asakṛt tena coktena kiṃ cid āgatamanyunā
c ayam uktaḥ prayaccheti jānatā vibhavaṃ laghu
a ekataḥśyāmakarṇānāṃ śubhrāṇāṃ śuddhajanmanām
c aṣṭau śatāni me dehi hayānāṃ candravarcasām
a gurvartho dīyatām eṣa yadi gālava manyase
c ity evam āha sakrodho viśvāmitras tapodhanaḥ
a so 'yaṃ śokena mahatā tapyamāno dvijarṣabhaḥ
c aśaktaḥ pratikartuṃ tad bhavantaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ
a pratigṛhya naravyāghra tvatto bhikṣāṃ gatavyathaḥ
c kṛtvāpavargaṃ gurave cariṣyati mahat tapaḥ
a tapasaḥ saṃvibhāgena bhavantam api yokṣyate
c svena rājarṣitapasā pūrṇaṃ tvāṃ pūrayiṣyati
a yāvanti romāṇi haye bhavanti hi nareśvara
c tāvato vājidā lokān prāpnuvanti mahīpate
a pātraṃ pratigrahasyāyaṃ dātuṃ pātraṃ tathā bhavān
c śaṅkhe kṣīram ivāsaktaṃ bhavatv etat tathopamam
 nārada uvāca
a evam uktaḥ suparṇena tathyaṃ vacanam uttamam
c vimṛśyāvahito rājā niścitya ca punaḥ punaḥ
a yaṣṭā kratusahasrāṇāṃ dātā dānapatiḥ prabhuḥ
c yayātir vatsakāśīśa idaṃ vacanam abravīt
a dṛṣṭvā priyasakhaṃ tārkṣyaṃ gālavaṃ ca dvijarṣabham
c nidarśanaṃ ca tapaso bhikṣāṃ ślāghyāṃ ca kīrtitām
a atītya ca nṛpān anyān ādityakulasaṃbhavān
c matsakāśam anuprāptāv etau buddhim avekṣya ca
a adya me saphalaṃ janma tāritaṃ cādya me kulam
c adyāyaṃ tārito deśo mama tārkṣya tvayānagha
a vaktum icchāmi tu sakhe yathā jānāsi māṃ purā
c na tathā vittavān asmi kṣīṇaṃ vittaṃ hi me sakhe
a na ca śakto 'smi te kartuṃ mogham āgamanaṃ khaga
c na cāśām asya viprarṣer vitathāṃ kartum utsahe
a tat tu dāsyāmi yat kāryam idaṃ saṃpādayiṣyati
c abhigamya hatāśo hi nivṛtto dahate kulam
a nātaḥ paraṃ vainateya kiṃ cit pāpiṣṭham ucyate
c yathāśānāśanaṃ loke dehi nāstīti vā vacaḥ
a hatāśo hy akṛtārthaḥ san hataḥ saṃbhāvito naraḥ
c hinasti tasya putrāṃś ca pautrāṃś cākurvato 'rthinām
a tasmāc caturṇāṃ vaṃśānāṃ sthāpayitrī sutā mama
b mādhavī nāma tārkṣyeyaṃ sarvadharmapravādinī
c iyaṃ surasutaprakhyā sarvadharmopacāyinī
a sadā devamanuṣyāṇām asurāṇāṃ ca gālava
c kāṅkṣitā rūpato bālā sutā me pratigṛhyatām
a asyāḥ śulkaṃ pradāsyanti nṛpā rājyam api dhruvam
c kiṃ punaḥ śyāmakarṇānāṃ hayānāṃ dve catuḥśate
a sa bhavān pratigṛhṇātu mamemāṃ mādhavīṃ sutām
c ahaṃ dauhitravān syāṃ vai vara eṣa mama prabho
d tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā brāhmaṇaḥ saṃśitavrataḥ
a pratigṛhya ca tāṃ kanyāṃ gālavaḥ saha pakṣiṇā
c punar drakṣyāva ity uktvā pratasthe saha kanyayā
a upalabdham idaṃ dvāram aśvānām iti cāṇḍajaḥ
c uktvā gālavam āpṛcchya jagāma bhavanaṃ svakam
a gate patagarāje tu gālavaḥ saha kanyayā
c cintayānaḥ kṣamaṃ dāne rājñāṃ vai śulkato 'gamat
a so 'gacchan manasekṣvākuṃ haryaśvaṃ rājasattamam
c ayodhyāyāṃ mahāvīryaṃ caturaṅgabalānvitam
a kośadhānyabalopetaṃ priyapauraṃ dvijapriyam
c prajābhikāmaṃ śāmyantaṃ kurvāṇaṃ tapa uttamam
a tam upāgamya vipraḥ sa haryaśvaṃ gālavo 'bravīt
c kanyeyaṃ mama rājendra prasavaiḥ kulavardhinī
a iyaṃ śulkena bhāryārthe haryaśva pratigṛhyatām
c śulkaṃ te kīrtayiṣyāmi tac chrutvā saṃpradhāryatām
 nārada uvāca
a haryaśvas tv abravīd rājā vicintya bahudhā tataḥ
c dīrgham uṣṇaṃ ca niḥśvasya prajāhetor nṛpottamaḥ
a unnateṣūnnatā ṣaṭsu sūkṣmā sūkṣmeṣu saptasu
c gambhīrā triṣu gambhīreṣv iyaṃ raktā ca pañcasu
d śroṇyau lalāṭakakṣau ca ghrāṇaṃ ceti ṣaḍunnatam
d sūkṣmāṇy aṅguliparvāṇi keśalomanakhatvacaḥ
d svaraḥ sattvaṃ ca nābhiś ca trigambhīraṃ pracakṣate
d pāṇipādatale rakte netrāntāsyanakhāni ca
d pañcadīrghaṃ caturhrasvaṃ pañcasūkṣmaṃ ṣaḍunnatam
d saptaraktaṃ trivistīrṇaṃ trigambhīraṃ praśasyate
d pañcaiva dīrghā hanulocanāni
d bāhūrunāsāś ca sukhapradāni
d hrasvāni catvāri ca liṅgapṛṣṭhe
d grīvā ca jaṅghe ca hitapradāni
d sūkṣmāṇi pañca daśanāṅguliparvakeśās
d tvak caiva vai kararuhāś ca naduḥkhitānām
d vakṣo 'tha kaṅkṣānakhanāsikāsyam
d aṃsāntikaṃ ceti ṣaḍunnatāni
d netrāntapādakaratālvadharoṣṭhajihvā
d raktā nakhāś ca khalu sarvasukhāvahāni
a bahudevāsurālokā bahugandharvadarśanā
c bahulakṣaṇasaṃpannā bahuprasavadhāriṇī
a samartheyaṃ janayituṃ cakravartinam ātmajam
c brūhi śulkaṃ dvijaśreṣṭha samīkṣya vibhavaṃ mama
 gālava uvāca
a ekataḥśyāmakarṇānāṃ śatāny aṣṭau dadasva me
c hayānāṃ candraśubhrāṇāṃ deśajānāṃ vapuṣmatām
a tatas tava bhavitrīyaṃ putrāṇāṃ jananī śubhā
c araṇīva hutāśānāṃ yonir āyatalocanā
 nārada uvāca
a etac chrutvā vaco rājā haryaśvaḥ kāmamohitaḥ
c uvāca gālavaṃ dīno rājarṣir ṛṣisattamam
a dve me śate saṃnihite hayānāṃ yad vidhās tava
c eṣṭavyāḥ śataśas tv anye caranti mama vājinaḥ
a so 'ham ekam apatyaṃ vai janayiṣyāmi gālava
c asyām etaṃ bhavān kāmaṃ saṃpādayatu me varam
a etac chrutvā tu sā kanyā gālavaṃ vākyam abravīt
c mama datto varaḥ kaś cit kena cid brahmavādinā
a prasūtyante prasūtyante kanyaiva tvaṃ bhaviṣyasi
c sa tvaṃ dadasva māṃ rājñe pratigṛhya hayottamān
a nṛpebhyo hi caturbhyas te pūrṇāny aṣṭau śatāni vai
c bhaviṣyanti tathā putrā mama catvāra eva ca
a kriyatāṃ mama saṃhāro gurvarthaṃ dvijasattama
c eṣā tāvan mama prajñā yathā vā manyase dvija
a evam uktas tu sa muniḥ kanyayā gālavas tadā
c haryaśvaṃ pṛthivīpālam idaṃ vacanam abravīt
a iyaṃ kanyā naraśreṣṭha haryaśva pratigṛhyatām
c caturbhāgena śulkasya janayasvaikam ātmajam
a pratigṛhya sa tāṃ kanyāṃ gālavaṃ pratinandya ca
c samaye deśakāle ca labdhavān sutam īpsitam
a tato vasumanā nāma vasubhyo vasumattaraḥ
c vasuprakhyo narapatiḥ sa babhūva vasupradaḥ
a atha kāle punar dhīmān gālavaḥ pratyupasthitaḥ
c upasaṃgamya covāca haryaśvaṃ prītimānasam
a jāto nṛpa sutas te 'yaṃ bālabhāskarasaṃnibhaḥ
c kālo gantuṃ naraśreṣṭha bhikṣārtham aparaṃ nṛpam
a haryaśvaḥ satyavacane sthitaḥ sthitvā ca pauruṣe
c durlabhatvād dhayānāṃ ca pradadau mādhavīṃ punaḥ
a mādhavī ca punar dīptāṃ parityajya nṛpaśriyam
c kumārī kāmato bhūtvā gālavaṃ pṛṣṭhato 'nvagāt
a tvayy eva tāvat tiṣṭhantu hayā ity uktavān dvijaḥ
c prayayau kanyayā sārdhaṃ divodāsaṃ prajeśvaram
 gālava uvāca
a mahāvīryo mahīpālaḥ kāśīnām īśvaraḥ prabhuḥ
c divodāsa iti khyāto bhaimasenir narādhipaḥ
a tatra gacchāvahe bhadre śanair āgaccha mā śucaḥ
c dhārmikaḥ saṃyame yuktaḥ satyaś caiva janeśvaraḥ
 nārada uvāca
a tam upāgamya sa munir nyāyatas tena satkṛtaḥ
c gālavaḥ prasavasyārthe taṃ nṛpaṃ pratyacodayat
 divodāsa uvāca
a śrutam etan mayā pūrvaṃ kim uktvā vistaraṃ dvija
c kāṅkṣito hi mayaiṣo 'rthaḥ śrutvaitad dvijasattama
a etac ca me bahumataṃ yad utsṛjya narādhipān
c mām evam upayāto 'si bhāvi caitad asaṃśayam
a sa eva vibhavo 'smākam aśvānām api gālava
c aham apy ekam evāsyāṃ janayiṣyāmi pārthivam
 nārada uvāca
a tathety uktvā dvijaśreṣṭhaḥ prādāt kanyāṃ mahīpateḥ
c vidhipūrvaṃ ca tāṃ rājā kanyāṃ pratigṛhītavān
a reme sa tasyāṃ rājarṣiḥ prabhāvatyāṃ yathā raviḥ
c svāhāyāṃ ca yathā vahnir yathā śacyāṃ sa vāsavaḥ
a yathā candraś ca rohiṇyāṃ yathā dhūmorṇayā yamaḥ
c varuṇaś ca yathā gauryāṃ yathā carddhyāṃ dhaneśvaraḥ
a yathā nārāyaṇo lakṣmyāṃ jāhnavyāṃ ca yathodadhiḥ
c yathā rudraś ca rudrāṇyāṃ yathā vedyāṃ pitāmahaḥ
a adṛśyantyāṃ ca vāsiṣṭho vasiṣṭhaś cākṣamālayā
c cyavanaś ca sukanyāyāṃ pulastyaḥ saṃdhyayā yathā
a agastyaś cāpi vaidarbhyāṃ sāvitryāṃ satyavān yathā
c yathā bhṛguḥ pulomāyām adityāṃ kaśyapo yathā
d himavāṃś caiva menāyāṃ gandhavatyāṃ parāśaraḥ
a reṇukāyāṃ yathārcīko haimavatyāṃ ca kauśikaḥ
b maudgalyaś candrasenāyām adityāṃ kāśyapo yathā
c bṛhaspatiś ca tārāyāṃ śukraś ca śataparvayā
a yathā bhūmyāṃ bhūmipatir urvaśyāṃ ca purūravāḥ
c ṛcīkaḥ satyavatyāṃ ca sarasvatyāṃ yathā manuḥ
d śakuntalāyāṃ duḥṣanto dhṛtyāṃ dharmaś ca śāśvataḥ
d damayantyāṃ nalaś caiva satyavatyāṃ ca nāradaḥ
d jaratkārur jaratkārvāṃ pulastyaś ca pratīcyayā
d menakāyāṃ yathorṇāyus tumburuś caiva rambhayā
d vāsukiḥ śataśīrṣāyāṃ kumāryāṃ ca dhanaṃjayaḥ
d vaidehyāṃ ca yathā rāmo rukmiṇyāṃ ca janārdanaḥ
d pulastyaś ca bharadvājyāṃ vṛttyāṃ dharmaś ca śāśvataḥ
a tathā tu ramamāṇasya divodāsasya bhūpateḥ
c mādhavī janayām āsa putram ekaṃ pratardanam
a athājagāma bhagavān divodāsaṃ sa gālavaḥ
c samaye samanuprāpte vacanaṃ cedam abravīt
a niryātayatu me kanyāṃ bhavāṃs tiṣṭhantu vājinaḥ
c yāvad anyatra gacchāmi śulkārthaṃ pṛthivīpate
a divodāso 'tha dharmātmā samaye gālavasya tām
c kanyāṃ niryātayām āsa sthitaḥ satye mahīpatiḥ
 nārada uvāca
a tathaiva sā śriyaṃ tyaktvā kanyā bhūtvā yaśasvinī
c mādhavī gālavaṃ vipram anvayāt satyasaṃgarā
a gālavo vimṛśann eva svakāryagatamānasaḥ
c jagāma bhojanagaraṃ draṣṭum auśīnaraṃ nṛpam
a tam uvācātha gatvā sa nṛpatiṃ satyavikramam
c iyaṃ kanyā sutau dvau te janayiṣyati pārthivau
a asyāṃ bhavān avāptārtho bhavitā pretya ceha ca
c somārkapratisaṃkāśau janayitvā sutau nṛpa
a śulkaṃ tu sarvadharmajña hayānāṃ candravarcasām
c ekataḥśyāmakarṇānāṃ deyaṃ mahyaṃ catuḥśatam
a gurvartho 'yaṃ samārambho na hayaiḥ kṛtyam asti me
c yadi śakyaṃ mahārāja kriyatāṃ mā vicāryatām
a anapatyo 'si rājarṣe putrau janaya pārthiva
c pitṝn putraplavena tvam ātmānaṃ caiva tāraya
a na putraphalabhoktā hi rājarṣe pātyate divaḥ
c na yāti narakaṃ ghoraṃ yatra gacchanty anātmajāḥ
a etac cānyac ca vividhaṃ śrutvā gālavabhāṣitam
c uśīnaraḥ prativaco dadau tasya narādhipaḥ
a śrutavān asmi te vākyaṃ yathā vadasi gālava
c vidhis tu balavān brahman pravaṇaṃ hi mano mama
a śate dve tu mamāśvānām īdṛśānāṃ dvijottama
c itareṣāṃ sahasrāṇi subahūni caranti me
a aham apy ekam evāsyāṃ janayiṣyāmi gālava
c putraṃ dvija gataṃ mārgaṃ gamiṣyāmi parair aham
a mūlyenāpi samaṃ kuryāṃ tavāhaṃ dvijasattama
c paurajānapadārthaṃ tu mamārtho nātmabhogataḥ
a kāmato hi dhanaṃ rājā pārakyaṃ yaḥ prayacchati
c na sa dharmeṇa dharmātman yujyate yaśasā na ca
a so 'haṃ pratigrahīṣyāmi dadātv etāṃ bhavān mama
c kumārīṃ devagarbhābhām ekaputrabhavāya me
a tathā tu bahukalyāṇam uktavantaṃ narādhipam
c uśīnaraṃ dvijaśreṣṭho gālavaḥ pratyapūjayat
a uśīnaraṃ pratigrāhya gālavaḥ prayayau vanam
c reme sa tāṃ samāsādya kṛtapuṇya iva śriyam
a kandareṣu ca śailānāṃ nadīnāṃ nirjhareṣu ca
c udyāneṣu vicitreṣu vaneṣūpavaneṣu ca
a harmyeṣu ramaṇīyeṣu prāsādaśikhareṣu ca
c vātāyanavimāneṣu tathā garbhagṛheṣu ca
a tato 'sya samaye jajñe putro bālaraviprabhaḥ
c śibir nāmnābhivikhyāto yaḥ sa pārthivasattamaḥ
a upasthāya sa taṃ vipro gālavaḥ pratigṛhya ca
c kanyāṃ prayātas tāṃ rājan dṛṣṭavān vinatātmajam
 nārada uvāca
a gālavaṃ vainateyo 'tha prahasann idam abravīt
c diṣṭyā kṛtārthaṃ paśyāmi bhavantam iha vai dvija
a gālavas tu vacaḥ śrutvā vainateyena bhāṣitam
c caturbhāgāvaśiṣṭaṃ tad ācakhyau kāryam asya hi
a suparṇas tv abravīd enaṃ gālavaṃ patatāṃ varaḥ
c prayatnas te na kartavyo naiṣa saṃpatsyate tava
a purā hi kanyakubje vai gādheḥ satyavatīṃ sutām
c bhāryārthe 'varayat kanyām ṛcīkas tena bhāṣitaḥ
a ekataḥśyāmakarṇānāṃ hayānāṃ candravarcasām
c bhagavan dīyatāṃ mahyaṃ sahasram iti gālava
a ṛcīkas tu tathety uktvā varuṇasyālayaṃ gataḥ
c aśvatīrthe hayāṃl labdhvā dattavān pārthivāya vai
a iṣṭvā te puṇḍarīkeṇa dattā rājñā dvijātiṣu
c tebhyo dve dve śate krītvā prāptās te pārthivais tadā
a aparāṇy api catvāri śatāni dvijasattama
c nīyamānāni saṃtāre hṛtāny āsan vitastayā
e evaṃ na śakyam aprāpyaṃ prāptuṃ gālava karhi cit
a imām aśvaśatābhyāṃ vai dvābhyāṃ tasmai nivedaya
c viśvāmitrāya dharmātman ṣaḍbhir aśvaśataiḥ saha
e tato 'si gatasaṃmohaḥ kṛtakṛtyo dvijarṣabha
a gālavas taṃ tathety uktvā suparṇasahitas tataḥ
c ādāyāśvāṃś ca kanyāṃ ca viśvāmitram upāgamat
 gālava uvāca
a aśvānāṃ kāṅkṣitārthānāṃ ṣaḍ imāni śatāni vai
c śatadvayena kanyeyaṃ bhavatā pratigṛhyatām
a asyāṃ rājarṣibhiḥ putrā jātā vai dhārmikās trayaḥ
c caturthaṃ janayatv ekaṃ bhavān api narottama
a pūrṇāny evaṃ śatāny aṣṭau turagāṇāṃ bhavantu te
c bhavato hy anṛṇo bhūtvā tapaḥ kuryāṃ yathāsukham
 nārada uvāca
a viśvāmitras tu taṃ dṛṣṭvā gālavaṃ saha pakṣiṇā
c kanyāṃ ca tāṃ varārohām idam ity abravīd vacaḥ
a kim iyaṃ pūrvam eveha na dattā mama gālava
c putrā mamaiva catvāro bhaveyuḥ kulabhāvanāḥ
a pratigṛhṇāmi te kanyām ekaputraphalāya vai
c aśvāś cāśramam āsādya tiṣṭhantu mama sarvaśaḥ
a sa tayā ramamāṇo 'tha viśvāmitro mahādyutiḥ
c ātmajaṃ janayām āsa mādhavīputram aṣṭakam
a jātamātraṃ sutaṃ taṃ ca viśvāmitro mahādyutiḥ
c saṃyojyārthais tathā dharmair aśvais taiḥ samayojayat
a athāṣṭakaḥ puraṃ prāyāt tadā somapuraprabham
c niryātya kanyāṃ śiṣyāya kauśiko 'pi vanaṃ yayau
a gālavo 'pi suparṇena saha niryātya dakṣiṇām
c manasābhipratītena kanyām idam uvāca ha
a jāto dānapatiḥ putras tvayā śūras tathāparaḥ
c satyadharmarataś cānyo yajvā cāpi tathāparaḥ
a tad āgaccha varārohe tāritas te pitā sutaiḥ
c catvāraś caiva rājānas tathāhaṃ ca sumadhyame
a gālavas tv abhyanujñāya suparṇaṃ pannagāśanam
b gālavaḥ prayayau śīghraṃ yayātiṃ nahuṣātmajam
c pitur niryātya tāṃ kanyāṃ prayayau vanam eva ha
 nārada uvāca
a sa tu rājā punas tasyāḥ kartukāmaḥ svayaṃvaram
c upagamyāśramapadaṃ gaṅgāyamunasaṃgame
a gṛhītamālyadāmāṃ tāṃ ratham āropya mādhavīm
c pūrur yaduś ca bhaginīm āśrame paryadhāvatām
a nāgayakṣamanuṣyāṇāṃ patatrimṛgapakṣiṇām
c śailadrumavanaukānām āsīt tatra samāgamaḥ
a nānāpuruṣadeśānām īśvaraiś ca samākulam
c ṛṣibhir brahmakalpaiś ca samantād āvṛtaṃ vanam
a nirdiśyamāneṣu tu sā vareṣu varavarṇinī
c varān utkramya sarvāṃs tān vanaṃ vṛtavatī varam
a avatīrya rathāt kanyā namaskṛtvā ca bandhuṣu
c upagamya vanaṃ puṇyaṃ tapas tepe yayātijā
a upavāsaiś ca vividhair dīkṣābhir niyamais tathā
c ātmano laghutāṃ kṛtvā babhūva mṛgacāriṇī
a vaiḍūryāṅkurakalpāni mṛdūni haritāni ca
c carantī śaṣpamukhyāni tiktāni madhurāṇi ca
a sravantīnāṃ ca puṇyānāṃ surasāni śucīni ca
c pibantī vārimukhyāni śītāni vimalāni ca
a vaneṣu mṛgarājeṣu siṃhaviproṣiteṣu ca
c dāvāgnivipramukteṣu śūnyeṣu gahaneṣu ca
a carantī hariṇaiḥ sārdhaṃ mṛgīva vanacāriṇī
c cacāra vipulaṃ dharmaṃ brahmacaryeṇa saṃvṛtā
a yayātir api pūrveṣāṃ rājñāṃ vṛttam anuṣṭhitaḥ
c bahuvarṣasahasrāyur ayujat kāladharmaṇā
a pūrur yaduś ca dvau vaṃśau vardhamānau narottamau
c tābhyāṃ pratiṣṭhito loke paraloke ca nāhuṣaḥ
a mahīyate narapatir yayātiḥ svargam āsthitaḥ
c maharṣikalpo nṛpatiḥ svargāgryaphalabhug vibhuḥ
a bahuvarṣasahasrākhye kāle bahuguṇe gate
c rājarṣiṣu niṣaṇṇeṣu mahīyaḥsu maharṣiṣu
a avamene narān sarvān devān ṛṣigaṇāṃs tathā
c yayātir mūḍhavijñāno vismayāviṣṭacetanaḥ
a tatas taṃ bubudhe devaḥ śakro balaniṣūdanaḥ
c te ca rājarṣayaḥ sarve dhig dhig ity evam abruvan
a vicāraś ca samutpanno nirīkṣya nahuṣātmajam
c ko nv ayaṃ kasya vā rājñaḥ kathaṃ vā svargam āgataḥ
a karmaṇā kena siddho 'yaṃ kva vānena tapaś citam
c kathaṃ vā jñāyate svarge kena vā jñāyate 'py uta
a evaṃ vicārayantas te rājānaḥ svargavāsinaḥ
c dṛṣṭvā papracchur anyonyaṃ yayātiṃ nṛpatiṃ prati
a vimānapālāḥ śataśaḥ svargadvārābhirakṣiṇaḥ
c pṛṣṭā āsanapālāś ca na jānīmety athābruvan
a sarve te hy āvṛtajñānā nābhyajānanta taṃ nṛpam
c sa muhūrtād atha nṛpo hataujā abhavat tadā
 nārada uvāca
a atha pracalitaḥ sthānād āsanāc ca paricyutaḥ
c kampitenaiva manasā dharṣitaḥ śokavahninā
a mlānasragbhraṣṭavijñānaḥ prabhraṣṭamukuṭāṅgadaḥ
c vighūrṇan srastasarvāṅgaḥ prabhraṣṭābharaṇāmbaraḥ
a adṛśyamānas tān paśyann apaśyaṃś ca punaḥ punaḥ
c śūnyaḥ śūnyena manasā prapatiṣyan mahītalam
a kiṃ mayā manasā dhyātam aśubhaṃ dharmadūṣaṇam
c yenāhaṃ calitaḥ sthānād iti rājā vyacintayat
a te tu tatraiva rājānaḥ siddhāś cāpsarasas tathā
c apaśyanta nirālambaṃ yayātiṃ taṃ paricyutam
a athaitya puruṣaḥ kaś cit kṣīṇapuṇyanipātakaḥ
c yayātim abravīd rājan devarājasya śāsanāt
a atīva madamattas tvaṃ na kaṃ cin nāvamanyase
c mānena bhraṣṭaḥ svargas te nārhas tvaṃ pārthivātmaja
e na ca prajñāyase gaccha patasveti tam abravīt
a pateyaṃ satsv iti vacas trir uktvā nahuṣātmajaḥ
c patiṣyaṃś cintayām āsa gatiṃ gatimatāṃ varaḥ
a etasminn eva kāle tu naimiṣe pārthivarṣabhān
c caturo 'paśyata nṛpas teṣāṃ madhye papāta saḥ
a pratardano vasumanāḥ śibirauśīnaro 'ṣṭakaḥ
c vājapeyena yajñena tarpayanti sureśvaram
a teṣām adhvarajaṃ dhūmaṃ svargadvāram upasthitam
c yayātir upajighran vai nipapāta mahīṃ prati
a bhūmau svarge ca saṃbaddhāṃ nadīṃ dhūmamayīṃ nṛpaḥ
c sa gaṅgām iva gacchantīm ālambya jagatīpatiḥ
a śrīmatsv avabhṛthāgryeṣu caturṣu pratibandhuṣu
c madhye nipatito rājā lokapālopameṣu ca
a caturṣu hutakalpeṣu rājasiṃhamahāgniṣu
c papāta madhye rājarṣir yayātiḥ puṇyasaṃkṣaye
a tam āhuḥ pārthivāḥ sarve pratimānam iva śriyaḥ
c ko bhavān kasya vā bandhur deśasya nagarasya vā
a yakṣo vāpy atha vā devo gandharvo rākṣaso 'pi vā
c na hi mānuṣarūpo 'si ko vārthaḥ kāṅkṣitas tvayā
 yayātir uvāca
a yayātir asmi rājarṣiḥ kṣīṇapuṇyaś cyuto divaḥ
c pateyaṃ satsv iti dhyāyan bhavatsu patitas tataḥ
 rājāna ūcuḥ
a satyam etad bhavatu te kāṅkṣitaṃ puruṣarṣabha
c sarveṣāṃ naḥ kratuphalaṃ dharmaś ca pratigṛhyatām
 yayātir uvāca
a nāhaṃ pratigrahadhano brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo hy aham
c na ca me pravaṇā buddhiḥ parapuṇyavināśane
 nārada uvāca
a etasminn eva kāle tu mṛgacaryākramāgatām
c mādhavīṃ prekṣya rājānas te 'bhivādyedam abruvan
a kim āgamanakṛtyaṃ te kiṃ kurvaḥ śāsanaṃ tava
c ājñāpyā hi vayaṃ sarve tava putrās tapodhane
a teṣāṃ tad bhāṣitaṃ śrutvā mādhavī parayā mudā
c pitaraṃ samupāgacchad yayātiṃ sā vavanda ca
a dṛṣṭvā mūrdhnā natān putrāṃs tāpasī vākyam abravīt
c dauhitrās tava rājendra mama putrā na te parāḥ
e ime tvāṃ tārayiṣyanti diṣṭam etat purātanam
a ahaṃ te duhitā rājan mādhavī mṛgacāriṇī
c mayāpy upacito dharmas tato 'rdhaṃ pratigṛhyatām
a yasmād rājan narāḥ sarve apatyaphalabhāginaḥ
c tasmād icchanti dauhitrān yathā tvaṃ vasudhādhipa
a tatas te pārthivāḥ sarve śirasā jananīṃ tadā
c abhivādya namaskṛtya mātāmaham athābruvan
a uccair anupamaiḥ snigdhaiḥ svarair āpūrya medinīm
c mātāmahaṃ nṛpatayas tārayanto divaś cyutam
a atha tasmād upagato gālavo 'py āha pārthivam
c tapaso me 'ṣṭabhāgena svargam ārohatāṃ bhavān
 nārada uvāca
a pratyabhijñātamātro 'tha sadbhis tair narapuṃgavaḥ
b samāruroha nṛpatir aspṛśan vasudhātalam
c yayātir divyasaṃsthāno babhūva vigatajvaraḥ
d nārada uvāca
d pratyujjagāma taṃ sthānaṃ devalokaṃ narādhipaḥ
d avyāpya divyasaṃsthānaṃ babhūva vigatajvaraḥ
a divyamālyāmbaradharo divyābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ
c divyagandhaguṇopeto na pṛthvīm aspṛśat padā
a tato vasumanāḥ pūrvam uccair uccārayan vacaḥ
c khyāto dānapatir loke vyājahāra nṛpaṃ tadā
a prāptavān asmi yal loke sarvavarṇeṣv agarhayā
c tad apy atha ca dāsyāmi tena saṃyujyatāṃ bhavān
a yat phalaṃ dānaśīlasya kṣamāśīlasya yat phalam
c yac ca me phalam ādhāne tena saṃyujyatāṃ bhavān
a tataḥ pratardano 'py āha vākyaṃ kṣatriyapuṃgavaḥ
c yathā dharmaratir nityaṃ nityaṃ yuddhaparāyaṇaḥ
a prāptavān asmi yal loke kṣatradharmodbhavaṃ yaśaḥ
c vīraśabdaphalaṃ caiva tena saṃyujyatāṃ bhavān
d yathā dharmaratir nityaṃ tena satyena khaṃ vraja
a śibirauśīnaro dhīmān uvāca madhurāṃ giram
c yathā bāleṣu nārīṣu vaihāryeṣu tathaiva ca
a saṃgareṣu nipāteṣu tathāpad vyasaneṣu ca
c anṛtaṃ noktapūrvaṃ me tena satyena khaṃ vraja
a yathā prāṇāṃś ca rājyaṃ ca rājan karma sukhāni ca
c tyajeyaṃ na punaḥ satyaṃ tena satyena khaṃ vraja
a yathā satyena me dharmo yathā satyena pāvakaḥ
c prītaḥ śakraś ca satyena tena satyena khaṃ vraja
a aṣṭakas tv atha rājarṣiḥ kauśiko mādhavīsutaḥ
c anekaśatayajvānaṃ vacanaṃ prāha dharmavit
a śataśaḥ puṇḍarīkā me gosavāś ca citāḥ prabho
c kratavo vājapeyāś ca teṣāṃ phalam avāpnuhi
a na me ratnāni na dhanaṃ na tathānye paricchadāḥ
c kratuṣv anupayuktāni tena satyena khaṃ vraja
d yadi satyaṃ bravīmy etat tena satyena vai vraja
a yathā yathā hi jalpanti dauhitrās taṃ narādhipam
c tathā tathā vasumatīṃ tyaktvā rājā divaṃ yayau
a evaṃ sarve samastās te rājānaḥ sukṛtais tadā
c yayātiṃ svargato bhraṣṭaṃ tārayām āsur añjasā
a dauhitrāḥ svena dharmeṇa yajñadānakṛtena vai
c caturṣu rājavaṃśeṣu saṃbhūtāḥ kulavardhanāḥ
e mātāmahaṃ mahāprājñaṃ divam āropayanti te
 rājāna ūcuḥ
a rājadharmaguṇopetāḥ sarvadharmaguṇānvitāḥ
c dauhitrās te vayaṃ rājan divam āroha pārthivaḥ
 nārada uvāca
a sadbhir āropitaḥ svargaṃ pārthivair bhūridakṣiṇaiḥ
c abhyanujñāya dauhitrān yayātir divam āsthitaḥ
a abhivṛṣṭaś ca varṣeṇa nānāpuṣpasugandhinā
c pariṣvaktaś ca puṇyena vāyunā puṇyagandhinā
a acalaṃ sthānam āruhya dauhitraphalanirjitam
c karmabhiḥ svair upacito jajvāla parayā śriyā
a upagītopanṛttaś ca gandharvāpsarasāṃ gaṇaiḥ
c prītyā pratigṛhītaś ca svarge dundubhinisvanaiḥ
a abhiṣṭutaś ca vividhair devarājarṣicāraṇaiḥ
c arcitaś cottamārgheṇa daivatair abhinanditaḥ
a prāptaḥ svargaphalaṃ caiva tam uvāca pitāmahaḥ
c nirvṛtaṃ śāntamanasaṃ vacobhis tarpayann iva
a catuṣpādas tvayā dharmaś cito lokyena karmaṇā
c akṣayas tava loko 'yaṃ kīrtiś caivākṣayā divi
e punas tavādya rājarṣe sukṛteneha karmaṇā
a āvṛtaṃ tamasā cetaḥ sarveṣāṃ svargavāsinām
c yena tvāṃ nābhijānanti tato 'jñātvāsi pātitaḥ
a prītyaiva cāsi dauhitrais tāritas tvam ihāgataḥ
c sthānaṃ ca pratipanno 'si karmaṇā svena nirjitam
e acalaṃ śāśvataṃ puṇyam uttamaṃ dhruvam avyayam
 yayātir uvāca
a bhagavan saṃśayo me 'sti kaś cit taṃ chettum arhasi
c na hy anyam aham arhāmi praṣṭuṃ lokapitāmaha
a bahuvarṣasahasrāntaṃ prajāpālanavardhitam
c anekakratudānaughair arjitaṃ me mahat phalam
a kathaṃ tad alpakālena kṣīṇaṃ yenāsmi pātitaḥ
c bhagavan vettha lokāṃś ca śāśvatān mama nirjitān
d kathaṃ nu mama tatsarvaṃ vipranaṣṭaṃ mahādyute
 pitāmaha uvāca
a bahuvarṣasahasrāntaṃ prajāpālanavardhitam
c anekakratudānaughair yat tvayopārjitaṃ phalam
a tad anenaiva doṣeṇa kṣīṇaṃ yenāsi pātitaḥ
c abhimānena rājendra dhikkṛtaḥ svargavāsibhiḥ
a nāyaṃ mānena rājarṣe na balena na hiṃsayā
c na śāṭhyena na māyābhir loko bhavati śāśvataḥ
a nāvamānyās tvayā rājann avarotkṛṣṭamadhyamāḥ
b yayāteś caiva rājarṣeḥ suhṛdāṃ bhūtim icchatām
c na hi mānapradagdhānāṃ kaś cid asti samaḥ kva cit
a patanārohaṇam idaṃ kathayiṣyanti ye narāḥ
c viṣamāṇy api te prāptās tariṣyanti na saṃśayaḥ
 nārada uvāca
a eṣa doṣo 'bhimānena purā prāpto yayātinā
c nirbandhataś cātimātraṃ gālavena mahīpate
a śrotavyaṃ hitakāmānāṃ suhṛdāṃ bhūtim icchatām
c na kartavyo hi nirbandho nirbandho hi kṣayodayaḥ
a tasmāt tvam api gāndhāre mānaṃ krodhaṃ ca varjaya
c saṃdhatsva pāṇḍavair vīra saṃrambhaṃ tyaja pārthiva
d sa bhavān suhṛdo vaśyaṃ vaco gṛhṇātu mānṛtam
d samarthair vigrahaṃ kṛtvā viṣamastho bhaviṣyasi
d vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ
d evam ukto nṛpaśreṣṭha nāradena suyodhanaḥ
d nātiṣṭhad vacane tasmiṃs tatontas tasya tādṛśaḥ
a dadāti yat pārthiva yat karoti
yad vā tapas tapyati yaj juhoti
c na tasya nāśo 'sti na cāpakarṣo
nānyas tad aśnāti sa eva kartā
a idaṃ mahākhyānam anuttamaṃ mataṃ
bahuśrutānāṃ gataroṣarāgiṇām
c samīkṣya loke bahudhā pradhāvitā
trivargadṛṣṭiḥ pṛthivīm upāśnute
d etat puṇyatamaṃ rājan yayāteś caritaṃ mahat
d yac chrutvā śrāvayitvā ca svargaṃ yānti ha mānavāḥ
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a bhagavann evam evaitad yathā vadasi nārada
c icchāmi cāham apy evaṃ na tv īśo bhagavann aham
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a evam uktvā tataḥ kṛṣṇam abhyabhāṣata bhārata
c svargyaṃ lokyaṃ ca mām āttha dharmyaṃ nyāyyaṃ ca keśava
a na tv ahaṃ svavaśas tāta kriyamāṇaṃ na me priyam
b na maṃsyante durātmānaḥ putrā mama janārdana
c aṅga duryodhanaṃ kṛṣṇa mandaṃ śāstrātigaṃ mama
a anunetuṃ mahābāho yatasva puruṣottama
b na śṛṇoti mahābāho vacanaṃ sādhu bhāṣitam
b gāndhāryāś ca hṛṣīkeśa vidurasya ca dhīmataḥ
b anyeṣāṃ caiva suhṛdāṃ bhīṣmādīnāṃ hitaiṣiṇām
b sa tvaṃ pāpamatiṃ krūraṃ pāpacittam acetanam
b anuśādhi durātmānaṃ svayaṃ duryodhanaṃ nṛpam
c suhṛtkāryaṃ tu sumahat kṛtaṃ te syāj janārdana
a tato 'bhyāvṛtya vārṣṇeyo duryodhanam amarṣaṇam
c abravīn madhurāṃ vācaṃ sarvadharmārthatattvavit
a duryodhana nibodhedaṃ madvākyaṃ kurusattama
c samarthaṃ te viśeṣeṇa sānubandhasya bhārata
a mahāprājña kule jātaḥ sādhv etat kartum arhasi
c śrutavṛttopasaṃpannaḥ sarvaiḥ samudito guṇaiḥ
a dauṣkuleyā durātmāno nṛśaṃsā nirapatrapāḥ
c ta etad īdṛśaṃ kuryur yathā tvaṃ tāta manyase
a dharmārthayuktā loke 'smin pravṛttir lakṣyate satām
c asatāṃ viparītā tu lakṣyate bharatarṣabha
a viparītā tv iyaṃ vṛttir asakṛl lakṣyate tvayi
c adharmaś cānubandho 'tra ghoraḥ prāṇaharo mahān
a anekaśas tvannimittam ayaśasyaṃ ca bhārata
c tam anarthaṃ pariharann ātmaśreyaḥ kariṣyasi
a bhrātṝṇām atha bhṛtyānāṃ mitrāṇāṃ ca paraṃtapa
c adharmyād ayaśasyāc ca karmaṇas tvaṃ pramokṣyase
a prājñaiḥ śūrair mahotsāhair ātmavadbhir bahuśrutaiḥ
c saṃdhatsva puruṣavyāghra pāṇḍavair bharatarṣabha
a tad dhitaṃ ca priyaṃ caiva dhṛtarāṣṭrasya dhīmataḥ
c pitāmahasya droṇasya vidurasya mahāmateḥ
a kṛpasya somadattasya bāhlīkasya ca dhīmataḥ
c aśvatthāmno vikarṇasya saṃjayasya viśāṃ pate
a jñātīnāṃ caiva bhūyiṣṭhaṃ mitrāṇāṃ ca paraṃtapa
c śame śarma bhavet tāta sarvasya jagatas tathā
a hrīmān asi kule jātaḥ śrutavān anṛśaṃsavān
c tiṣṭha tāta pituḥ śāstre mātuś ca bharatarṣabha
a etac chreyo hi manyante pitā yac chāsti bhārata
c uttamāpadgataḥ sarvaḥ pituḥ smarati śāsanam
a rocate te pitus tāta pāṇḍavaiḥ saha saṃgamaḥ
c sāmātyasya kuruśreṣṭha tat tubhyaṃ tāta rocatām
a śrutvā yaḥ suhṛdāṃ śāstraṃ martyo na pratipadyate
c vipākānte dahaty enaṃ kiṃpākam iva bhakṣitam
a yas tu niḥśreyasaṃ vākyaṃ mohān na pratipadyate
c sa dīrghasūtro hīnārthaḥ paścāttāpena yujyate
a yas tu niḥśreyasaṃ śrutvā prāptam evābhipadyate
c ātmano matam utsṛjya sa loke sukham edhate
a yo 'rthakāmasya vacanaṃ prātikūlyān na mṛṣyate
c śṛṇoti pratikūlāni dviṣatāṃ vaśam eti saḥ
a satāṃ matam atikramya yo 'satāṃ vartate mate
c śocante vyasane tasya suhṛdo nacirād iva
a mukhyān amātyān utsṛjya yo nihīnān niṣevate
c sa ghorām āpadaṃ prāpya nottāram adhigacchati
a yo 'satsevī vṛthācāro na śrotā suhṛdāṃ sadā
c parān vṛṇīte svān dveṣṭi taṃ gauḥ śapati bhārata
a sa tvaṃ virudhya tair vīrair anyebhyas trāṇam icchasi
c aśiṣṭebhyo 'samarthebhyo mūḍhebhyo bharatarṣabha
a ko hi śakrasamāñ jñātīn atikramya mahārathān
c anyebhyas trāṇam āśaṃset tvad anyo bhuvi mānavaḥ
a janmaprabhṛti kaunteyā nityaṃ vinikṛtās tvayā
c na ca te jātu kupyanti dharmātmāno hi pāṇḍavāḥ
a mithyāpracaritās tāta janmaprabhṛti pāṇḍavāḥ
c tvayi samyaṅ mahābāho pratipannā yaśasvinaḥ
a tvayāpi pratipattavyaṃ tathaiva bharatarṣabha
c sveṣu bandhuṣu mukhyeṣu mā manyuvaśam anvagāḥ
a trivargayuktā prājñānām ārambhā bharatarṣabha
c dharmārthāv anurudhyante trivargāsaṃbhave narāḥ
a pṛthak tu viniviṣṭānāṃ dharmaṃ dhīro 'nurudhyate
c madhyamo 'rthaṃ kaliṃ bālaḥ kāmam evānurudhyate
a indriyaiḥ prasṛto lobhād dharmaṃ viprajahāti yaḥ
c kāmārthāv anupāyena lipsamāno vinaśyati
a kāmārthau lipsamānas tu dharmam evāditaś caret
c na hi dharmād apaity arthaḥ kāmo vāpi kadā cana
a upāyaṃ dharmam evāhus trivargasya viśāṃ pate
c lipsamāno hi tenāśu kakṣe 'gnir iva vardhate
a sa tvaṃ tātānupāyena lipsase bharatarṣabha
c ādhirājyaṃ mahad dīptaṃ prathitaṃ sarvarājasu
a ātmānaṃ takṣati hy eṣa vanaṃ paraśunā yathā
c yaḥ samyag vartamāneṣu mithyā rājan pravartate
d amitro nātikartavyo nātideyaḥ kadā cana
d jīvitaṃ hy api duḥkhārtā na tyajanti kadā cana
a na tasya hi matiṃ chindyād yasya necchet parābhavam
c avicchinnasya dhīrasya kalyāṇe dhīyate matiḥ
a tyaktātmānaṃ na bādheta triṣu lokeṣu bhārata
c apy anyaṃ prākṛtaṃ kiṃ cit kim u tān pāṇḍavarṣabhān
a amarṣavaśam āpanno na kiṃ cid budhyate naraḥ
c chidyate hy ātataṃ sarvaṃ pramāṇaṃ paśya bhārata
a śreyas te durjanāt tāta pāṇḍavaiḥ saha saṃgamaḥ
c tair hi saṃprīyamāṇas tvaṃ sarvān kāmān avāpsyasi
a pāṇḍavair nirjitāṃ bhūmiṃ bhuñjāno rājasattama
c pāṇḍavān pṛṣṭhataḥ kṛtvā trāṇam āśaṃsase 'nyataḥ
a duḥśāsane durviṣahe karṇe cāpi sasaubale
c eteṣv aiśvaryam ādhāya bhūtim icchasi bhārata
a na caite tava paryāptā jñāne dharmārthayos tathā
c vikrame cāpy aparyāptāḥ pāṇḍavān prati bhārata
a na hīme sarvarājānaḥ paryāptāḥ sahitās tvayā
c kruddhasya bhīmasenasya prekṣituṃ mukham āhave
a idaṃ saṃnihitaṃ tāta samagraṃ pārthivaṃ balam
c ayaṃ bhīṣmas tathā droṇaḥ karṇaś cāyaṃ tathā kṛpaḥ
a bhūriśravāḥ saumadattir aśvatthāmā jayadrathaḥ
c aśaktāḥ sarva evaite pratiyoddhuṃ dhanaṃjayam
a ajeyo hy arjunaḥ kruddhaḥ sarvair api surāsuraiḥ
c mānuṣair api gandharvair mā yuddhe ceta ādhithāḥ
a dṛśyatāṃ vā pumān kaś cit samagre pārthive bale
c yo 'rjunaṃ samare prāpya svastimān āvrajed gṛhān
a kiṃ te janakṣayeṇeha kṛtena bharatarṣabha
c yasmiñ jite jitaṃ te syāt pumān ekaḥ sa dṛśyatām
a yaḥ sa devān sagandharvān sayakṣāsurapannagān
c ajayat khāṇḍavaprasthe kas taṃ yudhyeta mānavaḥ
a tathā virāṭanagare śrūyate mahad adbhutam
c ekasya ca bahūnāṃ ca paryāptaṃ tan nidarśanam
d yuddhe yena mahādevaḥ sākṣāt saṃtoṣitaḥ śivaḥ
a tam ajeyam anādhṛṣyaṃ vijetuṃ jiṣṇum acyutam
c āśaṃsasīha samare vīram arjunam ūrjitam
a maddvitīyaṃ punaḥ pārthaṃ kaḥ prārthayitum arhati
c yuddhe pratīpam āyāntam api sākṣāt puraṃdaraḥ
a bāhubhyām uddhared bhūmiṃ dahet kruddha imāḥ prajāḥ
c pātayet tridivād devān yo 'rjunaṃ samare jayet
a paśya putrāṃs tathā bhrātṝñ jñātīn saṃbandhinas tathā
c tvatkṛte na vinaśyeyur ete bharatasattama
a astu śeṣaṃ kauravāṇāṃ mā parābhūd idaṃ kulam
c kulaghna iti nocyethā naṣṭakīrtir narādhipa
a tvām eva sthāpayiṣyanti yauvarājye mahārathāḥ
c mahārājye ca pitaraṃ dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ janeśvaram
a mā tāta śriyam āyāntīm avamaṃsthāḥ samudyatām
c ardhaṃ pradāya pārthebhyo mahatīṃ śriyam āpsyasi
a pāṇḍavaiḥ saṃśamaṃ kṛtvā kṛtvā ca suhṛdāṃ vacaḥ
c saṃprīyamāṇo mitraiś ca ciraṃ bhadrāṇy avāpsyasi
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tataḥ śāṃtanavo bhīṣmo duryodhanam amarṣaṇam
c keśavasya vacaḥ śrutvā provāca bharatarṣabha
a kṛṣṇena vākyam ukto 'si suhṛdāṃ śamam icchatā
c anupaśyasva tat tāta mā manyuvaśam anvagāḥ
a akṛtvā vacanaṃ tāta keśavasya mahātmanaḥ
c śreyo na jātu na sukhaṃ na kalyāṇam avāpsyasi
a dharmyam arthaṃ mahābāhur āha tvāṃ tāta keśavaḥ
c tam artham abhipadyasva mā rājan nīnaśaḥ prajāḥ
a imāṃ śriyaṃ prajvalitāṃ bhāratīṃ sarvarājasu
c jīvato dhṛtarāṣṭrasya daurātmyād bhraṃśayiṣyasi
a ātmānaṃ ca sahāmātyaṃ saputrapaśubāndhavam
c sahamitram asadbuddhyā jīvitād bhraṃśayiṣyasi
a atikrāman keśavasya tathyaṃ vacanam arthavat
c pituś ca bharataśreṣṭha vidurasya ca dhīmataḥ
a mā kulaghno 'ntapuruṣo durmatiḥ kāpathaṃ gamaḥ
c pitaraṃ mātaraṃ caiva vṛddhau śokāya mā dadaḥ
a atha droṇo 'bravīt tatra duryodhanam idaṃ vacaḥ
c amarṣavaśam āpannaṃ niḥśvasantaṃ punaḥ punaḥ
a dharmārthayuktaṃ vacanam āha tvāṃ tāta keśavaḥ
c tathā bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavas taj juṣasva narādhipa
a prājñau medhāvinau dāntāv arthakāmau bahuśrutau
c āhatus tvāṃ hitaṃ vākyaṃ tad ādatsva paraṃtapa
a anutiṣṭha mahāprājña kṛṣṇabhīṣmau yad ūcatuḥ
c mā vaco laghubuddhīnāṃ samāsthās tvaṃ paraṃtapa
a ye tvāṃ protsāhayanty ete naite kṛtyāya karhi cit
c vairaṃ pareṣāṃ grīvāyāṃ pratimokṣyanti saṃyuge
a mā kurūñ jīghanaḥ sarvān putrān bhrātṝṃs tathaiva ca
c vāsudevārjunau yatra viddhy ajeyaṃ balaṃ hi tat
a etac caiva mataṃ satyaṃ suhṛdoḥ kṛṣṇabhīṣmayoḥ
c yadi nādāsyase tāta paścāt tapsyasi bhārata
a yathoktaṃ jāmadagnyena bhūyān eva tato 'rjunaḥ
c kṛṣṇo hi devakīputro devair api durutsahaḥ
a kiṃ te sukhapriyeṇeha proktena bharatarṣabha
c etat te sarvam ākhyātaṃ yathecchasi tathā kuru
e na hi tvām utsahe vaktuṃ bhūyo bharatasattama
a tasmin vākyāntare vākyaṃ kṣattāpi viduro 'bravīt
c duryodhanam abhiprekṣya dhārtarāṣṭram amarṣaṇam
a duryodhana na śocāmi tvām ahaṃ bharatarṣabha
c imau tu vṛddhau śocāmi gāndhārīṃ pitaraṃ ca te
a yāv anāthau cariṣyete tvayā nāthena durhṛdā
c hatamitrau hatāmātyau lūnapakṣāv iva dvijau
a bhikṣukau vicariṣyete śocantau pṛthivīm imām
c kulaghnam īdṛśaṃ pāpaṃ janayitvā kupūruṣam
a atha duryodhanaṃ rājā dhṛtarāṣṭro 'bhyabhāṣata
c āsīnaṃ bhrātṛbhiḥ sārdhaṃ rājabhiḥ parivāritam
a duryodhana nibodhedaṃ śauriṇoktaṃ mahātmanā
c ādatsva śivam atyantaṃ yogakṣemavad avyayam
a anena hi sahāyena kṛṣṇenākliṣṭakarmaṇā
c iṣṭān sarvān abhiprāyān prāpsyāmaḥ sarvarājasu
a susaṃhitaḥ keśavena gaccha tāta yudhiṣṭhiram
c cara svastyayanaṃ kṛtsnaṃ bhāratānām anāmayam
a vāsudevena tīrthena tāta gacchasva saṃgamam
c kālaprāptam idaṃ manye mā tvaṃ duryodhanātigāḥ
a śamaṃ ced yācamānaṃ tvaṃ pratyākhyāsyasi keśavam
c tvadartham abhijalpantaṃ na tavāsty aparābhavaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a dhṛtarāṣṭravacaḥ śrutvā bhīṣmadroṇau samarthya tau
c duryodhanam idaṃ vākyam ūcatuḥ śāsanātigam
a yāvat kṛṣṇāv asaṃnaddhau yāvat tiṣṭhati gāṇḍivam
c yāvad dhaumyo na senāgnau juhotīha dviṣadbalam
a yāvan na prekṣate kruddhaḥ senāṃ tava yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c hrīniṣedho maheṣvāsas tāvac chāmyatu vaiśasam
a yāvan na dṛṣyate pārthaḥ sveṣv anīkeṣv avasthitaḥ
c bhīmaseno maheṣvāsas tāvac chāmyatu vaiśasam
a yāvan na carate mārgān pṛtanām abhiharṣayan
b bhīmaseno gadāpāṇis tāvat saṃśāmya pāṇḍavaiḥ
c yāvan na śātayaty ājau śirāṃsi gajayodhinām
a gadayā vīraghātinyā phalānīva vanaspateḥ
c kālena paripakvāni tāvac chāmyatu vaiśasam
a nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥ
c virāṭaś ca śikhaṇḍī ca śaiśupāliś ca daṃśitāḥ
a yāvan na praviśanty ete nakrā iva mahārṇavam
c kṛtāstrāḥ kṣipram asyantas tāvac chāmyatu vaiśasam
d yāvan na niśitā bāṇāḥ śarīreṣu mahīkṣitām
d yāvan na praviśanty ete tāvac chāmyatu vaiśasam
a yāvan na sukumāreṣu śarīreṣu mahīkṣitām
c gārdhrapatrāḥ patanty ugrās tāvac chāmyatu vaiśasam
a candanāgarudigdheṣu hāraniṣkadhareṣu ca
c noraḥsu yāvad yodhānāṃ maheṣvāsair maheṣavaḥ
a kṛtāstraiḥ kṣipram asyadbhir dūrapātibhir āyasāḥ
c abhilakṣyair nipātyante tāvac chāmyatu vaiśasam
a abhivādayamānaṃ tvāṃ śirasā rājakuñjaraḥ
c pāṇibhyāṃ pratigṛhṇātu dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a dhvajāṅkuśapatākāṅkaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ te sudakṣiṇaḥ
c skandhe nikṣipatāṃ bāhuṃ śāntaye bharatarṣabha
a ratnauṣadhisametena ratnāṅgulitalena ca
c upaviṣṭasya pṛṣṭhaṃ te pāṇinā parimārjatu
a śālaskandho mahābāhus tvāṃ svajāno vṛkodaraḥ
c sāmnābhivadatāṃ cāpi śāntaye bharatarṣabha
a arjunena yamābhyāṃ ca tribhis tair abhivāditaḥ
c mūrdhni tān samupāghrāya premṇābhivada pārthiva
a dṛṣṭvā tvāṃ pāṇḍavair vīrair bhrātṛbhiḥ saha saṃgatam
c yāvad ānandajāśrūṇi pramuñcantu narādhipāḥ
a ghuṣyatāṃ rājadhānīṣu sarvasaṃpan mahīkṣitām
c pṛthivī bhrātṛbhāvena bhujyatāṃ vijvaro bhava
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a śrutvā duryodhano vākyam apriyaṃ kurusaṃsadi
c pratyuvāca mahābāhuṃ vāsudevaṃ yaśasvinam
a prasamīkṣya bhavān etad vaktum arhati keśava
c mām eva hi viśeṣeṇa vibhāṣya parigarhase
a bhaktivādena pārthānām akasmān madhusūdana
c bhavān garhayate nityaṃ kiṃ samīkṣya balābalam
a bhavān kṣattā ca rājā ca ācāryo vā pitāmahaḥ
c mām eva parigarhante nānyaṃ kaṃ cana pārthivam
a na cāhaṃ lakṣaye kaṃ cid vyabhicāram ihātmanaḥ
c atha sarve bhavanto māṃ vidviṣanti sarājakāḥ
a na cāhaṃ kaṃ cid atyartham aparādham ariṃdama
c vicintayan prapaśyāmi susūkṣmam api keśava
a priyābhyupagate dyūte pāṇḍavā madhusūdana
c jitāḥ śakuninā rājyaṃ tatra kiṃ mama duṣkṛtam
a yat punar draviṇaṃ kiṃ cit tatrājīyanta pāṇḍavāḥ
c tebhya evābhyanujñātaṃ tat tadā madhusūdana
a aparādho na cāsmākaṃ yat te hy akṣaparājitāḥ
c ajeyā jayatāṃ śreṣṭha pārthāḥ pravrājitā vanam
a kena cāpy apavādena virudhyante 'ribhiḥ saha
c aśaktāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ kṛṣṇa prahṛṣṭāḥ pratyamitravat
a kim asmābhiḥ kṛtaṃ teṣāṃ kasmin vā punar āgasi
c dhārtarāṣṭrāñ jighāṃsanti pāṇḍavāḥ sṛñjayaiḥ saha
a na cāpi vayam ugreṇa karmaṇā vacanena vā
c vitrastāḥ praṇamāmeha bhayād api śatakratoḥ
a na ca taṃ kṛṣṇa paśyāmi kṣatradharmam anuṣṭhitam
c utsaheta yudhā jetuṃ yo naḥ śatrunibarhaṇa
a na hi bhīṣmakṛpadroṇāḥ sagaṇā madhusūdana
c devair api yudhā jetuṃ śakyāḥ kim uta pāṇḍavaiḥ
a svadharmam anutiṣṭhanto yadi mādhava saṃyuge
c śastreṇa nidhanaṃ kāle prāpsyāmaḥ svargam eva tat
a mukhyaś caivaiṣa no dharmaḥ kṣatriyāṇāṃ janārdana
c yac chayīmahi saṃgrāme śaratalpagatā vayam
a te vayaṃ vīraśayanaṃ prāpsyāmo yadi saṃyuge
c apraṇamyaiva śatrūṇāṃ na nas tapsyati mādhava
a kaś ca jātu kule jātaḥ kṣatradharmeṇa vartayan
c bhayād vṛttiṃ samīkṣyaivaṃ praṇamed iha kasya cit
a udyacched eva na named udyamo hy eva pauruṣam
c apy aparvaṇi bhajyeta na named iha kasya cit
a iti mātaṅgavacanaṃ parīpsanti hitepsavaḥ
c dharmāya caiva praṇamed brāhmaṇebhyaś ca madvidhaḥ
a acintayan kaṃ cid anyaṃ yāvajjīvaṃ tathācaret
c eṣa dharmaḥ kṣatriyāṇāṃ matam etac ca me sadā
a rājyāṃśaś cābhyanujñāto yo me pitrā purābhavat
c na sa labhyaḥ punar jātu mayi jīvati keśava
a yāvac ca rājā dhriyate dhṛtarāṣṭro janārdana
c nyastaśastrā vayaṃ te vāpy upajīvāma mādhava
a yady adeyaṃ purā dattaṃ rājyaṃ paravato mama
c ajñānād vā bhayād vāpi mayi bāle janārdana
a na tad adya punar labhyaṃ pāṇḍavair vṛṣṇinandana
c dhriyamāṇe mahābāho mayi saṃprati keśava
a yāvad dhi sūcyās tīkṣṇāyā vidhyed agreṇa mādhava
c tāvad apy aparityājyaṃ bhūmer naḥ pāṇḍavān prati
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tataḥ prahasya dāśārhaḥ krodhaparyākulekṣaṇaḥ
c duryodhanam idaṃ vākyam abravīt kurusaṃsadi
a lapsyase vīraśayanaṃ kāmam etad avāpsyasi
c sthiro bhava sahāmātyo vimardo bhavitā mahān
a yac caivaṃ manyase mūḍha na me kaś cid vyatikramaḥ
c pāṇḍaveṣv iti tat sarvaṃ nibodhata narādhipāḥ
a śriyā saṃtapyamānena pāṇḍavānāṃ mahātmanām
c tvayā durmantritaṃ dyūtaṃ saubalena ca bhārata
a kathaṃ ca jñātayas tāta śreyāṃsaḥ sādhusaṃmatāḥ
c tathānyāyyam upasthātuṃ jihmenājihmacāriṇaḥ
a akṣadyūtaṃ mahāprājña satām aratināśanam
c asatāṃ tatra jāyante bhedāś ca vyasanāni ca
a tad idaṃ vyasanaṃ ghoraṃ tvayā dyūtamukhaṃ kṛtam
c asamīkṣya sadācāraiḥ sārdhaṃ pāpānubandhanaiḥ
a kaś cānyo jñātibhāryāṃ vai viprakartuṃ tathārhati
c ānīya ca sabhāṃ vaktuṃ yathoktā draupadī tvayā
a kulīnā śīlasaṃpannā prāṇebhyo 'pi garīyasī
c mahiṣī pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ tathā vinikṛtā tvayā
a jānanti kuravaḥ sarve yathoktāḥ kurusaṃsadi
c duḥśāsanena kaunteyāḥ pravrajantaḥ paraṃtapāḥ
a samyagvṛtteṣv alubdheṣu satataṃ dharmacāriṣu
c sveṣu bandhuṣu kaḥ sādhuś cared evam asāṃpratam
a nṛśaṃsānām anāryāṇāṃ paruṣāṇāṃ ca bhāṣaṇam
c karṇaduḥśāsanābhyāṃ ca tvayā ca bahuśaḥ kṛtam
a saha mātrā pradagdhuṃ tān bālakān vāraṇāvate
c āsthitaḥ paramaṃ yatnaṃ na samṛddhaṃ ca tat tava
a ūṣuś ca suciraṃ kālaṃ pracchannāḥ pāṇḍavās tadā
c mātrā sahaikacakrāyāṃ brāhmaṇasya niveśane
a viṣeṇa sarpabandhaiś ca yatitāḥ pāṇḍavās tvayā
c sarvopāyair vināśāya na samṛddhaṃ ca tat tava
d evaṃvṛttaḥ kathaṃ rājye sthātum arhasi pāpakṛt
d sa rājyāc ca sukhāc caiva hāsyase kulapāṃsana
a evaṃbuddhiḥ pāṇḍaveṣu mithyāvṛttiḥ sadā bhavān
c kathaṃ te nāparādho 'sti pāṇḍaveṣu mahātmasu
d yac caibhyo yācamānebhyaḥ pitryam aṃśaṃ na ditsasi
d tac ca pāpa pradātāsi bhraṣṭaiśvaryo nipātitaḥ
a kṛtvā bahūny akāryāṇi pāṇḍaveṣu nṛśaṃsavat
c mithyāvṛttir anāryaḥ sann adya vipratipadyase
a mātāpitṛbhyāṃ bhīṣmeṇa droṇena vidureṇa ca
c śāmyeti muhur ukto 'si na ca śāmyasi pārthiva
a śame hi sumahān arthas tava pārthasya cobhayoḥ
c na ca rocayase rājan kim anyad buddhilāghavāt
a na śarma prāpsyase rājann utkramya suhṛdāṃ vacaḥ
c adharmyam ayaśasyaṃ ca kriyate pārthiva tvayā
a evaṃ bruvati dāśārhe duryodhanam amarṣaṇam
c duḥśāsana idaṃ vākyam abravīt kurusaṃsadi
a na cet saṃdhāsyase rājan svena kāmena pāṇḍavaiḥ
c baddhvā kila tvāṃ dāsyanti kuntīputrāya kauravāḥ
a vaikartanaṃ tvāṃ ca māṃ ca trīn etān manujarṣabha
c pāṇḍavebhyaḥ pradāsyanti bhīṣmo droṇaḥ pitā ca te
a bhrātur etad vacaḥ śrutvā dhārtarāṣṭraḥ suyodhanaḥ
c kruddhaḥ prātiṣṭhatotthāya mahānāga iva śvasan
a viduraṃ dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ ca mahārājaṃ ca bāhlikam
c kṛpaṃ ca somadattaṃ ca bhīṣmaṃ droṇaṃ janārdanam
a sarvān etān anādṛtya durmatir nirapatrapaḥ
c aśiṣṭavad amaryādo mānī mānyāvamānitā
a taṃ prasthitam abhiprekṣya bhrātaro manujarṣabham
c anujagmuḥ sahāmātyā rājānaś cāpi sarvaśaḥ
a sabhāyām utthitaṃ kruddhaṃ prasthitaṃ bhrātṛbhiḥ saha
c duryodhanam abhiprekṣya bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo 'bravīt
a dharmārthāv abhisaṃtyajya saṃrambhaṃ yo 'numanyate
c hasanti vyasane tasya durhṛdo nacirād iva
a durātmā rājaputro 'yaṃ dhārtarāṣṭro 'nupāyavit
c mithyābhimānī rājyasya krodhalobhavaśānugaḥ
a kālapakvam idaṃ manye sarvakṣatraṃ janārdana
c sarve hy anusṛtā mohāt pārthivāḥ saha mantribhiḥ
a bhīṣmasyātha vacaḥ śrutvā dāśārhaḥ puṣkarekṣaṇaḥ
c bhīṣmadroṇamukhān sarvān abhyabhāṣata vīryavān
a sarveṣāṃ kuruvṛddhānāṃ mahān ayam atikramaḥ
c prasahya mandam aiśvarye na niyacchata yan nṛpam
a tatra kāryam ahaṃ manye prāptakālam ariṃdamāḥ
c kriyamāṇe bhavec chreyas tat sarvaṃ śṛṇutānaghāḥ
a pratyakṣam etad bhavatāṃ yad vakṣyāmi hitaṃ vacaḥ
c bhavatām ānukūlyena yadi roceta bhāratāḥ
a bhojarājasya vṛddhasya durācāro hy anātmavān
c jīvataḥ pitur aiśvaryaṃ hṛtvā manyuvaśaṃ gataḥ
a ugrasenasutaḥ kaṃsaḥ parityaktaḥ sa bāndhavaiḥ
c jñātīnāṃ hitakāmena mayā śasto mahāmṛdhe
a āhukaḥ punar asmābhir jñātibhiś cāpi satkṛtaḥ
c ugrasenaḥ kṛto rājā bhojarājanyavardhanaḥ
a kaṃsam ekaṃ parityajya kulārthe sarvayādavāḥ
c saṃbhūya sukham edhante bhāratāndhakavṛṣṇayaḥ
a api cāpy avadad rājan parameṣṭhī prajāpatiḥ
c vyūḍhe devāsure yuddhe 'bhyudyateṣv āyudheṣu ca
a dvaidhībhūteṣu lokeṣu vinaśyatsu ca bhārata
c abravīt sṛṣṭimān devo bhagavāṃl lokabhāvanaḥ
a parābhaviṣyanty asurā daiteyā dānavaiḥ saha
c ādityā vasavo rudrā bhaviṣyanti divaukasaḥ
a devāsuramanuṣyāś ca gandharvoragarākṣasāḥ
c asmin yuddhe susaṃyattā haniṣyanti parasparam
d vartamānaṃ jagat sarvaṃ muhūrtān na bhaviṣyati
d anyanāśena jagato lokasya ca paraṃtapa
a iti matvābravīd dharmaṃ parameṣṭhī prajāpatiḥ
c varuṇāya prayacchaitān baddhvā daiteyadānavān
a evam uktas tato dharmo niyogāt parameṣṭhinaḥ
c varuṇāya dadau sarvān baddhvā daiteyadānavān
a tān baddhvā dharmapāśaiś ca svaiś ca pāśair jaleśvaraḥ
c varuṇaḥ sāgare yatto nityaṃ rakṣati dānavān
a tathā duryodhanaṃ karṇaṃ śakuniṃ cāpi saubalam
c baddhvā duḥśāsanaṃ cāpi pāṇḍavebhyaḥ prayacchata
a tyajet kulārthe puruṣaṃ grāmasyārthe kulaṃ tyajet
c grāmaṃ janapadasyārthe ātmārthe pṛthivīṃ tyajet
a rājan duryodhanaṃ baddhvā tataḥ saṃśāmya pāṇḍavaiḥ
c tvatkṛte na vinaśyeyuḥ kṣatriyāḥ kṣatriyarṣabha
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a kṛṣṇasya vacanaṃ śrutvā dhṛtarāṣṭro janeśvaraḥ
c viduraṃ sarvadharmajñaṃ tvaramāṇo 'bhyabhāṣata
a gaccha tāta mahāprājñāṃ gāndhārīṃ dīrghadarśinīm
c ānayeha tayā sārdham anuneṣyāmi durmatim
a yadi sāpi durātmānaṃ śamayed duṣṭacetasam
c api kṛṣṇāya suhṛdas tiṣṭhema vacane vayam
a api lobhābhibhūtasya panthānam anudarśayet
c durbuddher duḥsahāyasya samarthaṃ bruvatī vacaḥ
a api no vyasanaṃ ghoraṃ duryodhanakṛtaṃ mahat
c śamayec cirarātrāya yogakṣemavad avyayam
a rājñas tu vacanaṃ śrutvā viduro dīrghadarśinīm
c ānayām āsa gāndhārīṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrasya śāsanāt
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a eṣa gāndhāri putras te durātmā śāsanātigaḥ
c aiśvaryalobhād aiśvaryaṃ jīvitaṃ ca prahāsyati
a aśiṣṭavad amaryādaḥ pāpaiḥ saha durātmabhiḥ
c sabhāyā nirgato mūḍho vyatikramya suhṛdvacaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a sā bhartur vacanaṃ śrutvā rājaputrī yaśasvinī
c anvicchantī mahac chreyo gāndhārī vākyam abravīt
a ānayeha sutaṃ kṣipraṃ rājyakāmukam āturam
c na hi rājyam aśiṣṭena śakyaṃ dharmārthalopinā
d āptum āptaṃ tathāpīdam avinītena sarvathā
a tvaṃ hy evātra bhṛśaṃ garhyo dhṛtarāṣṭra sutapriyaḥ
c yo jānan pāpatām asya tatprajñām anuvartase
a sa eṣa kāmamanyubhyāṃ pralabdho moham āsthitaḥ
c aśakyo 'dya tvayā rājan vinivartayituṃ balāt
a rājyapradāne mūḍhasya bāliśasya durātmanaḥ
c duḥsahāyasya lubdhasya dhṛtarāṣṭro 'śnute phalam
a kathaṃ hi svajane bhedam upekṣeta mahāmatiḥ
c bhinnaṃ hi svajanena tvāṃ prasahiṣyanti śatravaḥ
a yā hi śakyā mahārāja sāmnā dānena vā punaḥ
c nistartum āpadaḥ sveṣu daṇḍaṃ kas tatra pātayet
a śāsanād dhṛtarāṣṭrasya duryodhanam amarṣaṇam
c mātuś ca vacanāt kṣattā sabhāṃ prāveśayat punaḥ
a sa mātur vacanākāṅkṣī praviveśa sabhāṃ punaḥ
c abhitāmrekṣaṇaḥ krodhān niḥśvasann iva pannagaḥ
a taṃ praviṣṭam abhiprekṣya putram utpatham āsthitam
c vigarhamāṇā gāndhārī samarthaṃ vākyam abravīt
a duryodhana nibodhedaṃ vacanaṃ mama putraka
c hitaṃ te sānubandhasya tathāyatyāṃ sukhodayam
d duryodhana yad āha tvāṃ pitā bharatasattama
d bhīṣmo droṇaḥ kṛpaḥ kṣattā suhṛdāṃ kuru tad vacaḥ
a bhīṣmasya tu pituś caiva mama cāpacitiḥ kṛtā
c bhaved droṇamukhānāṃ ca suhṛdāṃ śāmyatā tvayā
a na hi rājyaṃ mahāprājña svena kāmena śakyate
c avāptuṃ rakṣituṃ vāpi bhoktuṃ vā bharatarṣabha
a na hy avaśyendriyo rājyam aśnīyād dīrgham antaram
c vijitātmā tu medhāvī sa rājyam abhipālayet
a kāmakrodhau hi puruṣam arthebhyo vyapakarṣataḥ
c tau tu śatrū vinirjitya rājā vijayate mahīm
a lokeśvaraprabhutvaṃ hi mahad etad durātmabhiḥ
c rājyaṃ nāmepsitaṃ sthānaṃ na śakyam abhirakṣitum
a indriyāṇi mahat prepsur niyacched arthadharmayoḥ
c indriyair niyatair buddhir vardhate 'gnir ivendhanaiḥ
a avidhyeyāni hīmāni vyāpādayitum apy alam
c avidheyā ivādāntā hayāḥ pathi kusārathim
a avijitya ya ātmānam amātyān vijigīṣate
c ajitātmājitāmātyaḥ so 'vaśaḥ parihīyate
a ātmānam eva prathamaṃ deśarūpeṇa yo jayet
c tato 'mātyān amitrāṃś ca na moghaṃ vijigīṣate
a vaśyendriyaṃ jitāmātyaṃ dhṛtadaṇḍaṃ vikāriṣu
c parīkṣyakāriṇaṃ dhīram atyantaṃ śrīr niṣevate
a kṣudrākṣeṇeva jālena jhaṣāv apihitāv ubhau
c kāmakrodhau śarīrasthau prajñānaṃ tau vilumpataḥ
a yābhyāṃ hi devāḥ svaryātuḥ svargasyāpidadhur mukham
c bibhyato 'nuparāgasya kāmakrodhau sma vardhitau
a kāmaṃ krodhaṃ ca lobhaṃ ca dambhaṃ darpaṃ ca bhūmipaḥ
c samyag vijetuṃ yo veda sa mahīm abhijāyate
a satataṃ nigrahe yukta indriyāṇāṃ bhaven nṛpaḥ
c īpsann arthaṃ ca dharmaṃ ca dviṣatāṃ ca parābhavam
a kāmābhibhūtaḥ krodhād vā yo mithyā pratipadyate
c sveṣu cānyeṣu vā tasya na sahāyā bhavanty uta
a ekībhūtair mahāprājñaiḥ śūrair arinibarhaṇaiḥ
c pāṇḍavaiḥ pṛthivīṃ tāta bhokṣyase sahitaḥ sukhī
a yathā bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo droṇaś cāpi mahārathaḥ
c āhatus tāta tat satyam ajeyau kṛṣṇapāṇḍavau
a prapadyasva mahābāhuṃ kṛṣṇam akliṣṭakāriṇam
c prasanno hi sukhāya syād ubhayor eva keśavaḥ
a suhṛdām arthakāmānāṃ yo na tiṣṭhati śāsane
c prājñānāṃ kṛtavidyānāṃ sa naraḥ śatrunandanaḥ
a na yuddhe tāta kalyāṇaṃ na dharmārthau kutaḥ sukham
c na cāpi vijayo nityaṃ mā yuddhe ceta ādhithāḥ
a bhīṣmeṇa hi mahāprājña pitrā te bāhlikena ca
c datto 'ṃśaḥ pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ bhedād bhītair ariṃdama
a tasya caitat pradānasya phalam adyānupaśyasi
c yadbhuṅkṣe pṛthivīṃ sarvāṃ śūrair nihatakaṇṭakām
a prayaccha pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ yathocitam ariṃdama
c yadīcchasi sahāmātyo bhoktum ardhaṃ mahīkṣitām
a alam ardhaṃ pṛthivyās te sahāmātyasya jīvanam
c suhṛdāṃ vacane tiṣṭhan yaśaḥ prāpsyasi bhārata
a śrīmadbhir ātmavadbhir hi buddhimadbhir jitendriyaiḥ
c pāṇḍavair vigrahas tāta bhraṃśayen mahataḥ sukhāt
a nigṛhya suhṛdāṃ manyuṃ śādhi rājyaṃ yathocitam
c svam aṃśaṃ pāṇḍuputrebhyaḥ pradāya bharatarṣabha
a alam ahnā nikāro 'yaṃ trayodaśa samāḥ kṛtaḥ
c śamayainaṃ mahāprājña kāmakrodhasamedhitam
a na caiṣa śaktaḥ pārthānāṃ yas tvadartham abhīpsati
c sūtaputro dṛḍhakrodho bhrātā duḥśāsanaś ca te
a bhīṣme droṇe kṛpe karṇe bhīmasene dhanaṃjaye
c dhṛṣṭadyumne ca saṃkruddhe na syuḥ sarvāḥ prajā dhruvam
a amarṣavaśam āpanno mā kurūṃs tāta jīghanaḥ
c sarvā hi pṛthivī spṛṣṭā tvat pāṇḍavakṛte vadham
a yac ca tvaṃ manyase mūḍha bhīṣmadroṇakṛpādayaḥ
c yotsyante sarvaśaktyeti naitad adyopapadyate
a samaṃ hi rājyaṃ prītiś ca sthānaṃ ca vijitātmanām
c pāṇḍaveṣv atha yuṣmāsu dharmas tv abhyadhikas tataḥ
a rājapiṇḍabhayād ete yadi hāsyanti jīvitam
c na hi śakṣyanti rājānaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram udīkṣitum
a na lobhād arthasaṃpattir narāṇām iha dṛśyate
c tad alaṃ tāta lobhena praśāmya bharatarṣabha
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tat tu vākyam anādṛtya so 'rthavan mātṛbhāṣitam
c punaḥ pratasthe saṃrambhāt sakāśam akṛtātmanām
a tataḥ sabhāyā nirgamya mantrayām āsa kauravaḥ
c saubalena matākṣeṇa rājñā śakuninā saha
d duryodhanaṃ dhārtarāṣṭraṃ karṇaṃ duḥśāsano 'bravīt
d no cet saṃdhāsyase rājan svena kāmena pāṇḍavaiḥ
d baddhvaiva tvāṃ pradāsyanti pāṇḍuputrāya bhārata
d vaikartanaṃ tvāṃ ca māṃ ca trīn etān bharatarṣabha
d pāṇḍavebhyaḥ pradāsyanti bhīṣmadroṇau pitā ca te
d duḥśāsanasya tad vākyaṃ niśamya bharatarṣabha
d duryodhano dhārtarāṣṭro niḥśvasya prahasann iva
d ekāntam upasaṃgamya mantraṃ punar amantrayat
a duryodhanasya karṇasya śakuneḥ saubalasya ca
c duḥśāsanacaturthānām idam āsīd viceṣṭitam
a purāyam asmān gṛhṇāti kṣiprakārī janārdanaḥ
c sahito dhṛtarāṣṭreṇa rājñā śāṃtanavena ca
a vayam eva hṛṣīkeśaṃ nigṛhṇīma balād iva
c prasahya puruṣavyāghram indro vairocaniṃ yathā
a śrutvā gṛhītaṃ vārṣṇeyaṃ pāṇḍavā hatacetasaḥ
c nirutsāhā bhaviṣyanti bhagnadaṃṣṭrā ivoragāḥ
a ayaṃ hy eṣāṃ mahābāhuḥ sarveṣāṃ śarma varma ca
c asmin gṛhīte varade ṛṣabhe sarvasātvatām
e nirudyamā bhaviṣyanti pāṇḍavāḥ somakaiḥ saha
a tasmād vayam ihaivainaṃ keśavaṃ kṣiprakāriṇam
c krośato dhṛtarāṣṭrasya baddhvā yotsyāmahe ripūn
a teṣāṃ pāpam abhiprāyaṃ pāpānāṃ duṣṭacetasām
c iṅgitajñaḥ kaviḥ kṣipram anvabudhyata sātyakiḥ
a tadartham abhiniṣkramya hārdikyena sahāsthitaḥ
c abravīt kṛtavarmāṇaṃ kṣipraṃ yojaya vāhinīm
a vyūḍhānīkaḥ sabhādvāram upatiṣṭhasva daṃśitaḥ
c yāvad ākhyāmy ahaṃ caitat kṛṣṇāyākliṣṭakarmaṇe
a sa praviśya sabhāṃ vīraḥ siṃho giriguhām iva
c ācaṣṭa tam abhiprāyaṃ keśavāya mahātmane
a dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ tataś caiva viduraṃ cānvabhāṣata
c teṣām etam abhiprāyam ācacakṣe smayann iva
a dharmād apetam arthāc ca karma sādhuvigarhitam
c mandāḥ kartum ihecchanti na cāvāpyaṃ kathaṃ cana
a purā vikurvate mūḍhāḥ pāpātmānaḥ samāgatāḥ
c dharṣitāḥ kāmamanyubhyāṃ krodhalobhavaśānugāḥ
a imaṃ hi puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ jighṛkṣanty alpacetasaḥ
c paṭenāgniṃ prajvalitaṃ yathā bālā yathā jaḍāḥ
a sātyakes tad vacaḥ śrutvā viduro dīrghadarśivān
c dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ mahābāhum abravīt kurusaṃsadi
d yathā vārāṇasī dagdhā sāśvā sarathakuñjarā
d sānubandhas tu kṛṣṇena kāśīnām ṛṣabho hataḥ
d tathā nāgapuraṃ dagdhvā śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ
d svayaṃ kāleśvaro bhūtvā nāśayiṣyati kauravān
d pārijātaharaṃ hy enam ekaṃ yadusukhāvaham
d nābhyavartata saṃrabdho vṛtrahā vasubhiḥ saha
d prāpya nirmocane pāśān ṣaṭsahasrāṃs tarasvinaḥ
d hṛtās te vāsudevena hy upasaṃkramya kauravān
d dvāram āsādya saubhasya vidhūya gadayā girim
d dyumatsenaḥ sahāmātyaḥ kṛṣṇena vinipātitaḥ
d śeṣavattvāt kurūṇāṃ tu dharmāpekṣī tathācyutaḥ
d kṣamate puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ śaktaḥ san pāpakarmaṇām
d ete hi yadi govindam icchanti saha rājabhiḥ
d adyaivātithayaḥ sarve bhaviṣyanti yamasya te
d yathā vāyos tṛṇāgrāṇi vaśaṃ yānti balīyasaḥ
d tathā cakrabhṛtaḥ sarve vaśam eṣyanti kauravāḥ
a rājan parītakālās te putrāḥ sarve paraṃtapa
c ayaśasyam aśakyaṃ ca karma kartuṃ samudyatāḥ
a imaṃ hi puṇḍarīkākṣam abhibhūya prasahya ca
c nigrahītuṃ kilecchanti sahitā vāsavānujam
a imaṃ puruṣaśārdūlam apradhṛṣyaṃ durāsadam
c āsādya na bhaviṣyanti pataṃgā iva pāvakam
d ete na śaktāḥ sarve hi sāhasāt kartum udyatāḥ
a ayam icchan hi tān sarvān yatamānāñ janārdanaḥ
c siṃho mṛgān iva kruddho gamayed yamasādanam
a na tv ayaṃ ninditaṃ karma kuryāt kṛṣṇaḥ kathaṃ cana
c na ca dharmād apakrāmed acyutaḥ puruṣottamaḥ
a vidureṇaivam ukte tu keśavo vākyam abravīt
c dhṛtarāṣṭram abhiprekṣya suhṛdāṃ śṛṇvatāṃ mithaḥ
a rājann ete yadi kruddhā māṃ nigṛhṇīyur ojasā
c ete vā mām ahaṃ vainān anujānīhi pārthiva
a etān hi sarvān saṃrabdhān niyantum aham utsahe
c na tv ahaṃ ninditaṃ karma kuryāṃ pāpaṃ kathaṃ cana
a pāṇḍavārthe hi lubhyantaḥ svārthād dhāsyanti te sutāḥ
c ete ced evam icchanti kṛtakāryo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c   sāmātyāḥ saha bandhubhiḥ
c adyaiva kṛtakṛtyas tu
a adyaiva hy aham etāṃś ca ye caitān anu bhārata
b nigṛhya rājye rājānaṃ sthāpayiṣyāmi pāṇḍavam
b eṣa me niścayo rājan yady eṣo 'sya viniścayaḥ
b nardantu sahitāḥ śaṅkhāḥ paṇavānakanisvanaiḥ
b anāyāsena pārthānāṃ vartatāṃ ca śivaṃ mahat
c nigṛhya rājan pārthebhyo dadyāṃ kiṃ duṣkṛtaṃ bhavet
a idaṃ tu na pravarteyaṃ ninditaṃ karma bhārata
c saṃnidhau te mahārāja krodhajaṃ pāpabuddhijam
a eṣa duryodhano rājan yathecchati tathāstu tat
c ahaṃ tu sarvān samayān anujānāmi bhārata
a etac chrutvā tu viduraṃ dhṛtarāṣṭro 'bhyabhāṣata
c kṣipram ānaya taṃ pāpaṃ rājyalubdhaṃ suyodhanam
a sahamitraṃ sahāmātyaṃ sasodaryaṃ sahānugam
c śaknuyāṃ yadi panthānam avatārayituṃ punaḥ
a tato duryodhanaṃ kṣattā punaḥ prāveśayat sabhām
c akāmaṃ bhrātṛbhiḥ sārdhaṃ rājabhiḥ parivāritam
a atha duryodhanaṃ rājā dhṛtarāṣṭro 'bhyabhāṣata
c karṇaduḥśāsanābhyāṃ ca rājabhiś cābhisaṃvṛtam
a nṛśaṃsa pāpabhūyiṣṭha kṣudrakarmasahāyavān
c pāpaiḥ sahāyaiḥ saṃhatya pāpaṃ karma cikīrṣasi
a aśakyam ayaśasyaṃ ca sadbhiś cāpi vigarhitam
c yathā tvādṛśako mūḍho vyavasyet kulapāṃsanaḥ
a tvam imaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣam apradhṛṣyaṃ durāsadam
c pāpaiḥ sahāyaiḥ saṃhatya nigrahītuṃ kilecchasi
a yo na śakyo balātkartuṃ devair api savāsavaiḥ
c taṃ tvaṃ prārthayase manda bālaś candramasaṃ yathā
a devair manuṣyair gandharvair asurair uragaiś ca yaḥ
c na soḍhuṃ samare śakyas taṃ na budhyasi keśavam
a durgrahaḥ pāṇinā vāyur duḥsparśaḥ pāṇinā śaśī
c durdharā pṛthivī mūrdhnā durgrahaḥ keśavo balāt
a ity ukte dhṛtarāṣṭreṇa kṣattāpi viduro 'bravīt
c duryodhanam abhiprekṣya dhārtarāṣṭram amarṣaṇam
a saubhadvāre vānarendro dvivido nāma nāmataḥ
c śilāvarṣeṇa mahatā chādayām āsa keśavam
d duryodhana nibodhedaṃ vacanaṃ mama sāṃpratam
a grahītukāmo vikramya sarvayatnena mādhavam
c grahītuṃ nāśakat tatra taṃ tvaṃ prārthayase balāt
a nirmocane ṣaṭ sahasrāḥ pāśair baddhvā mahāsurāḥ
c grahītuṃ nāśakaṃś cainaṃ taṃ tvaṃ prārthayase balāt
a prāgjyotiṣagataṃ śauriṃ narakaḥ saha dānavaiḥ
c grahītuṃ nāśakat tatra taṃ tvaṃ prārthayase balāt
d anekayugavarṣāyur nihatya narakaṃ mṛdhe
d nītvā kanyāsahasrāṇi upayeme yathāvidhi
a anena hi hatā bālye pūtanā śiśunā tathā
c govardhano dhāritaś ca gavārthe bharatarṣabha
a ariṣṭo dhenukaś caiva cāṇūraś ca mahābalaḥ
c aśvarājaś ca nihataḥ kaṃsaś cāriṣṭam ācaran
a jarāsaṃdhaś ca vakraś ca śiśupālaś ca vīryavān
c bāṇaś ca nihataḥ saṃkhye rājānaś ca niṣūditāḥ
a varuṇo nirjito rājā pāvakaś cāmitaujasā
c pārijātaṃ ca haratā jitaḥ sākṣāc chacīpatiḥ
a ekārṇave śayānena hatau tau madhukaiṭabhau
b janmāntaram upāgamya hatavān vālinaṃ tathā
b anye ca bhrātaras tasya kumbhakarṇādayo mṛdhe
b bibhīṣaṇaṃ tu saṃsthāpya sītāṃ cādāya maithilīm
b pālayām āsa vidhivad rājyaṃ nihatakaṇṭakam
c janmāntaram upāgamya hayagrīvas tathā hataḥ
a ayaṃ kartā na kriyate kāraṇaṃ cāpi pauruṣe
c yad yad icched ayaṃ śauris tat tat kuryād ayatnataḥ
a taṃ na budhyasi govindaṃ ghoravikramam acyutam
c āśīviṣam iva kruddhaṃ tejorāśim anirjitam
a pradharṣayan mahābāhuṃ kṛṣṇam akliṣṭakāriṇam
c pataṃgo 'gnim ivāsādya sāmātyo na bhaviṣyasi
d tato 'nādṛtya vākyāni duḥśāsanapurogamāḥ
d niyantumanaso duṣṭāḥ kṛṣṇaṃ matvā suyodhanam
d babandhuḥ pāśajālena devamāyāvimohitāḥ
d prākrośantaṃ ca rājānaṃ pratimucya savismayāḥ
d ity adhikaṃ kva cit pustake dṛṣṭaṃ tad asaṃbaddhaṃ pratīyate
d katham āsīd idam iti tad adbhutam ivābhavat
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a vidureṇaivam ukte tu keśavaḥ śatrupūgahā
c duryodhanaṃ dhārtarāṣṭram abhyabhāṣata vīryavān
d yadā yadā paśyasi vānaradhvajaṃ
d dhanurdharaṃ pāṇḍavamadhyamaṃ raṇe
d gadāgrahastaṃ bhramataṃ vṛkodaraṃ
d tadā tadā dāsyasi sarvamedinīm
a eko 'ham iti yan mohān manyase māṃ suyodhana
c paribhūya ca durbuddhe grahītuṃ māṃ cikīrṣasi
a ihaiva pāṇḍavāḥ sarve tathaivāndhakavṛṣṇayaḥ
c ihādityāś ca rudrāś ca vasavaś ca maharṣibhiḥ
a evam uktvā jahāsoccaiḥ keśavaḥ paravīrahā
c tasya saṃsmayataḥ śaurer vidyudrūpā mahātmanaḥ
d yugapac ca viniṣpetuḥ sahitāḥ sarvadevatāḥ
e aṅguṣṭhamātrās tridaśā mumucuḥ pāvakārciṣaḥ
a tasya brahmā lalāṭastho rudro vakṣasi cābhavat
c lokapālā bhujeṣv āsann agnir āsyād ajāyata
d ugrāyudhadharāḥ sarve divyena vapuṣānvitāḥ
a ādityāś caiva sādhyāś ca vasavo 'thāśvināv api
c marutaś ca sahendreṇa viśvedevās tathaiva ca
e babhūvuś caiva rūpāṇi yakṣagandharvarakṣasām
a prādurāstāṃ tathā dorbhyāṃ saṃkarṣaṇadhanaṃjayau
c dakṣiṇe 'thārjuno dhanvī halī rāmaś ca savyataḥ
a bhīmo yudhiṣṭhiraś caiva mādrīputrau ca pṛṣṭhataḥ
c andhakā vṛṣṇayaś caiva pradyumnapramukhās tataḥ
a agre babhūvuḥ kṛṣṇasya samudyatamahāyudhāḥ
c śaṅkhacakragadāśaktiśārṅgalāṅgalanandakāḥ
a adṛśyantodyatāny eva sarvapraharaṇāni ca
c nānābāhuṣu kṛṣṇasya dīpyamānāni sarvaśaḥ
a netrābhyāṃ nas tataś caiva śrotrābhyāṃ ca samantataḥ
c prādurāsan mahāraudrāḥ sadhūmāḥ pāvakārciṣaḥ
e romakūpeṣu ca tathā sūryasyeva marīcayaḥ
f sahasracaraṇaḥ śrīmāñ śatabāhuḥ sahasradṛk
f talāni nāgalokaś ca gulphādho dadṛśe tadā
f candrasūryau tathā netre grahā vai sarvataḥ sthitāḥ
f ūrdhvalokāś ca sarve 'pi kukṣau tasya vyavasthitāḥ
f saritaḥ sāgarāś caiva svedas tasya mahātmanaḥ
f asthīni parvatāḥ sarve vṛkṣā romāṇi tasya hi
f nimeṣaṇaṃ rātryahani jihvāyāṃ śāradā tathā
a taṃ dṛṣṭvā ghoram ātmānaṃ keśavasya mahātmanaḥ
c nyamīlayanta netrāṇi rājānas trastacetasaḥ
a ṛte droṇaṃ ca bhīṣmaṃ ca viduraṃ ca mahāmatim
c saṃjayaṃ ca mahābhāgam ṛṣīṃś caiva tapodhanān
e prādāt teṣāṃ sa bhagavān divyaṃ cakṣur janārdanaḥ
f tatrādbhutam abhūd rājan dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ svacakṣuṣī
f labdhavān vāsudevasya viśvarūpadidṛkṣayā
f labdhacakṣuṣam āsīnaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ narādhipāḥ
f vismitā ṛṣibhiḥ sārdhaṃ tuṣṭuvur madhusūdanam
f dhṛtarāṣṭrāya pradadau bhagavān divyacakṣuṣī
f dadarśa paramaṃ rūpaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭro 'mbikāsutaḥ
f tato devāḥ sagandharvāḥ kiṃnarāś ca mahoragāḥ
f ṛṣayaś ca mahābhāgā lokapālaiḥ samanvitāḥ
f praṇamya śirasā devaṃ tuṣṭuvuḥ prāñjali sthitāḥ
f krodhaṃ prabho saṃhara saṃhara svaṃ
f rūpaṃ ca yad darśitam ātmasaṃstham
f yāvat tv ime devagaṇaiḥ sametā
f lokāḥ samastā bhuvi nāśam īyuḥ
f tvaṃ ca kartā vikartā ca tvam eva parirakṣase
f tvayā vyāptam idaṃ sarvaṃ jagat sthāvarajaṅgamam
f kiyanmātrā mahīpālāḥ kiṃvīryāḥ kiṃparākramāḥ
f yeṣām arthe mahābāho divyaṃ rūpaṃ pradarśivān
f evam uccāritā vācaḥ saha devair vibhus tathā
a tad dṛṣṭvā mahad āścaryaṃ mādhavasya sabhātale
c devadundubhayo neduḥ puṣpavarṣaṃ papāta ca
d tvam eva puṇḍarīkākṣa sarvasya jagataḥ prabhuḥ
d tasmān me yādavaśreṣṭha prasādaṃ kartum arhasi
d bhagavan mama netrāṇām antardhānaṃ vṛṇe punaḥ
d vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
d bhavantaṃ dṛṣṭavān asmi nānyaṃ draṣṭum ihotsahe
d tato 'bravīn mahābāhur dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ janārdanaḥ
d adṛśyamāne netre dve bhavetāṃ kurunandana
a cacāla ca mahī kṛtsnā sāgaraś cāpi cukṣubhe
c vismayaṃ paramaṃ jagmuḥ pārthivā bharatarṣabha
d duryodhano 'tha durbuddhiḥ karṇādyair durjanaiḥ saha
d mādhavasya vapur dṛṣṭvā babhūva trastacetanaḥ
a tataḥ sa puruṣavyāghraḥ saṃjahāra vapuḥ svakam
c tāṃ divyām adbhutāṃ citrām ṛddhimattām ariṃdamaḥ
d sarvalokeśvaraḥ śauriḥ sarvadevābhivanditaḥ
a tataḥ sātyakim ādāya pāṇau hārdikyam eva ca
c ṛṣibhis tair anujñāto niryayau madhusūdanaḥ
a ṛṣayo 'ntarhitā jagmus tatas te nāradādayaḥ
c tasmin kolāhale vṛtte tad adbhutam abhūt tadā
a taṃ prasthitam abhiprekṣya kauravāḥ saha rājabhiḥ
c anujagmur naravyāghraṃ devā iva śatakratum
a acintayann ameyātmā sarvaṃ tad rājamaṇḍalam
c niścakrāma tataḥ śauriḥ sadhūma iva pāvakaḥ
a tato rathena śubhreṇa mahatā kiṅkiṇīkinā
c hemajālavicitreṇa laghunā meghanādinā
a sūpaskareṇa śubhreṇa vaiyāghreṇa varūthinā
c sainyasugrīvayuktena pratyadṛśyata dārukaḥ
a tathaiva ratham āsthāya kṛtavarmā mahārathaḥ
c vṛṣṇīnāṃ saṃmato vīro hārdikyaḥ pratyadṛśyata
a upasthitarathaṃ śauriṃ prayāsyantam ariṃdamam
c dhṛtarāṣṭro mahārājaḥ punar evābhyabhāṣata
a yāvad balaṃ me putreṣu paśyasy etaj janārdana
c pratyakṣaṃ te na te kiṃ cit parokṣaṃ śatrukarśana
a kurūṇāṃ śamam icchantaṃ yatamānaṃ ca keśava
c viditvaitām avasthāṃ me nātiśaṅkitum arhasi
d nirguṇair api govinda putrair upakṛtaṃ mama
d trailokyanātha pādau te yadayatnān namaskṛtau
a na me pāpo 'sty abhiprāyaḥ pāṇḍavān prati keśava
c jñātam eva hi te vākyaṃ yan mayoktaḥ suyodhanaḥ
a jānanti kuravaḥ sarve rājānaś caiva pārthivāḥ
c śame prayatamānaṃ māṃ sarvayatnena mādhava
a tato 'bravīn mahābāhur dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ janeśvaram
c droṇaṃ pitāmahaṃ bhīṣmaṃ kṣattāraṃ bāhlikaṃ kṛpam
a pratyakṣam etad bhavatāṃ yad vṛttaṃ kurusaṃsadi
c yathā cāśiṣṭavan mando roṣād asakṛd utthitaḥ
a vadaty anīśam ātmānaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭro mahīpatiḥ
c āpṛcche bhavataḥ sarvān gamiṣyāmi yudhiṣṭhiram
a āmantrya prasthitaṃ śauriṃ rathasthaṃ puruṣarṣabham
c anujagmur maheṣvāsāḥ pravīrā bharatarṣabhāḥ
a bhīṣmo droṇaḥ kṛpaḥ kṣattā dhṛtarāṣṭro 'tha bāhlikaḥ
c aśvatthāmā vikarṇaś ca yuyutsuś ca mahārathaḥ
a tato rathena śubhreṇa mahatā kiṅkiṇīkinā
c kurūṇāṃ paśyatāṃ prāyāt pṛthāṃ draṣṭuṃ pitṛṣvasām
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a praviśyātha gṛhaṃ tasyāś caraṇāv abhivādya ca
c ācakhyau tat samāsena yad vṛttaṃ kurusaṃsadi
 vāsudeva uvāca
a uktaṃ bahuvidhaṃ vākyaṃ grahaṇīyaṃ sahetukam
c ṛṣibhiś ca mayā caiva na cāsau tad gṛhītavān
a kālapakvam idaṃ sarvaṃ duryodhanavaśānugam
b sarvaṃ kṣatraṃ kṣaṇenaiva dahyate pārthavahninā
c āpṛcche bhavatīṃ śīghraṃ prayāsye pāṇḍavān prati
a kiṃ vācyāḥ pāṇḍaveyās te bhavatyā vacanān mayā
c tad brūhi tvaṃ mahāprājñe śuśrūṣe vacanaṃ tava
 kunty uvāca
a brūyāḥ keśava rājānaṃ dharmātmānaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
c bhūyāṃs te hīyate dharmo mā putraka vṛthā kṛthāḥ
a śrotriyasyeva te rājan mandakasyāvipaścitaḥ
c anuvākahatā buddhir dharmam evaikam īkṣate
a aṅgāvekṣasva dharmaṃ tvaṃ yathā sṛṣṭaḥ svayaṃbhuvā
c urastaḥ kṣatriyaḥ sṛṣṭo bāhuvīryopajīvitā
e krūrāya karmaṇe nityaṃ prajānāṃ paripālane
a śṛṇu cātropamām ekāṃ yā vṛddhebhyaḥ śrutā mayā
c mucukundasya rājarṣer adadāt pṛthivīm imām
e purā vaiśravaṇaḥ prīto na cāsau tāṃ gṛhītavān
a bāhuvīryārjitaṃ rājyam aśnīyām iti kāmaye
c tato vaiśravaṇaḥ prīto vismitaḥ samapadyata
a mucukundas tato rājā so 'nvaśāsad vasuṃdharām
c bāhuvīryārjitāṃ samyak kṣatradharmam anuvrataḥ
a yaṃ hi dharmaṃ carantīha prajā rājñā surakṣitāḥ
c caturthaṃ tasya dharmasya rājā bhārata vindati
a rājā carati ced dharmaṃ devatvāyaiva kalpate
c sa ced adharmaṃ carati narakāyaiva gacchati
a daṇḍanītiḥ svadharmeṇa cāturvarṇyaṃ niyacchati
c prayuktā svāminā samyag adharmebhyaś ca yacchati
a daṇḍanītyāṃ yadā rājā samyak kārtsnyena vartate
c tadā kṛtayugaṃ nāma kālaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ pravartate
a kālo vā kāraṇaṃ rājño rājā vā kālakāraṇam
c iti te saṃśayo mā bhūd rājā kālasya kāraṇam
a rājā kṛtayugasraṣṭā tretāyā dvāparasya ca
c yugasya ca caturthasya rājā bhavati kāraṇam
a kṛtasya kāraṇād rājā svargam atyantam aśnute
c tretāyāḥ kāraṇād rājā svargaṃ nātyantam aśnute
e pravartanād dvāparasya yathābhāgam upāśnute
f kaleḥ pravartanād rājā pāpam atyantam aśnute
a tato vasati duṣkarmā narake śāśvatīḥ samāḥ
a   kālaṃ bhavati kāraṇam
a anityarājā vasati
c rājadoṣeṇa hi jagat spṛśyate jagataḥ sa ca
a rājadharmān avekṣasva pitṛpaitāmahocitān
c naitad rājarṣivṛttaṃ hi yatra tvaṃ sthātum icchasi
a na hi vaiklavyasaṃsṛṣṭa ānṛśaṃsye vyavasthitaḥ
c prajāpālanasaṃbhūtaṃ kiṃ cit prāpa phalaṃ nṛpaḥ
a na hy etām āśiṣaṃ pāṇḍur na cāhaṃ na pitāmahaḥ
c prayuktavantaḥ pūrvaṃ te yayā carasi medhayā
a yajño dānaṃ tapaḥ śauryaṃ prajāsaṃtānam eva ca
c māhātmyaṃ balam ojaś ca nityam āśaṃsitaṃ mayā
a nityaṃ svāhā svadhā nityaṃ dadur mānuṣadevatāḥ
c dīrgham āyur dhanaṃ putrān samyag ārādhitāḥ śubhāḥ
a putreṣv āśāsate nityaṃ pitaro daivatāni ca
c dānam adhyayanaṃ yajñaṃ prajānāṃ paripālanam
a etad dharmam adharmaṃ vā janmanaivābhyajāyathāḥ
c te stha vaidyāḥ kule jātā avṛttyā tāta pīḍitāḥ
a yat tu dānapatiṃ śūraṃ kṣudhitāḥ pṛthivīcarāḥ
c prāpya tṛptāḥ pratiṣṭhante dharmaḥ ko 'bhyadhikas tataḥ
a dānenānyaṃ balenānyaṃ tathā sūnṛtayāparam
c sarvataḥ pratigṛhṇīyād rājyaṃ prāpyeha dhārmikaḥ
a brāhmaṇaḥ pracared bhaikṣaṃ kṣatriyaḥ paripālayet
c vaiśyo dhanārjanaṃ kuryāc chūdraḥ paricarec ca tān
a bhaikṣaṃ vipratiṣiddhaṃ te kṛṣir naivopapadyate
c kṣatriyo 'si kṣatāt trātā bāhuvīryopajīvitā
a pitryam aṃśaṃ mahābāho nimagnaṃ punar uddhara
c sāmnā dānena bhedena daṇḍenātha nayena ca
a ito duḥkhataraṃ kiṃ nu yad ahaṃ hīnabāndhavā
c parapiṇḍam udīkṣāmi tvāṃ sūtvāmitranandana
a yudhyasva rājadharmeṇa mā nimajjīḥ pitāmahān
c mā gamaḥ kṣīṇapuṇyas tvaṃ sānujaḥ pāpikāṃ gatim
 parair vihanyamānasya jīvitenāpi kiṃ phalam
 kunty uvāca
a atrāpy udāharantīmam itihāsaṃ purātanam
c vidurāyāś ca saṃvādaṃ putrasya ca paraṃtapa
a atra śreyaś ca bhūyaś ca yathā sā vaktum arhati
c yaśasvinī manyumatī kule jātā vibhāvarī
a kṣatradharmaratā dhanyā vidurā dīrghadarśinī
c viśrutā rājasaṃsatsu śrutavākyā bahuśrutā
a vidurā nāma vai satyā jagarhe putram aurasam
c nirjitaṃ sindhurājena śayānaṃ dīnacetasam
e anandanam adharmajñaṃ dviṣatāṃ harṣavardhanam
a na mayā tvaṃ na pitrāsi jātaḥ kvābhyāgato hy asi
c nirmanyur upaśākhīyaḥ puruṣaḥ klībasādhanaḥ
a yāvajjīvaṃ nirāśo 'si kalyāṇāya dhuraṃ vaha
c mātmānam avamanyasva mainam alpena bībharaḥ
e manaḥ kṛtvā sukalyāṇaṃ mā bhais tvaṃ pratisaṃstabha
a uttiṣṭha he kāpuruṣa mā śeṣvaivaṃ parājitaḥ
c amitrān nandayan sarvān nirmāno bandhuśokadaḥ
a supūrā vai kunadikā supūro mūṣikāñjaliḥ
c susaṃtoṣaḥ kāpuruṣaḥ svalpakenāpi tuṣyati
a apy arer ārujan daṃṣṭrām āśveva nidhanaṃ vraja
c api vā saṃśayaṃ prāpya jīvite 'pi parākrama
a apy areḥ śyenavac chidraṃ paśyes tvaṃ viparikraman
c vinadan vātha vā tūṣṇīṃ vyomni vāpariśaṅkitaḥ
a tvam evaṃ pretavac cheṣe kasmād vajrahato yathā
c uttiṣṭha he kāpuruṣa mā śeṣvaivaṃ parājitaḥ
a māstaṃ gamas tvaṃ kṛpaṇo viśrūyasva svakarmaṇā
c mā madhye mā jaghanye tvaṃ mādho bhūs tiṣṭha corjitaḥ
a alātaṃ tindukasyeva muhūrtam api vijvala
c mā tuṣāgnir ivānarciḥ kākaraṅkhā jijīviṣuḥ
e muhūrtaṃ jvalitaṃ śreyo na tu dhūmāyitaṃ ciram
a mā ha sma kasya cid gehe janī rājñaḥ kharīmṛduḥ
c kṛtvā mānuṣyakaṃ karma sṛtvājiṃ yāvad uttamam
e dharmasyānṛṇyam āpnoti na cātmānaṃ vigarhate
a alabdhvā yadi vā labdhvā nānuśocanti paṇḍitāḥ
c ānantaryaṃ cārabhate na prāṇānāṃ dhanāyate
a udbhāvayasva vīryaṃ vā tāṃ vā gaccha dhruvāṃ gatim
c dharmaṃ putrāgrataḥ kṛtvā kiṃnimittaṃ hi jīvasi
a iṣṭāpūrtaṃ hi te klība kīrtiś ca sakalā hatā
c vicchinnaṃ bhogamūlaṃ te kiṃnimittaṃ hi jīvasi
a śatrur nimajjatā grāhyo jaṅghāyāṃ prapatiṣyatā
c viparicchinnamūlo 'pi na viṣīdet kathaṃ cana
e udyamya dhuram utkarṣed ājāneyakṛtaṃ smaran
a kuru sattvaṃ ca mānaṃ ca viddhi pauruṣam ātmanaḥ
c udbhāvaya kulaṃ magnaṃ tvatkṛte svayam eva hi
a yasya vṛttaṃ na jalpanti mānavā mahad adbhutam
c rāśivardhanamātraṃ sa naiva strī na punaḥ pumān
a dāne tapasi śaurye ca yasya na prathitaṃ yaśaḥ
c vidyāyām arthalābhe vā mātur uccāra eva saḥ
a śrutena tapasā vāpi śriyā vā vikrameṇa vā
c janān yo 'bhibhavaty anyān karmaṇā hi sa vai pumān
a na tv eva jālmīṃ kāpālīṃ vṛttim eṣitum arhasi
c nṛśaṃsyām ayaśasyāṃ ca duḥkhāṃ kāpuruṣocitām
a yam enam abhinandeyur amitrāḥ puruṣaṃ kṛśam
c lokasya samavajñātaṃ nihīnāśanavāsasam
a aholābhakaraṃ dīnam alpajīvanam alpakam
c nedṛśaṃ bandhum āsādya bāndhavaḥ sukham edhate
a avṛttyaiva vipatsyāmo vayaṃ rāṣṭrāt pravāsitāḥ
c sarvakāmarasair hīnāḥ sthānabhraṣṭā akiṃcanāḥ
a avarṇakāriṇaṃ satsu kulavaṃśasya nāśanam
c kaliṃ putrapravādena saṃjaya tvām ajījanam
a niramarṣaṃ nirutsāhaṃ nirvīryam arinandanam
c mā sma sīmantinī kā cij janayet putram īdṛśam
a mā dhūmāya jvalātyantam ākramya jahi śātravān
c jvala mūrdhany amitrāṇāṃ muhūrtam api vā kṣaṇam
a etāvān eva puruṣo yad amarṣī yad akṣamī
c kṣamāvān niramarṣaś ca naiva strī na punaḥ pumān
a saṃtoṣo vai śriyaṃ hanti tathānukrośa eva ca
c anutthānabhaye cobhe nirīho nāśnute mahat
a ebhyo nikṛtipāpebhyaḥ pramuñcātmānam ātmanā
c āyasaṃ hṛdayaṃ kṛtvā mṛgayasva punaḥ svakam
a puraṃ viṣahate yasmāt tasmāt puruṣa ucyate
c tam āhur vyarthanāmānaṃ strīvad ya iha jīvati
a śūrasyorjitasattvasya siṃhavikrāntagāminaḥ
c diṣṭabhāvaṃ gatasyāpi vighase modate prajā
a ya ātmanaḥ priyasukhe hitvā mṛgayate śriyam
c amātyānām atho harṣam ādadhāty acireṇa saḥ
 putra uvāca
a kiṃ nu te mām apaśyantyāḥ pṛthivyā api sarvayā
c kim ābharaṇakṛtyaṃ te kiṃ bhogair jīvitena vā
 mātovāca
a kim adyakānāṃ ye lokā dviṣantas tān avāpnuyuḥ
c ye tv ādṛtātmanāṃ lokāḥ suhṛdas tān vrajantu naḥ
a bhṛtyair vihīyamānānāṃ parapiṇḍopajīvinām
c kṛpaṇānām asattvānāṃ mā vṛttim anuvartithāḥ
a anu tvāṃ tāta jīvantu brāhmaṇāḥ suhṛdas tathā
c parjanyam iva bhūtāni devā iva śatakratum
a yam ājīvanti puruṣaṃ sarvabhūtāni saṃjaya
c pakvaṃ drumam ivāsādya tasya jīvitam arthavat
a yasya śūrasya vikrāntair edhante bāndhavāḥ sukham
c tridaśā iva śakrasya sādhu tasyeha jīvitam
a svabāhubalam āśritya yo 'bhyujjīvati mānavaḥ
c sa loke labhate kīrtiṃ paratra ca śubhāṃ gatim
 vidurovāca
a athaitasyām avasthāyāṃ pauruṣaṃ hātum icchasi
c nihīnasevitaṃ mārgaṃ gamiṣyasy acirād iva
a yo hi tejo yathāśakti na darśayati vikramāt
c kṣatriyo jīvitākāṅkṣī stena ity eva taṃ viduḥ
a arthavanty upapannāni vākyāni guṇavanti ca
c naiva saṃprāpnuvanti tvāṃ mumūrṣum iva bheṣajam
a santi vai sindhurājasya saṃtuṣṭā bahavo janāḥ
c daurbalyād āsate mūḍhā vyasanaughapratīkṣiṇaḥ
a sahāyopacayaṃ kṛtvā vyavasāyya tatas tataḥ
c anuduṣyeyur apare paśyantas tava pauruṣam
a taiḥ kṛtvā saha saṃghātaṃ giridurgālayāṃś cara
c kāle vyasanam ākāṅkṣan naivāyam ajarāmaraḥ
a saṃjayo nāmataś ca tvaṃ na ca paśyāmi tat tvayi
c anvarthanāmā bhava me putra mā vyarthanāmakaḥ
a samyagdṛṣṭir mahāprājño bālaṃ tvāṃ brāhmaṇo 'bravīt
c ayaṃ prāpya mahat kṛcchraṃ punar vṛddhiṃ gamiṣyati
a tasya smarantī vacanam āśaṃse vijayaṃ tava
c tasmāt tāta bravīmi tvāṃ vakṣyāmi ca punaḥ punaḥ
a yasya hy arthābhinirvṛttau bhavanty āpyāyitāḥ pare
c tasyārthasiddhir niyatā nayeṣv arthānusāriṇaḥ
a samṛddhir asamṛddhir vā pūrveṣāṃ mama saṃjaya
c evaṃ vidvān yuddhamanā bhava mā pratyupāhara
a nātaḥ pāpīyasīṃ kāṃ cid avasthāṃ śambaro 'bravīt
c yatra naivādya na prātar bhojanaṃ pratidṛśyate
a patiputravadhād etat paramaṃ duḥkham abravīt
c dāridryam iti yat proktaṃ paryāyamaraṇaṃ hi tat
a ahaṃ mahākule jātā hradād dhradam ivāgatā
c īśvarī sarvakalyāṇair bhartrā paramapūjitā
a mahārhamālyābharaṇāṃ sumṛṣṭāmbaravāsasam
c purā dṛṣṭvā suhṛdvargo mām apaśyat sudurgatām
a yadā māṃ caiva bhāryāṃ ca draṣṭāsi bhṛśadurbale
c na tadā jīvitenārtho bhavitā tava saṃjaya
a dāsakarmakarān bhṛtyān ācāryartvik purohitān
c avṛttyāsmān prajahato dṛṣṭvā kiṃ jīvitena te
a yadi kṛtyaṃ na paśyāmi tavādyeha yathā purā
c ślāghanīyaṃ yaśasyaṃ ca kā śāntir hṛdayasya me
a neti ced brāhmaṇān brūyāṃ dīryate hṛdayaṃ mama
c na hy ahaṃ na ca me bhartā neti brāhmaṇam uktavān
a vayam āśrayaṇīyāḥ sma nāśritāraḥ parasya ca
c sānyān āśritya jīvantī parityakṣyāmi jīvitam
a apāre bhava naḥ pāram aplave bhava naḥ plavaḥ
c kuruṣva sthānam asthāne mṛtān saṃjīvayasva naḥ
a sarve te śatravaḥ sahyā na cej jīvitum icchasi
c atha ced īdṛśīṃ vṛttiṃ klībām abhyupapadyase
a nirviṇṇātmā hatamanā muñcaitāṃ pāpajīvikām
c ekaśatruvadhenaiva śūro gacchati viśrutim
a indro vṛtravadhenaiva mahendraḥ samapadyata
c māhendraṃ ca grahaṃ lebhe lokānāṃ ceśvaro 'bhavat
a nāma viśrāvya vā saṃkhye śatrūn āhūya daṃśitān
c senāgraṃ vāpi vidrāvya hatvā vā puruṣaṃ varam
a yadaiva labhate vīraḥ suyuddhena mahad yaśaḥ
c tadaiva pravyathante 'sya śatravo vinamanti ca
a tyaktvātmānaṃ raṇe dakṣaṃ śūraṃ kāpuruṣā janāḥ
c avaśāḥ pūrayanti sma sarvakāmasamṛddhibhiḥ
a rājyaṃ vāpy ugravibhraṃśaṃ saṃśayo jīvitasya vā
c pralabdhasya hi śatror vai śeṣaṃ kurvanti sādhavaḥ
a svargadvāropamaṃ rājyam atha vāpy amṛtopamam
c ruddham ekāyane matvā patolmuka ivāriṣu
d bhuṅkṣva yuddhena me śatrūñ jitvā tu raṇamūrdhani
d niyacchann itarān varṇān vinayan sarvaduṣkṛtān
a jahi śatrūn raṇe rājan svadharmam anupālaya
c mā tvā paśyet sukṛpaṇaṃ śatruḥ śrīmān kadā cana
a asmadīyaiś ca śocadbhir nadadbhiś ca parair vṛtam
c api tvāṃ nānupaśyeyaṃ dīnā dīnam avasthitam
a uṣya sauvīrakanyābhiḥ ślāghasvārthair yathā purā
c mā ca saindhavakanyānām avasan no vaśaṃ gamaḥ
a yuvā rūpeṇa saṃpanno vidyayābhijanena ca
c yas tvādṛśo vikurvīta yaśasvī lokaviśrutaḥ
e voḍhavye dhury anaḍuvan manye maraṇam eva tat
a yadi tvām anupaśyāmi parasya priyavādinam
c pṛṣṭhato 'nuvrajantaṃ vā kā śāntir hṛdayasya me
a nāsmiñ jātu kule jāto gacched yo 'nyasya pṛṣṭhataḥ
c na tvaṃ parasyānudhuraṃ tāta jīvitum arhasi
a ahaṃ hi kṣatrahṛdayaṃ veda yat pariśāśvatam
c pūrvaiḥ pūrvataraiḥ proktaṃ paraiḥ paratarair api
d śāśvataṃ cāvyayaṃ caiva prajāpativinirmitam
a yo vai kaś cid ihājātaḥ kṣatriyaḥ kṣatradharmavit
c bhayād vṛttisamīkṣo vā na named iha kasya cit
a udyacched eva na named udyamo hy eva pauruṣam
c apy aparvaṇi bhajyeta na named iha kasya cit
a mātaṅgo matta iva ca parīyāt sumahāmanāḥ
c brāhmaṇebhyo namen nityaṃ dharmāyaiva ca saṃjaya
a niyacchann itarān varṇān vinighnan sarvaduṣkṛtaḥ
c sasahāyo 'sahāyo vā yāvajjīvaṃ tathā bhavet
 putra uvāca
a kṛṣṇāyasasyeva ca te saṃhatya hṛdayaṃ kṛtam
c mama mātas tv akaruṇe vairaprajñe hy amarṣaṇe
a aho kṣatrasamācāro yatra mām aparaṃ yathā
b niyojayasi yuddhāya paramāteva māṃ tathā
c īdṛśaṃ vacanaṃ brūyād bhavatī putram ekajam
a kiṃ nu te mām apaśyantyāḥ pṛthivyā api sarvayā
c kim ābharaṇakṛtyaṃ te kiṃ bhogair jīvitena vā
d mayi vā saṃgarahate priyaputre viśeṣataḥ
d mohāt saṃgarhase mātaḥ priyaṃ putraṃ viśeṣataḥ
 mātovāca
a sarvārambhā hi viduṣāṃ tāta dharmārthakāraṇāt
c tān evābhisamīkṣyāhaṃ saṃjaya tvām acūcudam
a sa samīkṣyakramopeto mukhyaḥ kālo 'yam āgataḥ
c asmiṃś ced āgate kāle kāryaṃ na pratipadyase
e asaṃbhāvitarūpas tvaṃ sunṛśaṃsaṃ kariṣyasi
a taṃ tvām ayaśasā spṛṣṭaṃ na brūyāṃ yadi saṃjaya
b aham eva bhaveyaṃ te ripur atyantaro mahān
c kharīvātsalyam āhus tan niḥsāmarthyam ahetukam
a sadbhir vigarhitaṃ mārgaṃ tyaja mūrkhaniṣevitam
c avidyā vai mahaty asti yām imāṃ saṃśritāḥ prajāḥ
a tava syād yadi sadvṛttaṃ tena me tvaṃ priyo bhaveḥ
c dharmārthaguṇayuktena netareṇa kathaṃ cana
e daivamānuṣayuktena sadbhir ācaritena ca
a yo hy evam avinītena ramate putranaptṛṇā
c anutthānavatā cāpi moghaṃ tasya prajāphalam
c   durvinītena durdhiyā
c ramate yas tu putreṇa
a akurvanto hi karmāṇi kurvanto ninditāni ca
c sukhaṃ naiveha nāmutra labhante puruṣādhamāḥ
a yuddhāya kṣatriyaḥ sṛṣṭaḥ saṃjayeha jayāya ca
c krūrāya karmaṇe nityaṃ prajānāṃ paripālane
e jayan vā vadhyamāno vā prāpnotīndrasalokatām
a na śakrabhavane puṇye divi tad vidyate sukham
c yad amitrān vaśe kṛtvā kṣatriyaḥ sukham aśnute
a manyunā dahyamānena puruṣeṇa manasvinā
c nikṛteneha bahuśaḥ śatrūn pratijigīṣayā
a ātmānaṃ vā parityajya śatrūn vā vinipātya vai
b yat sukhaṃ prāpyate tena na tad anyatra vidyate
b prāpyate neha śāntir hi nityam eva tu saṃjaya
c ato 'nyena prakāreṇa śāntir asya kuto bhavet
a iha prājño hi puruṣaḥ svalpam apriyam icchati
c yasya svalpaṃ priyaṃ loke dhruvaṃ tasyālpam apriyam
a priyābhāvāc ca puruṣo naiva prāpnoti śobhanam
c dhruvaṃ cābhāvam abhyeti gatvā gaṅgeva sāgaram
 putra uvāca
a neyaṃ matis tvayā vācyā mātaḥ putre viśeṣataḥ
c kāruṇyam evātra paśya bhūtveha jaḍamūkavat
 mātovāca
a ato me bhūyasī nandir yad evam anupaśyasi
c codyaṃ māṃ codayasy etad bhṛśaṃ vai codayāmi te
a atha tvāṃ pūjayiṣyāmi hatvā vai sarvasaindhavān
c ahaṃ paśyāmi vijayaṃ kṛtsnaṃ bhāvinam eva te
 putra uvāca
a akośasyāsahāyasya kutaḥ svid vijayo mama
c ity avasthāṃ viditvemām ātmanātmani dāruṇām
e rājyād bhāvo nivṛtto me tridivād iva duṣkṛteḥ
a īdṛśaṃ bhavatī kaṃ cid upāyam anupaśyati
c tan me pariṇataprajñe samyak prabrūhi pṛcchate
e kariṣyāmi hi tat sarvaṃ yathāvad anuśāsanam
 mātovāca
a putrātmā nāvamantavyaḥ pūrvābhir asamṛddhibhiḥ
c abhūtvā hi bhavanty arthā bhūtvā naśyanti cāpare
a amarṣeṇaiva cāpy arthā nārabdhavyāḥ subāliśaiḥ
c sarveṣāṃ karmaṇāṃ tāta phale nityam anityatā
a anityam iti jānanto na bhavanti bhavanti ca
c atha ye naiva kurvanti naiva jātu bhavanti te
a aikaguṇyam anīhāyām abhāvaḥ karmaṇāṃ phalam
c atha dvaiguṇyam īhāyāṃ phalaṃ bhavati vā na vā
a yasya prāg eva viditā sarvārthānām anityatā
c nuded vṛddhisamṛddhī sa pratikūle nṛpātmaja
a utthātavyaṃ jāgṛtavyaṃ yoktavyaṃ bhūtikarmasu
c bhaviṣyatīty eva manaḥ kṛtvā satatam avyathaiḥ
e maṅgalāni puraskṛtya brāhmaṇaiś ceśvaraiḥ saha
a prājñasya nṛpater āśu vṛddhir bhavati putraka
c abhivartati lakṣmīs taṃ prācīm iva divākaraḥ
a nidarśanāny upāyāṃś ca bahūny uddharṣaṇāni ca
c anudarśitarūpo 'si paśyāmi kuru pauruṣam
e puruṣārtham abhipretaṃ samāhartum ihārhasi
a kruddhāṃl lubdhān parikṣīṇān avakṣiptān vimānitān
c spardhinaś caiva ye ke cit tān yukta upadhāraya
a etena tvaṃ prakāreṇa mahato bhetsyase gaṇān
c mahāvega ivoddhūto mātariśvā balāhakān
a teṣām agrapradāyī syāḥ kalyotthāyī priyaṃvadaḥ
c te tvāṃ priyaṃ kariṣyanti puro dhāsyanti ca dhruvam
a yadaiva śatrur jānīyāt sapatnaṃ tyaktajīvitam
c tadaivāsmād udvijate sarpād veśmagatād iva
a taṃ viditvā parākrāntaṃ vaśe na kurute yadi
c nirvādair nirvaded enam antatas tad bhaviṣyati
a nirvādād āspadaṃ labdhvā dhanavṛddhir bhaviṣyati
c dhanavantaṃ hi mitrāṇi bhajante cāśrayanti ca
a skhalitārthaṃ punas tāta saṃtyajanty api bāndhavāḥ
c apy asminn āśrayante ca jugupsanti ca tādṛśam
a śatruṃ kṛtvā yaḥ sahāyaṃ viśvāsam upagacchati
c ataḥ saṃbhāvyam evaitad yad rājyaṃ prāpnuyād iti
 mātovāca
a naiva rājñā daraḥ kāryo jātu kasyāṃ cid āpadi
c atha ced api dīrṇaḥ syān naiva varteta dīrṇavat
a dīrṇaṃ hi dṛṣṭvā rājānaṃ sarvam evānudīryate
c rāṣṭraṃ balam amātyāś ca pṛthak kurvanti te matim
a śatrūn eke prapadyante prajahaty apare punaḥ
c anv eke prajihīrṣanti ye purastād vimānitāḥ
a ya evātyantasuhṛdas ta enaṃ paryupāsate
c aśaktayaḥ svastikāmā baddhavatsā iḍā iva
e śocantam anuśocanti pratītān iva bāndhavān
a api te pūjitāḥ pūrvam api te suhṛdo matāḥ
c ye rāṣṭram abhimanyante rājño vyasanam īyuṣaḥ
e mā dīdaras tvaṃ suhṛdo mā tvāṃ dīrṇaṃ prahāsiṣuḥ
a prabhāvaṃ pauruṣaṃ buddhiṃ jijñāsantyā mayā tava
c ullapantyā samāśvāsaṃ balavān iva durbalam
a yady etat saṃvijānāsi yadi samyag bravīmy aham
c kṛtvāsaumyam ivātmānaṃ jayāyottiṣṭha saṃjaya
a asti naḥ kośanicayo mahān aviditas tava
c tam ahaṃ veda nānyas tam upasaṃpādayāmi te
a santi naikaśatā bhūyaḥ suhṛdas tava saṃjaya
c sukhaduḥkhasahā vīra śatārhā anivartinaḥ
a tādṛśā hi sahāyā vai puruṣasya bubhūṣataḥ
c īṣad ujjihataḥ kiṃ cit sacivāḥ śatrukarśanāḥ
 putra uvāca
a kasya tv īdṛśakaṃ vākyaṃ śrutvāpi svalpacetasaḥ
c tamo na vyapahanyeta sucitrārthapadākṣaram
a udake dhūr iyaṃ dhāryā sartavyaṃ pravaṇe mayā
c yasya me bhavatī netrī bhaviṣyad bhūtadarśinī
a ahaṃ hi vacanaṃ tvattaḥ śuśrūṣur aparāparam
c kiṃ cit kiṃ cit prativadaṃs tūṣṇīm āsaṃ muhur muhuḥ
a atṛpyann amṛtasyeva kṛcchrāl labdhasya bāndhavāt
c udyacchāmy eṣa śatrūṇāṃ niyamāya jayāya ca
 kunty uvāca
a sadaśva iva sa kṣiptaḥ praṇunno vākyasāyakaiḥ
c tac cakāra tathā sarvaṃ yathāvad anuśāsanam
a idam uddharṣaṇaṃ bhīmaṃ tejovardhanam uttamam
c rājānaṃ śrāvayen mantrī sīdantaṃ śatrupīḍitam
a jayo nāmetihāso 'yaṃ śrotavyo vijigīṣuṇā
c mahīṃ vijayate kṣipraṃ śrutvā śatrūṃś ca mardati
a idaṃ puṃsavanaṃ caiva vīrājananam eva ca
c abhīkṣṇaṃ garbhiṇī śrutvā dhruvaṃ vīraṃ prajāyate
a vidyāśūraṃ tapaḥśūraṃ damaśūraṃ tapasvinam
c brāhmyā śriyā dīpyamānaṃ sādhuvādena saṃmatam
a arciṣmantaṃ balopetaṃ mahābhāgaṃ mahāratham
c dhṛṣṭavantam anādhṛṣyaṃ jetāram aparājitam
a niyantāram asādhūnāṃ goptāraṃ dharmacāriṇām
c tadarthaṃ kṣatriyā sūte vīraṃ satyaparākramam
d iti śrutvā vaco mātuḥ saṃjayaḥ śatrubhiḥ saha
d kṛtavān saṃyugaṃ kṛṣṇa jayaṃ ca prāptavān dhruvam
 kunty uvāca
a arjunaṃ keśava brūyās tvayi jāte sma sūtake
c upopaviṣṭā nārībhir āśrame parivāritā
a athāntarikṣe vāg āsīd divyarūpā manoramā
c sahasrākṣasamaḥ kunti bhaviṣyaty eṣa te sutaḥ
a eṣa jeṣyati saṃgrāme kurūn sarvān samāgatān
c bhīmasenadvitīyaś ca lokam udvartayiṣyati
a putras te pṛthivīṃ jetā yaśaś cāsya divaspṛśam
c hatvā kurūn grāmajanye vāsudevasahāyavān
a pitryam aṃśaṃ pranaṣṭaṃ ca punar apy uddhariṣyati
c bhrātṛbhiḥ sahitaḥ śrīmāṃs trīn medhān āhariṣyati
d tathā cares tvaṃ śvetāśva yathā vāg abhyabhāṣata
a taṃ satyasaṃdhaṃ bībhatsuṃ savyasācinam acyuta
c yathāham evaṃ jānāmi balavantaṃ durāsadam
e tathā tad astu dāśārha yathā vāg abhyabhāṣata
a dharmaś ced asti vārṣṇeya tathā satyaṃ bhaviṣyati
c tvaṃ cāpi tat tathā kṛṣṇa sarvaṃ saṃpādayiṣyasi
a nāhaṃ tad abhyasūyāmi yathā vāg abhyabhāṣata
c namo dharmāya mahate dharmo dhārayati prajāḥ
