a etad dhanaṃjayo vācyo nityodyukto vṛkodaraḥ
c yadarthaṃ kṣatriyā sūte tasya kālo 'yam āgataḥ
e na hi vairaṃ samāsādya sīdanti puruṣarṣabhāḥ
a viditā te sadā buddhir bhīmasya na sa śāmyati
c yāvadantaṃ na kurute śatrūṇāṃ śatrukarśanaḥ
d tāvad eva mahābāhur niśāsu na sukhaṃ labhet
a sarvadharmaviśeṣajñāṃ snuṣāṃ pāṇḍor mahātmanaḥ
c brūyā mādhava kalyāṇīṃ kṛṣṇāṃ kṛṣṇa yaśasvinīm
a yuktam etan mahābhāge kule jāte yaśasvini
c yan me putreṣu sarveṣu yathāvat tvam avartithāḥ
a mādrīputrau ca vaktavyau kṣatradharmaratāv ubhau
b vikramādhigatā hy arthāḥ kṣatradharmaratāv ubhau
c vikrameṇārjitān bhogān vṛṇītaṃ jīvitād api
a vikramādhigatā hy arthāḥ kṣatradharmeṇa jīvataḥ
c mano manuṣyasya sadā prīṇanti puruṣottama
a yac ca vaḥ prekṣamāṇānāṃ sarvadharmopacāyinī
c pāñcālī paruṣāṇy uktā ko nu tat kṣantum arhati
a na rājyaharaṇaṃ duḥkhaṃ dyūte cāpi parājayaḥ
c pravrājanaṃ sutānāṃ vā na me tad duḥkhakāraṇam
d sarvadharmaviśeṣajñāṃ kule jātāṃ yaśasvinīm
a yat tu sā bṛhatī śyāmā sabhāyāṃ rudatī tadā
c aśrauṣīt paruṣā vācas tan me duḥkhataraṃ matam
a strīdharmiṇī varārohā kṣatradharmaratā sadā
c nādhyagacchat tadā nāthaṃ kṛṣṇā nāthavatī satī
a taṃ vai brūhi mahābāho sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varam
c arjunaṃ puruṣavyāghraṃ draupadyāḥ padavīṃ cara
a viditau hi tavātyantaṃ kruddhāv iva yamāntakau
c bhīmārjunau nayetāṃ hi devān api parāṃ gatim
a tayoś caitad avajñānaṃ yat sā kṛṣṇā sabhāgatā
c duḥśāsanaś ca yad bhīmaṃ kaṭukāny abhyabhāṣata
e paśyatāṃ kuruvīrāṇāṃ tac ca saṃsmārayeḥ punaḥ
a pāṇḍavān kuśalaṃ pṛccheḥ saputrān kṛṣṇayā saha
c māṃ ca kuśalinīṃ brūyās teṣu bhūyo janārdana
e ariṣṭaṃ gaccha panthānaṃ putrān me paripālaya
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a abhivādyātha tāṃ kṛṣṇaḥ kṛtvā cābhipradakṣiṇam
c niścakrāma mahābāhuḥ siṃhakhelagatis tataḥ
a tato visarjayām āsa bhīṣmādīn kurupuṃgavān
c āropya ca rathe karṇaṃ prāyāt sātyakinā saha
a tataḥ prayāte dāśārhe kuravaḥ saṃgatā mithaḥ
c jajalpur mahad āścaryaṃ keśave paramādbhutam
a pramūḍhā pṛthivī sarvā mṛtyupāśasitā kṛtā
c duryodhanasya bāliśyān naitad astīti cābruvan
a tato niryāya nagarāt prayayau puruṣottamaḥ
c mantrayām āsa ca tadā karṇena suciraṃ saha
a visarjayitvā rādheyaṃ sarvayādavanandanaḥ
b aśvatthāmānam āhūya mantrayitvā punaḥ punaḥ
c tato javena mahatā tūrṇam aśvān acodayat
a te pibanta ivākāśaṃ dārukeṇa pracoditāḥ
c hayā jagmur mahāvegā manomārutaraṃhasaḥ
a te vyatītya tam adhvānaṃ kṣipraṃ śyenā ivāśugāḥ
c uccaiḥ sūryam upaplavyaṃ śārṅgadhanvānam āvahan
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a kuntyās tu vacanaṃ śrutvā bhīṣmadroṇau mahārathau
c duryodhanam idaṃ vākyam ūcatuḥ śāsanātigam
a śrutaṃ te puruṣavyāghra kuntyāḥ kṛṣṇasya saṃnidhau
c vākyam arthavad avyagram uktaṃ dharmyam anuttamam
a tat kariṣyanti kaunteyā vāsudevasya saṃmatam
c na hi te jātu śāmyerann ṛte rājyena kaurava
a kleśitā hi tvayā pārthā dharmapāśasitās tadā
c sabhāyāṃ draupadī caiva taiś ca tan marṣitaṃ tava
a kṛtāstraṃ hy arjunaṃ prāpya bhīmaṃ ca kṛtaniśramam
c gāṇḍīvaṃ ceṣudhī caiva rathaṃ ca dhvajam eva ca
d nakulaṃ sahadevaṃ ca balavīryasamanvitau
e sahāyaṃ vāsudevaṃ ca na kṣaṃsyati yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a pratyakṣaṃ te mahābāho yathā pārthena dhīmatā
c virāṭanagare pūrvaṃ sarve sma yudhi nirjitāḥ
a dānavān ghorakarmāṇo nivātakavacān yudhi
c raudram astraṃ samādhāya dagdhavān astravahninā
a karṇaprabhṛtayaś ceme tvaṃ cāpi kavacī rathī
c mokṣitā ghoṣayātrāyāṃ paryāptaṃ tan nidarśanam
a praśāmya bharataśreṣṭha bhrātṛbhiḥ saha pāṇḍavaiḥ
c rakṣemāṃ pṛthivīṃ sarvāṃ mṛtyor daṃṣṭrāntaraṃ gatām
a jyeṣṭho bhrātā dharmaśīlo vatsalaḥ ślakṣṇavāk śuciḥ
c taṃ gaccha puruṣavyāghraṃ vyapanīyeha kilbiṣam
a dṛṣṭaś cet tvaṃ pāṇḍavena vyapanītaśarāsanaḥ
c prasannabhrukuṭiḥ śrīmān kṛtā śāntiḥ kulasya naḥ
a tam abhyetya sahāmātyaḥ pariṣvajya nṛpātmajam
c abhivādaya rājānaṃ yathāpūrvam ariṃdama
a abhivādayamānaṃ tvāṃ pāṇibhyāṃ bhīmapūrvajaḥ
c pratigṛhṇātu sauhārdāt kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a siṃhaskandhorubāhus tvāṃ vṛttāyatamahābhujaḥ
c pariṣvajatu bāhubhyāṃ bhīmaḥ praharatāṃ varaḥ
a siṃhagrīvo guḍākeśas tatas tvāṃ puṣkarekṣaṇaḥ
c abhivādayatāṃ pārthaḥ kuntīputro dhanaṃjayaḥ
a āśvineyau naravyāghrau rūpeṇāpratimau bhuvi
c tau ca tvāṃ guruvat premṇā pūjayā pratyudīyatām
a muñcantv ānandajāśrūṇi dāśārhapramukhā nṛpāḥ
c saṃgaccha bhrātṛbhiḥ sārdhaṃ mānaṃ saṃtyajya pārthiva
a praśādhi pṛthivīṃ kṛtsnāṃ tatas taṃ bhrātṛbhiḥ saha
c samāliṅgya ca harṣeṇa nṛpā yāntu parasparam
a alaṃ yuddhena rājendra suhṛdāṃ śṛṇu kāraṇam
c dhruvaṃ vināśo yuddhe hi kṣatriyāṇāṃ pradṛśyate
a jyotīṃṣi pratikūlāni dāruṇā mṛgapakṣiṇaḥ
c utpātā vividhā vīra dṛśyante kṣatranāśanāḥ
a viśeṣata ihāsmākaṃ nimittāni vināśane
c ulkābhir hi pradīptābhir vadhyate pṛtanā tava
a vāhanāny aprahṛṣṭāni rudantīva viśāṃ pate
c gṛdhrās te paryupāsante sainyāni ca samantataḥ
a nagaraṃ na yathāpūrvaṃ tathā rājaniveśanam
c śivāś cāśivanirghoṣā dīptāṃ sevanti vai diśam
a kuru vākyaṃ pitur mātur asmākaṃ ca hitaiṣiṇām
c tvayy āyatto mahābāho śamo vyāyāma eva ca
a na cet kariṣyasi vacaḥ suhṛdām arikarśana
c tapsyase vāhinīṃ dṛṣṭvā pārthabāṇaprapīḍitām
a bhīmasya ca mahānādaṃ nadataḥ śuṣmiṇo raṇe
c śrutvā smartāsi me vākyaṃ gāṇḍīvasya ca nisvanam
e yady etad apasavyaṃ te bhaviṣyati vaco mama
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a evam uktas tu vimanās tiryagdṛṣṭir adhomukhaḥ
c saṃhatya ca bhruvor madhyaṃ na kiṃ cid vyājahāra ha
a taṃ vai vimanasaṃ dṛṣṭvā saṃprekṣyānyonyam antikāt
c punar evottaraṃ vākyam uktavantau nararṣabhau
 bhīṣma uvāca
a śuśrūṣum anasūyaṃ ca brahmaṇyaṃ satyasaṃgaram
c pratiyotsyāmahe pārtham ato duḥkhataraṃ nu kim
 droṇa uvāca
a aśvatthāmni yathā putre bhūyo mama dhanaṃjaye
c bahumānaḥ paro rājan saṃnatiś ca kapidhvaje
a taṃ cet putrāt priyataraṃ pratiyotsye dhanaṃjayam
c kṣatradharmam anuṣṭhāya dhig astu kṣatrajīvikām
a yasya loke samo nāsti kaś cid anyo dhanurdharaḥ
c matprasādāt sa bībhatsuḥ śreyān anyair dhanurdharaiḥ
a mitradhrug duṣṭabhāvaś ca nāstiko 'thānṛjuḥ śaṭhaḥ
c na satsu labhate pūjāṃ yajñe mūrkha ivāgataḥ
a vāryamāṇo 'pi pāpebhyaḥ pāpātmā pāpam icchati
c codyamāno 'pi pāpena śubhātmā śubham icchati
a mithyopacaritā hy ete vartamānā hy anu priye
c ahitatvāya kalpante doṣā bharatasattama
a tvam uktaḥ kuruvṛddhena mayā ca vidureṇa ca
c vāsudevena ca tathā śreyo naivābhipadyase
a asti me balam ity eva sahasā tvaṃ titīrṣasi
c sagrāhanakramakaraṃ gaṅgāvegam ivoṣṇage
a vāsa eva yathā hi tvaṃ prāvṛṇvāno 'dya manyase
c srajaṃ tyaktām iva prāpya lobhād yaudhiṣṭhirīṃ śriyam
a draupadīsahitaṃ pārthaṃ sāyudhair bhrātṛbhir vṛtam
c vanastham api rājyasthaḥ pāṇḍavaṃ ko 'tijīvati
a nideśe yasya rājānaḥ sarve tiṣṭhanti kiṃkarāḥ
c tam ailavilam āsādya dharmarājo vyarājata
a kuberasadanaṃ prāpya tato ratnāny avāpya ca
c sphītam ākramya te rāṣṭraṃ rājyam icchanti pāṇḍavāḥ
a dattaṃ hutam adhītaṃ ca brāhmaṇās tarpitā dhanaiḥ
c āvayor gatam āyuś ca kṛtakṛtyau ca viddhi nau
a tvaṃ tu hitvā sukhaṃ rājyaṃ mitrāṇi ca dhanāni ca
c vigrahaṃ pāṇḍavaiḥ kṛtvā mahad vyasanam āpsyasi
a draupadī yasya cāśāste vijayaṃ satyavādinī
c tapoghoravratā devī na tvaṃ jeṣyasi pāṇḍavam
a mantrī janārdano yasya bhrātā yasya dhanaṃjayaḥ
c sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ kathaṃ jeṣyasi pāṇḍavam
a sahāyā brāhmaṇā yasya dhṛtimanto jitendriyāḥ
c tam ugratapasaṃ vīraṃ kathaṃ jeṣyasi pāṇḍavam
a punar uktaṃ ca vakṣyāmi yat kāryaṃ bhūtim icchatā
c suhṛdā majjamāneṣu suhṛtsu vyasanārṇave
a alaṃ yuddhena tair vīraiḥ śāmya tvaṃ kuruvṛddhaye
c mā gamaḥ sasutāmātyaḥ sabalaś ca parābhavam
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a rājaputraiḥ parivṛtas tathāmātyaiś ca saṃjaya
c upāropya rathe karṇaṃ niryāto madhusūdanaḥ
a kim abravīd rathopasthe rādheyaṃ paravīrahā
c kāni sāntvāni govindaḥ sūtaputre prayuktavān
a oghameghasvanaḥ kāle yat kṛṣṇaḥ karṇam abravīt
c mṛdu vā yadi vā tīkṣṇaṃ tan mamācakṣva saṃjaya
 saṃjaya uvāca
a ānupūrvyeṇa vākyāni ślakṣṇāni ca mṛdūni ca
c priyāṇi dharmayuktāni satyāni ca hitāni ca
a hṛdayagrahaṇīyāni rādheyaṃ madhusūdanaḥ
c yāny abravīd ameyātmā tāni me śṛṇu bhārata
 vāsudeva uvāca
a upāsitās te rādheya brāhmaṇā vedapāragāḥ
c tattvārthaṃ paripṛṣṭāś ca niyatenānasūyayā
a tvam eva karṇa jānāsi vedavādān sanātanān
c tvaṃ hy eva dharmaśāstreṣu sūkṣmeṣu pariniṣṭhitaḥ
a kānīnaś ca sahoḍhaś ca kanyāyāṃ yaś ca jāyate
c voḍhāraṃ pitaraṃ tasya prāhuḥ śāstravido janāḥ
a so 'si karṇa tathā jātaḥ pāṇḍoḥ putro 'si dharmataḥ
c nigrahād dharmaśāstrāṇām ehi rājā bhaviṣyasi
a pitṛpakṣe hi te pārthā mātṛpakṣe ca vṛṣṇayaḥ
c dvau pakṣāv abhijānīhi tvam etau puruṣarṣabha
a mayā sārdham ito yātam adya tvāṃ tāta pāṇḍavāḥ
c abhijānantu kaunteyaṃ pūrvajātaṃ yudhiṣṭhirāt
a pādau tava grahīṣyanti bhrātaraḥ pañca pāṇḍavāḥ
c draupadeyās tathā pañca saubhadraś cāparājitaḥ
a rājāno rājaputrāś ca pāṇḍavārthe samāgatāḥ
c pādau tava grahīṣyanti sarve cāndhakavṛṣṇayaḥ
a hiraṇmayāṃś ca te kumbhān rājatān pārthivāṃs tathā
c oṣadhyaḥ sarvabījāni sarvaratnāni vīrudhaḥ
a rājanyā rājakanyāś cāpy ānayantv abhiṣecanam
c ṣaṣṭhe ca tvāṃ tathā kāle draupady upagamiṣyati
d agniṃ juhotu vai dhaumyaḥ saṃśitātmā dvijottamaḥ
a adya tvām abhiṣiñcantu cāturvaidyā dvijātayaḥ
c purohitaḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ vyāghracarmaṇy avasthitam
a tathaiva bhrātaraḥ pañca pāṇḍavāḥ puruṣarṣabhāḥ
c draupadeyās tathā pañca pāñcālāś cedayas tathā
a ahaṃ ca tvābhiṣekṣyāmi rājānaṃ pṛthivīpatim
c yuvarājo 'stu te rājā kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a gṛhītvā vyajanaṃ śvetaṃ dharmātmā saṃśitavrataḥ
c upānvārohatu rathaṃ kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a chatraṃ ca te mahac chvetaṃ bhīmaseno mahābalaḥ
c abhiṣiktasya kaunteya kaunteyo dhārayiṣyati
a kiṅkiṇīśatanirghoṣaṃ vaiyāghraparivāraṇam
c rathaṃ śvetahayair yuktam arjuno vāhayiṣyati
a abhimanyuś ca te nityaṃ pratyāsanno bhaviṣyati
c nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca draupadeyāś ca pañca ye
a pāñcālās tvānuyāsyanti śikhaṇḍī ca mahārathaḥ
c ahaṃ ca tvānuyāsyāmi sarve cāndhakavṛṣṇayaḥ
e dāśārhāḥ parivārās te dāśārṇāś ca viśāṃ pate
a bhuṅkṣva rājyaṃ mahābāho bhrātṛbhiḥ saha pāṇḍavaiḥ
b āroha tu rathaṃ pārthair bhrātṛbhiḥ saha pāṇḍavaiḥ
c japair homaiś ca saṃyukto maṅgalaiś ca pṛthagvidhaiḥ
a purogamāś ca te santu draviḍāḥ saha kuntalaiḥ
c āndhrās tālacarāś caiva cūcupā veṇupās tathā
a stuvantu tvādya bahuśaḥ stutibhiḥ sūtamāgadhāḥ
c vijayaṃ vasuṣeṇasya ghoṣayantu ca pāṇḍavāḥ
a sa tvaṃ parivṛtaḥ pārthair nakṣatrair iva candramāḥ
c praśādhi rājyaṃ kaunteya kuntīṃ ca pratinandaya
a mitrāṇi te prahṛṣyantu vyathantu ripavas tathā
c saubhrātraṃ caiva te 'dyāstu bhrātṛbhiḥ saha pāṇḍavaiḥ
 karṇa uvāca
a asaṃśayaṃ sauhṛdān me praṇayāc cāttha keśava
c sakhyena caiva vārṣṇeya śreyaskāmatayaiva ca
a sarvaṃ caivābhijānāmi pāṇḍoḥ putro 'smi dharmataḥ
c nigrahād dharmaśāstrāṇāṃ yathā tvaṃ kṛṣṇa manyase
a kanyā garbhaṃ samādhatta bhāskarān māṃ janārdana
c ādityavacanāc caiva jātaṃ māṃ sā vyasarjayat
a so 'smi kṛṣṇa tathā jātaḥ pāṇḍoḥ putro 'smi dharmataḥ
c kuntyā tv aham apākīrṇo yathā na kuśalaṃ tathā
a sūto hi mām adhiratho dṛṣṭvaiva anayad gṛhān
c rādhāyāś caiva māṃ prādāt sauhārdān madhusūdana
a matsnehāc caiva rādhāyāḥ sadyaḥ kṣīram avātarat
c sā me mūtraṃ purīṣaṃ ca pratijagrāha mādhava
a tasyāḥ piṇḍavyapanayaṃ kuryād asmadvidhaḥ katham
c dharmavid dharmaśāstrāṇāṃ śravaṇe satataṃ rataḥ
a tathā mām abhijānāti sūtaś cādhirathaḥ sutam
c pitaraṃ cābhijānāmi tam ahaṃ sauhṛdāt sadā
a sa hi me jātakarmādi kārayām āsa mādhava
c śāstradṛṣṭena vidhinā putraprītyā janārdana
a nāma me vasuṣeṇeti kārayām āsa vai dvijaiḥ
c bhāryāś coḍhā mama prāpte yauvane tena keśava
a tāsu putrāś ca pautrāś ca mama jātā janārdana
c tāsu me hṛdayaṃ kṛṣṇa saṃjātaṃ kāmabandhanam
a na pṛthivyā sakalayā na suvarṇasya rāśibhiḥ
c harṣād bhayād vā govinda anṛtaṃ vaktum utsahe
a dhṛtarāṣṭrakule kṛṣṇa duryodhanasamāśrayāt
c mayā trayodaśa samā bhuktaṃ rājyam akaṇṭakam
a iṣṭaṃ ca bahubhir yajñaiḥ saha sūtair mayāsakṛt
c āvāhāś ca vivāhāś ca saha sūtaiḥ kṛtā mayā
a māṃ ca kṛṣṇa samāśritya kṛtaḥ śastrasamudyamaḥ
c duryodhanena vārṣṇeya vigrahaś cāpi pāṇḍavaiḥ
a tasmād raṇe dvairathe māṃ pratyudyātāram acyuta
c vṛtavān paramaṃ hṛṣṭaḥ pratīpaṃ savyasācinaḥ
a vadhād bandhād bhayād vāpi lobhād vāpi janārdana
c anṛtaṃ notsahe kartuṃ dhārtarāṣṭrasya dhīmataḥ
a yadi hy adya na gaccheyaṃ dvairathaṃ savyasācinā
c akīrtiḥ syād dhṛṣīkeśa mama pārthasya cobhayoḥ
a asaṃśayaṃ hitārthāya brūyās tvaṃ madhusūdana
c sarvaṃ ca pāṇḍavāḥ kuryus tvadvaśitvān na saṃśayaḥ
a mantrasya niyamaṃ kuryās tvam atra puruṣottama
c etad atra hitaṃ manye sarvayādavanandana
a yadi jānāti māṃ rājā dharmātmā saṃśitavrataḥ
c kuntyāḥ prathamajaṃ putraṃ na sa rājyaṃ grahīṣyati
a prāpya cāpi mahad rājyaṃ tad ahaṃ madhusūdana
c sphītaṃ duryodhanāyaiva saṃpradadyām ariṃdama
a sa eva rājā dharmātmā śāśvato 'stu yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c netā yasya hṛṣīkeśo yoddhā yasya dhanaṃjayaḥ
a pṛthivī tasya rāṣṭraṃ ca yasya bhīmo mahārathaḥ
c nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca draupadeyāś ca mādhava
d dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pāñcālyaḥ sātyakiś ca mahārathaḥ
a uttamaujā yudhāmanyuḥ satyadharmā ca somakiḥ
c caidyaś ca cekitānaś ca śikhaṇḍī cāparājitaḥ
a indragopakavarṇāś ca kekayā bhrātaras tathā
c indrāyudhasavarṇaś ca kuntibhojo mahārathaḥ
a mātulo bhīmasenasya senajic ca mahārathaḥ
c śaṅkhaḥ putro virāṭasya nidhis tvaṃ ca janārdana
a mahān ayaṃ kṛṣṇa kṛtaḥ kṣatrasya samudānayaḥ
c rājyaṃ prāptam idaṃ dīptaṃ prathitaṃ sarvarājasu
a dhārtarāṣṭrasya vārṣṇeya śastrayajño bhaviṣyati
c asya yajñasya vettā tvaṃ bhaviṣyasi janārdana
e ādhvaryavaṃ ca te kṛṣṇa kratāv asmin bhaviṣyati
a hotā caivātra bībhatsuḥ saṃnaddhaḥ sa kapidhvajaḥ
c gāṇḍīvaṃ sruk tathājyaṃ ca vīryaṃ puṃsāṃ bhaviṣyati
a aindraṃ pāśupataṃ brāhmaṃ sthūṇākarṇaṃ ca mādhava
c mantrās tatra bhaviṣyanti prayuktāḥ savyasācinā
a anuyātaś ca pitaram adhiko vā parākrame
c grāvastotraṃ sa saubhadraḥ samyak tatra kariṣyati
a udgātātra punar bhīmaḥ prastotā sumahābalaḥ
c vinadan sa naravyāghro nāgānīkāntakṛd raṇe
a sa caiva tatra dharmātmā śaśvad rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c japair homaiś ca saṃyukto brahmatvaṃ kārayiṣyati
a śaṅkhaśabdāḥ samurajā bheryaś ca madhusūdana
c utkṛṣṭasiṃhanādāś ca subrahmaṇyo bhaviṣyati
a nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca mādrīputrau yaśasvinau
c śāmitraṃ tau mahāvīryau samyak tatra kariṣyataḥ
d rathadhvajāś ca kalpante yūpāś ca vitate kratau
d maitrāvaruṇa āgnīdhrau mahāvīryau bhaviṣyataḥ
a kalmāṣadaṇḍā govinda vimalā rathaśaktayaḥ
c yūpāḥ samupakalpantām asmin yajñe janārdana
a karṇinālīkanārācā vatsadantopabṛṃhaṇāḥ
c tomarāḥ somakalaśāḥ pavitrāṇi dhanūṃṣi ca
a asayo 'tra kapālāni puroḍāśāḥ śirāṃsi ca
c havis tu rudhiraṃ kṛṣṇa asmin yajñe bhaviṣyati
a idhmāḥ paridhayaś caiva śaktyo 'tha vimalā gadāḥ
c sadasyā droṇaśiṣyāś ca kṛpasya ca śaradvataḥ
a iṣavo 'tra paristomā muktā gāṇḍīvadhanvanā
c mahārathaprayuktāś ca droṇadrauṇipracoditāḥ
a prātiprasthānikaṃ karma sātyakiḥ sa kariṣyati
c dīkṣito dhārtarāṣṭro 'tra patnī cāsya mahācamūḥ
a ghaṭotkaco 'tra śāmitraṃ kariṣyati mahābalaḥ
c atirātre mahābāho vitate yajñakarmaṇi
a dakṣiṇā tv asya yajñasya dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ pratāpavān
c vaitāne karmaṇi tate jāto yaḥ kṛṣṇa pāvakāt
a yad abruvam ahaṃ kṛṣṇa kaṭukāni sma pāṇḍavān
c priyārthaṃ dhārtarāṣṭrasya tena tapye 'dya karmaṇā
a yadā drakṣyasi māṃ kṛṣṇa nihataṃ savyasācinā
c punaś citis tadā cāsya yajñasyātha bhaviṣyati
a duḥśāsanasya rudhiraṃ yadā pāsyati pāṇḍavaḥ
c ānardaṃ nardataḥ samyak tadā sutyaṃ bhaviṣyati
a yadā droṇaṃ ca bhīṣmaṃ ca pāñcālyau pātayiṣyataḥ
c tadā yajñāvasānaṃ tad bhaviṣyati janārdana
a duryodhanaṃ yadā hantā bhīmaseno mahābalaḥ
c tadā samāpsyate yajño dhārtarāṣṭrasya mādhava
a snuṣāś ca prasnuṣāś caiva dhṛtarāṣṭrasya saṃgatāḥ
c hateśvarā hatasutā hatanāthāś ca keśava
a gāndhāryā saha rodantyaḥ śvagṛdhrakurarākule
c sa yajñe 'sminn avabhṛtho bhaviṣyati janārdana
a vidyāvṛddhā vayovṛddhāḥ kṣatriyāḥ kṣatriyarṣabha
c vṛthāmṛtyuṃ na kurvīraṃs tvatkṛte madhusūdana
a śastreṇa nidhanaṃ gacchet samṛddhaṃ kṣatramaṇḍalam
c kurukṣetre puṇyatame trailokyasyāpi keśava
a tad atra puṇḍarīkākṣa vidhatsva yad abhīpsitam
c yathā kārtsnyena vārṣṇeya kṣatraṃ svargam avāpnuyāt
a yāvat sthāsyanti girayaḥ saritaś ca janārdana
c tāvat kīrtibhavaḥ śabdaḥ śāśvato 'yaṃ bhaviṣyati
a brāhmaṇāḥ kathayiṣyanti mahābhāratam āhavam
c samāgameṣu vārṣṇeya kṣatriyāṇāṃ yaśodharam
d teṣām āyuś ca putrāś ca dhanaṃ caiva bhaviṣyati
d śṛṇvatāṃ cāpi martyānāṃ svargasthānaṃ bhaviṣyati
a samupānaya kaunteyaṃ yuddhāya mama keśava
c mantrasaṃvaraṇaṃ kurvan nityam eva paraṃtapa
 saṃjaya uvāca
a karṇasya vacanaṃ śrutvā keśavaḥ paravīrahā
c uvāca prahasan vākyaṃ smitapūrvam idaṃ tadā
a api tvāṃ na tapet karṇa rājyalābhopapādanā
c mayā dattāṃ hi pṛthivīṃ na praśāsitum icchasi
a dhruvo jayaḥ pāṇḍavānām itīdaṃ
na saṃśayaḥ kaś cana vidyate 'tra
c jayadhvajo dṛśyate pāṇḍavasya
samucchrito vānararāja ugraḥ
a divyā māyā vihitā bhauvanena
samucchritā indraketuprakāśā
c divyāni bhūtāni bhayāvahāni
dṛśyanti caivātra bhayānakāni
a na sajjate śailavanaspatibhya
ūrdhvaṃ tiryag yojanamātrarūpaḥ
c śrīmān dhvajaḥ karṇa dhanaṃjayasya
samucchritaḥ pāvakatulyarūpaḥ
a yadā drakṣyasi saṃgrāme śvetāśvaṃ kṛṣṇasārathim
c aindram astraṃ vikurvāṇam ubhe caivāgnimārute
a gāṇḍīvasya ca nirghoṣaṃ visphūrjitam ivāśaneḥ
c na tadā bhavitā tretā na kṛtaṃ dvāparaṃ na ca
a yadā drakṣyasi saṃgrāme kuntīputraṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
c japahomasamāyuktaṃ svāṃ rakṣantaṃ mahācamūm
a ādityam iva durdharṣaṃ tapantaṃ śatruvāhinīm
c na tadā bhavitā tretā na kṛtaṃ dvāparaṃ na ca
a yadā drakṣyasi saṃgrāme bhīmasenaṃ mahābalam
c duḥśāsanasya rudhiraṃ pītvā nṛtyantam āhave
a prabhinnam iva mātaṅgaṃ pratidviradaghātinam
c na tadā bhavitā tretā na kṛtaṃ dvāparaṃ na ca
d na yāty aśūnya eko 'pi na ca śūnyaṃ pratiṣṭhitam
d na lokapālās tiṣṭhanti na ca te dviguṇāḥ smṛtāḥ
d naiva sapta tathānye vai nava saṃkhyā na vidyate
d etadvādvapadaṃ tatra bhaviṣyati kathaṃ cana
a yadā drakṣyasi saṃgrāme mādrīputrau mahārathau
c vāhinīṃ dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ kṣobhayantau gajāv iva
a vigāḍhe śastrasaṃpāte paravīrarathārujau
c na tadā bhavitā tretā na kṛtaṃ dvāparaṃ na ca
a yadā drakṣyasi saṃgrāme droṇaṃ śāṃtanavaṃ kṛpam
c suyodhanaṃ ca rājānaṃ saindhavaṃ ca jayadratham
a yuddhāyāpatatas tūrṇaṃ vāritān savyasācinā
c na tadā bhavitā tretā na kṛtaṃ dvāparaṃ na ca
a brūyāḥ karṇa ito gatvā droṇaṃ śāṃtanavaṃ kṛpam
c saumyo 'yaṃ vartate māsaḥ suprāpayavasendhanaḥ
a pakvauṣadhivanasphītaḥ phalavān alpamakṣikaḥ
c niṣpaṅko rasavat toyo nātyuṣṇaśiśiraḥ sukhaḥ
a saptamāc cāpi divasād amāvāsyā bhaviṣyati
c saṃgrāmaṃ yojayet tatra tāṃ hy āhuḥ śakradevatām
a tathā rājño vadeḥ sarvān ye yuddhāyābhyupāgatāḥ
c yad vo manīṣitaṃ tad vai sarvaṃ saṃpādayāmi vaḥ
a rājāno rājaputrāś ca duryodhanavaśānugāḥ
c prāpya śastreṇa nidhanaṃ prāpsyanti gatim uttamām
 saṃjaya uvāca
a keśavasya tu tad vākyaṃ karṇaḥ śrutvā hitaṃ śubham
c abravīd abhisaṃpūjya kṛṣṇaṃ madhuniṣūdanam
e jānan māṃ kiṃ mahābāho saṃmohayitum icchasi
a yo 'yaṃ pṛthivyāḥ kārtsnyena vināśaḥ samupasthitaḥ
c nimittaṃ tatra śakunir ahaṃ duḥśāsanas tathā
e duryodhanaś ca nṛpatir dhṛtarāṣṭrasuto 'bhavat
a asaṃśayam idaṃ kṛṣṇa mahad yuddham upasthitam
c pāṇḍavānāṃ kurūṇāṃ ca ghoraṃ rudhirakardamam
a rājāno rājaputrāś ca duryodhanavaśānugāḥ
c raṇe śastrāgninā dagdhāḥ prāpsyanti yamasādanam
a svapnā hi bahavo ghorā dṛśyante madhusūdana
c nimittāni ca ghorāṇi tathotpātāḥ sudāruṇāḥ
a parājayaṃ dhārtarāṣṭre vijayaṃ ca yudhiṣṭhire
c śaṃsanta iva vārṣṇeya vividhā lomaharṣaṇāḥ
a prājāpatyaṃ hi nakṣatraṃ grahas tīkṣṇo mahādyutiḥ
c śanaiścaraḥ pīḍayati pīḍayan prāṇino 'dhikam
a kṛtvā cāṅgārako vakraṃ jyeṣṭhāyāṃ madhusūdana
c anurādhāṃ prārthayate maitraṃ saṃśamayann iva
a nūnaṃ mahad bhayaṃ kṛṣṇa kurūṇāṃ samupasthitam
c viśeṣeṇa hi vārṣṇeya citrāṃ pīḍayate grahaḥ
a somasya lakṣma vyāvṛttaṃ rāhur arkam upeṣyati
c divaś colkāḥ patanty etāḥ sanirghātāḥ sakampanāḥ
a niṣṭananti ca mātaṅgā muñcanty aśrūṇi vājinaḥ
c pānīyaṃ yavasaṃ cāpi nābhinandanti mādhava
a prādurbhūteṣu caiteṣu bhayam āhur upasthitam
c nimitteṣu mahābāho dāruṇaṃ prāṇināśanam
a alpe bhukte purīṣaṃ ca prabhūtam iha dṛśyate
c vājināṃ vāraṇānāṃ ca manuṣyāṇāṃ ca keśava
a dhārtarāṣṭrasya sainyeṣu sarveṣu madhusūdana
c parābhavasya tal liṅgam iti prāhur manīṣiṇaḥ
a prahṛṣṭaṃ vāhanaṃ kṛṣṇa pāṇḍavānāṃ pracakṣate
c pradakṣiṇā mṛgāś caiva tat teṣāṃ jayalakṣaṇam
a apasavyā mṛgāḥ sarve dhārtarāṣṭrasya keśava
c vācaś cāpy aśarīriṇyas tat parābhavalakṣaṇam
d janasyāsvasthakāriṇyas tat parābhavalakṣaṇam
a mayūrāḥ puṣpaśakunā haṃsāḥ sārasacātakāḥ
c jīvaṃ jīvakasaṃghāś cāpy anugacchanti pāṇḍavān
a gṛdhrāḥ kākā baḍāḥ śyenā yātudhānāḥ śalāvṛkāḥ
c makṣikāṇāṃ ca saṃghātā anugacchanti kauravān
a dhārtarāṣṭrasya sainyeṣu bherīṇāṃ nāsti nisvanaḥ
c anāhatāḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ nadanti paṭahāḥ kila
a udapānāś ca nardanti yathā govṛṣabhās tathā
c dhārtarāṣṭrasya sainyeṣu tat parābhavalakṣaṇam
a māṃsaśoṇitavarṣaṃ ca vṛṣṭaṃ devena mādhava
c tathā gandharvanagaraṃ bhānumantam upasthitam
e saprākāraṃ saparikhaṃ savapraṃ cārutoraṇam
a kṛṣṇaś ca parighas tatra bhānum āvṛtya tiṣṭhati
c udayāstamaye saṃdhye vedayāno mahad bhayam
d ekapakṣākṣicaraṇā nartakā ghoradarśanāḥ
d pakṣiṇo vyasṛjan ghoraṃ tat parābhavalakṣaṇam
e ekā sṛg vāśate ghoraṃ tat parābhavalakṣaṇam
a kṛṣṇagrīvāś ca śakunā lambamānā bhayānakāḥ
c saṃdhyām abhimukhā yānti tat parābhavalakṣaṇam
a brāhmaṇān prathamaṃ dveṣṭi gurūṃś ca madhusūdana
c bhṛtyān bhaktimataś cāpi tat parābhavalakṣaṇam
a pūrvā dig lohitākārā śastravarṇā ca dakṣiṇā
c āmapātrapratīkāśā paścimā madhusūdana
d uttarā śaṅkhavarṇābhā diśāṃ varṇā udāhṛtāḥ
a pradīptāś ca diśaḥ sarvā dhārtarāṣṭrasya mādhava
c mahad bhayaṃ vedayanti tasminn utpātalakṣaṇe
a sahasrapādaṃ prāsādaṃ svapnānte sma yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c adhirohan mayā dṛṣṭaḥ saha bhrātṛbhir acyuta
a śvetoṣṇīṣāś ca dṛśyante sarve te śuklavāsasaḥ
c āsanāni ca śubhrāṇi sarveṣām upalakṣaye
a tava cāpi mayā kṛṣṇa svapnānte rudhirāvilā
c āntreṇa pṛthivī dṛṣṭā parikṣiptā janārdana
a asthisaṃcayam ārūḍhaś cāmitaujā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c suvarṇapātryāṃ saṃhṛṣṭo bhuktavān ghṛtapāyasam
a yudhiṣṭhiro mayā dṛṣṭo grasamāno vasuṃdharām
c tvayā dattām imāṃ vyaktaṃ bhokṣyate sa vasuṃdharām
a uccaṃ parvatam ārūḍho bhīmakarmā vṛkodaraḥ
c gadāpāṇir naravyāghro vīkṣann iva mahīm imām
a kṣapayiṣyati naḥ sarvān sa suvyaktaṃ mahāraṇe
c viditaṃ me hṛṣīkeśa yato dharmas tato jayaḥ
a pāṇḍuraṃ gajam ārūḍho gāṇḍīvī sa dhanaṃjayaḥ
c tvayā sārdhaṃ hṛṣīkeśa śriyā paramayā jvalan
a yūyaṃ sarvān vadhiṣyadhvaṃ tatra me nāsti saṃśayaḥ
c pārthivān samare kṛṣṇa duryodhanapurogamān
a nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca sātyakiś ca mahārathaḥ
c śuddhakeyūrakaṇṭhatrāḥ śuklamālyāmbarāvṛtāḥ
a adhirūḍhā naravyāghrā naravāhanam uttamam
c traya ete mahāmātrāḥ pāṇḍuracchatravāsasaḥ
a śvetoṣṇīṣāś ca dṛśyante traya eva janārdana
c dhārtarāṣṭrasya sainyeṣu tān vijānīhi keśava
a aśvatthāmā kṛpaś caiva kṛtavarmā ca sātvataḥ
c raktoṣṇīṣāś ca dṛśyante sarve mādhava pārthivāḥ
a uṣṭrayuktaṃ samārūḍhau bhīṣmadroṇau janārdana
c mayā sārdhaṃ mahābāho dhārtarāṣṭreṇa cābhibho
a agastyaśāstāṃ ca diśaṃ prayātāḥ sma janārdana
c acireṇaiva kālena prāpsyāmo yamasādanam
a ahaṃ cānye ca rājāno yac ca tat kṣatramaṇḍalam
c gāṇḍīvāgniṃ pravekṣyāma iti me nāsti saṃśayaḥ
 kṛṣṇa uvāca
a upasthitavināśeyaṃ nūnam adya vasuṃdharā
c tathā hi me vacaḥ karṇa nopaiti hṛdayaṃ tava
a sarveṣāṃ tāta bhūtānāṃ vināśe samupasthite
c anayo nayasaṃkāśo hṛdayān nāpasarpati
 karṇa uvāca
a api tvā kṛṣṇa paśyāma jīvanto 'smān mahāraṇāt
c samuttīrṇā mahābāho vīrakṣayavināśanāt
a atha vā saṃgamaḥ kṛṣṇa svarge no bhavitā dhruvam
c tatredānīṃ sameṣyāmaḥ punaḥ sārdhaṃ tvayānagha
 saṃjaya uvāca
a ity uktvā mādhavaṃ karṇaḥ pariṣvajya ca pīḍitam
c visarjitaḥ keśavena rathopasthād avātarat
a tataḥ svaratham āsthāya jāmbūnadavibhūṣitam
c sahāsmābhir nivavṛte rādheyo dīnamānasaḥ
a tataḥ śīghrataraṃ prāyāt keśavaḥ sahasātyakiḥ
c punar uccārayan vāṇīṃ yāhi yāhīti sārathim
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a asiddhānunaye kṛṣṇe kurubhyaḥ pāṇḍavān gate
c abhigamya pṛthāṃ kṣattā śanaiḥ śocann ivābravīt
a jānāsi me jīvaputre bhāvaṃ nityam anugrahe
c krośato na ca gṛhṇīte vacanaṃ me suyodhanaḥ
a upapanno hy asau rājā cedipāñcālakekayaiḥ
c bhīmārjunābhyāṃ kṛṣṇena yuyudhānayamair api
a upaplavye niviṣṭo 'pi dharmam eva yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c kāṅkṣate jñātisauhārdād balavān durbalo yathā
a rājā tu dhṛtarāṣṭro 'yaṃ vayovṛddho na śāmyati
c mattaḥ putramadenaiva vidharme pathi vartate
a jayadrathasya karṇasya tathā duḥśāsanasya ca
c saubalasya ca durbuddhyā mithobhedaḥ pravartate
a adharmeṇa hi dharmiṣṭhaṃ hṛtaṃ vai rājyam īdṛśam
c yeṣāṃ teṣām ayaṃ dharmaḥ sānubandho bhaviṣyati
a hriyamāṇe balād dharme kurubhiḥ ko na saṃjvaret
c asāmnā keśave yāte samudyokṣyanti pāṇḍavāḥ
a tataḥ kurūṇām anayo bhavitā vīranāśanaḥ
c cintayan na labhe nidrām ahaḥsu ca niśāsu ca
a śrutvā tu kuntī tad vākyam arthakāmena bhāṣitam
c aniṣṭanantī duḥkhārtā manasā vimamarśa ha
a dhig astv arthaṃ yatkṛte 'yaṃ mahāñ jñātivadhe kṣayaḥ
c vartsyate suhṛdāṃ hy eṣāṃ yuddhe 'smin vai parābhavaḥ
a pāṇḍavāś cedipāñcālā yādavāś ca samāgatāḥ
c bhāratair yadi yotsyanti kiṃ nu duḥkham ataḥ param
a paśye doṣaṃ dhruvaṃ yuddhe tathā yuddhe parābhavam
c adhanasya mṛtaṃ śreyo na hi jñātikṣaye jayaḥ
d iti me cintayantyā vai hṛdi duḥkhaṃ pravartate
a pitāmahaḥ śāṃtanava ācāryaś ca yudhāṃ patiḥ
c karṇaś ca dhārtarāṣṭrārthaṃ vardhayanti bhayaṃ mama
a nācāryaḥ kāmavāñ śiṣyair droṇo yudhyeta jātu cit
c pāṇḍaveṣu kathaṃ hārdaṃ kuryān na ca pitāmahaḥ
a ayaṃ tv eko vṛthādṛṣṭir dhārtarāṣṭrasya durmateḥ
c mohānuvartī satataṃ pāpo dveṣṭi ca pāṇḍavān
a mahaty anarthe nirbandhī balavāṃś ca viśeṣataḥ
c karṇaḥ sadā pāṇḍavānāṃ tan me dahati sāṃpratam
a āśaṃse tv adya karṇasya mano 'haṃ pāṇḍavān prati
c prasādayitum āsādya darśayantī yathātatham
a toṣito bhagavān yatra durvāsā me varaṃ dadau
c āhvānaṃ devasaṃyuktaṃ vasantyāḥ pitṛveśmani
a sāham antaḥpure rājñaḥ kuntibhojapuraskṛtā
c cintayantī bahuvidhaṃ hṛdayena vidūyatā
a balābalaṃ ca mantrāṇāṃ brāhmaṇasya ca vāgbalam
c strībhāvād bālabhāvāc ca cintayantī punaḥ punaḥ
a dhātryā viśrabdhayā guptā sakhījanavṛtā tadā
c doṣaṃ pariharantī ca pituś cāritrarakṣiṇī
a kathaṃ nu sukṛtaṃ me syān nāparādhavatī katham
c bhaveyam iti saṃcintya brāhmaṇaṃ taṃ namasya ca
a kautūhalāt tu taṃ labdhvā bāliśyād ācaraṃ tadā
c kanyā satī devam arkam āsādayam ahaṃ tataḥ
a yo 'sau kānīnagarbho me putravat parivartitaḥ
c kasmān na kuryād vacanaṃ pathyaṃ bhrātṛhitaṃ tathā
a iti kuntī viniścitya kāryaṃ niścitam uttamam
c kāryārtham abhiniryāya yayau bhāgīrathīṃ prati
a ātmajasya tatas tasya ghṛṇinaḥ satyasaṅginaḥ
b gaṅgātīre pṛthāpaśyad upasthānagataṃ vṛṣam
c gaṅgātīre pṛthāśṛṇvad upādhyayananisvanam
a prāṅmukhasyordhvabāhoḥ sā paryatiṣṭhata pṛṣṭhataḥ
c japyāvasānaṃ kāryārthaṃ pratīkṣantī tapasvinī
a atiṣṭhat sūryatāpārtā karṇasyottaravāsasi
c kauravyapatnī vārṣṇeyī padmamāleva śuṣyatī
a ā pṛṣṭhatāpāj japtvā sa parivṛtya yatavrataḥ
c dṛṣṭvā kuntīm upātiṣṭhad abhivādya kṛtāñjaliḥ
e yathānyāyaṃ mahātejā mānī dharmabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
f utsmayan praṇataḥ prāha kuntīṃ vaikartano vṛṣaḥ
 karṇa uvāca
a rādheyo 'ham ādhirathiḥ karṇas tvām abhivādaye
c prāptā kimarthaṃ bhavatī brūhi kiṃ karavāṇi te
 kunty uvāca
a kaunteyas tvaṃ na rādheyo na tavādhirathaḥ pitā
c nāsi sūtakule jātaḥ karṇa tad viddhi me vacaḥ
a kānīnas tvaṃ mayā jātaḥ pūrvajaḥ kukṣiṇā dhṛtaḥ
c kuntibhojasya bhavane pārthas tvam asi putraka
a prakāśakarmā tapano yo 'yaṃ devo virocanaḥ
c ajījanat tvāṃ mayy eṣa karṇa śastrabhṛtāṃ varam
a kuṇḍalī baddhakavaco devagarbhaḥ śriyā vṛtaḥ
c jātas tvam asi durdharṣa mayā putra pitur gṛhe
a sa tvaṃ bhrātṝn asaṃbuddhvā mohād yad upasevase
c dhārtarāṣṭrān na tad yuktaṃ tvayi putra viśeṣataḥ
a etad dharmaphalaṃ putra narāṇāṃ dharmaniścaye
c yat tuṣyanty asya pitaro mātā cāpy ekadarśinī
a arjunenārjitāṃ pūrvaṃ hṛtāṃ lobhād asādhubhiḥ
c ācchidya dhārtarāṣṭrebhyo bhuṅkṣva yaudhiṣṭhirīṃ śriyam
a adya paśyantu kuravaḥ karṇārjunasamāgamam
c saubhrātreṇa tad ālakṣya saṃnamantām asādhavaḥ
a karṇārjunau vai bhavatāṃ yathā rāmajanārdanau
c asādhyaṃ kiṃ nu loke syād yuvayoḥ sahitātmanoḥ
a karṇa śobhiṣyase nūnaṃ pañcabhir bhrātṛbhir vṛtaḥ
c vedaiḥ parivṛto brahmā yathā vedāṅgapañcamaiḥ
a upapanno guṇaiḥ śreṣṭho jyeṣṭhaḥ śreṣṭheṣu bandhuṣu
c sūtaputreti mā śabdaḥ pārthas tvam asi vīryavān
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tataḥ sūryān niścaritāṃ karṇaḥ śuśrāva bhāratīm
c duratyayāṃ praṇayinīṃ pitṛvad bhāskareritām
a satyam āha pṛthā vākyaṃ karṇa mātṛvacaḥ kuru
c śreyas te syān naravyāghra sarvam ācaratas tathā
a evam uktasya mātrā ca svayaṃ pitrā ca bhānunā
c cacāla naiva karṇasya matiḥ satyadhṛtes tadā
 karṇa uvāca
a na te na śraddadhe vākyaṃ kṣatriye bhāṣitaṃ tvayā
c dharmadvāraṃ mamaitat syān niyogakaraṇaṃ tava
a akaron mayi yat pāpaṃ bhavatī sumahātyayam
c avakīrṇo 'smi te tena tad yaśaḥkīrtināśanam
a ahaṃ ca kṣatriyo jāto na prāptaḥ kṣatrasatkriyām
c tvatkṛte kiṃ nu pāpīyaḥ śatruḥ kuryān mamāhitam
a kriyākāle tv anukrośam akṛtvā tvam imaṃ mama
c hīnasaṃskārasamayam adya māṃ samacūcudaḥ
a na vai mama hitaṃ pūrvaṃ mātṛvac ceṣṭitaṃ tvayā
c sā māṃ saṃbodhayasy adya kevalātmahitaiṣiṇī
a kṛṣṇena sahitāt ko vai na vyatheta dhanaṃjayāt
c ko 'dya bhītaṃ na māṃ vidyāt pārthānāṃ samitiṃ gatam
a abhrātā viditaḥ pūrvaṃ yuddhakāle prakāśitaḥ
c pāṇḍavān yadi gacchāmi kiṃ māṃ kṣatraṃ vadiṣyati
a sarvakāmaiḥ saṃvibhaktaḥ pūjitaś ca sadā bhṛśam
c ahaṃ vai dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ kuryāṃ tad aphalaṃ katham
a upanahya parair vairaṃ ye māṃ nityam upāsate
c namaskurvanti ca sadā vasavo vāsavaṃ yathā
a mama prāṇena ye śatrūñ śaktāḥ pratisamāsitum
c manyante 'dya kathaṃ teṣām ahaṃ bhindyāṃ manoratham
a mayā plavena saṃgrāmaṃ titīrṣanti duratyayam
c apāre pārakāmā ye tyajeyaṃ tān ahaṃ katham
a ayaṃ hi kālaḥ saṃprāpto dhārtarāṣṭropajīvinām
c nirveṣṭavyaṃ mayā tatra prāṇān aparirakṣatā
a kṛtārthāḥ subhṛtā ye hi kṛtyakāla upasthite
c anavekṣya kṛtaṃ pāpā vikurvanty anavasthitāḥ
a rājakilbiṣiṇāṃ teṣāṃ bhartṛpiṇḍāpahāriṇām
c naivāyaṃ na paro loko vidyate pāpakarmaṇām
a dhṛtarāṣṭrasya putrāṇām arthe yotsyāmi te sutaiḥ
c balaṃ ca śaktiṃ cāsthāya na vai tvayy anṛtaṃ vade
a ānṛśaṃsyam atho vṛttaṃ rakṣan satpuruṣocitam
c ato 'rthakaram apy etan na karomy adya te vacaḥ
a na tu te 'yaṃ samārambho mayi mogho bhaviṣyati
c vadhyān viṣahyān saṃgrāme na haniṣyāmi te sutān
e yudhiṣṭhiraṃ ca bhīmaṃ ca yamau caivārjunād ṛte
a arjunena samaṃ yuddhaṃ mama yaudhiṣṭhire bale
c arjunaṃ hi nihatyājau saṃprāptaṃ syāt phalaṃ mayā
e yaśasā cāpi yujyeyaṃ nihataḥ savyasācinā
a na te jātu naśiṣyanti putrāḥ pañca yaśasvini
c nirarjunāḥ sakarṇā vā sārjunā vā hate mayi
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a iti karṇavacaḥ śrutvā kuntī duḥkhāt pravepatī
c uvāca putram āśliṣya karṇaṃ dhairyād akampitam
a evaṃ vai bhāvyam etena kṣayaṃ yāsyanti kauravāḥ
c yathā tvaṃ bhāṣase karṇa daivaṃ tu balavattaram
a tvayā caturṇāṃ bhrātṝṇām abhayaṃ śatrukarśana
c dattaṃ tat pratijānīhi saṃgarapratimocanam
a anāmayaṃ svasti ceti pṛthātho karṇam abravīt
c tāṃ karṇo 'bhyavadat prītas tatas tau jagmatuḥ pṛthak
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a āgamya hāstinapurād upaplavyam ariṃdamaḥ
c pāṇḍavānāṃ yathāvṛttaṃ keśavaḥ sarvam uktavān
a saṃbhāṣya suciraṃ kālaṃ mantrayitvā punaḥ punaḥ
c svam evāvasathaṃ śaurir viśrāmārthaṃ jagāma ha
a visṛjya sarvān nṛpatīn virāṭapramukhāṃs tadā
c pāṇḍavā bhrātaraḥ pañca bhānāv astaṃgate sati
a saṃdhyām upāsya dhyāyantas tam eva gatamānasāḥ
c ānāyya kṛṣṇaṃ dāśārhaṃ punar mantram amantrayan
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a tvayā nāgapuraṃ gatvā sabhāyāṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrajaḥ
c kim uktaḥ puṇḍarīkākṣa tan naḥ śaṃsitum arhasi
 vāsudeva uvāca
a mayā nāgapuraṃ gatvā sabhāyāṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrajaḥ
c tathyaṃ pathyaṃ hitaṃ cokto na ca gṛhṇāti durmatiḥ
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a tasminn utpatham āpanne kuruvṛddhaḥ pitāmahaḥ
c kim uktavān hṛṣīkeśa duryodhanam amarṣaṇam
e ācāryo vā mahābāho bhāradvājaḥ kim abravīt
f pitā vā dhṛtarāṣṭras taṃ gāndhārī vā kim abravīt
a pitā yavīyān asmākaṃ kṣattā dharmabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
c putraśokābhisaṃtaptaḥ kim āha dhṛtarāṣṭrajam
a kiṃ ca sarve nṛpatayaḥ sabhāyāṃ ye samāsate
c uktavanto yathātattvaṃ tad brūhi tvaṃ janārdana
a uktavān hi bhavān sarvaṃ vacanaṃ kurumukhyayoḥ
b dhārtarāṣṭrasya teṣāṃ hi vacanaṃ kurusaṃsadi
b pratikūlam ayuktaṃ ca hṛdayaṃ nopasarpati
c kāmalobhābhibhūtasya mandasya prājñamāninaḥ
a apriyaṃ hṛdaye mahyaṃ tan na tiṣṭhati keśava
c teṣāṃ vākyāni govinda śrotum icchāmy ahaṃ vibho
a yathā ca nābhipadyeta kālas tāta tathā kuru
c bhavān hi no gatiḥ kṛṣṇa bhavān nātho bhavān guruḥ
 vāsudeva uvāca
a śṛṇu rājan yathā vākyam ukto rājā suyodhanaḥ
c madhye kurūṇāṃ rājendra sabhāyāṃ tan nibodha me
a mayā vai śrāvite vākye jahāsa dhṛtarāṣṭrajaḥ
c atha bhīṣmaḥ susaṃkruddha idaṃ vacanam abravīt
a duryodhana nibodhedaṃ kulārthe yad bravīmi te
c tac chrutvā rājaśārdūla svakulasya hitaṃ kuru
a mama tāta pitā rājañ śaṃtanur lokaviśrutaḥ
c tasyāham eka evāsaṃ putraḥ putravatāṃ varaḥ
a tasya buddhiḥ samutpannā dvitīyaḥ syāt kathaṃ sutaḥ
c ekaputram aputraṃ vai pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ
a na cocchedaṃ kulaṃ yāyād vistīryeta kathaṃ yaśaḥ
c tasyāham īpsitaṃ buddhvā kālīṃ mātaram āvaham
a pratijñāṃ duṣkarāṃ kṛtvā pitur arthe kulasya ca
c arājā cordhvaretāś ca yathā suviditaṃ tava
e pratīto nivasāmy eṣa pratijñām anupālayan
a tasyāṃ jajñe mahābāhuḥ śrīmān kurukulodvahaḥ
c vicitravīryo dharmātmā kanīyān mama pārthivaḥ
a svaryāte 'haṃ pitari taṃ svarājye saṃnyaveśayam
c vicitravīryaṃ rājānaṃ bhṛtyo bhūtvā hy adhaścaraḥ
a tasyāhaṃ sadṛśān dārān rājendra samudāvaham
c jitvā pārthivasaṃghātam api te bahuśaḥ śrutam
a tato rāmeṇa samare dvandvayuddham upāgamam
c sa hi rāmabhayād ebhir nāgarair vipravāsitaḥ
e dāreṣv atiprasaktaś ca yakṣmāṇaṃ samapadyata
a yadā tv arājake rāṣṭre na vavarṣa sureśvaraḥ
c tadābhyadhāvan mām eva prajāḥ kṣudbhayapīḍitāḥ
 prajā ūcuḥ
a upakṣīṇāḥ prajāḥ sarvā rājā bhava bhavāya naḥ
c ītayo nuda bhadraṃ te śaṃtanoḥ kulavardhana
a pīḍyante te prajāḥ sarvā vyādhibhir bhṛśadāruṇaiḥ
c alpāvaśiṣṭā gāṅgeya tāḥ paritrātum arhasi
a vyādhīn praṇudya vīra tvaṃ prajā dharmeṇa pālaya
c tvayi jīvati mā rāṣṭraṃ vināśam upagacchatu
 bhīṣma uvāca
a prajānāṃ krośatīnāṃ vai naivākṣubhyata me manaḥ
c pratijñāṃ rakṣamāṇasya sadvṛttaṃ smaratas tathā
a tataḥ paurā mahārāja mātā kālī ca me śubhā
c bhṛtyāḥ purohitācāryā brāhmaṇāś ca bahuśrutāḥ
e mām ūcur bhṛśasaṃtaptā bhava rājeti saṃtatam
a pratīparakṣitaṃ rāṣṭraṃ tvāṃ prāpya vinaśiṣyati
c sa tvam asmaddhitārthaṃ vai rājā bhava mahāmate
a ity uktaḥ prāñjalir bhūtvā duḥkhito bhṛśam āturaḥ

a tato 'haṃ prāñjalir bhūtvā mātaraṃ saṃprasādayam
c nāmba śaṃtanunā jātaḥ kauravaṃ vaṃśam udvahan

a viśeṣatas tvadarthaṃ ca dhuri mā māṃ niyojaya
c ahaṃ preṣyaś ca dāsaś ca tavāmba sutavatsale

c ayācaṃ bhrātṛdāreṣu tadā vyāsaṃ mahāmunim
a saha mātrā mahārāja prasādya tam ṛṣiṃ tadā
c apatyārtham ayācaṃ vai prasādaṃ kṛtavāṃś ca saḥ
e trīn sa putrān ajanayat tadā bharatasattama
a andhaḥ karaṇahīneti na vai rājā pitā tava
c rājā tu pāṇḍur abhavan mahātmā lokaviśrutaḥ
a sa rājā tasya te putrāḥ pitur dāyādyahāriṇaḥ
c mā tāta kalahaṃ kārṣī rājyasyārdhaṃ pradīyatām
a mayi jīvati rājyaṃ kaḥ saṃpraśāset pumān iha
c māvamaṃsthā vaco mahyaṃ śamam icchāmi vaḥ sadā

c matam etat pitus tubhyaṃ gāndhāryā vidurasya ca
a śrotavyaṃ yadi vṛddhānāṃ mātiśaṅkīr vaco mama
c nāśayiṣyasi mā sarvam ātmānaṃ pṛthivīṃ tathā
 vāsudeva uvāca
a bhīṣmeṇokte tato droṇo duryodhanam abhāṣata
c madhye nṛpāṇāṃ bhadraṃ te vacanaṃ vacanakṣamaḥ
a prātīpaḥ śaṃtanus tāta kulasyārthe yathotthitaḥ
c tathā devavrato bhīṣmaḥ kulasyārthe sthito 'bhavat
a tataḥ pāṇḍur narapatiḥ satyasaṃdho jitendriyaḥ
c rājā kurūṇāṃ dharmātmā suvrataḥ susamāhitaḥ
a jyeṣṭhāya rājyam adadād dhṛtarāṣṭrāya dhīmate
c yavīyasas tathā kṣattuḥ kuruvaṃśavivardhanaḥ
a tataḥ siṃhāsane rājan sthāpayitvainam acyutam
c vanaṃ jagāma kauravyo bhāryābhyāṃ sahito 'nagha

c preṣyavat puruṣavyāghro vālavyajanam utkṣipan

c anvapadyanta vidhivad yathā pāṇḍuṃ narādhipam
a visṛjya dhṛtarāṣṭrāya rājyaṃ sa vidurāya ca
c cacāra pṛthivīṃ pāṇḍuḥ sarvāṃ parapuraṃjayaḥ
a kośasaṃjanane dāne bhṛtyānāṃ cānvavekṣaṇe
c bharaṇe caiva sarvasya viduraḥ satyasaṃgaraḥ
a saṃdhivigrahasaṃyukto rājñaḥ saṃvāhanakriyāḥ
c avaikṣata mahātejā bhīṣmaḥ parapuraṃjayaḥ
a siṃhāsanastho nṛpatir dhṛtarāṣṭro mahābalaḥ
c anvāsyamānaḥ satataṃ vidureṇa mahātmanā
a kathaṃ tasya kule jātaḥ kulabhedaṃ vyavasyasi
c saṃbhūya bhrātṛbhiḥ sārdhaṃ bhuṅkṣva bhogāñ janādhipa
a bravīmy ahaṃ na kārpaṇyān nārthahetoḥ kathaṃ cana
