a nāhaṃ tvatto 'bhikāṅkṣiṣye vṛttyupāyaṃ janādhipa
c yato bhīṣmas tato droṇo yad bhīṣmas tv āha tat kuru
a dīyatāṃ pāṇḍuputrebhyo rājyārdham arikarśana
c samam ācāryakaṃ tāta tava teṣāṃ ca me sadā
a aśvatthāmā yathā mahyaṃ tathā śvetahayo mama
c bahunā kiṃ pralāpena yato dharmas tato jayaḥ
a evam ukte mahārāja droṇenāmitatejasā
c vyājahāra tato vākyaṃ viduraḥ satyasaṃgaraḥ
e pitur vadanam anvīkṣya parivṛtya ca dharmavit
a devavrata nibodhedaṃ vacanaṃ mama bhāṣataḥ
c pranaṣṭaḥ kauravo vaṃśas tvayāyaṃ punar uddhṛtaḥ
a tan me vilapamānasya vacanaṃ samupekṣase
c ko 'yaṃ duryodhano nāma kule 'smin kulapāṃsanaḥ
a yasya lobhābhibhūtasya matiṃ samanuvartase
c anāryasyākṛtajñasya lobhopahatacetasaḥ
e atikrāmati yaḥ śāstraṃ pitur dharmārthadarśinaḥ
a ete naśyanti kuravo duryodhanakṛtena vai
c yathā te na praṇaśyeyur mahārāja tathā kuru
a māṃ caiva dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ ca pūrvam eva mahādyute
c citrakāra ivālekhyaṃ kṛtvā mā sma vināśaya
e prajāpatiḥ prajāḥ sṛṣṭvā yathā saṃharate tathā
a nopekṣasva mahābāho paśyamānaḥ kulakṣayam
c atha te 'dya matir naṣṭā vināśe pratyupasthite
e vanaṃ gaccha mayā sārdhaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭreṇa caiva ha
a baddhvā vā nikṛtiprajñaṃ dhārtarāṣṭraṃ sudurmatim
c sādhv idaṃ rājyam adyāstu pāṇḍavair abhirakṣitam
a prasīda rājaśārdūla vināśo dṛśyate mahān
c pāṇḍavānāṃ kurūṇāṃ ca rājñāṃ cāmitatejasām
a virarāmaivam uktvā tu viduro dīnamānasaḥ
c pradhyāyamānaḥ sa tadā niḥśvasaṃś ca punaḥ punaḥ
a tato 'tha rājñaḥ subalasya putrī
dharmārthayuktaṃ kulanāśabhītā
c duryodhanaṃ pāpamatiṃ nṛśaṃsaṃ
rājñāṃ samakṣaṃ sutam āha kopāt
a ye pārthivā rājasabhāṃ praviṣṭā
brahmarṣayo ye ca sabhāsado 'nye
c śṛṇvantu vakṣyāmi tavāparādhaṃ
pāpasya sāmātyaparicchadasya
a rājyaṃ kurūṇām anupūrvabhogyaṃ
kramāgato naḥ kuladharma eṣaḥ
c tvaṃ pāpabuddhe 'tinṛśaṃsakarman
rājyaṃ kurūṇām anayād vihaṃsi
a rājye sthito dhṛtarāṣṭro manīṣī
tasyānujo viduro dīrghadarśī
c etāv atikramya kathaṃ nṛpatvaṃ
duryodhana prārthayase 'dya mohāt
a rājā ca kṣattā ca mahānubhāvau
bhīṣme sthite paravantau bhavetām
c ayaṃ tu dharmajñatayā mahātmā
na rājyakāmo nṛvaro nadījaḥ
a rājyaṃ tu pāṇḍor idam apradhṛṣyaṃ
tasyādya putrāḥ prabhavanti nānye
c rājyaṃ tad etan nikhilaṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ
paitāmahaṃ putrapautrānugāmi
a yad vai brūte kurumukhyo mahātmā
devavrataḥ satyasaṃdho manīṣī
c sarvaṃ tad asmābhir ahatya dharmaṃ
grāhyaṃ svadharmaṃ paripālayadbhiḥ
a anujñayā cātha mahāvratasya
brūyān nṛpo yad viduras tathaiva
c kāryaṃ bhavet tat suhṛdbhir niyujya
dharmaṃ puraskṛtya sudīrghakālam
a nyāyāgataṃ rājyam idaṃ kurūṇāṃ
yudhiṣṭhiraḥ śāstu vai dharmaputraḥ
c pracodito dhṛtarāṣṭreṇa rājñā
puraskṛtaḥ śāṃtanavena caiva
 vāsudeva uvāca
a evam ukte tu gāndhāryā dhṛtarāṣṭro janeśvaraḥ
c duryodhanam uvācedaṃ nṛpamadhye janādhipa
a duryodhana nibodhedaṃ yat tvāṃ vakṣyāmi putraka
c tathā tat kuru bhadraṃ te yady asti pitṛgauravam
a somaḥ prajāpatiḥ pūrvaṃ kurūṇāṃ vaṃśavardhanaḥ
c somād babhūva ṣaṣṭho vai yayātir nahuṣātmajaḥ
a tasya putrā babhūvuś ca pañca rājarṣisattamāḥ
c teṣāṃ yadur mahātejā jyeṣṭhaḥ samabhavat prabhuḥ
d tasyābhavaṃs trayaḥ putrā druhyo 'nuḥ pūrur eva ca
a pūrur yavīyāṃś ca tato yo 'smākaṃ vaṃśavardhanaḥ
c śarmiṣṭhāyāḥ saṃprasūto duhitur vṛṣaparvaṇaḥ
a yaduś ca bharataśreṣṭha devayānyāḥ suto 'bhavat
c dauhitras tāta śukrasya kāvyasyāmitatejasaḥ
a yādavānāṃ kulakaro balavān vīryasaṃmataḥ
c avamene sa tu kṣatraṃ darpapūrṇaḥ sumandadhīḥ
a na cātiṣṭhat pituḥ śāstre baladarpavimohitaḥ
b kulakṣayaṃ cakārāsau rājyalobhād akāraṇāt
c avamene ca pitaraṃ bhrātṝṃś cāpy aparājitaḥ
a pṛthivyāṃ caturantāyāṃ yadur evābhavad balī
c vaśe kṛtvā sa nṛpatīn avasan nāgasāhvaye
a taṃ pitā paramakruddho yayātir nahuṣātmajaḥ
c śaśāpa putraṃ gāndhāre rājyāc ca vyaparopayat
a ya cainam anvavartanta bhrātaro baladarpitam
c śaśāpa tān api kruddho yayātis tanayān atha
a yavīyāṃsaṃ tataḥ pūruṃ putraṃ svavaśavartinam
c rājye niveśayām āsa vidheyaṃ nṛpasattamaḥ
a evaṃ jyeṣṭho 'py athotsikto na rājyam abhijāyate
c yavīyāṃso 'bhijāyante rājyaṃ vṛddhopasevayā
a tathaiva sarvadharmajñaḥ pitur mama pitāmahaḥ
c pratīpaḥ pṛthivīpālas triṣu lokeṣu viśrutaḥ
a tasya pārthivasiṃhasya rājyaṃ dharmeṇa śāsataḥ
c trayaḥ prajajñire putrā devakalpā yaśasvinaḥ
a devāpir abhavaj jyeṣṭho bāhlīkas tadanantaram
c tṛtīyaḥ śaṃtanus tāta dhṛtimān me pitāmahaḥ
a devāpis tu mahātejās tvagdoṣī rājasattamaḥ
c dhārmikaḥ satyavādī ca pituḥ śuśrūṣaṇe rataḥ
a paurajānapadānāṃ ca saṃmataḥ sādhusatkṛtaḥ
c sarveṣāṃ bālavṛddhānāṃ devāpir hṛdayaṃgamaḥ
a prājñaś ca satyasaṃdhaś ca sarvabhūtahite rataḥ
c vartamānaḥ pituḥ śāstre brāhmaṇānāṃ tathaiva ca
a bāhlīkasya priyo bhrātā śaṃtanoś ca mahātmanaḥ
c saubhrātraṃ ca paraṃ teṣāṃ sahitānāṃ mahātmanām
a atha kālasya paryāye vṛddho nṛpatisattamaḥ
c saṃbhārān abhiṣekārthaṃ kārayām āsa śāstrataḥ
e maṅgalāni ca sarvāṇi kārayām āsa cābhibhūḥ
a taṃ brāhmaṇāś ca vṛddhāś ca paurajānapadaiḥ saha
c sarve nivārayām āsur devāper abhiṣecanam
a sa tac chrutvā tu nṛpatir abhiṣekanivāraṇam
c aśrukaṇṭho 'bhavad rājā paryaśocata cātmajam
a evaṃ vadānyo dharmajñaḥ satyasaṃdhaś ca so 'bhavat
c priyaḥ prajānām api saṃs tvagdoṣeṇa pradūṣitaḥ
a hīnāṅgaṃ pṛthivīpālaṃ nābhinandanti devatāḥ
c iti kṛtvā nṛpaśreṣṭhaṃ pratyaṣedhan dvijarṣabhāḥ
a tataḥ pravyathitātmāsau putraśokasamanvitaḥ
c mamāra taṃ mṛtaṃ dṛṣṭvā devāpiḥ saṃśrito vanam
a bāhlīko mātulakule tyaktvā rājyaṃ vyavasthitaḥ
c pitṛbhrātṝn parityajya prāptavān puram ṛddhimat
a bāhlīkena tv anujñātaḥ śaṃtanur lokaviśrutaḥ
c pitary uparate rājan rājā rājyam akārayat
a tathaivāhaṃ matimatā paricintyeha pāṇḍunā
c jyeṣṭhaḥ prabhraṃśito rājyād dhīnāṅga iti bhārata
a pāṇḍus tu rājyaṃ saṃprāptaḥ kanīyān api san nṛpaḥ
c vināśe tasya putrāṇām idaṃ rājyam ariṃdama
e mayy abhāgini rājyāya kathaṃ tvaṃ rājyam icchasi
f arājaputro hy asvāmī pārakyaṃ hartum icchasi
a yudhiṣṭhiro rājaputro mahātmā
nyāyāgataṃ rājyam idaṃ ca tasya
c sa kauravasyāsya janasya bhartā
praśāsitā caiva mahānubhāvaḥ
a sa satyasaṃdhaḥ satatāpramattaḥ
śāstre sthito bandhujanasya sādhuḥ
c priyaḥ prajānāṃ suhṛdānukampī
jitendriyaḥ sādhujanasya bhartā
a kṣamā titikṣā dama ārjavaṃ ca
satyavratatvaṃ śrutam apramādaḥ
c bhūtānukampā hy anuśāsanaṃ ca
yudhiṣṭhire rājaguṇāḥ samastāḥ
a arājaputras tvam anāryavṛtto
lubdhas tathā bandhuṣu pāpabuddhiḥ
c kramāgataṃ rājyam idaṃ pareṣāṃ
hartuṃ kathaṃ śakṣyasi durvinītaḥ
a prayaccha rājyārdham apetamohaḥ
savāhanaṃ tvaṃ saparicchadaṃ ca
c tato 'vaśeṣaṃ tava jīvitasya
sahānujasyaiva bhaven narendra
 vāsudeva uvāca
a evam ukte tu bhīṣmeṇa droṇena vidureṇa ca
c gāndhāryā dhṛtarāṣṭreṇa na ca mando 'nvabudhyata
a avadhūyotthitaḥ kruddho roṣāt saṃraktalocanaḥ
c anvadravanta taṃ paścād rājānas tyaktajīvitāḥ
a ajñāpayac ca rājñas tān pārthivān duṣṭacetasaḥ
c prayādhvaṃ vai kurukṣetraṃ puṣyo 'dyeti punaḥ punaḥ
a tatas te pṛthivīpālāḥ prayayuḥ sahasainikāḥ
c bhīṣmaṃ senāpatiṃ kṛtvā saṃhṛṣṭāḥ kālacoditāḥ
a akṣauhiṇyo daśaikā ca pārthivānāṃ samāgatāḥ
c tāsāṃ pramukhato bhīṣmas tālaketur vyarocata
e yad atra yuktaṃ prāptaṃ ca tad vidhatsva viśāṃ pate
a uktaṃ bhīṣmeṇa yad vākyaṃ droṇena vidureṇa ca
c gāndhāryā dhṛtarāṣṭreṇa samakṣaṃ mama bhārata
e etat te kathitaṃ rājan yadvṛttaṃ kurusaṃsadi
a sāma ādau prayuktaṃ me rājan saubhrātram icchatā
c abhedāt kuruvaṃśasya prajānāṃ ca vivṛddhaye
a punar bhedaś ca me yukto yadā sāma na gṛhyate
c karmānukīrtanaṃ caiva devamānuṣasaṃhitam
a yadā nādriyate vākyaṃ sāmapūrvaṃ suyodhanaḥ
c tadā mayā samānīya bheditāḥ sarvapārthivāḥ
a adbhutāni ca ghorāṇi dāruṇāni ca bhārata
c amānuṣāṇi karmāṇi darśitāni ca me vibho
a bhartsayitvā tu rājñas tāṃs tṛṇīkṛtya suyodhanam
c rādheyaṃ bhīṣayitvā ca saubalaṃ ca punaḥ punaḥ
a nyūnatāṃ dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ nindāṃ caiva punaḥ punaḥ
c bhedayitvā nṛpān sarvān vāgbhir mantreṇa cāsakṛt
a punaḥ sāmābhisaṃyuktaṃ saṃpradānam athābruvam
c abhedāt kuruvaṃśasya kāryayogāt tathaiva ca
a te bālā dhṛtarāṣṭrasya bhīṣmasya vidurasya ca
c tiṣṭheyuḥ pāṇḍavāḥ sarve hitvā mānam adhaścarāḥ
a prayacchantu ca te rājyam anīśās te bhavantu ca
c yathāha rājā gāṅgeyo viduraś ca tathāstu tat
a sarvaṃ bhavatu te rājyaṃ pañca grāmān visarjaya
c avaśyaṃ bharaṇīyā hi pitus te rājasattama
a evam uktas tu duṣṭātmā naiva bhāvaṃ vyamuñcata
c daṇḍaṃ caturthaṃ paśyāmi teṣu pāpeṣu nānyathā
a niryātāś ca vināśāya kurukṣetraṃ narādhipāḥ
c etat te kathitaṃ sarvaṃ yadvṛttaṃ kurusaṃsadi
a na te rājyaṃ prayacchanti vinā yuddhena pāṇḍava
c vināśahetavaḥ sarve pratyupasthitamṛtyavaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a janārdanavacaḥ śrutvā dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c bhrātṝn uvāca dharmātmā samakṣaṃ keśavasya ha
a śrutaṃ bhavadbhir yadvṛttaṃ sabhāyāṃ kurusaṃsadi
c keśavasyāpi yad vākyaṃ tat sarvam avadhāritam
a tasmāt senāvibhāgaṃ me kurudhvaṃ narasattamāḥ
c akṣauhiṇyas tu saptaitāḥ sametā vijayāya vai
a tāsāṃ me patayaḥ sapta vikhyātās tān nibodhata
c drupadaś ca virāṭaś ca dhṛṣṭadyumnaśikhaṇḍinau
a sātyakiś cekitānaś ca bhīmasenaś ca vīryavān
c ete senāpraṇetāro vīrāḥ sarve tanutyajaḥ
a sarve vedavidaḥ śūrāḥ sarve sucaritavratāḥ
c hrīmanto nītimantaś ca sarve yuddhaviśāradāḥ
e iṣvastrakuśalāś caiva tathā sarvāstrayodhinaḥ
a saptānām api yo netā senānāṃ pravibhāgavit
c yaḥ saheta raṇe bhīṣmaṃ śarārciḥpāvakopamam
a tvaṃ tāvat sahadevātra prabrūhi kurunandana
c svamataṃ puruṣavyāghra ko naḥ senāpatiḥ kṣamaḥ
 sahadeva uvāca
a saṃyukta ekaduḥkhaś ca vīryavāṃś ca mahīpatiḥ
c yaṃ samāśritya dharmajñaṃ svam aṃśam anuyuñjmahe
a matsyo virāṭo balavān kṛtāstro yuddhadurmadaḥ
c prasahiṣyati saṃgrāme bhīṣmaṃ tāṃś ca mahārathān
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tathokte sahadevena vākye vākyaviśāradaḥ
c nakulo 'nantaraṃ tasmād idaṃ vacanam ādade
a vayasā śāstrato dhairyāt kulenābhijanena ca
c hrīmān kulānvitaḥ śrīmān sarvaśāstraviśāradaḥ
a veda cāstraṃ bharadvājād durdharṣaḥ satyasaṃgaraḥ
c yo nityaṃ spardhate droṇaṃ bhīṣmaṃ caiva mahābalam
a ślāghyaḥ pārthivasaṃghasya pramukhe vāhinīpatiḥ
c putrapautraiḥ parivṛtaḥ śataśākha iva drumaḥ
a yas tatāpa tapo ghoraṃ sadāraḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ
c roṣād droṇavināśāya vīraḥ samitiśobhanaḥ
a pitevāsmān samādhatte yaḥ sadā pārthivarṣabhaḥ
c śvaśuro drupado 'smākaṃ senām agre prakarṣatu
a sa droṇabhīṣmāv āyāntau sahed iti matir mama
c sa hi divyāstravid rājā sakhā cāṅgiraso nṛpaḥ
a mādrīsutābhyām ukte tu svamate kurunandanaḥ
c vāsavir vāsavasamaḥ savyasācy abravīd vacaḥ
a yo 'yaṃ tapaḥprabhāvena ṛṣisaṃtoṣaṇena ca
c divyaḥ puruṣa utpanno jvālāvarṇo mahābalaḥ
a dhanuṣmān kavacī khaḍgī ratham āruhya daṃśitaḥ
c divyair hayavarair yuktam agnikuṇḍāt samutthitaḥ
a garjann iva mahāmegho rathaghoṣeṇa vīryavān
c siṃhasaṃhanano vīraḥ siṃhavikrāntavikramaḥ
a siṃhorasko mahābāhuḥ siṃhavakṣā mahābalaḥ
c siṃhapragarjano vīraḥ siṃhaskandho mahādyutiḥ
a subhrūḥ sudaṃṣṭraḥ suhanuḥ subāhuḥ sumukho 'kṛśaḥ
c sujatruḥ suviśālākṣaḥ supādaḥ supratiṣṭhitaḥ
a abhedyaḥ sarvaśastrāṇāṃ prabhinna iva vāraṇaḥ
c jajñe droṇavināśāya satyavādī jitendriyaḥ
a dhṛṣṭadyumnam ahaṃ manye sahed bhīṣmasya sāyakān
c vajrāśanisamasparśān dīptāsyān uragān iva
a yamadūtasamān vege nipāte pāvakopamān
c rāmeṇājau viṣahitān vajraniṣpeṣadāruṇān
a puruṣaṃ taṃ na paśyāmi yaḥ saheta mahāvratam
c dhṛṣṭadyumnam ṛte rājann iti me dhīyate matiḥ
a kṣiprahastaś citrayodhī mataḥ senāpatir mama
c abhedyakavacaḥ śrīmān mātaṅga iva yūthapaḥ
d arjunenaivam ukte tu bhīmo vākyaṃ samādade
 bhīma uvāca
a vadhārthaṃ yaḥ samutpannaḥ śikhaṇḍī drupadātmajaḥ
c vadanti siddhā rājendra ṛṣayaś ca samāgatāḥ
a yasya saṃgrāmamadhyeṣu divyam astraṃ vikurvataḥ
c rūpaṃ drakṣyanti puruṣā rāmasyeva mahātmanaḥ
a na taṃ yuddheṣu paśyāmi yo vibhindyāc chikhaṇḍinam
c śastreṇa samare rājan saṃnaddhaṃ syandane sthitam
a dvairathe viṣahen nānyo bhīṣmaṃ rājan mahāvratam
c śikhaṇḍinam ṛte vīraṃ sa me senāpatir mataḥ
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a sarvasya jagatas tāta sārāsāraṃ balābalam
c sarvaṃ jānāti dharmātmā gatam eṣyac ca keśavaḥ
a yam āha kṛṣṇo dāśārhaḥ so 'stu no vāhinīpatiḥ
c kṛtāstro hy akṛtāstro vā vṛddho vā yadi vā yuvā
a eṣa no vijaye mūlam eṣa tāta viparyaye
c atra prāṇāś ca rājyaṃ ca bhāvābhāvau sukhāsukhe
a eṣa dhātā vidhātā ca siddhir atra pratiṣṭhitā
c yam āha kṛṣṇo dāśārhaḥ sa naḥ senāpatiḥ kṣamaḥ
e bravītu vadatāṃ śreṣṭho niśā samativartate
a tataḥ senāpatiṃ kṛtvā kṛṣṇasya vaśavartinam
c rātriśeṣe vyatikrānte prayāsyāmo raṇājiram
e adhivāsitaśastrāś ca kṛtakautukamaṅgalāḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā dharmarājasya dhīmataḥ
c abravīt puṇḍarīkākṣo dhanaṃjayam avekṣya ha
a mamāpy ete mahārāja bhavadbhir ya udāhṛtāḥ
c netāras tava senāyāḥ śūrā vikrāntayodhinaḥ
e sarva ete samarthā hi tava śatrūn pramarditum
a indrasyāpi bhayaṃ hy ete janayeyur mahāhave
c kiṃ punar dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ lubdhānāṃ pāpacetasām
a mayāpi hi mahābāho tvatpriyārtham ariṃdama
c kṛto yatno mahāṃs tatra śamaḥ syād iti bhārata
e dharmasya gatam ānṛṇyaṃ na sma vācyā vivakṣatām
a kṛtārthaṃ manyate bālaḥ so ''tmānam avicakṣaṇaḥ
c dhārtarāṣṭro balasthaṃ ca manyate ''tmānam āturaḥ
a yujyatāṃ vāhinī sādhu vadhasādhyā hi te matāḥ
c na dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ śakṣyanti sthātuṃ dṛṣṭvā dhanaṃjayam
a bhīmasenaṃ ca saṃkruddhaṃ yamau cāpi yamopamau
c yuyudhānadvitīyaṃ ca dhṛṣṭadyumnam amarṣaṇam
a abhimanyuṃ draupadeyān virāṭadrupadāv api
c akṣauhiṇīpatīṃś cānyān narendrān dṛḍhavikramān
a sāravad balam asmākaṃ duṣpradharṣaṃ durāsadam
c dhārtarāṣṭrabalaṃ saṃkhye vadhiṣyati na saṃśayaḥ
d dhṛṣṭadyumnam ahaṃ manye senāpatim ariṃdama
a evam ukte tu kṛṣṇena saṃprahṛṣyan narottamāḥ
c teṣāṃ prahṛṣṭamanasāṃ nādaḥ samabhavan mahān
a yoga ity atha sainyānāṃ tvaratāṃ saṃpradhāvatām
c hayavāraṇaśabdaś ca nemighoṣaś ca sarvaśaḥ
e śaṅkhadundubhinirghoṣas tumulaḥ sarvato 'bhavat
f tad ugraṃ sāgaranibhaṃ kṣubdhaṃ balasamāgamam
f rathapattigajodagraṃ mahormibhir ivākulam
f dhāvatām āhvayānānāṃ tanutrāṇi ca badhnatām
a prayāsyatāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ sasainyānāṃ samantataḥ
c gaṅgeva pūrṇā durdharṣā samadṛśyata vāhinī
a agrānīke bhīmaseno mādrīputrau ca daṃśitau
c saubhadro draupadeyāś ca dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥ
e prabhadrakāś ca pāñcālā bhīmasenamukhā yayuḥ
a tataḥ śabdaḥ samabhavat samudrasyeva parvaṇi
c hṛṣṭānāṃ saṃprayātānāṃ ghoṣo divam ivāspṛśat
a prahṛṣṭā daṃśitā yodhāḥ parānīkavidāraṇāḥ
c teṣāṃ madhye yayau rājā kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a śakaṭāpaṇaveśāś ca yānayugyaṃ ca sarvaśaḥ
c kośayantrāyudhaṃ caiva ye ca vaidyāś cikitsakāḥ
a phalgu yac ca balaṃ kiṃ cit tathaiva kṛśadurbalam
c tat saṃgṛhya yayau rājā ye cāpi paricārakāḥ
a upaplavye tu pāñcālī draupadī satyavādinī
c saha strībhir nivavṛte dāsīdāsasamāvṛtā
a kṛtvā mūlapratīkārān gulmaiḥ sthāvarajaṅgamaiḥ
c skandhāvāreṇa mahatā prayayuḥ pāṇḍunandanāḥ
a dadato gāṃ hiraṇyaṃ ca brāhmaṇair abhisaṃvṛtāḥ
c stūyamānā yayū rājan rathair maṇivibhūṣitaiḥ
a kekayā dhṛṣṭaketuś ca putraḥ kāśyasya cābhibhūḥ
c śreṇimān vasudānaś ca śikhaṇḍī cāparājitaḥ
a hṛṣṭās tuṣṭāḥ kavacinaḥ saśastrāḥ samalaṃkṛtāḥ
c rājānam anvayuḥ sarve parivārya yudhiṣṭhiram
a jaghanārdhe virāṭaś ca yajñasenaś ca somakiḥ
c sudharmā kuntibhojaś ca dhṛṣṭadyumnasya cātmajāḥ
a rathāyutāni catvāri hayāḥ pañcaguṇās tataḥ
c pattisainyaṃ daśaguṇaṃ sādinām ayutāni ṣaṭ
a anādhṛṣṭiś cekitānaś cedirājo 'tha sātyakiḥ
c parivārya yayuḥ sarve vāsudevadhanaṃjayau
a āsādya tu kurukṣetraṃ vyūḍhānīkāḥ prahāriṇaḥ
c pāṇḍavāḥ samadṛśyanta nardanto vṛṣabhā iva
a te 'vagāhya kurukṣetraṃ śaṅkhān dadhmur ariṃdamāḥ
c tathaiva dadhmatuḥ śaṅkhau vāsudevadhanaṃjayau
a pāñcajanyasya nirghoṣaṃ visphūrjitam ivāśaneḥ
c niśamya sarvasainyāni samahṛṣyanta sarvaśaḥ
a śaṅkhadundubhisaṃsṛṣṭaḥ siṃhanādas tarasvinām
c pṛthivīṃ cāntarikṣaṃ ca sāgarāṃś cānvanādayat
a tato deśe same snigdhe prabhūtayavasendhane
c niveśayām āsa tadā senāṃ rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a parihṛtya śmaśānāni devatāyatanāni ca
c āśramāṃś ca maharṣīṇāṃ tīrthāny āyatanāni ca
a madhurānūṣare deśe śive puṇye mahīpatiḥ
c niveśaṃ kārayām āsa kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a tataś ca punar utthāya sukhī viśrāntavāhanaḥ
c prayayau pṛthivīpālair vṛtaḥ śatasahasraśaḥ
a vidrāvya śataśo gulmān dhārtarāṣṭrasya sainikān
c paryakrāmat samantāc ca pārthena saha keśavaḥ
a śibiraṃ māpayām āsa dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥ
c sātyakiś ca rathodāro yuyudhānaḥ pratāpavān
a āsādya saritaṃ puṇyāṃ kurukṣetre hiraṇvatīm
c sūpatīrthāṃ śucijalāṃ śarkarāpaṅkavarjitām
a khānayām āsa parikhāṃ keśavas tatra bhārata
c guptyartham api cādiśya balaṃ tatra nyaveśayat
a vidhir yaḥ śibirasyāsīt pāṇḍavānāṃ mahātmanām
c tadvidhāni narendrāṇāṃ kārayām āsa keśavaḥ
a prabhūtajalakāṣṭhāni durādharṣatarāṇi ca
c bhakṣyabhojyopapannāni śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
a śibirāṇi mahārhāṇi rājñāṃ tatra pṛthak pṛthak
c vimānānīva rājendra niviṣṭāni mahītale
a tatrāsañ śilpinaḥ prājñāḥ śataśo dattavetanāḥ
c sarvopakaraṇair yuktā vaidyāś ca suviśāradāḥ
a jyādhanurvarmaśastrāṇāṃ tathaiva madhusarpiṣoḥ
c sasarja rasapāṃsūnāṃ rāśayaḥ parvatopamāḥ
a bahūdakaṃ suyavasaṃ tuṣāṅgārasamanvitam
c śibire śibire rājā saṃcakāra yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a mahāyantrāṇi nārācās tomararṣṭiparaśvadhāḥ
c dhanūṃṣi kavacādīni hṛdy abhūvan nṛṇāṃ tadā
a gajāḥ kaṅkaṭasaṃnāhā lohavarmottaracchadāḥ
c adṛśyaṃs tatra giryābhāḥ sahasraśatayodhinaḥ
a niviṣṭān pāṇḍavāṃs tatra jñātvā mitrāṇi bhārata
c abhisasrur yathoddeśaṃ sabalāḥ sahavāhanāḥ
a caritabrahmacaryās te somapā bhūridakṣiṇāḥ
c jayāya pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ samājagmur mahīkṣitaḥ
 janamejaya uvāca
a yudhiṣṭhiraṃ sahānīkam upayāntaṃ yuyutsayā
c saṃniviṣṭaṃ kurukṣetre vāsudevena pālitam
a virāṭadrupadābhyāṃ ca saputrābhyāṃ samanvitam
c kekayair vṛṣṇibhiś caiva pārthivaiḥ śataśo vṛtam
a mahendram iva cādityair abhiguptaṃ mahārathaiḥ
c śrutvā duryodhano rājā kiṃ kāryaṃ pratyapadyata
a etad icchāmy ahaṃ śrotuṃ vistareṇa tapodhana
c saṃbhrame tumule tasmin yadāsīt kurujāṅgale
a vyathayeyur hi devānāṃ senām api samāgame
c pāṇḍavā vāsudevaś ca virāṭadrupadau tathā
a dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pāñcālyaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca mahārathaḥ
c yuyudhānaś ca vikrānto devair api durāsadaḥ
a etad icchāmy ahaṃ śrotuṃ vistareṇa tapodhana
c kurūṇāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ ca yad yad āsīd viceṣṭitam
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a pratiyāte tu dāśārhe rājā duryodhanas tadā
c karṇaṃ duḥśāsanaṃ caiva śakuniṃ cābravīd idam
a akṛtenaiva kāryeṇa gataḥ pārthān adhokṣajaḥ
c sa enān manyunāviṣṭo dhruvaṃ vakṣyaty asaṃśayam
a iṣṭo hi vāsudevasya pāṇḍavair mama vigrahaḥ
c bhīmasenārjunau caiva dāśārhasya mate sthitau
a ajātaśatrur apy adya bhīmārjunavaśānugaḥ
c nikṛtaś ca mayā pūrvaṃ saha sarvaiḥ sahodaraiḥ
a virāṭadrupadau caiva kṛtavairau mayā saha
c tau ca senāpraṇetārau vāsudevavaśānugau
a bhavitā vigrahaḥ so 'yaṃ tumulo lomaharṣaṇaḥ
c tasmāt sāṃgrāmikaṃ sarvaṃ kārayadhvam atandritāḥ
a śibirāṇi kurukṣetre kriyantāṃ vasudhādhipāḥ
c suparyāptāvakāśāni durādeyāni śatrubhiḥ
a āsannajalakāṣṭhāni śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
c acchedyāhāramārgāṇi ratnoccayacitāni ca
e vividhāyudhapūrṇāni patākādhvajavanti ca
a samāś ca teṣāṃ panthānaḥ kriyantāṃ nagarād bahiḥ
c prayāṇaṃ ghuṣyatām adya śvobhūta iti māciram
a te tatheti pratijñāya śvobhūte cakrire tathā
c hṛṣṭarūpā mahātmāno vināśāya mahīkṣitām
a tatas te pārthivāḥ sarve tac chrutvā rājaśāsanam
c āsanebhyo mahārhebhya udatiṣṭhann amarṣitāḥ
a bāhūn parighasaṃkāśān saṃspṛśantaḥ śanaiḥ śanaiḥ
c kāñcanāṅgadadīptāṃś ca candanāgarubhūṣitān
a uṣṇīṣāṇi niyacchantaḥ puṇḍarīkanibhaiḥ karaiḥ
c antarīyottarīyāṇi bhūṣaṇāni ca sarvaśaḥ
a te rathān rathinaḥ śreṣṭhā hayāṃś ca hayakovidāḥ
c sajjayanti sma nāgāṃś ca nāgaśikṣāsu niṣṭhitāḥ
a atha varmāṇi citrāṇi kāñcanāni bahūni ca
c vividhāni ca śastrāṇi cakruḥ sajjāni sarvaśaḥ
a padātayaś ca puruṣāḥ śastrāṇi vividhāni ca
c upajahruḥ śarīreṣu hemacitrāṇy anekaśaḥ
a tad utsava ivodagraṃ saṃprahṛṣṭanarāvṛtam
c nagaraṃ dhārtarāṣṭrasya bhāratāsīt samākulam
a janaughasalilāvarto rathanāgāśvamīnavān
c śaṅkhadundubhinirghoṣaḥ kośasaṃcayaratnavān
a citrābharaṇavarmormiḥ śastranirmalaphenavān
c prāsādamālādrivṛto rathyāpaṇamahāhradaḥ
a yodhacandrodayodbhūtaḥ kururājamahārṇavaḥ
c adṛśyata tadā rājaṃś candrodaya ivārṇavaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a vāsudevasya tad vākyam anusmṛtya yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c punaḥ papraccha vārṣṇeyaṃ kathaṃ mando 'bravīd idam
a asminn abhyāgate kāle kiṃ ca naḥ kṣamam acyuta
c kathaṃ ca vartamānā vai svadharmān na cyavemahi
a duryodhanasya karṇasya śakuneḥ saubalasya ca
c vāsudeva matajño 'si mama sabhrātṛkasya ca
a vidurasyāpi te vākyaṃ śrutaṃ bhīṣmasya cobhayoḥ
c kuntyāś ca vipulaprajña prajñā kārtsnyena te śrutā
a sarvam etad atikramya vicārya ca punaḥ punaḥ
c yan naḥ kṣamaṃ mahābāho tad bravīhy avicārayan
a śrutvaitad dharmarājasya dharmārthasahitaṃ vacaḥ
c meghadundubhinirghoṣaḥ kṛṣṇo vacanam abravīt
a uktavān asmi yad vākyaṃ dharmārthasahitaṃ hitam
c na tu tan nikṛtiprajñe kauravye pratitiṣṭhati
a na ca bhīṣmasya durmedhāḥ śṛṇoti vidurasya vā
c mama vā bhāṣitaṃ kiṃ cit sarvam evātivartate
a na sa kāmayate dharmaṃ na sa kāmayate yaśaḥ
c jitaṃ sa manyate sarvaṃ durātmā karṇam āśritaḥ
a bandham ājñāpayām āsa mama cāpi suyodhanaḥ
c na ca taṃ labdhavān kāmaṃ durātmā śāsanātigaḥ
a na ca bhīṣmo na ca droṇo yuktaṃ tatrāhatur vacaḥ
c sarve tam anuvartante ṛte viduram acyuta
a śakuniḥ saubalaś caiva karṇaduḥśāsanāv api
c tvayy ayuktāny abhāṣanta mūḍhā mūḍham amarṣaṇam
a kiṃ ca tena mayoktena yāny abhāṣanta kauravāḥ
c saṃkṣepeṇa durātmāsau na yuktaṃ tvayi vartate
a na pārthiveṣu sarveṣu ya ime tava sainikāḥ
c yat pāpaṃ yan na kalyāṇaṃ sarvaṃ tasmin pratiṣṭhitam
a na cāpi vayam atyarthaṃ parityāgena karhi cit
c kauravaiḥ śamam icchāmas tatra yuddham anantaram
a tac chrutvā pārthivāḥ sarve vāsudevasya bhāṣitam
c abruvanto mukhaṃ rājñaḥ samudaikṣanta bhārata
a yudhiṣṭhiras tv abhiprāyam upalabhya mahīkṣitām
c yogam ājñāpayām āsa bhīmārjunayamaiḥ saha
a tataḥ kilakilābhūtam anīkaṃ pāṇḍavasya ha
c ājñāpite tadā yoge samahṛṣyanta sainikāḥ
a avadhyānāṃ vadhaṃ paśyan dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c niṣṭanan bhīmasenaṃ ca vijayaṃ cedam abravīt
a yadarthaṃ vanavāsaś ca prāptaṃ duḥkhaṃ ca yan mayā
c so 'yam asmān upaity eva paro 'narthaḥ prayatnataḥ
a yasmin yatnaḥ kṛto 'smābhiḥ sa no hīnaḥ prayatnataḥ
c akṛte tu prayatne 'smān upāvṛttaḥ kalir mahān
a kathaṃ hy avadhyaiḥ saṃgrāmaḥ kāryaḥ saha bhaviṣyati
c kathaṃ hatvā gurūn vṛddhān vijayo no bhaviṣyati
a tac chrutvā dharmarājasya savyasācī paraṃtapaḥ
c yad uktaṃ vāsudevena śrāvayām āsa tad vacaḥ
a uktavān devakīputraḥ kuntyāś ca vidurasya ca
c vacanaṃ tat tvayā rājan nikhilenāvadhāritam
a na ca tau vakṣyato 'dharmam iti me naiṣṭhikī matiḥ
c na cāpi yuktaṃ kaunteya nivartitum ayudhyataḥ
a tac chrutvā vāsudevo 'pi savyasācivacas tadā
c smayamāno 'bravīt pārtham evam etad iti bruvan
a tatas te dhṛtasaṃkalpā yuddhāya sahasainikāḥ
c pāṇḍaveyā mahārāja tāṃ rātriṃ sukham āvasan
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a vyuṣitāyāṃ rajanyāṃ tu rājā duryodhanas tataḥ
c vyabhajat tāny anīkāni daśa caikaṃ ca bhārata
a narahastirathāśvānāṃ sāraṃ madhyaṃ ca phalgu ca
c sarveṣv eteṣv anīkeṣu saṃdideśa mahīpatiḥ
a sānukarṣāḥ satūṇīrāḥ savarūthāḥ satomarāḥ
c sopāsaṅgāḥ saśaktīkāḥ saniṣaṅgāḥ sapothikāḥ
a sadhvajāḥ sapatākāś ca saśarāsanatomarāḥ
c rajjubhiś ca vicitrābhiḥ sapāśāḥ saparistarāḥ
a sakacagrahavikṣepāḥ satailaguḍavālukāḥ
c sāśīviṣaghaṭāḥ sarve sasarjarasapāṃsavaḥ
a saghaṇṭāphalakāḥ sarve vāsīvṛkṣādanānvitāḥ
a   sāyoguḍajalopalāḥ
a saśālabhindipālāś ca samadhūc chiṣṭamudgarāḥ
a sakāṇḍadaṇḍakāḥ sarve sasīraviṣatomarāḥ
a saśūrpapiṭakāḥ sarve sadātrāṅkuśatomarāḥ
a sakīlakrakacāḥ sarve
c vyāghracarmaparīvārā vṛtāś ca dvīpicarmabhiḥ
a savastayaḥ saśṛṅgāś ca saprāsavividhāyudhāḥ
c sakuṭhārāḥ sakuddālāḥ satailakṣaumasarpiṣaḥ
d rukmajālapraticchannā nānāmaṇivibhūṣitāḥ
d vyāghracarmaparīdhānāḥ suveṣāḥ samalaṃkṛtāḥ
a citrānīkāḥ suvapuṣo jvalitā iva pāvakāḥ
c tathā kavacinaḥ śūrāḥ śastreṣu kṛtaniśramāḥ
a kulīnā hayayonijñāḥ sārathye viniveśitāḥ
c baddhāriṣṭā baddhakakṣyā baddhadhvajapatākinaḥ
d baddhābharaṇanirvyūhā baddhacarmāsipaṭṭiśāḥ
a caturyujo rathāḥ sarve sarve śastrasamāyutāḥ
c saṃhṛṣṭavāhanāḥ sarve sarve śataśarāsanāḥ
a dhuryayor hayayor ekas tathānyau pārṣṇisārathī
c tau cāpi rathināṃ śreṣṭhau rathī ca hayavit tathā
a nagarāṇīva guptāni durādeyāni śatrubhiḥ
c āsan rathasahasrāṇi hemamālīni sarvaśaḥ
a yathā rathās tathā nāgā baddhakakṣyāḥ svalaṃkṛtāḥ
c babhūvuḥ sapta puruṣā ratnavanta ivādrayaḥ
a dvāv aṅkuśadharau teṣu dvāv uttamadhanurdharau
c dvau varāsidharau rājann ekaḥ śaktipatākadhṛk
a gajair mattaiḥ samākīrṇaṃ savarmāyudhakośakaiḥ
c tad babhūva balaṃ rājan kauravyasya sahasraśaḥ
a vicitrakavacāmuktaiḥ sapatākaiḥ svalaṃkṛtaiḥ
c sādibhiś copasaṃpannā āsann ayutaśo hayāḥ
a susaṃgrāhāḥ susaṃtoṣā hemabhāṇḍaparicchadāḥ
c anekaśatasāhasrās te ca sādivaśe sthitāḥ
a nānārūpavikārāś ca nānākavacaśastriṇaḥ
c padātino narās tatra babhūvur hemamālinaḥ
a rathasyāsan daśa gajā gajasya daśa vājinaḥ
c narā daśa hayasyāsan pādarakṣāḥ samantataḥ
a rathasya nāgāḥ pañcāśan nāgasyāsañ śataṃ hayāḥ
c hayasya puruṣāḥ sapta bhinnasaṃdhānakāriṇaḥ
a senā pañcaśataṃ nāgā rathās tāvanta eva ca
b pañcāśac ca śataṃ cāśvā narāḥ pañcaguṇās tataḥ
c daśasenā ca pṛtanā pṛtanā daśavāhinī
a vāhinī pṛtanā senā dhvajinī sādinī camūḥ
c akṣauhiṇīti paryāyair niruktātha varūthinī
e evaṃ vyūḍhāny anīkāni kauraveyeṇa dhīmatā
a akṣauhiṇyo daśaikā ca saṃkhyātāḥ sapta caiva ha
c akṣauhiṇyas tu saptaiva pāṇḍavānām abhūd balam
e akṣauhiṇyo daśaikā ca kauravāṇām abhūd balam
a narāṇāṃ pañcapañcāśad eṣā pattir vidhīyate
c senāmukhaṃ ca tisras tā gulma ity abhisaṃjñitaḥ
a daśa gulmā gaṇas tv āsīd gaṇās tv ayutaśo 'bhavan
c duryodhanasya senāsu yotsyamānāḥ prahāriṇaḥ
a tatra duryodhano rājā śūrān buddhimato narān
c prasamīkṣya mahābāhuś cakre senāpatīṃs tadā
a pṛthag akṣauhiṇīnāṃ ca praṇetṝn narasattamān
c vidhipūrvaṃ samānīya pārthivān abhyaṣecayat
a kṛpaṃ droṇaṃ ca śalyaṃ ca saindhavaṃ ca mahāratham
c sudakṣiṇaṃ ca kāmbojaṃ kṛtavarmāṇam eva ca
a droṇaputraṃ ca karṇaṃ ca bhūriśravasam eva ca
c śakuniṃ saubalaṃ caiva bāhlīkaṃ ca mahāratham
a divase divase teṣāṃ prativelaṃ ca bhārata
c cakre sa vividhāḥ saṃjñāḥ pratyakṣaṃ ca punaḥ punaḥ
a tathā viniyatāḥ sarve ye ca teṣāṃ padānugāḥ
b hṛṣṭāḥ puṣṭāḥ susaṃnaddhā vikrame dṛḍhaniścayāḥ
c babhūvuḥ sainikā rājan rājñaḥ priyacikīrṣavaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tataḥ śāṃtanavaṃ bhīṣmaṃ prāñjalir dhṛtarāṣṭrajaḥ
c saha sarvair mahīpālair idaṃ vacanam abravīt
a ṛte senāpraṇetāraṃ pṛtanā sumahaty api
c dīryate yuddham āsādya pipīlikapuṭaṃ yathā
a na hi jātu dvayor buddhiḥ samā bhavati karhi cit
c śauryaṃ ca nāma netṝṇāṃ spardhate ca parasparam
a śrūyate ca mahāprājña haihayān amitaujasaḥ
c abhyayur brāhmaṇāḥ sarve samucchritakuśadhvajāḥ
a tān anvayus tadā vaiśyāḥ śūdrāś caiva pitāmaha
c ekatas tu trayo varṇā ekataḥ kṣatriyarṣabhāḥ
a te sma yuddheṣv abhajyanta trayo varṇāḥ punaḥ punaḥ
b tathāpi niyatāḥ sarve kṣatriyās tu jaghanyajāḥ
c kṣatriyās tu jayanty eva bahulaṃ caikato balam
a tatas te kṣatriyān eva papracchur dvijasattamāḥ
c tebhyaḥ śaśaṃsur dharmajñā yāthātathyaṃ pitāmaha
a vayam ekasya śṛṇumo mahābuddhimato raṇe
c bhavantas tu pṛthak sarve svabuddhivaśavartinaḥ
a tatas te brāhmaṇāś cakrur ekaṃ senāpatiṃ dvijam
c nayeṣu kuśalaṃ śūram ajayan kṣatriyāṃs tataḥ
a evaṃ ye kuśalaṃ śūraṃ hite sthitam akalmaṣam
c senāpatiṃ prakurvanti te jayanti raṇe ripūn
a bhavān uśanasā tulyo hitaiṣī ca sadā mama
c asaṃhāryaḥ sthito dharme sa naḥ senāpatir bhava
a raśmīvatām ivādityo vīrudhām iva candramāḥ
c kubera iva yakṣāṇāṃ marutām iva vāsavaḥ
a parvatānāṃ yathā meruḥ suparṇaḥ patatām iva
c kumāra iva bhūtānāṃ vasūnām iva havyavāṭ
a bhavatā hi vayaṃ guptāḥ śakreṇeva divaukasaḥ
c anādhṛṣyā bhaviṣyāmas tridaśānām api dhruvam
a prayātu no bhavān agre devānām iva pāvakiḥ
c vayaṃ tvām anuyāsyāmaḥ saurabheyā ivarṣabham
d ity uktvā pādayos tasya nipapāta narādhipaḥ
d rakṣāsmān rājaśārdūla tvām ahaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ
 bhīṣma uvāca
a evam etan mahābāho yathā vadasi bhārata
c yathaiva hi bhavanto me tathaiva mama pāṇḍavāḥ
a api caiva maya śreyo vācyaṃ teṣāṃ narādhipa
c yoddhavyaṃ tu tavārthāya yathā sa samayaḥ kṛtaḥ
a na tu paśyāmi yoddhāram ātmanaḥ sadṛśaṃ bhuvi
c ṛte tasmān naravyāghrāt kuntīputrād dhanaṃjayāt
a sa hi veda mahābāhur divyāny astrāṇi sarvaśaḥ
c na tu māṃ vivṛto yuddhe jātu yudhyeta pāṇḍavaḥ
a ahaṃ sa ca kṣaṇenaiva nirmanuṣyam idaṃ jagat
c kuryāṃ śastrabalenaiva sasurāsurarākṣasam
a na tv evotsādanīyā me pāṇḍoḥ putrā narādhipa
c tasmād yodhān haniṣyāmi prayogeṇāyutaṃ sadā
a evam eṣāṃ kariṣyāmi nidhanaṃ kurunandana
c na cet te māṃ haniṣyanti pūrvam eva samāgame
a senāpatis tv ahaṃ rājan samayenāpareṇa te
c bhaviṣyāmi yathākāmaṃ tan me śrotum ihārhasi
a karṇo vā yudhyatāṃ pūrvam ahaṃ vā pṛthivīpate
c spardhate hi sadātyarthaṃ sūtaputro mayā raṇe
 karṇa uvāca
a nāhaṃ jīvati gāṅgeye yotsye rājan kathaṃ cana
c hate bhīṣme tu yotsyāmi saha gāṇḍīvadhanvanā
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tataḥ senāpatiṃ cakre vidhivad bhūridakṣiṇam
c dhṛtarāṣṭrātmajo bhīṣmaṃ so 'bhiṣikto vyarocata
a tato bherīś ca śaṅkhāṃś ca śataśaś caiva puṣkarān
c vādayām āsur avyagrāḥ puruṣā rājaśāsanāt
a siṃhanādāś ca vividhā vāhanānāṃ ca nisvanāḥ
c prādurāsann anabhre ca varṣaṃ rudhirakardamam
a nirghātāḥ pṛthivīkampā gajabṛṃhitanisvanāḥ
c āsaṃś ca sarvayodhānāṃ pātayanto manāṃsy uta
a vācaś cāpy aśarīriṇyo divaś colkāḥ prapedire
c śivāś ca bhayavedinyo nedur dīptasvarā bhṛśam
a senāpatye yadā rājā gāṅgeyam abhiṣiktavān
c tadaitāny ugrarūpāṇi abhavañ śataśo nṛpa
a tataḥ senāpatiṃ kṛtvā bhīṣmaṃ parabalārdanam
c vācayitvā dvijaśreṣṭhān niṣkair gobhiś ca bhūriśaḥ
a vardhamāno jayāśīrbhir niryayau sainikair vṛtaḥ
c āpageyaṃ puraskṛtya bhrātṛbhiḥ sahitas tadā
e skandhāvāreṇa mahatā kurukṣetraṃ jagāma ha
a parikramya kurukṣetraṃ karṇena saha kauravaḥ
c śibiraṃ māpayām āsa same deśe narādhipaḥ
a madhurānūṣare deśe prabhūtayavasendhane
c yathaiva hāstinapuraṃ tadvac chibiram ābabhau
 janamejaya uvāca
a āpageyaṃ mahātmānaṃ bhīṣmaṃ śastrabhṛtāṃ varam
c pitāmahaṃ bhāratānāṃ dhvajaṃ sarvamahīkṣitām
a bṛhaspatisamaṃ buddhyā kṣamayā pṛthivīsamam
c samudram iva gāmbhīrye himavantam iva sthiram
a prajāpatim ivaudārye tejasā bhāskaropamam
c mahendram iva śatrūṇāṃ dhvaṃsanaṃ śaravṛṣṭibhiḥ
a raṇayajñe pratibhaye svābhīle lomaharṣaṇe
c dīkṣitaṃ cirarātrāya śrutvā rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a kim abravīn mahābāhuḥ sarvadharmaviśāradaḥ
c bhīmasenārjunau vāpi kṛṣṇo vā pratyapadyata
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a āpaddharmārthakuśalo mahābuddhir yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c sarvān bhrātṝn samānīya vāsudevaṃ ca sātvatam
e uvāca vadatāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ sāntvapūrvam idaṃ vacaḥ
a paryākrāmata sainyāni yattās tiṣṭhata daṃśitāḥ
c pitāmahena vo yuddhaṃ pūrvam eva bhaviṣyati
e tasmāt saptasu senāsu praṇetṝn mama paśyata
 vāsudeva uvāca
a yathārhati bhavān vaktum asmin kāla upasthite
c tathedam arthavad vākyam uktaṃ te bharatarṣabha
a rocate me mahābāho kriyatāṃ yad anantaram
c nāyakās tava senāyām abhiṣicyantu sapta vai
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tato drupadam ānāyya virāṭaṃ śinipuṃgavam
c dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ ca pāñcālyaṃ dhṛṣṭaketuṃ ca pārthivam
e śikhaṇḍinaṃ ca pāñcālyaṃ sahadevaṃ ca māgadham
a etān sapta maheṣvāsān vīrān yuddhābhinandinaḥ
c senāpraṇetṝn vidhivad abhyaṣiñcad yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a sarvasenāpatiṃ cātra dhṛṣṭadyumnam upādiśat
c droṇāntahetor utpanno ya iddhāñ jātavedasaḥ
a sarveṣām eva teṣāṃ tu samastānāṃ mahātmanām
c senāpatipatiṃ cakre guḍākeśaṃ dhanaṃjayam
a arjunasyāpi netā ca saṃyantā caiva vājinām
c saṃkarṣaṇānujaḥ śrīmān mahābuddhir janārdanaḥ
a tad dṛṣṭvopasthitaṃ yuddhaṃ samāsannaṃ mahātyayam
c prāviśad bhavanaṃ rājñaḥ pāṇḍavasya halāyudhaḥ
a sahākrūraprabhṛtibhir gadasāmbolmukādibhiḥ
c raukmiṇeyāhukasutaiś cārudeṣṇapurogamaiḥ
a vṛṣṇimukhyair abhigatair vyāghrair iva balotkaṭaiḥ
c abhigupto mahābāhur marudbhir iva vāsavaḥ
a nīlakauśeyavasanaḥ kailāsaśikharopamaḥ
c siṃhakhelagatiḥ śrīmān madaraktāntalocanaḥ
a taṃ dṛṣṭvā dharmarājaś ca keśavaś ca mahādyutiḥ
c udatiṣṭhat tadā pārtho bhīmakarmā vṛkodaraḥ
a gāṇḍīvadhanvā ye cānye rājānas tatra ke cana
c pūjayāṃ cakrur abhyetya te sma sarve halāyudham
a tatas taṃ pāṇḍavo rājā kare pasparśa pāṇinā
c vāsudevapurogās tu sarva evābhyavādayan
a virāṭadrupadau vṛddhāv abhivādya halāyudhaḥ
c yudhiṣṭhireṇa sahita upāviśad ariṃdamaḥ
a tatas teṣūpaviṣṭeṣu pārthiveṣu samantataḥ
c vāsudevam abhiprekṣya rauhiṇeyo 'bhyabhāṣata
a bhavitāyaṃ mahāraudro dāruṇaḥ puruṣakṣayaḥ
c diṣṭam etad dhruvaṃ manye na śakyam ativartitum
a asmād yuddhāt samuttīrṇān api vaḥ sasuhṛjjanān
c arogān akṣatair dehaiḥ paśyeyam iti me matiḥ
a sametaṃ pārthivaṃ kṣatraṃ kālapakvam asaṃśayam
c vimardaḥ sumahān bhāvī māṃsaśoṇitakardamaḥ
a ukto mayā vāsudevaḥ punaḥ punar upahvare
c saṃbandhiṣu samāṃ vṛttiṃ vartasva madhusūdana
a pāṇḍavā hi yathāsmākaṃ tathā duryodhano nṛpaḥ
c tasyāpi kriyatāṃ yuktyā saparyeti punaḥ punaḥ
a tac ca me nākarod vākyaṃ tvadarthe madhusūdanaḥ
c niviṣṭaḥ sarvabhāvena dhanaṃjayam avekṣya ca
a dhruvo jayaḥ pāṇḍavānām iti me niścitā matiḥ
c tathā hy abhiniveśo 'yaṃ vāsudevasya bhārata
a na cāham utsahe kṛṣṇam ṛte lokam udīkṣitum
c tato 'ham anuvartāmi keśavasya cikīrṣitam
a ubhau śiṣyau hi me vīrau gadāyuddhaviśāradau
c tulyasneho 'smy ato bhīme tathā duryodhane nṛpe
a tasmād yāsyāmi tīrthāni sarasvatyā niṣevitum
c na hi śakṣyāmi kauravyān naśyamānān upekṣitum
a evam uktvā mahābāhur anujñātaś ca pāṇḍavaiḥ
c tīrthayātrāṃ yayau rāmo nivartya madhusūdanam
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a etasminn eva kāle tu bhīṣmakasya mahātmanaḥ
c hiraṇyalomno nṛpateḥ sākṣād indrasakhasya vai
a āhṛtīnām adhipater bhojasyātiyaśasvinaḥ
c dākṣiṇātyapateḥ putro dikṣu rukmīti viśrutaḥ
a yaḥ kiṃpuruṣasiṃhasya gandhamādanavāsinaḥ
c śiṣyaḥ kṛtsnaṃ dhanurvedaṃ catuṣpādam avāptavān
a yo māhendraṃ dhanur lebhe tulyaṃ gāṇḍīvatejasā
c śārṅgeṇa ca mahābāhuḥ saṃmitaṃ divyam akṣayam
a trīṇy evaitāni divyāni dhanūṃṣi divicāriṇām
c vāruṇaṃ gāṇḍivaṃ tatra māhendraṃ vijayaṃ dhanuḥ
a śārṅgaṃ tu vaiṣṇavaṃ prāhur divyaṃ tejomayaṃ dhanuḥ
c dhārayām āsa yat kṛṣṇaḥ parasenābhayāvaham
a gāṇḍīvaṃ pāvakāl lebhe khāṇḍave pākaśāsaniḥ
c drumād rukmī mahātejā vijayaṃ pratyapadyata
a saṃchidya mauravān pāśān nihatya muram ojasā
c nirjitya narakaṃ bhaumam āhṛtya maṇikuṇḍale
a ṣoḍaśa strīsahasrāṇi ratnāni vividhāni ca
c pratipede hṛṣīkeśaḥ śārṅgaṃ ca dhanur uttamam
a rukmī tu vijayaṃ labdhvā dhanur meghasamasvanam
c vibhīṣayann iva jagat pāṇḍavān abhyavartata
a nāmṛṣyata purā yo 'sau svabāhubaladarpitaḥ
c rukmiṇyā haraṇaṃ vīro vāsudevena dhīmatā
a kṛtvā pratijñāṃ nāhatvā nivartiṣyāmi keśavam
c tato 'nvadhāvad vārṣṇeyaṃ sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varam
a senayā caturaṅgiṇyā mahatyā dūrapātayā
c vicitrāyudhavarmiṇyā gaṅgayeva pravṛddhayā
a sa samāsādya vārṣṇeyaṃ yogānām īśvaraṃ prabhum
b kṛtapratijño rājāsau vāsudevena nirjitaḥ
c vyaṃsito vrīḍito rājann ājagāma sa kuṇḍinam
a yatraiva kṛṣṇena raṇe nirjitaḥ paravīrahā
c tatra bhojakaṭaṃ nāma cakre nagaram uttamam
a sainyena mahatā tena prabhūtagajavājinā
c puraṃ tad bhuvi vikhyātaṃ nāmnā bhojakaṭaṃ nṛpa
a sa bhojarājaḥ sainyena mahatā parivāritaḥ
c akṣauhiṇyā mahāvīryaḥ pāṇḍavān samupāgamat
a tataḥ sa kavacī khaḍgī śarī dhanvī talī rathī
c dhvajenādityavarṇena praviveśa mahācamūm
a viditaḥ pāṇḍaveyānāṃ vāsudevapriyepsayā
c yudhiṣṭhiras tu taṃ rājā pratyudgamyābhyapūjayat
a sa pūjitaḥ pāṇḍusutair yathānyāyaṃ susatkṛtaḥ
c pratipūjya ca tān sarvān viśrāntaḥ sahasainikaḥ
e uvāca madhye vīrāṇāṃ kuntīputraṃ dhanaṃjayam
a sahāyo 'smi sthito yuddhe yadi bhīto 'si pāṇḍava
c kariṣyāmi raṇe sāhyam asahyaṃ tava śatrubhiḥ
a na hi me vikrame tulyaḥ pumān astīha kaś cana
b haniṣyāmi raṇe bhāgaṃ yan me dāsyasi pāṇḍava
b api droṇakṛpau vīrau bhīṣmakarṇāv atho punaḥ
b atha vā sarva evaite tiṣṭhantu vasudhādhipāḥ
c nihatya samare śatrūṃs tava dāsyāmi phalguna
a ity ukto dharmarājasya keśavasya ca saṃnidhau
c śṛṇvatāṃ pārthivendrāṇām anyeṣāṃ caiva sarvaśaḥ
a vāsudevam abhiprekṣya dharmarājaṃ ca pāṇḍavam
c uvāca dhīmān kaunteyaḥ prahasya sakhipūrvakam
a yudhyamānasya me vīra gandharvaiḥ sumahābalaiḥ
c sahāyo ghoṣayātrāyāṃ kas tadāsīt sakhā mama
a tathā pratibhaye tasmin devadānavasaṃkule
c khāṇḍave yudhyamānasya kaḥ sahāyas tadābhavat
a nivātakavacair yuddhe kālakeyaiś ca dānavaiḥ
c tatra me yudhyamānasya kaḥ sahāyas tadābhavat
a tathā virāṭanagare kurubhiḥ saha saṃgare
c yudhyato bahubhis tāta kaḥ sahāyo 'bhavan mama
a upajīvya raṇe rudraṃ śakraṃ vaiśravaṇaṃ yamam
c varuṇaṃ pāvakaṃ caiva kṛpaṃ droṇaṃ ca mādhavam
a dhārayan gāṇḍivaṃ divyaṃ dhanus tejomayaṃ dṛḍham
c akṣayyaśarasaṃyukto divyāstraparibṛṃhitaḥ
a kauravāṇāṃ kule jātaḥ pāṇḍoḥ putro viśeṣataḥ
c droṇaṃ vyapadiśañ śiṣyo vāsudevasahāyavān
d bhīto 'smīti kathaṃ brūyāṃ dadhāno gāṇḍivaṃ dhanuḥ
a katham asmadvidho brūyād bhīto 'smīty ayaśaskaram
c vacanaṃ naraśārdūla vajrāyudham api svayam
a nāsmi bhīto mahābāho sahāyārthaś ca nāsti me
c yathākāmaṃ yathāyogaṃ gaccha vānyatra tiṣṭha vā
d tac chrutvā vacanaṃ tasya vijayasya ca dhīmataḥ
a vinivartya tato rukmī senāṃ sāgarasaṃnibhām
c duryodhanam upāgacchat tathaiva bharatarṣabha
a tathaiva cābhigamyainam uvāca sa narādhipaḥ
c pratyākhyātaś ca tenāpi sa tadā śūramāninā
a dvāv eva tu mahārāja tasmād yuddhād vyapeyatuḥ
c rauhiṇeyaś ca vārṣṇeyo rukmī ca vasudhādhipaḥ
a gate rāme tīrthayātrāṃ bhīṣmakasya sute tathā
c upāviśan pāṇḍaveyā mantrāya punar eva hi
a samitir dharmarājasya sā pārthivasamākulā
c śuśubhe tārakācitrā dyauś candreṇeva bhārata
 janamejaya uvāca
a tathā vyūḍheṣv anīkeṣu kurukṣetre dvijarṣabha
c kim akurvanta kuravaḥ kālenābhipracoditāḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tathā vyūḍheṣv anīkeṣu yat teṣu bharatarṣabha
c dhṛtarāṣṭro mahārāja saṃjayaṃ vākyam abravīt
a ehi saṃjaya me sarvam ācakṣvānavaśeṣataḥ
c senāniveśe yadvṛttaṃ kurupāṇḍavasenayoḥ
a diṣṭam eva paraṃ manye pauruṣaṃ cāpy anarthakam
c yad ahaṃ jānamāno 'pi yuddhadoṣān kṣayodayān
a tathāpi nikṛtiprajñaṃ putraṃ durdyūtadevinam
c na śaknomi niyantuṃ vā kartuṃ vā hitam ātmanaḥ
a bhavaty eva hi me sūta buddhir doṣānudarśinī
c duryodhanaṃ samāsādya punaḥ sā parivartate
a evaṃ gate vai yad bhāvi tad bhaviṣyati saṃjaya
c kṣatradharmaḥ kila raṇe tanutyāgo 'bhipūjitaḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tvadyukto 'yam anupraśno mahārāja yathārhasi
c na tu duryodhane doṣam imam āsaktum arhasi
e śṛṇuṣvānavaśeṣeṇa vadato mama pārthiva
a ya ātmano duścaritād aśubhaṃ prāpnuyān naraḥ
c enasā na sa daivaṃ vā kālaṃ vā gantum arhati
a mahārāja manuṣyeṣu nindyaṃ yaḥ sarvam ācaret
c sa vadhyaḥ sarvalokasya ninditāni samācaran
a nikārā manujaśreṣṭha pāṇḍavais tvatpratīkṣayā
c anubhūtāḥ sahāmātyair nikṛtair adhidevane
a hayānāṃ ca gajānāṃ ca rājñāṃ cāmitatejasām
c vaiśasaṃ samare vṛttaṃ yat tan me śṛṇu sarvaśaḥ
a sthiro bhūtvā mahārāja sarvalokakṣayodayam
c yathābhūtaṃ mahāyuddhe śrutvā mā vimanā bhava
a na hy eva kartā puruṣaḥ karmaṇoḥ śubhapāpayoḥ
c asvatantro hi puruṣaḥ kāryate dāruyantravat
a ke cid īśvaranirdiṣṭāḥ ke cid eva yadṛcchayā
c pūrvakarmabhir apy anye traidham etad vikṛṣyate
d tasmād anartham āpannaḥ sthiro bhūtvā niśāmaya
 saṃjaya uvāca
a hiraṇvatyāṃ niviṣṭeṣu pāṇḍaveṣu mahātmasu
b nyaviśanta mahārāja kauraveyā yathāvidhi
b tatra duryodhano rājā niveśya balam ojasā
b saṃmānayitvā nṛpatīn nyasya gulmāṃs tathaiva ca
b ārakṣasya vidhiṃ kṛtvā yodhānāṃ tatra bhārata
b karṇaṃ duḥśāsanaṃ caiva śakuniṃ cāpi saubalam
b ānāyya nṛpatis tatra mantrayām āsa bhārata
c duryodhano mahārāja karṇena saha bhārata
d saṃbhāṣitvā ca karṇena bhrātrā duḥśāsanena ca
a saubalena ca rājendra tathā duḥśāsanena ca
c āhūyopahvare rājann ulūkam idam abravīt
a ulūka gaccha kaitavya pāṇḍavān sahasomakān
c gatvā mama vaco brūhi vāsudevasya śṛṇvataḥ
a idaṃ tat samanuprāptaṃ varṣapūgābhicintitam
c pāṇḍavānāṃ kurūṇāṃ ca yuddhaṃ lokabhayaṃkaram
a yad etat katthanāvākyaṃ saṃjayo mahad abravīt
b vāsudevasahāyasya garjataḥ sānujasya te
c madhye kurūṇāṃ kaunteya tasya kālo 'yam āgataḥ
e yathā vaḥ saṃpratijñātaṃ tat sarvaṃ kriyatām iti
f jyeṣṭhaṃ tathaiva kaunteyaṃ brūyās tvaṃ vacanān mama
f bhrātṛbhiḥ sahitaḥ sarvaiḥ somakaiś ca sakekayaiḥ
f kathaṃ vā dhārmiko bhūtvā tvam adharme manaḥ kṛthāḥ
f ya icchasi jagat sarvaṃ naśyamānaṃ nṛśaṃsavat
f abhayaṃ sarvabhūtebhyo dātā tvam iti me matiḥ
f śrūyate hi purā gītaḥ śloko 'yaṃ bharatarṣabha
f prahlādenātha bhadraṃ te hṛte rājye tu daivataiḥ
f yasya dharmadhvajo nityaṃ surādhvaja ivocchritaḥ
f pracchannāni ca pāpāni baiḍālaṃ nāma tad vratam
f atra te vartayiṣyāmi ākhyānam idam uttamam
f kathitaṃ nāradeneha pitur mama narādhipa
f mārjāraḥ kila duṣṭātmā niśceṣṭaḥ sarvakarmasu
f ūrdhvabāhuḥ sthito rājan gaṅgātīre kadā cana
f sa vai kṛtvā manaḥśuddhiṃ pratyayārthaṃ śarīriṇām
f karomi dharmam ity āha sarvān eva śarīriṇaḥ
f tasya kālena mahatā viśrambhaṃ jagmur aṇḍajāḥ
f sametya ca praśaṃsanti mārjāraṃ taṃ viśāṃ pate
f pūjyamānas tu taiḥ sarvaiḥ pakṣibhiḥ pakṣibhojanaḥ
f ātmakāryaṃ kṛtaṃ mene caryāyāś ca kṛtaṃ phalam
f atha dīrghasya kālasya taṃ deśaṃ mūṣikā yayuḥ
f dadṛśus taṃ ca te tatra dhārmikaṃ vratacāriṇam
f kāryeṇa mahatā yuktaṃ dambhayuktena bhārata
f teṣāṃ matir iyaṃ rājann āsīt tatra viniścaye
f bahumitrā vayaṃ sarve teṣāṃ no mātulo hy ayam
f rakṣāṃ karotu satataṃ vṛddhabālasya sarvaśaḥ
f upagamya tu te sarve biḍālam idam abruvan
f bhavatprasādād icchāmaś cartuṃ caiva yathāsukham
f bhavān no gatir avyagrā bhavān naḥ paramaḥ suhṛt
f te vayaṃ sahitāḥ sarve bhavantaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ
f bhavān dharmaparo nityaṃ bhavān dharme vyavasthitaḥ
f sa no rakṣa mahāprajña tridaśān iva vajrabhṛt
f evam uktas tu taiḥ sarvair mūṣikaiḥ sa viśāṃ pate
f pratyuvāca tataḥ sarvān mūṣikān mūṣikāntakṛt
f dvayor yogaṃ na paśyāmi tapaso rakṣaṇasya ca
f avaśyaṃ tu mayā kāryaṃ vacanaṃ bhavatāṃ hitam
f yuṣmābhir api kartavyaṃ vacanaṃ mama nityaśaḥ
f tapasāsmi pariśrānto dṛḍhaṃ niyamam āsthitaḥ
f na cāpi gamane śaktiṃ kāṃ cit paśyāmi cintayan
f so 'smi neyaḥ sadā tātā nadīkūlam itaḥ sukham
f tatheti taṃ pratijñāya mūṣikā bharatarṣabha
f vṛddhabālam atho sarve mārjārāya nyavedayan
f tataḥ sa pāpo duṣṭātmā mūṣikān atha bhakṣayan
f pīvaraś ca suvarṇaś ca dṛḍhabandhaś ca jāyate
f mūṣikāṇāṃ gaṇaś cātra bhṛśaṃ saṃkṣīyate 'tha saḥ
f mārjāro vardhate cāpi tejobalasamanvitaḥ
f tatas te mūṣikāḥ sarve sametyānyonyam abruvan
f mātulo vardhate nityaṃ vayaṃ kṣīyāmahe bhṛśam
f tataḥ prājñatamaḥ kaś ciḍ ḍiṇḍiko nāma mūṣikaḥ
f abravīd vacanaṃ rājan mūṣikāṇāṃ mahāgaṇam
f gacchatāṃ vo nadītīraṃ sahitānāṃ viśeṣataḥ
f pṛṣṭhato 'haṃ gamiṣyāmi sahaiva mātulena tu
f sādhu sādhv iti te sarve pūjayāṃ cakrire tadā
f cakruś caiva yathānyāyaṃ ḍiṇḍikasya vaco 'rthavat
f avijñānāt tataḥ so 'tha ḍiṇḍikaṃ hy upabhuktavān
f tatas te sahitāḥ sarve mantrayām āsur añjasā
f tatra vṛddhatamaḥ kaś cit koliko nāma mūṣikaḥ
f abravīd vacanaṃ rājañ jñātimadhye yathātatham
f na mātulo dharmakāmaś chadmamātraṃ kṛtā śikhā
f na mūlaphalabhakṣasya viṣṭhā bhavati lomaśā
f asya gātrāṇi vardhante gaṇaś ca parihīyate
f adya saptāṣṭadivasān ḍiṇḍiko 'pi na dṛśyate
f etac chrutvā vacaḥ sarve mūṣikā vipradudruvuḥ
f biḍālo 'pi sa duṣṭātmā jagāmaiva yathāgatam
f tathā tvam api duṣṭātman baiḍālaṃ vratam āsthitaḥ
f carasi jñātiṣu sadā biḍālo mūṣikeṣv iva
f anyathā kila te vākyam anyathā karma dṛśyate
f dambhanārthāya lokasya vedāś copaśamaś ca te
f tyaktvā chadma tv idaṃ rājan kṣatradharmaṃ samāśritaḥ
f kuru kāryāṇi sarvāṇi dharmiṣṭho 'si nararṣabha
f bāhuvīryeṇa pṛthivīṃ labdhvā bharatasattama
f dehi dānaṃ dvijātibhyaḥ pitṛbhyaś ca yathocitam
f kliṣṭāyā varṣapūgāṃś ca mātur mātṛhite sthitaḥ
f pramārjāśru raṇe jitvā saṃmānaṃ param āvaha
f pañca grāmā vṛtā yatnān nāsmābhir apavarjitāḥ
f yudhyāmahe kathaṃ saṃkhye kopayema ca pāṇḍavān
f tvatkṛte duṣṭabhāvasya saṃtyāgo vidurasya ca
f jātuṣe ca gṛhe dāhaṃ smara taṃ puruṣo bhava
f yac ca kṛṣṇam avocas tvam āyāntaṃ kurusaṃsadi
f ayam asmi sthito rājañ śamāya samarāya ca
f tasyāyam āgataḥ kālaḥ samarasya narādhipa
f etad arthaṃ mayā sarvaṃ kṛtam etad yudhiṣṭhira
f kiṃ nu yuddhāt paraṃ lābhaṃ kṣatriyo bahu manyate
f kiṃ ca tvaṃ kṣatriyakule jātaḥ saṃprathito bhuvi
f droṇād astrāṇi saṃprāpya kṛpāc ca bharatarṣabha
f tulyayonau samabale vāsudevaṃ samāśritaḥ
f brūyās tvaṃ vāsudevaṃ ca pāṇḍavānāṃ samīpataḥ
f ātmārthaṃ pāṇḍavārthaṃ ca yatto māṃ pratiyodhaya
f sabhāmadhye ca yad rūpaṃ māyayā kṛtavān asi
f tat tathaiva punaḥ kṛtvā sārjuno mām abhidrava
f indrajālaṃ ca māyāṃ vai kuhakā vāpi bhīṣaṇā
f āttaśastrasya saṃgrāme vahanti pratigarjanāḥ
f vayam apy utsahema dyāṃ khaṃ ca gacchema māyayā
f rasātalaṃ viśā 'mopi aindraṃ vā puram eva tu
f darśayema ca rūpāṇi svaśarīre bahūny api
f na tu paryāyataḥ siddhir buddhim āpnoti mānuṣīm
f manasaiva hi bhūtāni dhātaiva kurute vaśe
f yad bravīṣi ca vārṣṇeya dhārtarāṣṭrān ahaṃ raṇe
f ghātayitvā pradāsyāmi pārthebhyo rājyam uttamam
f ācacakṣe ca me sarvaṃ saṃjayas tava bhāṣitam
f maddvitīyena pārthena vairaṃ vaḥ savyasācinā
f sa satyasaṃgaro bhūtvā pāṇḍavārthe parākramī
f yudhyasvādya raṇe yattaḥ paśyāmaḥ puruṣo bhava
f yas tu śatrum abhijñāya śuddhaṃ pauruṣam āsthitaḥ
f karoti dviṣatāṃ śokaṃ sa jīvati sujīvitam
f akasmāc caiva te kṛṣṇa khyātaṃ loke mahad yaśaḥ
f adyedānīṃ vijānīmaḥ santi ṣaṇḍhāḥ saśṛṅgakāḥ
f madvidho nāpi nṛpatis tvayi yuktaḥ kathaṃ cana
f sannāhaṃ saṃyuge kartuṃ kaṃsabhṛtye viśeṣataḥ
a amarṣaṃ rājyaharaṇaṃ vanavāsaṃ ca pāṇḍava
c draupadyāś ca parikleśaṃ saṃsmaran puruṣo bhava
a yadarthaṃ kṣatriyā sūte garbhaṃ tad idam āgatam
c balaṃ vīryaṃ ca śauryaṃ ca paraṃ cāpy astralāghavam
e pauruṣaṃ darśayan yuddhe kopasya kuru niṣkṛtim
a parikliṣṭasya dīnasya dīrghakāloṣitasya ca
c na sphuṭed dhṛdayaṃ kasya aiśvaryād bhraṃśitasya ca
a kule jātasya śūrasya paravitteṣu gṛdhyataḥ
c ācchinnaṃ rājyam ākramya kopaṃ kasya na dīpayet
a yat tad uktaṃ mahad vākyaṃ karmaṇā tad vibhāvyatām
c akarmaṇā katthitena santaḥ kupuruṣaṃ viduḥ
a amitrāṇāṃ vaśe sthānaṃ rājyasya ca punarbhavaḥ
c dvāv arthau yudhyamānasya tasmāt kuruta pauruṣam
a asmān vā tvaṃ parājitya praśādhi pṛthivīm imām
c atha vā nihato 'smābhir vīralokaṃ gamiṣyasi
a rāṣṭrāt pravrājanaṃ kleśaṃ vanavāsaṃ ca pāṇḍava
c kṛṣṇāyāś ca parikleśaṃ saṃsmaran puruṣo bhava
a apriyāṇāṃ ca vacane pravrajatsu punaḥ punaḥ
c amarṣaṃ darśayādya tvam amarṣo hy eva pauruṣam
a krodho balaṃ tathā vīryaṃ jñānayogo 'stralāghavam
c iha te pārtha dṛśyantāṃ saṃgrāme puruṣo bhava
a taṃ ca tūbarakaṃ mūḍhaṃ bahvāśinam avidyakam
c ulūka madvaco brūyā asakṛd bhīmasenakam
d virāṭanagare pārtha yas tvaṃ sūdo hy abhūḥ purā
d ballavo nāma vikhyātas tan mamaiva hi pauruṣam
a aśaktenaiva yac chaptaṃ sabhāmadhye vṛkodara
c duḥśāsanasya rudhiraṃ pīyatāṃ yadi śakyate
d yad bravīṣi ca kaunteya dhārtarāṣṭrān ahaṃ raṇe
d nihaniṣyāmi tarasā tasya kālo 'yam āgataḥ
d tvaṃ hi bhojye puraskāryo bhakṣye peye ca bhārata
d kva yuddhaṃ kva ca bhoktavyaṃ yudhyasva puruṣo bhava
d śayiṣyase hato bhūmau gadām āliṅgya bhārata
d tad vṛthā ca sabhāmadhye valgitaṃ te vṛkodara
d ulūka nakulaṃ brūhi vacanān mama bhārata
d yudhyasvādya sthiro bhūtva paśyāmas tava pauruṣam
d yudhiṣṭhirānurāgaṃ ca dveṣaṃ ca mayi bhārata
d kṛṣṇāyāś ca parikleśaṃ smaredānīṃ yathātatham
d brūyās tvaṃ sahadevaṃ ca rājamadhye vaco mama
d yudhyedānīṃ raṇe yattaḥ kleśān smara ca pāṇḍava
d virāṭadrupadau cobhau brūyās tvaṃ vacanān mama
d na dṛṣṭapūrvā bhartāro bhṛtyair api mahāguṇaiḥ
d tathārthapatibhir bhṛtyā yataḥ sṛṣṭāḥ prajās tataḥ
d aślāghyo 'yaṃ narapatir yuvayor iti cāgatam
d te yūyaṃ saṃhatā bhūtvā tadvadhārthaṃ mamāpi ca
d ātmārthaṃ pāṇḍavārthaṃ ca prayudhyadhvaṃ mayā saha
d dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ ca pāñcālyaṃ brūyās tvaṃ vacanān mama
d eṣa te samayaḥ prāpto labdhavyaś ca tvayāpi saḥ
d droṇam āsādya samare jñāsyase hitam uttamam
d yudhyasva sasuhṛt pāpaṃ kuru karma suduṣkaram
d śikhaṇḍinam atho brūhi ulūka vacanān mama
d strīti matvā mahābāhur na haniṣyati kauravaḥ
d gāṅgeyo dhanvināṃ śreṣṭho yudhyedānīṃ sunirbhayam
d kuru karma raṇe yattaḥ paśyāmaḥ pauruṣaṃ tava
d evam uktvā tato rājā prahasyolūkam abravīt
d dhanaṃjayaṃ punar brūhi vāsudevasya śṛṇvataḥ
a lohābhihāro nirvṛttaḥ kurukṣetram akardamam
c puṣṭās te 'śvā bhṛtā yodhāḥ śvo yudhyasva sakeśavaḥ
d asamāgamya bhīṣmeṇa saṃyuge kiṃ vikatthase
d ārurukṣur yathā mandaḥ parvataṃ gandhamādanam
d evaṃ katthasi kaunteya akatthan puruṣo bhava
d sūtaputraṃ sudurdharṣaṃ śalyaṃ ca balināṃ varam
d droṇaṃ ca balināṃ śreṣṭhaṃ śacīpatisamaṃ yudhi
d ajitvā saṃyuge pārtha rājyaṃ katham ihecchasi
d brāhme dhanuṣi cācāryaṃ vedayor antagaṃ dvayoḥ
d yudhi dhuryam avikṣobhyam anīkacaram acyutam
d droṇaṃ mahādyutiṃ pārtha jetum icchasi tan mṛṣā
d na hi śuśruma vātena merum unmathitaṃ girim
d anilo vā vahen meruṃ dyaur vāpi nipaten mahīm
d yugaṃ vā parivarteta yady evaṃ syād yathāttha mām
d ko hy asti jīvitākāṅkṣī prāpyemam arimardanam
d pārtho vā itaro vāpi ko 'nyaḥ svasti gṛhān vrajet
d katham ābhyām abhidhyātaḥ saṃspṛṣṭo dāruṇena vā
d raṇe jīvan pramucyeta padā bhūmim upaspṛśan
d kiṃ darduraḥ kūpaśayo yathemāṃ
d na budhyase rājacamūṃ sametām
d durādharṣāṃ devacamūprakāśāṃ
d guptāṃ narendrais tridaśair iva dyām
d prācyaiḥ pratīcyair atha dākṣiṇātyair
d udīcyakāmbojaśakaiḥ khaśaiś ca
d śālvaiḥ samatsyaiḥ kurumadhyadeśyair
d mlecchaiḥ pulindair draviḍāndhrakāñcyaiḥ
d nānājanaughaṃ yudhi saṃpravṛddhaṃ
d gāṅgaṃ yathā vegam apāraṇīyam
d māṃ ca sthitaṃ nāgabalasya madhye
d yuyutsase manda kim alpabuddhe
d akṣayyāv iṣudhī caiva agnidattaṃ ca te ratham
d jānīmo hi raṇe pārtha ketuṃ divyaṃ ca bhārata
d akatthamāno yudhyasva katthase 'rjuna kiṃ bahu
d paryāyāt siddhir etasya naitat sidhyati katthanāt
d yadīdaṃ katthanāl loke sidhyet karma dhanaṃjaya
d sarve bhaveyuḥ siddhārthāḥ katthane ko hi durgataḥ
d jānāmi te vāsudevaṃ sahāyaṃ
d jānāmi te gāṇḍivaṃ tālamātram
d jānāmy ahaṃ tvādṛśo nāsti yoddhā
d jānānas te rājyam etad dharāmi
d na tu paryāyadharmeṇa siddhiṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ
d manasaivānukūlāni dhātaiva kurute vaśe
d trayodaśa samā bhuktaṃ rājyaṃ vilapatas tava
d bhūyaś caiva praśāsiṣye tvāṃ nihatya sabāndhavam
d kva tadā gāṇḍivaṃ te 'bhūd yat tvaṃ dāsapaṇair jitaḥ
d kva tadā bhīmasenasya balam āsīc ca phalguna
d sagadād bhīmasenād vā phālgunād vā sagāṇḍivāt
d na vai mokṣas tadā yo 'bhūd vinā kṛṣṇām aninditām
d sā vo dāsye samāpannān mocayām āsa pārṣatī
d amānuṣyaṃ samāpannān dāsakarmaṇy avasthitān
d avocaṃ yat ṣaṇḍhatilān ahaṃ vas tathyam eva tat
d dhṛtā hi veṇī pārthena virāṭanagare tadā
d sūdakarmaṇi viśrāntaṃ virāṭasya mahānase
d bhīmasenena kaunteya yat tu tan mama pauruṣam
d evam eva sadā daṇḍaṃ kṣatriyāḥ kṣatriye dadhuḥ
d veṇīṃ kṛtvā ṣaṇḍhaveṣaḥ kanyāṃ nartitavān asi
d na bhayād vāsudevasya na cāpi tava phālguna
d rājyaṃ pratipradāsyāmi yudhyasva sahakeśavaḥ
d na māyā hīndrajālaṃ vā kuhakā vāpi bhīṣaṇāḥ
d vyāttaśastrasya saṃgrāme vahanti pratigarjanāḥ
d vāsudevasahasraṃ vā phālgunānāṃ śatāni vā
d āsādya mām amogheṣuṃ draviṣyanti diśo daśa
d saṃyugaṃ gaccha bhīṣmeṇa bhindhi vā śirasā girim
d tarasva vā mahāgādhaṃ bāhubhyāṃ puruṣodadhim
d śāradvatamahāmīnaṃ saumadattitimiṃgilam
d bhīṣmavegam aparyantaṃ droṇagrāhadurāsadam
d karṇaśalyajhaṣāvartaṃ kāmbojavaḍavāmukham
d duḥśāsanaughaṃ śalaśalyamatsyaṃ
d suṣeṇacitrāyudhanāganakram
d jayadrathādriṃ purumitragādhaṃ
d durmarṣaṇodaṃ śakuniprapātam
d śastraugham akṣayyam abhipravṛddhaṃ
d yadāvagāhya śramanaṣṭacetāḥ
d bhaviṣyasi tvaṃ hatasarvabāndhavas
d tadā manas te paritāpam eṣyati
d tadā manas te tridivādivāśucer
d nivartitā pārtha mahīpraśāsanāt
d praśāmya rājyaṃ hi sudurlabhaṃ tvayā
d bubhūṣitaḥ svarga ivātapasvinā
 saṃjaya uvāca
a senāniveśaṃ saṃprāpya kaitavyaḥ pāṇḍavasya ha
c samāgataḥ pāṇḍaveyair yudhiṣṭhiram abhāṣata
a abhijño dūtavākyānāṃ yathoktaṃ bruvato mama
c duryodhanasamādeśaṃ śrutvā na kroddhum arhasi
 yudhiṣṭhira uvāca
a ulūka na bhayaṃ te 'sti brūhi tvaṃ vigatajvaraḥ
c yan mataṃ dhārtarāṣṭrasya lubdhasyādīrghadarśinaḥ
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tato dyutimatāṃ madhye pāṇḍavānāṃ mahātmanām
c sṛñjayānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ kṛṣṇasya ca yaśasvinaḥ
a drupadasya saputrasya virāṭasya ca saṃnidhau
c bhūmipānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ madhye vākyaṃ jagāda ha
a idaṃ tvām abravīd rājā dhārtarāṣṭro mahāmanāḥ
c śṛṇvatāṃ kuruvīrāṇāṃ tan nibodha narādhipa
a parājito 'si dyūtena kṛṣṇā cānāyitā sabhām
c śakyo 'marṣo manuṣyeṇa kartuṃ puruṣamāninā
a dvādaśaiva tu varṣāṇi vane dhiṣṇyād vivāsitāḥ
c saṃvatsaraṃ virāṭasya dāsyam āsthāya coṣitāḥ
a amarṣaṃ rājyaharaṇaṃ vanavāsaṃ ca pāṇḍava
c draupadyāś ca parikleśaṃ saṃsmaran puruṣo bhava
a aśaktena ca yac chaptaṃ bhīmasenena pāṇḍava
c duḥśāsanasya rudhiraṃ pīyatāṃ yadi śakyate
a lohābhihāro nirvṛttaḥ kurukṣetram akardamam
c samaḥ panthā bhṛtā yodhāḥ śvo yudhyasva sakeśavaḥ
a asamāgamya bhīṣmeṇa saṃyuge kiṃ vikatthase
c ārurukṣur yathā mandaḥ parvataṃ gandhamādanam
d evaṃ katthasi kaunteya akatthan kuru pauruṣam
d sūtaputraṃ sudurdharṣaṃ śalyaṃ ca balināṃ varam
a droṇaṃ ca yudhyatāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ śacīpatisamaṃ yudhi
c ajitvā saṃyuge pārtha rājyaṃ katham ihecchasi
a brāhme dhanuṣi cācāryaṃ vedayor antaraṃ dvayoḥ
c yudhi dhuryam avikṣobhyam anīkadharam acyutam
a droṇaṃ mohād yudhā pārtha yaj jigīṣasi tan mṛṣā
c na hi śuśruma vātena merum unmathitaṃ girim
a anilo vā vahen meruṃ dyaur vāpi nipaten mahīm
c yugaṃ vā parivarteta yady evaṃ syād yathāttha mām
a ko hy ābhyāṃ jīvitākāṅkṣī prāpyāstram arimardanam
c gajo vājī naro vāpi punaḥ svasti gṛhān vrajet
a katham ābhyām abhidhyātaḥ saṃsṛṣṭo dāruṇena vā
c raṇe jīvan vimucyeta padā bhūmim upaspṛśan
a kiṃ darduraḥ kūpaśayo yathemāṃ
na budhyase rājacamūṃ sametām
c durādharṣāṃ devacamūprakāśāṃ
guptāṃ narendrais tridaśair iva dyām
a prācyaiḥ pratīcyair atha dākṣiṇātyair

c śālvaiḥ samatsyaiḥ kurumadhyadeśair
mlecchaiḥ pulindair draviḍāndhrakāñcyaiḥ
a nānājanaughaṃ yudhi saṃpravṛddhaṃ
gāṅgaṃ yathā vegam avāraṇīyam
c māṃ ca sthitaṃ nāgabalasya madhye
yuyutsase manda kim alpabuddhe
a ity evam uktvā rājānaṃ dharmaputraṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
c abhyāvṛtya punar jiṣṇum ulūkaḥ pratyabhāṣata
a akatthamāno yudhyasva katthase 'rjuna kiṃ bahu
c paryāyāt siddhir etasya naitat sidhyati katthanāt
a yadīdaṃ katthanāt sidhyet karma loke dhanaṃjaya
c sarve bhaveyuḥ siddhārthā bahu kattheta durgataḥ
a jānāmi te vāsudevaṃ sahāyaṃ
jānāmi te gāṇḍivaṃ tālamātram
c jānāmy etat tvādṛśo nāsti yoddhā
rājyaṃ ca te jānamāno harāmi
a na tu paryāyadharmeṇa siddhiṃ prāpnoti bhūyasīm
c manasaiva hi bhūtāni dhātā prakurute vaśe
a trayodaśa samā bhuktaṃ rājyaṃ vilapatas tava
c bhūyaś caiva praśāsiṣye nihatya tvāṃ sabāndhavam
a kva tadā gāṇḍivaṃ te 'bhūd yat tvaṃ dāsapaṇe jitaḥ
c kva tadā bhīmasenasya balam āsīc ca phalguna
a sagadād bhīmasenāc ca pārthāc caiva sagāṇḍivāt
c na vai mokṣas tadā vo 'bhūd vinā kṛṣṇām aninditām
a sā vo dāsyaṃ samāpannān mokṣayām āsa bhāminī
c amānuṣyasamāyuktān dāsyakarmaṇy avasthitān
a avocaṃ yat ṣaṇḍhatilān ahaṃ vas tathyam eva tat
c dhṛtā hi veṇī pārthena virāṭanagare tadā
a sūdakarmaṇi ca śrāntaṃ virāṭasya mahānase
c bhīmasenena kaunteya yac ca tan mama pauruṣam
a evam eva sadā daṇḍaṃ kṣatriyāḥ kṣatriye dadhuḥ
c śreṇyāṃ kakṣyāṃ ca veṇyāṃ ca saṃyuge yaḥ palāyate
a na bhayād vāsudevasya na cāpi tava phalguna
c rājyaṃ pratipradāsyāmi yudhyasva sahakeśavaḥ
a na māyā hīndrajālaṃ vā kuhakā vā vibhīṣaṇī
c āttaśastrasya me yuddhe vahanti pratigarjanāḥ
a vāsudevasahasraṃ vā phalgunānāṃ śatāni vā
c āsādya mām amogheṣuṃ draviṣyanti diśo daśa
a saṃyugaṃ gaccha bhīṣmeṇa bhindhi tvaṃ śirasā girim
c prataremaṃ mahāgādhaṃ bāhubhyāṃ puruṣodadhim
a śāradvatamahīmānaṃ viviṃśatijhaṣākulam
c bṛhadbalasamuccālaṃ saumadattitimiṃgilam
d yuyutsutoyaṃ bhagadattamārutaṃ
d śuśugusic
hārdikyamahāsamudram
a duḥśāsanaughaṃ śalaśalyamatsyaṃ
suṣeṇacitrāyudhanāganakram
b bhīṣmavegam aparyantaṃ droṇagrāhadurāsadam
b karṇaśalyajhaṣāvartaṃ kāmbojavaḍavāmukham
c jayadrathādriṃ purumitragādhaṃ
durmarṣaṇodaṃ śakuniprapātam
a śastraugham akṣayyam atipravṛddhaṃ
yadāvagāhya śramanaṣṭacetāḥ
c bhaviṣyasi tvaṃ hatasarvabāndhavas
tadā manas te paritāpam eṣyati
a tadā manas te tridivād ivāśucer
nivartatāṃ pārtha mahīpraśāsanāt
c rājyaṃ praśāstuṃ hi sudurlabhaṃ tvayā
bubhūṣatā svarga ivātapasvinā
 saṃjaya uvāca
a ulūkas tv arjunaṃ bhūyo yathoktaṃ vākyam abravīt
c āśīviṣam iva kruddhaṃ tudan vākyaśalākayā
a tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā ruṣitāḥ pāṇḍavā bhṛśam
c prāg eva bhṛśasaṃkruddhāḥ kaitavyena pradharṣitāḥ
a nāsaneṣv avatiṣṭhanta bāhūṃś caiva vicikṣipuḥ
c āśīviṣā iva kruddhā vīkṣāṃ cakruḥ parasparam
a avākśirā bhīmasenaḥ samudaikṣata keśavam
c netrābhyāṃ lohitāntābhyām āśīviṣa iva śvasan
a ārtaṃ vātātmajaṃ dṛṣṭvā krodhenābhihataṃ bhṛśam
c utsmayann iva dāśārhaḥ kaitavyaṃ pratyabhāṣata
a prayāhi śīghraṃ kaitavya brūyāś caiva suyodhanam
c śrutaṃ vākyaṃ gṛhīto 'rtho mataṃ yat te tathāstu tat
d evam uktvā mahābāhuḥ keśavo rājasattama
d punar eva mahāprājñaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram udaikṣata
d sṛñjayānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ kṛṣṇasya ca yaśasvinaḥ
d drupadasya saputrasya virāṭasya ca saṃnidhau
d bhūmipānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ madhye vākyaṃ jagāda ha
d ulūko 'py arjunaṃ bhūyo yathoktaṃ vākyam abravīt
d āśīviṣam iva kruddhaṃ tudan vākyaśalākayā
d kṛṣṇādīṃś caiva tān sarvān yathoktaṃ vākyam abravīt
d ulūkasya tu tad vākyaṃ pāpaṃ dāruṇam īritam
d śrutvā vicukṣubhe pārtho lalāṭaṃ cāpy amārjayat
d tad avasthaṃ tadā dṛṣṭvā pārthaṃ sā samitir nṛpa
d nāmṛṣyanta mahārāja pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathāḥ
d adhikṣepeṇa kṛṣṇasya pārthasya ca mahātmanaḥ
d śrutvā te puruṣavyāghrāḥ krodhāj jajvalur acyutāḥ
d dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca sātyakiś ca mahārathaḥ
d kekayā bhrātaraḥ pañca rākṣasaś ca ghaṭotkacaḥ
d draupadeyābhimanyuś ca dhṛṣṭaketuś ca pārthivaḥ
d bhīmasenaś ca vikrānto yamajau ca mahārathau
d utpetur āsanāt sarve krodhasaṃraktalocanāḥ
d bāhūn pragṛhya rucirān raktacandanarūṣitān
d aṅgadaiḥ pārihāryaiś ca keyūraiś ca vibhūṣitān
d dantān danteṣu niṣpiṣya sṛkkiṇī parilelihan
d teṣām ākārabhāvajñaḥ kuntīputro vṛkodaraḥ
d udatiṣṭhat sa vegena krodhena prajvalann iva
d udvṛtya sahasā netre dantān kaṭakaṭāyya ca
d hastaṃ hastena niṣpiṣya ulūkaṃ vākyam abravīt
d aśaktānām ivāsmākaṃ protsāhananimittakam
d śrutaṃ te vacanaṃ mūrkha yat tvāṃ duryodhano 'bravīt
d tan me kathayato manda śruṇu vākyaṃ durāsadam
d sarvakṣatrasya madhye tvaṃ yad vakṣyasi suyodhanam
d śṛṇvataḥ sūtaputrasya pituś ca tvaṃ durātmanaḥ
d asmābhiḥ prītikāmais tu bhrātur jyeṣṭhasya nityaśaḥ
d marṣitaṃ te durācāra tat tvaṃ na bahu manyase
d preṣitaś ca hṛṣīkeśaḥ śamākāṅkṣī kurūn prati
d kulasya hitakāmena dharmarājena dhīmatā
d tvaṃ kālacodito nūnaṃ gantukāmo yamakṣayam
d gacchasvāhavam asmābhis tac ca śvo bhavitā dhruvam
d mayāpi ca pratijñāto vadhaḥ sabhrātṛkasya te
d sa tathā bhavitā pāpa nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
d velām atikramet sadyaḥ sāgaro varuṇālayaḥ
d parvatāś ca viśīryeyur mayoktaṃ na mṛṣā bhavet
d sahāyas te yadi yamaḥ kubero rudra eva vā
d yathāpratijñaṃ durbuddhe prakariṣyanti pāṇḍavāḥ
d duḥśāsanasya rudhiraṃ pātā cāsmi yathepsitam
d yaś ceha pratisaṃrabdhaḥ kṣatriyo mābhiyāsyati
d api bhīṣmaṃ puraskṛtya taṃ neṣyāmi yamakṣayam
d yac caitad uktaṃ vacanaṃ mayā kṣatrasya saṃsadi
d yathaitad bhavitā satyaṃ tathaivātmānam ālabhe
d bhīmasenavacaḥ śrutvā sahadevo 'py amarṣaṇaḥ
d krodhasaṃraktanayanas tato vākyam uvāca ha
d śauṭīraśūrasadṛśam anīkajanasaṃsadi
d śṛṇu pāpa vaco mahyaṃ yad vācyo hi pitā tvayā
d nāsmākaṃ bhavitā bhedaḥ kadā cit kurubhiḥ saha
d dhṛtarāṣṭrasya saṃbandho yadi na syāt tvayā saha
d tvaṃ tu lokavināśāya dhṛtarāṣṭrakulasya ca
d utpanno vairapuruṣaḥ svakulaghnaś ca pāpakṛt
d janmaprabhṛti cāsmākaṃ pitā te pāpapūruṣaḥ
d ahitāni nṛśaṃsāni nityaśaḥ kartum icchati
d tasya vairānuṣaṅgasya gantāsmy antaṃ sudurgamam
d aham ādau nihatya tvāṃ śakuneḥ saṃprapaśyataḥ
d tato 'smi śakuniṃ hantā miṣatāṃ sarvadhanvinām
d bhīmasya vacanaṃ śrutvā sahadevasya cobhayoḥ
d uvāca phālguno vākyaṃ bhīmasenaṃ smayann iva
d bhīmasena na te santi yeṣāṃ vairaṃ tvayā saha
d mandā gṛheṣu sukhino mṛtyupāśavaśaṃ gatāḥ
d ulūkaś ca na te vācyaḥ paruṣaṃ puruṣottama
d dūtāḥ kim aparādhyante yathoktasyānubhāṣiṇaḥ
d evam uktvā mahābāhuṃ bhīmaṃ bhīmaparākramam
d dhṛṣṭadyumnamukhān vīrān suhṛdaḥ samabhāṣata
d śrutaṃ vas tasya pāpasya dhārtarāṣṭrasya bhāṣitam
d kutsanā vāsudevasya mama caiva viśeṣataḥ
d śrutvā bhavantaḥ saṃrabdhā asmākaṃ hitakāmyayā
d prabhāvād vāsudevasya bhavatāṃ ca prayatnataḥ
d samagraṃ pārthivaṃ kṣatraṃ sarvaṃ na gaṇayāmy aham
d bhavadbhiḥ samanujñāto vākyam asya yad uttaram
d ulūke prāpayiṣyāmi yad vakṣyāmi suyodhanam
d śvobhūte katthitasyāsya prativākyaṃ camūmukhe
d gāṇḍīvenābhidhāsyāmi klībā hi vacanottarāḥ
d tatas te pārthivāḥ sarve praśaśaṃsur dhanaṃjayam
d tena vākyopacāreṇa vismitā rājasattamāḥ
d anunīya ca tān sarvān yathāmānyaṃ yathāvayaḥ
d dharmarājas tadā vākyaṃ tat prāpyaṃ pratyabhāṣata
d ātmānam avamanvāno na hi syāt pārthivottamaḥ
d tatrottaraṃ pravakṣyāmi tava śuśrūṣaṇe rataḥ
d ulūkaṃ bharataśreṣṭha sāmapūrvam athorjitam
d duryodhanasya tad vākyaṃ niśamya bharatarṣabha
d atilohitanetrābhyām āśīviṣa iva śvasan
d smayamāna iva krodhāt sṛkkiṇī parisaṃlihan
d janārdanam abhiprekṣya bhrātṝṃś caivedam abravīt
d abhyabhāṣata kaitavyaṃ pragṛhya vipulaṃ bhujam
d ulūka gaccha kaitavya brūhi tāta suyodhanam
d kṛtaghnaṃ vairapuruṣaṃ durmatiṃ kulapāṃsanam
d pāṇḍaveṣu sadā pāpa nityaṃ jihmaṃ pravartase
d svavīryād yaḥ parākramya pāpa āhvayate parān
d abhītaḥ pūrayan vākyam eṣa vai kṣatriyaḥ pumān
d sa pāpa kṣatriyo bhūtvā asmān āhūya saṃyuge
d mānyāmānyān puraskṛtya yuddhaṃ mā gāḥ kulādhama
d ātmavīryaṃ samāśritya bhṛtyavīryaṃ ca kaurava
d āhvayasva raṇe pārthān sarvathā kṣatriyo bhava
d paravīryaṃ samāśritya yaḥ samāhvayate parān
d aśaktaḥ svayam ādātum etad eva napuṃsakam
d yas tvaṃ pareṣāṃ vīryeṇa ātmānaṃ bahu manyase
d katham evam aśaktas tvam asmān samabhigarjasi
a madvacaś cāpi bhūyas te vaktavyaḥ sa suyodhanaḥ
c śva idānīṃ pradṛśyethāḥ puruṣo bhava durmate
a manyase yac ca mūḍha tvaṃ na yotsyati janārdanaḥ
c sārathyena vṛtaḥ pārthair iti tvaṃ na bibheṣi ca
a jaghanyakālam apy etad bhaved yat sarvapārthivān
c nirdaheyam ahaṃ krodhāt tṛṇānīva hutāśanaḥ
a yudhiṣṭhiraniyogāt tu phalgunasya mahātmanaḥ
c kariṣye yudhyamānasya sārathyaṃ viditātmanaḥ
a yady utpatasi lokāṃs trīn yady āviśasi bhūtalam
c tatra tatrārjunarathaṃ prabhāte drakṣyase 'grataḥ
a yac cāpi bhīmasenasya manyase moghagarjitam
c duḥśāsanasya rudhiraṃ pītam ity avadhāryatām
a na tvāṃ samīkṣate pārtho nāpi rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c na bhīmaseno na yamau pratikūlaprabhāṣiṇam
 saṃjaya uvāca
a duryodhanasya tad vākyaṃ niśamya bharatarṣabhaḥ
c netrābhyām atitāmrābhyāṃ kaitavyaṃ samudaikṣata
a sa keśavam abhiprekṣya guḍākeśo mahāyaśāḥ
c abhyabhāṣata kaitavyaṃ pragṛhya vipulaṃ bhujam
a svavīryaṃ yaḥ samāśritya samāhvayati vai parān
c abhītaḥ pūrayañ śaktiṃ sa vai puruṣa ucyate
a paravīryaṃ samāśritya yaḥ samāhvayate parān
c kṣatrabandhur aśaktatvāl loke sa puruṣādhamaḥ
a sa tvaṃ pareṣāṃ vīryeṇa manyase vīryam ātmanaḥ
c svayaṃ kāpuruṣo mūḍhaḥ parāṃś ca kṣeptum icchasi
a yas tvaṃ vṛddhaṃ sarvarājñāṃ hitabuddhiṃ jitendriyam
c maraṇāya mahābuddhiṃ dīkṣayitvā vikatthase
a bhāvas te vidito 'smābhir durbuddhe kulapāṃsana
c na haniṣyanti gaṅgeyaṃ pāṇḍavā ghṛṇayeti ca
a yasya vīryaṃ samāśritya dhārtarāṣṭra vikatthase
c hantāsmi prathamaṃ bhīṣmaṃ miṣatāṃ sarvadhanvinām
a kaitavya gatvā bharatān sametya
suyodhanaṃ dhārtarāṣṭraṃ bravīhi
c tathety āha arjunaḥ savyasācī
niśāvyapāye bhavitā vimardaḥ
a yad vo 'bravīd vākyam adīnasattvo
madhye kurūṇāṃ harṣayan satyasaṃdhaḥ
c ahaṃ hantā pāṇḍavānām anīkaṃ
śālveyakāṃś ceti mamaiṣa bhāraḥ
a hanyām ahaṃ droṇam ṛte hi lokaṃ
na te bhayaṃ vidyate pāṇḍavebhyaḥ
c tato hi te labdhatamaṃ ca rājyaṃ
kṣayaṃ gatāḥ pāṇḍavāś ceti bhāvaḥ
a sa darpapūrṇo na samīkṣase tvam
anartham ātmany api vartamānam
c tasmād ahaṃ te prathamaṃ samūhe
hantā samakṣaṃ kuruvṛddham eva
a sūryodaye yuktasenaḥ pratīkṣya
dhvajī rathī rakṣa ca satyasaṃdham
c ahaṃ hi vaḥ paśyatāṃ dvīpam enaṃ
rathād bhīṣmaṃ pātayitāsmi bāṇaiḥ
a śvobhūte katthanāvākyaṃ vijñāsyati suyodhanaḥ
c arditaṃ śarajālena mayā dṛṣṭvā pitāmaham
a yad uktaś ca sabhāmadhye puruṣo hrasvadarśanaḥ
c kruddhena bhīmasenena bhrātā duḥśāsanas tava
a adharmajño nityavairī pāpabuddhir nṛśaṃsakṛt
c satyāṃ pratijñāṃ nacirād rakṣyase tāṃ suyodhana
a abhimānasya darpasya krodhapāruṣyayos tathā
c naiṣṭhuryasyāvalepasya ātmasaṃbhāvanasya ca
a nṛśaṃsatāyās taikṣṇyasya dharmavidveṣaṇasya ca
c adharmasyātivādasya vṛddhātikramaṇasya ca
a darśanasya ca vakrasya kṛtsnasyāpanayasya ca
c drakṣyasi tvaṃ phalaṃ tīvram acireṇa suyodhana
a vāsudevadvitīye hi mayi kruddhe narādhipa
c āśā te jīvite mūḍha rājye vā kena hetunā
a śānte bhīṣme tathā droṇe sūtaputre ca pātite
c nirāśo jīvite rājye putreṣu ca bhaviṣyasi
a bhrātṝṇāṃ nidhanaṃ dṛṣṭvā putrāṇāṃ ca suyodhana
c bhīmasenena nihato duṣkṛtāni smariṣyasi
a na dvitīyāṃ pratijñāṃ hi pratijñāsyati keśavaḥ
c satyaṃ bravīmy ahaṃ hy etat sarvaṃ satyaṃ bhaviṣyati
d yudhiṣṭhiro 'pi kaitavyam ulūkam idam abravīt
d ulūka madvaco brūhi gatvā tāta suyodhanam
d svena vṛttena me vṛttaṃ nādhigantuṃ tvam arhasi
d ubhayor antaraṃ veda sūnṛtānṛtayor api
d na cāhaṃ kāmaye pāpam api kīṭapipīlayoḥ
d kiṃ punar jñātiṣu vadhaṃ kāmayeyaṃ kathaṃ cana
d etadarthaṃ mayā tāta pañca grāmā vṛtāḥ purā
d kathaṃ tava sudurbuddhe na prekṣe vyasanaṃ mahat
d sa tvaṃ kāmaparītātmā mūḍhabhāvāc ca katthase
d tathaiva vāsudevasya na gṛhṇāsi hitaṃ vacaḥ
d kiṃ cedānīṃ bahūktena yudhyasva saha bāndhavaiḥ
d mama vipriyakartāraṃ kaitavya brūhi kauravam
d śrutaṃ vākyaṃ gṛhīto 'rtho mataṃ yat te tathāstu tat
d bhīmasenas tato vākyaṃ bhūya āha nṛpātmajam
d ulūka madvaco brūhi durmatiṃ pāpapūruṣam
d śaṭhaṃ naikṛtikaṃ pāpaṃ durācāraṃ suyodhanam
d gṛdhrodare vā vastavyaṃ pure vā nāgasāhvaye
d pratijñātaṃ mayā yac ca sabhāmadhye narādhama
d kartāhaṃ tad vacaḥ satyaṃ satyenaiva śapāmi te
d duḥśāsanasya rudhiraṃ hatvā pāsyāmy ahaṃ mṛdhe
d sakthinī tava bhaṅktvaiva hatvā hi tava sodarān
d sarveṣāṃ dhārtarāṣṭrāṇām ahaṃ mṛtyuḥ suyodhana
d sarveṣāṃ rājaputrāṇām abhimanyur asaṃśayam
d karmaṇā toṣayiṣyāmi bhūyaś caiva vacaḥ śṛṇu
d hatvā suyodhana tvāṃ vai sahitaṃ sarvasodaraiḥ
d ākramiṣye padā mūrdhni dharmarājasya paśyataḥ
d nakulas tu tato vākyam idam āha mahīpate
d ulūka brūhi kauravyaṃ dhārtarāṣṭraṃ suyodhanam
d śrutaṃ te gadato vākyaṃ sarvam eva yathātatham
d tathā kartāsmi kauravya yathā tvam anuśāsi mām
d sahadevo 'pi nṛpate idam āha vaco 'rthavat
d suyodhana matir yā te vṛthaiṣā te bhaviṣyati
d śociṣyase mahārāja saputrajñātibāndhavaḥ
d imaṃ ca kleśam asmākaṃ hṛṣṭo yat tvaṃ nikatthase
d virāṭadrupadau vṛddhāv ulūkam idam ūcatuḥ
d dāsabhāvaṃ niyaccheva sādhor iti matiḥ sadā
d tau ca dāsāv adāsau vā pauruṣaṃ yasya yādṛśam
d śikhaṇḍī tu tato vākyam ulūkam idam abravīt
d vaktavyo bhavatā rājā pāpeṣv abhirataḥ sadā
d paśya tvaṃ māṃ raṇe rājan kurvāṇaṃ karma dāruṇam
d yasya vīryaṃ samāsādya manyase vijayaṃ yudhi
d tam ahaṃ pātayiṣyāmi rathāt tava pitāmaham
d ahaṃ bhīṣmavadhāt sṛṣṭo nūnaṃ dhātrā mahātmanā
d so 'haṃ bhīṣmaṃ haniṣyāmi miṣatāṃ sarvadhanvinām
d dhṛṣṭadyumno 'pi kaitavyam ulūkam idam abravīt
d suyodhano mama vaco vaktavyo nṛpateḥ sutaḥ
d ahaṃ droṇaṃ haniṣyāmi sagaṇaṃ sahabāndhavam
d kartā cāhaṃ tathā karma yathā nānyaḥ kariṣyati
d tam abravīd dharmarājaḥ kāruṇyārthaṃ vaco mahat
d nāhaṃ jñātivadhaṃ rājan kāmayeyaṃ kathaṃ cana
d tavaiva doṣād durbuddhe sarvam etat tv anāvṛtam
d avaśyaṃ ca mayā kāryaṃ sarveṣāṃ caritaṃ mahat
d sa gaccha māciraṃ tāta ulūka yadi manyase
d iha vā tiṣṭha bhadraṃ te vayaṃ hi tava bāndhavāḥ
d ulūkas tu tato rājan dharmaputraṃ yudhiṣṭhiram
d āmantrya prayayau tatra yatra rājā suyodhanaḥ
d ulūkas tata āgamya duryodhanam amarṣaṇam
d arjunasya samādeśaṃ yathoktaṃ sarvam abravīt
d vāsudevasya bhīmasya dharmarājasya pauruṣam
d nakulasya virāṭasya drupadasya ca bhārata
d sahadevasya ca vaco dhṛṣṭadyumnaśikhaṇḍinoḥ
a ity uktaḥ kaitavo rājaṃs tad vākyam upadhārya ca
c anujñāto nivavṛte punar eva yathāgatam
a upāvṛtya tu pāṇḍubhyaḥ kaitavyo dhṛtarāṣṭrajam
c gatvā yathoktaṃ tat sarvam uvāca kurusaṃsadi
a keśavārjunayor vākyaṃ niśamya bharatarṣabhaḥ
a   yathoktaṃ sarvam abravīt
a kaitavyasya tu tad vākyaṃ
c duḥśāsanaṃ ca karṇaṃ ca śakuniṃ cābhyabhāṣata
a ājñāpayata rājñaś ca balaṃ mitrabalaṃ tathā
c yathā prāg udayāt sarvā yuktā tiṣṭhaty anīkinī
a tataḥ karṇasamādiṣṭā dūtāḥ pratvaritā rathaiḥ
c uṣṭravāmībhir apy anye sadaśvaiś ca mahājavaiḥ
a tūrṇaṃ pariyayuḥ senāṃ kṛtsnāṃ karṇasya śāsanāt
c ājñāpayanto rājñas tān yogaḥ prāg udayād iti
 saṃjaya uvāca
a ulūkasya vacaḥ śrutvā kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c senāṃ niryāpayām āsa dhṛṣṭadyumnapurogamām
a padātinīṃ nāgavatīṃ rathinīm aśvavṛndinīm
c caturvidhabalāṃ bhīmām akampyāṃ pṛthivīm iva
a bhīmasenādibhir guptāṃ sārjunaiś ca mahārathaiḥ
c dhṛṣṭadyumnavaśāṃ durgāṃ sāgarastimitopamām
a tasyās tv agre maheṣvāsaḥ pāñcālyo yuddhadurmadaḥ
c droṇaprepsur anīkāni dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ prakarṣati
a yathābalaṃ yathotsāhaṃ rathinaḥ samupādiśat
c arjunaṃ sūtaputrāya bhīmaṃ duryodhanāya ca
a aśvatthāmne ca nakulaṃ śaibyaṃ ca kṛtavarmaṇe
c saindhavāya ca vārṣṇeyaṃ yuyudhānam upādiśat
a śikhaṇḍinaṃ ca bhīṣmāya pramukhe samakalpayat
c sahadevaṃ śakunaye cekitānaṃ śalāya ca
a dhṛṣṭaketuṃ ca śalyāya gautamāyottamaujasam
c draupadeyāṃś ca pañcabhyas trigartebhyaḥ samādiśat
a vṛṣasenāya saubhadraṃ śeṣāṇāṃ ca mahīkṣitām
c samarthaṃ taṃ hi mene vai pārthād abhyadhikaṃ raṇe
a evaṃ vibhajya yodhāṃs tān pṛthak ca saha caiva ha
c jvālāvarṇo maheṣvāso droṇam aṃśam akalpayat
a dhṛṣṭadyumno maheṣvāsaḥ senāpatipatis tataḥ
c vidhivad vyūhya medhāvī yuddhāya dhṛtamānasaḥ
a yathādiṣṭāny anīkāni pāṇḍavānām ayojayat
c jayāya pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ yattas tasthau raṇājire
 dhṛtarāṣṭra uvāca
a pratijñāte phalgunena vadhe bhīṣmasya saṃjaya
c kim akurvanta me mandāḥ putrā duryodhanādayaḥ
a hatam eva hi paśyāmi gāṅgeyaṃ pitaraṃ raṇe
c vāsudevasahāyena pārthena dṛḍhadhanvanā
a sa cāparimitaprajñas tac chrutvā pārthabhāṣitam
c kim uktavān maheṣvāso bhīṣmaḥ praharatāṃ varaḥ
a senāpatyaṃ ca saṃprāpya kauravāṇāṃ dhuraṃdharaḥ
c kim aceṣṭata gāṅgeyo mahābuddhiparākramaḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tatas tat saṃjayas tasmai sarvam eva nyavedayat
c yathoktaṃ kuruvṛddhena bhīṣmeṇāmitatejasā
 saṃjaya uvāca
a senāpatyam anuprāpya bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo nṛpa
c duryodhanam uvācedaṃ vacanaṃ harṣayann iva
a namaskṛtvā kumārāya senānye śaktipāṇaye
c ahaṃ senāpatis te 'dya bhaviṣyāmi na saṃśayaḥ
a senākarmaṇy abhijño 'smi vyūheṣu vividheṣu ca
c karma kārayituṃ caiva bhṛtān apy abhṛtāṃs tathā
a yātrāyāneṣu yuddheṣu labdhapraśamaneṣu ca
c bhṛśaṃ veda mahārāja yathā veda bṛhaspatiḥ
a vyūhān api mahārambhān daivagāndharvamānuṣān
c tair ahaṃ mohayiṣyāmi pāṇḍavān vyetu te jvaraḥ
a so 'haṃ yotsyāmi tattvena pālayaṃs tava vāhinīm
c yathāvac chāstrato rājan vyetu te mānaso jvaraḥ
 duryodhana uvāca
a na vidyate me gāṅgeya bhayaṃ devāsureṣv api
c samasteṣu mahābāho satyam etad bravīmi te
a kiṃ punas tvayi durdharṣe senāpatye vyavasthite
c droṇe ca puruṣavyāghre sthite yuddhābhinandini
a bhavadbhyāṃ puruṣāgryābhyāṃ sthitābhyāṃ vijayo mama
c na durlabhaṃ kuruśreṣṭha devarājyam api dhruvam
a rathasaṃkhyāṃ tu kārtsnyena pareṣām ātmanas tathā
c tathaivātirathānāṃ ca vettum icchāmi kaurava
a pitāmaho hi kuśalaḥ pareṣām ātmanas tathā
c śrotum icchāmy ahaṃ sarvaiḥ sahaibhir vasudhādhipaiḥ
 bhīṣma uvāca
a gāndhāre śṛṇu rājendra rathasaṃkhyāṃ svake bale
c ye rathāḥ pṛthivīpāla tathaivātirathāś ca ye
a bahūnīha sahasrāṇi prayutāny arbudāni ca
c rathānāṃ tava senāyāṃ yathāmukhyaṃ tu me śṛṇu
a bhavān agre rathodāraḥ saha sarvaiḥ sahodaraiḥ
c duḥśāsanaprabhṛtibhir bhrātṛbhiḥ śatasaṃmitaiḥ
a sarve kṛtapraharaṇāś chedyabhedyaviśāradāḥ
c rathopasthe gajaskandhe gadāyuddhe 'sicarmaṇi
a saṃyantāraḥ prahartāraḥ kṛtāstrā bhārasādhanāḥ
c iṣvastre droṇaśiṣyāś ca kṛpasya ca śaradvataḥ
a ete haniṣyanti raṇe pāñcālān yuddhadurmadān
c kṛtakilbiṣāḥ pāṇḍaveyair dhārtarāṣṭrā manasvinaḥ
a tato 'haṃ bharataśreṣṭha sarvasenāpatis tava
c śatrūn vidhvaṃsayiṣyāmi kadarthīkṛtya pāṇḍavān
e na tv ātmano guṇān vaktum arhāmi vidito 'smi te
a kṛtavarmā tv atiratho bhojaḥ praharatāṃ varaḥ
c arthasiddhiṃ tava raṇe kariṣyati na saṃśayaḥ
a astravidbhir anādhṛṣyo dūrapātī dṛḍhāyudhaḥ
c haniṣyati ripūṃs tubhyaṃ mahendro dānavān iva
a madrarājo maheṣvāsaḥ śalyo me 'tiratho mataḥ
c spardhate vāsudevena yo vai nityaṃ raṇe raṇe
a bhāgineyān nijāṃs tyaktvā śalyas te rathasattamaḥ
c eṣa yotsyati saṃgrāme kṛṣṇaṃ cakragadādharam
a sāgarormisamair vegaiḥ plāvayann iva śātravān
c bhūriśravāḥ kṛtāstraś ca tava cāpi hitaḥ suhṛt
a saumadattir maheṣvāso rathayūthapayūthapaḥ
c balakṣayam amitrāṇāṃ sumahāntaṃ kariṣyati
a sindhurājo mahārāja mato me dviguṇo rathaḥ
c yotsyate samare rājan vikrānto rathasattamaḥ
a draupadīharaṇe pūrvaṃ parikliṣṭaḥ sa pāṇḍavaiḥ
c saṃsmaraṃs taṃ parikleśaṃ yotsyate paravīrahā
a etena hi tadā rājaṃs tapa āsthāya dāruṇam
c sudurlabho varo labdhaḥ pāṇḍavān yoddhum āhave
a sa eṣa rathaśārdūlas tad vairaṃ saṃsmaran raṇe
c yotsyate pāṇḍavāṃs tāta prāṇāṃs tyaktvā sudustyajān
 bhīṣma uvāca
a sudakṣiṇas tu kāmbojo ratha ekaguṇo mataḥ
c tavārthasiddhim ākāṅkṣan yotsyate samare paraiḥ
a etasya rathasiṃhasya tavārthe rājasattama
c parākramaṃ yathendrasya drakṣyanti kuravo yudhi
a etasya rathavaṃśo hi tigmavegaprahāriṇām
c kāmbojānāṃ mahārāja śalabhānām ivāyatiḥ
a nīlo māhiṣmatīvāsī nīlavarmadharas tava
c rathavaṃśena śatrūṇāṃ kadanaṃ vai kariṣyati
a kṛtavairaḥ purā caiva sahadevena pārthivaḥ
c yotsyate satataṃ rājaṃs tavārthe kurusattama
a vindānuvindāv āvantyau sametau rathasattamau
c kṛtinau samare tāta dṛḍhavīryaparākramau
a etau tau puruṣavyāghrau ripusainyaṃ pradhakṣyataḥ
c gadāprāsāsinārācais tomaraiś ca bhujacyutaiḥ
a yuddhābhikāmau samare krīḍantāv iva yūthapau
c yūthamadhye mahārāja vicarantau kṛtāntavat
a trigartā bhrātaraḥ pañca rathodārā matā mama
c kṛtavairāś ca pārthena virāṭanagare tadā
a makarā iva rājendra samuddhatataraṅgiṇīm
c gaṅgāṃ vikṣobhayiṣyanti pārthānāṃ yudhi vāhinīm
a te rathāḥ pañca rājendra yeṣāṃ satyaratho mukham
c ete yotsyanti samare saṃsmarantaḥ purā kṛtam
a vyalīkaṃ pāṇḍaveyena bhīmasenānujena ha
c diśo vijayatā rājañ śvetavāhena bhārata
d kadarthīkṛtya saṃgrāme dāpitāḥ karam uttamam
a te haniṣyanti pārthānāṃ samāsādya mahārathān
c varān varān maheṣvāsān kṣatriyāṇāṃ dhuraṃdharāḥ
a lakṣmaṇas tava putras tu tathā duḥśāsanasya ca
c ubhau tau puruṣavyāghrau saṃgrāmeṣv anivartinau
a taruṇau sukumārau ca rājaputrau tarasvinau
c yuddhānāṃ ca viśeṣajñau praṇetārau ca sarvaśaḥ
a rathau tau rathaśārdūla matau me rathasattamau
c kṣatradharmaratau vīrau mahat karma kariṣyataḥ
a daṇḍadhāro mahārāja ratha eko nararṣabhaḥ
c yotsyate samaraṃ prāpya svena sainyena pālitaḥ
a bṛhadbalas tathā rājā kausalyo rathasattamaḥ
c ratho mama matas tāta dṛḍhavegaparākramaḥ
a eṣa yotsyati saṃgrāme svāṃ camūṃ saṃpraharṣayan
c ugrāyudho maheṣvāso dhārtarāṣṭrahite rataḥ
d eṣa yotsyati saṃgrāme ratha ekaguṇo mataḥ
a kṛpaḥ śāradvato rājan rathayūthapayūthapaḥ
c priyān prāṇān parityajya pradhakṣyati ripūṃs tava
a gautamasya maharṣer ya ācāryasya śaradvataḥ
c kārttikeya ivājeyaḥ śarastambāt suto 'bhavat
a eṣa senāṃ bahuvidhāṃ vividhāyudhakārmukām
c agnivat samare tāta cariṣyati vimardayan
 bhīṣma uvāca
a śakunir mātulas te 'sau ratha eko narādhipa
c prasajya pāṇḍavair vairaṃ yotsyate nātra saṃśayaḥ
a etasya sainyā durdharṣāḥ samare 'pratiyāyinaḥ
c vikṛtāyudhabhūyiṣṭhā vāyuvegasamā jave
a droṇaputro maheṣvāsaḥ sarveṣām ati dhanvinām
c samare citrayodhī ca dṛḍhāstraś ca mahārathaḥ
a etasya hi mahārāja yathā gāṇḍīvadhanvanaḥ
c śarāsanād vinirmuktāḥ saṃsaktā yānti sāyakāḥ
a naiṣa śakyo mayā vīraḥ saṃkhyātuṃ rathasattamaḥ
c nirdahed api lokāṃs trīn icchann eṣa mahāyaśāḥ
a krodhas tejaś ca tapasā saṃbhṛto ''śramavāsinā
c droṇenānugṛhītaś ca divyair astrair udāradhīḥ
a doṣas tv asya mahān eko yenaiṣa bharatarṣabha
c na me ratho nātiratho mataḥ pārthivasattama
a jīvitaṃ priyam atyartham āyuṣkāmaḥ sadā dvijaḥ
c na hy asya sadṛśaḥ kaś cid ubhayoḥ senayor api
a hanyād ekarathenaiva devānām api vāhinīm
c vapuṣmāṃs talaghoṣeṇa sphoṭayed api parvatān
a asaṃkhyeyaguṇo vīraḥ prahartā dāruṇadyutiḥ
c daṇḍapāṇir ivāsahyaḥ kālavat pracariṣyati
a yugāntāgnisamaḥ krodhe siṃhagrīvo mahāmatiḥ
c eṣa bhārata yuddhasya pṛṣṭhaṃ saṃśamayiṣyati
a pitā tv asya mahātejā vṛddho 'pi yuvabhir varaḥ
c raṇe karma mahat kartā tatra me nāsti saṃśayaḥ
d pitāsya tu raṇe karma mahat kartā na saṃśayaḥ
a astravegāniloddhūtaḥ senākakṣendhanotthitaḥ
c pāṇḍuputrasya sainyāni pradhakṣyati jaye dhṛtaḥ
a rathayūthapayūthānāṃ yūthapaḥ sa nararṣabhaḥ
c bhāradvājātmajaḥ kartā karma tīvraṃ hitāya vaḥ
a sarvamūrdhābhiṣiktānām ācāryaḥ sthaviro guruḥ
c gacched antaṃ sṛñjayānāṃ priyas tv asya dhanaṃjayaḥ
a naiṣa jātu maheṣvāsaḥ pārtham akliṣṭakāriṇam
c hanyād ācāryakaṃ dīptaṃ saṃsmṛtya guṇanirjitam
a ślāghaty eṣa sadā vīraḥ pārthasya guṇavistaraiḥ
c putrād abhyadhikaṃ caiva bhāradvājo 'nupaśyati
a hanyād ekarathenaiva devagandharvadānavān
c ekībhūtān api raṇe divyair astraiḥ pratāpavān
a pauravo rājaśārdūlas tava rājan mahārathaḥ
c mato mama ratho vīra paravīrarathārujaḥ
a svena sainyena sahitaḥ pratapañ śatruvāhinīm
c pradhakṣyati sa pāñcālān kakṣaṃ kṛṣṇagatir yathā
a satyavrato rathavaro rājaputro mahārathaḥ
c tava rājan ripubale kālavat pracariṣyati
a etasya yodhā rājendra vicitrakavacāyudhāḥ
c vicariṣyanti saṃgrāme nighnantaḥ śātravāṃs tava
a vṛṣaseno rathāgryas te karṇaputro mahārathaḥ
c pradhakṣyati ripūṇāṃ te balāni balināṃ varaḥ
a jalasaṃdho mahātejā rājan rathavaras tava
c tyakṣyate samare prāṇān māgadhaḥ paravīrahā
a eṣa yotsyati saṃgrāme gajaskandhaviśāradaḥ
c rathena vā mahābāhuḥ kṣapayañ śatruvāhinīm
a ratha eṣa mahārāja mato mama nararṣabhaḥ
c tvadarthe tyakṣyati prāṇān saha sainyo mahāraṇe
a eṣa vikrāntayodhī ca citrayodhī ca saṃgare
c vītabhīś cāpi te rājañ śātravaiḥ saha yotsyate
a bāhlīko 'tirathaś caiva samare cānivartitā
c mama rājan mato yuddhe śūro vaivasvatopamaḥ
a na hy eṣa samaraṃ prāpya nivarteta kathaṃ cana
c yathā satatago rājan nābhihatya parān raṇe
a senāpatir mahārāja satyavāṃs te mahārathaḥ
c raṇeṣv adbhutakarmā ca rathaḥ pararathārujaḥ
a etasya samaraṃ dṛṣṭvā na vyathāsti kathaṃ cana
c utsmayann abhyupaity eṣa parān rathapathe sthitān
a eṣa cāriṣu vikrāntaḥ karma satpuruṣocitam
c kartā vimarde sumahat tvadarthe puruṣottamaḥ
a alāyudho rākṣasendraḥ krūrakarmā mahābalaḥ
c haniṣyati parān rājan pūrvavairam anusmaran
a eṣa rākṣasasainyānāṃ sarveṣāṃ rathasattamaḥ
c māyāvī dṛḍhavairaś ca samare vicariṣyati
a prāgjyotiṣādhipo vīro bhagadattaḥ pratāpavān
c gajāṅkuśadharaśreṣṭho rathe caiva viśāradaḥ
a etena yuddham abhavat purā gāṇḍīvadhanvanaḥ
c divasān subahūn rājann ubhayor jayagṛddhinoḥ
a tataḥ sakhāyaṃ gāndhāre mānayan pākaśāsanam
c akarot saṃvidaṃ tena pāṇḍavena mahātmanā
a eṣa yotsyati saṃgrāme gajaskandhaviśāradaḥ
c airāvatagato rājā devānām iva vāsavaḥ
 bhīṣma uvāca
a acalo vṛṣakaś caiva bhrātarau sahitāv ubhau
c rathau tava durādharṣau śatrūn vidhvaṃsayiṣyataḥ
a balavantau naravyāghrau dṛḍhakrodhau prahāriṇau
c gāndhāramukhyau taruṇau darśanīyau mahābalau
a sakhā te dayito nityaṃ ya eṣa raṇakarkaśaḥ
c protsāhayati rājaṃs tvāṃ vigrahe pāṇḍavaiḥ saha
a paruṣaḥ katthano nīcaḥ karṇo vaikartanas tava
c mantrī netā ca bandhuś ca mānī cātyantam ucchritaḥ
a eṣa naiva rathaḥ pūrṇo nāpy evātiratho nṛpa
c viyuktaḥ kavacenaiṣa sahajena vicetanaḥ
e kuṇḍalābhyāṃ ca divyābhyāṃ viyuktaḥ satataṃ ghṛṇī
a abhiśāpāc ca rāmasya brāhmaṇasya ca bhāṣaṇāt
c karaṇānāṃ viyogāc ca tena me 'rdharatho mataḥ
e naiṣa phalgunam āsādya punar jīvan vimokṣyate
 saṃjaya uvāca
a tato 'bravīn mahābāhur droṇaḥ śastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
c evam etad yathāttha tvaṃ na mithyāstīti kiṃ cana
a raṇe raṇe 'timānī ca vimukhaś caiva dṛśyate
c ghṛṇī karṇaḥ pramādī ca tena me 'rdharatho mataḥ
a etac chrutvā tu rādheyaḥ krodhād utphullalocanaḥ
c uvāca bhīṣmaṃ rājendra tudan vāgbhiḥ pratodavat
a pitāmaha yatheṣṭaṃ māṃ vākśarair upakṛntasi
c anāgasaṃ sadā dveṣād evam eva pade pade
e marṣayāmi ca tat sarvaṃ duryodhanakṛtena vai
a tvaṃ tu māṃ manyase 'śaktaṃ yathā kāpuruṣaṃ tathā
c bhavān ardharatho mahyaṃ mato nāsty atra saṃśayaḥ
a sarvasya jagataś caiva gāṅgeya na mṛṣā vade
c kurūṇām ahito nityaṃ na ca rājāvabudhyate
a ko hi nāma samāneṣu rājasūdāttakarmasu
c tejovadham imaṃ kuryād vibhedayiṣur āhave
e yathā tvaṃ guṇanirdeśād aparādhaṃ cikīrṣasi
a na hāyanair na palitair na vittair na ca bandhubhiḥ
c mahārathatvaṃ saṃkhyātuṃ śakyaṃ kṣatrasya kaurava
a balajyeṣṭhaṃ smṛtaṃ kṣatraṃ mantrajyeṣṭhā dvijātayaḥ
c dhanajyeṣṭhāḥ smṛtā vaiśyāḥ śūdrās tu vayasādhikāḥ
a yathecchakaṃ svayaṃgrāhād rathān atirathāṃs tathā
c kāmadveṣasamāyukto mohāt prakurute bhavān
a duryodhana mahābāho sādhu samyag avekṣyatām
c tyajyatāṃ duṣṭabhāvo 'yaṃ bhīṣmaḥ kilbiṣakṛt tava
a bhinnā hi senā nṛpate duḥsaṃdheyā bhavaty uta
c maulāpi puruṣavyāghra kim u nānā samutthitā
a eṣāṃ dvaidhaṃ samutpannaṃ yodhānāṃ yudhi bhārata
c tejovadho naḥ kriyate pratyakṣeṇa viśeṣataḥ
a rathānāṃ kva ca vijñānaṃ kva ca bhīṣmo 'lpacetanaḥ
c aham āvārayiṣyāmi pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm
a āsādya mām amogheṣuṃ gamiṣyanti diśo daśa
c pāṇḍavāḥ sahapañcālāḥ śārdūlaṃ vṛṣabhā iva
a kva ca yuddhavimardo vā mantrāḥ suvyāhṛtāni vā
c kva ca bhīṣmo gatavayā mandātmā kālamohitaḥ
a spardhate hi sadā nityaṃ sarveṇa jagatā saha
c na cānyaṃ puruṣaṃ kaṃ cin manyate moghadarśanaḥ
a śrotavyaṃ khalu vṛddhānām iti śāstranidarśanam
c na tv evāpy ativṛddhānāṃ punar bālā hi te matāḥ
a aham eko haniṣyāmi pāṇḍavān nātra saṃśayaḥ
c suyuddhe rājaśārdūla yaśo bhīṣmaṃ gamiṣyati
a kṛtaḥ senāpatis tv eṣa tvayā bhīṣmo narādhipa
c senāpatiṃ guṇo gantā na tu yodhān kathaṃ cana
a nāhaṃ jīvati gāṅgeye yotsye rājan kathaṃ cana
c hate tu bhīṣme yodhāsmi sarvair eva mahārathaiḥ
 bhīṣma uvāca
a samudyato 'yaṃ bhāro me sumahān sāgaropamaḥ
c dhārtarāṣṭrasya saṃgrāme varṣapūgābhicintitaḥ
a tasminn abhyāgate kāle pratapte lomaharṣaṇe
c mithobhedo na me kāryas tena jīvasi sūtaja
a na hy ahaṃ nādya vikramya sthaviro 'pi śiśos tava
c yuddhaśraddhāṃ raṇe chindyāṃ jīvitasya ca sūtaja
a jāmadagnyena rāmeṇa mahāstrāṇi pramuñcatā
