a prabhātāyāṃ tu śarvaryāṃ punar eva sutas tava
c madhye sarvasya sainyasya pitāmaham apṛcchata
a pāṇḍaveyasya gāṅgeya yad etat sainyam uttamam
c prabhūtanaranāgāśvaṃ mahārathasamākulam
a bhīmārjunaprabhṛtibhir maheṣvāsair mahābalaiḥ
c lokapālopamair guptaṃ dhṛṣṭadyumnapurogamaiḥ
a apradhṛṣyam anāvāryam udvṛttam iva sāgaram
c senāsāgaram akṣobhyam api devair mahāhave
a kena kālena gāṅgeya kṣapayethā mahādyute
c ācāryo vā maheṣvāsaḥ kṛpo vā sumahābalaḥ
a karṇo vā samaraślāghī drauṇir vā dvijasattamaḥ
c divyāstraviduṣaḥ sarve bhavanto hi bale mama
a etad icchāmy ahaṃ jñātuṃ paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi me
c hṛdi nityaṃ mahābāho vaktum arhasi tan mama
 bhīṣma uvāca
a anurūpaṃ kuruśreṣṭha tvayy etat pṛthivīpate
c balābalam amitrāṇāṃ sveṣāṃ ca yadi pṛcchasi
a śṛṇu rājan mama raṇe yā śaktiḥ paramā bhavet
c astravīryaṃ raṇe yac ca bhujayoś ca mahābhuja
a ārjavenaiva yuddhena yoddhavya itaro janaḥ
c māyāyuddhena māyāvī ity etad dharmaniścayaḥ
a hanyām ahaṃ mahābāho pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm
c divase divase kṛtvā bhāgaṃ prāgāhnikaṃ mama
a yodhānāṃ daśasāhasraṃ kṛtvā bhāgaṃ mahādyute
c sahasraṃ rathinām ekam eṣa bhāgo mato mama
a anenāhaṃ vidhānena saṃnaddhaḥ satatotthitaḥ
c kṣapayeyaṃ mahat sainyaṃ kālenānena bhārata
a yadi tv astrāṇi muñceyaṃ mahānti samare sthitaḥ
c śatasāhasraghātīni hanyāṃ māsena bhārata
 saṃjaya uvāca
a śrutvā bhīṣmasya tad vākyaṃ rājā duryodhanas tadā
c paryapṛcchata rājendra droṇam aṅgirasāṃ varam
a ācārya kena kālena pāṇḍuputrasya sainikān
c nihanyā iti taṃ droṇaḥ pratyuvāca hasann iva
a sthaviro 'smi kuruśreṣṭha mandaprāṇaviceṣṭitaḥ
c astrāgninā nirdaheyaṃ pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm
a yathā bhīṣmaḥ śāṃtanavo māseneti matir mama
c eṣā me paramā śaktir etan me paramaṃ balam
a dvābhyām eva tu māsābhyāṃ kṛpaḥ śāradvato 'bravīt
c drauṇis tu daśarātreṇa pratijajñe balakṣayam
e karṇas tu pañcarātreṇa pratijajñe mahāstravit
a tac chrutvā sūtaputrasya vākyaṃ sāgaragāsutaḥ
c jahāsa sasvanaṃ hāsaṃ vākyaṃ cedam uvāca ha
a na hi tāvad raṇe pārthaṃ bāṇakhaḍgadhanurdharam
c vāsudevasamāyuktaṃ rathenodyantam acyutam
a samāgacchasi rādheya tenaivam abhimanyase
c śakyam evaṃ ca bhūyaś ca tvayā vaktuṃ yatheṣṭataḥ
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a etac chrutvā tu kaunteyaḥ sarvān bhrātṝn upahvare
c āhūya bharataśreṣṭha idaṃ vacanam abravīt
a dhārtarāṣṭrasya sainyeṣu ye cārapuruṣā mama
c te pravṛttiṃ prayacchanti mamemāṃ vyuṣitāṃ niśām
a duryodhanaḥ kilāpṛcchad āpageyaṃ mahāvratam
c kena kālena pāṇḍūnāṃ hanyāḥ sainyam iti prabho
a māseneti ca tenokto dhārtarāṣṭraḥ sudurmatiḥ
c tāvatā cāpi kālena droṇo 'pi pratyajānata
a gautamo dviguṇaṃ kālam uktavān iti naḥ śrutam
c drauṇis tu daśarātreṇa pratijajñe mahāstravit
a tathā divyāstravit karṇaḥ saṃpṛṣṭaḥ kurusaṃsadi
c pañcabhir divasair hantuṃ sa sainyaṃ pratijajñivān
a tasmād aham apīcchāmi śrotum arjuna te vacaḥ
c kālena kiyatā śatrūn kṣapayer iti saṃyuge
a evam ukto guḍākeśaḥ pārthivena dhanaṃjayaḥ
c vāsudevam avekṣyedaṃ vacanaṃ pratyabhāṣata
a sarva ete mahātmānaḥ kṛtāstrāś citrayodhinaḥ
c asaṃśayaṃ mahārāja hanyur eva balaṃ tava
a apaitu te manastāpo yathāsatyaṃ bravīmy aham
c hanyām ekarathenāhaṃ vāsudevasahāyavān
a sāmarān api lokāṃs trīn sahasthāvarajaṅgamān
c bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhaviṣyac ca nimeṣād iti me matiḥ
d yāvad icched dharir ayaṃ tāvad asti na cānyathā
a yat tad ghoraṃ paśupatiḥ prādād astraṃ mahan mama
c kairāte dvandvayuddhe vai tad idaṃ mayi vartate
a yad yugānte paśupatiḥ sarvabhūtāni saṃharan
c prayuṅkte puruṣavyāghra tad idaṃ mayi vartate
a tan na jānāti gāṅgeyo na droṇo na ca gautamaḥ
c na ca droṇasuto rājan kuta eva tu sūtajaḥ
a na tu yuktaṃ raṇe hantuṃ divyair astraiḥ pṛthagjanam
c ārjavenaiva yuddhena vijeṣyāmo vayaṃ parān
a tatheme puruṣavyāghrāḥ sahāyās tava pārthiva
c sarve divyāstraviduṣaḥ sarve yuddhābhinandinaḥ
d vīravratadharāḥ sarve sarve sucaritavratāḥ
a vedāntāvabhṛthasnātāḥ sarva ete 'parājitāḥ
c nihanyuḥ samare senāṃ devānām api pāṇḍava
a śikhaṇḍī yuyudhānaś ca dhṛṣṭadyumnaś ca pārṣataḥ
c bhīmaseno yamau cobhau yudhāmanyūttamaujasau
a virāṭadrupadau cobhau bhīṣmadroṇasamau yudhi
b śaṅkhaś caiva mahābāhur haiḍimbaś ca mahābalaḥ
b putro 'syāñjanaparvā tu mahābalaparākramaḥ
b śaineyaś ca mahābāhuḥ sahāyo raṇakovidaḥ
b abhimanyuś ca balavān draupadyāḥ pañca cātmajāḥ
c svayaṃ cāpi samartho 'si trailokyotsādane api
a krodhād yaṃ puruṣaṃ paśyes tvaṃ vāsavasamadyute
c kṣipraṃ na sa bhaved vyaktam iti tvāṃ vedmi kaurava
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
a tataḥ prabhāte vimale dhārtarāṣṭreṇa coditāḥ
c duryodhanena rājānaḥ prayayuḥ pāṇḍavān prati
a āplāvya śucayaḥ sarve sragviṇaḥ śuklavāsasaḥ
c gṛhītaśastrā dhvajinaḥ svasti vācya hutāgnayaḥ
a sarve vedavidaḥ śūrāḥ sarve sucaritavratāḥ
c sarve karmakṛtaś caiva sarve cāhavalakṣaṇāḥ
a āhaveṣu parāṃl lokāñ jigīṣanto mahābalāḥ
c ekāgramanasaḥ sarve śraddadhānāḥ parasya ca
a vindānuvindāv āvantyau kekayā bāhlikaiḥ saha
c prayayuḥ sarva evaite bhāradvājapurogamāḥ
a aśvatthāmā śāṃtanavaḥ saindhavo 'tha jayadrathaḥ
c dākṣiṇātyāḥ pratīcyāś ca pārvatīyāś ca ye rathāḥ
a gāndhārarājaḥ śakuniḥ prācyodīcyāś ca sarvaśaḥ
c śakāḥ kirātā yavanāḥ śibayo 'tha vasātayaḥ
a svaiḥ svair anīkaiḥ sahitāḥ parivārya mahāratham
c ete mahārathāḥ sarve dvitīye niryayur bale
a kṛtavarmā sahānīkas trigartāś ca mahābalāḥ
c duryodhanaś ca nṛpatir bhrātṛbhiḥ parivāritaḥ
a śalo bhūriśravāḥ śalyaḥ kausalyo 'tha bṛhadbalaḥ
c ete paścād avartanta dhārtarāṣṭrapurogamāḥ
a te samena pathā yātvā yotsyamānā mahārathāḥ
c kurukṣetrasya paścārdhe vyavatiṣṭhanta daṃśitāḥ
a duryodhanas tu śibiraṃ kārayām āsa bhārata
c yathaiva hāstinapuraṃ dvitīyaṃ samalaṃkṛtam
a na viśeṣaṃ vijānanti purasya śibirasya vā
c kuśalā api rājendra narā nagaravāsinaḥ
a tādṛśāny eva durgāṇi rājñām api mahīpatiḥ
c kārayām āsa kauravyaḥ śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ
a pañcayojanam utsṛjya maṇḍalaṃ tad raṇājiram
c senāniveśās te rājann āviśañ śatasaṃghaśaḥ
a tatra te pṛthivīpālā yathotsāhaṃ yathābalam
c viviśuḥ śibirāṇy āśu dravyavanti sahasraśaḥ
a teṣāṃ duryodhano rājā sasainyānāṃ mahātmanām
c vyādideśa sabāhyānāṃ bhakṣyabhojyam anuttamam
a sagajāśvamanuṣyāṇāṃ ye ca śilpopajīvinaḥ
c ye cānye 'nugatās tatra sūtamāgadhabandinaḥ
a vaṇijo gaṇikā vārā ye caiva prekṣakā janāḥ
c sarvāṃs tān kauravo rājā vidhivat pratyavaikṣata
 vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca
 saṃjayenaivam uktas tu dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ sudurmanāḥ
 vipulaṃ cintayaṃs tathau gāndhāryā vidureṇa ca
a tathaiva rājā kaunteyo dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
c dhṛṣṭadyumnamukhān vīrāṃś codayām āsa bhārata
a cedikāśikarūṣāṇāṃ netāraṃ dṛḍhavikramam
c senāpatim amitraghnaṃ dhṛṣṭaketum athādiśat
a virāṭaṃ drupadaṃ caiva yuyudhānaṃ śikhaṇḍinam
c pāñcālyau ca maheṣvāsau yudhāmanyūttamaujasau
a te śūrāś citravarmāṇas taptakuṇḍaladhāriṇaḥ
c ājyāvasiktā jvalitā dhiṣṇyeṣv iva hutāśanāḥ
e aśobhanta maheṣvāsā grahāḥ prajvalitā iva
a so 'tha sainyaṃ yathāyogaṃ pūjayitvā nararṣabhaḥ
c dideśa tāny anīkāni prayāṇāya mahīpatiḥ
a abhimanyuṃ bṛhantaṃ ca draupadeyāṃś ca sarvaśaḥ
c dhṛṣṭadyumnamukhān etān prāhiṇot pāṇḍunandanaḥ
a bhīmaṃ ca yuyudhānaṃ ca pāṇḍavaṃ ca dhanaṃjayam
c dvitīyaṃ preṣayām āsa balaskandhaṃ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
a bhāṇḍaṃ samāropayatāṃ caratāṃ saṃpradhāvatām
c hṛṣṭānāṃ tatra yodhānāṃ śabdo divam ivāspṛśat
a svayam eva tataḥ paścād virāṭadrupadānvitaḥ
c tathānyaiḥ pṛthivīpālaiḥ saha prāyān mahīpatiḥ
a bhīmadhanvāyanī senā dhṛṣṭadyumnapuraskṛtā
c gaṅgeva pūrṇā stimitā syandamānā vyadṛśyata
a tataḥ punar anīkāni vyayojayata buddhimān
c mohayan dhṛtarāṣṭrasya putrāṇāṃ buddhinisravam
a draupadeyān maheṣvāsān abhimanyuṃ ca pāṇḍavaḥ
c nakulaṃ sahadevaṃ ca sarvāṃś caiva prabhadrakān
a daśa cāśvasahasrāṇi dvisāhasraṃ ca dantinaḥ
c ayutaṃ ca padātīnāṃ rathāḥ pañcaśatās tathā
a bhīmasenaṃ ca durdharṣaṃ prathamaṃ prādiśad balam
c madhyame tu virāṭaṃ ca jayatsenaṃ ca māgadham
a mahārathau ca pāñcālyau yudhāmanyūttamaujasau
c vīryavantau mahātmānau gadākārmukadhāriṇau
e anvayātāṃ tato madhye vāsudevadhanaṃjayau
f tau dṛṣṭvā pṛthivīpālān naṣṭam ity eva menire
f antarikṣagatāḥ sarve devāḥ sendrapurogamāḥ
a babhūvur atisaṃrabdhāḥ kṛtapraharaṇā narāḥ
c teṣāṃ viṃśatisāhasrā dhvajāḥ śūrair adhiṣṭhitāḥ
a pañca nāgasahasrāṇi rathavaṃśāś ca sarvaśaḥ
c padātayaś ca ye śūrāḥ kārmukāsigadādharāḥ
e sahasraśo 'nvayuḥ paścād agrataś ca sahasraśaḥ
a yudhiṣṭhiro yatra sainye svayam eva balārṇave
c tatra te pṛthivīpālā bhūyiṣṭhaṃ paryavasthitāḥ
a tatra nāgasahasrāṇi hayānām ayutāni ca
c tathā rathasahasrāṇi padātīnāṃ ca bhārata
d cekitānaḥ svasainyena mahatā pārthivarṣabha
d dhṛṣṭaketuś ca cedīnāṃ praṇetā pārthivo yayau
d sātyakiś ca maheṣvāso vṛṣṇīnāṃ pravaro rathaḥ
d vṛtaḥ śatasahasreṇa rathānāṃ praṇudan balī
d kṣatradevabrahmadevau rathasthau puruṣarṣabhau
d jaghanaṃ pālayantau ca pṛṣṭhato 'nuprajagmatuḥ
d śakaṭāpaṇaveśāś ca yānaṃ yugyaṃ ca sarvaśaḥ
d tatra nāgasahasrāṇi hayānām ayutāni ca
d phalgu sarvaṃ kalatraṃ ca yat kiṃ cit kṛśadurbalam
d kośasaṃcayavāhāṃś ca koṣṭhāgāraṃ tathaiva ca
d gajānīkena saṃgṛhya śanaiḥ prāyād yudhiṣṭhiraḥ
d tam anvayāt satyadhṛtiḥ saucittir yuddhadurmadaḥ
d śreṇimān vasudānaś ca putraḥ kāśyasya vā vibhuḥ
d rathā viṃśatisāhasrā ye teṣām anuyāyinaḥ
d hayānāṃ caiva koṭyaś ca mahatāṃ kiṅkiṇīkinām
d gajā viṃśatisāhasrā īṣādantāḥ prahāriṇaḥ
d kulīnā bhinnakaraṭā meghā iva visarpiṇaḥ
d ṣaṣṭir nāgasahasrāṇi daśānyāni ca bhārata
d yudhiṣṭhirasya yāny āsan yudhi senā mahātmanaḥ
d kṣaranta iva jīmūtāḥ prabhinnakaraṭāmukhāḥ
d rājānam anvayuḥ paścāc calanta iva parvatāḥ
d evaṃ tasya balaṃ bhīmaṃ kuntīputrasya dhīmataḥ
e yad āśrityābhiyuyudhe dhārtarāṣṭraṃ suyodhanam
a tato 'nye śataśaḥ paścāt sahasrāyutaśo narāḥ
c nadantaḥ prayayus teṣām anīkāni sahasraśaḥ
a tatra bherīsahasrāṇi śaṅkhānām ayutāni ca
c vādayanti sma saṃhṛṣṭāḥ sahasrāyutaśo narāḥ
